
brahmasUtrabhAShyaM

shrIshaN^karAcAryabhagavatpAdair viracitam.

(1.1)
|| prathame.adhyAye, prathamaH pAdaH || 

atra pAde spaShTabrahmaliN^gayuktAnAM vAkyAnAM vicAraH ||

1. brahmajij~nAsAdhikaraNam

|| 1.1.1 ||

yuShmadasmatpratyayagocarayor viShayaviShayiNoH tamaHprakAshavad viruddhasvabhAvayoH itaretarabhAvAnupapattau siddhAyAM taddharmANAM api sutarAm itaretarabhAvAnupapattiH | ityato.asmatpratyayagocare viShayiNi cidAtmake yuShmatpratyayagocarasya viShayasya cAdhyAsaH, tadviparyayeNa viShayiNaH taddharmANAM ca viShaye.adhyAso mithyeti bhavituM yuktam | tathApyanyonyasminn anyonyAtmakatAm anyonyadharmAMshcAdhyasyetaretarAvivekena, atyantaviviktayor mithyAj~nAnanimittaH satyAnR^ite mithunIkR^ite, aham idaM mamedaM iti naisargiko.ayaM lokavyavahAraH | Aha -- ko.ayam adhyAso nAmeti | ucyate -- smR^itirUpaH paratra pUrvadR^iShTAvabhAsaH | taM kecid anyatrAnyadharmAdhyAsa iti vadanti | kecit tu yatra yad adhyAsaH tad vivekAgrahanibandhano bhrama iti | anye tu yatra yad adhyAsaH tasyaiva viparItadharmatvakalpanAm AcakShate iti | sarvathApi tu anyasyAnyadharmAvabhAsatAM na vyabhicarati | tathA ca loke.anubhavaH -- shuktikA hi rajatavad avabhAsate, ekashcandraH sadvitIyavad iti | 

kathaM punaH pratyagAtmanyaviShaye.adhyAso viShayataddharmANAM ? sarvo hi puro.avasthite viShaye viShayAntaram adhyasyati, yuShmatpratyayApetasya ca pratyagAtmano.aviShayatvaM bravIShi | ucyate -- na tAvad ayam ekAntenAviShayaH, asmatpratyayaviShayatvAt, aparokShatvAcca pratyagAtmaprasiddheH | na cAyam asti niyamaH puro.avasthita eva viShaye viShayAntaram adhyasitavyam iti | apratyakShe.api hyAkAshe bAlAstalamalinatAdyadhyasyanti | evam aviruddhaH pratyagAtmanyapyanAtmAdhyAsaH | tam etam evaMlakShaNam adhyAsaM paNDitA avidyeti manyante | tadvivekena ca vastusvarUpAvadhAraNaM vidyAm AhuH | 

tatraivaM sati yatra yad adhyAsaH tatkR^itena doSheNa guNena vANumAtreNApi sa na sambadhyate | tam etam avidyAkhyam AtmAnAtmanoH itaretarAdhyAsaM puraskR^itya sarve pramANaprameyavyavahArA laukikA vaidikAshca pravR^ittAH | sarvANi ca shAstrANi vidhipratiShedhamokShaparANi | kathaM punar avidyAvad viShayANi pratyakShAdIni pramANAni shAstrANi ceti ? ucyate -- dehendriyAdiShvahaMmamAbhimAnarahitasya pramAtR^itvanupapattau pramANapravR^ittyanupapatteH | nahi indriyANyanupAdAya pratyakShAdivyavahAraH sambhavati | na cAdhiShThAnam antareNendriyANAM vyavahAraH sambhavati | na cAnadhyastAtmabhAvena dehena kashcid vyApriyate | na caitasmin sarvasminn asati asaN^gasyAtmanaH pramAtR^itvam upapadyate | na ca pramAtR^itvam antareNa pramANapravR^ittir asti | tasmAd avidyAvad viShayANyeva pratyakShAdIni pramANAni shAstrANi ca | pashvAdibhishcAvisheShAt | yathA hi pashvAdayaH shabdAdibhiH shrotrAdInAM sambandhe sati shabdAdivij~nAne pratikUle jAte, tato nivartante, anukUle ca pravartante | yathA daNDodyatakaraM puruSham abhimukham upalabhya mAM hantum ayam icchatIti palAyitum Arabhate, haritatR^iNapUrNpANim upalabhya taM pratyabhimukhI bhavanti, evaM puruShA api vyutpannacittAH krUradR^iShTIn AkroshataH khaDgodyatakarAn balavata upalabhya tato nivartante, tadviparItAn prati pravartante, ataH samAnaH pashvAdibhiH puruShANAM pramANaprameyavyavahAraH | 

pashvAdInAM ca prasiddho.avivekapuraHsaraH pratyakShAdivyavahAraH | tatsAmAnyadarshanAd vyutpattimatAm api puruShANAM pratyakShAdivyavahAraH tatkAlaH samAna iti nishcIyate | shAstrIye tu vyavahAre yadyapi buddhipUrvakArI nAviditvAtmanaH paralokasambandham adhikriyate, tathApi na vedAntavedyam ashanAyAdyatItam apetabrahmakShatrAdibhedam asaMsAryAtmatattvam adhikAre.apekShyate, anupayogAd adhikAravirodhAcca | prAk ca tathAbhUtAtmavij~nAnAt pravartamAnaM shAstram avidyAvad viShayatvaM nAtivartate | 

tathA hi -- brAhmaNo yajeta ityAdIni shAstrANyAtmani varNAshramavayo.avasthAdivisheShAdhyAsam Ashritya pravartante | adhyAso nAma atasmiMH tadbuddhiH ityavocAma | tad yathA putrabhAryAdiShu vikaleShu sakaleShu vA aham eva vikalaH, sakalo veti bAhyadharmAnAtmanyadhyasyati, tathA dehadharmAn sthUlo.ahaM kR^isho.ahaM gauro.ahaM tiShThAmi gacchAmi laN^ghayAmi ceti | tathendriyadharmAn mUkaH kANaH klIbaH andho.aham iti | tathAntaHkaraNadharmAn kAmasaN^kalpavicikitsAdhyavasAyAdIn | evam ahaMpratyayinam asheShasvapracArasAkShiNi pratyagAtmanyadhyasya taM ca pratyaAtmAnaM sarvasAkShiNaM tadviparyayeNAntaHkaraNAdiShvadhyasyati |

evam ayam anAdir ananto naisargiko.adhyAso mithyApratyayarUpaH kartR^itvabhoktR^itvapravartakaH sarvalokapratyakShaH | asyAnarthahetoH prahANAya AtmaikatvavidyApratipattaye sarve vedAntA Arabhyante | yathA cAyam arthaH sarveShAM vedAntAnAM tathA vayam asyAM shArIrakamImAMsAyAM pradarshayiShyAmaH | vedAntamImAMsAshAstrasya vyAcikhyAsitasyedam AdimaM sUtram -- 

athAto brahmajij~nAsA ||

tatra athashabdaH AnantaryArthaH parigR^ihyate | nAdhikArArthaH, brahmajij~nAsAyA anadhikAryatvAt | maN^galasya ca vAkyArthe samanvayAbhAvAt | arthAntaraprayukta eva hyathashabdaH shrutyA maN^galaprayojano bhavati | pUrvaprakR^itApekShAyAshca phalata AnantaryAvyatirekAt | sati ca AnantaryArthatve, yathA dharmajij~nAsA pUrvavR^ittaM vedAdhyayanaM niyamenApekShate, evaM brahmajij~nAsApi yat pUrvavR^ittaM niyamenApekShate tad vaktavyam | svAdhyAyAdhyayanAnantaryaM tu samAnam | 

nanviha karmAvabodhAnantaryaM visheShaH | na | dharmajij~nAsAyAH prAg api adhItavedAntasya brahmajij~nAsopapatteH | yathA ca hR^idayAdyavadAnAnAm AnantaryaniyamaH, kramasya vivakShitatvAt, na tatheha kramo vivakShitaH | sheShasheShitve adhikR^itAdhikAre vA pramANAbhAvAt dharmabrahmajij~nAsayoH | phalajij~nAsyabhedAcca | abhyudayaphalaM dharmaj~nAnam, taccAnuShThAnApekSham | niHshreyasaphalaM tu brahmaj~nAnam, na cAnuShThAnAntarApekSham | bhavyashca dharmo jij~nAsyo na j~nAnakAle.asti, puruShavyApAratantratvAt | iha tu bhUtaM brahma jij~nAsyaM nityavR^ittatvAn na puruShavyApAratantram | codanApravR^ittibhedAcca | yA hi codanA dharmasya lakShaNam, sA svaviShaye niyuJNjAnaiva puruSham avabodhayati | brahmacodanA tu puruSham avabodhayatyeva kevalam | avabodhasya codanAjanyatvAn na puruSho.avabodhe niyujyate -- yathA akShArthasaMnikarSheNArthAvabodhe, tadvat | tasmAt kim api vaktavyam, yadanantaraM brahmajij~nAsopadishyata iti | ucyate -- nityAnityavastuvivekaH, ihAmutrArthabhogavirAgaH, shamadamAdisAdhanasampat, mumukShutvaM ca | teShu hi satsu, prAg api dharmajij~nAsAyA UrdhvaM ca, shakyate brahma jij~nAsituM j~nAtuM ca | na viparyaye | tasmAt athashabdena yathoktasAdhanasampattyAnantaryam upadishyate || 

ataHshabdaH hetvarthaH | yasmAd veda eva agnihotrAdInAM shreyaHsAdhanAnAm anityaphalatAM darshayati -- tad yatheha karmacito lokaH kShIyata evam evAmutra puNyacito lokaH kShIyate [chA.u. 8.1.6] ityAdiH | tathA brahmaj~nAnAd api paraM puruShArthaM darshayati -- brahmavid Apnoti param [tai.u. 2.1] ityAdiH | tasmAt yathoktasAdhanasampattyanantaraM brahmajij~nAsA kartavyA || 

brahmaNo jij~nAsA brahmajij~nAsA | brahma ca vakShyamANalakShaNam janmAdyasya yataH iti | ata eva na brahmashabdasya jAtyAdyarthAntaram AshaN^kitavyam | brahmaNa iti karmaNi ShaShThI, na sheShe | jij~nAsyApekShatvAjjij~nAsAyAH, jij~nAsyAntarAnirdeshAcca | 

nanu sheShaShaShThIparigrahe.api brahmaNo jij~nAsAkarmatvaM na virudhyate, sambandhasAmAnyasya visheShaniShThatvAt | evam api pratyakShaM brahmaNaH karmatvam utsR^ijya sAmAnyadvAreNa parokShaM karmatvaM kalpayato vyarthaH prayAsaH syAt | na vyarthaH, brahmAshritAsheShavicArapratij~nAnArthatvAd iti cet, na | pradhAnaparigrahe tadapekShitAnAm apyarthAkShiptatvAt | brahma hi j~nAnenAptum iShTatamatvAt pradhAnam | tasmin pradhAne jij~nAsAkarmaNi parigR^ihIte, yair jij~nAsitair vinA brahma jij~nAsitaM na bhavati, tAnyarthAkShiptAnyeveti na pR^ithaksUtrayitavyAni | yathA rAjAsau gacchati ityukte saparivArasya rAj~no gamanam uktaM bhavati, tadvat | shrutyanugamAcca | yato vA imAni bhUtAni jAyante [tai.u. 3.1] ityAdyAH shrutayaH | tad vijij~nAsasva tad brahma [tai.u. 3.1] iti pratyakSham eva brahmaNo jij~nAsAkarmatvaM darshayanti | tacca karmaNi ShaShThIparigrahe sUtreNAnugataM bhavati | tasmAd brahmaNa iti karmaNi ShaShThI || 

j~nAtum icchA jij~nAsA | avagatiparyantaM j~nAnaM san vAcyAyA icchAyAH karma, phalaviShayatvAd icchAyAH | j~nAnena hi pramANenAvagantum iShTaM brahma | brahmAvagatir hi puruShArthaH, niHsheShasaMsArabIjAvidyAdyanarthanibarhaNAt | tasmAd brahma 
jij~nAsitavyam || 

tat punar brahma prasiddham aprasiddhaM vA syAt | yadi prasiddhaM na jij~nAsitavyam | athAprasiddhaM naiva shakyaM jij~nAsitum iti | ucyate -- asti tAvad brahma nityashuddhabuddhamuktasvabhAvaM sarvaj~naM sarvashaktisamanvitam | brahmashabdasya hi vyutpAdyamAnasya nityashuddhatvAd ayo.arthAH pratIyante, bR^iMhater dhAtor arthAnugamAt | sarvasyAtmatvAcca brahmAstitvaprasiddhiH | sarvo hyAtmAstitvaM pratyeti, na nAham asmi iti | yadi hi nAtmAstitvaprasiddhiH syAt, sarvo lokaH nAham asmi iti pratIyAt | 

AtmA ca brahma | yadi tarhi loke brahma Atmatvena prasiddham asti, tato j~nAtam evetyajij~nAsyatvaM punar Apannam | na | tadvisheShaM prati vipratipatteH | dehamAtraM caitanyavishiShTAmAtmeti prAkR^itA janA laukAyatikAshca pratipannAH | indriyANyeva cetanAnyAtmetyapare, mana ityanye | vij~nAnamAtraM kShaNikam ityeke | shUnyam ityapare | asti dehAdivyatiriktaH saMsArI kartA bhoktetyapare | bhoktaiva kevalaM na kartetyeke | asti tadvyatirikta IshvaraH sarvaj~naH sarvashaktiH iti kecit | AtmA sa bhoktuH ityapare | evaM bahavo vipratipannA yuktivAkyatadAbhAsasamAshrayAH santaH | tatrAvicArya yat kiMcit pratipadyamAno niHshreyasAt pratihanyeta, anarthaM ceyAt | tasmAd brahmajij~nAsopanyAsamukhena vedAntavAkyamImAMsA tadavirodhitarkopakaraNA niHshreyasaprayojanA prastUyate ||1|| 
2. janmAdyadhikaraNam 

|| 1.1.2 ||

brahma jij~nAsitavyam ityuktam | kiMlakShaNaM punaH tad brahmetyata Aha bhagavAn sUtrakAraH -- 

janmAdyasya yataH ||

janma utpattiH AdiH asya -- iti tadguNasaMvij~nAno bahuvrIhiH | janmasthitibhaN^gaM samAsArthaH | janmanashcAditvaM shrutinirdeshApekShaM vastuvR^ittApekShaM ca | shrutinirdeshaH tAvat -- yato vA imAni bhUtAni jAyante [tai.u. 3.1] iti, asmin vAkye janmasthitipralayAnAM kramadarshanAt | vastuvR^ittam api -- janmanA labdhasattAkasya dharmiNaH sthitipralayasambhavAt | asyeti pratyakShAdisaMnidhApitasya dharmiNa idam AnirdeshaH | ShaShThI janmAdidharmasambandhArthA | yata iti kAraNanirdeshaH | asya jagato nAmarUpAbhyAM vyAkR^itasya anekakartR^ibhoktR^isaMyuktasya pratiniyatadeshakAlanimittakriyAphalAshrayasya manasApyacintyaracanArUpasya janmasthitibhaN^gaM yataH sarvaj~nAt sarvashakteH kAraNAd bhavati, tad brahmeti vAkyasheShaH | anyeShAm api bhAvavikArANAM triShv evAntarbhAva iti janmasthitinAshAnAm iha grahaNam | yAskaparipaThitAnAM tu jAyate.asti ityAdInAM grahaNe teShAM jagataH sthitikAle sambhAvyamAnatvAn mUlakAraNAd utpattisthitinAshA jagato na gR^ihItAH syuH ityAshaN^kyeta | tan mA shaN^ki | iti yA utpattir brahmaNaH kAraNAt, tatraiva sthitiH pralayashca, te gR^ihyante | na ca yathoktavisheShaNasya jagato yathoktavisheShaNam IshvaraM muktvA, anyataH pradhAnAd acetanAt aNubhyo vA abhAvAd vA saMsAriNo vA utpattyAdi sambhAvayituM shakyam | na ca svabhAvataH, vishiShTAdeshakAlanimittAnAm ihopAdAnAt | etad evAnumAnaM saMsArivyatirikteshvarAstitvAdisAdhanaM manyante IshvarakAraNavAdinaH || 

nanvihApi tad evopanyastaM janmAdisUtre | na | vedAntavAkyakusumagrathanArthatvAt sUtrANAm | vedAntavAkyAni hi sUtrair udAhR^itya vicAryante | vAkyArthavicAraNAdhyavasAnanirvR^ittA hi brahmAvagatiH, nAnumAnAdipramANAntaranirvR^ittA | satsu tu vedAntavAkyeShu jagato janmAdikAraNavAdiShu, tadarthagrahaNadArDhyAya anumAnam api vedAntavAkyAvirodhi pramANaM bhavat, na nivAryate, shrutyaiva ca sahAyatvena tarkasyApyabhyupetatvAt | tathA hi -- shrotavyo mantavyaH iti shrutiH paNDito medhAvI gandhArAn evopasampadyetaivam eveha, AcAryavAn puruSho veda [chA.u. 6.14.2] iti ca puruShabuddhisAhAyyam Atmano darshayati | na dharmajij~nasAyAm iva shrutyAdaya eva pramANaM brahmajij~nAsAyAm | kintu shrutyAdayo.anubhavAdayashca yathAsambhavam iha pramANam, anubhavAvasAnatvAd bhUtavastuviShayatvAcca brahmaj~nAnasya | kartavye hi viShaye nAnubhavApekShAstIti shrutyAdInAm eva prAmANyaM syAt, puruShAdhInAtmalAbhatvAcca kartavyasya | kartum akartum anyathA vA kartuM shakyaM laukikaM vaidikaM ca karma | yathA ashvena gacchati, padbhyAm, anyathA vA, na vA gacchatIti | tathA atirAtre ShoDashinaM gR^ihNAti, nAtirAtre ShoDashinaM gR^ihNAti udite juhoti, anudite juhoti iti | 

vidhipratiShedhAshca atra arthavantaH syuH, vikalpotsargApavAdAshca | na tu vastu evam, naivam asti, nAsti iti vA vikalpyate | vikalpanAH tu puruShabuddhyapekShAH | na vastuyAthAtmyaj~nAnaM puruShabuddhyapekSham | kiM tarhi vastutantram eva tat | na hi sthANAv ekasmin sthANur vA, puruSho.anyo vA iti tattvaj~nAnaM bhavati | tatra puruSho.anyo vA iti mithyAj~nAnam | sthANur eva iti tattvaj~nAnam, vastutantratvAt | evaM bhUtavastuviShayANAM prAmANyaM vastutantram | tatraivaM sati brahmaj~nAnam api vastutantram eva, bhUtavastuviShayatvAt | 

nanu, bhUtavastuviShayatve brahmaNaH pramANAntaraviShayatvam eveti vedAntavAkyavicAraNA anarthikaiva prAptA | na | indriyAviShayatvena sambandhAgrahaNAt | svabhAvato viShayaviShayANIndriyANi, na brahmaviShayANi | sati hIndriyaviShayatve brahmaNaH, idaM brahmaNA sambaddhaM kAryam iti gR^ihyeta | kAryamAtram eva tu gR^ihyamANam -- kiM brahmaNA sambaddham? kim anyena kenacid vA sambaddham? -- iti na shakyaM nishcetum | tasmAjjanmAdisUtraM nAnumAnopanyAsArtham, kiM tarhi vedAntavAkyapradarshanArtham | kiM punaH tad vedAntavAkyaM yat sUtreNeha lilakShayiShitam | bhR^igur ve vAruNiH | varuNaM pitaram upasasAra | adhIhi bhagavo brahmeti [tai.u. 3.1] ityupakramyAha -- yato vA imAni bhUtAni jAyante | yena jAtAni jIvanti | yat prayantyabhisaMvishanti | tad vijij~nAsasva | tad brahmeti [tai.u. 3.1] tasya ca nirNayavAkyam -- AnandAd dhyeva khalvimAni bhUtAni jAyante | Anandena jAtAni jIvanti | AnandaM prayantyabhisaMvishanti [tai.u. 3.6] iti | anyAnyapyevaM jAtIyakAni vAkyAni nityashuddhabuddhamuktasvabhAvasarvaj~nasvarUpakAraNaviShayANi udAhartavyAni ||2||

 -- o)0(o -- 
3. shAstrayonitvAdhikaraNam

|| 1.1.3 || 

jagatkAraNatvapradarshanena sarvaj~naM brahmetyupakShiptam, tad eva draDhayann Aha -- 

shAstrayonitvAt || 

mahata R^igvedAdeH shAstrasya anekavidyAsthAnopabR^iMhitasya pradIpavat sarvArthAvadyotinaH sarvaj~nakalpasya yoniH kAraNaM brahma | na hIdR^ishasya shAstrasya R^igvedAdilakShaNasya sarvaj~naguNAnvitasya sarvaj~nAd anyataH sambhavo.asti | yad yad vistarArthaM shAstraM yasmAt puruShavisheShAt sambhavati, yathA vyAkaraNAdi pANinyAdeH j~neyaikadeshArtham api, sa tato.apyadhikataravij~nAna iti prasiddhaM loke | kim u vaktavyam -- anekashAkhAbhedabhinnasya devatiryaN^manuShyavarNAshramAdipravibhAgahetoH R^igvedAdyAkhyasya sarvaj~nAnAkarasya aprayatnenaiva lIlAnyAyena puruShaniHshvAsavat yasmAn mahato bhUtAt yoneH sambhavaH -- asya mahato bhUtasya niHshvasitam etat yad R^igvedaH [bR^i.A.u. 2.4.10] ityAdishruteH | tasya mahato bhUtasya niratishayaM sarvaj~natvaM sarvashaktimattvaM ceti || 

athavA yathoktam R^igvedAdishAstraM yoniH kAraNaM pramANam asya brahmaNo yathAvat svarUpAdhigame | shAstrAd eva pramANAt jagato janmAdikAraNaM brahmAdhigamyata ityabhiprAyaH | shAstram udAhR^itaM pUrvasUtre -- yato vA imAni bhUtAni jAyante [tai.u. 3.1] ityAdi | 

kimarthaM tarhIdaM sUtram, yAvatA pUrvasUtreNaiva evaMjAtIyakaM shAstram udAharatA shAstrayonitvaM brahmaNo darshitam ? ucyate -- tatra sUtrAkShareNa spaShTaM shAstrasyAnupAdAnAjjanmAdisUtreNa kevalam anumAnam upanyastam ityAshaN^kyeta | tAm AshaN^kAM nivartayitum idaM sUtraM pravavR^ite -- shAstrayonitvAt iti ||3|| 
 
 -- o)0(o -- 
4. samanvayAdhikaraNam

|| 1.1.4 ||

kathaM punar brahmaNaH shAstrapramANakatvam ucyate, yAvatA AmnAyasya kriyArthatvAd Anarthakyam atadarthAnAm [jai.sU. 1.2.1] iti kriyAparatvaM shAstrasya pradarshitam | ato vedAntAnAm Anarthakyam, akriyArthatvAt, kartR^idevatAdiprakAshanArthatvena vA kriyAvidhisheShatvam, upAsanAdikriyAntaravidhAnArthatvaM vA | na hi pariniShThitavastusvarUpapratipAdanaM sambhavati | pratyakShAdiviShayatvAt pariniShThitavastunaH, tatpratipAdane ca heyopAdeyarahite puruShArthAbhAvAt | ata eva so.arodIt ityevam AdInAm AnarthakyaM mA bhUd iti, vidhinA tv ekavAkyatvAt stutyarthena vidhInAM syuH [jai.sU. 1.2.7] iti stAvakatvenArthavattvam uktam | mantrANAM ca iShe tvA ityAdInAM kriyAtatsAdhanAbhidhAyakatvena karmasamavAyitvam uktam | ato na kvacid api vedavAkyAnAM vidhisaMsparsham antareNArthavattA dR^iShTA upapannA vA | na ca pariniShThite vastusvarUpe vidhiH sambhavati, kriyAviShayatvAd vidheH tasmAt karmApekShitakartR^idevatAdisvarUpaprakAshanena kriyAvidhisheShatvaM vedAntAnAm |

atha prakaraNAntarabhayAn naitad abhyupagamyate, tathApi svavAkyagatopAsanAdikarmaparatvam | tasmAn na brahmaNaH shAstrayonitvam iti prApte, ucyate -- 

tat tu samanvayAt ||

tushabdaH pUrvapakShavyAvR^ittyarthaH | tad brahma sarvaj~naM sarvashakti jagadutpattisthitilayakAraNaM vedAntashAstrAd avagamyate | katham? samanvayAt | sarveShu hi vedAnteShu vAkyAni tAt paryeNaitasyArthasya pratipAdakatvena samanugatAni | sad eva somyedam agra AsIt ekam evAdvitIyam [chAndo. 6.2.1], AtmA vA idam eka evAgra AsIt [ai.A. 2.1.1.1], tad etad brahmApUrvam anaparam anantaram abAhyam [?], ayam AtmA brahma sarvAnubhUH [bR^i.A.u 2.5.19], brahmaivedam amR^itaM purastAt [mu.u. 2.2.11] ityAdIni | na ca tadgatAnAM padAnAM brahmasvarUpaviShaye nishcite samanvaye.avagamyamAne arthAntarakalpanA yuktA, shrutahAnyashrutakalpanAprasaN^gAt | na ca teShAM kartR^idevatAdisvarUpapratipAdanaparatA avasIyate, tat kena kaM pashyet [bR^i.A.u 2.4.13] ityAdikriyAkArakaphalanirAkaraNashruteH | na ca pariniShThitavastusvarUpatve.api pratyakShAdiviShayatvaM brahmaNaH, tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7] iti brahmAtmabhAvasya shAstram antareNAnavagamyamAnatvAt | yat tu heyopAdeyarahitatvAd upadeshAnarthakyam iti, naiSha doShaH | heyopAdeyashUnyabrahmAtmatAvagamAd eva sarvakleshaprahANAt puruShArthasiddhiH | devatAdipratipAdanaparasya tu svavAkyagatopAsanArthatve.api na kashcid virodhaH | na tu tathA brahmaNa upAsanAvidhisheShatvaM sambhavati, ekatve heyopAdeyashUnyatayA kriyAkArakAdidvaitavij~nAnopamardopapatteH | na hi brahmaikatvavij~nAnenonmathitasya dvaitavij~nAnasya punaH sambhavo.asti yenopAsanAvidhisheShatvaM brahmaNaH pratipAdyeta | yadyapyanyatra vedavAkyAnAM vidhisaMsparsham antareNa pramANatvaM na dR^iShTam, tathApyAtmavij~nAnasya phalaparyantatvAn na tadviShayasya shAstrasya prAmANyaM shakyaM pratyAkhyAtum | na cAnumAnagamyaM shAstraprAmANyam, yenAnyatra dR^iShTAM nidarshanam apekShyeta | tasmAt siddhaM brahmaNaH shAstrapramANakatvam || 

atrApare pratyavatiShThante -- yadyapi shAstrapramANakaM brahma, tathApi pratipattividhiviShayatayaiva shAstreNa brahma samarpyate | yathA yUpAhavanIyAdInyalaukikAnyapi vidhisheShatayA shAstreNa samarpyante, tadvat | kuta etat? pravR^ittinivR^ittiprayojanaparatvAcchAstrasya | tathA hi shAstratAt paryavidAm anukramaNam -- dR^iShTo hi tasyArthaH karmAvabodhanaM nAma iti | codaneti kriyAyAH pravartakaM vacanam tasya j~nAnam upadeshaH [jai.sU. 1.1.5], tadbhUtAnAM kriyArthena samAmnAyaH [jai.sU. 1.1.25], AmnAyasya kriyArthatvAd Anarthakyam atadarthAnAm [jai.sU. 1.2.1] iti ca | ataH puruShaM kvacid viShayavisheShe pravartayat kutashcid viShayavisheShAn nivartayaccArthavacchAstram | taccheShatayA cAnyad upayuktam | tatsAmAnyAd vedAntAnAm api tathaivArthavattvaM syAt | sati ca vidhiparatve, yathA svargAdikAmasyAgnihotrAdisAdhanaM vidhIyate, evam amR^itatvakAmasya brahmaj~nAnaM vidhIyata iti yuktam | 

nanviha jij~nAsyavailakShaNyam uktam -- karmakANDe bhavyo dharmo jij~nAsyaH, iha tu bhUtaM nityanirvR^ittaM brahma jij~nAsyam iti | tatra dharmaj~nAnaphalAd anuShThAnasApekShAd vilakShaNaM brahmaj~nAnaphalaM bhavitum arhati | nArhatyevaM bhavitum, kAryavidhiprayuktasyaiva brahmaNaH pratipAdyamAnatvAt | AtmA vA are draShTavyaH [bR^i.A.u 2.4.5], ya AtmApahatapApmA [chA.u. 8.7.1]...so.anveShTavyaH sa vijij~nAsitavyaH, AtmetyevopAsIta AtmAnam eva lokam upAsIta [bR^i.A.u. 1.4.15], brahma veda brahmaiva bhavati [mu.u. 3.2.9] ityAdiShu vidhAneShu satsu, ko.asAvatmA? kiM tad brahma? ityAkAN^kShAyAM tat svarUpasamarpaNena sarve vedAntA upayuktAH -- nityaH sarvaj~naH sarvagato nityatR^ipto nityashuddhabuddhamuktasvabhAvo vij~nAnam AnandaM brahma [bR^i.A.u. 3.9.7] ityevamAdayaH | tadupAsanAcca shAstradR^iShTo.adR^iShTo mokShaH phalaM bhaviShyati | kartavyavidhyananupraveshe tu vastumAtrakathane hAnopAdAnAsambhavAt saptadvIpA vasumatI rAjAsau gacchati ityAdivAkyAd vedAntavAkyAnAm Anarthakyam eva syAt | 

nanu vastumAtrakathane.api rajjuH iyam, nAyaM sarpaH ityAdau bhrAntijanitabhItinivartanenArthavattvaM dR^iShTam | tathehApyasaMsAryAtmavastukathanena saMsAritvabhrAntinivartanenArthavattvaM syAt | syAd etad evam, yadi rajjusvarUpashravaNamAtreNeva sarpabhrAntiH, saMsAritvabhrAntir brahmasvarUpashravaNamAtreNa nivarteta | na tu nivartate | shrutabrahmaNo.api yathApUrvaM sukhaduHkhAdisaMsAridharmadarshanAt, shrotavyo mantavyo nididhyAsitavyaH iti ca shravaNottarakAlayor manananididhyAsanayor vidhidarshanAt | tasmAt pratipattividhiviShayatayaiva shAstrapramANakaM brahmAbhyupagantavyam iti || 

atrAbhidhIyate -- na | karmabrahmavidyAphalayor vaailakShaNyAt | shArIraM vAcikaM mAnasaM ca karma shrutismR^itisiddhaM dharmAkhyam, yad viShayA jij~nAsA athAto dharmajij~nAsA iti sUtritA | adharmo.api hiMsAdiH pratiShedhacodanAlakShaNatvAjjij~nAsyaH parihArAya | tayoshcodanAlakShaNayor arthAnarthayor dharmAdharmayoH phale pratyakShe sukhaduHkhe sharIravAN^manobhir evopabhujyamAne viShayendriyasaMyogajanye brahmAdiShu sthAvarAnteShu prasirA | manuShyatvAd Arabhya brahmAnteShu dehavatsu sukhatAratamyam anushrUyate | tatashca tarAtor dharmasyApi tAratamyaM gamyate | dharmatAratamyAd adhikAritAratamyam | prasiddhaM cArthitvasAmarthyavidvattAdikR^itam adhikAritAratamyam | 

tathA ca yAgAdyanuShThAyinAm eva vidyAsamAdhivisheShAd uttareNa pathA gamanam, kevalaiH iShTApUrtadattasAdhanair dhUmAdikrameNa dakShiNena pathA gamanam, tatrApi sukhatAratamyam, tatsAdhanatAratamyaM ca shAstrAt yAvat sampAtam uShitvA ityasmAd gamyate | tathA manuShyAdiShu sthAvarAnteShu sukhalavashcodanAlakShaNadharmasAdhya eveti gamyate tAratamyena vartamAnaH | tathordhvagateShvadhogateShu ca dehavatsu duHkhatAratamyadarshanAt tarAtor adharmasya pratiShedhacodanAlakShaNasya tadanuShThAyinAM ca tAratamyaM gamyate | evam avidyAdidoShavatAM dharmAdharmatAratamyanimittaM sharIropAdAnapUrvakaM sukhaduHkhatAratamyam anityaM saMsArarUpaM shrutismR^itinyAyaprasiddham | 
tathA ca shrutiH na ha vai sasharIrasya sataH priyApriyayor apahatir asti [chA.u. 8.12.1] iti yathAvarNitaM saMsArarUpam anuvadati | asharIraM vAva santaM na priyApriye spR^ishataH iti priyApriyasparshanapratiShedhAccodanAlakShaNadharmakAryatvaM mokShAkhyasyAsharIratvasya pratiShidhyata iti gamyate | dharmakAryatve hi priyApriyasparshanapratiShedho nopapadyeta | asharIratvam eva dharmakAryam iti cet, na | tasya svAbhAvikatvAt --

brahmadarshanasarvAtmabhAvayor madhye kartavyAntaravAraNAyodAhAryam -- yathA tiShThan gAyati iti tiShThatigAyatyor madhye tatkartR^ikaM kAryAntaraM nAstIti gamyate | tvaM hi naH pitA yo.asmAkam avidyAyAH paraM pAraM tArayasi [pra.u. 6.8], shrutaM hyeva me bhagavaddR^ishebhyaH tarati shokam Atmavid iti | so.ahaM bhagavaH shocAmi, taM mA bhagavAJNchokasya pAraM tArayatu [chA.u. 7.1.3], tasmai mR^iditakaShAyAya tamasaH pAraM darshayati bhagavAn sanAtkumAraH [chA.u. 7.26.2], iti caivamAdyAH shrutayo mokShapratibandhanivR^ittimAtram evAtmaj~nAnasya phalaM darshayanti | tathA ca AcAryapraNItaM nyAyopabR^iMhitaM sUtram -- duHkhajanmapravR^ittidoShamithyAj~nAnAnAm uttarottarApAye tadanantarApAyAd apavargaH [nyA.sU. 1.1.2] iti | mithyAj~nAnApAyashca brahmAtmaikatvavij~nAnAd bhavati |

nApyAjyAvekShaNAdikarmavat karmAN^gasaMskArarUpam | sampadAdirUpe hi brahmAtmaikatvavij~nAne.abhyupagamyamAne, tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7], ahaM brahmAsmi [bR^i.A.u. 1.4.10], ayam AtmA brahma [bR^i.A.u. 2.5.19] ityevamAdInAM vAkyAnAM brahmAtmaikatvavastupratipAdanaparaH padasamanvayaH pIDyeta | bhidyate hR^idayagranthishchidyante sarvasaMshayAH [mu.u. 2.2.8] iti caivamAdInyavidyAnivR^ittiphalashravaNAnyuparudhyeran | brahma veda brahmaiva bhavati [mu.u. 3.2.9] iti caivamAdIni tadbhAvApattivacanAni sampadAdirUpatve na sAmaJNjasyenopapadyeran | tasmAn na sampadAdirUpaM brahmAtmaikatvavij~nAnam | ato na puruShavyApAratantrA brahmavidyA | kiM tarhi, pratyakShAdipramANaviShayavastuj~nAnavad vastutantraiva | evambhUtasya brahmaNaH tajj~nAnasya ca na kayAcid yuktyA shakyaH kAryAnupraveshaH kalpayitum | na ca vidikriyAkarmatvena kAryAnupravesho brahmaNaH -- anyad eva tadviditAd atho aviditAd adhi [ke.u. 1.3] iti vidikriyAkarmatvapratiShedhAt, yenedaM sarvaM vijAnAti taM kena vijAnIyAt iti ca | tathopAstikriyAkarmatvapratiShedho.api bhavati -- yadvAcAnabhyuditaM yena vAg abhyudyate ityaviShayatvaM brahmaNa upanyasya, tad eva brahma tvaM viddhi, nedaM yad idam upAsate iti | aviShayatve brahmaNaH shAstrayonitvAnupapattiH iti cet, na | avidyAkalpitabhedanivR^ittiparatvAcchAstrasya | na hi shAstram idantayA viShayabhUtaM brahma pratipipAdayiShati | kiM tarhi, pratyagAtmatvenAviShayatayA pratipAdayat avidyAkalpitaM vedyaveditR^ivedanAdibhedam apanayati | 

tathA ca shAstram -- 
yasyAmataM tasya mataM, mataM yasya na veda saH | avij~nAtaM vijAnatAM vij~nAtam avijAnatAm [ke.u. 2.3], na dR^iShTer draShTAraM pashyer na shruteH, shrotAraM shrR^iNuyA na mater mantAraM manvIthA, na vij~nAter vij~nAtAraM vijAnIyAH [bR^i.A.u. 3.4.2] iti caivamAdi | 

ato.avidyAkalpitasaMsAritvanivartanena nityamuktAtmasvarUpasamarpaNAn na mokShasyAnityatvadoShaH | yasya tUtpAdyo mokShaH, tasya mAnasaM vAcikaM kAyikaM vA kAryam apekShata iti yuktam | tathA vikAryatve ca | tayoH pakShayor mokShasya dhruvam anityatvam | na hi dadhyAdi vikAryam utpAdyaM vA ghaTAdi nityaM dR^iShTaM loke | na ca ApyatvenApi kAryApekShA, svAtmasvarUpatve satyanApyatvAt | svarUpavyatiriktatve.api brahmaNo nApyatvam, sarvagatatvena nityAptasvarUpatvAt sarveNa brahmaNa AkAshasyeva | nApi saMskAryo mokShaH, yena vyApAram apekSheta | saMskAro hi nAma saMskAryasya guNAdhAnena vA syAt, doShApanayanena vA | na tAvad guNAdhAnena sambhavati, anAdheyAtishayabrahmasvarUpatvAn mokShasya | 

nApi doShApanayanena, nityashuddhabrahmasvarUpatvAn mokShasya | svAtmadharma eva san tirobhUto mokShaH kriyayAtmani saMskriyamANe.abhivyajyate -- yathA Adarsho nigharvANakriyayA saMskriyamANe bhAsvaratvaM dharma iti cet, na | kriyAshrayatvAnupapatter AtmanaH | yadAshrayA kriyA, tam avikurvatI naivAtmAnaM labhate | yadyAtmA svAshrayakriyayA vikriyeta, anityatvam AtmanaH prasajyeta | avikAryo.aya mucyate iti caivamAdIni vAkyAni bAdhyeran | taccAniShTam | tasmAn na svAshrayA kriyA AtmanaH sambhavati | anyAshrayAyAH tu kriyAyA aviShayatvAn na tayAtmA saMskriyate | 

nanu dehAshrayayA snAnAcamanayaj~nopavItadhAraNAdikayA kriyayA dehI saMskriyamANo dR^iShTaH, na | dehAdisaMhatasyaivAvidyAgR^ihItasyAtmanaH saMskriyamANatvAt | pratyakShaM hi snAnAcamanAder dehasamavAyitvam | tayA dehAshrayayA tatsaMhata eva kashcid avidyayAtmatvena parigR^ihItaH saMskriyata iti yuktam | yathA dehAshrayacikitsAnimittena dhAtusAmyena tatsaMhatasya tadabhimAnina Arogyaphalam, aham arogaH iti yatra buddhir utpadyate -- evaM snAnAcamanayaj~nopavItadhAraNAdikayA ahaM shuddhaH saMskR^itaH iti yatra buddhir utpadyate, sa saMskriyate | sa ca dehena saMhata eva | tenaiva ahaMkartrA ahampratyayaviShayeNa pratyayinA sarvAH kriyA nirvartyante | tatphalaM ca sa evAshnAti, tayor anyaH pippalaM svAdvatti anashnann anyo.abhicAkashIti [mu.u. 3.1.1] iti mantravarNAt -- AtmendriyamanoyuktaM bhoktetyAhur manIShiNaH iti ca | tathA,

kimarthAni tarhi AtmA vA are draShTavyaH shrotavyaH [bR^i.A.u 2.4.5] ityAdIni vidhicchAyAni vacanAni? -- svAbhAvikapravR^ittiviShayavimukhIkaraNArthAnIti brUmaH | yo hi bahirmukhaH pravartate puruShaH iShTaM me bhUyAd aniShTaM mA bhUt iti, na ca tatrAtyantikaM puruShArthaM labhate, tam AtyantikapuruShArthavAJNchinaM svAbhAvikAt kAryakaraNasaMghAtapravR^ittigocarAd vimukhIkR^itya pratyagAtmasrotastayA pravartayanti AtmA vA are draShTavyaH [bR^i.A.u 2.4.5] ityAdIni | tasyAtmAnveShaNAya pravR^ittasyAheyam anupAdeyaM cAtmatattvam upadishyate -- idaM sarvaM yad ayam AtmA [bR^i.A.u. 2.4.6] yatra tu asya sarvam AtmaivAbhUt tat kena kaM pashyet... etad buddhvA buddhimAn syAt kR^itakR^ityashca bhArata [gItA 15.20] iti ca smR^itiH | tasmAn na pratipattividhisheShatayA brahmaNaH samarpaNam || 

yad api kecid AhuH -- pravR^ittinivR^ittividhitaccheShavyatirekeNa kevalavastuvAdI vedabhAgo nAstIti, tan na | aupaniShadasya puruShasyAnanyasheShatvAt yo.asAv upaniShatsv evAdhigataH puruSho.asaMsArI brahmasvarUpaH utpAdyAdicaturvidhadravyavilakShaNaH svaprakaraNastho.ananyasheShaH, nAsau nAstIti nAdhigamyata iti vA shakyaM vaditum | sa eSha neti netyAtmA ityAtmashabdAt Atmanashca pratyAkhyAtum ashakyatvAt, ya eva nirAkartA tasyaivAtmatvAt | 

nanvatmA ahampratyayaviShayatvAd upaniShatsv eva vij~nAyata ityanupapannam | na, tatsAkShitvena pratyuktatvAt | na hyahampratyayaviShayakartR^ivyatirekeNa tatsAkShI sarvabhUtasthaH sama ekaH kUTasthanityaH puruSho vidhikANDe tarkasamaye vA kenacid adhigataH sarvasyAtmA | ataH sa na kenacit pratyAkhyAtuM shakyaH, vidhisheShatvaM vA netum -- AtmatvAd eva ca sarveShAm -- na heyo nApyupAdeyaH | sarvaM hi vinashyadvikArajAtaM puruShAntaM vinashyati | puruSho hi vinAshahetvabhAvAd avinAshI | vikriyAhetvabhAvAcca kUTasthanityaH | ata eva nityashuddhabuddhamuktasvabhAvaH | tasmAt puruShAn na paraM kiMcit sA kAShThA sA parA gatiH [ka.u. 1.3.11], taM tu aupaniShadaM puruShaM pR^icchAmi [bR^i.A.u. 3.9.23] iti caupaniShadatvavisheShaNaM puruShasyopaniShatsu prAdhAnyena prakAshyamAnatve upapadyate | ato bhUtavastuparo vedabhAgo nAstIti vacanaM sAhasamAtram || 

yad api shAstratAtparyavidAm anukramaNam -- dR^iShTo hi tasyArthaH karmAvabodhanam ityevamAdi, tat dharmajij~nAsAviShayatvAd vidhipratiShedhashAstrAbhiprAyaM draShTavyam | api ca AmnAyasya kriyArthatvAd Anarthakyam atadarthAnAm ityetad ekAntenAbhyupagacchatAM bhUtopadeshAnAm AnarthakyaprasaN^gaH | pravR^ittinivR^ittivyatirekeNa bhUtaM ced vastUpadishati bhavyArthatvena, kUTasthanityaM bhUtaM nopadishatIti ko hetuH ? na hi bhUtam upadishyamAnaM kriyA bhavati | akriyAtve.api bhUtasya kriyAsAdhanatvAt kriyArtha eva bhUtopadesha iti cet, naiSha doShaH | kriyArthatve.api kriyAnirvartanashaktimadvastUpadiShTam eva | kriyArthatvaM tu prayojanaM tasya | na caitAvatA vastu anupadiShTaM bhavati | yadi nAmopadiShTaM kiM tava tena syAd iti, ucyate -- anavagatAtmavastUpadeshashca tathaiva bhavitum arhati | tadavagatyA mithyAj~nAnasya saMsArahetor nivR^ittiH prayojanaM kriyata ityavishiShTam arthavattvaM kriyAsAdhanavastUpadeshena | 

api ca brAhmaNo na hantavyaH iti caivam AdyA nivR^ittir upadishyate | na ca sA kriyA | nApi kriyAsAdhanam | akriyArthAnAm upadesho.anarthakashcet, brAhmaNo na hantavyaH ityAdi nivR^ittyupadeshAnAm AnarthakyaM prAptam | taccAniShTam | na ca svabhAvaprAptahantyarthAnurAgeNa naJNaH shakyam aprAptakriyArthatvaM kalpayitum, hananakriyAnivR^ittyaudAsInyavyatirekeNa | naJNashcaiSha svabhAvaH, yat svasambandhino.abhAvaM bodhayatIti | abhAvabuddhishcaudAsInye kAraNam | sA ca dagdhendhanAgnivat svayam evopashAmyati | tasmAt prasaktakriyAnivR^ittyaudAsInyam eva brAhmaNo na hantavyaH ityAdiShu pratiShedhArthaM manyAmahe, anyatra prajApativratAdibhyaH | tasmAt puruShArthAnupayogyupAkhyAnAdibhUtArthavAdaviShayam AnarthakyAbhidhAnaM draShTavyam || 

yad apyuktam -- kartavyavidhyanupravesham antareNa vastumAtram ucyamAnam anarthakaM syAt saptadvIpA vasumatI ityAdivad iti, tat parihR^itam | rajjuH iyam, nAyaM sarpaH iti vastumAtrakathane.api prayojanasya dR^iShTatvAt | 

nanu shrutabrahmaNo.api yathApUrvaM saMsAritvadarshanAn na rajjusvarUpakathanavad arthavattvam ityuktam | atrocyate -- nAvagatabrahmAtmabhAvasya yathApUrvaM saMsAritvaM shakyaM darshayitum, vedapramANajanitabrahmAtmabhAvavirodhAt | na hi sharIrAdyAtmAbhimAnino duHkhabhayAdimattvaM dR^iShTam iti, tasyaiva vedapramANajanitabrahmAtmAvagame tadabhimAnanivR^ittau tad eva mithyAj~nAnanimittaM duHkhabhayAdimattvaM bhavatIti shakyaM kalpayitum | 

na hi dhanino gR^ihasthasya dhanAbhimAnino dhanApahAranimittaM duHkhaM dR^iShTam iti, tasyaiva pravrajitasya dhanAbhimAnarahitasya tad eva dhanApahAranimittaM duHkhaM bhavati | 

na ca kuNDalinaH kuNDalitvAbhimAnanimittaM sukhaM dR^iShTam iti tasyaiva kuNDalaviyuktasya kuNDalitvAbhimAnarahitasya tad eva kuNDalitvAbhimAnanimittaM sukhaM bhavati | tad uktaM shrutyA -- asharIraM vAva santaM na priyApriye spR^ishataH iti | sharIre patite.asharIratvaM syAt, na jIvata iti cet, na, sasharIraM tu asya mithyAj~nAnanimittatvAt | 

na hyAtmanaH sharIrAtmAbhimAnalakShaNaM mithyAj~nAnaM muktvA anyataH sasharIratvaM shakyaM kalpayitum | nityam asharIratvam akarmanimittatvAd ityavocAma | tatkR^itadharmAdharmanimittaM sasharIratvam iti cet, na | sharIrasambandhasyAsiddhatvAt dharmAdharmayor AtmakR^itatvAsiddhiH, sharIrasambandhasya dharmAdharmayoH tatkR^itatvasya cetaretarAshrayatvaprasaN^gAt | andhaparamparaiShA anAditvakalpanA, kriyAsamavAyAbhAvAccAtmanaH kartR^itvAnupapatteH | saMnidhAnamAtreNa rAjaprabhR^itInAM dR^iShTaM kartR^itvam iti cet, na | dhanadAnAdyupArjitabhR^ityasambandhitvAt teShAM kartR^itvopapatteH | na tvatmano dhanadAnAdivaccharIrAdibhiH svasvAmibhAvasambandhanimittaM kiMcicchakyaM kalpayitum | mithyAbhimAnaH tu pratyakShaH sambandhahetuH | etena yajamAnatvam Atmano vyAkhyAtam | 

atrAhuH -- dehAdivyatiriktasyAtmanaH AtmIye dehAdAvahamabhimAno gauNaH, na mithyeti cet, na | prasiddhavastubhedasya gauNatvamukhyatvaprasiddhiH | yasya hi prasiddho vastubhedaH -- yathA kesarAdimAnAkR^itivisheSho.anvayavyatirekAbhyAM siMhashabdapratyayabhAN^ mukhyo.anyaH siddhaH, tatashcAnyaH puruShaH prAyikaiH krauryashauryAdibhiH siMhaguNaiH sampannaH siddhaH, tasya tasmin puruShe siMhashabdapratyayau gauNau bhavataH | nAprasiddhavastubhedasya | tasya tu anyatrAnyashabdapratyayau bhrAntinimittAv eva bhavataH, na gauNau | yathA mandAndhakAre sthANur ayam ityagR^ihyamANavisheShe puruShashabdapratyayau sthANuviShayau, yathA vA shuktikAyAm akasmAd rajatam idam iti nishcitau shabdapratyayau, tadvad dehAdisaMghAte, aham iti nirupacAreNa shabdapratyayAvatmAnAtmAvivekenotpadyamAnau kathaM gauNau shakyau vaditum | AtmAnAtmavivekinAm api paNDitAnAm ajAvipAlAnAm ivAviviktau shabdapratyayau bhavataH | tasmAd dehAdivyatiriktAtmAstitvavAdinAM dehAdAvahampratyayo mithyaiva, na gauNaH | tasmAn mithyApratyayanimittatvAt sasharIratvasya, siddhaM jIvato.api viduSho.asharIratvam | tathA ca brahmavidviShayA shrutiH -- tad yathAhinilrvayanI valmIke mR^itA pratyastA shayItaivam evedaM sharIraM shete athAyam asharIro.amR^itaH prANo brahmaiva teja eva iti | sacakShur acakShuH iva sakarNo.akarNa iva savAg avAgika samanA amanA iva saprANo.aprANa iva iti ca | smR^itir api -- sthitapraj~nasya kA bhAShA [gItA 2.54] ityAdyA sthitapraj~nasya lakShaNAnyAcakShANA viduShaH sarvapravR^ittyasambandhaM darshayati | tasmAn nAvagatabrahmAtmabhAvasya yathApUrvaM saMsAritvam | yasya tu yathApUrvaM saMsAritvaM nAsAvavagatabrahmAtmabhAva ityanavadyam || 

yat punar uktaM shravaNAt parAcInayor manananididhyAsanayor darshanAd vidhisheShatvaM brahmaNaH, na svarUpaparyavasAyitvam iti, tan na | shravaNavad avagatyarthatvAn manananididhyAsanayoH | yadi hyavagataM brahmAnyatra viniyujyeta, bhavet tadA vidhisheShatvam | na tu tad asti, manananididhyAsanayor api shravaNavadavagatyarthatvAt | tasmAn na pratipattividhiviShayatayA shAstrapramANakatvaM brahmaNaH sambhavatItyataH svatantram eva brahma shAstrapramANakaM vedAntavAkyasamanvayAd iti siddham | evaM ca sati athAto brahmajij~nAsA iti tadviShayaH pR^ithak shAstrArambha upapadyate | pratipattividhiparatve hi athAto dharmajij~nAsA ityevArabdhatvAn na pR^ithak shAstram Arabhyeta | ArabhyamANaM caivam Arabhyeta -- athAtaH parishiShTadharmajij~nAseti, athAtaH kratvarthapuruShArthayor jij~nAsA itivat | brahmAtmaikyAvagatistvapratij~nAteti tadartho yuktaH shAstrArambhaH -- athAto brahmajij~nAsA iti | tasmAt ahaM brahmAsmItyetadavasAnA eva sarve vidhayaH sarvANi cetarANi pramANAni | na hyaheyAnupAdeyAdvaitAtmAvagatau satyAm, nirviShayANyapramAtR^ikANi ca pramANAni bhavitum arhantIti | api cAhuH -- 

gauNamithyAtmano.asattve putradehAdibAdhanAt | 
sad brahmAtmAham ityevaM bodhe kAryaM kathaM bhavet || 
anveShTavyAtmavij~nAnAt prAkpramAtR^itvam AtmanaH | 
anviShTaH syAt pramAtaiva pApmadoShAdivarjitaH || 
dehAtmapratyayo yadvat pramANatvena kalpitaH | 
laukikaM tadvad evedaM pramANaM tvAtmanishcayAt || iti ||

evaM tAvad vedAntavAkyAnAM brahmAtmAvagatiprayojanAnA brahmAtmani tAtparyeNa samanvitAnAm antareNApi kAryAnupraveshaM brahmaNi paryavasAnam uktam | brahma ca sarvaj~naM sarvashakti jagadutpattisthitilayakAraNam ityuktam | sAN^khyAdayaH tu 
pariniShThitaM vastu pramANAntaragamyam eveti manyamAnAH pradhAnAdIni kAraNAntarANyanumimAnAH tatparatayaiva vedAntavAkyAni yojayanti | sarveShv eva vedAntavAkyeShu sR^iShTiviShayeShvanumAnenaiva kAryeNa kAraNaM lilakShayiShitam | pradhAnapuruShasaMyogA nityAnumeyA iti sAN^khyA manyante | kANAdAH tv etebhya eva vAkyebhya IshvaraM nimittakAraNam anumimate, aNUMshca samavAyikAraNam | evam anye.api tArkikA vAkyAbhAsayuktyAbhAsAvaShTAmbhAH pUrvapakShavAdina ihottiShThante | tatra padavAkyapramANaj~nenAcAryeNa vedAntavAkyAnAM brahmAtmAvagatiparatvapradarshanAya vAkyAbhAsayuktyAbhAsapratipattayaH pUrvapakShIkR^itya nirAkriyante || 

|| 1.1.5 ||

tatra sAN^khyAH pradhAnaM triguNam acetanaM svatantraM jagatkAraNam iti manyamAnA AhuH -- yAni vedAntavAkyAni sarvaj~nasya sarvashakter brahmaNo jagatkAraNatvaM pradarshayantItyavocaH, tAni pradhAnakAraNapakShe.api yojayituM shakyante | sarvashaktitvaM tAvat pradhAnasyApi svavikAraviShayam upapadyate | evaM sarvaj~natvam apyupapadyate | katham? yat tvaM j~nAnaM manyase, sa sattvadharmaH, sattvAt saMjAyate j~nAnam iti smR^iteH | tena ca sattvadharmeNa j~nAnena kAryakaraNavantaH puruShAH sarvaj~nA yoginaH prasiddhAH | sattvasya hi niratishayotkarShe sarvaj~natvaM prasiddham | na kevalasya akAryakaraNasya puruShasyopalabdhimAtrasya sarvaj~natvaM kiMcijj~natvaM vA kalpayituM shakyam | triguNatvAt tu pradhAnasya sarvaj~nAnakAraNabhUtaM sattvaM pradhAnAvasthAyAm api vidyata iti pradhAnasyAcetanasyaiva sataH sarvaj~natvam upacaryate vedAntavAkyeShu | avashyaM ca tu ayApi sarvaj~naM brahmetyabhyupagacchatA sarvaj~nAnashaktimattvenaiva sarvaj~natvam abhyupagantavyam | na hi sarvadA sarvaviShayaM j~nAnaM kurvad eva brahma vartate | tathA hi -- j~nAnasya nityatve j~nAnakriyAM prati svAtantryaM brahmaNo hIyeta | athAnityaM tad iti j~nAnakriyAyA uparame uparametApi brahma, tadA sarvaj~nAnashaktimattvenaiva sarvaj~natvam Apatati | api ca prAgutpatteH sarvakArakashUnyaM brahmeShyate tu ayA | na ca j~nAnasAdhanAnAM sharIrendriyAdInAm abhAve j~nAnotpattiH kasyacid upapannA | 

api ca pradhAnasyAnekAtmakasya pariNAmasambhavAt kAraNatvopapattir mR^idAdivat, nAsaMhatasyaikAtmakasya brahmaNaH | ityevaM prApte, idaM sUtram Arabhyate -- 

IkShater nAshabdam ||

na sAN^khyaparikalpitam acetanaM pradhAnaM jagataH kAraNaM shakyaM vedAnteShvashrayitum | ashabdaM hi tat | katham ashabdatvam? IkShateH IkShitR^itvashravaNAt kAraNasya | katham? evaM hi shrUyate -- sad eva somyedam agra AsId ekam evAdvitIyam [chA.u. 6.2.1] ityupakramya tad aikShata bahu syAM prajAyeyeti tat tejo.asR^ijata iti | tatra idaMshabdavAcyaM nAmarUpavyAkR^itaM jagat prAgutpatteH sadAtmanAvadhArya, tasyaiva prakR^itasya sacchabdavAcyasyekShaNapUrvakaM tejaHprabhR^iteH sraShTR^itvaM darshayati | tathAnyatra -- AtmA vA idam eka evAgra AsIt | nAnyat kiMcana miShat | sa aikShata lokAn nu sR^ijA iti | sa imAMl lokAn asR^ijata itIkShApUrvikAm eva sR^iShTim AcaShTe | kvacicca ShoDashakalaM puruShaM prastutyAha -- sa IkShAM cakre, sa prANam asR^ijata iti | IkShateH iti ca dhAtvarthanirdesho.abhipretaH, yajateH itivat, na dhAtunirdeshaH | tena yaH sarvaj~naH sarvavidyasya j~nAnamayaM tapaH | tasmAd etad brahma nAma rUpam annaM ca jAyate ityevamAdInyapi sarvaj~neshvarakAraNaparANi vAkyAnyudAhartavyAni || 

yat tUktaM sattvadharmeNa j~nAnena sarvaj~naM pradhAnaM bhaviShyatIti, tan nopapadyate | na hi pradhAnAvasthAyAM guNasAmyAt sattvadharmo j~nAnaM sambhavati |

nanUktaM sarvaj~nAnashaktimattvena sarvaj~naM bhaviShyatIti | tad api nopapadyate | yadi guNasAmye sati sattvavyapAshrayAM j~nAnashaktim Ashritya sarvaj~naM pradhAnam ucyeta, kAmaM rajastamovyapAshrayAm api j~nAnapratibandhakashaktim Ashritya kiMcijj~nam ucyeta | api ca nAsAkShikA sattvavR^ittir jAnAtinA abhidhIyate | na cAcetanasya pradhAnasya sAkShitvam asti | tasmAd anupapannaM pradhAnasya sarvaj~natvam | yoginAM tu cetanatvAt sattvotkarShanimittaM sarvaj~natvam upapannam ityanudAharaNam | 

atha punaH sAkShinimittam IkShitR^itvaM pradhAnasyApi kalpyeta, yathAgninimittamayaHpiNDAder dagdhR^itvam | tathA sati yannimittam IkShitR^itvaM pradhAnasya, tad eva sarvaj~naM brahma mukhyaM jagataH kAraNam iti yuktam | yat punar uktaM brahmaNo.api na mukhyaM sarvaj~natvam upapadyate, nityaj~nAnakriyatve j~nAnakriyAM prati svAtantryAsambhavAd iti | atrocyate -- idaM tAvad bhavAn praShTavyaH -- kathaM nityaj~nAnakriyatve sarvaj~natvahAniH iti | yasya hi sarvaviShayAvabhAsanakShamaM j~nAnaM nityam asti, so.asarvaj~na iti vipratiShiddham | anityatve hi j~nAnasya, kadAcijjAnAti kadAcin na jAnAtItyasarvaj~natvam api syAt | nAsau j~nAnanityatve doSho.asti | j~nAnanityatve j~nAnaviShayaH svAtantryavyapadesho nopapadyate iti cet, na | pratatauShNyaprakAshe.api savitari dahati prakAshayati iti svAtantryavyapadeshadarshanAt | 

nanu savitur dAhyaprakAshyasaMyoge sati dahati prakAshayati iti vyapadeshaH syAt | na tu brahmaNaH prAgutpatter j~nAnakarmasaMyogo.astIti viShamo dR^iShTAntaH | na | asatyapi karmaNi savitA prakAshate iti kartR^itvavyapadeshadarshanAt, evam asatyapi j~nAnakarmaNi brahmaNaH tad aikShata iti kartR^itvavyapadeshopapatter na vaiShamyam | karmApekShAyAM tu brahmaNi IkShitR^itvashrutayaH sutarAm upapannAH | 

kiM punaH tat karma, yat prAgutpatter Ishvaraj~nAnasya viShayo bhavatIti ? tattvAnyatvAbhyAm anirvacanIye nAmarUpe avyAkR^ite vyAcikIrShite iti brUmaH | yatprasAdAd dhi yoginAm apyatItAnAgataviShayaM pratyakShaM j~nAnam icchanti yogashAstravidaH, kim u vaktavyaM tasya nityasiddhasyeshvarasya sR^iShTisthitisaMhR^itiviShayaM nityaj~nAnaM bhavatIti | yad apyuktaM prAgutpatter brahmaNaH sharIrAdisambandham antareNekShitR^itvam anupapannam iti, na taccodyam avatarati | savitR^iprakAshavad brahmaNo j~nAnasvarUpanityatve j~nAnasAdhanApekShAnupapatteH | api cAvidyAdimataH saMsAriNaH sharIrAdyapekShA j~nAnotpattiH syAt | na j~nAnapratibandhakAraNarahitasyeshvarasya | mantrau cemAv Ishvarasya sharIrAdyanapekShatAm anAvaraNaj~nAnatAM ca darshayataH -- 

na tasya kAryaM karaNaM ca vidyate 
na tatsamashcAbhyadhikashca dR^ishyate | 
parAsya shaktir vividhaiva shrUyate 
svAbhAvikI j~nAnabalakriyA ca || [shve.u. 6.8] iti | 

apANipAdo javano grahItA 
pashyatyacakShuH sa shrR^iNotyakarNaH | 
sa vetti vedyaM na ca tasyAsti vettA 
tam Ahur agryaM puruShaM mahAntam || [shve.u. 3.19] iti ca | 

nanu nAsti tava j~nAnapratibandhakAraNarahiteshvarAd anyaH saMsArI -- nAnyo.ato.asti draShTA nAnyo.ato.asti vij~nAtA ityAdi shruteH | tatra kim idam ucyate -- saMsAriNaH sharIrAdyapekShA j~nAnotpattiH, neshvarasyeti? atrocyate -- satyaM neshvarAd anyaH saMsArI | tathApi dehAdisaMghAtopAdhisambandha iShyata eva, ghaTakarakagiriguhAdyupAdhisambandha iva vyomnaH | tatkR^itashca shabdapratyayavyavahAro lokasya dR^iShTaH -- ghaTacchidram karakacchidram ityAdiH, AkAshAvyatireke.api | tatkR^itA cAkAshe ghaTAkAshAdibhedamithyAbuddhir draShTA | tathehApi dehAdisaMghAtopAdhisambandhAvivekakR^iteshvarasaMsAribhedamithyAbuddhiH | dR^ishyate cAtmana eva sato dehAdisaMghAte.anAtmanyAtmatvAbhinivesho mithyAbuddhimAtreNa pUrvapUrveNa | sati caivaM saMsAritve dehAdyapekSham IkShitR^itvam upapannaM saMsAriNaH | yad apyuktaM pradhAnasyAnekAtmakatvAn mR^idAdivat kAraNatvopapattir nAsaMhatasya brahmaNa iti, tatpradhAnasyAshabdatvenaiva pratyuktam | yathA tu tarkeNApi brahmaNa eva kAraNatvaM nirvoDhuM shakyate, na pradhAnAdInAm, tathA prapaJNcayiShyati na vilakShaNatvAd asya -- ityevamAdinA ||5|| 

|| 1.1.6 ||

atrAha -- yad uktaM nAcetanaM pradhAnaM jagatkAraNam IkShitR^itvashravaNAd iti, tad anyathApyupapadyate | acetane.api cetanavad upacAradarshanAt | yathA pratyAsannapatanatAM nadyAH kUlasyAlakShya kUlaM pipatiShati ityacetane.api kUle cetanavad upacAro dR^iShTaH, tadvad acetane.api pradhAne pratyAsannasargo cetanavad upacAro bhaviShyati tad aikShata iti | yathA loke kashciccetanaH snAtvA bhuktvA cAparAhNe grAmaM rathena gamiShyAmi itIkShitvA anantaraM tathaiva niyamena pravartate, tathA pradhAnam api mahadAdyAkAreNa niyamena pravartate | tasmAccetanavad upacaryate | kasmAt punaH kAraNAt vihAya mukhyam IkShitR^itvam aupacArikaM kalpyate? tat teja aikShata tA Apa aikShanta iti cAcetanayor apyaptejasoshcetanavad upacAradarshanAt | tasmAt satkartR^ikam apIkShaNam aupacArikam iti gamyate, upacAraprAye vacanAt | -- ityevaM prApte, idaM sUtram Arabhyate -- 

gauNashcen nAtmashabdAt || 

yad uktaM pradhAnam acetanaM sacchabdavAcyaM tasminn aupacArikam IkShitR^itvam aptejasoH iveti, tad asat | kasmAt? AtmashabdAt | sad eva somyedam agra AsIt [chA.u. 6.2.1] ityupakramya, tad aikShata tat tejo.asR^ijata iti ca tejo.abannAnAM sR^iShTim uktvA, tad eva prakR^itaM sad IkShitR^i tAni ca tejo.abannAni devatAshabdena parAmR^ishyAha -- seyaM devataikShata hantAham imAH tisro devatA anena jIvenAtmanAnupravishya nAmarUpe vyAkaravANi [chA.u. 6.3.2] iti | tatra yadi pradhAnam acetanaM guNavR^ittyekShitR^i kalpyeta, tad eva prakR^itatvAt seyaM devatA iti parAmR^ishyeta | na tadA devatA jIvam AtmashabdenAbhidadhyAt | jIvo hi nAma cetanaH sharIrAdhyakShaH prANAnAM dhArayitA, tatprasiddher nirvacanAcca | sa katham acetanasya pradhAnasyAtmA bhavet ? AtmA hi nAma svarUpam | nAcetanasya pradhAnasya cetano jIvaH svarUpaM bhavitum arhati | 

atha tu cetanaM brahma mukhyam IkShitR^i parigR^ihyeta, tasya jIvaviShaya Atmashabdaprayoga upapadyate | tathA sa ya eSho.aNim aitadAtmyam idaM sarvaM tat satyaM sa AtmA tat tvam asi shvetaketo [chA.u. 6.8.7] ityatra sa AtmA iti prakR^itaM sad aNimAnam AtmAnam Atmashabdenopadishya, tat tvam asi shvetaketo [chA.u. 6.8.7] iti cetanasya shvetaketor Atmatvenopadishati | aptejasoH tu -- viShayatvAd acetanatvam, nAmarUpavyAkaraNAdau ca prayojyatvenaiva nirdeshAt, na cAtmashabdavat kiMcin mukhyatve kAraNam astIti -- yuktaM kUlavad gauNatvam IkShitR^itvasya | tayor api sadadhiShThitatvApekSham evekShitR^itvam | satastvAt mashabdAn na gauNam IkShitR^itvam ityuktam || 

|| 1.1.7 ||

athocyeta -- acetane.api pradhAne bhavatyAtmashabdaH, AtmanaH sarvArthakAritvAt | yathA rAj~naH sarvArthakAriNi bhR^itye bhavatyAtmashabdaH mamAtmA bhadrasenaH iti | pradhAnaM hi puruShasyAtmano bhogApavargo kurvad upakaroti, rAj~na iva bhR^ityaH sandhivigrahAdiShu vartamAnaH | athavaika evAtmashabdashcetanAcetanaviShayo bhaviShyati, bhUtAtmA indriyAtmA iti ca prayogadarshanAt | yathaika eva jyotiHshabdaH kratujvalanaviShayaH | tatra kuta etadAtmashabdAd IkShater agauNatvam ityata uttaraM paThati -- 

tanniShThasya mokShopadeshAt || 

na pradhAnam acetanam AtmashabdAlambanaM bhavitum arhati | sa AtmA iti prakR^itaM sad aNimAnam AdAya, tat tvam asi shvetaketo [chA.u. 6.8.7] iti cetanasya shvetaketor mokShayitavyasya tanniShThAm upadishya, AcAryavAn puruSho veda tasya tAvad eva ciraM yAvan na vimokShye.atha sampatsye [chA.u. 6.14.2] iti mokShopadeshAt | yadi hyacetanaM pradhAnaM sacchabdavAcyam tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7] iti grAhayet, mumukShuM cetanaM santam acetano.asIti, tadA viparItavAdi shAstraM puruShasyAnarthAyetyapramANaM syAt | na tu nirdoSham idaM shAstram apramANaM kalpayituM yuktam | yadi cAj~nasya sato mumukShor acetanam anAtmAnam Atmetyupadishet pramANabhUtaM shAstram, sa shraddadhAnatayA andhagolAN^gUlanyAyena tadAtmadR^iShTiM na parityajet, tadvyatiriktaM cAtmAnaM na pratipadyeta | tathA sati puruShArthAd vihanyeta, anarthaM vA R^icchet | tasmAd yathA svargAdyarthino.agnihotrAdisAdhanaM yathAbhUtam upadishati, tathA mumukShor api sa AtmA tat tvam asi shvetaketo [chA.u. 6.8.7] iti yathAbhUtam evAtmAnam upadishatIti yuktam | evaM ca sati taptaparashugrahaNamokShadR^iShTAntena satyAbhisandhasya mokShopadesha upapadyate | anyathA hyamukhye sadAtmatattvopadeshe, aham uktham asmIti vidyAt itivat sampanmAtram idam anityaphalaM syAt | tatra mokShopadesho nopapadyeta | tasmAn na sadaNimanyAtmashabdasya gauNatvam | bhR^itye tu svAmibhR^ityabhedasya pratyakShatvAd upapanno gauNa AtmashabdaH mamAtmA bhadrasenaH iti | 

api ca kvacid gauNaH shabdo dR^iShTa iti naitAvatA shabdapramANake.arthe gauNIkalpanA nyAyyA, sarvatrAnAshvAsaprasaN^gAt | yat tUktaM cetanAcetanayoH sAdhAraNa AtmashabdaH, kratujvalanayoH iva jyotiHshabda iti, tan na | anekArthatvasyAnyAyyatvAt | tasmAccetanaviShaya eva mukhya AtmashabdashcetanatvopacArAd bhUtAdiShu prayujyate -- bhUtAtmA indriyAtmA iti ca | sAdhAraNatve.apyAtmashabdasya na prakaraNam upapadaM vA kiMcin nishcAyakam antareNAnyataravR^ittitA nirdhArayituM shakyate | na cAtrAcetanasya nishcAyakaM kiMcit kAraNam asti | prakR^itaM tu sadIkShitR^i saMnihitashca cetanaH shvetaketuH | na hi cetanasya shvetaketor acetana AtmA sambhavatItyavocAma | tasmAccetanaviShaya ihAtmashabda iti nishcIyate | jyotiHshabdo.api laukikena prayogeNa jvalana eva rUDhaH, arthavAdakalpitena tu jvalanasAdR^ishyena kratau pravR^itta ityadR^iShTAntaH | 

athavA pUrvasUtra evAtmashabdaM nirastasamastagauNatvasAdhAraNatvAshaN^katayA vyAkhyAya, tataH svatantra eva pradhAnakAraNanirAkaraNahetur vyAkhyeyaH -- tanniShThasya mokShopadeshAt iti | tasmAn nAcetanaM pradhAnaM sacchabdavAcyam ||7|| 

 || 1.1.8 || 

kutashca na pradhAnaM sacchabdavAcyam? -- 

heyatvAvacanAcca ||

yadyanAtmaiva pradhAnaM sacchabdavAcyam, sa AtmA tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7] itIhopadiShTaM syAt | sa tadupadeshashravaNAd anAtmaj~natayA tanniShTho mA bhUd iti, mukhyam AtmAnam upadidikShu shAstraM tasya heyatvaM brUyAt | yathArundhatIM didarshayiShuH tatsamIpasthAM sthUlAM tArAmamukhyAM prathamam arundhatIti grAhayitvA, tAM pratyAkhyAya, pashcAd arundhatIm eva grAhayati | tadvan nAyam Atmeti brUyAt | na caivam avocat | sanmAtrAtmAvagatiniShThaiva hi ShaShThaprapAThake parisamAptir dR^ishyate | cashabdaH pratij~nAvirodhAbhyuccayapradarshanArthaH | satyapi heyatvavacane pratij~nAvirodhaH prasajyeta | kAraNavij~nAnAd dhi sarvaM vij~nAtam iti pratij~nAtam -- uta tam Adesham aprAkShyo yenAshrutaM shrutaM bhavatyamataM matam avij~nAtaM vij~nAtam [chA.u. 6.1.3] iti | kathaM nu bhagavaH sa Adesho bhavatIti | yathA somyaikena mR^itpiNDena sarvaM mR^inmayaM vij~nAtaM syAd vAcArambhaNaM vikAro nAmadheyaM mR^ittiketyeva satyam evaM somya sa Adesho bhavati [chA.u. 6.1.4, 6] iti vAkyopakrame shravaNAt | na ca sacchabdavAcye pradhAne bhogyavargakAraNe heyatvenAheyatvena vA vij~nAte bhoktR^ivargo vij~nAto bhavati, apradhAnavikAratvAd bhoktR^ivargasya | tasmAn na pradhAnaM sacchabdavAcyam ||8|| 

|| 1.1.9 ||

svApyayAt ||

tad eva sacchabdavAcyaM kAraNaM prakR^itya shrUyate -- yatraitat puruShaH svapiti nAma, satA somya tadA sampanno bhavati | svam apIto bhavati | tasmAd enaM svapitItyAcakShate | svaM hyapIto bhavati [chA.u. 6.8.1] iti | eShA shrutiH svapitItyetatpuruShasya lokaprasiddhaM nAma nirvakti | svashabdenehAtmocyate | yaH prakR^itaH sacchabdavAcyaH tam apIto bhavatyapi gato bhavatItyarthaH | apipUrvasyaitair layArthatvaM prasiddham, prabhavApyayAvityutpattipralayayoH prayogadarshanAt | manaHpracAropAdhivisheShasambandhAd indriyArthAn gR^ihNaMH tadvisheShApanno jIvo jAgarti | tadvAsanAvishiShTaH svapnAn pashyan manaHshabdavAcyo bhavati | sa upAdhidvayoparame suShuptAvasthAyAm upAdhikR^itavisheShAbhAvAt svAtmani pralIna iveti svaM hyapIto bhavati ityucyate | yathA hR^idayashabdanirvacanaM shrutyA darshitam -- sa vA eSha AtmA hR^idi, tasyaitad eva niruktam -- hR^idyayam iti | tasmAd dhR^idayam iti | yathA vAshanAyodanyAshabdapravR^ittimUlaM darshayati shrutiH -- Apa eva tad ashitaM nayante teja eva tat pItaM nayate iti ca | evaM svam AtmAnaM sacchabdavAcyam apIto bhavati itImam arthaM svapitinAmanirvacanena darshayati | na ca cetana AtmA acetanaM pradhAnaM svarUpatvena pratipadyeta | yadi punaH pradhAnam evAtmIyatvAt svashabdenaivocyeta, evam api cetano.acetanam apyetIti viruddham Apadyeta | 

shrutyantaraM ca -- prAj~nenAtmanA sampariShvakto na bAhyaM kiMcana veda nAntaram iti suShuptAvasthAyAM cetane apyayaM darshayati | ato yasminn apyayaH sarveShAM cetanAnAM taccetanaM sacchabdavAcyaM jagataH kAraNaM syAt, nAcetanaM pradhAnam ||9|| 

|| 1.1.10 ||

kutashca na pradhAnaM jagataH kAraNam? -- 

gatisAmAnyAt ||

yadi tArkikasamaya iva vedAnteShvapi bhinnA kAraNAvagagatir abhaviShyat, kvaciccetanaM brahma jagataH kAraNam, kvacid acetanaM pradhAnam, kvacid anyad eveti, tataH kadAcit pradhAnakAraNavAdAnurodhenApIkShatyAdishravaNam akalpayiShyat | na tv etad asti | samAnaiva hi sarveShu vedAnteShu cetanakAraNAvagatiH | yathAgner jvalataH sarvA disho visphuliN^gA vipratiShTherann evam evaitasmAd AtmanaH sarve prANA yathAyatanaM vipratiShThante prANebhyo devA devebhyo lokAH iti, tasmAd vA etasmAd Atmana AkAshaH sambhUtaH iti, Atmana evedaM sarvam iti, Atmana eSha prANo jAyate iti ca AtmanaH kAraNatvaM darshayanti sarve vedAntAH | Atmashabdashca cetanavacana ityavocAma | mahacca prAmANyakAraNam etat, yad vedAntavAkyAnAM cetanakAraNatve samAnagatitvam, cakShurAdInAm iva rUpAdiShu | ato gatisamAnyAt sarvaj~naM brahma jagataH kAraNam ||10|| 


|| 1.1.11 ||

atha sphuTam eva nirguNasya vAcyatvam Aha -- 

shrutatvAcca ||

svashabdenaiva ca sarvaj~na Ishvaro jagataH kAraNam iti shrUyate, shvetAshvatarANAM mantropaniShadi sarvaj~nam IshvaraM prakR^itya -- sa kAraNaM karaNAdhipAdhipo na cAsya kashcijjanitA na cAdhipaH [shve.u. 6.9] iti | tasmAt sarvaj~naM brahma jagataH kAraNam, nAcetanaM pradhAnam anyad veti siddham || 

janmAdyasya yataH ityArabhya shrutatvAcca ityetadantaiH sUtrair yAnyudAhR^itAni vedAntavAkyAni, teShAM sarvaj~naH sarvashaktir Ishvaro jagato janmasthitipralayakAraNam ityetasyArthasya pratipAdakatvaM nyAyapUrvakaM pratipAditam | gatisAmAnyopanyAsena ca sarve vedAntAshcetanakAraNavAdina iti vyAkhyAtam | ataH parasya granthasya kim utthAnam iti, ucyate -- dvirUpaM hi brahmAvagamyate -- nAmarUpavikArabhedopAdhivishiShTam, tadviparItaM ca sarvopAdhivivarjitam | yatra hi dvaitam iva bhavati, tad itara itaraM pashyati, yatra tu asya sarvam AtmaivAbhUt, tat kena kaM pashyet yatra nAnyat pashyati nAnyacchR^iNoti nAnyad vijAnAti sa bhUmA | atha yatrAnyat pashyatyanyacchR^iNotyanyad vijAnAti tad alpam | yo vai bhUmA tad amR^itam [bR^i.A.u. 4.5.15] | atha yad alpaM tanmartyam sarvANi rUpANi vicitya dhIro nAmAni kR^itvAbhivadanyad Aste 

niShkalaM niShkriyaM shAntaM niravadyaM niraJNjanam | 
amR^itasya paraM setuM dagdhendhanam ivAnalam || [shve.u. 6.19]

neti neti, asthUlam anaNvahrasvam adIrgham [bR^i.A.u. 3.8.8] iti, nyUnam anyat sthAnaM sampUrNam anyat iti caivaM sahasrasho vidyAvidyAviShayabhedena brahmaNo dvirUpatAM darshayanti vedAntavAkyAni | tatrAvidyAvasthAyAM brahmaNa upAsyopAsakAdilakShaNaH sarvo vyavahAraH | tatra kAnicid brahmaNa upAsanAnyabhyudayArthAni, kAnicit kramamuktyarthAni, kAnicit karmasamR^iddhyarthAni | teShAM guNavisheShopAdhibhedena bhedaH | eka eva tu para AtmeshvaraH taiH tair guNavisheShair vishiShTa upAsyo yadyapi bhavati, tathApi yathAguNopAsanam eva phalAni bhidyante | taM yathA yathopAsate tad eva bhavati iti shruteH, yathA kratur asmiMl loke puruSho bhavati, tathetaH pretya bhavati [chA.u. 3.14.2] iti ca | smR^iteshca -- 

yaM yaM vApi smaran bhAvaM tyajatyante kalevaram | 
taM tam evaiti kaunteya sadA tadbhAvabhAvitaH || iti | 

yadyapyeka AtmA sarvabhUteShu sthAvarajaN^gameShu gUDhaH, tathApi cittopAdhivisheShatAratamyAd AtmanaH kUTasthanityasyaikarUpasyApyuttarottaram AviShkR^itasya tAratamyam aishvaryashaktivisheShaiH shrUyate -- tasya ya AtmAnam AvistarAM veda ityatra | smR^itAvapi -- 

yad yad vibhUtimat sattvaM shrImad Urjitam eva vA | 
tat tad evAvagaccha tvaM mama tejo.aMshasambhavam || iti 

yatra yatra vibhUtyAdyatishayaH, sa sa Ishvara ityupAsyatayA codyate | evam ihApyAdityamaNDale hiraNmayaH puruShaH sarvapApmodayaliN^gAt para eveti vakShyati | evam AkAshaH talliN^gAt [ve.sU. 1.1.22] ityAdiShu draShTavyam | evaM sadyomuktikAraNam apyAtmaj~nAnam upAdhivisheShadvAreNopadishyamAnam apyavivakShitopAdhisambandhavisheShaM parAparaviShayatvena sandihyamAnaM vAkyagatiparyAlocanayA nirNetavyaM bhavati -- yathehaiva tAvat Anandamayo.abhyAsAt [ve.sU. 1.1.12] iti | evam ekam api brahmApekShitopAdhisambandhaM nirastopAdhisambandhaM copAsyatvena j~neyatvena ca vedAnteShUpadishyata iti pradarshayituM paro grantha Arabhyate ||11|| 

  -- o)0(o -- 

6. AnandamayAdhikaraNam

|| 1.1.12 ||

yacca gatisAmAnyAt ityacetanakAraNanirAkaraNam uktam, tad api vAkyAntarANi brahmaviShayANi vyAcakShANena brahmaviparItakAraNaniShedhena prapaJNcyate -- taittirIyake annamayaM prANamayaM manomayaM vij~nAnamayaM cAnukramyAm nAyate -- tasmAd vA etasmAd vij~nAnamayAd anyo.antara AtmAnandamayaH iti | tatra saMshayaH -- kim ihAnandamayashabdena param eva brahmocyate, yat prakR^itam satyaM j~nAnam anantaM brahma [tai.u. 2.3] iti, kiM vAnnamayAdivad brahmaNo.arthAntaram iti | kiM tAvat prAptam? brahmaNo.arthAntaram amukhya AtmAnandamayaH syAt | kasmAt? annamayAdyamukhyAtmapravAhapatitatvAt | 

athApi syAt sarvAntaratvAd Anandamayo mukhya evAtmeti | na syAt priyAdyavayavayogAcchArIratvashravaNAcca | mukhyashced AtmA syAn na priyAdisaMsparshaH syAt | iha tu tasya priyam eva shiraH ityAdi shrUyate | shArIratvaM ca shrUyate -- tasyaiSha eva shArIra AtmA yaH pUrvasya iti | tasya pUrvasya vij~nAnamayasyaiSha eva shArIra AtmA ya eSha Anandamaya ityarthaH | na ca sasharIrasya sataH priyApriyasaMsparsho vArayituM shakyaH | tasmAt saMsAryevAnandamaya AtmetyevaM prApte, idam ucyate -- 

Anandamayo.abhyAsAt ||

para evAtmAnandamayo bhavitum arhati | kutaH? abhyAsAt | parasminn eva hyAtmanyAnandashabdo bahukR^itvo.abhyasyate | AnandamayaM prastutya raso vai saH iti tasyaiva rasatvam uktvA, ucyate -- rasaM hyevAyaM labdhvAnandI bhavati | ko hyevAnyAt kaH prANyAt yad eSha AkAsha Anando na syAt | eSha hyevAnandayAti saiShAnandasya mImAMsA bhavati etam Anandamayam AtmAnam upasaMkrAmati AnandaM brahmaNo vidvAn na bibheti kutashcana [tai.u. 2.7] iti | Anando brahmeti vyajAnAt iti ca | shrutyantare ca vij~nAnam AnandaM brahma [bR^i.A.u. 3.9.7] iti brahmaNyevAnandashabdo dR^iShTaH | evam Anandashabdasya bahukR^itvo brahmaNyabhyAsAd Anandamaya AtmA brahmeti gamyate | 

yat tUktam annamayAdyamukhyAtmapravAhapatitatvAd AnandamayasyApyamukhyatvam iti, nAsau doShaH, Anandamayasya sarvAntaratvAt | mukhyam eva hyAtmAnam upadidikShu shAstraM lokabuddhim anusarat, annamayaM sharIram anAtmAnam atyantamUDhAnAm Atmatvena prasiddham anUdya mUShAniShiktadrutatAmrAdipratimAvat tato.antaraM tato.antaram ityevaM pUrveNa pUrveNa samAnam uttaram uttaram anAtmAnam Atmeti grAhayat, pratipattisaukaryApekShayA sarvAntaraM mukhyam Anandamayam AtmAnam upadidesheti shliShTataram | yathArundhatIdarshane bahvIShvapi tArAsvamukhyAsvarundhatIShu darshitAsu, yA antyA pradarshyate sA mukhyaivArundhatI bhavati | evam ihApyAnandamayasya sarvAntaratvAn mukhyam Atmatvam | yat tu brUShe, priyAdInAM shirastvAdikalpanAnupapannA mukhyasyAtmana iti -- atItAnantaropAdhijanitA sA | na svAbhAvikItyadoShaH | shArIratvam apyAnandamayasyAnnamayAdisharIraparamparayA pradarshyamAnatvAt | na punaH sAkShAd eva shArIratvaM saMsArivat | tasmAd AnandamayaH para evAtmA ||12|| 

|| 1.1.13 ||

vakArashabdAn neti cen na prAcuryAt ||

atrAha -- nAnandamayaH para AtmA bhavitum arhati | kasmAt? vikArashabdAt | prakR^itivacanAd ayam anyaH shabdo vikAravacanaH samadhigataH AnandamayaH iti, mayaTo vikArArthatvAt | tasmAd annamayAdishabdavadvikAraviShaya evAyam Anandamayashabda iti cet, na | prAcuryArthe.api mayaTaH smaraNAt | tat prakR^itavacane mayaT iti hi pracuratAyAm api mayaTa smaryate | yathA annamayo yaj~naH ityannapracura ucyate, evam AnandapracuraM brahmAnandamayam ucyate | AnandapracuratvaM ca brahmaNo manuShyatvAd Arabhyottarasminn uttarasmin sthAne shataguNa Ananda ityuktvA brahmAnandasya niratishayatvAvadhAraNAt | tasmAt prAcuryArthe mayaT || 


|| 1.1.14 ||

tarAtuvyapadeshAcca ||

itashca prAcuryArthe mayaT | yasmAd AnandahetutvaM brahmaNo vyapadishati shrutiH -- eSha hyevAnandayAti iti AnandayatItyarthaH | yo hyanyAn Anandayati sa pracurAnanda iti prasiddhaM bhavati | yathA loke yo.anyeShAM dhanikatvam ApAdayati sa pracuradhana iti gamyate, tadvat | tasmAt prAcuryArthe.api mayaTaH sambhavAd AnandamayaH para evAtmA ||14|| 

|| 1.1.15 ||

mAntravarNikam eva ca gIyate ||

itashcAnandamayaH para evAtmA | yasmAt brahmavid Apnoti param [tai.u. 2.1] ityupakramya, satyaM j~nAnam anantaM brahma [tai.u. 2.3] ityasmin mantre yat brahma prakR^itaM satyaj~nAnAnantavisheShaNair nirdhAritam, yasmAd AkAshAdikrameNa sthAvarajaN^gamAni bhUtAnyajAyanta, yacca bhUtAni sR^iShTvA tAnyanupravishya guhAyAm avasthitaM sarvAntaram, yasya vij~nAnAya anyo.antara AtmA anyo.antara AtmA iti prakrAntam, tanmantravarNikam eva brahmeha gIyate -- anyo.antara AtmAnandamayaH iti | mantrabrAhmaNayoshcaikArthatvaM yuktam, avirodhAt | anyathA hi prakR^itahAnAprakR^itaprakriye syAtAm | na cAnnamayAdibhya ivAnandamayAd anyo.antara AtmAbhidhIyate | etanniShThaiva ca bhArgavI vAruNI vidyA -- Anando brahmeti vyajAnAt iti | tasmAd AnandamayaH para evAtmA ||15||

|| 1.1.16 || 

netaro.anupapatteH ||

itashcAnandamayaH para evAtmA, netaraH | itara IshvarAdanyaH saMsArI jIva ityarthaH | na jIva AnandamayashabdenAbhidhIyate | kasmAt? anupapatteH | AnandamayaM hi prakR^itya shrUyate -- so.akAmayata | bahu syAM prajAyeyeti | sa tapo.atapyata | sa tapaH taptvA | idaM sarvam asR^ijata | yad idaM kiM ca [tai.u. 2.6] iti | tatra prAksharIrAdyutpatter abhidhyAnam, sR^ijyamAnAnAM ca vikArANAM sraShTur avyatirekaH, sarvavikArasR^iShTishca na parasmAd Atmano.anyatropapadyate ||16||

|| 1.1.17 ||

bhedavyapadeshAcca ||

itashca nAnandamayaH saMsArI | yasmAd AnandamayAdhikAre raso vai saH | rasaM hyevAyaM labdinA andI bhavati [tai.u. 2.7] iti jIvAnandamayau bhedena vyapadishati | na hi labdhaiva labdhavyo bhavati | kathaM tarhi AtmAnveShTavyaH AtmalAbhAn na paraM vidyate iti shrutismR^itI, yAvatA na labdhaiva labdhavyo bhavatItyuktam? bADham -- tathApyAtmano.apracyutAtmabhAvasyaiva sataH tattvAnavabodhanimitto mithyaiva dehAdiShvanAtmasu Atmatvanishcayo laukiko dR^iShTaH | tena dehAdibhUtasyAtmano.api AtmA -- ananviShTaH anveShTavyaH, alabdhaH labdhavyaH, ashrutaH shrotavyaH, amataH mantavyaH, avij~nAtaH vij~nAtavyaH -- ityAdibhedavyapadesha upapadyate | pratiShidhyata eva tu paramArthataH sarvaj~nAt parameshvarAd anyo draShTA shrotA vA nAnyo.ato.asti draShTA ityAdinA | parameshvaraH tu avidyAkalpitAcchArIrAt kartur bhoktuH vij~nAnAtmAkhyAt anyaH | yathA mAyAvinashcarmakhaDgadharAt sUtreNAkAsham adhirohataH sa eva mAyAvI paramArtharUpo bhUmiShTho.anyaH | yathA vA ghaTAkAshAd upAdhiparicchinnAd anupAdhiparicchinna AkAsho.anyaH | IdR^ishaM ca vij~nAnAtmaparamAtmabhedam Ashritya netaro.anupapatteH bhedavyapadeshAcca ityuktam ||17|| 

|| 1.1.18 ||

kAmAcca nAnumAnApekShA ||

AnandamayAdhikAre ca, so.akAmayata bahu syAM prajAyeyeti [tai.u. 2.6] iti kAmayitR^itvanirdeshAcca nAnumAnikam api sAN^khyaparikalpitam acetanaM pradhAnam Anandamayatvena kAraNatvena vA apekShitavyam | IkShater nAshabdam iti nirAkR^itam api pradhAnaM pUrvasUtrodAhR^itAM kAmayitR^itvashrutim Ashritya prasaN^gAt punar nirAkriyate gatisAmAnyaprapaJNcanAya ||18|| 

|| 1.1.19 ||

asminn asya ca tadyogaM shAsti ||

itashca na pradhAne jIve vAnandamayashabdaH | yasmAd asminn Anandamaye prakR^ita Atmani, pratibuddhasyAsya jIvasya, tadyogaM shAsti -- tad AtmanA yogaH tadyogaH, tadbhAvApattiH, muktiH ityarthaH -- tad yogaM shAsti shAstram -- yadA hyevaiSha etasminn adR^ishye.anAtmye.anirukte.anilayane.abhayaM pratiShThAM vindate | atha so.abhayaM gato bhavati | yadA hyevaiSha etasminn udaram antaraM kurute | atha tasya bhayaM bhavati iti | etad uktaM bhavati -- yad etasminn Anandamaye.alpam apyantaram atAdAtmyarUpaM pashyati, tadA saMsArabhayAn na nivartate | yadA tv etasminn Anandamaye nirantaraM tAdAtmyena pratitiShThati, tadA saMsArabhayAn nivartata iti | tacca paramAtmaparigrahe ghaTate, na pradhAnaparigrahe jIvaparigrahe vA | tasmAd AnandamayaH paramAtmeti siddham || 

idaM tviha vaktavyam -- sa vA eSha puruSho.annarasamayaH tasmAd vA etasmAd annarasamayAd anyo.antara AtmA prANamayaH, tasmAt anyo.antara AtmA manomayaH, tasmAt anyo.antara AtmA vij~nAnamayaH iti ca vikArArthe mayaTpravAhe sati, Anandamaya evAkasmAd ardhajaratIyanyAyena katham iva mayaTaH prAcuryArthatvaM brahmaviShayatvaM cAshrIyata iti | mAntravarNikabrahmAdhikArAd iti cet, na | annamayAdInAm api tarhi brahmatvaprasaN^gaH | 

atrAha -- yuktam annamayAdInAm abrahmatvam, tasmAt tasmAd AntarasyAntarasya anyasyAnyasya Atmana ucyamAnatvAt | AnandamayAt tu na kashcid anya Antara Atmocyate | tenAnandamayasya brahmatvam, anyathA prakR^itahAnAprakR^itaprakriyAprasaN^gAd iti |

atrocyate -- yadyapyannamayAdibhya ivAnandamayAt anyo.antara AtmA iti na shrUyate, tathApi nAnandamayasya brahmatvam | yata AnandamayaM prakR^itya shrUyate -- tasya priyam eva shiraH, modo dakShiNaH pakShaH, pramoda uttaraH pakShaH, Ananda AtmA, brahma pucchaM pratiShThA [tai.u. 2.4] iti | tatra yad brahmeha mantravarNe prakR^itam satyaM j~nAnam anantaM brahma [tai.u. 2.3] iti, tad iha brahma pucchaM pratiShThA ityucyate | tad vijij~nApayiShayaivAnnamayAdaya AnandamayaparyantAH paJNca koshAH kalpyante | tatra kutaH prakR^itahAnAprakR^itaprakriyAprasaN^gaH | 

nanvanandamayasyAvayavatvena brahma pucchaM pratiShThA ityucyate, annamayAdInAm iva idaM pucchaM pratiShThA ityAdi | tatra kathaM brahmaNaH svapradhAnatvaM shakyaM vij~nAtum? prakR^itatvAd iti brUmaH | 

nanvanandamayAvayavatvenApi brahmaNi vij~nAyamAne na prakR^itatvaM hIyate, Anandamayasya brahmatvAd iti | atrocyate -- tathA sati tad eva brahma Anandamaya AtmA avayavI, tad eva ca brahma pucchaM pratiShThA avayava ityasAmaJNjasyaM syAt | anyataraparigrahe tu, yuktam brahma pucchaM pratiShThA ityatraiva brahmanirdesha Ashrayitum, brahmashabdasaMyogAt | nAnandamayavAkye, brahmashabdasaMyogAbhAvAd iti | api ca brahma pucchaM pratiShThetyuktvedam ucyate -- tad apyeSha shloko bhavati | 

asann eva sa bhavati | asad brahmeti veda cet | 
asti brahmeti ced veda | santam enaM tato viduH || [tai.u. 2.5] iti | 

asmiMshca shloke.ananukR^iShyAnandamayaM brahmaNa eva bhAvAbhAvavedanayor guNadoShAbhidhAnAd gamyate -- brahma pucchaM pratiShThA ityatra brahmaNa eva svapradhAnatvam iti | na cAnandamayasyAtmano bhAvAbhAvAshaN^kA yuktA, priyamodAdivishiShTasyAnandamayasya sarvalokaprasiddhatvAt | kathaM punaH svapradhAnaM sad brahma Anandamayasya pucchatvena nirdishyate -- brahma pucchaM pratiShThA iti? naiSha doShaH | pucchavat puccham, pratiShThA parAyaNam ekanIDAM laukikasyAnandajAtasya brahmAnandaH ityetad anena vivakShyate, nAvayavatvam | etasyaivAnandasyAnyAni bhUtAni mAtrAm upajIvanti iti shrutyantarAt | api cAnandamayasya brahmatve priyAdyavayavatvena savisheShaM brahmAbhyupagantavyam | nirvisheShaM tu brahma vAkyasheShe shrUyate, vAN^manasayor agocaratvAbhidhAnAt -- 

yato vAco nivartante | aprApya manasA saha | 
AnandaM brahmaNo vidvAn | na bibheti kutashcana || [tai.u. 2.8] iti | 

api cAnandapracura ityukte duHkhAlpIyastvam api gamyate | prAcuryasya loke pratiyogyalpatvApekShatvAt | tathA ca sati yatra nAnyat pashyati, nAnyacchR^iNoti, nAnyad vijAnAti, sa bhUmA iti bhUmni brahmaNi tadvyatiriktAbhAvashrutir uparudhyeta | pratisharIraM ca priyAdibhedAdAnandamayasya bhinnatvam | brahma tu na pratisharIraM bhidyate, satyaM j~nAnam anantaM brahma [tai.u. 2.3] ityAnantyashruteH 

eko devaH sarvabhUteShu gUDhaH 
sarvavyApI sarvabhUtAntarAtmA [shve.u. 6.11] iti ca shrutyantarAt | 

na cAnandamayAbhyAsaH shrUyate | prAtipadikArthamAtram eva hi sarvatrAbhyasyate -- raso vai saH | rasaM hyevAyaM labdhvAnandI bhavati | ko hyevAnyAt kaH prANyAt | yad eSha AkAsha Anando na syAt saiShAnandasya mImAMsA bhavati | AnandaM brahmaNo vidvAn na bibheti kutashcana iti, Anando brahmeti vyajAnAt iti ca | yadi cAnandamayashabdasya brahmaviShayatvaM nishcitaM bhavet, tata uttareShvanandamAtraprayogeShvapyAnandamayAbhyAsaH kalpyeta | na tvanandamayasya brahmatvam asti, priyashirastvAdibhir hetubhiH ityavocAma | tasmAcchrutyantare vij~nAnam AnandaM brahma [bR^i.A.u. 3.9.7] ityAnandapadaprAtipadikasya brahmaNi prayogadarshanAt, yad eSha AkAsha Anando na syAt iti brahmaviShayaH prayogo, na tvanandamayAbhyAsa ityavagantavyam | yaH tu ayaM mayaDantasyaivAnandamayashabdasyAbhyAsaH etam Anandamayam AtmAnam upasaMkrAmati iti, na tasya brahmaviShayatvam asti | vikArAtmanAm evAnnamayAdInAm anAtmanAm upasaMkramitavyAnAM pravAhe patitatvAt | 

nanvanandamayasyopasaMkramitavyasyAnnamayAdivad abrahmatve sati naiva viduSho brahmaprAptiH phalaM nirdiShTaM bhavet | naiSha doShaH, AnandamayopasaMkramaNanirdeshenaiva viduShaH pucchapratiShThAbhUtabrahmaprApteH phalasya nirdiShTatvAt, tad apyeSha shloko bhavati yato vAco nivartante [tai.u. 2.8] ityAdinA ca prapaJNcyamAnatvAt | yA tvanandamayasaMnidhAne so.akAmayata bahu syAM prajAyeyeti [tai.u. 2.6] itIyaM shrutir udAhR^itA, sA brahma pucchaM pratiShThA ityanena saMnihitatareNa brahmaNA sambadhyamAnA nAnandamayasya brahmatAM pratibodhayati | tadapekShatvAccottarasya granthasya raso vai saH ityAder nAnandamayaviShayatA | 

nanu so.akAmayata [tai.u. 2.6] iti brahmaNi puMliN^ganirdesho nopapadyate | nAyaM doShaH, tasmAd vA etasmAd Atmana AkAshaH sambhUtaH ityatra puMliN^genApyAtmashabdena brahmaNaH prakR^itatvAt | yat tu bhArgavI vAruNI vidyA -- Anando brahmeti vyajAnAt iti, tasyAM mayaDashravaNAt priyashirastvAdyashravaNAcca yuktam Anandasya brahmatvam | tasmAd aNumAtram api visheSham anAshritya na svata eva priyashirastvAdi brahmaNa upapadyate | na ceha savisheShaM brahma pratipipAdayiShitam, vAN^manasagocarAtikramaNashruteH | tasmAd annamayAdiShvivAnandamaye.api vikArArtha eva mayaT vij~neyaH, na prAcuryArthaH || 

sUtrANi tv evaM vyAkhyeyAni -- brahma pucchaM pratiShThA ityatra kim AnandamayAvayavatvena brahma vivakShyate, uta svapradhAnatveneti | pucchashabdAd avayavatveneti prApte, ucyate -- Anandamayo.abhyAsAt Anandamaya AtmA ityatra brahma pucchaM pratiShThA iti svapradhAnam eva brahmopadishyate | abhyAsAt asann eva sa bhavati ityasmin nigamanashloke brahmaNa eva kevalasyAbhyasyamAnatvAt | vikArashabdAn neti cen na prAcuryAt vikArashabdo.avayavashabdo.abhipretaH | puccham ityavayavashabdAn na svapradhAnatvaM brahmaNa iti yad uktam, tasya parihAro vaktavyaH | atrocyate -- nAyaM doShaH, prAcuryAd apyavayavashabdopapatteH | prAcuryaM prAyApattiH, avayavaprAye vacanam ityarthaH | annamayAdInAM hi shiraAdiShu pucchAnteShvavayaveShUkteShvanandamayasyApi shiraAdInyavayavAntarANyuktvA avayavaprAyApattyA brahma pucchaM pratiShThA ityAha, nAvayavavivakShayA | yat kAraNam abhyAsAt iti svapradhAnatvaM brahmaNaH samarthitam | tarAtuvyapadeshAcca sarvasya hi vikArajAtasya sAnandamayasya kAraNatvena brahma vyapadishyate -- idaM sarvam asR^ijata, yad idaM kiM ca iti | na ca kAraNaM sad brahma svavikArasyAnandamayasya mukhyayA vR^ittyAvayava upapadyate | aparANyapi sUtrANi yathAsambhavaM pucchavAkyanirdiShTasyaiva brahmaNa upapAdakAni draShTavyAni ||19||

antaradhikaraNam || 

|| 1.1.20 || 

idam AmnAyate -- 

atha ya eSho.antar Aditye hiraNmayaH puruSho dR^ishyate hiraNyashmashrur hiraNyakesha A praNakhAt sarva eva suvarNaH tasya yathA kapyAsaM puNDarIkam evam akShiNI tasyod iti nAma sa eSha sarvebhyaH pApmabhya udita udeti ha vai sarvebhyaH pApmabhyo ya evaM veda [chA.u. 1.6.67] ityadhidaivatam | athAdhyAtmam api atha ya eSho.antar akShiNi puruSho dR^ishyate [chA.u. 1.7.5] ityAdi | 

tatra saMshayaH -- kiM vidyAkarmAtishayavashAt prAptotkarShaH kashcit saMsArI sUryamaNDale cakShuShi copAsyatvena shrUyate, kiM vA nityasiddhaH parameshvaraH? iti | kiM tAvat prAptam? saMsArIti | kutaH? rUpavattvashravaNAt | AdityapuruShe tAvat hiraNyashmashruH ityAdi rUpam udAhR^itam | akShipuruShe.api tad evAtideshena prApyate tasyaitasya tad eva rUpaM yad amuShya rUpam iti | na ca parameshvarasya rUpavattvaM yuktam, ashabdam asparsham arUpam avyayam [ka.u. 1.3.15] iti shruteH | AdhArashravaNAcca -- ya eSho.antar Aditye ya eSho.antar akShiNi iti | na hyanAdhArasya svamahimapratiShThitasya sarvavyApinaH parameshvarasyAdhAra upadishyeta | sa bhagavaH kasmin pratiShThita iti sve mahimni iti, AkAshavat sarvagatashca nityaH iti ca shrutI bhavataH | aishvaryamaryAdAshruteshca -- sa eSha ye cAmuShmAt parAJNco lokAH teShAM ceShTo devakAmAnAM ca ityAdityapuruShasya aishvaryamaryAdA | sa eSha ye caitasmAd arvAJNco lokAH teShAM ceShTo manuShyakAmAnAM ca ityakShipuruShasya | na ca parameshvarasya maryAdAvad aishvaryaM yuktam | eSha sarveshvara eSha bhUtAdhipatir eSha bhUtapAla eSha setur vidharaNa eShAM lokAnAm asambhedAya ityavisheShashruteH | tasmAn nAkShyAdityayor antaH parameshvara ityevaM prApte -- 

antaH taddharmopadeshAt ||

brUmaH -- antaH taddharmopadeshAt iti | ya eSho.antarAditye ya eSho.antarakShiNi iti ca shrUyamANaH puruShaH parameshvara eva, na saMsArI | kutaH? taddharmopadeshAt | tasya hi parameshvarasya dharmA ihopadiShTaH | tad yathA -- tasyod iti nAma iti shrAvayitvA tasyAdityapuruShasya nAma sa eSha sarvebhyaH pApmabhya uditaH iti sarvapApmApagamena nirvakti | tad eva ca kR^itanirvacanaM nAmAkShipuruShasyApyatidishati -- yannAma tannAma iti | sarvapApmApagamashca paramAtmana eva shrUyate -- ya AtmApahatapApmA [chA.u. 8.7.1] ityAdau | tathA cAkShuShe puruShe saiva R^ik tat sAma tad ukthaM tad yajuH tad brahma iti R^iksAmAdyAtmakatAM nirdhArayati | sA ca parameshvarasyopapadyate, sarvakAraNatvAt sarvAtmakatvopapatteH | pR^ithivyagnyAdyAtmake cAdhidaivatam R^iksAme, vAkprANAdyAtmake cAdhyAtmam anukramyAha -- tasya rk ca sAma ca geShNau ityadhidaivatam | tathAdhyAtmam api -- yAvamuShya geShNau tau geShNau iti | tacca sarvAtmakatve satyevopapadyate | tad ya ime vINAyAM gAyantyetaM tv eva te gAyanti tasmAt te dhanasanayaH iti ca laukikeShvapi gAneShvasyaiva gIyamAnatvaM darshayati | tacca parameshvaraparigraha eva ghaTate -- 

yad yad vibhUtimat sattvaM 
shrImad Urjitam eva vA | 
tat tad evAvagaccha tvaM 
mama tejo.aMshasambhavam || [gItA 10.42] iti bhagavadgItAdarshanAt | 

lokakAmeshitR^itvam api niraN^kushaM shrUyamANaM parameshvaraM gamayati | yat tUktaM hiraNyashmashrutvAdirUpavattvashravaNaM parameshvare nopapadyata iti, atra brUmaH -- syAt parameshvarasyApIcchAvashAn mAyAmayaM rUpaM sAdhakAnugrahArtham, 

mAyA hyeShA mayA sR^iShTA yan mAM pashyasi nArada | 
sarvabhUtaguNair yuktiM maivaM mAM j~nAtum arhasi || iti smaraNAt | 

api ca, yatra tu nirastasarvavisheShaM pArameshvaraM rUpam upadishyate, bhavati tatra shAstram ashabdam asparsham arUpam avyayam [ka.u. 1.3.15] ityAdi | sarvakAraNatvAt tu vikAradharmair api kaishcid vishiShTaH parameshvara upAsyatvena nirdishyate -- sarvakarmA sarvakAmaH sarvagandhaH sarvarasaH ityAdinA | tathA hiraNyashmashrutvAdinirdesho.api bhaviShyati | yad apyAdhArashravaNAn na parameshvara iti, atrocyate -- svamahimapratiShThasyApyAdhAravisheShopadesha upAsanArtho bhaviShyati | sarvagatatvAd brahmaNo vyomavat sarvAntaratvopapatteH | aishvaryamaryAdAshravaNam apyadhyAtmAdhidaivatavibhAgApekSham upAsanArtham eva | tasmAt parameshvara evAkShyAdityayor antar upadishyate ||20||
 
|| 1.1.21 || 

bhedavyapadeshAccAnyaH || 

asti cAdityAdisharIrAbhimAnibhyo jIvebhyo.anya Ishvaro.antaryAmI -- ya Aditye tiShThann AdityAd antaro yam Adityo na veda yasyAdityaH sharIraM ya Adityam antaro yamayatyeSha ta AtmAntaryAmyamR^itaH iti shrutyantare bhedavyapadeshAt | tatra hi AdityAd antaro yam Adityo na veda iti veditur AdityAd vij~nAnAtmano.anyo.antaryAmI spaShTaM nirdishyate | sa evehApyantar Aditye puruSho bhavitum arhati, shrutisAmAnyAt | tasmAt parameshvara evehopadishyata iti siddham ||21||

AkAshAdhikaraNam |

|| 1.1.22 ||

idam Amananti -- asya lokasya kA gatiH ityAkAsha iti hovAca sarvANi ha vA imAni bhUtAnyAkAshAd eva samutpadyanta AkAshaM pratyastaM yantyAkAsho hyevaibhyo jyAyAn AkAshaH parAyaNam [chA.u. 1.9.1] iti | 

tatra saMshayaH -- kim AkAshashabdena paraM brahmAbhidhIyate, uta bhUtAkAsham iti | kutaH saMshayaH ? ubhayatra prayogadarshanAt | bhUtavisheShe tAvat suprasiddho lokavedayor AkAshashabdaH | brahmaNyapi kvacit prayujyamAno dR^ishyate, yatra vAkyasheShavashAd asAdhAraNaguNashravaNAd vA nirdhAritaM brahma bhavati -- yathA yad eSha AkAsha Anando na syAt iti AkAsho ha vai nAma nAmarUpayor nirvahitA te yad antarA tad brahma iti caivam Adau | 

ataH saMshayaH | kiM punar atra yuktam? bhUtAkAsham iti | kutaH? tad dhi prasiddhatareNa prayogeNa shIghraM buddhim Arohati | na cAyam AkAshashabda ubhayoH sAdhAraNaH shakyo vij~nAtum, anekArthatvaprasaN^gAt | tasmAd brahmaNi gauNa eva AkAshashabdo bhavitum arhati | vibhutvAdibhir hi bahubhir dharmaiH sadR^isham AkAshena brahma bhavati | na ca mukhyasambhave gauNo.artho grahaNam arhati | sambhavati ceha mukhyasyaivAkAshasya grahaNam | 

nanu bhUtAkAshaparigrahe vAkyasheSho nopapadyate -- sarvANi ha vA imAni bhUtAnyAkAshAd eva samutpadyante [chA.u. 1.9.1] ityAdiH | naiSha doShaH, bhUtAkAshasyApi vAyvAdikrameNa kAraNatvopapatteH | vij~nAyate hi -- tasmAd vA etasmAd Atmana AkAshaH sambhUta AkAshAd vAyur vAyor agniH ityAdi | jyAyaH tu aparAyaNatve api bhUtAntarApekShayopapadyete bhUtAkAshasyApi | tasmAd AkAshashabdena bhUtAkAshasya grahaNam | ityevaM prApte brUmaH -- 

AkAshaH talliN^gAt || 

AkAshashabdeneha brahmaNo grahaNaM yuktam | kutaH? talliN^gAt | parasya hi brahmaNa idaM liN^gam -- sarvANi ha vA imAni bhUtAnyAkAshAd eva samutpadyante iti | parasmAd dhi brahmaNo bhUtAnAm utpattiH iti vedAnteShu maryAdA | 

nanu bhUtAkAshasyApi vAyvAdikrameNa kAraNatvaM darshitam | satyaM darshitam | tathApi mUlakAraNasya brahmaNo.aparigrahAt, AkAshAd evetyavadhAraNaM sarvANIti ca bhUtavisheShaNaM nAnukUlaM syAt | tathA AkAshaM pratyastaM yanti iti brahmaliN^gam, AkAsho hyevaibhyo jyAyAn AkAshaH parAyaNam iti ca jyAyastvaparAyaNatve | jyAyastvaM hyanApekShikaM paramAtmanyevaikasminn AmnAtam -- jyAyAn pR^ithivyA jyAyAn antarikShAjjyAyAn divo jyAyAnebhyo lokebhyaH iti | tathA parAyaNatvam api paramakAraNatvAt paramAtmanyeva upapannataraM bhavati | shrutishca -- vij~nAnam AnandaM brahma [bR^i.A.u. 3.9.7] rAtir dAtuH parAyaNam iti | api cAntavat tu adoSheNa shAlAvatyasya pakShaM ninditvA, anantaM kiMcid vaktukAmena jaivalinAkAshaH parigR^ihItaH | taM cAkAsham udgIthe sampAdyopasaMharati -- sa eSha parovarIyAn udgIthaH sa eSho.anantaH iti | taccAnantyaM brahmaliN^gam | yat punar uktaM bhUtAkAshaM prasiddhibalena prathamataraM pratIyata iti, atra brUmaH -- prathamataraM pratItam api tadvAkyasheShagatAn brahmaguNAn dR^iShTvA na parigR^ihyate | darshitashca brahmaNyapyAkAshashabdaH AkAsho ha vai nAma nAmarUpayor nirvahitA ityAdau | tathAkAshaparyAyavAcinAm api brahmaNi prayogo dR^ishyate -- R^ico akShare parame vyoman yasmin devA adhi vishve niSheduH saiShA bhArgavI vAruNI vidyA parame vyoman pratiShThitA | oM kaM brahma khaM brahma khaM purANam iti caivam Adau | vAkyopakrame.api vartamAnasyAkAshashabdasya vAkyasheShavashAd yuktA brahmaviShayatvAvadhAraNA | agnir adhIte.anuvAkam iti hi vAkyopakramagato.apyagnishabdo mANavakaviShayo dR^ishyate | tasmAd AkAshashabdaM brahmeti siddham ||22||
