prANAdhikaraNaM

|| 1.1.23 || 

udgIthe -- prastotaryA devatA prastAvam anvAyattA ityupakramya shrUyate -- katamA sA devateti, prANa iti hovAca, sarvANi ha vA imAni bhUtAni prANam evAbhisaMvishanti, prANamabhyujjihate, saiShA devatA prastAvamanvAyattA iti | tatra saMshayanirNayau pUrvavad eva draShTavyau | prANabandhanaM hi somya manaH prANasya prANam iti caivamAdau brahmaviShayaH prANashabdo dR^ishyate | vAyuvikAre tu prasiddhataro lokavedayoH | ata iha prANashabdena katarasyopAdAnaM yuktam iti bhavati saMshayaH | kiM punar atra yuktam? vAyuvikArasya paJNcavR^itteH prANasyopAdAnaM yuktam | tatra hi prasiddhataraH prANashabda ityavocAma | 

nanu pUrvavadihApi talliN^gAd brahmaNa eva grahaNaM yuktam | ihApi hi vAkyasheShe bhUtAnAM saMveshanodgamanaM pArameshvaraM karma pratIyate | na, mukhye.api prANe bhUtasaMveshanodgamanasya darshanAt | evaM hyAmnAyate -- yadA vai puruShaH svapiti prANaM tarhi vAg apyeti prANaM cakShuH prANaM shrotraM prANaM manaH, sa yadA prabudhyate prANAd evAdhi punar jAyante iti | pratyakShaM caitat -- svApakAle prANavR^ittAvaparilupyamAnAyAm indriyavR^ittayaH parilupyante, prabodhakAle ca punaH prAdurbhavantIti | indriyasAratvAcca bhUtAnAm aviruddho mukhye prANe.api bhUtasaMveshanodgamanavAdI vAkyasheShaH | api cAdityo.annaM codgIthapratihArayor devate prastAvadevatAyAH prANasyAnantaraM nirdishyeta | na ca tayor brahmatvam asti | tatsAmAnyAcca prANasyApi na brahmatvam ityevaM prApte -- 

ata eva prANaH || 

sUtrakAra Aha -- ata eva prANaH iti | talliN^gAd iti pUrvasUtre nirdiShTam | ata eva talliN^gAt prANashabdam api paraM brahma bhavitum arhati | prANasyApi hi brahmaliN^gasambandhaH shrUyate -- sarvANi ha vA imAni bhUtAni prANam evAbhisaMvishanti prANam abhyujjihate iti | prANanimittau sarveShAM bhUtAnAm utpattipralayAv ucyamAnau prANasya brahmatAM gamayataH | 

nanUktaM mukhyaprANaparigrahe.api saMveshanodgamanadarshanam aviruddham, svApaprabodhayor darshanAd iti | atrocyate -- svApaprabodhayoH indriyANAm eva kevalAnAM prANAshrayaM saMveshanodgamanaM dR^ishyate, na sarveShAM bhUtAnAm | iha tu sendriyANAM sasharIrANAM ca jIvAviShTAnAM bhUtAnAm, sarvANi ha vA imAni bhUtAni iti shruteH | yadApi bhUtashrutir mahAbhUtaviShayA parigR^ihyate, tadApi brahmaliN^gatvam aviruddham | 

nanu sahApi viShayaiH indriyANAM svApaprabodhayoH prANe.apyayaM prANAcca prabhavaM shrR^iNumaH -- yadA suptaH svapnaM na kaMcana pashyatyathAsmin prANa evaikadhA bhavati tadainaM vAk sarvair nAmabhiH sahApyeti iti | tatrApi talliN^gAt prANashabdaM brahmeva | yat punar uktam annAd ityasaMnidhAnAt prANasyAbrahmatvam iti, tad ayuktam | vAkyasheShabalena prANashabdasya brahmaviShayatAyAM pratIyamAnAyAM saMnidhAnasyAkiMcitkaratvAt | yat punaH prANashabdasya paJNcavR^ittau prasiddhataratvam, tad AkAshashabdasyeva pratividheyam | tasmAt siddhaM prastAvadevatAyAH prANasya brahmatvam || 

atra kecid udAharanti -- prANasya prANam prANabandhanaM hi somya manaH iti ca | tad ayuktam | shabdabhedAt prakaraNAcca saMshayAnupapatteH | yathA pituH piteti prayoge, anyaH pitA ShaShThInirdiShTAt, prathamAnirdiShTaH, pituH pitA iti gamyate | tadvat prANasya prANam iti shabdabhedAt prasiddhAt prANAt anyaH prANasya prANa iti nishcIyate | na hi sa eva tasyeti bhedanirdeshArho bhavati | yasya ca prakaraNe yo nirdishyate nAmAntareNApi sa eva tatra prakaraNI nirdiShTa iti gamyate | yathA jyotiShTomAdhikAre vasante vasante jyotiShA yajeta ityatra jyotiHshabdo jyotiShTomaviShayo bhavati, tathA parasya brahmaNaH prakaraNe prANabandhanaM hi somya manaH iti shrutaH prANashabdo vAyuvikAramAtraM katham avagamayet | ataH saMshayAviShayatvAn naitad udAharaNaM yuktam | prastAvadevatAyAM tu prANe saMshayapUrvapakShanirNayA upapAditAH ||23||

 -- o)0(o -- 

jyotishcaraNAdhikaraNam 

|| 1.1.24 ||

idam Amananti -- 

atha yad ataH paro divo jyotir dIpyate, vishvataH pR^iShTheShu sarvataH pR^iShTheShvanuttameShUttameShu lokeShvidaM vAva tad yad idam asmin nantaH puruShe jyotiH [chA.u. 3.13.7] iti | 

tatra saMshayaH -- kim iha jyotiHshabdenAdityAdikaM jyotir abhidhIyate, kiM vA para AtmA? iti | arthAntaraviShayasyApi prANashabdasya talliN^gAd brahmaviShayatvam uktam | iha tu talliN^gam evAsti nAstIti vicAryate | kiM tAvat prAptam? AdityAdikam eva jyotiHshabdena parigR^ihyata iti | kutaH? prasiddhiH | tamo jyotiH iti hImau shabdau parasparapratidvandviviShayau prasiddhau | cakShurvR^itter nirodhakaM shArvarAdikaM tama ucyate | tasyA evAnugrAhakam AdityAdikaM jyotiH | tathA dIpyate itIyam api shrutir AdityAdiviShayA prasiddhA | na hi rUpAdihInaM brahma dIpyata iti mukhyAM shrutim arhati | dyumaryAdatvashruteshca | na hi carAcarabIjasya brahmaNaH sarvAtmakasya dyaurmaryAdA yuktA | kAryasya tu jyotiShaH paricchinnasya dyaur maryAdA syAt | paro divo jyotiH iti ca brAhmaNam | 

nanu kAryasyApi jyotiShaH sarvatra gamyamAnatvAd dyumaryAdAvattvam asamaJNjasam | astu tarhyatrivR^itkR^itaM tejaH prathamajam | na, atrivR^itkR^itasya tejasaH prayojanAbhAvAd iti | idam eva prayojanaM yad upAsyatvam iti cet, na | prayojanAntaraprayuktasyaivAdityAder upAsyatvadarshanAt, tAsAM trivR^itaM trivR^itam ekaikAM karavANi iti cAvisheShashruteH | na cAtrivR^itkR^itasyApi tejaso dyumaryAdatvaM prasiddham | astu tarhi trivR^itkR^itam eva tat tejo jyotiHshabdam | 

nanUktam arvAg api divo.avagamyate.agnyAdikaM jyotiH iti | naiSha doShaH | sarvatrApi gamyamAnasya jyotiShaH paro divaH ityupAsanArthaH pradeshavisheShaparigraho na virudhyate | na tu niShpradeshasyApi brahmaNaH pradeshavisheShakalpanA bhAginI | sarvataH pR^iShTheShvanuttameShUttameShu lokeShu iti cAdhArabahutvashrutiH kArye jyotiShyupapadyatetarAm | idaM vAva tadyad idam asmin nantaH puruShe jyotiH iti ca kaukSheye jyotiShi paraM jyotiradhyasyamAnaM dR^ishyate | sArUpyanimittAshcAdhyAsA bhavanti -- yathA tasya bhUH iti shira ekaM hi shira ekam etadakSharam iti | kaukSheyasya tu jyotiShaH prasiddhamabrahmatvam | tasyaiShA dR^iShTiH tasyaiShA shrutiH iti cauShNyaghoShavishiShTatvasya shravaNAt | tadetaddR^iShTAM ca shrutaM cetyupAsIta iti ca shruteH | cakShuShyashca shruto bhavati ya evaM veda iti cAlpaphalashravaNAdabrahmatvam | mahate hi phalAya brahmopAsanamiShyate | na cAnyadapi kiMcitsvavAkye prANAkAshavajjyotiSho.asti brahmatvaliN^gam | na ca pUrvasminn api vAkye brahma nirdiShTam asti, gAyatrI vA idaM sarvaM bhUtam iti cchandonirdeshAt | athApi kathaMcitpUrvasmin vAkye brahma nirdiShTaM syAt, evam api na tasyeha pratyabhij~nAnam asti | tatra hi tripAdasyAmR^itaM divi iti dyauradhikaraNatvena shrUyate | atra punaH paro divo 
jyotiH iti dyaurmaryAdAtvena tasmAt prAkR^itaM jyotiriha grAhyam ityevaM prApte -- 

jyotishcaraNAbhidhAnAt ||

brUmaH -- jyotiriha brahma grAhyam | kutaH? caraNAbhidhAnAt, pAdAbhidhAnAdityarthaH | pUrvasmin hi vAkye catuShpAdbrahma nirdiShTam -- tAvAnasya mahimA tato jyAyAM shca puruShaH | pAdo.asya sarvA bhUtAni tripAdasyAmR^itaM divi ityanena mantreNa | tatra yaccatuShpado brahmaNastirapAdamR^itaM dyusambandhirUpaM nirdiShTam, tad eveha dyusambandhAnnirdiShTam iti pratyabhij~nAyate | tatparityajya prAkR^itaM jyotiH kalpayataH prakR^itahAnAprakR^itaprakriye prasajyeyAtAm | na kevalaM jyotirvAkya eva brahmAnuvR^ittiH | parasyAm api hi shANDilyavidyAyAmanuvartiShyate brahma | tasmAd iha jyotiH iti brahma pratipattavyam | yat tUktam -- jyotir dIpyate iti caitau shabdau kArye jyotiShi prasiddhAviti, nAyaM doShaH | prakaraNAdbrahmAvagame satyanayoH shabdayor avisheShakatvAt, dIpyamAnakAryajyotirupalakShite brahmaNyapi prayogasambhavAt | yena sUryastapati tejaseddhaH iti ca mantravarNAt | yad vA, nAyaM jyotiHshabdashcakShurvR^itterevAnugrAhake tejasi vartate, anyatrApi prayogadarshanAt -- vAcaivAyaM jyotiShAste mano jyotirjuShatAm iti ca | tasmAd yadyatkasyacidavabhAsakaM tattajjyotiHshabdenAbhidhIyate | tathA sati brahmaNo.api caitanyarUpasya samastajagadavabhAsahetutvAd upapanno jyotiHshabdaH | 

tam eva bhAntam anubhAti sarvaM 
tasya bhAsA sarvam idaM vibhAti |
tad devA jyotiShAM jyotir 
Ayur hopAsate.amR^itam || ityAdishrutibhyashca | 

yad apyuktaM dyumaryAdatvaM sarvagatasya brahmaNo nopapadyata iti, atrocyate -- sarvagatasyApi brahmaNa upAsanArthaH pradeshavisheShaparigraho na virudhyate | nanUktaM niShpradeshasya brahmaNaH pradeshavisheShakalpanA nopapadyata iti | nAyaM doShaH, niShpradeshasyApi brahmaNa upAdhivisheShasambandhAt pradeshavisheShakalpanopapatteH | tathA hi -- Aditye, cakShuShi, hR^idaye iti pradeshavisheShasambandhIni brahmaNaH upAsanAni shrUyante | etena vishvataH pR^iShTheShu ityAdhArabahutvam upapAditam | yad apyetad uktam auShNyaghoShAbhyAmanumite kaukSheye kArye jyotiShyadhyasyamAnatvAt param api divaH kAryajyotireveti, tadapyayuktam | parasyApi brahmaNo nAmAdipratIkatvavatkaukSheyajyotiShpratIkatvopapatteH | dR^iShTaM ca shrutaM cetyupAsIta iti tu pratIkadvArakaM dR^iShTatvaM shrutatvaM ca bhaviShyati | yad apyuktamalpaphalashravaNAcca na brahmeti, tadanupapannam | na hi iyate phalAya brahmAshrayaNIyam, iyate na iti niyame hetur asti | yatra hi nirastasarvavisheShasambandhaM paraM brahmAtmatvenopadishyate, tatraikarUpam eva phalaM mokSha ityavagamyate | yatra tu guNavisheShasambandhaM pratIkavisheShasambandhaM vA brahmopadishyate, tatra saMsAragocarANyevoccAvacAni phalAni dR^ishyante -- annAdo vasudAno vindate vasu ya evaM veda ityAdyAsu shrutiShu | yadyapi na svavAkye kiMcijjyotiSho brahmatvaliN^gam asti, tathApi pUrvasmin vAkye dR^ishyamAnaM grahItavyaM bhavati | tad uktaM sUtrakAreNa -- jyotishcaraNAbhidhAnAd iti | kathaM punar vAkyAntaragatena brahmasaMnidhAnena jyotiHshrutiH svaviShayAt shakyA pracyAvayitum? naiSha doShaH, atha yadataH paro divo jyotiH iti prathamatarapaThitena yacchabdena sarvanAmnA dyusambandhAt pratyabhij~nAyamAne pUrvavAkyanirdiShTo brahmaNi svasAmarthyena parAmR^iShTo satyarthAjjyotiHshabdasyApi brahmaviShayatvopapatteH | tasmAd iha jyotiH iti brahma pratipattavyam ||

|| 1.1.25 ||

chando.abhidhAnAnneti cenna tathA ceto.arpaNanigadAttathA hi darshanam ||

atha yad uktaM pUrvasminn api vAkye na brahmAbhihitam asti, gAyatrI vA idaM sarvaM bhUtaM yad idaM kiM ca [chA.u. 3.12.1] iti gAyatryAkhyasya cchandaso.abhihitatvAd iti | tat parihartavyam | kathaM punashchando.abhidhAnAn na brahmAbhihitam iti shakyate vaktum? yAvatA tAvAn asya mahimA ityetasyAm R^ici catuShpAdbrahma darshitam | naitad asti | gAyatrI vA idaM sarvam iti gAyatrIm upakramya, tAm eva bhUtapR^ithivIsharIrahR^idayavAkprANaprabhedair vyAkhyAya, saiShA catuShpadA ShaDvidhA gAyatrI tad etad R^icAbhyanUktaM tAvAn asya mahimA iti tasyAm eva vyAkhyAtarUpAyAM gAyatryAm udAhR^ito mantraH katham akasmAd brahma catuShpAd abhidadhyAt | yo.api tatra yad vai tad brahma [chA.u. 3.12.5,6] iti brahmashabdaH, so.api cchandasaH prakR^itatvAcchandoviShaya eva | ya etAm evaM brahmopaniShadaM veda [chA.u. 3.11.3] ityatra hi vedopaniShadam iti vyAcakShate | tasmAcchando.abhidhAnAn na brahmaNaH prakR^itatvam iti cet, naiSha doShaH | 

tathA ceto.arpaNanigadAt -- tathA gAyatryAkhyacchandodvAreNa, tadanugate brahmaNi cetaso.arpaNaM cittasamAdhAnam anena brAhmaNavAkyena nigadyate -- gAyatrI vA idaM sarvam iti | na hyakSharasaMniveshamAtrAyA gAyatryAH sarvAtmakatvaM sambhavati | tasmAd yad gAyatryAkhyavikAre.anugataM jagatkAraNaM brahma nirdiShTam, tad iha sarvam ityucyate, yathA sarvaM khalvidaM brahma [chA.u. 3.14.1] iti | kAryaM ca kAraNAd avyatiriktam iti vakShyAmaH -- tad ananyatvam ArambhaNashabdAdibhyaH ityatra | tathAnyatrApi vikAradvAreNa brahmaNa upAsanaM dR^ishyate -- etaM hyeva bahvR^icA mahatyukthe mImAMsanta etam agnAvadhvaryava etaM mahAvrate cchandogAH iti | tasmAd asti cchando.abhidhAne.api pUrvasmin vAkye catuShpAd brahma nirdiShTam | tad eva jyotirvAkye.api parAmR^ishyata upAsanAntaravidhAnAya | apara Aha | sAkShAd eva gAyatrIshabdena brahma pratipAdyate, saMkhyAsAmAnyAt | yathA gAyatrI catuShpadA ShaDakSharaiH pAdaiH, tathA brahma catuShpAt | tathAnyatrApi cchando.abhidhAyI shabdo.arthAntare saMkhyAsAmAnyAt prayujyamAno dR^ishyate | tad yathA -- te vA ete paJNcAnye paJNcAnye dasha santaH tatkR^itam ityupakramyAha saiShA virAD annAdI iti | asmin pakShe brahmaivAbhihitam iti na cchando.abhidhAnam | sarvathApyasti pUrvasmin vAkye prakR^itaM brahma iti ||25||

|| 1.1.26 ||

bhUtAdipAdavyapadeshopapatteshcaivam || 

itashcaivam abhyupagantavyam asti pUrvasmin vAkye prakR^itaM brahmeti | yato bhUtAdIn pAdAn vyapadishati shrutiH | bhUtapR^ithivI sharIrahR^idayAni hi nirdishyAha -- saiShA catuShpadA ShaDvidhA gAyatrI iti | na hi brahmAnAshrayaNe kevalasya cchandaso bhUtAdayaH pAdA upapadyante | api ca brahmAnAshrayaNe neyam R^ik sambadhyeta --  tAvAn asya mahimA iti | anayA hi R^icA svarasena brahmaivAbhidhIyate, pAdo.asya sarvabhUtAni tripAdasyAmR^itaM divi iti sarvAtmatvopapatteH | puruShasUkte.apIyam R^ik brahmaparatayaiva samAmnAyate | smR^itishca brahmaNa evaMrUpatAM darshayati --  viShTabhyAham idaM kR^itsnam ekAMshena sthito jagat iti | yad vai tad brahma iti ca nirdeshaH | evaM sati mukhyArtha upapadyate | te vA ete paJNca brahmapuruShAH iti ca hR^idayasuShiShu brahmapuruShashrutir brahmasambandhitAyAM vivakShitAyAM sambhavati | tasmAd asti pUrvasmin vAkye brahma prakR^itam | tad eva brahma jyotir vAkye dyusambandhAt pratyabhij~nAyamAnaM parAmR^ishyata iti sthitam ||26||

|| 1.1.27 ||

upadeshabhedAn neti cen nobhayasminn apyavirodhAt ||

yad apyetad uktam -- pUrvatra tripAdasyAmR^itaM divIti saptamyA dyaur AdhAratvenopadiShTa | iha punar atha yad ataH paro divaH [chA.u. 3.12.6] iti paJNcamyA maryAdAtvena | tasmAd upadeshabhedAn na tasyeha pratyabhij~nAnam astIti -- tat parihartavyam | atrocyate -- nAyaM doShaH, ubhayasminn apyavirodhAt | ubhayasminn api saptamyante paJNcamyante copadeshe na pratyabhij~nAnaM virudhyate | yathA loke vR^ikShAgreNa sambaddho.api shyena ubhayathopadishyamAno dR^ishyate -- vR^ikShAgre shyeno vR^ikShAgrAt parataH shyena iti ca, evaM divyeva sad brahma divaH param ityupadishyate | apara Aha -- yathA loke vR^ikShAgreNAsambaddho.api shyena ubhayathopadishyamAno dR^ishyate -- vR^ikShAgre shyeno vR^ikShAgrAt parataH shyena iti ca, evaM divaH param api sad brahma divItyupadishyate | tasmAd asti pUrvanirdiShTasya brahmaNa iha pratyabhij~nAnam | ataH param eva brahma jyotiHshabdam iti siddham ||

11. prAtardanAdhikaraNam 

|| 1.1.28 || 

asti kauShItakibrAhmaNopaniShadIndrapratardanAkhyAyikA -- pratardano ha vai daivodAsirindrasya priyaM dhAmopajagAma yuddhena ca pauruSheNa ca ityArabhyAmnAtA | tasyAM shrUyate -- sa hovAca prANo.asmi praj~nAtmA taM mAmAyur amR^itam ityupAssva [kau.brA. 3.2] iti | tathottaratrApi -- atha khalu prANa eva praj~nAtmedaM sharIraM parigR^ihyotthApayati [kau.brA. 3.9] iti | tathA na vAcaM vijij~nAsIta vaktAraM vidyAt iti | ante ca, sa eSha prANa eva praj~nAtmAnando.ajaro.amR^itaH ityAdi | 

tatra saMshayaH -- kim iha prANashabdena vAyumAtram abhidhIyate, uta devatAtmA, uta jIvaH, athavA paraM brahmeti ? 

nanu ata eva prANaH ityatra varNitaM prANashabdasya brahmaparatvam | ihApi ca brahmaliN^gam asti -- Anando.ajaro.amR^itaH ityAdi | katham iha punaH saMshayaH sambhavati? -- anekaliN^gadarshanAd iti brUmaH | na kevalam iha brahmaliN^gam evopalabhyate | santi hItaraliN^gAnyapi -- mAm eva vijAnIhi itIndrasya vacanaM devatAtmaliN^gam | idaM sharIraM parigR^ihyotthApayati iti prANaliN^gam | na vAcaM vijij~nAsIta vaktAraM vidyAt ityAdi jIvaliN^gam | ata upapannaH saMshayaH | tatra prasiddhervAyuH prANa iti prApte -- 

prANaH tathA.anugamAt || 

idam ucyate -- prANashabdaM brahma vij~neyam | kutaH? tathAnugamAt | tathA hi paurvAparyeNa paryAlocyamAne vAkye padAnAM samanvayo brahmapratipAdanapara upalabhyate | upakrame, tAvat varaM vR^iNIShva itIndreNoktaH pratardanaH paramaM puruShArthaM varam upacikShepa -- tvam eva me varaM vR^iNIShva yaM tvaM manuShyAya hitatamaM manyase iti | tasmai hitatamatvenopadishyamAnaH prANaH kathaM paramAtmA na syAt | na hyanyatra paramAtmavij~nAnAd dhitatamaprAptir asti, tam eva viditvAt imR^ityum eti nAnyaH panthA vidyate.ayanAya [shve.u. 3.8] ityAdishrutibhyaH | tathA sa yo mAM veda na ha vai tasya kenacana karmaNA loko mIyate na steyena na bhrUNahatyayA ityAdi ca brahmaparigrahe ghaTate | brahmavij~nAnena hi sarvakarmakShayaH prasiddhaH -- kShIyante cAsya karmANi tasmin dR^iShTo parAvare ityAdyAsu shrutiShu | praj~nAtmatvaM ca brahmapakSha evopapadyate | na hyacetanasya vAyoH praj~nAtmatvaM sambhavati | tathopasaMhAre.api Anando.ajaro.amR^itaH ityAnandatvAdIni ca na brahmaNo.anyatra samyak sambhavanti | sa na sAdhunA karmaNA bhUyAn bhavati no evAsAdhunA karmaNA kanIyAn eSha hyeva sAdhu karma kArayati taM yam ebhyo lokebhya unninIShate | eSha u evAsAdhu karma kArayati taM yamebhyo lokebhyo.adho ninIShate iti, eSha lokAdhipatir eSha lokapAla eSha lokeshaH [kau.u. 3.8] iti ca | sarvam etat parasmin brahmaNyAshrIyamANe.anugantuM shakyate, na mukhye prANe | tasmAt prANo brahma ||28||

|| 1.1.29 ||

na vaktur AtmopadeshAd iti ced 
adhyAtmasambandhabhUmA hyasmin || 

yad uktaM prANo brahmeti, tad AkShipyate -- na paraM brahma prANashabdam | kasmAt? vaktur AtmopadeshAt | vaktA hIndro nAma kashcid vigrahavAn devatAvisheShaH svamAtmAnaM pratardanAyAcacakShe -- mAm eva vijAnIhi ityupakramya prANo.asmi praj~nAtmA ityahaMkAravAdena | sa eva vaktur AtmatvenopadishyamAnaH prANaH kathaM brahma syAt? na hi brahmaNo vaktR^itvaM sambhavati, avAgamanAH ityAdishrutibhyaH | tathA vigrahasambandhibhir eva brahmaNyasambhavadbhir dharmaiH indra AtmAnaM tuShTAva -- trishIrShANaM tvAShTram ahanamarunmukhAn R^iShIn shAlAvR^ikebhyaH prAyaccham ityevam AdibhiH | prANatvaM cendrasya balavattvAd upapadyate | prANo vai balam [bR^i.A.u. 4.14.4] iti hi vij~nAyate | balasya cendro devatA prasiddhA | yA ca kAcid balaprakR^itiH, indrasya karmaiva tad iti hi vadanti | 
praj~nAtmatvam apyapratihataj~nAnatvAd devatAtmanaH sambhavati | apratihataj~nAnA devatA iti hi vadanti | nishcite caivaM devatAtmopadeshe hitatamatvAdivacanAni yathAsambhavaM tadviShayANyeva yojayitavyAni | tasmAd vaktuH indrasyAtmopadeshAt na prANo brahmetyAkShipya pratisamAdhIyate -- adhyAtmasambandhabhUmA hyasmin iti | adhyAtmasambandhaH pratyagAtmasambandhaH, tasya bhUmA bAhulyam, asminn adhyAye upalabhyate | yAvad dhyasmiJNsharIre prANo vasati tAvad AyuH [kau.u. 2.2] iti prANasyaiva praj~nAtmanaH pratyagbhUtasyAyuShpradAnopasaMhArayoH svAtantryaM darshayati, na devatAvisheShasya parAcInasya | tathAstitve ca prANAnAM niHshreyasam ityadhyAtmam evendriyAshrayaM prANaM darshayati | tathA prANa eva praj~nAtmedaM sharIraM parigR^ihyotthApayati iti | na vAcaM vijij~nAsIta vaktAraM vidyAt iti copakramya, tad yathA rathasyAreShu nemir arpitA nAbhAvarA arpitA evam evaitA bhUtamAtrAH praj~nAmAtrAsvarpitAH praj~nAmAtrAH prANe.arpitAH, sa eSha prANa eva praj~nAtmAnando.ajaro.amR^itaH iti viShayendriyavyavahArAranAbhibhUtaM pratyagAtmAnam evopasaMharati | sa ma Atmeti vidyAt iti copasaMhAraH pratyagAtmaparigrahe sAdhuH, na parAcInaparigrahe | ayam AtmA brahma sarvAnubhUH [bR^i.A.u. 2.5.19] iti ca shrutyantaram | tasmAd adhyAtmasambandhabAhulyAd brahmopadesha evAyam, na devatAtmopadeshaH || 

|| 1.1.30 ||

kathaM tarhi vaktur AtmopadeshaH? -- 

shAstradR^iShTyA tUpadesho vAmadevavat ||

indro nAma devatAtmA svam AtmAnaM paramAtmatvena aham eva paraM brahma ityArSheNa darshanena yathAshAstraM pashyan upadishati sma -- mAm eva vijAnIhi iti | yathA -- tad dhaitat pashyann R^iShir vAmadevaH pratipede.ahaM manur abhavaM sUryashca [bR^i.A.u. 1.4.10] iti, tadvat | tad yo yo devAnAM pratyabudhyata sa eva tad abhavat iti shruteH | yat punar uktam -- mAm eva vijAnIhi ityuktvA, vigrahacarmaiH indraH svam AtmAnaM tuShTAva tvAShTarvadhAdibhiH iti, tat parihartavyam | atrocyate -- na tAvat tvAShTarvadhAdInAM vij~neyendrastutyarthatvena upanyAsaH -- yasmAd evaM karmAham, tasmAn mAM vijAnIhi iti | kathaM tarhi? vij~nAnastutyarthatvena | yat kAraNaM tvAShTar vadhAdIni sAhasAnyupanyasya pareNa -- vij~nAnastutim anusandadhAti -- tasya me tatra loma ca na mIyate sa yo mAM veda na ha vai tasya kena ca karmaNA loke mIyate ityAdinA | 

etad uktaM bhavati -- yasmAd IdR^ishAnyapi krUrANi karmANi kR^itavato mama brahmabhUtasya lomApi na hiMsyate, sa yo.anyo.api mAM veda, na tasya kenacid api karmaNA loko hiMsyata iti | vij~neyaM tu brahmaiva prANo.asmi praj~nAtmA iti vakShyamANam | tasmAd brahmavAkyam etat ||30||

 -- o)0(o -- 

|| 1.1.31 || 

jIvamukhyaprANaliN^gAn neti cen, na,
upAsAtraividhyAd AshritatvAd iha tadyogAt || 

yadyapyadhyAtmasambandhabhUmadarshanAn na parAcInasya devatAtmana upadeshaH, tathApi na brahmavAkyaM bhavitum arhati | kutaH? jIvaliN^gAt mukhyaprANaliN^gAcca | jIvasya tAvad asmin vAkye vispaShTaM liN^gam upalabhyate -- na vAcaM vijij~nAsIta vaktAraM vidyAt [kau.u. 3.8] ityAdi | atra hi vAgAdibhiH karaNair vyApR^itasya kAryakaraNAdhyakShasya jIvasya vij~neyatvam abhidhIyate | 

tathA mukhyaprANaliN^gam api -- atha khalu prANa eva praj~nAtmedaM sharIraM parigR^ihyotthApayati iti | sharIradhAraNaM ca mukhyaprANasya dharmaH | prANasaMvAde vAgAdIn prANAn prakR^itya -- tAn variShThaH prANa uvAca mA moham Apad yathAham evaitat paJNcadhAtmAnaM pravibhajyaitad bANam avaShTabhya vidhArayAmi [pra.u. 2.3] iti shravaNAt | ye tu imaM sharIraM parigR^ihya iti paThanti, teShAm imaM jIvam indriyagrAmaM vA parigR^ihya sharIram utthApayatIti vyAkhyeyam | praj~nAtmatvam api jIve tAvaccetanatvAd upapannam | mukhye.api prANe praj~nAsAdhanaprANAntarAshrayatvAd upapannam eva | evaM jIvamukhyaprANaparigrahe ca, prANapraj~nAtmanoH sahavR^ittitvenAbhedanirdeshaH, svarUpeNa ca bhedanirdeshaH, ityubhayathApi nirdesha upapadyate -- yo vai prANaH sA praj~nA yA vai praj~nA sa prANaH saha hyetAvasmiJNsharIre vasataH sahotkrAmataH iti | 

brahmaparigrahe tu kiM kasmAd bhidyeta ? tasmAd iha jIvamukhyaprANayor anyatara ubhau vA pratIyeyAtAM na brahmeti cet, naitad evam | upAsAtraividhyAt | evaM sati trividham upAsanaM prasajyeta -- jIvopAsanaM mukhyaprANopAsanaM brahmopAsanaM ceti | na caitad ekasmin vAkye.abhyupagantuM yuktam | upakramopasaMhArAbhyAM hi vAkyaikavAkyatvam avagamyate | mAm eva vijAnIhi ityupakramya, prANo.asmi praj~nAtmA taM mamAyur amR^itam ityupAssva ityuktvA, ante sa eSha prANa eva praj~nAtmAnando.ajaro.amR^itaH ityekarUpAv upakramopasaMhArau dR^ishyete | tatrArthaikatvaM yuktam Ashrayitum | na ca brahmaliN^gam anyaparatvena pariNetuM shakyam | dashAnAM bhUtamAtrANAM praj~nAmAtrANAM ca brahmaNo.anyatra arpaNAnupapatteH | AshritatvAcca anyatrApi brahmaliN^gavashAt prANashabdasya brahmaNi pravR^itteH, ihApi ca hitatamopanyAsAdibrahmaliN^gayogAt, brahmopadesha evAyam iti gamyate | 

yat tu mukhyaprANaliN^gaM darshitam -- idaM sharIraM parigR^ihyotthApayati iti, tad asat | prANavyApArasyApi paramAtmAyattatvAt paramAtmanyupacarituM shakyatvAt  -- 

na prANena nApAnena martyo jIvati kashcana | 
itareNa tu jIvanti yasminn etAv upAshritau || [ka.u. 2.2.5] iti shruteH | 

yad api na vAcaM vijij~nAsIta vaktAraM vidyAt ityAdi jIvaliN^gaM darshitam, tad api na brahmapakShaM nivArayati | na hi jIvo nAmAtyantabhinno brahmaNaH, tattvam asi, ahaM brahmAsmi [bR^i.A.u. 1.4.10] ityAdishrutibhyaH | buddhyAdyupAdhikR^itaM tu visheSham Ashritya brahmaiva san jIvaH kartA bhoktA cetyucyate | tasyopAdhikR^itavisheShaparityAgena svarUpaM brahma darshayitum na vAcaM vijij~nAsIta vaktAraM vidyAt ityAdinA pratyagAtmAbhimukhIkaraNArtha upadesho na virudhyate | yadvAcAnabhyuditaM yena vAg abhyudyate | tad eva brahma tvaM viddhi nedaM yad idam upAsate ityAdi ca shrutyantaraM vacanAdikriyAvyApR^itasyaivAtmano brahmatvaM darshayati | yat punar etad uktam -- saha hyetAvasmiJNsharIre vasataH sahotkrAmataH iti prANapraj~nAtmanor bhedadarshanaM brahmavAdino nopapadyata iti, naiSha doShaH | j~nAnakriyAshaktidvayAshrayayor buddhiprANayoH pratyagAtmopAdhibhUtayor bhedanirdeshopapatteH | upAdhidvayopahitasya tu pratyagAtmanaH svarUpeNAbheda ityataH prANa eva praj~nAtmA ityekIkaraNam aviruddham || 

athavA nopAsAtraividhyAd AshritatvAd iha tadyogAt ityasyAyam anyo.arthaH -- na brahmavAkye.api jIvamukhyaprANaliN^gaM virudhyate | katham? upAsAtraividhyAt | trividham iha brahmaNa upAsanaM vivakShitam -- prANadharmeNa, praj~nAdharmeNa, svadharmeNa ca | tatra Ayur amR^itam ityupAssvAyuH prANaH iti, idaM sharIraM parigR^ihyotthApayati iti tasmAd etad evoktham upAsIta iti ca prANadharmaH | atha yathAsyai praj~nAyai sarvANi bhUtAnyekIbhavanti tad vyAkhyAsyAmaH ityupakramya vAg evAsyA ekam aN^gam adUduhat tasyai nAma parastAt prativihitA bhUtamAtrA praj~nayA vAcaM samAruhya vAcA sarvANi nAmAnyApnoti ityAdiH praj~nAdharmaH | tA vA etA dashaiva bhUtamAtrA adhipraj~naM dasha praj~nAmAtrA adhibhUtam | yadi bhUtamAtrA na syur na praj~nAmAtrAH syuH | yadi praj~nAmAtrA na syur na bhUtamAtrAH syuH | na hyanyatarato rUpaM kiMcana sidhyet | no etan nAnA | tad yathA rathasyAreShu nemir arpitA nAbhAvarA arpitA evam evaitA bhUtamAtrAH praj~nAmAtrAsvarpitAH praj~nAmAtrAH prANe.arpitAH sa eSha prANa eva praj~nAtmA ityAdir brahmadharmaH | tasmAd brahmaNa evaitad upAdhidvayadharmeNa svadharmeNa caikam upAsanaM trividhaM vivakShitam | anyatrApi manomayaH prANasharIraH [chA.u. 3.14.2] ityAdAv upAdhidharmeNa brahmaNa upAsanamAshritam | ihApi tadyujyate vAkyasyopakramopasaMhArAbhyAm ekArthatvAvagamAt prANapraj~nAtmabrahmaliN^gAvagamAcca | tasmAd brahmavAkyam evaitad iti siddham ||31||

iti shrImatparamahaMsaparivrAjakAcAryasya shrIgovindabhagavatpUjyapAdashiShyasya shrImacchaN^karabhagavataH kR^itau shArIrakamImAMsAsUtrabhAShye 
prathamAdhyAyasya prathamaH pAdaH ||

(1.2)
|| prathame.adhyAye dvitIyaH pAdaH || 

atrAspaShTabrahmaliN^gayuktavAkyAnAm upAsyabrahmaviShayANAM vicAraH ||

1. sarvatraprasiddhyadhikaraNam 

|| 1.2.1 ||

prathame pAde janmAdyasya yataH ityAkAshAdeH samastasya jagato janmAdikAraNaM brahmetyuktam | tasya samastajagatkAraNasya brahmaNo vyApitvaM, nityatvaM, sarvaj~natvaM, sarvashaktitvaM, sarvAtmatvaM ityevaMjAtIyakA dharmA uktA eva bhavanti | arthAntaraprasiddhAnAM ca keShAMcicchabdAnAM brahmaviShayatvahetupratipAdanena kAnicid vAkyAni spaShTabrahmaliN^gAni sandihyamAnAni brahmaparatayA nirNItAni | punar apyanyAni vAkyAnyaspaShTabrahmaliN^gAni sandihyante -- kiM param brahma pratipAdayantyAho svid arthAntaraM kiJNcid iti | tannirNayAya dvitIyatR^itIyau pAdAvarabhyete |

idam AmnAyate -- 

sarvaM khalvidaM brahma tajjalAn iti shAnta upAsIta | atha khalu kratumayaH puruSho yathA kratur asmiMl loke puruSho bhavati tathetaH pretya bhavati sa kratuH kurvIta | manomayaH prANasharIraH [chA.u. 3.14.12] ityAdi |

tatra saMshayaH -- kim iha manomayatvAdibhir dharmaiH shArIra AtmopAsyatvenopadishyate, Aho svit paraM brahmeti ? kiM tAvat prAptam? shArIra iti | kutaH? tasya hi kAryakaraNAdhipateH prasiddho manaAdibhiH sambandhaH, na parasya brahmaNaH | aprANo hyamanAH shubhraH [mu.u. 2.1.2] ityAdi shrutibhyaH | 

nanu sarvaM khalvidaM brahma [chA.u. 3.14.1] iti svashabdenaiva brahmopAttam | katham iha shArIra AtmopAsyatvenAshaN^kyate? naiSha doShaH | nedaM vAkyaM brahmopAsanavidhiparam | kiM tarhi? shamavidhiparam | yat kAraNam sarvaM khalvidaM brahma tajjalAn iti shAnta upAsIta [chA.u. 3.14.1] ityAha | etad uktaM bhavati -- yasmAt sarvam idaM vikArajAtaM brahmaiva, tajjatvAt tallatvAt tadanatvAcca -- na ca sarvasyaikAtmatve rAgAdayaH sambhavanti -- tasmAt shAnta upAsIteti | na ca shamavidhiparatve satyanena vAkyena brahmopAsanaM niyantuM shakyate | upAsanaM tu sa kratuM kurvIta ityanena vidhIyate | kratuH saN^kalpo dhyAnam ityarthaH | tasya ca viShayatvena shrUyate -- manomayaH prANasharIraH [chA.u. 3.14.2] iti jIvaliN^gam | 

ato brUmaH -- jIvaviShayam etadupAsanam iti | sarvakarmA sarvakAmaH ityAdyapi shrUyamANaM paryAyeNa jIvaviShayam upapadyate | eSha ma AtmAntarhR^idaye.aNIyAn vrIher vA yavAd vA [chA.u. 3.14.3] iti ca hR^idayAyatanatvam aNIyastvaM cArAgramAtrasya jIvasyAvakalpate, nAparicchinnasya brahmaNaH | 

nanu jyAyAn pR^ithivyAH ityAdyapi na paricchinne.avakalpata iti | atra brUmaH -- na tAvad aNIyastvaM jyAyastvaM cobhayam ekasmin samAshrayituM shakyam, virodhAt | anyatarAshrayaNe ca, prathamashrutatvAd aNIyastvaM yuktam Ashrayitum | jyAyastvaM tu brahmabhAvApekShayA bhaviShyatIti | nishcite ca jIvaviShayatve yadante brahmasaN^kIrtanam -- etad brahma iti, tad api prakR^itaparAmarshArthatvAjjIvaviShayam eva | tasmAn manomayatvAdibhir dharmair java upAsyaH | ityevaM prApte brUmaH -- 

sarvatra prasiddhopadeshAt ||

param eva brahmeha manomayatvAdibhir dharmair upAsyam | kutaH? sarvatra prasiddhopadeshAt | yat sarveShu vedAnteShu prasiddhaM brahmashabdasyAlambanaM jagatkAraNam, iha ca sarvaM khalvidaM brahma [chA.u. 3.14.1] iti vAkyopakrame shrutam, tad eva manomayatvAdidharmair vishiShTam upadishyata iti yuktam | evaM ca sati prakR^itahAnAprakR^itaprakriye na bhaviShyataH | 

nanu vAkyopakrame shamavidhivivakShayA brahma nirdiShTaM na svavivakShayetyuktam | atrocyate -- yadyapi shamavidhivivakShayA brahma nirdiShTam, tathApi manomayatvAdiShUpadishyamAneShu tad eva brahma saMnihitaM bhavati, jIvaH tu na saMnihitaH, na ca svashabdenopAtta iti vaiShamyam ||1||

|| 1.2.2 ||

vivakShitaguNopapatteshca ||

vaktum iShTA vivakShitAH | yadyapyapauruSheye vede vaktur abhAvAt necchArthaH sambhavati, tathApyupAdAnena phalenopacaryate | loke.api yacchabdAbhihitam upAdeyaM bhavati tad vivakShitam ityucyate, yad anupAdeyaM tad avivakShitam iti | tadvad vede.apyupAdeyatvenAbhihitaM vivakShitaM bhavati, itarad avivakShitam | upAdAnAnupAdAne tu 
vedavAkyatAt paryAtAt paryAbhyAm avagamyete | tad iha ye vivakShitA guNA upAsanAyAm upAdeyatvenopadiShTAH satyasaN^kalpaprabhR^itayaH, te parasmin brahmaNyupapadyante | satyasaN^kalpatvaM hi sR^iShTisthitisaMhAreShvapratibaddhashaktitvAt paramAtmana evAvakalpate | paramAtmaguNatvena ca ya AtmApahatapApmA ityatra satyakAmaH satyasaN^kalpaH [chA.u. 8.7.1] iti shrutam, AkAshAtmA iti ca | AkAshavad AtmA asyetyarthaH | sarvagatatvAdibhir dharmaiH sambhavatyAkAshena sAmyaM brahmaNaH | jyAyAn pR^ithivyAH ityAdinA caitad eva darshayati | yad api AkAsha AtmA asyeti vyAkhyAyate, tad api sambhavati sarvajagatkAraNasya sarvAtmano brahmaNa AkAshAtmatvam | ata eva sarvakarmA ityAdi | evam ihopAsyatayA vivakShitA guNA brahmaNyupapadyante | yat tUktam -- manomayaH prANasharIraH [chA.u. 3.14.2] iti jIvaliN^gam, na tad brahmaNyupapadyata iti | tad api brahmaNyupapadyata iti brUmaH | sarvAtmatvAd dhi brahmaNo jIvasambandhIni manomayatvAdIni brahmasambandhIni bhavanti | tathA ca brahmaviShaye shrutismR^itI bhavataH --  

tvaM strI tvaM pumAn asi tvaM kumAra uta vA kumArI | 
tvaM jIrNo daNDo na vaJNcasi tvaM jAto bhavasi vishvatomukhaH || iti | 

sarvataH pANipAdaM tat sarvato.akShishiromukham | 
sarvataH shrutimal loke sarvam AvR^itya tiShThati || iti ca | 

aprANo hyamanAH shubhraH [mu.u. 2.1.2] iti shrutiH shuddhabrahmaviShayA, iyaM tu shrutiH manomayaH prANasharIraH [chA.u. 3.14.2] iti saguNabrahmaviShayeti visheShaH | ato vivakShitaguNopapatteH param eva brahma ihopAsyatvenopadiShTam iti gamyate ||

|| 1.2.3 ||

anupapatteH tu na shArIraH ||

pUrveNa sUtreNa brahmaNi vivakShitAnAM guNAnAm upapattir uktA | anena shArIre teShAm anupapattir ucyate | tushabdo.avadhAraNArthaH | brahmaivoktena nyAyena manomayatvAdiguNam | na tu shArIro jIvo manomayatvAdiguNaH | yat kAraNam --  satyasaN^kalpaH AkAshAtmA avAkI anAdaraH jyAyAn pR^ithivyAH [chA.u. 3.14.2] iti caivaMjAtIyakA guNA na shArIre AJNjasyenopapadyante | shArIra iti sharIre bhava ityarthaH | 

nanv Ishvaro.api sharIre bhavati | satyam, sharIre bhavati | na tu sharIra eva bhavati | jyAyAn pR^ithivyA jyAyAn antarikShAt AkAshavat sarvagatashca nityaH iti ca vyApitvashravaNAt | jIvaH tu sharIra eva bhavati, tasya bhogAdhiShThAnAccharIrAd anyatra vR^ittyabhAvAt ||3||

|| 1.2.4 ||

karmakartR^ivyapadeshAcca ||

itashca na shArIro manomayatvAdiguNaH | yasmAt karmakartR^ivyapadesho bhavati -- etam itaH pretyAbhisambhavitAsmi [chA.u. 3.14.4] iti | etam iti prakR^itaM manomayatvAdiguNam upAsyam AtmAnaM karmatvena prApyatvena vyapadishati | abhisambhavitAsmIti shArIram upAsakaM kartR^itvena prApakatvena | abhisambhavitAsmIti prAptAsmItyarthaH | na ca satyAM gatAv ekasya karmakartR^ivyapadesho yuktaH | tathopAsyopAsakabhAvo.api bhedAdhiShThAna eva | tasmAd api na shArIro manomayatvAdivishiShTaH ||4||

|| 1.2.5 ||

shabdavisheShAt ||

itashca shArIrAd anyo manomayatvAdiguNaH | yasmAcchabdavisheSho bhavati samAnaprakaraNe shrutyantare -- yathA vrIhir vA yavo vA shyAmAko vA shyAmAkataNDulo vaivam ayam antarAtman puruSho hiraNmayaH iti | shArIrasyAtmano yaH shabdo.abhidhAyakaH saptamyantaH --  antarAtmann iti | tasmAd vishiShTo.anyaH prathamAntaH puruShashabdo manomayatvAdivishiShTasyAtmano.abhidhAyakaH | tasmAt tayor bhedo.adhigamyate ||5||

|| 1.2.6 ||

smR^iteshca ||

smR^itishca shArIraparamAtmanor bhedaM darshayati --  

IshvaraH sarvabhUtAnAM hR^iddeshe.arjuna tiShThati | 
bhrAmayan sarvabhUtAni yantrArUDhAni mAyayA || [gItA 18.61] ityAdyA | 

atrAha -- kaH punar ayaM shArIro nAma paramAtmano.anyaH, yaH pratiShidhyate -- anupapatteH tu na shArIraH ityAdinA? shrutiH tu nAnyo.ato.asti draShTA nAnyo.ato.asti shrotA ityevaMjAtIyakA paramAtmano.anyam AtmAnaM vArayati | tathA smR^itir api kShetraj~naM cApi mAM viddhi sarvakShetreShu bhArata [gItA 13.2] ityevaMjAtIyaketi |

atrocyate --  satyam evaitat -- para evAtmA dehendriyamanobuddhyupAdhibhiH paricchidyamAno bAlaiH shArIra ityupacaryate | yathA ghaTakarakAdyupAdhivashAd aparicchinnam api nabhaH paricchinnavad avabhAsate, tadvat | tadapekShayA ca karmakartR^itvAdibhedavyavahAro na virudhyate prAk tattvam asi ityAtmaikatvopadeshagrahaNAt | gR^ihIte tvatmaikatve bandhamokShAdisarvavyavahAraparisamAptir eva syAt ||6||

|| 1.2.7 ||

arbhakaukastvAt tadvyapadeshAcca neti cet, na,
nicAyyatvAd evaM vyomavacca ||

arbhakam alpam oko nIDAm, eSha ma AtmAntarhR^idaye [chA.u. 3.14.3] iti paricchinnAyatanatvAt, svashabdena ca aNIyAn vrIher vA yavAd vA ityaNIyastvavyapadeshAt, shArIra evArAgramAtro jIva ihopadishyate, na sarvagataH paramAtmA -- iti yad uktaM tat parihartavyam | atrocyate -- nAyaM doShaH | na tAvat paricchinnadeshasya sarvagatatvavyapadeshaH katham apyupapadyate | sarvagatasya tu sarvadesheShu vidyamAnatvAt paricchinnadeshavyapadesho.api kayAcid apekShayA sambhavati | yathA samastavasudhAdhipatir api hi san ayodhyAdhipatiH iti vyapadishyate | kayA punar apekShayA sarvagataH sann Ishvaro.arbhakaukA aNIyAMshca vyapadishyata iti | nicAyyatvAd evam iti brUmaH | 

evam aNIyastvAdiguNagaNopeta IshvaraH, tatra hR^idayapuNDarIke, nicAyyo draShTavya upadishyate | yathA sAlagrAme hariH | tatrAsya buddhivij~nAnaM grAhakam | sarvagato.apIshvaraH tatropAsyamAnaH prasIdati | vyomavaccaitad draShTavyam | yathA sarvagatam api sad vyoma sUcIpAshAdyapekShayArbhakauko.aNIyashceti vyapadishyate, evaM brahmApi | tad evaM nicAyyatvApekShaM brahmaNo.arbhakaukastvam aNIyastvaM ca, na pAramArthikam | 
tatra yad AshaN^kyate -- hR^idayAyatanatvAd brahmaNo hR^idayAnAM ca pratisharIraM bhinnatvAd bhinnAyatanAnAM ca shukAdInAm anekatvasAvayavatvAnityatvAdidoShadarshanAd brahmaNo.api tadvat prasaN^ga iti, tad api parihR^itaM bhavati ||7||

|| 1.2.8 ||

sambhogaprAptiH iti cen, na, vaisheShyAt ||

vyomavat sarvagatasya brahmaNaH sarvaprANihR^idayasambandhAt, cidrUpatayA ca shArIrAd avishiShTatvAt, sukhaduHkhAdisambhogo.apyavishiShTaH prasajyeta | ekatvAcca -- na hi parasmAd Atmano.anyaH kashcid AtmA saMsArI vidyate, nAnyo.ato.asti vij~nAtA ityAdi shrutibhyaH | tasmAt parasyaiva brahmaNaH sambhogaprAptiH iti cet, na | vaisheShyAt | na tAvat sarvaprANihR^idayasambandhAt cidrUpatayA ca shArIravad brahmaNaH sambhogaprasaN^gaH, vaisheShyAt | visheSho hi bhavati shArIraparameshvarayoH | ekaH kartA bhoktA dharmAdharmAdisAdhanaH sukhaduHkhAdimAMshca | ekaH tadviparIto.apahatapApmatvAdiguNaH | etasmAd anayor visheShAd ekasya bhogaH, netarasya | yadi ca saMnidhAnamAtreNa vastushaktim anAshritya kAryasambandho.abhyupagamyeta, AkAshAdInAm api dAhAdiprasaN^gaH | sarvagatAn ekAtmavAdinAm api samAv etau codyaparihArau | 

yad apyekatvAd brahmaNa AtmAntarAbhAvAcchArIrasya bhogena brahmaNo bhogaprasaN^gaH iti, atra vadAmaH -- idaM tAvad devAnAM priyaH praShTavyaH -- katham ayaM tu ayAtmAntarAbhAvo.adhyavasita iti | tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7], ahaM brahmAsmi [bR^i.A.u. 1.4.10], nAnyo.ato.asti vij~nAtA ityAdishAstrebhya iti cet, yathAshAstraM tarhi shAstrIyo.arthaH pratipattavyaH, na tatrArdhajaratIyaM labhyam | shAstraM ca tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7] ityapahatapApmatvAdivisheShaNaM brahma shArIrasyAtmatvenopadishacchArIrasyaiva tAvad upabhoktR^itvaM vArayati | kutaH tadupabhogena brahmaNa upabhogaprasaN^gaH ? athAgR^ihItaM shArIrasya brahmaNaikatvam, tadA mithyAj~nAnanimittaH shArIrasyopabhogaH | na tena paramArtharUpasya brahmaNaH saMsparshaH | na hi bAlaiH tala -- malinatAdibhir vyomni vikalpyamAne talamalinatAdivishiShTam eva paramArthato vyoma bhavati | tad Aha -- na, vaisheShyAd iti | naikatve.api shArIrasyopabhogena brahmaNa upabhogaprasaN^gaH, vaisheShyAt | visheSho hi bhavati mithyAj~nAnasamyagj~nAnayoH | mithyAj~nAnakalpita upabhogaH, samyagj~nAnadR^iShTam ekatvam | na ca mithyAj~nAnakalpitenopabhogena samyagj~nAnadR^iShTaM vastu saMspR^ishyate | tasmAn nopabhogagandho.api shakya Ishvarasya kalpayitum ||8||
2. attAdhikaraNam

|| 1.2.9 ||


kaThavallIShu paThyate -- 

yasya brahma ca kShatraM cobhe bhavata odanaH | 
mR^ityur yasyopasecanaM ka itthA veda yatra saH || [ka.u. 1.2.25] iti | 

atra kashcid odanopasecanasUcito.attA pratIyate | tatra kim agnir attA syAt, uta jIvaH, athavA paramAtmA, iti saMshayaH | visheShAnavadhAraNAt, trayANAM cAgnijIvaparamAtmanAm asmin granthe prashnopanyAsopalabdheH | kiM tAvat prAptam? agnir atteti | kutaH? agnir annAdaH iti shrutiprasiddhibhyAm | jIvo vA attA syAt tayor anyaH pippalaM svAdvatti iti darshanAt | na paramAtmA, anashnann anyo.abhicAkashIti [mu.u. 3.1.1] iti darshanAd ityevaM prApte -- 

attA carAcaragrahaNAt ||

brUmaH -- attAtra paramAtmA bhavitum arhati | kutaH? carAcaragrahaNAt | carAcaraM hi sthAvarajaN^gamaM mR^ityUpasecanam ihAdyatvena pratIyate | tAdR^ishasya cAdyasya na paramAtmano.anyaH kArtsnyenAttA sambhavati | paramAtmA tu vikArajAtam upasaMharan sarvam attItyupapadyate | 

nanviha carAcaragrahaNaM nopalabhyate | kathaM siddhavaccarAcaragrahaNaM hetutvenopAdIyate? naiSha doShaH, mR^ityUpasecanatvenehAdyatvena sarvasya prANinikAyasya pratIyamAnatvAt, brahmakShatrayoshca prAdhAnyAt pradarshanArthatvopapatteH | yat tu paramAtmano.api nAttR^itvaM sambhavati, anashnann anyo.abhicAkashIti iti darshanAd iti | atrocyate -- karmaphalabhogasya pratiShedhakam etad darshanam, tasya saMnihitatvAt | na vikArasaMhArasya pratiShedhakam, sarvavedAnteShu sR^iShTisthitisaMhArakAraNatvena brahmaNaH prasiddhatvAt | tasmAt paramAtmaivehAttA bhavitum arhati ||9||

|| 1.2.10 || 

prakaraNAcca || 

itashca paramAtmaivehAttA bhavitum arhati | yat kAraNaM prakaraNam idaM paramAtmanaH -- na jAyate mriyate vA vipashcit [ka.u. 1.2.18] ityAdi | prakR^itagrahaNaM ca nyAyyam | ka itthA veda yatra saH iti ca durvij~nAnatvaM paramAtmaliN^gam ||10||

 -- o)0(o -- 

3. guhApraviShTAdhikaraNam 

|| 1.2.11 ||

kaThavallIShv eva paThante -- 

R^itaM pibantau sukR^itasya loke 
guhAM praviShTau parame parArdhe | 
chAyAtapau brahmavido vadanti 
paJNcAgnayo ye ca triNAciketAH || [ka.u. 1.3.1] iti | 

tatra saMshayaH -- kim iha buddhijIvau nirdiShTau, uta jIvaparamAtmAnAm iti | yadi buddhijIvau, tato buddhipradhAnAt kAryakaraNasaMghAtAd vilakShaNo jIvaH pratipAdito bhavati | tad apIha pratipAdayitavyam, yeyaM prete vicikisA manuShye.astItyeke nAyam astIti caike | etadvidyAm anushiShTaH tvayAhaM varANAm eSha varaH tR^itIyaH iti pR^iShTatvAt | 

atha jIvaparamAtmAnau, tato jIvAd vilakShaNaH paramAtmA pratipAdito bhavati | tad apIha pratipAdayitavyam -- anyatra dharmAd anyatrAdharmAd anyatrAsmAt kR^itAkR^itAt | anyatra bhUtAcca bhavyAcca yat tat pashyasi tad vada iti pR^iShTatvAt | atrAhAkSheptA -- ubhAvapyetau pakShau na sambhavataH | kasmAt? R^itapAnaM hi karmaphalopabhogaH, sukR^itasya loke iti liN^gAt | tacca cetanasya kShetraj~nasya sambhavati, nAcetanAyA buddhiH | pibantau iti dvivacanena dvayoH pAnaM darshayati shrutiH | ato buddhikShetraj~napakShaH tAvan na sambhavati | ata eva kShetraj~naparamAtmapakSho.api na sambhavati | cetane.api paramAtmani R^itapAnAsambhavAt, anashnann anyo.abhicAkashIti [mu.u. 3.1.1] iti mantravarNAd iti | 

atrocyate -- naiSha doShaH | chatriNo gacchantItyekenApi cchatriNA bahUnAm acchatriNAM chatritvopacAradarshanAt | evam ekenApi pibatA dvau pibantAv ucyeyAtAm | yad vA, jIvaH tAvat pibati | IshvaraH tu pAyayati | pAyayann api pibatItyucyate, pAcayitaryapi paktR^itvaprasiddhidarshanAt | buddhikShetraj~naparigraho.api sambhavati | karaNe kartR^itvopacArAt, edhAMsi pacanti iti prayogadarshanAt | na cAdhyAtmAdhikAre.anyau kaucid dvAv R^itaM pibantau sambhavataH | tasmAd buddhijIvau syAtAM jIvaparamAtmAnau veti saMshayaH || 

kiM tAvat prAptam? buddhikShetraj~nAviti | kutaH? guhAM praviShTau iti visheShaNAt | yadi sharIraM guhA, yadi vA hR^idayam, ubhayathApi buddhikShetraj~nau guhAM praviShTAv upapadyete | na ca sati sambhave sarvagatasya brahmaNo vishiShTadeshatvaM yuktaM kalpayitum | sukR^itasya loke iti ca karmagocarAn atikramaM darshayati | paramAtmA tu na sukR^itasya vA duShkR^itasya vA gocare vartate, na karmaNA vardhate no kanIyAn iti shruteH | chAyAtapau iti ca cetanAcetanayor nirdesha upapadyate, chAyAtapavatparasparavilakShaNatvAt | tasmAd buddhikShetraj~nAvihocyeyAtAm ityevaM prApte -- 

guhAM praviShTAvatmAnau hi taddarshanAt ||

brUmaH -- vij~nAnAtmaparamAtmAnAvihocyeyAtAm | kasmAt? AtmAnau hi tAv ubhAvapi cetanau samAnasvabhAvau | saMkhyAshravaNe ca samAnasvabhAveShv eva loke pratItir dR^ishyate | asya gaur dvitIyo.anveShTavyaH ityukte, gaur eva dvitIyo.anviShyate, nAshvaH puruSho vA | tad iha R^itapAnena liN^gena nishcite vij~nAnAtmani dvitIyAnveShaNAyAM samAnasvabhAvashcetanaH paramAtmaiva pratIyate | 

nanUktaM guhAhitatvadarshanAn na paramAtmA pratyetavya iti | guhAhitatvadarshanAd eva paramAtmA pratyetavya iti vadAmaH | guhAhitatvaM tu shrutismR^itiShvasakR^it paramAtmana eva dR^ishyate -- guhAhitaM gahvareShThaM purANam yo veda nihitaM guhAyAM parame vyoman AtmAnam anviccha guhAM praviShTam ityAdyAsu | sarvagatasyApi brahmaNa upalabdhyartho deshavisheShopadesho na virudhyata ityetad apyuktam eva | sukR^italokavartitvaM tu cchatritvavad ekasminn api vartamAnam ubhayor aviruddham | chAyAtapau ityapyaviruddham | chAyAtapavatparasparavilakShaNatvAt saMsAritvAsaMsAritvayoH, avidyAkR^itatvAt saMsAritvasya pAramArthikatvAccAsaMsAritvasya | tasmAd vij~nAnAtmaparamAtmAnau guhAM praviShTau gR^ihyete ||11|| 

|| 1.2.12 ||

kutashca vij~nAnAtmaparamAtmAnau gR^ihyete? -- 

visheShaNAcca ||

visheShaNaM ca vij~nAnAtmaparamAtmanor eva bhavati | AtmAnaM rathinaM viddhi sharIraM ratham eva tu [ka.u. 1.3.3] ityAdinA pareNa granthena rathirathAdirUpakakalpanayA vij~nAnAtmAnaM rathinaM saMsAramokShayor gantAraM kalpayati | so.adhvanaH pAram Apnoti tadviShNoH paramaM padam iti paramAtmAnaM gantavyaM kalpayati | tathA, 

taM durdarshaM gUDham anupraviShTaM 
guhAhitaM gahvareShThaM purANam | 
adhyAtmayogAdhigamena devaM 
matvA dhIro harShashokau jahAti || [ka.u. 1.2.12] iti |

pUrvasminn api granthe mantR^imantavyatvenaitAv eva visheShitau | prakaraNaM cedaM paramAtmanaH | brahmavido vadanti iti ca vaktR^ivisheShopAdAnaM paramAtmaparigrahe ghaTate | tasmAd iha jIvaparamAtmAnAv ucyeyAtAm | eSha eva nyAyaH -- dvA suparNA sayujA sakhAyA ityevam AdiShvapi | tatrApi hyadhyAtmAdhikArAn na prAkR^itau suparNAv ucyete | tayor anyaH pippalaM svAdvatti ityadanaliN^gAd vij~nAnAtmA bhavati | anashnann anyo.abhicAkashIti [mu.u. 3.1.1] ityanashanacetanatvAbhyAM paramAtmA | anantare ca mantre tAv eva draShTR^idraShTavyabhAvena vishinaShTi -- 
samAne vR^ikShe puruSho nimagno
.anIshayA shocati muhyamAnaH | 
juShTaM yadA pashyatyanyam Isham
asya mahimAnam iti vItashokaH || [mu.u. 3.1.2] iti |

apara Aha -- dvA suparNA iti neyam R^igasyAdhikaraNasya siddhAntaM bhajate, paiN^girahasyabrAhmaNenAnyathA vyAkhyAtatvAt -- tayor anyaH pippalaM svAdvattIti sattvam anashnann anyo.abhicAkashItIty, anashnann anyo.abhipashyati j~naH tAv etau sattvakShetraj~nau iti | sattvashabdo jIvaH kShetraj~nashabdaH paramAtmeti yad ucyate, tan na | sattvakShetraj~nashabdayor antaHkaraNashArIraparatayA prasiddhatvAt | tatraiva ca vyAkhyAtatvAt  -- tad etat sattvaM yena svapnaM pashyati, atha yo.ayaM shArIra upadraShTA sa kShetraj~naH tAv etau sattvakShetraj~nau iti | 

nApyasyAdhikaraNasya pUrvapakShabhAvaM bhajate | na hyatra shArIraH kShetraj~naH kartR^itvabhoktR^itvAdinA saMsAradharmeNopeto vivakShyate | kathaM tarhi? sarvasaMsAradharmAtIto brahmasvabhAvashcaitanyamAtrasvarUpaH | 

anashnann anyo.abhicAkashItItyanashnann anyo.abhipashyati j~naH iti vacanAt, tattvam asi, kShetraj~naM cApi mAM viddhi ityAdi shrutismR^itibhyashca | tAvatA ca vidyopasaMhAradarshanam evam evAvakalpate, tAv etau sattvakShetraj~nau na ha vA evaMvidi kiMcana raja AdhvaMsate ityAdi | kathaM punar asmin pakShe tayor anyaH pippalaM svAdvattIti sattvam ityacetane sattve bhoktR^itvavacanam iti, ucyate -- neyaM shrutir acetanasya sattvasya bhoktR^itvaM vakShyAmIti pravR^ittA | kiM tarhi? cetanasya kShetraj~nasyAbhoktR^itvaM brahmasvabhAvatAM ca vakShyAmIti | tadarthaM sukhaduHkhAdivikriyAvati sattve bhoktR^itvam adhyAropayati | idaM hi kartR^itvaM bhoktR^itvaM ca sattvakShetraj~nayoH itaretarasvabhAvAvivekakR^itaM kalpyate | paramArthataH tu nAnyatarasyApi sambhavati, acetanatvAt sattvasya, avikriyatvAcca kShetraj~nasya | avidyApratyupasthApitasvabhAvatvAcca sattvasya sutarAM na sambhavati | tathA ca shrutiH -- yatra vA anyad iva syAt tatrAnyo.anyat pashyet ityAdinA svapnadR^iShTahastyAdivyavahAravad avidyAviShaya eva kartR^itvAdivyavahAraM darshayati | yatra tu asya sarvam AtmaivAbhUt tat kena kaM pashyet [bR^i.A.u. 4.5.15] ityAdinA ca vivekinaH kartR^itvAdivyavahAraM nivArayati ||

 -- o)0(o -- 
4. antarAdhikaraNam

|| 1.2.13 ||

ya eSho.akShiNi puruSho dR^ishyata eSha Atmeti hovAcaitad amR^itam abhayam etad brahmeti tad yadyapyasmin sarpir vodakaM vA siJNcati vartmanI eva gacchati [chA.u. 4.15.1] ityAdi shrUyate | 

tatra saMshayaH -- kim ayaM pratibimbAtmAkShyadhikaraNo nirdishyate, atha vij~nAnAtmA, uta devatAtmendriyasyAdhiShThAtA, athaveshvara iti | kiM tAvat prAptam? chAyAtmA puruShapratirUpa iti | kutaH? tasya dR^ishyamAnatvaprasiddhaH, ya eSho.akShiNi puruSho dR^ishyate iti ca prasiddhavad upadeshAt | vij~nAnAtmano vAyaM nirdesha iti yuktam | sa hi cakShuShA rUpaM pashyaMshcakShuShi saMnihito bhavati | AtmashabdashcAsmin pakShe.anukUlo bhavati | AdityapuruSho vA cakShuSho.anugrAhakaH pratIyate -- rashmibhir eSho.asmin pratiShThitaH iti shruteH, amR^itatvAd InAM ca devatAtmanyapi kathaMcit sambhavAt | neshvaraH, sthAnavisheShanirdeshAt | ityevaM prApte -- 

antara upapatteH ||

brUmaH -- parameshvara evAkShiNyabhyantaraH puruSha ihopadiShTa iti | kasmAt? upapatteH | upapadyate hi parameshvare guNajAtam ihopadishyamAnam | AtmatvaM tAvan mukhyayA vR^ittyA parameshvare upapadyate, sa AtmA tattvam asi iti shruteH | amR^itatvAbhayatve ca tasminn asakR^icchrUyete | tathA parameshvarAnurUpam etad akShisthAnam | yathA hi parameshvaraH sarvadoShair aliptaH, apahatapApmatvAdishravaNAt | tathAkShisthAnaM sarvaleparahitam upadiShTam tad yadyapyasmin sarpir vodakaM vA siJNcati, vartmanI eva gacchati iti shruteH | saMyadvAmatvAdiguNopadeshashca tasminn avakalpate | etaM saMyadvAma ityAcakShate | etaM hi sarvANi vAmAnyabhisaMyanti, eSha u eva vAmanIr eSha hi sarvANi vAmAni nayati | eSha u eva bhAmanIr eSha hi sarveShu lokeShu bhAti iti ca | ata upapatter antaraH parameshvaraH ||13||

|| 1.2.14 ||

sthAnAdivyapadeshAcca ||

kathaM punar AkAshavat sarvagatasya brahmaNo.akShyalpaM sthAnam upapadyata iti, atrocyate -- bhaved eShAnavakptiH, yadyetad evaikaM sthAnam asya nirdiShTaM bhavet | santi hyanyAnyapi pR^ithivyAdIni sthAnAnyasya nirdiShTAni -- yaH pR^ithivyAM tiShThan [bR^i.A.u. 3.7.3] ityAdinA | teShu hi cakShur api nirdiShTam yashcakShuShi tiShThan [bR^i.A.u. 3.7.18] iti | sthAnAdivyapadeshAd ityAdigrahaNenaitad darshayati -- na kevalaM sthAnam evaikam anucitaM brahmaNo nirdishyate | kiM tarhi, nAma rUpam ityevaMjAtIyakam apyanAmarUpasya brahmaNo.anucitaM nirdishyamAnaM dR^ishyate -- tasyod iti nAma [chA.u. 1.6.7] hiraNyashmashruH [chA.u. 1.6.6] ityAdi | nirguNam api sad brahma nAmarUpagatair guNaiH sa0guNam upAsanArthaM tatra tatropadishyata ityetad apyuktam eva | sarvagatasyApi brahmaNa upalabdhyarthaM sthAnavisheSho na virudhyate, sAlagrAma iva viShNoH ityetad apyuktam eva ||14||

|| 1.2.15 ||

sukhavishiShTAbhidhAnAd eva ca ||

api ca naivAtra vivaditavyam -- kiM brahmAsmin vAkye.abhidhIyate, na veti | sukhavishiShTAbhidhAnAd eva brahmatvaM siddham | sukhavishiShTaM hi brahma yad vAkyopakrame prakrAntam prANo brahma kaM brahma khaM brahma iti, tad evehAbhihitam | prakR^itaparigrahasya nyAyyatvAt, AcAryaH tu te gatiM vaktA iti ca gatimAtrAbhidhAnapratij~nAnAt | kathaM punar vAkyopakrame sukhavishiShTaM brahma vij~nAyata iti, ucyate -- prANo brahma kaM brahma khaM brahma [chA.u. 4.10.4] ityetad agnInAM vacanaM shrutvopakosala uvAca -- vijAnAmyahaM yat prANo brahma, kaM ca khaM ca tu na vijAnAmi [chA.u. 4.10.5] iti | tatredaM prativacanam -- yad vAva kaM tad eva khaM yad eva khaM tad eva kam [chA.u. 4.10.5] iti | 

tatra khaMshabdo bhUtAkAshe nirUDho loke | yadi tasya visheShaNatvena kaMshabdaH sukhavAcI nopAdIyeta, tathA sati kevale bhUtAkAshe brahmashabdo nAmAdiShviva pratIkAbhiprAyeNa prayukta iti pratItiH syAt | tathA kaMshabdasya viShayendriyasamparkajanite sAmaye sukhe prasiddhatvAt, yadi tasya khaMshabdo visheShaNatvena nopAdIyeta | laukikaM sukhaM brahmeti pratItiH syAt | itaretaravisheShitau tu kaMkhaMshabdau sukhAtmakaM brahma gamayataH | tatra dvitIye brahmashabde.anupAdIyamAne kaM khaM brahma ityevocyamAne kaMshabdasya visheShaNatvenaivopayuktatvAt sukhasya guNasyAdhyeyatvaM syAt | tan mA bhUt -- ityubhayoH kaMkhaMshabdayor brahmashabdashirastvam -- kaM brahma khaM brahma iti | iShTaM hi sukhasyApi guNasya guNivad dhyeyatvam | tad evaM vAkyopakrame sukhavishiShTaM brahmopadiShTam | pratyekaM ca gArhapatyAdayo.agnayaH svaM svaM mahimAnam upadishya eShA somya te.asmadvidyAtmavidyA ca ityupasaMharantaH pUrvatra brahma nirdiShTam iti j~nApayanti | AcAryaH tu te gatiM vaktA iti ca gatimAtrAbhidhAnapratij~nAnam arthAntaravivakShAM vArayati | yathA puShkarapalAsha Apo na shliShyanta evam evaMvidi pApaM karma na shliShyate iti cAkShisthAnaM puruShaM vijAnataH pApmanAnupaghAtaM bruvann akShisthAnasya puruShasya brahmatvaM darshayati | tasmAt prakR^itasyaiva brahmaNo.akShisthAnatAM saMyadvAmatvAdiguNatAM coktvA arcirAdikAM tadvido gatiM vakShyAmItyupakramate -- ya eSho.akShiNi puruSho dR^ishyata eSha Atmeti hovAca [chA.u. 4.15.1] iti ||15||

|| 1.2.16 ||

shrutopaniShatkagatyabhidhAnAcca ||

itashcAkShisthAnaH puruShaH parameshvaraH, yasmAcchrutopaniShatkasya shrutarahasyavij~nAnasya brahmavido yA gatir devayAnAkhyA prasiddhA shrutau -- athottareNa tapasA brahmacaryeNa shraddhayA vidyayAtmAnam anviShyAdityam abhijayante | etad vai prANAnAm Ayatanam etad amR^itam abhayam etat parAyaNam etasmAn na punar Avartante iti | 

smR^itAvapi -- 
agnir jyotir ahaH shuklaH ShaNmAsA uttarAyaNam | 
tatra prayAtA gacchanti brahma brahmavido janAH || [gItA 8.shrutshrut] iti |

saivehAkShipuruShavido.abhidhIyamAnA dR^ishyate | atha yad u caivAsmiJNshavyaM kurvanti yadi ca nArciSham evAbhisambhavanti ityupakramya AdityAccandramasaM candramaso vidyutaM tat puruSho.amAnavaH sa enAn brahma gamayatyeSha devapatho brahmapatha etena pratipadyamAnA imaM mAnavam AvartaM nAvartante iti | tad iha brahmavid viShayayA prasiddhayA gatyA akShisthAnasya brahmatvaM nishcIyate ||16||

|| 1.2.17 || 

anavasthiter asambhavAcca netaraH ||

yat punar uktaM chAyAtmA, vij~nAnAtmA, devatAtmA vA syAd akShisthAna iti, atrocyate -- na cchAyAtmAdiH itara iha grahaNam arhati | kasmAt? anavasthiteH | na tAvacchAyAtmanashcakShuShi nityam avasthAnaM sambhavati | yadaiva hi kashcit puruShashcakShur AsIdati, tadA cakShuShi puruShacchAyA dR^ishyate | apagate tasmin na dR^ishyate | ya eSho.akShiNi puruShaH iti ca shrutiH saMnidhAnAt svacakShuShi dR^ishyamAnaM puruSham upAsyatvenopadishati | na copAsanAkAle cchAyAkaraM kaMcit puruShaM cakShuHsamIpe saMnidhApyopAsta iti yuktaM kalpayitum | asyaiva sharIrasya nAsham anveSha nashyati iti shrutishchAyAtmano.apyanavasthitatvaM darshayati | asambhAvacca | tasminn amR^itatvAdInAM guNAnAM na cchAyAtmani pratItiH | tathA vij~nAnAtmano.api sAdhAraNe kR^itsnasharIrendriyasambandhe sati na cakShuShyevAvasthitatvaM shakyaM vaktum | brahmaNaH tu sarvavyApino.api dR^iShTa upalabdhyartho hR^idayAdideshavisheShasambandhaH | samAnashca vij~nAnAtmanyapyamR^itatvAdInAM guNAnAm asambhavaH | yadyapi vij~nAnAtmA paramAtmano.ananya eva, tathApyavidyAkAmakarmakR^itaM tasmin martyatvam adhyAropitaM bhayaM cetyamR^itatvAbhayatve nopapadyete | saMyadvAmatvAdayashcaitasminn anaishvaryAd anupapannA eva | devatAtmanaH tu rashmibhir eSho.asmin pratiShThitaH iti shruteH yadyapi cakShuShyavasthAnaM syAt, tathApyAtmatvaM tAvan na sambhavati, parAgrUpatvAt | amR^itatvAdayo.api na sambhavanti, utpattipralayashravaNAt | amaratvam api devAnAM cirakAlAvasthAnApekSham | aishvaryam api parameshvarAyattam, na svAbhAvikam | 

bhIShAsmAd vAtaH pavate, bhIShodeti sUryaH | 
bhIShAsmAd agnishcendrashca mR^ityur dhAvati paJNcamaH || iti mantravarNAt | 

tasmAt parameshvara evAyam akShisthAnaH pratyetavyaH | asmiMshca pakShe dR^ishyate iti prasiddhavad upAdAnaM shAstrAdyapekShaM vidvadviShayaM prarocanArtham iti vyAkhyeyam ||17||

5. antaryAmyadhikaraNam

|| 1.2.18 ||

ya imaM ca lokaM paraM ca lokaM sarvANi ca bhUtAnyantaro yamayati [bR^i.A.u. 3.7.1] ityupakramya shrUyate -- yaH pR^ithivyAM tiShThan pR^ithivyA antaro yaM pR^ithivI na veda yasya pR^ithivI sharIraM yaH pR^ithivIm antaro yamayatyeSha ta AtmAntaryAmyamR^itaH [bR^i.A.u. 3.7.3] ityAdi | atrAdhidaivatam adhilokam adhivedam adhiyaj~nam adhibhUtam adhyAtmaM ca kashcid antaravasthito yamayitA antaryAmIti shrUyate | sa kim adhidaivAdyabhimAnI devatAtmA kashcit, kiM vA prAptANimAdyaishvaryaH kashcid yogI, kiM vA paramAtmA, kiM vArthAntaraM kiJNcit ? ityapUrvasaMj~nAdarshanAt saMshayaH | kiM tAvan naH pratibhAti? saMj~nAyA aprasiddhatvAt saMj~ninApyaprasiddhinArthAntareNa kenacid bhavitavyam iti | athavA nAnirUpitarUpam arthAntaraM kiMcid api shakyam astItyabhyupagantum | antaryAmishabdashcAntaryamanayogena pravR^itto nAtyantam aprasiddhaH | tasmAt pR^ithivyAdyabhimAnI kashcid devo.antaryAmI syAt | tathA ca shrUyate -- pR^ithivyeva yasyAyatanam agnir loko mano jyotiH ityAdi | sa ca kAryakaraNavattvAt pR^ithivyAdIn antaH tiShThanyam ayatIti yuktaM devatAtmano yamayitR^itvam | yogino vA kasyacit siddhasya sarvAnupraveshena yamayitR^itvaM syAt | na tu paramAtmA pratIyate, akAryakaraNatvAt | ityevaM prApte -- 

antaryAmyadhidaivAdiShu taddharmavyapadeshAt ||

idam ucyate -- yo.antaryAmyadhidaivAdiShu shrUyate, sa paramAtmaiva syAt, nAnya iti | kutaH? taddharmavyapadeshAt | tasya hi paramAtmano dharmA iha nirdishyamAnA dR^ishyante | pR^ithivyAdi tAvad adhidaivAdibhedabhinnaM samastaM vikArajAtam antaH tiShThan yamayatIti paramAtmano yamayitR^itvaM dharma upapadyate | sarvavikArakAraNatve sati sarvashaktyupapatteH | eSha ta AtmAntaryAmyamR^itaH iti cAtmatvAmR^itatve mukhye paramAtmana upapadyete | yaM pR^ithivI na veda iti ca pR^ithivIdevatAyA avij~neyam antaryAmiNaM bruvan devatAtmano.anyam antaryAmiNaM darshayati | pR^ithivI devatA hyaham asmi pR^ithivItyAtmAnaM vijAnIyAt | tathA adR^iShTo.ashrutaH ityAdi vyapadesho rUpAdivihInatvAt paramAtmana upapadyata iti | 

yat tu akAryakaraNasya paramAtmano yamayitR^itvaM nopapadyata iti, naiSha doShaH | yAn niyacchati tat kAryakaraNair eva tasya kAryakaraNavattvopapatteH | tasyApyanyo niyantetyanavasthAdoShashca na sambhavati, bhedAbhAvAt | bhede hi satyanavasthAdoShopapattiH | tasmAt paramAtmaivAntaryAmI ||18||
|| 1.2.19 ||

na ca smArtam ataddharmAbhilApAt ||

syAd etat -- adR^iShTatvAdayo dharmAH sAN^khyasmR^itikalpitasya pradhAnasyApyupapadyante, rUpAdihInatayA tasya tair abhyupagamAt | apratarkyam avij~neyaM prasuptam iva sarvataH iti hi smaranti | tasyApi niyantR^itvaM sarvavikArakAraNatvAd upapadyate | tasmAt pradhAnam antaryAmishabdaM syAt | IkShater nAshabdam ityatra nirAkR^itam api sat pradhAnam ihAdR^iShTatvAdivyapadeshasambhavena punar AshaN^kyate | ata uttaram ucyate -- na ca smArtaM pradhAnam antaryAmishabdaM bhavitum arhati | kasmAt? ataddharmAbhilApAt | yadyapyadR^iShTatvAdivyapadeshaH pradhAnasya sambhavati, tathApi na draShTR^itvAdivyapadeshaH sambhavati, pradhAnasyAcetanatvena tair abhyupagamAt | adR^iShTo draShTAshrutaH shrotAmato mantAvij~nAto vij~nAtA iti hi vAkyasheSha iha bhavati | Atmatvam api na pradhAnasyopapadyate ||19|| 

|| 1.2.20 ||

yadi pradhAnam AtmatvadraShTR^itvAdyasambhavAn nAntaryAmyabhyupagamyate, shArIraH tarhyantaryAmI bhavatu | shArIro hi cetanatvAd draShTA shrotA mantA vij~nAtA ca bhavati, AtmA ca pratyaktvAt | amR^itashca, dharmAdharmaphalopabhogopapatteH | adR^iShTatvAdayashca dharmAH shArIre suprasiddhAH | darshanAdikriyAyAH kartari pravR^ittivirodhAt, na dR^iShTer draShTAraM pashyeH [bR^i.A.u. 3.4.2] ityAdi shrutibhyashca | tasya ca kAryakaraNasaMghAtam antar yamayituM shIlam, bhoktR^itvAt | tasmAcchArIro.antaryAmItyata uttaraM paThati -- 

shArIrashcobhaye.api hi bhedenainam adhIyate || 

neti pUrvasUtrAd anuvartate | shArIrashca nAntaryAmI syAt | kasmAt? yadyapi draShTR^itvAdayo dharmAH tasya sambhavanti, tathApi ghaTAkAshavad upAdhiparicchinnatvAn na kArtsnyena pR^ithivyAdiShvantar avasthAtuM niyantuM ca shaknoti | api cobhaye.api hi shAkhinaH kANvA mAdhyandinAshcAntaryAmiNo bhedenainaM shArIraM pR^ithivyAdivad adhiShThAnatvena niyamyatvena cAdhIyate --  yo vij~nAne tiShThan iti kANvAH, ya Atmani tiShThan iti mAdhyandinAH | ya Atmani tiShThan ityasmiMH tAvat pAThe bhavatyAtmashabdaH shArIrasya vAcakaH | yo vij~nAne tiShThan ityasminn api pAThe vij~nAnashabdena shArIra ucyate, vij~nAnamayo hi shArIra iti | tasmAcchArIrAd anya Ishvaro.antaryAmIti siddham | kathaM punar ekasmin dehe dvau draShTArAv upapadyete ? yashcAyam Ishvaro.antaryAmI, yashcAyam itaraH shArIraH? kA punaH ihAnupapattiH? nAnyo.ato.asti draShTA ityAdi shrutivacanaM virudhyeta | atra hi prakR^itAd antaryAmiNo.anyaM draShTAraM shrotAraM mantAraM vij~nAtAraM cAtmAnaM pratiShedhati | niyantrantarapratiShedhArtham etad vacanam iti cet, na | niyantrantarAprasaN^gAd avisheShashravaNAcca | 

atrocyate -- avidyApratyupasthApitakAryakaraNopAdhinimitto.ayaM shArIrAntaryAmiNor bhedavyapadeshaH, na pAramArthikaH | eko hi pratyagAtmA bhavati, na dvau pratyagAtmAnau sambhavataH | ekasyaiva tu bhedavyavahAra upAdhikR^itaH, yathA ghaTAkAsho mahAkAsha iti | tatashca j~nAtR^ij~neyAdibhedashrutayaH pratyakShAdIni ca pramANAni saMsArAnubhavo vidhipratiShedhashAstraM ceti sarvam etad upapadyate | tathA ca shrutiH -- yatra hi dvaitam iva bhavati tad itara itaraM pashyati ityavidyAviShaye sarvaM vyavahAraM darshayati | yatra tu asya sarvam AtmaivAbhUt tat kena kaM pashyet [bR^i.A.u. 4.5.15] iti vidyAviShaye sarvaM vyavahAraM vArayati ||20||

 -- o)0(o -- 
6. adR^ishyAdhikaraNam

|| 1.2.21 ||

atha parA yayA tad akSharam adhigamyate ||

yat tad adR^ishyam agrAhyam agotram
avarNam acakShuHshrotraM tad apANipAdam |
nityaM vibhuM sarvagataM susUkShmaM
tad avyayaM yad bhUtayoniM paripashyanti dhIrAH || [mu.u. 1.1.56]

iti shrUyate | tatra saMshayaH -- kim ayam adR^ishyatvAdiguNako bhUtayoniH pradhAnaM syAt, uta shArIraH, Aho svit parameshvaraH ? iti | tatra pradhAnam acetanaM bhUtayoniH iti yuktam, acetanAnAm eva tatra dR^iShTAntatvenopAdAnAt | 

yathorNanAbhiH sR^ijate gR^ihNate ca 
yathA pR^ithivyAm oShadhayaH sambhavanti | 
yathA sataH puruShAt keshalomAni 
tathAkSharAt sambhavatIha vishvam || [mu.u. 1.1.7] iti | 

nanUrNanAbhiH puruShashca cetanAviha dR^iShTAntatvenopAttau | neti brUmaH | na hi kevalasya cetanasya tatra sUtrayonitvaM keshalomayonitvaM vAsti | cetanAdhiShThitaM hyacetanam UrNanAbhisharIraM sUtrasya yoniH, puruShasharIraM ca keshalomnAm iti prasiddham | api ca pUrvatrAdR^iShTatvAd yabhilApasambhave.api draShTR^itvAd yabhilApAsambhavAn na pradhAnam abhyupagatam | iha tu adR^ishyatvAdayo dharmAH pradhAne sambhavanti | na cAtra virudhyamAno dharmaH kashcid abhilapyate | 

nanu yaH sarvaj~naH sarvavit ityayaM vAkyasheSho.acetane pradhAne na sambhavati, kathaM pradhAnaM bhUtayoniH pratij~nAyata ? iti | atrocyate -- yayA tad akSharam adhigamyate yat tad apAshyam ityakSharashabdenAdR^ishyatvAdiguNakaM bhUtayoniM shrAvayitvA, punar ante shrAvayiShyati -- akSharAt parataH paraH iti | tatra yaH paro.akSharAcchrutaH, sa sarvaj~naH sarvavit sambhaviShyati | pradhAnam eva tu akSharashabdanirdiShTaM bhUtayoniH | yadA tu yonishabdo nimittavAcI, tadA shArIro.api bhUtayoniH syAt, dharmAdharmAbhyAM bhUtajAtasyopArjanAd iti | evaM prApte -- 

adR^ishyatvAdiguNako dharmokteH ||

abhidhIyate -- yo.ayam adR^ishyatvAdiguNako bhUtayoniH, sa parameshvara eva syAt, nAnya iti | katham etad avagamyate? dharmokteH | parameshvarasya hi dharma ihocyamAno dR^ishyate -- yaH sarvaj~naH sarvavit [mu.u. 1.1.9] iti | na hi pradhAnasyAcetanasya shArIrasya vopAdhiparicchinnadR^iShTeH sarvaj~natvaM sarvavittvaM vA sambhavati | 

nanvakSharashabdanirdiShTAdbhUtayoneH parasyaiva etat sarvaj~natvaM sarvavittvaM ca, na bhUtayoniviShayam ityuktam | atrocyate -- naivaM sambhavati | yatkAraNam akSharAt sambhavatIha vishvam iti prakR^itaM bhUtayonim iha jAyamAnaprakR^ititvena nirdishya, anantaram api jAyamAnaprakR^ititvenaiva sarvaj~naM nirdishati -- 

yaH sarvaj~naH sarvavid yasya j~nAnamayaM tapaH | 
tasmAd etad brahma nAma rUpam annaM ca jAyate || [mu.u. 1.1.9] iti | 

tasmAn nirdeshasAmyena pratyabhij~nAyamAnatvAt prakR^itasyaivAkSharasya bhUtayoneH sarvaj~natvaM sarvavittvaM ca dharma ucyata iti gamyate | akSharAt parataH paraH ityatrApi ca prakR^itAdbhUtayonekSharAt paraH kashcid abhidhIyate | 

katham etad avagamyate? yenAkSharaM puruShaM veda satyaM provAca tAM tattvatto brahmavidyAm [mu.u. 1.2.13] iti prakR^itasyaivAkSharasya bhUtayoner adR^ishyatvAdiguNakasya vaktavyatvena pratij~nAtatvAt | kathaM tarhi akSharAt parataH paraH iti vyapadishyata ? iti, uttarasUtre tad vakShyAmaH | api cAtra dve vidye veditavye ukte -- parA caivAparA ca [mu.u. 1.1.4] iti | tatrAparAm R^igvedAdilakShaNAM vidyAm uktvA bravIti -- atha parA yayA tad akSharam adhigamyate [mu.u. 1.1.5] ityAdi | tatra parasyA vidyAyA viShayatvenAkSharaM shrutam | yadi punaH parameshvarAd anyad adR^ishyatvAdiguNakam akSharaM parikalpyeta, neyaM parA vidyA syAt | parAparavibhAgo hyayaM vidyayoH abhyudayaniHshreyasaphalatayA parikalpyate | na ca pradhAnasya vidyA niHshreyasaphalA kenacid abhyupagamyate | tisrashca vidyAH pratij~nAyeran, tvatpakShe.akSharAdbhUtayoneH parasya paramAtmanaH pratipAdyamAnatvAt | 

dve eva tu vidye veditavye iha nirdiShTo | kasmin nu bhagavo vij~nAte sarvam idaM vij~nAtaM bhavati [mu.u. 1.1.3] iti caikavij~nAnena sarvavij~nAnApekShaNaM sarvAtmake brahmaNi vivakShyamANe.avakalpate, nAcetanamAtraikAyatane pradhAne, bhogyavyatirikte vA bhoktari | api ca sa brahmavidyAM sarvavidyApratiShThAm atharvAya jyeShThaputrAya prAha iti brahmavidyAM prAdhAnyenopakramya parAparavibhAgena parAM vidyAm akSharAdhigamanIM darshayan tasyA brahmavidyAtvaM darshayati | sA ca brahmavidyAsamAkhyA tadadhigamyasya akSharasyAbrahmatve bAdhitA syAt | aparA R^igvedAdilakShaNA karmavidyA brahmavidyopakrame upanyasyate brahmavidyAprashaMsAyai -- 

plavA hyete adR^iDhA yaj~narUpA 
aShTAdashoktam avaraM yeShu karma | 
etaccharAyo ye.abhinandanti mUDhA 
jarAM mR^ityuM te punar evApi yanti ||

ityevam AdinindAvacanAt | ninditvA cAparAM vidyAM tato viraktasya paravidyAdhikAraM darshayati -- 

parIkShya lokAn karmacitAn brAhmaNo 
nirvedam AyAn nAstyakR^itaH kR^itena | 
tadvij~nAnArthaM sa gurum evAbhigacchet
samitpANiH shrotriyaM brahmaniShTham || [mu.u. 1.2.12] iti | 

yat tUktam -- acetanAnAM pR^ithivyAdInAM dR^iShTAntatvenopAdAnAd dArShTAntikenApyacetanenaiva bhUtayoninA bhavitavyam iti, tad ayuktam | na hi dR^iShTAntadArShTAntikayor atyantasAmyena bhavitavyam iti niyamo.asti | api ca sthUlAH pR^ithivyAdayo dR^iShTAntatvenopAttA iti na sthUla eva dArShTAntiko bhUtayonir abhyupagamyate | tasmAd adR^ishyatvAdiguNako bhUtayoniH parameshvara eva ||21||

|| 1.2.22 ||

visheShaNabhedavyapadeshAbhyAM ca netarau || 

itashca parameshvara eva bhUtayoniH, netarau -- shArIraH pradhAnaM vA | kasmAt? visheShaNabhedavyapadeshAbhyAm | vishinaShTi hi prakR^itaM bhUtayoniM shArIrAd vilakShaNatvena -- divyo hyamUrtaH puruShaH sabAhyAbhyantaro hyajaH | aprANo hyamanAH shubhraH [mu.u. 2.1.2] iti | na hyetad divyatvAdivisheShaNam avidyApratyupasthApitanAmarUpaparicchedAbhimAninaH taddharmAn svAtmani kalpayataH shArIrasyopapadyate | tasmAt sAkShAd aupaniShadaH puruSha ihocyate | tathA pradhAnAd api prakR^itaM bhUtayoniM bhedena vyapadishati -- akSharAt parataH paraH iti | akSharam avyAkR^itaM nAmarUpabIjashaktirUpaM bhUtasUkShmam IshvarAshrayaM tasyaivopAdhibhUtam, sarvasmAd vikArAt paro yo.avikAraH, tasmAt parataH paraH iti bhedena vyapadishan paramAtmAnam iha vivakShitaM darshayati | nAtra pradhAnaM nAma kiMcit svatantraM tattvam abhyupagamya, tasmAd bhedavyapadesha ucyate | kiM tarhi? yadi pradhAnam api kalpyamAnaM shrutyavirodhenAvyAkR^itAdishabdavAcyaM bhUtasUkShmaM parikalpyeta, kalpyatAm | tasmAd bhedavyapadeshAt parameshvaro bhUtayoniH ityetad iha pratipAdyate ||22|| 

|| 1.2.23 || 

kutashca parameshvaro bhUtayoniH? -- 

rUpopanyAsAcca ||

api ca akSharAt parataH paraH ityasyAnantaram etasmAjjAyate prANaH [mu.u. 2.1.3] iti prANaprabhR^itInAM pR^ithivIparyantAnAM tattvAnAM sargam uktvA, tasyaiva bhUtayoneH sarvavikArAtmakaM rUpam upanyasyamAnaM pashyAmaH -- 

agnir mUrdhA cakShuShI candrasUryau 
dishaH shrotre vAgvivR^itAshca vedAH | 
vAyuH prANo hR^idayaM vishvam asya 
padbhyAM pR^ithivI hyeSha sarvabhUtAntarAtmA || iti | 

tacca parameshvarasyaivocitam, sarvavikArakAraNatvAt | na shArIrasya tanumahimnaH | nApi pradhAnasya ayaM rUpopanyAsaH sambhavati, sarvabhUtAntarAtmatvAsambhavAt | tasmAt parameshvara eva bhUtayoniH, netarAviti gamyate | kathaM punar bhUtayoner ayaM rUpopanyAsa iti gamyate? prakaraNAt, eShaH iti ca prakR^itAnukurvANAt | bhUtayoniM hi prakR^itya etasmAjjAyate prANaH eSha sarvabhUtAntarAtmA [mu.u. 2.1.3] iti vacanaM bhUtayoniviShayam eva bhavati | yathA upAdhyAyaM prakR^itya etasmAd adhIShva, eSha vedavedAN^gapAragaH iti vacanam upAdhyAyaviShayaM bhavati, tadvat | kathaM punar adR^ishyatvAdiguNakasya bhUtayoner vigrahavadrUpaM sambhavati? sarvAtmatvavivakShayedam ucyate, na tu vigrahavattvavivakShayA ityadoShaH, aham annam aham annam aham annam, aham annAdaH ityAdivat | 

anye punar manyante -- nAyaM bhUtayoneH rUpopanyAsaH, jAyamAnatvenopanyAsAt | 

etasmAjjAyate prANo manaH sarvendriyANi ca | 
khaM vAyur jyotir ApaH pR^ithivI vishvasya dhAriNI || [mu.u. 2.1.3]

iti hi pUrvatra prANAdi pR^ithivyantaM tattvajAtaM jAyamAnatvena niradikShat | uttaratrApi ca tasmAd agniH samidho yasya sUryaH inyevam Adi atashca sarvA oShadhayo rasAshca ityevam antaM jAmAnatvenaiva nirdekShyati | ihaiva katham akasmAd antarAle bhUtayoneH rUpam upanyasyet? sarvAtmatvam api sR^iShTiM parisamApyopadekShyati -- puruSha evedaM vishvaM karma ityAdinA | shrutismR^ityoshca trailokyasharIrasya prajApater janmAdi nirdishyamAnam upalabhAmahe -- 

hiraNyagarbhaH samavartatAgre 
bhUtasya jAtaH patir eka AsIt | 
sa dAdhAra pR^ithivIM dyAm utemAM 
kasmai devAya haviShA vidhema || iti |

samavartateti ajAyatetyarthaH -- tathA, sa vai sharIrI prathamaH sa vai puruSha ucyate | AdikartA sa bhUtAnAM brahmAgre samavartata iti ca | vikArapuruShasyApi sarvabhUtAntarAtmatvaM sambhavati, prANAtmanA sarvabhUtAnAm adhyAtmam avasthAnAt | asmin pakShe puruSha evedaM vishvaM karma ityAdisarvarUpopanyAsaH parameshvarapratipattihetuH iti vyAkhyeyam ||23||

7. vaishvAnarAdhikaraNam

|| 1.2.24 || 

vaishvAnaraH sAdhAraNashabdavisheShAt || 

ko na AtmA kiM brahmeti [chA.u. 5.11.1] AtmAnam evemaM vaishvAnaraM sampratyadhyeShi tam eva no brUhIti [chA.u. 5.11.6] 

ity copakramya dyusUryavAyvAkAshavAripR^ithivInAM sutejastvAdiguNayogam ekaikopAsananindayA ca vaishvAnaraM pratyeShAM mUrdhAdibhAvam upadishyAmnAyate --  

yaH tv etam evaM prAdeshamAtram abhivimAnam AtmAnaM vaishvAnaram upAste sa sarveShu lokeShu sarveShu bhUteShu sarveShvatmasvannam atti || tasya ha vA etasyAtmano vaishvAnarasya mUrdhaiva sutejAshcakShur vishvarUpaH prANaH pR^ithagvartmAtmA sandeho bahulo bastir eva rayiH pR^ithivyeva pAdAvura eva vedirlomAni barhir hR^idayaM gArhapatyo mano.anvAhAryapacana Asyam AhavanIyaH || [chA.u. 5.18.12] ityAdi |

tatra saMshayaH -- kiM vaishvAnarashabdena jATharo.agnir upadishyate, uta bhUtAgniH, atha tadabhimAninI devatA, athavA shArIraH, Aho svit parameshvaraH ? iti | kiM punar atra saMshayakAraNam? vaishvAnara iti jATharabhUtAgnidevatAnAM sAdhAraNashabdaprayogAt, Atmeti ca shArIraparameshvarayoH | tatra kasyopAdAnaM nyAyyaM, kasya vA hAnam ? iti bhavati saMshayaH | kiM tAvat prAptam? jATharo.agniH iti | kutaH? tatra hi visheSheNa kvacit prayogo dR^ishyate -- ayam agnir vaishvAnaro yo.ayam antaH puruShe yenedam annaM pacyate yad idam adyate ityAdau | agnimAtraM vA syAt, tatsAmAnyenApi prayogadarshanAt -- vishvasmA agniM bhuvanAya devA vaishvAnaraM ketumahnAmakR^iNvan ityAdau agnisharIrA vA devatA syAt, tasyAm api prayogadarshanAt -- vaishvAnarasya sumatau syAma rAjA hi kaM bhuvanAnAm abhi shrIH ityevam AdyAyAH shruter devatAyAm aishvaryAdyupetAyAM sambhavAt | athAtmashabdasAmAnAdhikaraNyAd upakrame ca ko na AtmA kiM brahma iti kevalAtmashabdaprayogAd Atmashabdavashena vaishvAnarashabdaH pariNeya ityucyate, tathApi shArIra AtmA syAt | tasya bhoktR^itvena vaishvAnarasaMnikarShAt, prAdeshamAtram iti ca visheShaNasya tasminn upAdhiparicchinne sambhavAt | tasmAn neshvaro vaishvAnara ityevaM prAptam || 

tatredam ucyate -- vaishvAnaraH paramAtmA bhavitum arhati | kutaH? sAdhAraNashabdavisheShAt | sAdhAraNashabdayor visheShaH sAdhAraNashabdavisheShaH | yadyapyetAv ubhAvapyAtmavaishvAnarashabdau sAdhAraNashabdau -- vaishvAnarashabdaH tu trayANAM sAdhAraNaH, Atmashabdashca dvayoH -- tathApi visheSho dR^ishyate, -- yena parameshvaraparatvaM tayor abhyupagamyate -- tasya ha vA etasyAtmano vaishvAnarasya mUrdhaiva sutejAH ityAdiH | atra hi parameshvara eva dyumUrdhatvAdivishiShTo.avasthAntaragataH pratyagAtmatvenopanyasta AdhyAnAyeti gamyate, kAraNatvAt | kAraNasya hi sarvAbhiH kAryagatAbhir avasthAbhir avasthAvattvAt dyulokAdyavayavatvam upapadyate | sa sarveShu lokeShu sarveShu bhUteShu sarveShvatmasvannam atti iti ca sarvalokAdyAshrayaM phalaM shrUyamANaM paramakAraNaparigrahe sambhavati, evaM hAsya sarve pApmAnaH pradUyante iti ca tadvidaH sarvapApmapradAhashravaNam, ko na AtmA kiM brahma iti cAtmabrahmashabdAbhyAm upakramaH | ityevam antAni brahmaliN^gAni parameshvaram eva gamayanti | tasmAt parameshvara eva vaishvAnaraH ||24||

|| 1.2.25 ||

smaryamANam anumAnaM syAd iti || 


itashca parameshvara eva vaishvAnaraH | yasmAt parameshvarasyaiva agnir AsyaM dyaur mUrdhA itIdR^ishaM trailokyAtmakaM rUpaM smaryate -- 

yasyAgnir AsyaM dyaur mUrdhA khaM nAbhishcaraNau kShitiH | 
sUryashcakShur dishaH shrotraM tasmai lokAtmane namaH || iti | 

tat smaryamANaM rUpaM mUlabhUtAM shrutim anumApayad asya vaishvAnarashabdasya parameshvaraparatve anumAnaM liN^gaM gamakaM syAd ityarthaH | itishabdo hetvarthe -- yasmAd idaM gamakam, tasmAd api vaishvAnaraH paramAtmaivetyarthaH | yadyapi stutiH iyam -- tasmai lokAtmane namaH iti, tathApi stutitvam api nAsati mUlabhUte vedavAkye samyak IdR^ishena rUpeNa sambhavati | 

dyAM mUrdhAnaM yasya viprA vadanti 
khaM vai nAbhiM candrasUryau ca netre | 
dishaH shrotre viddhi pAdau kShitiM ca 
so.acintyAtmA sarvabhUtapraNetA ||

ityevaMjAtIyakA ca smR^itiH ihodAhartavyA ||25||

|| 1.2.26 ||

shabdAdibhyo.antaHpratiShThAnAcca neti cen na, 
tathAdR^iShTyupadeshAsambhavAt, 
puruShavidham api cainam adhIyate ||

atrAha -- na parameshvaro vaishvAnaro bhavitum arhati | kutaH? shabdAdibhyo.antaHpratiShThAnAcca | shabdaH tAvat -- vaishvAnarashabdo na parameshvare sambhavati, arthAntare rUDhatvAt | tathAgnishabdaH sa eSho.agnir vaishvAnaraH iti | AdishabdAt hR^idayaM gArhapatyaH ityAdyagnitretAprakalpanam | tad yad bhaktaM prathamam Agacchet tad dhomIyam ityAdinA ca prANAhutyadhikaraNatAsaN^kIrtanam | etebhyo hetubhyo jATharo vaishvAnaraH pratyetavyaH | tathAntaHpratiShThAnam api shrUyate -- puruShe.antaH pratiShThitaM veda iti | tacca jAThare sambhavati | yad apyuktam mUrdhaiva sutejAH ityAder visheShAt kAraNAt paramAtmA vaishvAnara iti |

atra brUmaH -- kuto nv eSha nirNayaH, yad ubhayathApi visheShapratibhAne sati parameshvaraviShaya eva visheSha AshrayaNIyo na jATharaviShaya iti | athavA bhUtAgner antar bahishcAvatiShThamAnasyaiSha nirdesho bhaviShyati | tasyApi hi dyulokAdisambandho mantravarNe avagamyate -- yo bhAnunA pR^ithivIM dyAm utemAm AtatAna rodasI antarikSham [R^i.ve. 10.88.3] ityAdau | 

athavA taccharIrAyA devatAyA aishvaryayogAt dyulokAdyavayavatvaM bhaviShyati | tasmAn na parameshvaro vaishvAnara iti || 

atrocyate -- na tathAdR^iShTyopadeshAd iti | na shabdAdibhyaH kAraNebhyaH parameshvarasya pratyAkhyAnaM yuktam | kutaH? tathA jATharAparityAgena, dR^iShTyopadeshAt | parameshvaradR^iShTir hi jAThare vaishvAnare ihopadishyate -- mano brahmetyupAsIta ityAdivat | athavA jATharavaishvAnaropAdhiH parameshvara iha draShTavyatvenopadishyate -- manomayaH prANasharIro bhArUpaH ityAdivat | yadi ceha parameshvaro na vivakShyeta, kevala eva jATharo.agnir vivakShyeta, tataH mUrdhaiva sutejAH ityAder visheShasyAsambhava eva syAt | yathA tu devatAbhUtAgnivyapAshrayeNApyayaM visheSha upapAdayituM na shakyate, tathottarasUtre vakShyAmaH | yadi ca kevala eva jATharo vivakShyeta, puruShe.antaHpratiShThitatvaM kevalaM tasya syAt | na tu puruShatvam | puruSham api cainam adhIyate vAjasaneyinaH -- sa eSho.agnir vaishvAnaro yat puruShaH sa yo haitam evam agniM vaishvAnaraM puruShaM puruShe.antaH pratiShThitaM veda iti | parameshvarasya tu sarvAtmatvAt puruShatvaM puruShe.antaHpratiShThitatvaM cobhayam upapadyate | ye tu puruShavidham api cainam adhIyate iti sUtrAvayavaM paThanti, teShAm eSho.arthaH -- kevalajATharaparigrahe puruShe.antaHpratiShThitatvaM kevalaM syAt | na tu puruShavidhatvam | puruShavidham api cainam adhIyate vAjasaneyinaH -- puruShavidhaM puruShe.antaH pratiShThitaM veda iti | puruShavidhatvaM ca prakaraNAt yad adhidaivataM dyumUrdhatvAdi pR^ithivIpratiShThitatvAntam, yaccAdhyAtmaM prasiddhaM mUrdhatvAdi cubukapratiShThitatvAntam, tat parigR^ihyate ||

|| 1.2.27 ||

ata eva na devatA bhUtaM ca ||

yat punar uktam -- bhUtAgner api mantravarNe dyulokAdisambandhadarshanAt mUrdhaiva sutejAH ityAdyavayavakalpanaM tasyaiva bhaviShyatIti, taccharIrAyA devatAyA vA aishvaryayogAd iti | tat parihartavyam | atrocyate -- ata evoktebhyo hetubhyo na devatA vaishvAnaraH | tathA bhUtAgnir api na vaishvAnaraH | na hi bhUtAgner auShNyaprakAshamAtrAtmakasya dyumUrdhatvAdikalpanopapadyate, vikArasya vikArAntarAtmatvAsambhavAt | tathA devatAyAH satyapyaishvaryayoge na dyumUrdhatvAdikalpanA sambhavati, akAraNatvAt parameshvarAdhIn aishvaryatvAcca | AtmashabdAsambhavashca sarveShv eShu pakSheShu sthita eva ||

|| 1.2.28 ||

sAkShAd apyavirodhaM jaiminiH ||

pUrvaM jATharAgnipratIko jATharAgnyupAdhiko vA parameshvara upAsya ityuktam antaHpratiShThitatvAdyanurodhena | idAnIM tu vinaiva pratIkopAdhikalpanAbhyAM sAkShAd api parameshvaropAsanaparigrahe na kashcid virodha iti jaiminir AcAryo manyate | 

nanu jATharAgnyaparigrahe.antaHpratiShThitatvavacanaM shabdAdIni ca kAraNAni virudhyerann iti | atrocyate -- antaHpratiShThitatvavacanaM tAvan na virudhyate | na hIha puruShavidhaM puruShe.antaH pratiShThitaM veda iti jATharAgnyabhiprAyeNedam ucyate, tasyAprakR^itatvAd asaMshabditatvAcca | kathaM tarhi, yat prakR^itaM mUrdhAdicubukAnteShu puruShAvayaveShu puruShavidhatvaM kalpitam, tadabhiprAyeNedam ucyate -- puruShavidhaM puruShe.antaH pratiShThitaM veda iti | yathA vR^ikShe shAkhAM pratiShThitAM pashyatIti, tadvat | 

athavA yaH prakR^itaH paramAtmAdhyAtmam adhidaivataM ca puruShavidhatvopAdhiH, tasya yat kevalaM sAkShirUpam, tadabhiprAyeNedam ucyate -- puruShavidhaM puruShe.antaH pratiShThitaM veda iti | nishcite ca pUrvAparAlocanavashena paramAtmaparigrahe, tadviShaya eva vaishvAnarashabdaH kenacid yogena vartiShyate -- vishvashcAyaM narashceti, vishveShAM vAyaM naraH, vishve vA narA asyeti vishvAnaraH paramAtmA, sarvAtmatvAt, vishvAnara eva vaishvAnaraH | taddhito.ananyArthaH, rAkShasavAyasAdivat | agnishabdo.apyagraNItvAdiyogAshrayaNena paramAtmaviShaya eva bhaviShyati | gArhapatyAdikalpanaM prANAhutyadhikaraNatvaM ca paramAtmano.api sarvAtmatvAd upapadyate ||28|

|| 1.2.29 ||

kathaM punaH parameshvaraparigrahe prAdeshamAtrashrutir upapadyata iti, tAM vyAkhyAtum Arabhate -- 

abhivyakteH ityAshmarathyaH ||

atimAtrasyApi parameshvarasya prAdeshamAtratvam abhivyaktinimittaM syAt | abhivyajyate kila prAdeshamAtraparimANaH parameshvara upAsakAnAM kR^ite | pradeshavisheSheShu vA hR^idayAdiShUpalabdhisthAneShu visheSheNAbhivyajyate | ataH parameshvare.api prAdeshamAtrashrutir abhivyakter upapadyata ityAshmarathya AcAryo manyate ||

|| 1.2.30 ||

anusmR^iter bAdariH ||

prAdeshamAtrahR^idayapratiShThitena vAyaM manasAnusmaryate | tena prAdeshamAtraH ityucyate | yathA prasthamitA yavAH prasthA ityucyante, tadvat | yadyapi ca yaveShu svagatam eva parimANaM prasthasambandhAd vyajyate, na ceha parameshvaragataM kiMcit parimANam asti -- yad dhR^idayasambandhAd vyajyeta | tathApi prayuktAyAH prAdeshamAtrashruteH sambhavati yathAkathaMcid anusmaraNam Alambanam ityucyate | prAdeshamAtratvena vAyamaprAdeshamAtro.apyanusmaraNIyaH prAdeshamAtrashrutyarthavattAyai | evam anusmR^itinimittA parameshvare prAdeshamAtrashrutiH iti bAdarir AcAryo manyate ||

|| 1.2.31 || 

sampatteH iti jaiminiH tathA hi darshayati ||

sampattinimittA vA syAt prAdeshamAtrashrutiH | kutaH? tathA hi samAnaprakaraNaM vAjasaneyibrAhmaNaM dyuprabhR^itIn pR^ithivIparyantAMH trailokyAtmano vaishvAnarasyAvayavAnadhyAtmamUrdhaprabhR^itiShu cubukaparyanteShu dehAvayaveShu sampAdayatprAdeshamAtrasampattiM parameshvarasya darshayati -- prAdeshamAtram iva ha vai devAH suviditA abhisampannAH tathA tu va evAnvakShyAmi yathA prAdeshamAtram evAbhisampAdayiShyAmIti | sa hovAca mUrdhAnam upadishann uvAcaiSha vA atiShThA vaishvAnara iti | cakShuShI upadishann uvAcaiSha vai sutejA vaishvAnara iti | nAsike upadishann uvAcaiSha vai pR^ithagvartmAtmA vaishvAnara iti | mukhyam AkAsham upadishann uvAcaiSha vai bahulo vaishvAnara iti | mukhyA apa upadishann uvAcaiSha vai rayir vaishvAnara iti | cubukam upadishann uvAcaiSha vai pratiShThA vaishvAnaraH iti | cubukam ityadharaM mukhaphalakam ucyate | yadyapi vAjasaneyake dyaur atiShThatvaguNA samAmnAyate, Adityashca sutejastvaguNaH, chAndogye punaH dyauH sutejastvaguNA samAmnAyate, Adityashca vishvarUpatvaguNaH | tathApi naitAvatA visheSheNa kiMcid dhIyate, prAdeshamAtrashruter avisheShAt, sarvashAkhApratyayatvAcca | sampattinimittAM prAdeshamAtrashrutiM yuktatarAM jaiminir AcAryo manyate ||31||

|| 1.2.32 || 

Amananti cainamasmin || 

Amananti cainaM parameshvaram asmin mUrdhacubukAntarAle jAbAlAH -- ya eSho.ananto.avyakta AtmA so.avimukte pratiShThita iti | so.avimuktaH kasmin pratiShThita iti | varaNAyAM nAsyAM ca madhye pratiShThita iti | kA vai varaNA kA ca nAsIti | tatra cemAm eva nAsikAm sarvANIndriyakR^itAni pApAni vArayatIti sA varaNA, sarvANIndriyakR^itAni pApAni nAshayatIti sA nAsI iti varaNAnAsIti nirucya, punar apyAmananti -- katamaccAsya sthAnaM bhavatIti | bhruvor ghrANasya ca yaH sandhiH sa eSha dyulokasya parasya ca sandhir bhavati iti | tasmAd upapannA parameshvare prAdeshamAtrashrutiH | abhivimAnashrutiH pratyagAtmatvAbhiprAyA | pratyagAtmatayA sarvaiH prANibhir abhivimIyata ityabhivimAnaH | abhigato vAyaM pratyagAtmatvAt, vimAnashca mAnaviyogAt ityabhivimAnaH | abhivimimIte vA sarvaM jagat, kAraNatvAd ityabhivimAnaH | tasmAt parameshvaro vaishvAnara iti siddham ||32||

iti shrImatparamahaMsaparivrAjakAcAryasya shrIgovindabhagavatpUjyapAdashiShyasya shrImacchaN^karabhagavataH kR^itau shArIrakamImAMsAsUtrabhAShye prathamAdhyAyasya dvitIyaH pAdaH || 

 

(1.3)

|| prathamAdhyAye tR^itIyaH pAdaH || 

atrAspaShTabrahmaliN^gAnAM prAyo j~neyabrahmaviShayANAM vicAraH |
evaM pAdatrayeNApi vAkyavicAraH ||

1. dyubhvAdyadhikaraNam
