|| 1.3.1 || 

idaM shrUyate -- 

yasmin dyauH pR^ithivI cAntarikSham 
otaM manaH saha prANaishca sarvaiH | 
tam evaikaM jAnatha AtmAnam anyA 
vAco vimuJNcathAmR^itasyaiSha setuH || [mu.u. 2.2.5] iti | 

atra yad etad dyuprabhR^itInAm otatvavacanAd AyatanaM kiMcid avagamyate, tat kiM paraM brahma syAt, Aho svid arthAntaram ? iti sandihyate | tatrArthAntaraM kim apyAyatanaM syAd iti prAptam | kasmAt? amR^itasyaiSha setuH iti shravaNAt | pAravAn hi loke setuH prakhyAtaH | na ca parasya brahmaNaH pAravattvaM shakyam abhyupagantum -- anantam apAram iti shravaNAt | arthAntare cAyatane parigR^ihyamANe smR^itiprasiddhaM pradhAnaM parigrahItavyam, tasya kAraNatvAd AyatanatvopapatteH | shrutiprasiddho vA vAyuH syAt -- vAyur vAva gautama tat sUtraM vAyunA vai gautama sUtreNAyaM ca lokaH parashca lokaH sarvANi ca bhUtAni sandR^ibdhAni bhavanti iti vAyor api vidhAraNatvashravaNAt | shArIro vA syAt | tasyApi bhoktR^itvAt, bhogyaM prapaJNcaM pratyAyatanatvopapatteH ityevaM prApte -- 

dyubhvAdyAyatanaM svashabdAt ||

idam Aha -- dyubhvAdyAyatanam iti | dyaushca bhUshca dyubhuvau, dyubhuvau AdI yasya tadidaM dyubhvAdi | yadetadasmin vAkye dyauH pR^ithivyantarikShaM manaH prANA ityevamAtmakaM jagat otatvena nirdiShTAm, tasyAyatanaM paraM brahma bhavitum arhati | kutaH? svashabdAt AtmashabdAdityarthaH | Atmashabdo hIha bhavati -- tam evaikaM jAnatha AtmAnam iti | Atmashabdashca paramAtmaparigrahe samyagavakalpate, nArthAntaraparigrahe | kvacicca svashabdenaiva brahmaNa Ayatanatva shrUyate -- sanmUlAH somyemAH sarvAH prajAH sadAyatanAH satpratiShThAH iti | svashabdenaiva ceha purastAdupariShTAcca brahma saN^kIrtyate -- puruSha evedaM vishvaM karma tapo brahma parAmR^itam iti, brahmaivedamamR^itaM purastAdbrahma pashcAdbrahma dakShiNatashcottareNa iti ca | tatra tvAyatanAyatanavadbhAvashravaNAt | sarvaM brahmeti ca sAmAnAdhikaraNyAt, yathA hyanekAtmako vR^ikShaH shAkhA skandho mUlaM ceti, evaM nAnAraso vicitra AtmetyAshaN^kA sambhavati | tAM nivartayituM sAvadhAraNam Aha -- tam evaikaM jAnatha AtmAnam iti | etad uktaM bhavati -- na kAryaprapaJNcavishiShTo vicitra AtmA vij~neyaH | kiM tarhi, avidyAkR^itaM kAryaprapaJNcaM vidyayA pravilApayantaH tam evaikam AyatanabhUtam AtmAnaM jAnatha ekarasam iti | yathA yasminn Aste devadattaH tad Anaya ityukte Asanam evAnayati, na devadattam | tadvad AyatanabhUtasyaivaikarasasyAtmano vij~neyatvam upadishyate | vikArAn R^itAbhisandhasya cApavAdaH shrUyate -- mR^ityoH sa mR^ityum Apnoti ya iha nAneva pashyati iti | sarvaM brahma iti tu sAmAnAdhikaraNyaM prapaJNcavilApanArtham, na anekarasatApratipAdanArtham, sa yathA saindhavaghano.anantaro.abAhyaH kR^itsno rasaghana evaivaM vA are.ayam AtmAnantaro.abAhyaH kR^itsnaH praj~nAnaghana eva ityekarasatAshravaNAt | tasmAd dyubhvAdyAyatanaM paraM brahma | 

yat tUktam -- setushruteH, setoshca pAravattvopapatteH, brahmaNo.arthAntareNa dyubhvAdyAyatanena bhavitavyam iti, atrocyate -- vidhAraNatvamAtram eva setushrutyA vivakShyate, na pAravattvAdi | na hi mR^iddArumayo loke setur dR^iShTa ityatrApi mR^iddArumaya eva setur abhyupagamyate | setushabdArtho.api vidhAraNatvamAtram eva, na pAravattvAdi, ShiJNo bandhanakarmaNaH setushabdavyutpatteH | apara Aha -- tam evaikaM jAnatha AtmAnam iti yad etat saN^kIrtitam Atmaj~nAnam, yaccaitat anyA vAco vimuJNcatha iti vAgvimocanam, tat atra amR^itatvasAdhanatvAt, amR^itasyaiSha setuH iti setushrutyA saN^kIrtyate | na tu dyubhvAdyAyatanam | tatra yad uktam -- setushruter brahmaNo.arthAntareNa dyubhvAdyAyatanena bhavitavyam iti, etad ayuktam ||1||


 || 1.3.2 || 

muktopasR^ipyavyapadeshAt ||

itashca param eva brahma dyubhvAdyAyatanam | yasmAn muktopasR^ipyatAsya vyapadishyamAnA dR^ishyate | muktair upasR^ipyaM muktopasR^ipyam | dehAdiShvanAtmasu aham asmItyAtmabuddhir avidyA, tataH tatpUjanAdau rAgaH, tatparibhavAdau ca dveShaH, 
taducchedadarshanAd bhayaM mohashca -- ityevam ayam anantabhedo.anarthavrAtaH saMtataH sarveShAM naH pratyakShaH | tadviparyayeNAvidyArAgadveShAdidoShamuktair upasR^ipyam upagamyam etad iti dyubhvAdyAyatanaM prakR^itya vyapadesho bhavati | katham? 

bhidyate hR^idayagranthishchidyante sarvasaMshayAH | 
kShIyante cAsya karmANi tasmin dR^iShTo parAvare || [mu.u. 2.2.8]

ityuktvA, bravIti -- tathA vidvAn nAmarUpAd vimuktaH parAt paraM puruSham upaiti divyam [mu.u. 3.2.8] iti | brahmaNashca muktopasR^ipyatvaM prasiddhaM shAstre -- 

yadA sarve pramucyante kAmA ye.asya hR^idi shritAH | 
atha martyo.amR^ito bhavatyatra brahma samashnute || ityevam Adau | 

pradhAnAdInAM tu na kvacin muktopasR^ipyatvam asti prasiddham | api ca tam evaikaM jAnatha AtmAnamanyA vAco vimuJNcathAmR^itasyaiSha setuH iti vAgvimokapUrvakaM vij~neyatvam iha dyubhvAdyAyatanasyocyate | tacca shrutyantare brahmaNo dR^iShTam -- 

tam eva dhIro vij~nAya praj~nAM kurvIta brAhmaNaH |
nAnudhyAyAd bahUJNshabdAn vAco viglApanaM hi tat || [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.21] iti | 

tasmAd api dyubhvAdyAyatanaM paraM brahma ||2||

|| 1.3.3 || 

nAnumAnam atacchabdAt ||

yathA brahmaNaH pratipAdako vaisheShiko hetur uktaH, naivam arthAntarasya vaisheShiko hetuH pratipAdako.astItyAha | nAnumAnaM sAN^khyasmR^itiparikalpitaM pradhAnam iha dyubhvAdyAyatanatvena pratipattavyam | kasmAt? atacchabdAt | tasyAcetanasya pradhAnasya pratipAdakaH shabdaH tacchabdaH, na tacchabdo.atacchabdaH | na hyatrAcetanasya pradhAnasya pratipAdakaH kashcicchabdo.asti, yenAcetanaM pradhAnaM kAraNatvenAyatanatvena vAvagamyeta | tadviparItasya cetanasya pratipAdakashabdo.atrAsti -- yaH sarvaj~naH sarvavit [mu.u. 1.1.9] ityAdiH | ata eva na vAyur apIha dyubhvAdyAyatanatvenAshrIyate ||3||

|| 1.3.4 || 

prANabhR^icca ||

yadyapi prANabhR^ito vij~nAnAtmana AtmatvaM cetanatvaM ca sambhavati, tathApyupAdhiparicchinnaj~nAnasya sarvaj~natvAdyasambhave sati asmAd evAtacchabdAt prANabhR^id api na dyubhvAdyAyatanatvenAshrayitavyaH | na copAdhiparicchinnasyAvibhoH prANabhR^ito dyubhvAdyAyatanatvam api samyak sambhavati | pR^ithagyogakaraNam uttarArtham ||4|| 

|| 1.3.5 || 

kutashca na prANabhR^it dyubhvAdyAyatanatvenAshrayitavyaH? -- 

bhedavyapadeshAt ||

bhedavyapadeshashceha bhavati -- tam evaikaM jAnatha AtmAnam iti j~neyaj~nAtR^ibhAvena | tatra prANabhR^it tAvan mumukShutvAjj~nAtA | parisheShAd AtmashabdavAcyaM brahma j~neyaM dyubhvAdyAyatanam iti gamyate, na prANabhR^it ||5|| 

|| 1.3.6 || 

kutashca na prANabhR^it dyubhvAdyAyatanatvenAshrayitavyaH? -- 

akaraNAt || 

prakaraNaM cedaM paramAtmanaH -- kasmin nu bhagavo vij~nAte sarvam idaM vij~nAtaM bhavati [mu.u. 1.1.3] ityekavij~nAnena sarvavij~nAnApekShaNAt | paramAtmani hi sarvAtmake vij~nAte sarvam idaM vij~nAtaM syAt, na kevale prANabhR^iti ||6|| 

|| 1.3.7 || 

kutashca na prANabhR^it dyubhvAdyAyatanatvenAshrayitavyaH? -- 

sthityadanAbhyAM ca ||

dyubhvAdyAyatanaM ca prakR^itya, dvA suparNA sayujA sakhAyA ityatra sthityadane nirdishyete -- tayor anyaH pippalaM svAdvatti iti karmaphalAshanam | anashnann anyo.abhicAkashIti ityaudAsInyenAvasthAnam | tAbhyAM ca sthityadanAbhyAm IshvarakShetraj~nau tatra gR^ihyete | yadi ca Ishvaro dyubhvAdyAyatanatvena vivakShitaH, tataH tasya prakR^itasyeshvarasya kShetraj~nAt pR^ithagvacanam avakalpate | anyathA hyaprakR^itavacanam Akasmikam asambaddhaM syAt | 

nanu tavApi kShetraj~nasyeshvarAt pR^ithagvacanam Akasmikam eva prasajyeta | na, tasyAvivakShitatvAt | kShetraj~no hi kartR^itvena bhoktR^itvena ca pratisharIraM buddhyAdyupAdhisambaddhaH, lokata eva prasiddhaH, nAsau shrutyA tAtparyeNa vivakShyate | IshvaraH tu lokato.aprasiddhatvAcchrutyA tAtparyeNa vivakShyata iti na tasyAkasmikaM vacanaM yuktam | guhAM praviShTAvatmAnau hi [ve.sU. 1.2.11] iti | 

atrApyetad darshitam -- dvA suparNA ityasyAm R^ici IshvarakShetraj~nAv ucyete iti | yadApi paiN^gyupaniShatkR^itena vyAkhyAnenAsyAm R^ici sattvakShetraj~nAv ucyete, tadApi na virodhaH kashcit | katham? prANabhR^id dhIha ghaTAdicchidravat sattvAd yupAdhyabhimAnitvena pratisharIraM gR^ihyamANo dyubhvAdyAyatanaM na bhavatIti pratiShidhyate | yaH tu sarvasharIreShUpAdhibhir vinopalakShyate, par eva sa bhavati | yathA ghaTAdicchidrANi ghaTAdibhir upAdhibhir vinopalakShyamANAni mahAkAsha eva bhavanti, tadvat prANabhR^itaH parasmAd anyatvAnupapatteH pratiShedho nopapadyate | tasmAt sattvAd yupAdhyabhimAnina eva dyubhvAdyAyatanatvapratiShedhaH | tasmAt param eva brahma dyubhvAdyAyatanam | tad etat adR^ishyatvAdiguNako dharmokteH ityanenaiva siddham | tasyaiva hi bhUtayonivAkyasya madhye idaM paThitam -- yasmin dyauH pR^ithivI cAntarikSham [mu.u. 2.2.5] iti | prapaJNcArthaM tu punar upanyastam ||7||

  -- o)0(o -- 
bhUmAdhikaraNam

|| 1.3.8 || 

idaM samAmananti -- 

bhUmA tv eva vijij~nAsitavya iti bhUmAnaM bhagavo vijij~nAsa iti | yatra nAnyat pashyati nAnyacchR^iNoti nAnyad vijAnAti sa bhUmA | atha yatrAnyat pashyatyanyacchR^iNotyanyad vijAnAti tad alpam [chA.u. 7.23.1] ityAdi |

tatra saMshayaH -- kiM prANo bhUmA syAt, Aho svit paramAtmeti | kutaH saMshayaH? bhUmeti tAvad bahutvam abhidhIyate | bhorlopo bhU ca bahoH iti bhUmashabdasya bhAvapratyayAntatAsmaraNAt | kimAtmakaM punaH tad bahutvam iti visheShAkAN^kShAyAm prANo vA AshAyA bhUyAn iti saMnidhAnAt prANo bhUmeti pratibhAti | tathA shrutaM hyeva me bhagavaddR^ishebhyaH tarati shokam Atmavid iti | so.ahaM bhagavaH shocAmi taM mA bhagavAJNshokasya pAraM tArayatu iti prakaraNotthAnAt paramAtmA bhUmetyapi pratibhAti | tatra kasyopAdAnaM nyAyyam, kasya vA hAnam iti bhavati saMshayaH | 

kiM tAvat prAptam? prANo bhUmeti | kasmAt? bhUyaHprashnaprativacanaparamparAdarshanAt | yathA hi asti bhagavo nAmno bhUyaH [bR^i.A.u. 7.1.5] iti, vAg vAva nAmno bhUyasI [bR^i.A.u. 7.2.1] iti | tathA asti bhagavo vAco bhUyaH [bR^i.A.u. 7.2.2] iti, mano vAva vAco bhUyaH [bR^i.A.u. 7.3.1] iti ca -- nAmAdibhyo hi AprANAt bhUyaHprashnaprativacanapravAhaH pravR^ittaH | naivaM prANAt paraM bhUyaHprashnaprativacanaM dR^ishyate -- asti bhagavaH prANAd bhUyaH iti, ado vAva prANAd bhUyaH iti | prANam eva tu nAmAdibhya AshAntebhyo bhUyAMsam, prANo vA AshAyA bhUyAn ityAdinA saprapaJNcam uktvA, prANadarshinashcAtivAditvam ativAdyasItyativAdyasmIti brUyAn nApahnuvIta ityabhyanuj~nAya, eSha tu vA ativadati yaH satyenAtivadati iti prANavratam ativAditvam anukR^iShya, aparityajyaiva prANaM satyAdiparamparayA bhUmAnam avatArayan, prANam eva bhUmAnaM manyata iti gamyate | 

kathaM punaH prANe bhUmani vyAkhyAyamAne yatra nAnyat pashyati ityetad bhUmno lakShaNaparaM vacanaM vyAkhyAyeteti, ucyate -- suShuptAvasthAyAM prANagrasteShu karaNeShu darshanAdivyavahAranivR^ittidarshanAt sambhavati prANasyApi yatra nAnyat pashyatIti etallakShaNam | tathA ca shrutiH -- na shR^iNoti na pashyati ityAdinA sarvakaraNavyApArapratyastamayarUpAM suShuptyavasthAm uktvA, prANAgnaya evaitasmin pure jAgrati iti tasyAm evAvasthAyAM paJNcavR^itteH prANasya jAgaraNaM bruvatI, prANapradhAnAM suShuptyavasthAM darshayati | yaccaitad bhUmnaH sukhatvaM shrutam -- yo vai bhUmA tat sukham iti, tad apyaviruddham | atraiSha devaH svapnAn na pashyatyatha yad etasmiJNsharIre sukhaM bhavati iti suShuptyavasthAyAm eva sukhashravaNAt | yacca yo vai bhUmA tad amR^itam iti, tad api prANasyAviruddham | prANo vA amR^itam iti shruteH | 

kathaM punaH prANaM bhUmAnaM manyamAnasya tarati shokam Atmavit ityAtmavividiShayA prakaraNasyotthAnam upapadyate? prANa evehAtmA vivakShita iti brUmaH | tathA hi -- prANo ha pitA prANo mAtA prANo bhrAtA prANaH svasA prANa AcAryaH prANo brAhmaNaH iti prANam eva sarvAtmAnaM karoti, yathA vA arA nAbhau samarpitA evamasmin prANe sarvaM samarpitam iti ca | sarvAtmatvAranAbhinidarshanAbhyAM ca sambhavati vaipulyAtmikA bhUmarUpatA prANasya | tasmAt prANo bhUmetyevaM prAptam || 

bhUmA samprasAdAd adhyupadeshAt ||

tata idam ucyate -- paramAtmaiveha bhUmA bhavitum arhati, na prANaH | kasmAt? samprasAdAd adhyupadeshAt | samprasAda iti suShuptaM sthAnam ucyate | samyak prasIdatyasminn iti nirvacanAt, bR^ihadAraNyake ca svapnajAgaritasthAnAbhyAM saha pAThAt | tasyAM ca samprasAdAvasthAyAM prANo jAgartIti prANo.atra samprasAdo.abhipreyate | prANAd UrdhvaM bhUmna upadishyamAnatvAd ityarthaH | prANa eva ced bhUmA syAt, sa eva tasmAd Urdhvam upadishyetetyAshliShTam etat syAt | na hi nAmaiva nAmno bhUyaH iti nAmna Urdhvam upadiShTam | kiM tarhi, nAmno.anyad arthAntaram upadiShTaM vAgAkhyam vAg vAva nAmno bhUyasI iti | tathA vAgAdibhyo.api A prANAd arthAntaram eva tatra tatrordhvam upadiShTam | tadvat prANAd Urdhvam upadishyamAno bhUmA prANAd arthAntarabhUto bhavitum arhati | 

nanviha nAsti prashnaH -- asti bhagavaH prANAd bhUyaH iti | nApi prativacanam asti prANAd vAva bhUyo.asti iti | kathaM prANAd adhi bhUmopadishyata ityucyate? prANaviShayam eva cAtivAditvam uttaratrAnukR^iShyamANaM pashyAmaH -- eSha tu vA ativadati yaH satyenAtivadati iti | tasmAn nAsti prANAd adhyupadesha iti | atrocyate -- na tAvat prANaviShayasyaivAtivAditvasyaitad anukarShaNam iti shakyaM vaktum, visheShavAdAt -- yaH satyenAtivadati iti | 

nanu visheShavAdo.apyayaM prANaviShaya eva bhaviShyati | katham? yathA eSho.agnihotrI, yaH satyaM vadati ityukte, na satyavadanenAgnihotritvam | kena tarhi? agnihotreNaiva | tatsatyavadanaM tu agnihotriNo visheSha ucyate | tathA eSha tu vA ativadati, yaH satyenAtivadati ityukte, na satyavadanenAtivAditvam | kena tarhi? prakR^itena prANavij~nAnenaiva | satyavadanaM tu prANavido visheSho vivakShyata iti -- neti brUmaH | shrutyarthaparityAgaprasaN^gAt | shrutyA hyatra satyavadanenAtivAditvaM pratIyate -- yaH satyenAtivadati so.ativadati iti | nAtra prANavij~nAnasya saN^kIrtanam asti | prakaraNAt tu prANavij~nAnaM sambadhyeta | tatra prakaraNAnurodhena shrutiH parityaktA syAt | prakR^itavyAvR^ittyarthashca tushabdo na saMgaccheta -- eSha tu vA ativadati iti | satyaM tv eva vijij~nAsitavyam iti ca prayatnAntarakaraNam arthAntaravivakShAM sUcayati | tasmAd yathaikavedaprashaMsAyAM prakR^itAyAm, eSha tu mahAbrAhmaNaH, yashcaturo vedAn adhIte ityekavedebhyo.arthAntarabhUtashcaturvedaH prashasyate, tAdR^ig etad draShTavyam | na ca prashnaprativacanarUpayaivArthAntaravivakShayA bhavitavyam iti niyamo.asti | prakR^itasambandhAsambhavakAritatvAd arthAntaravivakShAyAH | tatra prANAntam anushAsanaM shrutvA tUShNImbhUtaM nAradaM svayam eva sanatkumAro vyutpAdayati -- yat prANavij~nAnena vikArAnR^itaviShayeNAtivAditvam anativAditvam eva tat -- eSha tu vA ativadati, yaH satyenAtivadati iti | tatra satyam iti paraM brahmocyate, paramArtharUpatvAt | satyaM j~nAnam anantaM brahma [tai.u. 2.3] iti ca shrutyantarAt | tathA vyutpAtitAya nAradAya so.ahaM bhagavaH satyenAtivadAni [chA.u. 7.16.1] ityevaM pravR^ittAya vij~nAnAdisAdhanaparamparayA bhUmAnam upadishati | tatra yat prANAd adhi satyaM vaktavyaM pratij~nAtam, tad eveha bhUmetyucyata iti gamyate | tasmAd asti prANAd adhi bhUmna upadesha iti -- ataH prANAd anyaH paramAtmA bhUmA bhavitum arhatIti | evaM cehAtmavividiShayA prakaraNasyotthAnam upapannaM bhaviShyati | prANa evehAtmA vivakShita ityetad api nopapadyate | na hi prANasya mukhyayA vR^ittyAtmatvam asti | na cAnyatra paramAtmaj~nAnAcchokavinivR^ittir asti, nAnyaH panthA vidyate.ayanAya iti shrutyantarAt | taM mA bhagavAJNshokasya pAraM tArayatu iti copakramyopasaMharati -- tasmai mR^iditakaShAyAya tamasaH pAraM darshayati bhagavAn sanatkumAraH [chA.u. 7.26.1] iti | tama iti shokAdikAraNam avidyocyeta | prANAnte cAnushAsane na prANasyAnyAyattatocyate | AtmataH prANaH iti ca brAhmaNam | prakaraNAnte paramAtmavivakShA bhaviShyati | bhUmAtra prANa eveti cet, na | sa bhagavaH kasmin pratiShThita iti sve mahimni ityAdinA bhUmna eva A prakaraNasamApter nanukarShaNAt | vaipulyAtmikA ca bhUmarUpatA sarvakAraNatvAt paramAtmanaH sutarAm upapadyate ||8||

|| 1.3.9 ||

dharmopapatteshca ||

api ca ye bhUmni shrUyante dharmAH, te paramAtmanyupapadyante | yatra nAnyat pashyati nAnyacchR^iNoti nAnyad vijAnAti sa bhUmA iti darshanAdivyavahArAbhAvaM bhUmani avagamayati | paramAtmani cAyaM darshanAdivyavahArAbhAvo.avagataH -- yatra tu asya sarvam AtmaivAbhUt tat kena kaM pashyet [bR^i.A.u. 4.5.15] ityAdishrutyantarAt | yo.apyasau suShuptyavasthAyAM darshanAdivyavahArAbhAva uktaH, so.apyAtmana evAsaN^gatvavivakShayoktaH, na prANasvabhAvavivakShayA, paramAtmaprakaraNAt | 

yad api tasyAm avasthAyAM sukhamuktam, tad apyAtmana eva sukharUpatvavivakShayoktam | yata Aha -- eSho.asya parama Ananda etasyaivAnandasyAnyAni bhUtAni mAtrAm upajIvanti iti | ihApi yo vai bhUmA tat sukhaM nAlpe sukham asti bhUmaiva sukham [chA.u. 7.23.1] iti sAmayasukhanirAkaraNena brahmaiva sukhaM bhUmAnaM darshayati | yo vai bhUmA tad amR^itam ityamR^itatvam apIha shrUyamANaM paramakAraNaM gamayati | vikArANAm amR^itatvasyApekShikatvAt, ato.anyad Artam iti ca shrutyantarAt | tathA ca satyatvaM svamahimapratiShThitatvaM sarvagatatvaM sarvAtmatvam iti caite dharmAH shrUyamANAH paramAtmanyevopapadyante, nAnyatra | tasmAd bhUmA paramAtmeti siddham ||9||

  -- o)0(o -- 
akSharAdhikaraNam

|| 1.3.10 || 

akSharam ambarAntadhR^iteH ||

kasmin nu khalvakAsha otashca protashceti sa hovAcaitad vai tad akSharaM gArgi brAhmaNA abhivadantyasthUlam anaNu [bR^i.A.u. 3.8.8] ityAdi shrUyate | tatra saMshayaH -- kim akSharashabdena varNa ucyate, kiM vA parameshvaraH ? iti | tatrAkSharasam AmnAya ityAdAvakSharashabdasya varNe prasiddhatvAt, prasiddhyatikramya cAyuktatvAt, oMkAra evedaM sarvam ityAdau ca shrutyantare varNasyApyupAsyatvena sarvAtmakatvAvadhAraNAt, varNa evAkSharashabda ityevaM prApte, ucyate -- para evAtmAkSharashabdavAcyaH | kasmAt? ambarAntadhR^iteH pR^ithivyAder AkAshAntasya vikArajAtasya dhAraNAt | tatra hi pR^ithivyAdeH samastavikArajAtasya kAlatrayavibhaktasya AkAsha eva tad otaM ca protaM ca ityAkAshe pratiShThitatvam uktvA, kasmin nu khalvakAsha otashca protashca ityanena prashnenedam akSharam avatAritam | tathA copasaMhR^itam -- etasmin nu khalvakShare gArgyAkAsha otashca protashca [bR^i.A.u. 3.8.11] iti | na ceyam ambarAntadhR^itir brahmaNo.anyatra sambhavati | yad api oMkAra evedaM sarvam iti, tad api brahmapratipattiH AdhanatvAt stutyarthaM draShTavyam | tasmin na kSharati ashnute ceti nityatvavyApitvAbhyAm akSharaM param eva brahma || 

|| 1.3.11 ||

syAd etat -- kAryasya cet kAraNAdhInatvam ambarAntadhR^itir abhyupagamyate, pradhAnakAraNavAdino.apIyam upapadyate | katham ambarAntadhR^iter brahmatvapratipattiH iti? ata uttaraM paThati -- 

sA ca prashAsanAt ||

sA ca ambarAntadhR^itiH parameshvarasyaiva karma | kasmAt? prashAsanAt | prashAsanaM hIha shrUyate -- etasya vA akSharasya prashAsane gArgi sUryAcandramasau vidhR^itau tiShThataH [bR^i.A.u. 3.8.9] ityAdi | prashAsanaM ca pArameshvaraM karma | na acetanasya prashAsanaM bhavati | na hyacetanAnAM ghaTAdikAraNAnAM mR^idAdInAM ghaTAdiviShayaM prashAsanam asti ||11||

|| 1.3.12 || 

anyabhAvavyAvR^itteshca ||

anyabhAvavyAvR^itteshca kAraNAd brahmaivAkSharashabdavAcyam, tasyaivAmbarAntadhR^itiH karma, nAnyasya kasyacit | kim idam anyabhAvavyAvR^itteH iti? anyasya bhAvo.anyabhAvaH tasmAd vyAvR^ittiH anyabhAvavyAvR^ittiH iti tasyAH | etad uktaM bhavati -- yad anyad brahmaNo.akSharashabdavAcyam ihAshaN^kyate tadbhAvAt idam ambarAntavidhAraNam akSharaM vyAvartayati shrutiH -- tad vA etad akSharaM gArgi adR^iShTaM draShTR^i ashrutaM shrotR^i amataM mantR^i avij~nAtaM vij~nAtR^i iti | tatrAdR^iShTatvAdivyapadeshaH pradhAnasyApi sambhavati | draShTR^itvAdivyapadeshaH tu na tasya sambhavati, acetanatvAt | tathA nAnyad ato.asti draShTR^i, nAnyad ato.asti shrotR^i, nAnyad ato.asti mantR^i, nAnyad ato.asti vij~nAtR^i ityAtmabhedapratiShedhAt, na shArIrasyApyupAdhimato.akSharashabdavAcyatvam | acakShuShkam ashrotram avAgamanaH iti copAdhimattApratiShedhAt | na hi nirupAdhikaH shArIro nAma bhavati | tasmAt param eva brahmAkSharam iti nishcayaH ||12||


4. IkShatikarmAdhikaraNam 

|| 1.3.13 || 

etad vai satyakAma paraM cAparaM ca brahma yad oMkAraH tasmAd vidvAn etenaivAyatane naikataram anveti [pra.u. 5.2] iti prakR^itya shrUyate -- yaH punar etaM trimAtreNom ityetenaivAkShareNa paraM puruSham abhidhyAyIta [pra.u. 5.5] iti | kim asmin vAkye paraM brahmAbhidhyAtavyam upadishyate, Aho svid aparam ? iti | etenaivAyatanena param aparaM vai kataram anvetIti prakR^itatvAt saMshayaH | 

tatrAparam idaM brahmeti prAptam | kasmAt? sa tejasi sUrye sampannaH sa sAmabhir unnIyate brahmalokam iti ca tadvido deshaparicchinnasya phalasyocyamAnatvAt | na hi parabrahmavid deshaparicchinnaM phalam ashnuvIteti yuktam | sarvagatatvAt parasya brahmaNaH | nanvaparabrahmaparigrahe paraM puruSham iti visheShaNaM nopapadyate | naiSha doShaH -- piNDApekShayA prANasya paratvopapatteH | ityevaM prApte, abhidhIyate -- 
 
IkShatikarmavyapadeshAt saH |

param eva brahma iha abhidhyAtavyam upadishyate | kasmAt? IkShatikarmavyapadeshAt | IkShatir darshanam | darshanavyApyam IkShatikarma | IkShatikarmatvenAsyAbhidhyAtavyasya puruShasya vAkyasheShe vyapadesho bhavati -- sa etasmAjjIvaghanAt parAt paraM purishayaM puruSham IkShate iti | tatra abhidhyAyater atathAbhUtam api vastu karma bhavati, manorathakalpitasyApyabhidhyAyatikarmatvAt | IkShateH tu tathAbhUtam eva vastu loke karma dR^iShTam, ityataH paramAtmaivAyaM samyagdarshanaviShayabhUta IkShatikarmatvena vyapadiShTa iti gamyate | sa eva ceha parapuruShashabdAbhyAm abhidhyAtavyaH pratyabhij~nAyate | 

nanvabhidhyAne paraH puruSha uktaH, IkShaNe tu parAt paraH | katham itara itaratra pratyabhij~nAyata iti, atrocyate -- parapuruShashabdau tAvad ubhayatra sAdhAraNau | na cAtra jIvaghanashabdena prakR^ito.abhidhyAtavyaH paraH puruShaH parAmR^ishyate | yena tasmAt parAt paro.ayam IkShitavyaH puruSho.anyaH syAt | kaH tarhi jIvaghana iti, ucyate -- ghano mUrtiH, jIvalakShaNo ghanaH jIvaghanaH | saindhavakhilyavat yaH paramAtmano jIvarUpaH khilyabhAva upAdhikR^itaH, parashca viShayendriyebhyaH, so.atra jIvaghana iti | apara Aha -- sa sAmabhir unnIyate brahmalokam ityatItAnantaravAkyanirdiShTo yo brahmalokaH parashca lokAntarebhyaH, so.atra jIvaghana ityucyate | jIvAnAM hi sarveShAM karaNaparivR^itAnAM sarvakaraNAtmani hiraNyagarbhe brahmalokanivAsini saMghAtopapatter bhavati brahmaloko jIvaghanaH | tasmAt paro yaH puruShaH paramAtmA IkShaNakarmabhUtaH, sa evAbhidhyAne.api karmabhUta iti gamyate | paraM puruSham iti ca visheShaNaM paramAtmaparigraha evAvakalpate | paro hi puruShaH paramAtmaiva bhavati yasmAt paraM kiMcid anyan nAsti | puruShAn na paraM kiMcit sA kAShThA sA parA gatiH [ka.u. 1.3.11] iti ca shrutyantarAt | paraM cAparaM ca brahma yad oMkAraH iti ca vibhajya, anantaram oMkAreNa paraM puruSham abhidhyAtavyaM bruvan, param eva brahma paraM puruShaM gamayati | yathA pAdodaraH tvacA vinirmucyata evaM ha vai sa pApmanA vinirmucyate iti pApmavinirmokaphalavacanaM paramAtmAnam ihAbhidhyAtavyaM sUcayati | atha yad uktaM paramAtmAbhidhyAyino na deshaparicchinnaM phalaM yujyata iti, atrocyate -- trimAtreNoMkAreNAlambanena paramAtmAnam abhidhyAyataH phalaM brahmalokaprAptiH, krameNa ca samyagdarshanotpattiH, -- iti kramamuktyabhiprAyam etad bhaviShyatItyadoShaH ||13||

  -- o)0(o -- 
daharAdhikaraNam

|| 1.3.14 || 

dahara uttarebhyaH || 

atha yad idam asmin brahmapure daharaM puNDarIkaM veshma daharo.asminn antarAkAshaH tasmin yad antaH tad anveShTavyaM tad vAva vijij~nAsitavyam iti [chA.u. 8.1.1] 

ityAdi vAkyaM samAmnAyate | tatra yo.ayaM dahare hR^idayapuNDarIke dahara AkAshaH shrutaH, sa kiM bhUtAkAshaH, atha vij~nAnAtmA, athavA paramAtmeti saMshayyate | kutaH saMshayaH? AkAshabrahmapurashabdAbhyAm | AkAshashabdo hyayaM bhUtAkAshe parasmiMshca brahmaNi prayujyamAno dR^ishyate | tatra kiM bhUtAkAsha eva daharaH syAt, kiM vA para ? iti saMshayaH | 

tathA brahmapuram iti -- kiM jIvo.atra brahmanAmA, tasyedaM puraM sharIraM brahmapuram, athavA parasyaiva brahmaNaH puraM brahmapuram iti | tatra jIvasya parasya vAnyatarasya purasvAmino daharAkAshatve saMshayaH | tatrAkAshashabdasya bhUtAkAshe rUDhatvAd bhUtAkAsha eva daharashabda iti prAptam | tasya ca daharAyatanApekShayA daharatvam | yAvAn vA ayam AkAshaH tAvAn eSho.antarhR^idaya AkAshaH iti ca bAhyAbhyantarabhAvakR^itabhedasyopamAnopameyabhAvaH | dyAvApR^ithivyAdi ca tasminn antaH samAhitam, avakAshAtmanAkAshasyaikatvAt | 

athavA jIvo dahara iti prAptam, brahmapurashabdAt | jIvasya hIdaM puraM sat sharIraM brahmapuramityucyate, tasya svakarmaNopArjitatvAt | bhaktyA ca tasya brahmashabdavAcyatvam | na hi parasya brahmaNaH sharIreNa svasvAmibhAvaH sambandho.asti | tatra purasvAminaH puraikadeshe.avasthAnaM dR^iShTam, yathA rAj~naH | manaupAdhikashca jIvaH | manashca prAyeNa hR^idaye pratiShThitam -- ityato jIvasyaivedaM hR^idayAntaravasthAnaM syAt | daharatvam api tasyaiva ArAgropamitatvAt avakalpate | AkAshopamitatvAdi ca brahmAbhedavivakShayA bhaviShyati | na cAtra daharasyAkAshasyAnveShTavyatvaM vijij~nAsitavyatvaM ca shrUyate | tasminyadantaH iti paravisheShaNatvenopAdAnAd iti || 

ata uttaraM brUmaH -- parameshvara evAtra daharAkAsho bhavitum arhati, na bhUtAkAsho jIvo vA | kasmAt? uttarebhyaH vAkyasheShagatebhyo hetubhyaH | tathA hi -- anveShTavyatayAbhihitasya daharAkAshasya taM ced brUyuH ityupakramya, kiM tad atra vidyate yad anveShTavyaM yad vAva vijij~nAsitavyam ityevam AkShepapUrvakaM pratisamAdhAnavacanaM bhavati -- sa brUyAd yA vAnvA ayam AkAshaH tAvAn eSho.antarhR^idaya AkAsha ubhe asmin dyAvApR^ithivI antar eva samAhite ityAdi | tatra puNDarIkadaharatvena prAptadaharatvasyAkAshasya prasiddhAkAshaupamyena daharatvaM nivartayan bhUtAkAshatvaM daharasyAkAshasya nivartayatIti gamyate | yadyapyAkAshashabdo bhUtAkAshe rUDhaH, tathApi tenaiva tasyopamA nopapadyata iti bhUtAkAshashaN^kA nivartitA bhavati | 

nanv ekasyApyAkAshasya bAhyAbhyantaratvakalpitena bhedenopamAnopameyabhAvaH sambhavatItyuktam | naivaM sambhavati | agatikA hIyaM gatiH, yatkAlpanikabhedAshrayaNam | api ca kalpayitvA bhedam upamAnopameyabhAvaM varNayataH paricchinnatvAd abhyantarAkAshasya na bAhyAkAshaparimANatvam upapadyeta | nanu parameshvarasyApi jyAyAnAkAshAt iti shrutyantarAt naivAkAshaparimANatvam upapadyate | naiSha doShaH | puNDarIkaveShTanaprAptadaharatvanivR^ittiparatvAd vAkyasya na tAvattvapratipAdanaparatvam | ubhayapratipAdane hi vAkyaM bhidyeta | na ca kalpitabhede puNDarIkaveShTita AkAshaikadeshe dyAvApR^ithivyAdInAm antaH samAdhAnam upapadyate | eSha AtmApahatapApmA vijaro vimR^ityur vishoko vijighat so.apipAsaH satyakAmaH satyasaN^kalpaH [chA.u. 8.1.5] iti cAtmatvApahatapApmatvAdayashca guNA na bhUtAkAshe sambhavanti | yadyapyAtmashabdo jIve sambhavati, tathApItarebhyaH kAraNebhyo jIvAshaN^kApi nivartitA bhavati | na hyupAdhiparicchinnasyArAgropamitasya jIvasya puNDarIkaveShTAnakR^itaM daharatvaM shakyaM nivartayitum | brahmAbhedavivakShayA jIvasya sarvagatatvAdi vivakShyeteti cet | yadAtmatayA jIvasya sarvagatatvAdi vivakShyeta, tasyaivabrahmaNaH sAkShAt sarvagatatvAdi vivakShyatAm iti yuktam | yad apyuktam -- brahmapuram iti jIvena purasyopalakShitatvAd rAj~na iva jIvasyaivedaM purasvAminaH puraikadeshavartitvamastviti | atra brUmaH -- parasyaivedaM brahmaNaH puraM sat sharIraM brahmapuramityucyate, brahmashabdasya tasmin mukhyatvAt | tasyApyasti pureNAnena sambandhaH, upalabdhyadhiShThAnatvAt  -- sa etasmAjjIvaghanAt parAt paraM purishayaM puruShamIkShate sa vA ayaM puruShaH sarvAsu pUrShu purishayaH ityAdishrutibhyaH | athavA jIvapura evAsmin brahma saMnihitam upalakShyate, yathA sAlagrAme viShNuH saMnihita iti, tadvat | tad yatheha karmacito lokaH kShIyata evam evAmutra puNyacito lokaH kShIyate [chA.u. 8.1.6] iti ca karmaNAm antavatphalatvam uktvA, atha ya ihAtmAnam anuvidya vrajantyetAMshca satyAn kAmAMH teShAM sarveShu lokeShu kAmacAro bhavati iti prakR^itadaharAkAshavij~nAnasyAnantaphalatvaM vadan, paramAtmatvam asya sUcayati | yad apyetad uktam -- na daharasyAkAshasyAnveShTavyatvaM vijij~nAsitavyatvaM ca shrutaM paravisheShaNatvenopAdAnAd iti | atra brUmaH -- yadyAkAsho nAnveShTavyatvenoktaH syAt, yAvAn vA ayam AkAshaH tAvAn eSho.antarhR^idaya AkAshaH ityAdyAkAshasvarUpapradarshanaM nopapadyeta | 

nanv etad apyantarvartivastusadbhAvadarshanAyaiva pradarshyate, taM ced brUyur yad idam asmin brahmapure daharaM puNDarIkaM veshma daharo.asminn antarAkAshaH kiM tad atra vidyate, yad anveShTavyaM yad vAva vijij~nAsitavyam [chA.u. 8.1.1] ityAkShipya parihArAvasare AkAshaupamyopakrameNa dyAvapR^ithivyAdInAm antaHsamAhitatvapradarshanAt | naitad evam | evaM hi sati yad antaH samAhitaM dyAvApR^ithivyAdi tad anveShTavyaM vijij~nAsitavyaM coktaM syAt | tatra vAkyasheSho nopapadyeta | asmin kAmAH samAhitAH eSha AtmApahatapApmA [chA.u. 8.1.5] iti hi prakR^itaM dyAvApR^ithivyAdisamAdhAnAdhAram AkAsham AkR^iShya atha ya ihAtmAnam anuvidya vrajantyetAMshca satyAn kAmAn iti samuccayArthena cashabdenAtmAnaM kAmAdhAram AshritAMshca kAmAn vij~neyAn vAkyasheSho darshayati | tasmAd vAkyopakrame.api dahara evAkAsho hR^idayapuNDarIkAdhiShThAnaH sahAntaHsthaiH samAhitaiH pR^ithivyAdibhiH satyaishca kAmair vij~neya ukta iti gamyate | sa coktebhyo hetubhyaH parameshvara iti sthitam ||14||

|| 1.3.15 ||

gatishabdAbhyAM tathA hi dR^iShTaM liN^gaM ca ||

daharaH parameshvara uttarebhyo hetubhya ityuktam | ta evottare hetava idAnIM prapaJNcyante | itashca parameshvara eva daharaH | yasmAd daharavAkyasheShe parameshvarasyaiva pratipAdakau gatishabdau bhavataH -- imAH sarvAH prajA aharahar gacchantya etaM brahmalokaM na vindanti [chA.u. 8.3.2] iti | 

tatra prakR^itaM daharaM brahmalokashabdenAbhidhAya tadviShayA gatiH prajAshabdavAcyAnAM jIvAnAm abhidhIyamAnA daharasya brahmatAM gamayati | tathA hyaharaharjavAnAM suShuptAvasthAyAM brahmaviShayaM gamanaM dR^iShTaM shrutyantare -- satA somya tadA sampanno bhavati ityevam Adau | loke.api kila gADhaM suShuptam AcakShate brahmIbhUto brahmatAM gataH iti | tathA brahmalokashabdo.api prakR^ite dahare prayujyamAno jIvabhUtAkAshAshaN^kAM nivartayan brahmatAm asya gamayati | 

nanu kamalAsanalokam api brahmalokashabdo gamayet | gamayed yadi brahmaNo loka iti ShaShThIsamAsavR^ittyA vyutpAdyeta | sAmAnAdhikaraNyavR^ittyA tu vyutpAdyamAno brahmaiva loko brahmaloka iti param eva brahma gamayiShyati | etad eva cAharahar brahmalokagamanaM dR^iShTaM brahmalokashabdasya sAmAnAdhikaraNyavR^ittiparigrahe liN^gam | na hyaharahaH imAH prajAH kAryabrahmalokaM satyalokAkhyaM gacchantIti shakyaM kalpayitum ||15||

|| 1.3.16 || 

dhR^iteshca mahimno.asyAsminn upalabdheH || 

dhR^iteshca hetoH parameshvara evAyaM daharaH | katham? daharo.asminnantarAkAshaH iti hi prakR^itya AkAshaupamyapUrvakaM tasminsarvasamAdhAnamuktvA tasminn eva cAtmashabdaM prayujyApahatapApmatvAdiguNayogaM copadishya tam evAnativR^ittaprakaraNaM nirdishati -- atha ya AtmA sa seturvidhR^itireShAM lokAnAmasambhedAya iti | tatra vidhR^itirityAtmashabdasAmAnAdhikaraNyAdvidhArayitocyate | kticaH kartari smaraNAt | yathodakasantAnasya vidhArayitA loke setuH kShetrasampadAmasambhedAya, evamayam AtmA eShAm adhyAtmAdibhedabhinnAnAM lokAnAM varNAshramAdInAM ca vidhArayitA setuH, asambhedAya asaMkarAyeti | evam iha prakR^ite dahare vidharaNalakShaNaM mahimAnaM darshayati | ayaM ca mahimA parameshvara eva shrutyantarAdupalabhyate -- etasya vA akSharasya prashAsane gArgi sUryAcandramasau vidhR^itau tiShThataH [bR^i.A.u. 3.8.9] ityAdeH | tathAnyatrApi nishcite parameshvaravAkye shrUyate -- eSha sarveshvara eSha bhUtAdhipatireSha bhUtapAla eSha seturvidharaNa eShAM lokAnAmasambhedAya iti | evaM dhR^iteshca hetoH parameshvara evAyaM daharaH ||

|| 1.3.17 || 

prasiddhashca ||

itashca parameshvara eva daharo.asminn antarAkAshaH [chA.u. 8.1.1] ityucyate | yat kAraNam AkAshashabdaH parameshvare prasiddhaH -- AkAsho vai nAma nAmarUpayor nirvahitA sarvANi ha vA imAni bhUtAnyAkAshAd eva sam utpadyante ityAdiprayogadarshanAt | jIve tu na kvacid AkAshashabdaH prayujyamAno dR^ishyate | bhUtAkAshaH tu satyAm apyAkAshashabdaprasiddhau upamAnopameyabhAvAdyasambhavAn na grahItavya ityuktam ||17||

|| 1.3.18 || 

itaraparAmarshAt sa iti cen, nAsambhavAt || 

yadi vAkyasheShabalena dahara iti parameshvaraH parigR^ihyeta, asti hItarasthApi jIvasya vAkyasheShe parAmarshaH -- atha ya eSha samprasAdo.asmAccharIrAt samutthAya paraM jyotir upasampadya svena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyata eSha Atmeti hovAca [chA.u. 8.3.4] iti | atra hi samprasAdashabdaH shrutyantare suShuptAvasthAyAM dR^iShTatvAd avasthAvantaM jIvaM shaknotyupasthApayitum, nArthAntaram | tathA sharIravyapAshrayasyaiva jIvasya sharIrAt samutthAnaM sambhavati, yathAkAshavyapAshrayANAM vAyvAdInAm AkAshAt samutthAnam, tadvat | yathA cAdR^iShTo.api loke parameshvaraviShaya AkAshashabdaH parameshvaradharmasamabhivyAhArAt AkAsho vai nAma nAmarUpayor nirvahitA [chA.u. 8.14.1] ityevamAdau parameshvaraviShayo.abhyupagataH, evaM jIvaviShayo.api bhaviShyati | tasmAd itaraparAmarshAt daharo.asminn antarAkAshaH [chA.u. 8.1.1] ityatra sa eva jIva ucyata iti cet -- naitad evaM syAt | kasmAt? asambhavAt | na hi jIvo buddhyAdyupAdhiparicchedAbhimAnI san AkAshenopamIyeta | na copAdhidharmAn abhimanyamAnasyApahatapApmatvAdayo dharmAH sambhavanti | prapaJNcitaM caitat prathame sUtre | atirekAshaN^kAparihArAya atra tu punar upanyastam | paThiShyati copariShTAt -- anyArthashca parAmarshaH [ve.sU. 1.3.20] iti ||18||

|| 1.3.19 || 

uttarAcced AvirbhUtasvarUpaH tu ||

itaraparAmarshAdyA jIvAshaN^kA jAtA, sA asambhavAn nirAkR^itA | athedAnIM mR^itasyevAmR^itasekAt punaH samutthAnaM jIvAshaN^kAyAH kriyate -- uttarasmAt prAjApatyAd vAkyAt | tatra hi ya AtmApahatapApmA [chA.u. 8.7.1] ityapahatapApmatvAdiguNakam AtmAnam anveShTavyaM vijij~nAsitavyaM ca pratij~nAya, ya eSho.akShiNi puruSho dR^ishyata eSha AtmA iti bruvan akShisthaM draShTAraM jIvam AtmAnaM nirdishati | etaM tv eva te bhUyo.anuvyAkhyAsyAmi iti ca tam eva punaH punaH parAmR^ishya, ya eSha svapne mahIyamAnashcaratyeSha AtmA iti tad yatraitat suptaH samastaH samprasannaH svapnaM na vijAnAtyeSha AtmA iti ca jIvam evAvasthAntaragataM vyAcaShTe | tasyaiva cApahatapApmatvAdi darshayati -- etad amR^itam abhayam etad brahma iti | 

nAha khalvayam evaM sampratyAtmAnaM jAnAtyayam aham asmIti no evemAni bhUtAni iti ca suShuptAvasthAyAM doSham upalabhya, etaM tv eva te bhUyo.anuvyAkhyAsyAmi no evAnyatraitasmAt iti copakramya, sharIrasambandhanindApUrvakam eSha samprasAdo.asmAccharIrAt samutthAya paraM jyotir upasampadya svena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyate sa uttamaH puruShaH [chA.u. 8.12.3] iti jIvam eva sharIrAt samutthitam uttamaM puruShaM darshayati | tasmAd asti sambhavo jIve pArameshvarANAM dharmANAm | ataH daharo.asminn antarAkAshaH [chA.u. 8.1.1] iti jIva evokta iti cet kashcid brUyAt | taM prati brUyAt -- AvirbhUtasvarUpaH tu iti | tushabdaH pUrvapakShavyAvR^ittyarthaH | nottarasmAd api vAkyAd iha jIvasyAshaN^kA sambhavatItyarthaH | kasmAt? yataH tatrApyAvirbhUtasvarUpo jIvo vivakShyate | AvirbhUtaM svarUpam asyetyAvirbhUtasvarUpaH | bhUtapUrvagatyA jIvavacanam | 

etad uktaM bhavati -- ya eSho.akShiNi ityakShilakShitaM draShTAraM nirdishya, udasharAvabrAhmaNena enaM sharIrAtmatayA vyutthApya, etaM tv eva te iti punaH punaH tam eva vyAkhyeyatvenAkR^iShya, svapnasuShuptopanyAsakrameNa, paraM jyotir upasampadya svena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyate iti yad asya pAramArthikaM svarUpaM paraM brahma, tadrUpatayainaM jIvaM vyAcaShTe | na jaivena rUpeNa | yattat paraM jyotir upasampattavyaM shrutam, tat paraM brahma | taccApahatapApmatvAdidharmakam | tad eva ca jIvasya pAramArthikaM svarUpam -- tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7] ityAdi shAstrebhyaH, netarad upAdhikalpitam | yAvad eva hi sthANAviva puruShabuddhiM dvaitalakShaNAm avidyAM nivartayan kUTasthanityadR^iksvarUpam AtmAnam ahaM brahmAsmi [bR^i.A.u. 1.4.10] iti na pratipadyate, tAvajjIvasya jIvatvam | 

yadA tu dehendriyamanobuddhisaMghAtAd vyutthApya shrutyA pratibodhyate nAsi tvaM dehendriyamanobuddhisaMghAtaH, nApi saMsArI, kiM tarhi tad yat satyaM sa AtmA caitanyamAtrasvarUpaH tat tvam asIti | tadA kUTasthanityadR^iksvarUpam AtmAnaM pratibudhya asmAccharIrAdyabhimAnAt samuttiShThan sa eva kUTasthanityadR^iksvarUpa AtmA bhavati -- sa yo ha vai tat paramaM brahma veda brahmaiva bhavati [mu.u. 3.2.9] ityAdi shrutibhyaH | 

tad eva cAsya pAramArthikaM svarUpam, yena sharIrAt samutthAya svena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyate | kathaM punaH svaM ca rUpaM svenaiva ca niShpadyata iti sambhavati kUTasthanityasya? suvarNAdInAM tu dravyAntarasamparkAd abhibhUtasvarUpANAm anabhivyaktAsAdhAraNavisheShANAM kShAraprakShepAdibhiH shodhyamAnAnAM svarUpeNAbhiniShpattiH syAt | tathA nakShatrAdInAm ahanyabhibhUtaprakAshAnAm abhibhAvakaviyoge rAtrau svarUpeNAbhiniShpattiH syAt | na tu tathAtmacaitanyajyotiSho nityasya kenacid abhibhavaH sambhavati asaMsargitvAt vyomna iva, dR^iShTavirodhAcca | dR^iShTishrutimativij~nAtayo hi jIvasya svarUpam | tacca sharIrAd asamutthitasyApi jIvasya sadA niShpannam eva dR^ishyate | sarvo hi jIvaH pashyan shrR^iNvan manvAno vijAnan vyavaharati, anyathA vyavahArAnupapatteH | taccet sharIrAt samutthitasya niShpadyeta, prAksamutthAnAd dR^iShTo vyavahAro virudhyeta | 

ataH kimAtmakam idaM sharIrAt samutthAnam, kimAtmikA vA svarUpeNAbhiniShpattiH ? iti | atrocyate -- prAgvivekavij~nAnotpatteH sharIrendriyamanobuddhiviShayavedanopAdhibhir aviviktam iva jIvasya dR^iShTyAdijyotiHsvarUpaM bhavati | yathA shuddhasya sphaTikasya svAcchyaM shauklyaM ca svarUpaM prAgvivekagrahaNAd raktanIlAdyupAdhibhir aviviktam iva bhavati | pramANajanitavivekagrahaNAt tu parAcInaH sphaTikaH svAcchyena shauklyena ca svena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyata ityucyate prAg api tathaiva san | 

tathA dehAdyupAdhyaviviktasyaiva sato jIvasya shrutikR^itaM vivekavij~nAnaM sharIrAt samutthAnam, vivekavij~nAnaphalaM svarUpeNAbhiniShpattiH kevalAtmasvarUpAvagatiH | tathA vivekAvivekamAtreNaivAtmano.asharIratvaM sasharIratvaM ca mantravarNAt asharIraM sharIreShu, iti, sharIrastho.api kaunteya na karoti na lipyate iti ca sasharIratvAsharIratvavisheShAbhAvasmaraNAt | 

tasmAd vivekavij~nAnAbhAvAd anAvirbhUtasvarUpaH san vivekavij~nAnAd AvirbhUtasvarUpa ityucyate | na tu anyAdR^ishau AvirbhAvAnAvirbhAvau svarUpasya sambhavataH, svarUpatvAd eva | evaM mithyAj~nAnakR^ita eva jIvaparameshvarayor bhedaH, na vastukR^itaH | vyomavad asaN^gatvAvisheShAt | kutashcaitad evaM pratipattavyam? yataH ya eSho.akShiNi puruSho dR^ishyate ityupadishya etad amR^itam abhayam etad brahma ityupadishati | yo.akShiNi prasiddho draShTA draShTR^itvena vibhAvyate, so.amR^itAbhayalakShaNAd brahmaNo.anyashcet syAt, tato.amR^itAbhayabrahmasAmAnAdhikaraNyaM na syAt | 

nApi praticchAyAtmAyam akShilakShito nirdishyate, prajApater mR^iShAvAditvaprasaN^gAt | tathA dvitIye.api paryAye ya eSha svapne mahIyamAnashcarati iti na prathamaparyAyanirdiShTAd akShipuruShAd draShTur anyo nirdiShTaH, etaM tv eva te bhUyo.anuvyAkhyAsyAmi ityupakramAt | 

kiM ca, aham adya svapne hastinam adrAkSham, nedAnIM taM pashyAmi iti dR^iShTam eva pratibuddhaH pratyAcaShTe | draShTAraM tu tam eva pratyabhijAnAti -- ya evAhaM svapnam adrAkSham, sa evAhaM jAgaritaM pashyAmi iti | tathA tR^itIye.api paryAye -- nAha khalvayam evaM sampratyAtmAnaM jAnAtyayam aham asmIti no evemAni bhUtAni iti suShuptAvasthAyAM visheShavij~nAnAbhAvam eva darshayati, na vij~nAtAraM pratiShedhati | yat tu tatra vinAsham evApIto bhavati iti, tad api visheShavij~nAnavinAshAbhiprAyam eva, na vij~nAtR^ivinAshAbhiprAyam | na hi vij~nAtur vij~nAter viparilopo vidyate.avinAshitvAt [bR^i.A.u. 4.3.30] iti shrutyantarAt | tathA caturthe.api paryAye etaM tv eva te bhUyo.anuvyAkhyAsyAmi no evAnyatraitasmAt ityupakramya maghavan martyaM vA idaM sharIram ityAdinA prapaJNcena sharIrAdyupAdhisambandhapratyAkhyAnena samprasAdashabdoditaM jIvam svena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyate iti brahmasvarUpApannaM darshayan, na parasmAd brahmaNo.amR^itAbhayasvarUpAd anyaM jIvaM darshayati | 

kecit tu paramAtmavivakShAyAm etaM tv eva te iti jIvAkarShaNam anyAyyaM manyamAnA etam eva vAkyopakramasUcitam apahatapApmatvAdiguNakam AtmAnaM te bhUyo.anuvyAkhyAsyAmIti kalpayanti | teShAm etam iti saMnihitAvalambinI sarvanAmashrutir viprakR^iShyeta | bhUyaH shrutishcoparudhyeta | paryAyAntarAbhihitasya paryAyAntareNa anabhidhIyamAnatvAt | etaM tv eva te iti ca pratij~nAya prAkcaturthAt paryAyAd anyam anyaM vyAcakShANasya prajApateH pratArakatvaM prasajyeta | tasmAt yad avidyApratyupasthApitam apAramArthikaM jaivaM rUpaM kartR^itvabhoktR^itvarAgadveShAdidoShakaluShitam anekAnarthayogi, tadvilayanena tadviparItam apahatapApmatvAdiguNakaM pArameshvaraM svarUpaM vidyayA pratipadyate, sarpAdivilayaneneva rajjvAdIn | 

apare tu vAdinaH pAramArthikam eva jaivaM rUpam iti manyante.asmadIyAshca kecit | teShAM sarveShAm AtmaikatvasamyagdarshanapratipakShabhUtAnAM pratiShedhAyedaM shArIrakam Arabdham -- eka eva parameshvaraH kUTasthanityo vij~nAnadhAtur avidyayA, mAyayA mAyAvivat, anekadhA vibhAvyate, nAnyo vij~nAnadhAtur astIti | 

yat tvidaM parameshvaravAkye jIvam AshaN^kya pratiShedhati sUtrakAraH -- nAsambhavAt ityAdinA, tatrAyam abhiprAyaH -- nityashuddhabuddhamuktasvabhAve kUTasthanitye ekasminn asaN^ge paramAtmani tadviparItaM jaivaM rUpaM vyomnIva talamalAdi parikalpitam | tat AtmaikatvapratipAdanaparair vAkyair nyAyopetair etavAd apratiShedhaishcApaneShyAmIti -- paramAtmano jIvAd anyatvaM draDhayati | jIvasya tu na parasmAd anyatvaM pratipipAdayiShati | kiM tu anuvadatyevAvidyAkalpitaM lokaprasiddhaM jIvabhedam | evaM hi svAbhAvikakartR^itvabhoktR^itvAnuvAdena pravR^ittAH karmavidhayo na virudhyanta iti manyate | pratipAdyaM tu shAstrArtham Atmaikatvam eva darshayati -- shAstradR^iShTyA tUpadesho vAmadevavat ityAdinA | varNitashcAsmAbhiH vidvadavidvadbhedena karmavidhivirodhaparihAraH ||19||

|| 1.3.20 || 

anyArthashca parAmarshaH ||

atha yo.ayaM daharavAkyasheShe jIvaparAmarsho darshitaH -- atha ya eSha samprasAdaH [chA.u. 8.3.4] ityAdiH, sa dahare parameshvare vyAkhyAyamAne, na jIvopAsanopadeshaH, nApi prakR^itavisheShopadeshaH -- ityanarthakatvaM prApnotItyata Aha -- anyArtho.ayaM jIvaparAmarsho na jIvasvarUpaparyavasAyI | kiM tarhi, parameshvarasvarUpaparyavasAyI | katham? samprasAdashabdodito jIvo jAgaritavyavahAre dehendriyapaJNjarAdhyakSho bhUtvA, tadvAsanAnirmitAMshca svapnAn nADIcaro.anubhUya, shrAntaH sharaNaM prepsur ubhayarUpAd api sharIrAbhimAnAt samutthAya, suShuptAvasthAyAM paraM jyotir AkAshashabditaM paraM brahmopasampadya, visheShavij~nAnavattvaM ca parityajya, svena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyate | yad asyopasampattavyaM paraM jyotiH, yena svena rUpeNAyam abhiniShpadyate, sa eSha AtmApahatapApmatvAdiguNa upAsyaH -- ityevamartho.ayaM jIvaparAmarshaH parameshvaravAdino.apyupapadyate ||20||

|| 1.3.21 ||

alpashruteH iti cet tad uktam ||

yad apyuktam -- daharo.asminn antar AkAshaH [chA.u. 8.1.1] ityAkAshasyAlpatvaM shrUyamANaM parameshvare nopapadyate, jIvasya tu ArAgropamitasyAlpatvam avakalpata iti | tasya parihAro vaktavyaH | ukto hyasya parihAraH -- parameshvare.apyApekShikam alpatvam avakalpata iti, arbhakaukastvAt tadvyapadeshAcca neti cen na nicAyyatvAd evaM vyomavacca ityatra | sa eveha parihAro.anusandhAtavya iti sUcayati | shrutyaiva ca idam alpatvaM pratyuktaM prasiddhenAkAshenopamimAnayA yAvAn vA ayam AkAshaH tAvAn eSho.antarhR^idaya AkAshaH iti ||21||

|| 1.3.22 ||
anukR^ityadhikaraNam 

na tatra sUryo bhAti na candratArakaM 
nemA vidyuto bhAnti kuto.ayam agniH | 
tam eva bhAntam anubhAti sarvaM 
tasya bhAsA sarvam idaM vibhAti ||  [ka.u. 5.15, shve.u. 6.14, mu.u. 2.2.10] iti samAmananti | 

tatra yaM bhAntam anubhAti sarvaM yasya ca bhAsA sarvam idaM vibhAti, sa kiM tejodhAtuH kashcit, uta prAj~na Atmeti vicikitsAyAM tejodhAtuH iti tAvat prAptam | kutaH? tejodhAtUnAm eva sUryAdInAM bhAnapratiShedhAt | tejaHsvabhAvakaM hi candratArakAdi tejaHsvabhAvaka eva sUrye bhAsamAne ahani na bhAsata iti prasiddham | tathA saha sUryeNa sarvam idaM candratArakAdi yasmin na bhAsate, so.api tejaHsvabhAva eva kashcid ityavagamyate | anubhAnam api tejaHsvabhAvaka evopapadyate, samAnasvabhAvakeShvanukAradarshanAt | gacchantam anugacchati itivat | tasmAt tejodhAtuH kashcid ityevaM prApte -- 

anukR^iteH tasya ca ||

brUmaH -- prAj~na evAyam AtmA bhavitum arhati | kasmAt? anukR^iteH | anukaraNam anukR^itiH | yad etat tam eva bhAntam anubhAti sarvam ityanubhAnam, tatprAj~naparigrahe.avakalpate | bhArUpaH satyasaN^kalpaH [chA.u. 3.14.2] iti hi prAj~nam AtmAnam Amananti | na tu tejodhAtuM kaMcit sUryAdayo.anubhAntIti prasiddham | samatvAcca tejodhAtUnAM sUryAdInAM na tejodhAtum anyaM pratyapekShAsti, yaM bhAntam anubhAyuH | na hi pradIpaH pradIpAntaram anubhAti | yad apyuktaM samAnasvabhAvakeShvanukAro dR^ishyata iti -- nAyam ekAnto niyamaH | bhinnasvabhAvakeShvapi hyanukAro dR^ishyate | yathA sutapto.ayaHpiNDo.agnyanukR^itir agniM dahantam anudahati, bhaumaM vA rajo vAyuM vahantam anuvahatIti | anukR^iteH ityanubhAnam asusUcat | tasya ca iti caturthaM pAdam asya shlokasya sUcayati | tasya bhAsA sarvam idaM vibhAti iti ca tarAtukaM bhAnaM sUryAder ucyamAnaM prAj~nam AtmAnaM gamayati | tad devA jyotiShAM jyotir Ayur hopAsate.amR^itam iti hi prAj~nam AtmAnam Amananti | tejo.antareNa tu sUryAditejo vibhAtItyaprasiddham, viruddhaM ca | tejo.antareNa tejo.antarasya pratighAtAt | athavA na sUryAdInAm eva shlokaparipaThitAnAm idaM tarAtukaM vibhAnam ucyate | kiM tarhi, sarvam idam ityavisheShashruteH sarvasyaivAsya nAmarUpakriyAkArakaphalajAtasya yA abhivyaktiH, sA brahmajyotiHsattAnimittA | yathA sUryajyotiHsattAnimittA sarvasya rUpajAtasyAbhivyaktiH, tadvat | na tatra sUryo bhAti [ka.u. 5.15, shve.u. 6.14, mu.u. 2.2.10] iti ca tatrashabdam Aharan prakR^itagrahaNaM darshayati | prakR^itaM ca brahma, yasmin dyauH pR^ithivI cAntarikSham otam [mu.u. 2.2.5] ityAdinA | anantaraM ca -- 

hiraNmaye pare koshe virajaM brahma niShkalam | 
tacchubhraM jyotiShAM jyotiH tad yad Atmavido viduH || iti | 

kathaM tajjyotiShAM jyotiH ityata idam utthitam -- na tatra sUryo bhAti iti | yad apyuktam sUryAdInAM tejasAM bhAnapratiShedhaH tejodhAtAv evAnyasminn avakalpate, sUrya ivetareShAm iti | tatra tu sa eva tejodhAtur anyo na sambhavatItyupapAditam | brahmaNyapi caiShAM bhAnapratiShedho.avakalpate | yataH -- yad upalabhyate tat sarvaM brahmaNaiva jyotiShopalabhyate | brahma tu nAnyena jyotiShopalabhyate, svayaM jyotiHsvarUpatvAt, yena sUryAdayaH tasmin bhAyuH | brahma hi anyad vyanakti, na tu brahmAnyena vyajyate, AtmanaivAyaM jyotiShAste [bR^i.A.u. 4.3.6], agR^ihyo na hi gR^ihyate [bR^i.A.u. 4.2.4] ityAdi shrutibhyaH ||22||

|| 1.3.23 || 

api ca smaryate ||

api cedR^igrUpatvaM prAj~nasyaivAtmanaH smaryate bhagavadgItAsu -- na tadbhAsayate sUryo na shashAN^ko na pAvakaH | yadgatvA na nivartante taddhAma paramaM mama iti | yadAdityagataM tejo jagadbhAsayate.akhilam | yaccandramasi yaccAgnau tattejo viddhi mAmakam iti ca ||24||

  -- o)0(o -- 

pramitAdhikaraNam 

|| 1.3.24 || 

aN^guShThamAtraH puruSho madhya Atmani tiShThati iti shrUyate | tathA aN^guShThamAtraH puruSho jyotiH ivAdhUmakaH | IshAno bhUtabhavyasya sa evAdya sa u shva etad vai tat iti ca | tatra yo.ayam aN^guShThamAtraH puruShaH shrUyate, sa kiM vij~nAnAtmA, kiM vA paramAtmeti saMshayaH | tatra parimANopadeshAd vij~nAnAtmeti tAvat prAptam | na hyanantAyAm avistArasya paramAtmano.aN^guShThaparimANatvam upapadyate | vij~nAnAtmanaH tUpAdhimattvAt sambhavati kayAcit kalpanayAN^guShThamAtratvam | smR^iteshca -- 

atha satyavataH kAyAt pAshabaddhaM vashaM gatam | 
aN^guShThamAtraM puruShaM nishcakarSha yamo balAt || iti | 

na hi parameshvaro balAt yamena niShkraShTuM shakyaH | tena tatra saMsArI aN^guShThamAtro nishcitaH | sa evehApItyevaM prApte -- 

shabdAd eva pramitaH || 

brUmaH -- paramAtmaivAyam aN^guShThamAtraparimitaH puruSho bhavitum arhati | kasmAt? shabdAt -- IshAno bhUtabhavyasya iti | na hyanyaH parameshvarAd bhUtabhavyasya niraN^kusham IshitA | etad vai tat iti ca prakR^itaM pR^iShTam ihAnusandadhAti | etad vai tat, yat pR^iShTaM brahmetyarthaH | pR^iShTaM ceha brahma -- anyatra dharmAd anyatrAdharmAd anyatrAsmAt kR^itAkR^itAt | anyatra bhUtAcca bhavyAcca yat tat pashyasi tadvad va iti | shabdAd eveti -- abhidhAnashruter eva -- IshAna iti parameshvaro.avagamyata ityarthaH ||24|| 

|| 1.3.25 ||

kathaM punaH sarvagatasya paramAtmanaH parimANopadesha ityatra brUmaH -- 

hR^idyapekShayA tu manuShyAdhikAratvAt ||

sarvagatasyApi paramAtmano hR^idaye.avasthAnam apekShyAN^guShThamAtratvam idam ucyate | AkAshasyeva vaMshaparvApekSham aratnimAtratvam | na hyaJNjasA atimAtrasya paramAtmano.aN^guShThamAtratvam upapadyate | na cAnyaH paramAtmana iha grahaNam arhati IshAnashabdAdibhya ityuktam | 

nanu pratiprANibhedaM hR^idayAnAm anavasthitatvAt tadapekSham apyaN^guShThamAtratvaM nopapadyata ityata uttaram ucyate -- manuShyAdhikAratvAd iti | shAstraM hyavisheShapravR^ittam api manuShyAn evAdhikaroti | shaktatvAt, arthitvAt, aparyudastatvAt upanayanAdishAstrAcca -- iti varNitam etadadhikAralakShaNe | manuShyANAM ca niyataparimANaH kAyaH | aucityena niyataparimANam eva caiShAm aN^guShThamAtraM hR^idayam | ato manuShyAdhikAratvAcchAstrasya manuShyahR^idayAvasthAnApekSham aN^guShThamAtratvam upapannaM paramAtmanaH | yad apyuktam -- parimANopadeshAt smR^iteshca saMsAryevAyam aN^guShThamAtraH pratyetavya iti | tat pratyucyate -- sa AtmA tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7] ityAdivat saMsAriNa eva sato.aN^guShThamAtrasya brahmatvam idam upadishyata iti | dvirUpA hi vedAntavAkyAnAM pravR^ittiH -- kvacit paramAtmasvarUpanirUpaNaparA | kvacid vij~nAnAtmanaH paramAtmaikatvopadeshaparA | tad atra vij~nAnAtmanaH paramAtmanaikatvam upadishyate | nAN^guShThamAtratvaM kasyacit | etam evArthaM pareNa sphuTIkariShyati -- aN^guShThamAtraH puruSho.antarAtmA sadA janAnAM hR^idaye saMniviShTaH | taM svAccharIrAt pravR^ihen muJNjAdiveShIkAM dhairyeNa | taM vidyAcchukram amR^itam iti ||25||

  -- o)0(o -- 

7. devatAdhikaraNam

|| 1.3.26 ||

taduparyapi bAdarAyaNaH sambhavAt ||

aN^guShThamAtrashrutir manuShyahR^idayApekShA manuShyAdhikAratvAcchAstrasyetyuktam | tatprasaN^genedam ucyate | bADham, manuShyAn adhikaroti shAstram | na tu manuShyAn eveti iha brahmaj~nAne niyamo.asti | teShAM manuShyANAm upariShTAd ye devAdayaH, tAn apyadhikaroti shAstram iti bAdarAyaNa AcAryo manyate | kasmAt? sambhavAt | sambhavati hi teShAm apyarthitvAd yadhikArakAraNam | tatrArthitvaM tAvan mokShaviShayaM devAdInAm api sambhavati vikAraviShayavibhUtyanityatvAlocanAdinimittam | tathA sAmarthyam api teShAM sambhavati, mantrArthavAdetihAsapurANalokebhyo vigrahavattvAdyavagamAt | na ca teShAM kashcit pratiShedho.asti | na copanayanashAstreNaiShAm adhikAro nivartyeta, upanayanasya vedAdhyayanArthatvAt, teShAM ca svayaMpratibhAtavedatvAt | api caiShAM vidyAgrahaNArthaM brahmacaryAdi darshayati -- ekashataM ha vai varShANi maghavAn prajApatau brahmacaryam uvAsa [chA.u. 8.11.3], bhR^igur vai vAruNiH | varuNaM pitaram upasasAra | adhIhi bhagavo brahma [tai.u. 3.1] ityAdi | yad api karmasvanadhikArakAraNam uktam -- na devAnAM devatAntarAbhAvAt iti, na R^iShINAm, ArSheyAntarAbhAvAt iti | na tadvidyAsu asti | na hIndrAdInAM vidyAsvadhikriyamANAnAm indrAdyuddeshena kiMcit kR^ityam asti | na ca bhR^igvAdInAM bhR^igvAdisagotratayA | tasmAd devAdInAm api vidyAsvadhikAraH kena vAryate? devAdyadhikAre.apyaN^guShThamAtrashrutiH svAN^guShThApekShayA na virudhyeta ||26||

|| 1.3.27 ||

virodhaH karmaNIti cen nAnekapratipatter darshanAt ||

syAd etat -- yadi vigrahavattvAd yabhyupagamena devAdInAM vidyAsvadhikAro varNyeta, vigrahavattvAt R^itvigAdivadindrAdInAm api svarUpasaMnidhAnena karmAN^gabhAvo.abhyupagamyeta | tadA ca virodhaH karmaNi syAt | na hIndrAdInAM svarUpasaMnidhAnena yAgAN^gabhAvo dR^ishyate | na ca sambhavati, bahuShu yAgeShu yugapadekasyendrasya svarUpasaMnidhAnAnupapatteH iti cet, nAyam asti virodhaH | kasmAt? anekapratipatteH | ekasyApi devatAtmano yugapad anekasvarUpapratipattiH sambhavati | katham etad avagamyate? darshanAt | tathA hi -- kati devAH ityupakramya trayashca trI ca shatA trayashca trI ca sahasrA iti nirucya katame te ityasyAM pR^icchAyAm mahimAna evaiShAm ete trayastriMshat tv eva devAH iti bruvatI shrutiH ekaikasya devatAtmano yugapadanekarUpatAM darshayati | tathA trayastriMshato.api ShaDAdyantarbhAvakrameNa katama eko deva iti prANaH iti prANaikarUpatAM devAnAM darshayantI tasyaiva ekasya prANasya yugapadanekarUpatAM darshayati | tathA smR^itir api -- 
Atmano vai sharIrANi bahUni bharatarShabha | 
yogI kuryAd balaM prApya taishca sarvair mahIM caret || 
prApnuyAd viShayAn kaishcit kaishcid ugraM tapashcaret | 
saMkShipecca punaH tAni sUryo rashmigaNAn iva ||
ityevaMjAtIyakA prAptANimAdyaishvaryANAM yoginAm api yugapadanekasharIrayogaM darshayati | kim u vaktavyam AjAnasiddhAnAM devAnAm? anekarUpapratipattisambhavAcca ekaikA devatA bahubhI rUpair AtmAnaM pravibhajya bahuShu yAgeShu yugapadaN^gabhAvaM gacchatIti | paraishca na dR^ishyate, antardhAnAdishaktiyogAt -- ityupapadyate | anekapratipatter darshanAt ityasyAparA vyAkhyA -- vigrahavatAm api karmAN^gabhAvacodanAsu anekA pratipattir dR^ishyate | kvacid eko.api vigrahavAn anekatra yugapadaN^gabhAvaM na gacchati, yathA bahubhir bhojayadbhir naiko brAhmaNo yugapad bhojyate | kvaciccaiko.api vigrahavAn anekatra yugapad aN^gabhAvaM gacchati, yathA bahubhir namaskurvANair eko brAhmaNo yugapan namaskriyate | tadvad ihoddeshaparityAgAtmakatvAt yAgasya vigrahavatIm apyekAM devatAm uddishya bahavaH svaM svaM dravyaM yugapat parityakShyantIti vigrahavattve.api devAnAM na kiMcit karmaNi virudhyate ||27||

|| 1.3.28 ||

shabda iti cet, nAtaH prabhAvAt 
pratyakShAnumAnAbhyAm ||

mA nAma vigrahavattve devAdInAm abhyupagamyamAne karmaNi kashcid virodhaH prasaJNji | shabde tu virodhaH prasajyeta | katham? autpattikaM hi shabdasyArthena sambandham Ashritya anapekShatvAt iti vedasya prAmANyaM sthApitam | idAnIM tu vigrahavatI devatAbhyupagamyamAnA yadyapyaishvaryayogAd yugapad anekakarmasambandhIni havIMShi bhuJNjIta, tathApi vigrahayogAd asmadAdivajjananamaraNavatI seti, nityasya shabdasya nityenArthena nitye sambandhe pratIyamAne yad vaidike shabde prAmANyaM sthitam, tasya virodhaH syAd iti cet, nAyam apyasti virodhaH | kasmAt? ataH prabhavAt | ata eva hi vaidikAcchabdAd devAdikaM jagat prabhavati || 

nanu janmAdyasya yataH ityatra brahmaprabhavatvaM jagato.avadhAritam, katham iha shabdaprabhavatvam ucyate? api ca yadi nAma vaidikAcchabdAd asya prabhavo.abhyupagataH, katham etAvatA virodhaH shabde parihR^itaH? yAvatA vasavo rudrA AdityA vishvedevA maruta ityete.arthA anityA eva, utpattimattvAt | tadanityatve ca tadvAcinAM vaidikAnAM vasvAdishabdAnAm anityatvaM kena nivAryate? prasiddhaM hi loke devadattasya putra utpanne yaj~nadatta iti tasya nAma kriyata iti | tasmAd virodha eva shabda iti cet, na | gavAdishabdArthasambandhanityatvadarshanAt | na hi gavAdivyaktInAm utpattimattve tadAkR^itInAm apyutpattimattvaM syAt | dravyaguNakarmaNAM hi vyaktaya evotpadyante, nAkR^itayaH | AkR^itibhishca shabdAnAM sambandhaH, na vyaktibhiH, vyaktInAm AnantyAt sambandhagrahaNAnupapatteH | vyaktiShUtpadyamAnAsvapyAkR^itInAM nityatvAt na gavAdishabdeShu kashcid virodho dR^ishyate | tathA devAdivyaktiprabhavAbhyupagame.apyAkR^itinityatvAt na kashcid vasvAdishabdeShu virodha iti draShTavyam | AkR^itivisheShaH tu devAdInAM mantrArthavAdAdibhyo vigrahavattvAd yavagamAd avagantavyaH | sthAnavisheShasambandhanimittA vA indrAdishabdAH senApatyAdishabdavat | tatashca yo yaH tattatsthAnam adhitiShThati, sa sa indrAdishabdair abhidhIyata iti na doSho bhavati | na cedaM shabdaprabhavatvaM brahmaprabhavatvavad upAdAnakAraNatvAbhiprAyeNocyate | kathaM tarhi, sthitavAcakAtmanA nitye shabde nityArthasambandhini shabdavyavahArayogyArthavyaktiniShpattiH | ataH prabhavaH ityucyate | kathaM punar avagamyate shabdAt prabhavati jagad iti? -- pratyakShAnumAnAbhyAm | 

pratyakShaM hi shrutiH, prAmANyaM pratyanapekShatvAt | anumAnaM smR^itiH, prAmANyaM prati sApekShatvAt | te hi shabdapUrvAM sR^iShTiM darshayataH -- eta iti vai prajApatir devAn asR^ijatAsR^igram iti manuShyAn indava iti pitMH tiraH pavitram iti grahAnAshava iti stotraM vishvAnIti shastram  abhisaubhagetyanyAH prajAH [paJNcaviMshatibrAhmaNa 6.9.13.22, 6.12.1.3]  iti shrutiH | tathAnyatrApi sa manasA vAcaM mithunaM samabhavat ityAdinA tatra tatra shabdapUrvikA sR^iShTiH shrAvyate | smR^itir api -- anAdinidhanA nityA vAg utsR^iShTA svayambhuvA | Adau vedamayI divyA yataH sarvAH pravR^ittayaH iti | utsargo.apyayaM vAcaH sampradAyapravartanAtmako draShTavyaH, anAdinidhanAyA anyAdR^ishasyotsargasyAsambhavAt | tathA nAma rUpaM ca bhUtAnAM karmaNAM ca pravartanam | vedashabdebhya evAdau nirmame sa maheshvaraH iti | sarveShAM tu sa nAmAni karmANi ca pR^ithak pR^ithak | vedashabdebhya evAdau pR^ithak saMsthAshca nirmame iti ca | api ca cikIrShitam artham anutiShThan tasya vAcakaM shabdaM pUrvaM smR^itvA pashcAt tam artham anutiShThatIti sarveShAM naH pratyakSham etat | tathA prajApater api sraShTuH sR^iShToH pUrvaM vaidikAH shabdA manasi prAdurbabhUvuH, pashcAt tadanugatAnarthAn sasarjeti gamyate | tathA ca shrutiH sa bhUH iti vyAharat sa bhUmim asR^ijata ityevamAdikA bhUrAdishabdebhya eva manasi prAdurbhUtebhyo bhUrAdilokAn sR^iShTAn darshayati || 

kimAtmakaM punaH shabdam abhipretyedaM shabdaprabhavatvam ucyate? sphoTAm ityAha | varNapakShe hi teShAm utpannapradhvaMsitvAn nityebhyaH shabdebhyo devAdivyaktInAM prabhava ityanupapannaM syAt | utpannadhvaMsinashca varNAH, pratyuccAraNam anyathA cAnyathA ca pratIyamAnatvAt | tathA hyadR^ishyamAno.api puruShavisheSho.adhyayanadhvanishravaNAd eva visheShato nirdhAryate -- devadatto.ayam adhIte, yaj~nadatto.ayam adhIte iti | na cAyaM varNaviShayo.anyathAtvapratyayo mithyAj~nAnam, bAdhakapratyayAbhAvAt | na ca varNebhyo.arthAvagatir yuktAH na hyekaiko varNe.arthaM pratyAyayet, vyabhicArAt | na ca varNasamudAyapratyayo.asti, kramavartitvAd varNAnAm | pUrvapUrvavarNAnubhavajanitasaMskArasahito.antyo varNo.arthaM pratyAyayiShyatIti yadyucyeta, tan na | sambandhagrahaNApekSho hi shabdaH svayaM pratIyamAno.arthaM pratyAyayet, dhUmAdivat | na ca pUrvapUrvavarNAnubhavajanitasaMskArasahitasyAntyavarNasya pratItir asti, apratyakShatvAt saMskArANAm | kAryapratyAyitaiH saMskAraiH sahito.antyo varNo.arthaM pratyAyayiShyatIti cet, na | saMskArakAryasyApi smaraNasya kramavartitvAt | tasmAt sphoTA eva shabdaH | sa caikaikavarNapratyayAhitasaMskArabIje.antyavarNapratyayajanitaparipAke pratyayinyekapratyayaviShayatayA jhaTiti pratyavabhAsate | na cAyam ekapratyayo varNaviShayA smR^itiH, varNAnAm anekatvAd ekapratyayaviShayatvAnupapatteH | tasya ca pratyuccAraNaM pratyabhij~nAyamAnatvAn nityatvam, bhedapratyayasya varNaviShayatvAt | tasmAn nityAcchabdAt sphoTarUpAd abhidhAyakAt kriyAkArakaphalalakShaNaM jagad abhidheyabhUtaM prabhavatIti || 

varNA eva tu shabdaH iti bhagavAn upavarShaH | nanUtpannapradhvaMsitvaM varNAnAm uktam | tan na, ta eveti pratyabhij~nAnAt | sAdR^ishyAt pratyabhij~nAnaM keshAdiShviveti cet, na | pratyabhij~nAnasya pramANAntareNa bAdhAnupapatteH | pratyabhij~nAnam AkR^itinimittam iti cet, na | vyaktipratyabhij~nAnAt | yadi hi pratyuccAraNaM gavAdivyaktivad anyA anyA varNavyaktayaH pratIyeran, tata AkR^itinimittaM pratyabhij~nAnaM syAt | na tv etad asti | varNavyaktaya eva hi pratyuccAraNaM pratyabhij~nAyante | dvirgoshabda uccAritaH -- iti hi pratipattiH | na tu dvau goshabdAviti | 

nanu varNApyuccAraNabhedena bhinnAH pratIyante, devadattayaj~nadattayor adhyayanadhvanishravaNAd eva bhedapratIteH ityuktam | atrAbhidhIyate -- sati varNaviShaye nishcite pratyabhij~nAne, saMyogavibhAgAbhivyaN^gyatvAd varNAnAm, abhivyaJNjakavaicitryanimitto.ayaM varNaviShayo vicitraH pratyayaH, na svarUpanimittaH | api ca varNavyaktibhedavAdinApi pratyabhij~nAnasiddhaye varNAkR^itayaH kalpayitavyAH | tAsu ca paropAdhiko bhedapratyaya ityabhyupagantavyam | tadvaraM varNavyaktiShv eva paropAdhiko bhedapratyayaH, svarUpanimittaM ca pratyabhij~nAnam -- iti kalpanAlAghavam | eSha eva ca varNaviShayasya bhedapratyayasya bAdhakaH pratyayaH, yat pratyabhij~nAnam | kathaM hyekasmin kAle bahUnAm uccArayatAm eka eva san gakAro yugapadanekarUpaH syAt -- udAttashcAnudAttashca svaritashca sAnunAsikashca niranunAsikashceti | athavA dhvanikR^ito.ayaM bhedapratyayo na varNakR^ita ityadoShaH | 

kaH punar ayaM dhvanir nAma? yo dUrAd AkarNayato varNavivekam apratipadyamAnasya karNapatham avatarati | pratyAsItadatashca paTau mR^idutvAdibhedaM varNeShvasaJNjayati | tannibandhanAshcodAttAdayo visheShAH, na varNasvarUpanibandhanAH, varNAnAM pratyuccAraNaM pratyabhij~nAyamAnatvAt | evaM ca sati sAlambanA evaite udAttAdipratyayA bhaviShyanti | itarathA hi varNAnAM pratyabhij~nAyamAnAnAM nirbhedatvAt saMyogavibhAgakR^itA udAttAdivisheShAH kalpyeran | saMyogavibhAgAnAM cApratyakShatvAn na tadAshrayA visheShAH varNeShvadhyavasAtuM shakyanta ityato nirAlambanA eva ete udAttAdipratyayAH syuH | api ca naivaitadabhiniveShTavyam -- udAttAdibhedena varNAnAM pratyabhij~nAyamAnAnAM bhedo bhaved iti | na hyanyasya bhedenAnyasyAbhidyamAnasya bhedo bhavitum arhati | na hi vyaktibhedena jAtiM bhinnAM manyante | varNebhyashcArthapratIteH sambhavAt sphoTakalpanAnarthikA | na kalpayAmyahaM sphoTam, pratyakSham eva tv enam avagacchAmi, ekaikavarNagrahaNAhitasaMskArAyA buddhau jhaTiti pratyavabhAsanAd iti cet, na | asyA api buddhir varNaviShayatvAt | ekaikavarNagrahaNottarakAlA hIyam ekA buddhir gauH iti samastavarNaviShayA, nArthAntaraviShayA | katham etad avagamyate? yato.asyAm api buddhau gakArAdayo varNA anuvartante, na tu dakArAdayaH | yadi hyasyA buddhir gakArAdibhyo.arthAntaraM sphoTe viShayaH syAt, tato dakArAdaya iva gakArAdayo.apyasyA buddhir vyAvarteran | na tu tathAsti | tasmAd iyam ekabuddhir varNaviShayaiva smR^itiH | 
nanvanekatvAd varNAnAM naikabuddhiviShayatopapadyata ityuktam, tat prati brUmaH -- sambhavatyanekasyApyekabuddhiviShayatvam, paN^ktiH vanaM senA dasha shataM sahasram ityAdidarshanAt | yA tu gauH ityeko.ayaM shabda iti buddhiH, sA bahuShv eva varNeShv ekArthAvacchedanibandhanA aupacArikI vanasenAdibuddhivad eva | atrAha -- yadi varNA eva sAmastyena ekabuddhiviShayatAm ApadyamAnAH padaM syuH, tato jArA rAjA kapiH pika ityAdiShu padavisheShapratipattir na syAt | ta eva hi varNA itaratretaratra ca pratyavabhAsanta iti | atra vadAmaH -- satyapi samastavarNapratyavamarshe yathA kramAnurodhinya eva pipIlikAH paN^ktibuddhim Arohanti, evaM kramAnurodhina eva hi varNAH padabuddhim ArokShyanti | tatra varNAnAm avisheShe.api kramavisheShakR^itA padavisheShapratipattir na virudhyate | vR^iddhavyavahAre ceme varNAH kramAdyanugR^ihItA gR^ihItArthavisheShasambandhAH santaH svavyavahAre.apyekaikavarNagrahaNAnantaraM samastapratyavamarshinyAM buddhau tAdR^ishA eva pratyavabhAsamAnAH taM tam artham avyabhicAreNa pratyAyayiShyantIti varNavAdino laghIyasI kalpanA | sphoTavAdinaH tu dR^iShTahAniH, adR^iShTakalpanA ca | varNAshceme krameNa gR^ihyamANAH sphoTaM vyaJNjayanti sa sphoTe.arthaM vyanaktIti garIyasI kalpanA syAt || 

athApi nAma pratyuccAraNam anye.anye varNAH syuH, tathApi pratyabhij~nAlambanabhAvena varNasAmAnyAnAm avashyAbhyupagantavyatvAt, varNeShvarthapratipAdanaprakriyA racitA sA sAmAnyeShu saMcArayitavyA | tatashca nityebhyaH shabdebhyo devAdivyaktInAM prabhava ityaviruddham ||28||

|| 1.3.29 ||
ata eva ca nityatvam ||
kartur asmaraNAd iti sthite vedasya nityatve devAdivyaktiprabhavAbhyupagamena tasya virodham AshaN^kya ataH prabhavAt iti parihR^itya idAnIM tad eva vedanityatvaM sthitaM draDhayati -- ata eva ca nityatvam iti | ata eva niyatAkR^iter devAder jagato vedashabdaprabhavatvAt vedashabdanityatvam api pratyetavyam | tathA ca mantravarNaH -- yaj~nena vAcaH padavIyamAyaMH tAm anvavindan nR^iShiShu praviShTam iti sthitAm eva vAcam anuvinnAM darshayati | vedavyAsashcaivam eva smarati -- 

yugAnte.antarhitAn vedAn setihAsAn maharShayaH | 
lebhire tapasA pUrvam anuj~nAtAH svayambhuvA || iti ||

|| 1.3.30 || 

samAnanAmarUpatvAccAvR^ittAvapyavirodho darshanAt smR^iteshca ||

athApi syAt -- yadi pashvAdivyaktivad devAdivyaktayo.api santatyaivotpadyeran nirudhyeraMshca, tato.abhidhAnAbhidheyAbhidhAtR^ivyavahArAvicchedAt sambandhanityatvena virodhaH shabde parihriyeta | yadA tu khalu sakalaM trailokyaM parityaktanAmarUpaM nirlepaM pralIyate, prabhavati cAbhinavam iti shrutismR^itivAdA vadanti, tadA katham avirodha 
iti | tatredam abhidhIyate samAnanAmarUpatvAd iti | tadApi saMsArasyAnAditvaM tAvad abhyupagantavyam | pratipAdayiShyati cAcAryaH saMsArasyAnAditvam -- upapadyate cApyupalabhyate ca iti | anAdau ca saMsAre yathA svApaprabodhayoH pralayaprabhavashravaNe.api pUrvaprabodhavad uttaraprabodhe.api vyavahArAn na kashcid virodhaH, evaM kalpAntaraprabhavapralayayor apIti draShTavyam | svApaprabodhayoshca pralayaprabhavau shrUyete -- yadA suptaH svapnaM na kaMcana pashyatyathAsmin prANa evaikadhA bhavati tadainaM vAksarvair nAmabhiH sahApyeti cakShuH sarve rUpaiH sahApyeti shrotraM sarvaiH shabdaiH sahApyeti manaH sarvair dhyAnaiH sahApyeti sa yadA pratibudhyate yathAgner jvalataH sarvA disho visphuliN^gA vipratiShTherann evam evaitasmAd AtmanaH sarve prANA yathAyatanaM vipratiShThante prANebhyo devA devebhyo lokAH iti | syAd etat -- svApe puruShAntaravyavahArAvicchedAt svayaM ca suShuptaprabuddhasya pUrvaprabodhavyavahArAnusandhAnasambhavAd aviruddham | mahApralaye tu sarvavyavahArocchedAjjanmAntaravyavahAravacca kalpAntaravyavahArasyAnusandhAtum ashakyatvAd vaiShamyam iti | naiSha doShaH, satyapi sarvavyavahArocchedini mahApralaye parameshvarAnugrahAdIshvarANAM hiraNyagarbhAdInAM kalpAntaravyavahArAnusandhAnopapatteH | yadyapi prAkR^itAH prANino na janmAntaravyavahAram anusandadhAnA dR^ishyanta iti, tathApi na tatprAkR^itavad IshvarANAM bhavitavyam | yathA hi prANitvAvisheShe.api manuShyAdistambaparyanteShu j~nAnaishvaryAdipratibandhaH pareNa pareNa bhUyAn bhavan dR^ishyate | tathA manuShyAdiShv eva hiraNyagarbhaparyanteShu j~nAnaishvaryAdyabhivyaktir api pareNa pareNa bhUyasI bhavatItyetacchrutismR^itivAdeShvasakR^idevAnukalpAdau prAdur bhavatAM pAramaishvaryaM shrUyamANaM na shakyaM nAstIti vaditum | tatashcAtItakalpAnuShThitaprakR^iShTAj~nAnakarmaNAm IshvarANAM hiraNyagarbhAdInAM vartamAnakalpAdau prAdur bhavatAM parameshvarAnugR^ihItAnAM suptapratibuddhavatkalpAntaravyavahArAnusandhAnopapattiH | tathA ca shrutiH -- 

yo brahmANaM vidadhAti pUrvaM 
yo vai vedAMshca prahiNoti tasmai | 
taM hi devam AtmabuddhiprakAshaM 
mumukShur vai sharaNam ahaM prapadye || [shve.u. 6.18] iti | 

smaranti ca shaunakAdayaH -- madhucchandaHprabhR^itibhir R^iShibhir dAshatayyo dR^iShTaH iti | prativedaM caivam eva kANDAShryAdayaH smaryante | shrutir api R^iShij~nAnapUrvakam eva mantreNAnuShThAnaM darshayati -- yo ha vA aviditArSheyacchandodaivatabrAhmaNena mantreNa yAjayati vAdhyApayati vA sthANuM vacrchati gartaM vA pratipadyate ityupakramya tasmAd etAni mantre mantre vidyAt iti | prANinAM ca sukhaprAptaye dharmo vidhIyate | duHkhaparihArAya cAdharmaH pratiShidhyate | dR^iShTAnushravikasukhaduHkhaviShayau ca rAgadveShau bhavataH, na vilakShaNaviShayau -- ityato dharmAdharmaphalabhUtottarottarA sR^iShTir niShpadyamAnA pUrvasR^iShTisadR^ishyeva niShpadyate | smR^itishca bhavati -- teShAM ye yAni karmANi prAksR^iShTyAM pratipedire | tAnyeva te prapadyante sR^ijyamAnAH punaH punaH || hiMsrAhiMsre mR^idukrUre dharmAdharmAvR^itAnR^ite | tadbhAvitAH prapadyante tasmAt tattasya rocate iti | pralIyamAnam api cedaM jagacchaktyavasheSham eva pralIyate | shaktimUlam eva ca prabhavati | itarathA AkasmikatvaprasaN^gAt | na cAnekAkArAH shaktayaH shakyAH kalpayitum | tatashca vicchidya vicchidyApyudbhavatAM bhUrAdilokapravAhANAm, devatiryaN^manuShyalakShaNAnAM ca prANinikAyapravAhANAm, varNAshramadharmaphalavyavasthAnAM cAnAdau saMsAre niyatatvam indriyaviShayasambandhaniyatatvavatpratyetavyam | na hIndriyaviShayasambandhAder vyavahArasya pratisargamanyathAtvaM ShaShThendriyaviShayakalpaM shakyam utprekShitum | atashca sarvakalpAnAM tulyavyavahAratvAt kalpAntaravyavahArAnusandhAnakShamatvAcceshvarANAM samAnanAmarUpA eva pratisargaM visheShAH prAdurbhavanti | samAnanAmarUpatvAccAvR^ittAvapi mahAsargamahApralayalakShaNAyAM jagato.abhyupagamyamAnAyAM na kashcicchabdaprAmANyAdivirodhaH | samAnanAmarUpatAM ca shrutismR^itI darshayataH -- 
sUryAcandramasau dhAtA yathApUrvam akalpayat | 
divaM ca pR^ithivIM cAntarikShamatho suvaH || [R^i.ve. 10.190.3] iti | 
yathA pUrvasmin kalpe sUryAcandramaHprabhR^iti jagat kptam, tathAsminn api kalpe parameshvaro.akalpayad ityarthaH | tathA -- agnir vA akAmayata | annAdo devAnAM syAm iti | sa etam agnaye kR^ittikAbhyaH puroDAsham aShTakapAlaM niravapat iti nakShatreShTividhau yo.agnir niravapat yasmai vAgnaye niravapat, tayoH samAnanAmarUpatAM darshayati -- ityevaMjAtIyakA shrutiH ihodAhartavyA | smR^itir api -- 
R^iShINAM nAmadheyAni yAshca vedeShu dR^iShTayaH | 
sharvaryante prasUtAnAM tAnyevaibhyo dadAtyajaH || 
yatha rtuShv R^ituliN^gAni nAnArUpANi paryaye | 
dR^ishyante tAni tAnyeva tathA bhAvA yugAdiShu || 
yathAbhimAnino.atItAH tulyAH te sAmprataiH iha | 
devA devair atItair hi rUpair nAmabhir eva ca || ityevaMjAtIyakA draShTavyA ||30||

|| 1.3.31 ||
madhvAdiShvasambhavAd anadhikAraM jaiminiH ||

iha devAdInAm api brahmavidyAyAm astyadhikAra iti yat pratij~nAtaM tat paryAvartyate -- devAdInAm anadhikAraM jaiminir AcAryo manyate | kasmAt? madhvAdiShvasambhavAt | brahmavidyAyAm adhikArAbhyupagame hi vidyAtvAvisheShAt madhvAdividyAsvapyadhikAro.abhyupagamyeta | na caivaM sambhavati | katham? asau vA Adityo devamadhu [chA.u. 3.1.1] ityatra manuShyA AdityaM madhvadhyAsenopAsIran | devAdiShu hyupAsakeShvabhyupagamyamAneShvadityaH katham anyam Adityam upAsIta? punashcAdityavyapAshrayANi paJNca rohitAdInyamR^itAnyanukramya, vasavo rudrA AdityA marutaH sAdhyAshca paJNca devagaNAH krameNa tattadamR^itam upajIvantItyupadishya, sa ya etad evam amR^itaM veda vasUnAm evaiko bhUtvAgninaiva mukhenaitad evAmR^itaM dR^iShTvA tR^ipyati ityAdinA vasvAdyupajIvyAnyamR^itAni vijAnatAM vasvAdimahimaprAptiM darshayati | vasvAdayaH tu kAn anyAn vasvAdIn amR^itopajIvino vijAnIyuH? kaM vAnyaM vasvAdimahimAnaM prepseyuH? tathA -- agniH pAdo vAyuH pAda AdityaH pAdo dishaH pAdaH vAyur vA saMvargaH Adityo brahmetyAdeshaH ityAdiShu devatAtmopAsaneShu na teShAm eva devatAtmanAm adhikAraH sambhavati | tathA imAm eva gautamabharadvAjAvayaM vai gautamo.ayaM bharadvAjaH ityAdiShvapi R^iShisambandheShUpAsaneShu na teShAm eva R^iShINAm adhikAraH sambhavati ||31|| 
 
|| 1.3.32 ||

kutashca devAdInAm anadhikAraH -- 

jyotiShi bhAvAcca ||

yad idaM jyotirmaNDalaM dyusthAnam ahorAtrAbhyAM bambhramajjagad avabhAsayati, tasminn AdityAdayo devatAvacanAH shabdAH prayujyante | lokaprasiddhir vAkyasheShaprasiddhishca | na ca jyotirmaNDalasya hR^idayAdinA vigraheNa cetanatayA arthitvAdinA vA yogo.avagantuM shakyate, mR^idAdivad acetanatvAvagamAt | etenAgnyAdayo vyAkhyAtAH || 

syAd etat -- mantrArthavAdetihAsapurANalokebhyo devAdInAM vigrahavattvAdyavagamAd ayam adoSha iti cet, netyucyate | na tAval loko nAma kiMcit svatantraM pramANam asti | pratyakShAdibhya eva avyabhicaritaviShayebhyaH pramANebhyaH prasiddha evArtho lokAt prasiddha ityucyate | na cAtra pratyakShAdInAm anyatamaM pramANam asti | itihAsapurANAnAm api pauruSheyatvAt pramANAntaramUlatAm AkAN^kShati | arthavAdA api vidhinaikavAkyatvAt stutyarthAH santo na pArthagarthyena devAdInAM vigrahAdisadbhAve kAraNabhAvaM pratipadyante | mantrA api shrutyAdiviniyuktAH prayogasamavAyino.abhidhAnArthA na kasyacid arthasya pramANam ityAcakShate | tasmAd abhAvo devAdInAm adhikArasya ||32||

 -- o)0(o -- 

8. bhAvAdhikaraNam

|| 1.3.33 ||

bhAvaM tu bAdarAyaNo.asti hi ||

tushabdaH pUrvapakShaM vyAvartayati | bAdarAyaNaH tvacAryo bhAvam adhikArasya devAdInAm api manyate | yadyapi madhvAdividyAsu devatAdivyAmishrAsvasambhavo.adhikArasya, tathApyasti hi shuddhAyAM brahmavidyAyAM sambhavaH | arthitvasAmarthyApratiShedhAdyapekShatvAd adhikArasya | na ca kvacid asambhava ityetAvatA yatra sambhavaH tatrApyadhikAro.apodyeta | manuShyANAm api na sarveShAM brAhmaNAdInAM sarveShu rAjasUyAdiShvadhikAraH sambhavati | tatra yo nyAyaH so.atrApi bhaviShyati | brahmavidyAM ca prakR^itya bhavati liN^gadarshanaM shrautaM devAdyadhikArasya sUcakam -- tadyo yo devAnAM pratyabudhyata sa eva tadabhavat tathA R^iShINAM tathA manuShyANAm iti, te hocur hanta tam AtmAnam anvicchAmo yam AtmAnam anviShya sarvAMshca lokAn Apnoti sarvAMshca kAmAn iti, indro ha vai devAnAm abhipravavrAja virocano.asurANAm ityAdi ca | smArtam api ca gandharvayAj~navalkyasaMvAdAd iti |

yad apyuktam jyotiShi bhAvAcca iti, atra brUmaH -- jyotirAdiviShayA api AdityAdayo devatAvacanAH shabdAshcetanAvantam aishvaryAdyupetaM taM taM devatAtmAnaM samarpayanti, mantrArthavAdAdiShu tathA vyavahArAt | asti hyaishvaryayogAd devatAnAM jyotirAdyAtmabhishcAvasthAtuM yatheShTaM ca taM taM vigrahaM grahItuM sAmarthyam | tathA hi shrUyate subrahmaNyArthavAde -- medhAtither meSha -- iti -- medhAtithiM ha kANvAyanam indro meSho bhUtvA jahAra iti | smaryate ca -- AdityaH puruSho bhUtvA kuntIm upajagAma ha iti | mR^idAdiShvapi cetanA adhiShThAtAro.abhyupagamyante | mR^id abravIt Apo.abruvan ityAdi darshanAt | jyodirAdeH tu bhUtadhAtor AdityAdiShvapyacetanatvam abhyupagamyate | cetanAH tu adhiShThAtAro devatAtmAno mantrArthavAdAdiShu vyavahArAd ityuktam || 

yad apyuktam -- mantrArthavAdayor anyArthatvAn na devatAvigrahAdiprakAshanasAmarthyam iti, atra brUmaH -- pratyayApratyayau hi sadbhAvAsadbhAvayoH kAraNam | nAnyArthatvam ananyArthatvaM vA | tathA hyanyArtham api prasthitaH pathi patitaM tR^iNaparNAdyastItyeva pratipadyate | atrAha -- viShama upanyAsaH | tatra hi tR^iNaparNAdiviShayaM pratyakShaM pravR^ittam asti, yena tad astitvaM pratipadyate | atra punar vidhyuddeshaikavAkyabhAvena stutyarthe.arthavAde na pArthagarthyena vR^ittAntaviShayA pravR^ittiH shakyAdhyavasAtum | na hi mahAvAkye.arthapratyAyake.avAntaravAkyasya pR^ithakpratyAyakatvam asti | yathA na surAM pibet iti naJNvativAkye padatrayasambandhAt surApAnapratiShedha evaiko.artho.avagamyate | na punaH surAM pibed iti padadvayasambandhAt surApAnavidhir apIti | 

atrocyate -- viShama upanyAsaH | yuktaM yat surApAnapratiShedhe padAnvayasyaikatvAd avAntaravAkyArthasyAgrahaNam | vidhyuddeshArthavAdayoH tu arthavAdasthAni padAni pR^ithag anvayaM vR^ittAntaviShayaM pratipadya, anantaraM kaimarthyavashena kAmaM vidheH stAvakatvaM pratipadyante | yathA hi vAyavyaM shvetam Alabheta bhUtakAmaH ityatra vidhyuddeshavartinAM vAyavyAdipadAnAM vidhinA sambandhaH, naivam vAyur ve kShepiShThA devatA vAyum eva svena bhAgadheyenopadhAvati sa evainaM bhUtiM gamayati ityeShAm arthavAdagatAnAM padAnAm | na hi bhavati vAyur vA Alabheta iti kShepiShThA devatA vA Alabheta ityAdi | vAyusvabhAvasaN^kIrtanena tu avAntaram anvayaM pratipadya, evaM vishiShTadaivatyam idaM karmeti vidhiM stuvanti | tad yatra yo.avAntaravAkyArthaH pramANAntaragocaro bhavati, tatra tadanuvAdenArthavAdaH pravartate | yatra pramANAntaraviruddhaH, tatra guNavAdena | yatra tu tad ubhayaM nAsti, tatra kiM pramANAntarAbhAvAd guNavAdaH syAt, AhostvitpramANAntarAvirodhAd vidyamAnArthavAda iti -- pratItisharaNair vidyamAnArthavAda AshrayaNIyaH, na guNAnuvAdaH | etena mantro vyAkhyAtaH | 

api ca vidhibhir evendrAdidaivatyAni havIMShi codayadbhir apekShitam indrAdInAM svarUpam | na hi svarUparahitA indrAdayashcetasyAropayituM shakyante | na ca cetasyanArUDhAyai tasyai tasyai devatAyai haviH pradAtuM shakyate | shrAvayati ca -- yasyai devatAyai havir gR^ihItaM syAt tAM dhyAyed vaShaT kariShyan iti | na ca shabdamAtram arthasvarUpaM sambhavati, shabdArthayor bhedAt | tatra yAdR^ishaM mantrArthavAdayoH indrAdInAM svarUpam avagataM na tat tAdR^ishaM shabdapramANakena pratyAkhyAtuM yuktam | itihAsapurANam api vyAkhyAtena mArgeNa sambhavanmantrArthavAdamUlakatvAt prabhavati devatAvigrahAdi sAdhayitum | pratyakShAdimUlam api sambhavati | bhavati hyasmAkam apratyakSham api cirantanAnAM pratyakSham | tathA ca vyAsAdayo devAdibhiH pratyakShaM vyavaharantIti smaryate | yaH tu brUyAt -- idAnIntanAnAm iva pUrveShAm api nAsti devAdibhir vyavahartuM sAmarthyam iti, sa jagad vaicitryaM pratiShedhet | idAnIm iva ca nAnyadApi sArvabhaumaH kShatriyo.astIti brUyAt, tatashca rAjasUyAdicodanA uparundhyAt | idAnIm iva ca kAlAntare.apyavyavasthitaprAyAn varNAshramadharmAn pratijAnIta, tatashca vyavasthAvidhAyi shAstramanarthakaM kuryAt | tasmAd dharmotkarShavashAccirantanA devAdibhiH pratyakShaM vyavajahnuH iti shliShyate | 

api ca smaranti -- svAdhyAyAdiShTadevatAsamprayogaH ityAdi | yogo.apyaNimAdyaishvaryaprAptiphalakaH smaryamANo na shakyate sAhasamAtreNa pratyAkhyAtum | shrutishca yogamAhAtmyaM prakhyApayati -- pR^ithivyaptejo.anilakhe samutthite paJNcAtmake yogaguNe pravR^itte | na tasya rogo na jarA na mR^ityuH prAptasya yogAgnimayaM sharIram iti | R^iShINAm api mantrabrAhmaNadarshinAM sAmarthyaM nAsmadIyena sAmarthyenopamAtuM yuktam | tasmAt samUlam itihAsapurANaM lokaprasiddhir api na sati sambhave nirAlambanAdhyavasAtuM yuktA | tasmAd upapanno mantrAdibhyo devAdInAM vigrahavattvAdyavagamaH | tatashcArthitvAdisambhavAd upapanno devAdInAm api brahmavidyAyAm adhikAraH | kramamuktidarshanAnyapyevam evopapadyante ||33||

  -- o)0(o -- 
9. apashUdrAdhikaraNam

|| 1.3.34 ||

yathA manuShyAdhikAraniyamam apodya devAdInAm api vidyAsvadhikAra uktaH, tathaiva dvijAtyadhikAraniyamApavAdena shUdrasyApyadhikAraH syAd ityetAm AshaN^kAM nivartayitum idam adhikaraNam Arabhyate | tatra shUdrasyApyadhikAraH syAd iti tAvat prAptam | arthitvasAmarthyayoH sambhavAt, tasmAcchUdro yaj~ne.anavakptaH itivat shUdro vidyAyAm anavakpta iti niShedhAshravaNAt | yacca karmasvanadhikArakAraNaM shUdrasyAnagnitvam, na tadvidyAsvadhikArasyApavAdakam | na hyAhavanIyAdirahitena vidyA vedituM na shakyate | bhavati ca shrautaM liN^gaM shUdrAdhikArasyopodbalakam | saMvargavidyAyAM hi jAnashrutiM pautrAyaNaM shushrUShuM shUdrashabdena parAmR^ishati -- aha hAre tvA shUdra tavaiva saha gobhir astu iti | viduraprabhR^itayashca shUdrayoniprabhavA api vishiShTavij~nAnasampannAH smaryante | tasmAd adhikriyate shUdro vidyAsvityevaM prApte -- 

shug asya tadanAdarashravaNAt tad AdravaNAt sUcyate hi ||

brUmaH -- na shUdrasyAdhikAraH, vedAdhyayanAbhAvAt | adhItavedo hi viditavedArtho vedArtheShvadhikriyate | na ca shUdrasya vedAdhyayanam asti | upanayanapUrvakatvAd vedAdhyayanasya, upanayanasya ca varNatrayaviShayatvAt | yat tu arthitvam, na tad asati sAmarthye.adhikArakAraNaM bhavati | sAmarthyam api na laukikaM kevalam adhikArakAraNaM bhavati | shAstrIye.arthe shAstrIyasya sAmarthyasyApekShitatvAt, shAstrIyasya ca sAmarthyasyAdhyayananirAkaraNena nirAkR^itatvAt | yaccedam shUdro yaj~ne.anavakptaH iti, tat nyAyapUrvakatvAd vidyAyAm apyanavakptatvaM dyotayati | nyAyasya sAdhAraNatvAt | yat punaH saMvargavidyAyAM shUdrashabdashravaNaM liN^gaM manyase, na talliN^gam | nyAyAbhAvAt | nyAyokte hi liN^gadarshanaM, dyotakaM bhavati | na cAtra nyAyo.asti | kAmaM cAyaM shUdrashabdaH saMvargavidyAyAm evaikasyAM shUdram adhikuryAt, tadviShayatvAt | na sarvAsu vidyAsu | arthavAdasthatvAt tu na kvacid apyayaM shUdram adhikartum utsahate | shakyate cAyaM shUdrashabdo.adhikR^itaviShaye yojayitum | katham ityucyate -- kamvara enam etat santaM sayugvAnam iva raikvam Attha ityasmAd dhaMsavAkyAd Atmano.anAdaraM shrutavato jAnashruteH pautrAyaNasya shuk utpede | tAm R^iShI raikvaH shUdrashabdenAnena sUcayAm babhUva AtmanaH parokShaj~natAkhyApanAyeti gamyate, jAtishUdrasyAnadhikArAt | kathaM punaH shUdrashabdena shugutpannA sUcyata iti, ucyate -- tadAdravaNAt | shucam abhidudrAva, shucA vA abhidupve, shucA vA raikvam abhidudrAva -- iti shUdraH | avayavArthasambhavAt, rUDhyarthasya cAsambhavAt | dR^ishyate cAyam artho.asyAm AkhyAyikAyAm ||34||

|| 1.3.35 || 

kShatriyatvagateshcottaratra caitrarathena liN^gAt ||

itashca na jAtishUdro jAnashrutiH | yat kAraNaM prakaraNanirUpaNena kShatriyatvam asyottaratra caitrarathenAbhipratAriNA kShatriyeNa samabhivyAhArAl liN^gAd gamyate | uttaratra hi saMvargavidyAvAkyasheShe caitrarathir abhipratArI kShatriyaH saN^kIrtyate -- atha ha shaunakaM ca kApeyam abhipratAriNaM ca kAkShaseniM sUdena pariviShyamANau brahmacArI bibhikShe iti | caitrarathitvaM cAbhipratAriNaH kApeyayogAd avagantavyam | kApeyayogo hi citrarathasyAvagataH etena vai citrarathaM kApeyA ayAjayan iti | samAnAnvayAnAM ca prAyeNa samAnAnvayA yAjakA bhavanti | tasmAccaitrarathir nAmaikaH kShatrapatir ajAyata iti ca kShatrapatitvAvagamAt kShatriyatvam asyAvagantavyam | tena kShatriyeNAbhipratAriNA saha samAnAyAM saMvargavidyAyAM saN^kIrtanaM jAnashruter api kShatriyatvaM sUcayati | samAnAnAm eva hi prAyeNa samabhivyAhArA bhavanti | kShattR^ipreShaNAdyaishvaryayogAcca jAnashruteH kShatriyatvAvagatiH | ato na shUdrasyAdhikAraH ||35||

|| 1.3.36 || 

saMskAraparAmarshAt tadabhAvAbhilApAcca ||
