itashca na shUdrasyAdhikAraH, yad vidyApradesheShUpanayanAdayaH saMskArAH parAmR^ishyante -- taM hopaninye adhIhi bhagava iti hopasasAda brahmaparA brahmaniShThAH paraM brahmAnveShamANA eSha ha vai tat sarvaM vakShyatIti te ha samitpANayo bhagavantaM pippalAdam upasannAH iti ca | tAn hAnupanIyaiva ityapi pradarshitaivopanayanaprAptir bhavati | shUdrasya ca saMskArAbhAvo.abhilapyate shUdrashcaturtho varNa ekajAtiH ityekajAtitvasmaraNAt | na shUpA pAtakaM kiMcin na ca saMskAram arhati ityAdibhishca ||

|| 1.3.37 || 

tadabhAvanirdhAraNe ca pravR^itteH ||

itashca na shUdrasyAdhikAraH | yat satyavacanena shUdratvAbhAve nirdhArite jAbAlaM gautama upanetum anushAsituM ca pravavR^ite -- naitad abrAhmaNo vivaktum arhati samidhaM somyAharopa tvA neShye na satyAd agAH iti shrutiliN^gAt ||37||

|| 1.3.38 || 

shravaNAdhyayanArthapratiShedhAt smR^iteshca ||

itashca na shUdrasyAdhikAraH | yad asya smR^iteH shravaNAdhyayanArthapratiShedho bhavati | vedashravaNapratiShedhaH, vedAdhyayanapratiShedhaH, tadarthaj~nAnAnuShThAnayoshca pratiShedhaH shUdrasya smaryate | shravaNapratiShedhaH tAvat -- atha hAsya vedam upashR^iNvataH trapujatubhyAM shrotrapratipUraNam iti | padyu ha vA etacchamashAnaM yacchUdraH tasmAcchUdrasamIpe nAdhyetavyam iti ca | ata evAdhyayanapratiShedhaH | yasya hi samIpe.api nAdhyetavyaM bhavati, sa katham ashrutam adhIyIta | bhavati ca vedoccAraNe jihvAcchedaH, dhAraNe sharIrabheda iti | ata eva cArthAd arthaj~nAnAnuShThAnayoH pratiShedho bhavati -- na shUdrAya matiM dadyAt iti, dvijAtInAm adhyayanam ijyA dAnam iti ca | yeShAM punaH pUrvakR^itasaMskAravashAd viduradharmavyAdhaprabhR^itInAM j~nAnotpattiH, teShAM na shakyate phalaprAptiH pratiSheddhum, j~nAnasyaikAntikaphalatvAt | shrAvayeccaturo varNAn iti cetihAsapurANAdhigame cAturvarNyasyAdhikArasmaraNAt | vedapUrvakaH tu nAstyadhikAraH shUdrANAm iti sthitam ||38||

kampanAdhikaraNam 
|| 1.3.39 || 

avasitaH prAsaN^giko.adhikAravicAraH | prakR^itAm evedAnIM vAkyArthavicAraNAM pravartayiShyAmaH | 

yad idaM kiM ca jagat sarvaM prANa ejati niHsR^itam |
mahad bhayaM vajram udyataM ya etad vidur amR^itAH te bhavanti || [ka.u. 2.3.2] iti |

etad vAkyam ejR^i kampane iti dhAtvarthAnugamAl lakShitam | asmin vAkye sarvam idaM jagat prANAshrayaM spandate, mahacca kiMcidbhayakAraNaM vajrashabditam udyatam, tadvij~nAnAccAmR^itatvaprAptiH iti shrUyate | tatra, ko.asau prANaH, kiM tadbhayAnakaM vajram, ityapratipattervicAre kriyamANe, prAptaM tAvat -- prasiddhaH paJNcavR^ittirvAyuH prANa iti | prasiddhar eva cAshanirvajraM syAt | vAyoshcedaM mAhAtmyaM saN^kIrtyate | katham? sarvam idaM jagat paJNcavR^ittau vAyau prANashabdite pratiShThAya ejati | vAyunimittam eva ca mahadbhayAnakaM vajramudyamyate | vAyau hi parjanyabhAvena vivartamAne vidyutstanayitnuvR^iShThyAshanayo vivartanta ityAcakShate | vAyuvij~nAnAd eva cedamamR^itatvam | tathA hi shrutyantaram -- vAyur eva vyaShTirvAyuH samaShTirapa punar mR^ityuM jayati ya evaM veda iti | tasmAd vAyurayam iha pratipattavyaH ityevaM prApte -- 

kampanAt |

brUmaH -- brahmaivedam iha pratipattavyam | kutaH? pUrvottarAlocanAt | pUrvottarayor hi granthabhAgayor brahmaiva nirdishyamAnam upalabhAmahe | ihaiva katham akasmAd antarAle vAyuM nirdishyamAnaM pratipadyemahi? pUrvatra tAvat tad eva shukraM tad brahma tad evAmR^ita mucyate | tasmiMl lokAH shritAH sarve tad u nAtyeti kashcana iti brahma nirdiShTam | tad eva ihApi, saMnidhAnAt, jagat sarvaM prANa ejati iti ca lokAshrayatvapratyabhij~nAnAt nirdiShTam iti gamyate | prANashabdo.apyayaM paramAtmanyeva prayuktaH -- prANasya prANam iti darshanAt | ejayitR^itvam apIdaM paramAtmana evopapadyate, na vAyumAtrasya | tathA coktam -- 

na prANena nApAnena martyo jIvati kashcana | 
itareNa tu jIvanti yasminn etAv upAshritau || [kA. 2.5.5] iti | 

uttaratrApi -- 
bhayAd asyAgniH tapati bhayAt tapati sUryaH | 
bhayAd indrashca vAyushca mR^ityur dhAvati paJNcamaH || [kA. 2.6.3]

iti brahmaiva nirdekShyate, na vAyuH, sa vAyukasya jagato bhayahetutvAbhidhAnAt | tad eva ihApi saMnidhAnAt mahad bhayaM vajram udyatam iti ca bhayahetutvaM pratyabhij~nAnAn nirdiShTam iti gamyate | vajrashabdo.apyayaM bhayahetutvasAmAnyAt prayuktaH | yathA hi vajram udyataM mamaiva shirasi nipatet, yadyaham asya shAsanaM na kuryAm ityanena bhayena jano niyamena rAjAdishAsane pravartate, evam idam agnivAyusUryAdikaM jagat asmAd eva brahmaNo bibhyat niyamena svavyApAre pravartata iti -- bhayAnakaM vajropamitaM brahma | tathA ca brahmaviShayaM shrutyantaram -- 

bhIShAsmAd vAtaH pavate | bhIShodeti sUryaH | 
bhIShAsmAd agnishcendrashca | mR^ityur dhAvati paJNcamaH || [tai.u. 2.8.1] iti | 

amR^itatvaphalashravaNAd api brahmaivedam iti gamyate | brahmaj~nAnAd dhyamR^itatvaprAptiH, tam eva viditvAtimR^ityum eti nAnyaH panthA vidyate.ayanAya [shve.u. 3.8] iti mantravarNAt | yat tu vAyuvij~nAnAt kvacid amR^itatvam abhihitam, tad ApekShikam | tatraiva prakaraNAntarakaraNena paramAtmAnam abhidhAya ato.anyad Artam iti vAyvAder ArtatvAbhidhAnAt | prakaraNAd apyatra paramAtmanishcayaH | anyatra dharmAd anyatrAdharmAd anyatrAsmAt kR^itAkR^itAt | anyatra bhUtAcca bhavyAcca yat tat pashyasi tad vada iti paramAtmanaH pR^iShTatvAt ||39||

  -- o)0(o -- 

11. jyotiradhikaraNam 
|| 1.3.40 || 

eSha samprasAdo.asmAccharIrAt samutthAya paraM jyotir upasampadya svena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyate [chA.u. 8.3.4] iti shrUyate | 

tatra saMshayyate -- kiM jyotiHshabdaM cakShurviShayatamo.apahaM tejaH, kiM vA paraM brahmeti ? kiM tAvat prAptam? prasiddham eva tejo jyotiHshabdam iti | kutaH? jyotiHshabdasya rUDhatvAt | jyotishcaraNAbhidhAnAt ityatra hi prakaraNAjjyotiHshabdaH svArthaM parityajya brahmaNi vartate | na ceha tadvat kiMcit svArthaparityAge kAraNaM dR^ishyate | tathA ca nADIkhaNDo -- atha yatraitad asmAccharIrAd utkrAmatyathaitair eva rashmibhir Urdhvam Akramate [chA.u. 8.6.5] iti mumukShor AdityaprAptir abhihitA | tasmAt prasiddham eva tejo jyotiHshabdam iti | evaM prApte, brUmaH -- 

jyotir darshanAt || 

param eva brahma jyotiHshabdam | kasmAt? darshanAt | tasya hIha prakaraNe vaktavyatvenAnuvR^ittir dR^ishyate | ya AtmApahatapApmA [chA.u. 8.7.1] ityapahatapApmatvAdiguNakasyAtmanaH prakaraNAdAvanveShTavyatvena vijij~nAsitavyatvena ca pratij~nAnAt, etaM tv eva te bhUyo.anuvyAkhyAsyAmi [chA.u. 8.9.3] iti cAnusandhAnAt | asharIraM vAva santaM na priyApriye spR^ishataH iti cAsharIratAyai jyotiHsampatterasyAbhidhAnAt | brahmabhAvAccAnyatrAsharIratAnupapatteH | paraM jyotiH sa uttamaH puruShaH iti ca visheShaNAt | yat tUktaM mumukShorAdityaprAptirabhihiteti, nAsAvAtyantiko mokShaH, gatyutkrAntisambandhAt | na hyAtyantike mokShe gatyutkrAntI sta iti vakShyAmaH ||

12. arthAntaratvAdivyapadeshAdhikaraNam 

|| 1.3.41 ||

AkAsho vai nAma nAmarUpayor nirvahitA te yad antarA tad brahma tad amR^itaM sa AtmA [chA.u. 8.14.1] iti shrUyate | tatkim AkAshashabdaM paraM brahma, kiM vA prasiddham eva bhUtAkAsham iti vicAre -- bhUtaparigraho yuktaH | AkAshashabdasya tasmin rUDhatvAt | nAmarUpanirvahaNasya cAvakAshadAnadvAreNa tasmin yojayituM shakyatvAt | sraShTR^itvAd eshca spaShTasya brahmaliN^gasyAshravaNAd ityevaM prApte -- 

AkAsho.arthAntaratvAdivyapadeshAt ||

idam ucyate -- param eva brahma ihAkAshashabdaM bhavitum arhati | kasmAt? arthAntaratvAdivyapadeshAt | te yad antarA tad brahma iti hi nAmarUpAbhyAm arthAntarabhUtam AkAshaM vyapadishati | na ca brahmaNo.anyan nAmarUpAbhyAm arthAntaraM sambhavati, sarvasya vikArajAtasya nAmarUpAbhyAm eva vyAkR^itatvAt | nAmarUpayor api nirvahaNaM niraN^kushaM na brahmaNo.anyatra sambhavati, anena jIvenAtmanAnupravishya nAmarUpe vyAkaravANi iti brahmakartR^ikatvashravaNAt | 

nanu jIvasyApi pratyakShaM nAmarUpaviShayaM nirvoDhR^itvam asti | bADham asti | abhedaH tviha vivakShitaH | nAmarUpanirvahaNAbhidhAnAd eva ca sraShTR^itvAdi brahmaliN^gam abhihitaM bhavati | tad brahma tad amR^itaM sa AtmA iti ca brahmavAdasya liN^gAni | AkAshaH talliN^gAt [ve.sU. 1.1.22] ityasyaivAyaM prapaJNcaH ||41||

 -- o)0(o -- 

13. suShuptyutkrAntyadhikaraNam

|| 1.3.42 ||

vyapadeshAd ityanuvartate | bR^ihadAraNyake ShaShThe (?) prapAThake katama Atmeti yo.ayaM vij~nAnamayaH prANeShu hR^idyantarjyotiH puruShaH [bR^i.A.u. 4.3.7] ityupakramya bhUyAn AtmaviShayaH prapaJNcaH kR^itaH | tat kiM saMsArisvarUpamAtrAnvAkhyAnaparaM vAkyam, utAsaMsArisvarUpapratipAdanaparam iti viShayaH | kiM tAvat prAptam? saMsArisvarUpamAtraviShayam eveti | kutaH? upakramopasaMhArAbhyAm, upakrame yo.ayaM vij~nAnamayaH prANeShu iti shArIraliN^gAt | upasaMhAre ca sa vA eSha mahAn aja AtmA yo.ayaM vij~nAnamayaH prANeShu [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.22] iti tadaparityAgAt | madhye.api buddhAntAdyavasthopanyAsena tasyaiva prapaJNcanAd ityevaM prApte -- 

suShuptyutkrAntyor bhedena ||

brUmaH -- parameshvaropadeshaparam evedaM vAkyam, na shArIramAtrAnvAkhyAnaparam | kasmAt? suShuptAv utkrAntau ca shArIrAd bhedena parameshvarasya vyapadeshAt | suShuptau tAvat ayaM puruShaH prAj~nenAtmanA sampariShvakto na bAhyaM kiMcana veda nAntaram iti shArIrAd bhedena parameshvaraM vyapadishati | tatra puruShaH shArIraH syAt, tasya veditR^itvAt | 
bAhyAbhyantaravedanaprasaN^ge sati tatpratiShedhasambhavAt | prAj~naH parameshvaraH, sarvaj~natvalakShaNayA praj~nayA nityam aviyogAt | tathotkrAntAvapi ayaM shArIra AtmA prAj~nenAtmanAnvArUDha utsarjanyAti iti jIvAd bhedena parameshvaraM vyapadishati | tatrApi shArIro jIvaH syAt, sharIrasvAmitvAt | prAj~naH tu sa eva parameshvaraH |

tasmAt suShuptyutkrAntyor bhedena vyapadeshAt parameshvara evAtra vivakShita iti gamyate | yad uktam AdyantamadhyeShu shArIraliN^gAt tatparatvam asya vAkyasyeti | atra brUmaH -- upakrame tAvat yo.ayaM vij~nAnamayaH prANeShu iti na saMsArisvarUpaM vivakShitam | kiM tarhi, anUdya saMsArisvarUpaM pareNa brahmaNAsyaikatAM vivakShati | yataH dhyAyatIva lelAyatIva ityevam AdyuttaragranthapravR^ittiH saMsAridharmanirAkaraNaparA lakShyate | tathopasaMhAre.api yathopakramam evopasaMharati -- sa vA eSha mahAn aja AtmA yo.ayaM vij~nAnamayaH prANeShu [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.22] iti | yo.ayaM vij~nAnamayaH prANeShu saMsArI lakShyate, sa vA eSha mahAn aja AtmA parameshvara evAsmAbhiH pratipAdita ityarthaH | yaH tu madhye buddhAntAdyavasthopanyAsAt saMsArisvarUpavivakShAM manyate, sa prAcIm api dishaM prasthApitaH pratIcIm api dishaM pratiShTheta | yato na buddhAntAdyavasthopanyAsenAvasthAvattvaM saMsAritvaM vA vivakShati, kiM tarhi, avasthArahitatvam asaMsAritvaM ca | 

katham etad avagamyate? yat ata UrdhvaM vimokShAyaiva brUhi iti pade pade pR^icchati | yacca ananvAgataH tena bhavatyasaN^go hyayaM puruShaH iti pade pade prativakti | ananvAgataM puNyenAnanvAgataM pApena tIrNo hi tadA sarvAJNshokAn hR^idayasya bhavati iti ca | tasmAd asaMsArisvarUpapratipAdanaparam evaitadvAkyam ityavagantavyam ||42||

|| 1.3.43 ||

patyAdishabdebhyaH ||

itashcAsaMsArisvarUpapratipAdanaparam evaitadvAkyam ityavagantavyam | yad asmin vAkye patyAdayaH shabdA asaMsArisvarUpapratipAdanaparAH saMsArisvabhAvapratiShedhanAshca bhavanti -- sarvasya vashI sarvasyeshAnaH sarvasyAdhipatiH [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.22] ityevaMjAtIyakA asaMsArisvabhAvapratipAdanaparAH | sa na sAdhunA karmaNA bhUyAn no evAsAdhunA kanIyAn [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.22] ityevaMjAtIyakAH saMsArisvabhAvapratiShedhanAH | tasmAd asaMsArI parameshvara ihokta ityavagamyate ||43|| 

iti shrImatparamahaMsaparivrAjakAcAryasya shrIgovindabhagavatpUjyapAdashiShyasya shrImacchaMkarabhagavataH kR^itau shArIrakamImAMsAsUtrabhAShye 
prathamAdhyAyasya tR^itIyaH pAdaH
|| 1.3 ||

 -- o)0(o -- 
 
(1.4)
|| prathamAdhyAye caturthaH pAdaH || 

atra pradhAnaviShayatvena sandihyamAnAnAm avyaktAjAdipadAnAM cintanam ||
1. AnumAnikAdhikaraNam

|| 1.4.1 ||

brahmajij~nAsAyAM pratij~nAya brahmaNo lakShaNam uktam -- janmAdyasya yataH [ve.sU. 1.1.2] iti | tal lakShaNaM pradhAnasyApi samAnam ityAshaN^kya tad ashabdatvena nirAkR^itaM -- IkShater nAshabdaM [ve.sU. 1.1.5] iti | gatisAmAnyaM ca vedAntavAkyAnAM brahmakAraNavAdaM prati vidyate na pradhAnakAraNavAdaM pratIti prapaJNcitaM gatena granthena | idaM tvidAnIm avashiShTam AshaN^kyate -- yad uktaM pradhAnasyAshabdatvaM tad asiddham, kAsucicchAkhAsu pradhAnasamarpaNAbhAsAnAM shabdAnAM shrUyamANatvAt | ataH pradhAnasya kAraNatvaM vedasiddhaM eva mahadbhiH paramarShibhiH kapilaprabhR^itibhiH parigR^ihItam iti prasajyate | tad yAvat teShAM shabdAnAM anyaparatvaM na pratipAdyate tAvat sarvaj~naM brahma jagataH kAraNam iti pratipAditam apyAkulIbhavet | ataH teShAM anyaparatvaM darshayituM paraH sandarbhaH pravartate |

AnumAnikam apyekeShAm iti cen, na, 
sharIrarUpakavinyastagR^ihIter darshayati ca ||

AnumAnikam api anumAnanirUpitam api pradhAnam, ekeShAM shAkhinAM shabdavad upalabhyate | kAThake hi paThyate -- mahataH param avyaktam avyaktAt puruShaH paraH [ka.u. 1.3.11] iti | tatra ya eva yannAmAno yatkramAshca mahadavyaktapuruShAH smR^itiprasiddhAH, ta eveha pratyabhij~nAyante | tatrAvyaktam iti smR^itiprasiddham, shabdAdihInatvAcca na vyaktam avyaktam iti vyutpattisambhavAt, smR^itiprasiddhaM pradhAnam abhidhIyate | ataH tasya shabdavattvAd ashabdatvam anupapannam | tad eva ca jagataH kAraNaM shrutismR^itinyAyaprasiddhibhya iti cet, naitad evam -- na hyetat kAThakavAkyaM smR^itiprasiddhayor mahadavyaktayor astitvaparam | na hyatra yAdR^ishaM smR^itiprasiddhaM svatantraM kAraNaM triguNaM pradhAnam, tAdR^ishaM pratyabhij~nAyate | shabdamAtraM hyatrAvyaktam iti pratyabhij~nAyate | sa ca shabdo na vyaktam avyaktam iti yaugikatvAt anyasminn api sUkShme sudurlakShye ca prayujyate | na cAyaM kasmiMshcid rUDhaH | yA tu pradhAnavAdinAM rUDhiH, sA teShAm eva pAribhAShikI satI na vedArthanirUpaNe kAraNabhAvaM pratipadyate | na ca kramamAtrasAmAnyAt samAnArthapratipattir bhavati, asati tadrUpapratyabhij~nAne | na hyashcasthAne gAM pashyann ashvo.ayam ityamUDho.adhyavasyati | prakaraNanirUpaNAyAM cAtra na paraparikalpitaM pradhAnaM pratIyate, sharIrarUpakavinyastagR^ihIteH sharIraM hyatra ratharUpakavinyastam avyaktashabdena parigR^ihyate | kutaH? prakaraNAt parisheShAcca | 
tathA hyanantarAtIto grantha AtmasharIrAdInAM rathirathAdirUpakakptiM darshayati -- 

AtmAnaM rathinaM viddhi sharIraM ratham eva tu | 
buddhiM tu sArathiM viddhi manaH pragraham eva ca || 
indriyANi hayAnyAhur viShayAMH teShu gocarAn |
AtmendriyamanoyuktaM bhoktetyAhur manIShiNaH || [ka.u. 1.3.34] iti | 

taishcendriyAdibhir asaMyataiH saMsAram adhigacchati, saMyataiH tu adhvanaH pAraM tad viShNoH paramaM padam Apnoti -- iti darshayitvA, kiM tad adhvanaH pAraM viShNoH paramaM padam ityasyAm AkAN^kShAyAm, tebhya eva prakR^itebhyaH indriyAdibhyaH paratvena paramAtmAnam adhvanaH pAraM tad viShNoH paramaM padaM darshayati -- 

indriyebhyaH parA hyarthA arthebhyashca paraM manaH |
manasaH tu parA buddhir buddher AtmA mahAn paraH ||
mahataH param avyaktam avyaktAt puruShaH paraH |
puruShAn na paraM kiMcit sA kAShThA sA parA gatiH || [ka.u. 1.3.1011] iti |

tatra ya evendriyAdayaH pUrvasyAM ratharUpakakalpanAyAm ashvAdibhAvena prakR^itAH, ta eveha parigR^ihyante, prakR^itahAnAprakR^itaprakriyAparihArAya | tatra indriyamanobuddhayaH tAvat pUrvatra iha ca samAnashabdA eva | arthAH tu ye shabdAdayo viShayA indriyahayagocaratvena nirdiShTaH, teShAM cendriyebhyaH paratvam, indriyANAM ca grahatvaM viShayANAm atigrahatvam iti shrutiprasiddhaH | viShayebhyashca manasaH paratvam, manomUlatvAd viShayendriyavyavahArasya | manasaH tu parA buddhiH -- buddhiM hyAruhya bhogyajAtaM bhoktAram upasarpati | buddhir AtmA mahAn paraH -- yaH, sa AtmAnaM rathinaM viddhi [ka.u. 1.3.3] iti rathitvenopakShiptaH | kutaH? AtmashabdAt, bhoktushca bhogopakaraNAt paratvopapatteH | mahattvaM cAsya svAmitvAd upapannam | athavA -- 

mano mahAn matir brahmA pUr buddhiH khyAtir IshvaraH | 
praj~nA saMviccitishcaiva smR^itishca paripaThyate || iti smR^iteH, 

yo brahmANaM vidadhAti pUrvaM yo vai vedAMshca prahiNoti tasmai [shve.u. 6.18] iti ca shruteH | yA prathamajasya hiraNyagarbhasya buddhiH, sA sarvAsAM buddhInAM paramA pratiShThA | seha mahAn Atmetyucyate | sA ca pUrvatra buddhigrahaNenaiva gR^ihItA satI hi rug ihopadishyate, tasyA apyasmadIyAbhyo buddhibhyaH paratvopapatteH | etasmiMH tu pakShe paramAtmaviShayeNaiva pareNa puruShagrahaNena rathina Atmano grahaNaM draShTavyam, paramArthataH tu paramAtmavij~nAnAtmanor bhedAbhAvAt | tad evaM sharIram evaikaM parishiShyate | teShvitarANIndriyAdIni prakR^itAnyeva paramapadadidarshayiShayA samanukrAman parishiShyamANenehAntyenAvyaktashabdena parishiShyamANaM prakR^itaM sharIraM darshayatIti gamyate | sharIrendriyamanobuddhiviShayavedanAsaMyuktasya hyavidyAvato bhoktuH sharIrAdInAM rathAdirUpakakalpanayA saMsAramokShagatinirUpaNena pratyagAtmabrahmAvagatiH iha vivakShitA | tathA ca 

eSha sarveShu bhUteShu gUDho.atmA na prakAshate | 
dR^ishyate tu agryayA buddhyA sUkShmayA sUkShmadarshibhiH || [ka.u. 1.3.12] iti |

vaiShNavasya paramapadasya duravagamatvam uktvA tadavagamArthaM yogaM darshayati -- 

yacched vAN^manasI prAj~naH tad yacchejj~nAna Atmani | 
j~nAnam Atmani mahati niyacchet tad yacchecchAnta Atmani || [ka.u. 1.3.13] iti | 

etad uktaM bhavati -- vAcaM manasi saMyacchet vAgAdibAhyendriyavyApAram utsR^ijya manomAtreNAvatiShTheta | mano.api viShayavikalpAbhimukhaM vikalpadoShadarshanena j~nAnashabdoditAyAM buddhAvadhyavasAyasvabhAvAyAM dhArayet | tAm api buddhiM mahatyAtmani bhoktari agryAyAM vA buddhau sUkShmatApAdanena niyacchet | mahAntaM tvatmAnaM shAnta Atmani prakaraNavati parasmin puruShe parasyAM kAShThAyAM pratiShThApayed iti ca | tad evaM pUrvAparAlocanAyAM nAstyatra paraparikalpitasya pradhAnasyAvakAshaH ||1||

|| 1.4.2 ||

uktam etat -- prakaraNaparisheShAbhyAM sharIram avyaktashabdam, na pradhAnam iti | idam idAnIm AshaN^kyate -- katham avyaktashabdArhatvaM sharIrasya, yAvatA sthUlatvAt spaShTataram idaM sharIraM vyaktashabdArham, aspaShTavacanaH tu avyaktashabda iti | ata uttaram ucyate -- 

sUkShmaM tu tadarhatvAt ||

sUkShmaM tu iha kAraNAtmanA sharIraM vivakShyate, sUkShmasyAvyaktashabdArhatvAt | yadyapi sthUlam idaM sharIraM na svayam avyaktashabdam arhati, tathApi tasya tvarambhakaM bhUtasUkShmam avyaktashabdam arhati | prakR^itishabdashca vikAre dR^iShTaH -- yathA gobhiH shrINIta matsaram [R^i.ve. 9.46.4] iti shrutishca | tad dhIdaM tarhyavyAkR^itam AsIt [bR^i.A.u. 1.4.7] itIdam eva vyAkR^itanAmarUpavibhinnaM jagatprAgavasthAyAM parityaktavyAkR^itanAmarUpaM bIjashaktyavastham avyaktashabdayogyaM darshayati ||2||

|| 1.4.3 ||

tadadhInatvAd arthavat ||

atrAha -- yadi jagad idam anabhivyaktanAmarUpaM bIjAtmakaM prAgavastham avyaktashabdArham abhyupagamyeta, tad AtmanA ca sharIrasyApyavyaktashabdArhatvaM pratij~nAyeta, sa eva tarhi pradhAnakAraNavAda evaM satyApadyeta | asyaiva jagataH prAgavasthAyAH pradhAnatvenAbhyupagamAd iti | 

atrocyate -- yadi vayaM svatantrAM kAMcit prAgavasthAM jagataH kAraNatvena abhyupagacchema, prasaJNjayema tadA pradhAnakAraNavAdam | parameshvarAdhInA tviyam asmAbhiH prAgavasthA jagato.abhyupagamyate, na svatantrA | sA cAvashyAbhyupagantavyA | arthavatI hi sA | na hi tayA vinA parameshvarasya sraShTR^itvaM sidhyati, shaktirahitasya tasya pravR^ittyanupapatteH | muktAnAM ca punar anutpattiH | kutaH? vidyayA tasyA bIjashakter dAhAt | avidyAtmikA hi sA bIjashaktir avyaktashabdanirdeshyA parameshvarAshrayA mAyAmayI mahAsuShuptiH, yasyAM svarUpapratibodharahitAH sherate saMsAriNo jIvAH | tad etad avyaktaM kvacid AkAshashabdanirdiShTam -- etasmin nu khalvakShare gArgyAkAsha otashca protashca [bR^i.A.u. 3.8.11] iti shruteH | kvacid akSharashabdoditam -- akSharAt parataH paraH iti shruteH | kvacin mAyeti sUcitam -- mAyAM tu prakR^itiM vidyAn mAyinaM tu maheshvaram [shve.u. 4.10] iti mantravarNAt | avyaktA hi sA mAyA, tattvAnyatvanirUpaNasyAshakyatvAt | tad idaM mahataH param avyaktam ityuktam -- avyaktaprabhavatvAn mahataH, yadA hairaNyagarbhI buddhir mahAn | yadA tu jIvo mahAn | tadApyavyaktAdhInatvAjjIvabhAvasya -- mahataH param avyaktam ityuktam | avidyA hyavyaktam | avidyAvattvenaiva jIvasya sarvaH saMvyavahAraH saMtato vartate | tacca avyaktagataM mahataH paratvam abhedopacArAt tadvikAre sharIre parikalpyate | satyapi sharIravad indriyAdInAM tadvikAratvAvisheShe sharIrasyaivAbhedopacArAd avyaktashabdena grahaNam, indriyAdInAM svashabdair eva gR^ihItatvAt, parishiShTatvAcca sharIrasya || 

anye tu varNayanti -- dvividhaM hi sharIraM sthUlaM sUkShmaM ca | sthUlam, yad idam upalabhyate | sUkShmam, yad uttaratra vakShyate -- tadantarapratipattau raMhati sampariShvaktaH prashnanirUpaNAbhyAm iti | taccobhayam api sharIram avisheShAt pUrvatra rathatvena saN^kIrtitam | iha tu sUkShmam avyaktashabdena parigR^ihyate, sUkShmasyAvyaktashabdArhatvAt | tadadhInatvAcca bandhamokShavyavahArasya jIvAt tasya paratvam | yathArthAdhInatvAd indriyavyApArasyendriyebhyaH paratvam arthAnAm iti | taiH tv etad vaktavyam --  avisheSheNa sharIradvayasya pUrvatra rathatvena saN^kIrtitatvAt, samAnayoH prakR^itatvaparishiShTatvayoH, kathaM sUkShmam eva sharIram iha gR^ihyate, na punaH sthUlam apIti | AmnAtasyArthaM pratipattuM prabhavAmaH, nAmnAtaM paryanuyoktum, AmnAtaM cAvyaktapadaM sUkShmam eva pratipAdayituM shaknoti, netarat, vyaktatvAt tasyeti cet, na | ekavAkyatAdhInatvAd arthaM pratipatteH | na hIme pUrvottare AmnAte ekavAkyatAm anApadya kaMcid arthaM pratipAdayataH | prakR^itahAnAprakR^itaprakriyAprasaN^gAt | na cAkAN^kShAm antareNaikavAkyatApratipattir asti | tatrAvishiShTAyAM sharIradvayasya grAhyatvAkAN^kShAyAM yathAkAN^kShaM sambandhe.anabhyupagamyamAne ekavAkyataiva bAdhitA bhavati, kuta AmnAtasyArthasya pratipattiH? na caivaM mantavyam -- duHshodhatvAt sUkShmasyaiva sharIrasyeha grahaNam, sthUlasya tu dR^iShTabIbhatsatayA sushodhatvAd agrahaNam iti | yato naiveha shodhanaM kasyacid vivakShyate | na hyatra shodhanavidhAyi kiMcid AkhyAtam asti | anantaranirdiShTatvAt tu kiM tad viShNoH paramaM padam itIdam iha vivakShyate | tathA hIdam asmAt param idam asmAt param ityuktvA, puruShAn na paraM kiMcit [ka.u. 1.3.11] ityAha | sarvathApi tvanumAnikanirAkaraNopapatteH, tathA nAmAstu | na naH kiMcicchidyate ||3||

|| 1.4.4 || 

j~neyatvAvacanAcca ||

j~neyatvena ca sAN^khyaiH pradhAnaM smaryate, guNapuruShAntaraj~nAnAt kaivalyam iti vadadbhiH -- na hi guNasvarUpam aj~nAtvA guNebhyaH puruShasyAntaraM shakyaM j~nAtum iti | kvacicca vibhUtivisheShaprAptaye pradhAnaM j~neyam iti smaranti | na cedam ihAvyaktaM j~neyatvenocyate | padamAtraM hyavyaktashabdaH, nehAvyaktaM j~nAtavyam upAsitavyaM ceti vAkyam asti | na cAnupadiShTaM padArthaj~nAnaM puruShArtham iti shakyaM pratipattum | tasmAd api nAvyaktashabdena pradhAnam abhidhIyate | asmAkaM tu ratharUpakakptasharIrAdyanusaraNena viShNor eva paramaM padaM darshayitum ayam upanyAsa ityanavadyam ||4||

|| 1.4.5 || 

atrAha sAN^khyaH -- j~neyatvAvacanAt, ityasiddham | katham? shrUyate hyuttaratrAvyaktashabdoditasya pradhAnasya j~neyatvavacanam -- 

ashabdam asparsham arUpam avyayaM 
tathArasaM nityam agandhavacca yat | 
anAdyanantaM mahataH paraM dhruvaM 
nicAyya taM mR^ityumukhAt pramucyate || [ka.u. 1.3.15] iti | 

atra hi yAdR^ishaM shabdAdihInaM pradhAnaM mahataH paraM smR^itau nirUpitam, tAdR^isham eva nicAyyatvena nirdiShTam, tasmAt pradhAnam evedam | tad eva cAvyaktashabdanirdiShTam iti | atra brUmaH -- 

vadatIti cen na prAj~no hi prakaraNAt ||

neha pradhAnaM nicAyyatvena nirdiShTam | prAj~no hIha paramAtmA nicAyyatvena nirdiShTa iti gamyate | kutaH? prakaraNAt | prAj~nasya hi prakaraNaM vitataM vartate -- puruShAn na paraM kiMcit sA kAShThA sA parA gatiH [ka.u. 1.3.11] ityAdinirdeshAt, eSha sarveShu bhUteShu guDho.atmA na prakAshate [ka.u. 1.3.12] iti ca durj~nAnatvavacanena tasyaiva j~neyatvAkAN^kShaNAt, yacched vAN^manasI prAj~naH [ka.u. 1.3.13] iti ca tajj~nAnAyaiva vAgAdisaMyamasya vihitatvAt, mR^ityumukhapramokShaNaphalatvAcca | na hi pradhAnamAtraM nicAyya mR^ityumukhAt pramucyata iti sAN^khyaiH iShyate | cetanAtmavij~nAnAd dhi mR^ityumukhAt pramucyata iti teShAm abhyupagamaH | sarveShu vedAnteShu prAj~nasyaivAtmano.ashabdAdidharmatvam abhilapyate | tasmAn na pradhAnasyAtra j~neyatvam avyaktashabdanirdiShTatvaM vA ||5||

|| 1.4.6 ||

trayANAm eva caivam upanyAsaH prashnashca ||

itashca na pradhAnasyAvyaktashabdavAcyatvaM j~neyatvaM vA | yasmAt trayANAm eva padArthAnAm agnijIvaparamAtmanAm asmin granthe kaThavallIShu varapradAnasAmarthyAd vaktavyatayopanyAso dR^ishyate | tadviShaya eva ca prashnaH | nAto.anyasya prashna upanyAso vAsti | tatra tAvat -- 

sa tvam agniM svagryam adhyeShi mR^ityo 
prabrUhi taM shraddadhAnAya mahyam [ka.u. 1.1.13] ityagniviShayaH prashnaH | 

yeyaM prete vicikitsA manuShye
stItyeke nAyam astIti caike |
etad vidyAm anushiShTaH tvayA.ahaM
varANAm eSha varaH tR^itIyaH || [ka.u. 1.1.13] iti jIvaviShayaH prashnaH | 

anyatra dharmAd anyatrAdharmAd
anyatrAsmAt kR^itAkR^itAt |
anyatra bhUtAcca bhavyAcca
yat tat pashyasi tad vada || [ka.u. 1.2.14] iti paramAtmaviShayaH | 

prativacanam api -- 

lokAdim agniM tam uvAca tasmai 
yA iShTakA yAvatIr vA yathA vA || [ka.u. 1.1.15] ityagniviShayam | 

hanta ta idaM pravakShyAmi guhyaM brahma sanAtanam | 
yathA ca maraNaM prApya AtmA bhavati gautama ||
yonim anye prapadyante sharIratvAya dehinaH | 
sthANum anye.anusaMyanti yathAkarma yathAshrutam || [ka.u. 2.2.67] iti vyavahitaM jIvaviShayam | 

na jAyate mriyate vA vipashcit [ka.u. 1.2.18] ityAdi bahuprapaJNcaM paramAtmaviShayam | naivaM pradhAnaviShayaH prashno.asti | apR^iShTatvAccAnupanyasanIyatvaM tasyeti || 

atrAha -- yo.ayam AtmaviShayaH prashnaH -- yeyaM prete vicikitsA manuShye.asti [ka.u. 1.1.13] iti, kiM sa evAyam anyatra dharmAd anyatrAdharmAt [ka.u. 1.2.14] iti punar anukR^iShyate, kiM vA tato.anyo.ayam apUrvaH prashna utthApyata iti | kiM cAtaH? sa evAyaM prashnaH punar anukR^iShyata iti yadyucyeta, tadA dvayor AtmaviShayayoH prashnayor ekatApatter agniviShaya AtmaviShayashca dvAv eva prashnAvityato na vaktavyaM trayANAM prashnopanyAsAviti | athAnyo.ayam apUrvaH prashna utthApyata ityucyeta, tato yathaiva varapradAnavyatirekeNa prashnakalpanAyAm adoShaH | evaM prashnavyatirekeNApi pradhAnopanyAsakalpanAyAm adoShaH syAd iti || 

atrocyate -- naivaM vayam iha varapradAnavyatirekeNa prashnaM kaMcit kalpayAmaH, vAkyopakramasAmarthyAt | varapradAnopakramA hi mR^ityunaciketaHsaMvAdarUpA vAkyapravR^ittiH A samApteH kaThavallInAM lakShyate | mR^ityuH kila naciketase pitrA prahitAya trIn varAn pradadau | naciketAH kila teShAM prathamena vareNa pituH saumanasyaM vavre, dvitIyenAgnividyAm, tR^itIyenAtmavidyAm -- yeyaM prete iti varANAm eSha varaH tR^itIyaH [ka.u. 1.1.20] iti liN^gAt | tatra yadi anyatra dharmAt ityanyo.ayam apUrvaH prashna utthApyeta, tato varapradAnavyatirekeNApi prashnakalpanAd vAkyaM bAdhyeta | 

nanu praShTavyabhedAd apUrvo.ayaM prashno bhavitum arhati | apUrvo hi prashno jIvaviShayaH, yeyaM prete vicikitsA manuShye.asti nAstIti vicikitsAbhidhAnAt | jIvashca dharmAdigocaratvAt na anyatra dharmAt iti prashnam arhati | prAj~naH tu dharmAdyatItatvAt anyatra dharmAt iti prashnam arhati | prashnacchAyA ca na samAnA lakShyate, pUrvasyAstitvanAstitvaviShayatvAt, uttarasya dharmAdyatItavastuviShayatvAcca | tasmAt pratyabhij~nAnAbhAvAt prashnabhedaH | na pUrvasyaivottaratrAnukarShaNam iti cet, na | jIvaprAj~nayor ekatvAbhyupagamAt | bhavet praShTavyabhedAt prashnabhedo yadyanyo jIvaH prAj~nAt syAt | na tu anyatvam asti, tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7] ityAdi shrutyantarebhyaH | iha ca anyatra dharmAt ityasya prashnasya prativacanam na jAyate mriyate vA vipashcit [ka.u. 1.2.18] iti janmamaraNapratiShedhena pratipAdyamAnaM shArIraparameshvarayor abhedaM darshayati | sati hi prasaN^ge pratiShedho bhAgI bhavati | prasaN^gashca janmamaraNayoH sharIrasaMsparshAcchArIrasya bhavati, na parameshvarasya | tathA -- 

svapnAntaM jAgaritAntaM cobhau yenAnupashyati | 
mahAntaM vibhum AtmAnaM matvA dhIro na shocati || [ka.u. 2.1.4]

iti svapnajAgaritadR^isho jIvasyaiva mahattvavibhutvavisheShaNasya mananena shokavicchedaM darshayan na prAj~nAd anyo jIva iti darshayati | prAj~navij~nAnAd dhi shokaviccheda iti vedAntasiddhAntaH | tathAgre -- 

yad eveha tad amutra yad amutra tad anviha | 
mR^ityoH sa mR^ityum Apnoti ya iha nAneva pashyati || [ka.u. 2.1.10]

iti jIvaprAj~nabhedadR^iShTim apavadati | tathA jIvaviShayasyAstitvanAstitvaprashnasyAnantaram anyaM varaM naciketo vR^iNIShva [ka.u. 1.1.19] ityArabhya, mR^ityunA taiH taiH kAmaiH pralobhyamAno.api naciketA yadA na cacAla, tadainaM mR^ityur abhyudayaniHshreyasavibhAgapradarshanena vidyAvidyAvibhAgapradarshanena ca vidyAbhIpsinaM naciketasaM manye na tvA kAmA bahavo.alolupanta [ka.u. 1.2.4] iti prashasya, prashnam api tadIyaM prashaMsan yad uvAca -- 

taM durdarshaM gUDham anupraviShTaM 
guhAhitaM gahvareShThaM purANam | 
adhyAtmayogAdhigamena devaM 
matvA dhIro harShashokau jahAti || [ka.u. 1.2.12] iti |

tenApi jIvaprAj~nayor abheda eveha vivakShita iti gamyate | yat prashnanimittAM ca prashaMsAM mahatIM mR^ityoH pratyapadyata naciketAH, yadi taM vihAya prashaMsAnantaram anyam eva prashnam upakShipet, asthAna eva sA sarvA prashaMsA prasAritA syAt | tasmAt yeyaM prete ityasyaiva prashnasyaitad anukarShaNam anyatra dharmAt iti | yat tu prashnacchAyAvailakShaNyam uktam, tad adUShaNam, tadIyasyaiva visheShasya punaH pR^icchyamAnatvAt | pUrvatra hi dehAdivyatiriktasyAtmano.astitvaM pR^iShTam, uttaratra tu tasyaivAsaMsAritvaM pR^icchayata iti | yAvad dhyavidyA na nivartate, tAvad dharmAdigocaratvaM jIvasya jIvatvaM ca na nivartate, tannivR^ittau tu prAj~na eva tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7] iti shrutyA pratyAyyate | 

na cAvidyAvattve tadapagame ca vastunaH kashcid visheSho.asti | yathA kashcit santamase patitAM kAMcid rajjum ahiM manyamAno bhIto vepamAnaH palAyate, taM cAparo brUyAt mA bhaiShIH nAyam ahiH rajjur eveti, sa ca tad upashrutyAhikR^itaM bhayam utsR^ijed vepathuM palAyanaM ca, na tu ahibuddhikAle tadapagamakAle ca vastunaH kashcid visheShaH syAt -- tathaivaitad api draShTavyam | 

tatashca na jAyate mriyate vA [ka.u. 1.2.18] ityevamAdyapi bhavatyastitvanAstitvaprashnasya prativacanam | sUtraM tu avidyAkalpitajIvaprAj~nabhedApekShayA yojayitavyam -- ekatve.api hyAtmaviShayasya prashnasya prAyaNAvasthAyAM dehavyatiriktAstitvamAtravicikitsanAt kartR^itvAdisaMsArasvabhAvAnapohanAcca pUrvasya paryAyasya jIvaviShayatvam utprekShyate, uttarasya tu dharmAdyatyayasaN^kIrtanAt prAj~naviShayatvam iti | tatashca yuktA agnijIvaparamAtmakalpanA | pradhAnakalpanAyAM tu na varapradAnaM na prashno na prativacanam iti vaiShamyam ||6||

|| 1.4.7 ||

mahadvacca ||

yathA mahacchabdaH sAN^khyaiH sattAmAtre.api prathamaje prayuktaH, na tam eva vaidike.api prayoge.abhidhatte, buddher AtmA mahAn paraH [ka.u. 1.3.10], mahAntaM vibhum AtmAnam [ka.u. 1.2.22], vedAham etaM puruShaM mahAntam [shve.u. 3.8] ityevamAdAvatmashabdaprayogAdibhyo hetubhyaH | tathAvyaktashabdo.api na vaidike prayoge pradhAnam abhidhAtum arhati | atashca nAstyAnumAnikasya shabdavattvam ||7||

 --o)0(o--
2. camasAdhikaraNam

|| 1.4.8 ||

punar api pradhAnavAdI ashabdatvaM pradhAnasyAsiddham ityAha | kasmAt? mantravarNAt -- 

ajAm ekAM lohitashuklakR^iShNAM
bahvIH prajAH sR^ijamAnAM sarUpAH |
ajo hyeko juShamANo.anushete
jahAtyenAM bhuktabhogAm ajo.anyaH || [shve.u. 4.5] iti |

atra hi mantre lohitashuklakR^iShNashabdaiH rajaHsattvatamAMsyabhidhIyante | lohitaM rajaH, raJNjanAtmakatvAt, shuklaM sattvam, prakAshAtmakatvAt | kR^iShNaM tamaH, AvaraNAtmakatvAt | teShAM sAmyAvasthA avayavadharmair vyapadishyate -- lohitashuklakR^iShNeti | na jAyata iti ca ajA syAt, mUlaprakR^itir avikR^itiH ityabhyupagamAt | 

nanvajAshabdashchAgyAM rUDhaH | bADham | sA tu rUDhiH iha nAshrayituM shakyA, vidyAprakaraNAt | sA ca bahvIH prajAH traiguNyAnvitA janayati | tAM prakR^itim aja ekaH puruSho juShamANaH prIyamANaH sevamAno vA anushetetAm evAvidyayA Atmatvenopagamya sukhI duHkhI mUDho.aham ityavivekitayA saMsarati | anyaH punar ajaH puruSha utpannavivekaj~nAno virakto jahAtyenAM prakR^itiM bhuktabhogAM kR^itabhogApavargAM parityajati -- mucyata ityarthaH | tasmAcchrutimUlaiva pradhAnAdikalpanA kApilAnAm ityevaM prApte -- 

camasavad avisheShAt ||

brUmaH -- nAnena mantreNa shrutimattvaM sAN^khyavAd asya shakyam Ashrayitum | na hyayaM mantraH svAtantryeNa kaJNcid api vAdaM samarthayitum utsahate, sarvatrApi yayA kayAcit kalpanayA ajAtvAdisampAdanopapatteH, sAN^khyavAda evehAbhipreta iti visheShAvadhAraNakAraNAbhAvAt | camasavat -- yathA hi arvAgbilashcamasa UrdhvabudhnaH [bR^i.A.u. 2.2.3] ityasmin mantre svAtantryeNAyaM nAmAsau camaso.abhipreta iti na shakyate niyantum, sarvatrApi yathAkathaMcid arvAgbilatvAdikalpanopapatteH, evam ihApyavisheSho.ajAm ekAm ityasya mantrasya | nAsmin mantre pradhAnam evAjAbhipreteti shakyate niyantum ||8|| 

|| 1.4.9 ||

tatra tu idaM tacchira eSha hyarvAgbilashcamasa UrdhvabuddhnaH [bR^i.A.u. 2.2.3] iti vAkyasheShAccamasavisheShapratipattir bhavati | iha punaH keyam ajA pratipattavyetyatra brUmaH -- 

jyotirUpakramAtu tathA hyadhIyata eke ||

parameshvarAd utpannA jyotiHpramukhA tejo.abannalakShaNA caturvidhasya bhUtagrAmasya prakR^itibhUteyam ajA pratipattavyA | tushabdo.avadhAraNArthaH -- bhUtatrayalakShaNaiveyam ajA vij~neyA, na guNatrayalakShaNA | kasmAt? tathA hyeke shAkhinaH tejo.abannAnAM parameshvarAd utpattim AmnAya teShAm eva rohitAdirUpatAm Amananti -- yad agne rohitaM rUpaM tejasaH tadrUpaM yacchuklaM tad apAM yat kR^iShNaM tad annasya [chA.u. 6.4.1] iti | tAnyeveha tejo.abannAni pratyabhij~nAyante, rohitAdishabdasAmAnyAt, rohitAdInAM ca shabdAnAM rUpavisheSheShu mukhyatvAd bhAktatvAcca guNaviShayatvasya | asandigdhena ca sandigdhasya nigamanaM nyAyyaM manyante | tathehApi brahmavAdino vadanti kiM kAraNaM brahma [shve.u. 1.1] ityupakramya -- te dhyAnayogAnugatA apashyan devAtmashaktiM svaguNair nigUDhAm [shve.u. 1.3] iti pArameshvaryAH shakteH samastajagadvidhAyinyA vAkyopakrame.avagamAt, vAkyasheShe.api mAyAM tu prakR^itiM vidyAn mAyinaM tu maheshvaram [shve.u. 4.10] iti, yo yoniM yonim adhitiShThatyekaH [shve.u. 4.11] iti ca tasyA evAvagamAn na svatantrA kAcit prakR^itiH pradhAnaM nAmAjAmantreNAmnAyata iti shakyate vaktum | prakaraNAt tu saiva daivI shaktir avyAkR^itanAmarUpA nAmarUpayoH prAgavasthA anenApi mantreNAmnAyata ityucyate | tasyAshca svavikAraviShayeNa trairUpyeNa trairUpyam uktam ||9|| 

|| 1.4.10 ||

kathaM punaH tejo.abannAtmanA trairUpyeNa trirUpA ajA pratipattuM shakyate, yAvatA na tAvat tejo.abanneShvajAkR^itir asti, na ca tejo.abannAnAM jAtishravaNAd ajAtinimitto.apyajAshabdaH sambhavatIti | ata uttaraM paThati -- 

kalpanopadeshAcca madhvAdivad avirodhaH ||

nAyam ajAkR^itinimitto.ajAshabdaH | nApi yaugikaH | kiM tarhi, kalpanopadesho.ayam -- ajArUpakakptiH tejo.abannalakShaNAyAshcarAcarayoner upadishyate | yathA hi loke yadR^icchayA kAcid ajA rohitashuklakR^iShNavarNA syAd bahubarkarA sarUpabarkarA ca, tAM ca kashcid ajo juShamANo.anushayIta, kashciccainAM bhuktabhogAM jahyAt -- evam iyam api tejo.abannalakShaNA bhUtaprakR^itiH traivarNA bahu sarUpaM carAcaralakShaNaM vikArajAtaM janayati, aviduShA ca kShetraj~nenopabhujyate, viduShA ca parityajyata iti | na cedam AshaN^kitavyam -- ekaH kShetraj~no.anushete anyo jahAtItyataH kShetraj~nabhedaH pAramArthikaH pareShAm iShTaH prApnotIti | na hIyaM kShetraj~nabhedapratipipAdayiShA | kintu bandhamokShavyavasthApratipipAdayiShaivaiShA | prasiddhaM tu bhedam anUdya bandhamokShavyavasthA pratipAdyate | bhedaH tUpAdhinimitto mithyAj~nAnakalpitaH | na pAramArthikaH, 

eko devaH sarvabhUteShu gUDhaH 
sarvavyApI sarvabhUtAntarAtmA [shve.u. 6.11] ityAdi shrutibhyaH | 

madhvAdivat -- yathA AdityasyAmadhuno madhutvam [], vAcashcAdhenor dhenutvam [], dyulokAdInAM cAnagnInAm agnitvam [bR^i.A.u. 8.2.9]  -- ityevaMjAtIyakaM kalpyate, evam idam anajAyA ajAtvaM kalpyata ityarthaH | tasmAd avirodhaH tejo.abanneShvajAshabdaprayogasya ||10||

 --o)0(o--
3. saN^khyopasaN^grahAdhikaraNam

|| 1.4.11 ||

evaM parihR^ite.apyajAmantre punar apyanyasmAn mantrAt sAN^khyaH pratyavatiShThate -- 

yasmin paJNca paJNcajanA AkAshashca pratiShThitaH |
tam eva manya AtmAnaM vidvAn brahmAmR^ito.amR^itam || [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.17] iti |

asmin mantre paJNca paJNcajanA iti paJNcasaMkhyAviShayA aparA paJNcasaMkhyA shrUyate, paJNcashabdadvayadarshanAt | ta ete paJNca paJNcakAH paJNcaviMshatiH sampadyante | tayA ca paJNcaviMshatisaMkhyayA yAvantaH saMkhyeyA AkAN^kShyante, tAvantyeva ca tattvAni sAN^khyaiH saMkhyAyante -- 

mUlaprakR^itir avikR^itir mahadAdyAH prakR^itivikR^itayaH sapta | 
ShoDashakashca vikAro na prakR^itir na vikR^itiH puruShaH || [sAM.kA. 3] iti | 

tayA shrutiprasiddhayA paJNcaviMshatisaMkhyayA teShAM smR^itiprasiddhAnAM paJNcaviMshateH tattvAnAm upasaMgrahAt prAptaM punaH shrutimattvam eva pradhAnAdInAm |

na saN^khyopasaN^grahAd api nAnAbhAvAd atirekAcca ||

tato brUmaH -- na saMkhyopasaMgrahAd api pradhAnAdInAM shrutimattvaM pratyAshA kartavyA | kasmAt? nAnAbhAvAt | nAnA hyetAni paJNcaviMshatiH tattvAni | naiShAM paJNcashaH paJNcashaH sAdhAraNo dharmo.asti, yena paJNcaviMshater antarAle parAH paJNca paJNca saMkhyA nivisheran | na hyekanibandhanam antareNa nAnAbhUteShu dvitvAd ikAH saMkhyA nivishante | 

athocyeta -- paJNcaviMshatisaMkhyaiveyam avayavadvAreNa lakShyate, yathA paJNca sapta ca varShANi na vavarSha shatakratuH iti dvAdashavArShikIm anAvR^iShTiM kathayanti, tadvad iti | tad api nopapadyate | ayam evAsmin pakShe doShaH, yal lakShaNAshrayaNIyA syAt | parashcAtra paJNcashabdo janashabdena samastaH paJNcajanA iti, bhAShikasvareNaikapadatvanishcayAt | prayogAntare ca paJNcAnAM tvA paJNcajanAnAm [tai.A. 1.6.2.2] ityaikapadyaikasvaryaikavibhaktikatvAvagamAt | samastatvAcca na vIpsA paJNca paJNca iti | tena na paJNcakadvayagrahaNaM paJNca paJNceti | na ca paJNcasaMkhyAyA ekasyAH paJNcasaMkhyayA parayA visheShaNam paJNca paJNcakAH iti, upasarjanasya visheShaNenAsaMyogAt |

nanvapannapaJNcasaMkhyAkA janA eva punaH paJNcasaMkhyayA visheShyamANAH paJNcaviMshatiH pratyeShyante, yathA paJNca paJNcapUlya iti paJNcaviMshatiH pUlAH pratIyante, tadvat | neti brUmaH | yuktaM yat paJNcapUlIshabdasya samAhArAbhiprAyatvAt katIti satyAM bhedAkAN^kShAyAM paJNca paJNcapUlya iti visheShaNam | iha tu paJNca janA ityAdita eva bhedopAdAnAt katItyasatyAM bhedAkAN^kShAyAM na paJNca paJNcajanA iti visheShaNaM bhavet | bhavad apIdaM visheShaNaM paJNcasaMkhyAyA eva bhavet | tatra cokto doShaH | tasmAt paJNca paJNcajanA iti na paJNcaviMshatitattvAbhiprAyam | atirekAcca na paJNcaviMshatitattvAbhiprAyam | atireko hi bhavatyAtmAkAshAbhyAM paJNcaviMshatisaMkhyAyAH | AtmA tAvad iha pratiShThAM pratyAdhAratvena nirdiShTaH, yasmin iti saptamIsUcitasya tam eva manya AtmAnam ityAtmatvenAnukarShaNAt | AtmA ca cetanaH puruShaH | sa ca paJNcaviMshatAvantargata eveti na tasyaivAdhAratvam AdheyatvaM ca yujyeta | arthAntaraparigrahe vA tattvasaMkhyAtirekaH siddhAntaviruddhaH prasajyeta | tathA AkAshashca pratiShThitaH ityAkAshasyApi paJNcaviMshatAvantargatasya na pR^ithagupAdAnaM nyAyyam | arthAntaraparigrahe coktaM dUShaNam | kathaM ca saMkhyAmAtrashravaNe satyashrutAnAM paJNcaviMshatitattvAnAm upasaMgrahaH pratIyeta? janashabdasya tattveShvarUDhatvAt, arthAntaropasaMgrahe.api saMkhyopapatteH | 

kathaM tarhi paJNca paJNcajanA iti? ucyate -- diksaMkhye saMj~nAyAm [pA. 2.1.50] iti visheShasmaraNAt saMj~nAyAm eva paJNcashabdasya janashabdena samAsaH | tatashca rUDhatvAbhiprAyeNaiva kecit paJNcajanA nAma vivakShyante, na sAN^khyatattvAbhiprAyeNa | te katItyasyAm AkAN^kShAyAM punaH paJNceti prayujyate | paJNcajanA nAma ye kecit, te ca paJNcaivetyarthaH, saptarShayaH sapteti yathA ||11||

 -- o)0(o -- 

|| 1.4.12 ||

ke punaH te paJNcajanA nAmeti, tad ucyate -- 

prANAdayo vAkyasheShAt || 

yasmin paJNca paJNcajanAH ityata uttarasmin mantre brahmasvarUpanirUpaNAya prANAdayaH paJNca nirdiShTAH -- prANasya prANam uta cakShuShashcakShur uta shrotrasya shrotram annasyAnnaM manaso ye mano viduH [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.18] iti | te.atra vAkyasheShagatAH saMnidhAnAt paJNcajanA vivakShyante | kathaM punaH prANAdiShu janashabdaprayogaH ? tattveShu vA kathaM janashabdaprayogaH? samAne tu prasiddhyatikrame vAkyasheShavashAt prANAdaya eva grahItavyA bhavanti | janasambandhAcca prANAdayo janashabdabhAjo bhavanti | janavacanashca puruShashabdaH prANeShu prayuktaH -- te vA ete paJNca brahmapuruShAH ityatra | prANo ha pitA prANo ha mAtA ityAdi ca brAhmaNam | samAsabalAcca samudAyasya rUDhatvam aviruddham | 

kathaM punar asati prathamaprayoge rUDhiH shakyAshrayitum? shakyA udbhidAdivad ityAha -- prasiddhArthasaMnidhAne hyaprasiddhArthaH shabdaH prayujyamAnaH samabhivyAhArAt tadviShayo niyamyate | yathA udbhidA yajeta yUpaM chinatti vediM karoti iti, tathA ayam api paJNcajanashabdaH samAsAn vAkhyAnAd avagatasaMj~nAbhAvaH saMj~nyAkAN^kShI vAkyasheShasamabhivyAhR^iteShu prANAdiShu vartiShyate | kaishcit tu devAH pitaro gandharvA asurA rakShAMsi ca paJNca paJNcajanA vyAkhyAtAH | anyaishca catvAro varNA niShAdapaJNcamAH parigR^ihItAH | kvacicca yat pAJNcajanyayA vishA iti prajAparaH prayogaH paJNcajanashabdasya dR^ishyate | tatparigrahe.apIha na kashcid virodhaH | AcAryaH tu na paJNcaviMshateH tattvAnAm iha pratItir astItyevaMparatayA prANAdayo vAkyasheShAt iti jagAda ||12||

|| 1.4.13 || 

bhaveyuH tAvat prANAdayaH paJNcajanA mAdhyaMdinAnAm, ye.annaM prANAdiShvamananti | kANvAnAM tu kathaM prANAdayaH paJNcajanA bhaveyuH ? ye.annaM prANAdiShu nAmanantIti -- ata uttaraM paThati -- 

jyotiShaikeShAm asatyanne ||

asatyapi kANvAnAm anne jyotiShA teShAM paJNcasaMkhyA pUryeta | te.api hi yasmin paJNca paJNcajanAH ityataH pUrvasmin mantre brahmasvarUpanirUpaNAyaiva jyotir adhIyate tad devA jyotiShAM jyotiH iti | kathaM punar ubhayeShAm api tulyavad idaM jyotiH paThyamAnaM samAnamantragatayA paJNcasaMkhyayA keShAMcid gR^ihyate keShAMcin neti -- apekShAbhedAd ityAha -- mAdhyaMdinAnAM hi samAnamantrapaThitaprANAdipaJNcajanalAbhAn nAsmin mantrAntarapaThite jyotiShyapekShA bhavati | tadalAbhAt tu kANvAnAM bhavatyapekShA | apekShAbhedAcca samAne.api mantre jyotiSho grahaNAgrahaNe | yathA samAne.apyatirAtre vacanabhedAt ShoDashino grahaNAgrahaNe, tadvat | tad evaM na tAvacchrutiprasiddhiH kAcit pradhAnaviShayAsti | smR^itinyAyaprasiddhI tu parihariShyete ||13||

4. kAraNatvAdhikaraNam

|| 1.4.14 ||

pratipAditaM brahmaNo lakShaNam | pratipAditaM brahmaviShayaM gatisAmAnyaM vedAntavAkyAnAm | pratipAditaM ca pradhAnasyAshabdatvam | tatredam aparam AshaN^kyate -- na janmAdikAraNatvaM brahmaNo brahmaviShayaM vA gatisAmAnyaM vedAntavAkyAnAM pratipAdayituM shakyam | kasmAt? vigAnadarshanAt | prativedAntaM hyanyAnyA sR^iShTir upalabhyate, kramAdivaicitryAt | tathA hi -- kvacit Atmana AkAshaH sambhUtaH [tai.u. 2.1.3] ityAkAshAdikA sR^iShTir AmnAyate | kvacit tejaAdikA tat tejo.asR^ijata iti | kvacit prANAdikA sa prANam asR^ijata prANAccharddhAm iti | kvacid akrameNaiva lokAnAm utpattir AmnAyate -- sa imAn lokAn asR^ijata | ambho marIcIr maram ApaH iti | tathA kvacid asatpUrvikA sR^iShTiH paThyate -- asad vA idam agra AsIt tato vai sad ajAyata [chA.u. 6.2.1] iti, asad evedam agra AsIt tat sad AsIt tat samabhavat [chA.u. 3.19.1] iti ca | kvacid asadvAdanirAkaraNena satpUrvikA prakriyA pratij~nAyate -- tad dhaika Ahur asad evedam agra AsIt [chA.u. 6.2.1] ityupakramya, kutaH tu khalu somyaivaM syAd iti hovAca katham asataH sajjAyeteti sat tv eva somyedam agra AsIt [chA.u. 6.2.2] iti | kvacit svayaMkartR^ikaiva vyAkriyA jagato nigadyate -- tad dhedaM tarhyavyAkR^itam AsIt tan nAmarUpAbhyAm eva vyAkriyata [bR^i.A.u. 1.4.7] iti | 

evam anekadhA vipratipatter vastuni ca vikalpasyAnupapatter na vedAntavAkyAnAM jagatkAraNAvadhAraNaparatA nyAyyA | smR^itinyAyaprasiddhibhyAM tu kAraNAntaraparigraho nyAyya ityevaM prApte, brUmaH -- 

kAraNatvena cAkAshAdiShu yathAvyapadiShTokteH || 

satyapi prativedAntaM sR^ijyamAneShvakAshAdiShu kramAdidvArake vigAne, na sraShTari kiMcid vigAnam asti | kutaH? yathAvyapadiShTokteH -- yathAbhUto hyekasmin vedAnte sarvaj~naH sarveshvaraH sarvAtmaiko.advitIyaH kAraNatvena vyapadiShTAH, tathAbhUta eva vedAntAntareShvapi vyapadishyate | tad yathA -- satyaM j~nAnam anantaM brahma [tai.u. 2.3] iti | atra tAvajj~nAnashabdena pareNa ca tadviShayeNa kAmayitR^itvavacanena cetanaM brahma nyarUpayat | aparaprayojyatveneshvaraM kAraNam abravIt | tadviShayeNaiva pareNAtmashabdena sharIrAdikoshaparamparayA cAntaranupraveshanena sarveShAm antaH pratyagAtmAnaM niradhArayat | bahu syAM prajAyeya iti cAtmaviShayeNa bahubhavanAnushaMsanena sR^ijyamAnAnAM vikArANAM sraShTur abhedam abhAShata | tathA idaM sarvam asR^ijata | yad idaM kiM ca iti samastajagatsR^iShTinirdeshena prAksR^iShTer advitIyaM sraShTAram AcaShTe | tad atra yallakShaNaM brahma kAraNatvena vij~nAtam | tallakShaNam evAnyatrApi vij~nAyate -- sad eva somyedam agra AsId ekam evAdvitIyam tad aikShata bahu syAM prajAyeyeti tat tejo.asR^ijata iti | tathA, AtmA vA idam eka evAgra AsIn nAnyat kiMcana miShat | sa aikShata lokAn nu sR^ijai iti ca -- evaMjAtIyakasya kAraNasvarUpanirUpaNaparasya vAkyajAtasya prativedAntam avigItArthatvAt | 

kAryaviShayaM tu vigAnaM dR^ishyate -- kvacid AkAshAdikA sR^iShTiH kvacit tejAdiketyevaMjAtIyakam | na ca kAryaviShayeNa vigAnena kAraNam api brahma sarvavedAnteShvavigItam adhigamyamAnam avivakShitaM bhavitum arhatIti shakyate vaktum, atiprasaN^gAt | samAdhAsyati cAcAryaH kAryaviShayam api vigAnam na viyadashruteH ityArabhya | bhaved api kAryasya vigItatvam apratipAdyatvAt | na hyayaM sR^iShTyAdiprapaJNcaH pratipipAdayiShitaH | na hi tatpratibaddhaH kashcit puruShArtho dR^ishyate shrUyate vA | na ca kalpayituM shakyate, upakramopasaMhArAbhyAM tatra tatra brahmaviShayair vAkyaiH sAkam ekavAkyatAyA gamyamAnatvAt | darshayati ca sR^iShTyAdiprapaJNcasya brahmapratipattyarthatAm -- annena somya shuN^genApo mUlam anvicchAdbhiH somya shuN^gena tejo mUlam anviccha tejasA somya shuN^gena sanmUlam anviccha [chA.u. 6.8.4] iti | mR^idAdidR^iShTAntaishca kAryasya kAraNenAbhedaM vadituM sR^iShTyAdiprapaJNcaH shrAvyata iti gamyate | tathA ca sampradAyavido vadanti -- 

mR^illohavisphuliN^gAdyaiH sR^iShTir yA coditAnyathA | 
upAyaH so.avatArAya nAsti bhedaH kathaMcana || iti | 

brahmapratipattipratibaddhaM tu phalaM shrUyate -- brahmavid Apnoti param [tai.u. 2.1], tarati shokam Atmavit, tam eva viditvAtimR^ityum eti [shve.u. 3.8] iti | pratyakShAvagamaM cedaM phalam, tat tvam asi ityasaMsAryAtmatvapratipattau satyAM saMsAryAtmatvavyAvR^itteH ||14|| 

|| 1.4.15 || 

yat punaH kAraNaviShayaM vigAnaM darshitam asad vA idam agra AsIt ityAdi, tat parihartavyam | atrocyate -- 

samAkarShAt || 

asad vA idam agra AsIt iti nAtrAsannirAtmakaM kAraNatvena shrAvyate | 

yato.asann eva sa bhavati | asad brahmeti veda cet | 
asti brahmeti ced veda | santamenaM tato viduH || 

ityasadvAdApavAdenAstitvalakShaNaM brahmAnnamayAdikoshaparamparayA pratyagAtmAnaM nirdhArya, so.akAmayata [tai.u. 2.6] iti tam eva prakR^itaM samAkR^iShya, saprapaJNcAM sR^iShTiM tasmAcchravayitvA, tat satyam ityAcakShate iti copasaMhR^itya, tad apyeSha shloko bhavati iti tasminn eva prakR^ite.arthe shlokam imam udAharati -- asad vA idam agra AsIt iti | yadi tu asan nirAtmakam asmiJNshloke.abhipreyeta, tato.anyasamAkarShaNe.anyasyodAharaNAd asambaddhaM vAkyam Apadyeta | tasmAn nAmarUpavyAkR^itavastuviShayaH prAyeNa sacchabdaH prasiddha iti tadvyAkaraNAbhAvApekShayA prAgutpatteH sad eva brahmAsad ivAsId ityupacaryate | eShaiva asad evedam agra AsIt ityatrApi yojanA, tat sad AsIt iti samAkarShaNAt | atyantAbhAvAbhyupagame hi tat sad AsIt iti kiM samAkR^iShyeta? tad dhaika Ahur asad evedam agra AsIt ityatrApi na shrutyantarAbhiprAyeNAyam ekIyam atopanyAsaH, kriyAyAm iva vastuni vikalpasyAsambhavAt | tasmAcchrutiparigR^ihItasatpakShadArDhyAyaivAyaM mandamatiparikalpitasyAsatpakShasyopanyasya nirAsa iti draShTavyam | tad dhIdaM tarhyavyAkR^itam AsIt ityatrApi na niradhyakShasya jagato vyAkaraNaM kathyate, sa eSha iha praviShTA A nakhAgrebhyaH ityadhyakShasya vyAkR^itakAryAnupraveshitvena samAkarShAt | niradhyakShe vyAkaraNAbhyupagame hyanantareNa prakR^itAvalambinA sa ityanena sarvanAmnA kaH kAryAnupraveshitvena samAkR^iShyeta? cetanasya cAyam AtmanaH sharIre.anupraveshaH shrUyate, anupraviShTasya cetanatvashravaNAt -- pashyaMshcakShuH shrR^iNvaJNshrotraM manvAno manaH iti | api ca yAdR^isham idam adyatve nAmarUpAbhyAM vyAkriyamANaM jagat sAdhyakShaM vyAkriyate, evamAdisarge.apIti gamyate, dR^iShTaviparItakalpanAnupapatteH | shrutyantaram api anena jIvenAtmanAnupravishya nAmarUpe vyAkaravANi iti sAdhyakShAm eva jagato vyAkriyAM darshayati | vyAkriyatam ityapi karmakartari lakAraH satyeva parameshvare vyAkartari saukaryam apekShya draShTavyaH -- yathA lUyate kedAraH svayam eveti satyeva pUrNake lavitari | yad vA karmaNyevaiSha lakAro.arthAkShiptaM kartrantaram apekShya draShTavyaH -- yathA gamyate grAma iti ||15||

  -- o)0(o -- 
bAlAkyadhikaraNam 

|| 1.4.16 ||

kauShItakibrAhmaNe bAlAkyajAtashatrusaMvAde shrUyate -- yo vai bAlAka eteShAM puruShANAM kartA yasya vaitatkarma sa vai veditavyaH iti | tatra kiM jIvo veditavyatvenopadishyate, uta mukhyaH prANaH, uta paramAtmeti viShayaH | kiM tAvat prAptam? prANa iti | kutaH? yasya vaitatkarma iti shravaNAt, parispandalakShaNasya ca karmaNaH prANAshrayatvAt | vAkyasheShe ca athAsmin prANa evaikadhA bhavati iti prANashabdashravaNAt, prANashabdasya ca mukhye prANe prasiddhatvAt | ye caite purastAdbAlAkinA Aditye puruShashcandramasi puruShaH ityevamAdayaH puruShA nirdiShTAH, teShAm api bhavati prANaH kartA, prANAvasthAvisheShatvAd AdityAdidevatAtmanAm -- katama eko deva iti prANa iti sa brahma tyadityAcakShate iti shrutyantaraprasiddhaH | jIvo vAyam iha veditavyatayopadishyate | tasyApi dharmAdharmalakShaNaM karma shakyate shrAvayitum -- yasya vaitatkarma iti | so.api bhoktR^itvAd bhogopakaraNabhUtAnAmeteShAM puruShANAM ca kartopapadyate | vAkyasheShe jIvaliN^gamavagamyate -- yatkAraNaM veditavyatayopanyastasya puruShANAM karturvedanAyopetaM bAlAkiM prati bubodhayiShurajAtashatruH suptaM puruShamAmanrtya AmantraNashabdAshravaNAt prANAdInAmabhoktR^itvaM pratibodhya yaShTighAtotthApanAt prANAdivyatiriktaM jIvaM bhoktAraM pratibodhayati | tathA parastAd api jIvaliN^gamavagamyate -- tad yathA shreShThI svair bhuN^kte yathA vA svAH shreShThinaM bhuJNjantyevam evaiSha praj~nAtmaitairAtmabhir bhuN^kte evam evaita AtmAna etamAtmAnaM bhuJNjanti iti | prANabhR^ittvAcca jIvasyopapannaM prANashabdatvam | tasmAjjIvamukhyaprANayor anyatara iha grahaNIyaH, na parameshvaraH, talliN^gAnavagamAdityevaM prApte, brUmaH -- 

jagadvAcitvAt || 

parameshvara evAyameteShAM puruShANAM kartA syAt | kasmAt? upakramasAmarthyAt | iha hi bAlAkirajAtashatruNA saha brahma te bravANi iti saMvaditum upacakrame | sa ca katicidAdityAdyadhikaraNAn puruShAnamukhyabrahmadR^iShTibhAja uktvA tUShNIM babhUva | tamajAtashatruH mR^iShA vai khalu mA saMvadiShThA brahma te bravANi ityamukhyabrahmavAditayApodya, tatkartAramanyaM veditavyatayopacikShepa | yadi so.apyamukhyabrahmadR^iShTibhAksyAt, upakramo bAdhyeta | tasmAt parameshvara evAyaM bhavitum arhati | kartR^itvaM caiteShAM puruShANAM na parameshvarAdanyasya svAtantryeNAvakalpate | yasya vaitatkarma ityapi nAyaM parispandalakShaNasya dharmAdharmalakShaNasya vA karmaNo nirdeshaH, tayor anyatarasyApyaprakR^itatvAt, asaMshabditatvAcca | nApi puruShANAm ayaM nirdeshaH, eteShAM puruShANAM kartA ityeva teShAM nirdiShTatvAt, liN^gavacanavigAnAcca | nApi puruShaviShayasya karotyarthasya 
kriyAphalasya vAyaM nirdeshaH, kartR^ishabdenaiva tayorupAttatvAt | pArisheShyAt pratyakShasaMnihitaM jagat sarvanAmnaitacchabdena nirdishyate | kriyata iti ca tad eva jagatkarma | 

nanu jagadapyaprakR^itamasaMshabditaM ca | satyam etat | tathApyasati visheShopAdAne sAdhAraNenArthena saMnidhAnena saMnihitavastumAtrasyAyaM nirdesha iti gamyate, na vishiShTasya kasyacitta, visheShasaMnidhAnAbhAvAt | pUrvatra ca jagadekadeshabhUtAnAM puruShANAM visheShopAdAnAd avisheShitaM jagadevehopAdIyata iti gamyate | etad uktaM bhavati -- ya eteShAM puruShANAM jagadekadeshabhUtAnAM kartA -- kim anena visheSheNa? yasya vA kR^itsnam eva jagad avisheShitaM karmetivAshabda ekadeshAvacchinnakartR^itvavyAvR^ittyarthaH | ye bAlAkinA brahmatvAbhimatAH puruShAH kIrtitAH, teShAm abrahmatvakhyApanAya visheShopAdAnam | evaM brAhmaNaparivrAjakanyAyena sAmAnyavisheShAbhyAM jagataH kartA veditavyatayopadishyate | parameshvarashca sarvajagataH kartA sarvavedAnteShvavadhAritaH ||

jIvamukhyaprANaliN^ganneti cettadvyAkhyAtam || 1.4.17 || 

 || 1.4.17 || 

atha yad uktaM vAkyasheShagatAjjIvaliN^gAnmukhyaprANaliN^gAcca tayor evAnyatarasyeha grahaNaM nyAyyaM na parameshvarasyeti, tat parihartavyam | atrocyate -- parihR^itaM caitat nopAsAtraividhyAdAshritatvAd iha tadyogAt ityatra | trividhaM hyatropAsanam evaM sati prasajyeta -- jIvopAsanaM mukhyaprANopAsanaM brahmopAsanaM ceti | na caitannyAyyam | upakramopasaMhArAbhyAM hi brahmaviShayatvamasya vAkyasyAvagamyate | tatropakramasya tAvadbrahmaviShayatvaM darshitam | upasaMhArasyApi niratishayaphalashravaNAdbrahmaviShayatvaM dR^ishyate -- sarvAn pApmano.apahatya sarveShAM ca bhUtAnAM shraiShThyaM svArAjyamAdhipatyaM paryeti ya evaM veda iti | nanv evaM sati pratardanavAkyanirNayenaivedam api vAkyaM nirNIyeta | na nirNIyate, yasya vaitatkarma ityasya brahmaviShayatvena tatra anirdhAritatvAt | tasmAd atra jIvamukhyaprANashaN^kA punar utpadyamAnA nivartyate | prANashabdo.api brahmaviShayo dR^iShTAH prANabandhanaM hi somya manaH ityatra | jIvaliN^gamapyupakramopasaMhArayor brahmaviShayatvAd abhedAbhiprAyeNa yojayitavyam ||

anyArthaM tu jaiminiH prashnavyAkhyAnAbhyAm api caivameke || 1.4.18 || 

 || 1.4.18 || 

api ca naivAtra vivaditavyam -- jIvapradhAnaM vedaM vAkyaM syAt brahmapradhAnaM veti | yato.anyArthaM jIvaparAmarshaM brahmapratipattyarthamasmin vAkye jaiminir AcAryo manyate | kasmAt? prashnavyAkhyAnAbhyAm | prashnaH tAvatsuShuptapuruShapratibodhanena prANAdivyatirikte jIve pratibodhite punar javavyatiriktaviShayo dR^ishyate -- kvaiSha etadbAlAke puruSho.ashayiShTA kva vA etadabhUtkuta etadAgAt iti | prativacanam api -- yadA suptaH svapnaM na kaMcana pashyatyathAsmin prANa evaikadhA bhavati ityAdi, etasmAd AtmanaH sarve prANA yathAyatanaM vipratiShThante prANebhyo devA devebhyo lokAH iti ca suShuptikAle ca pareNa brahmaNA jIva ekatAM gacchati | parasmAcca brahmaNaH prANAdikaM jagajjAyata iti vedAntamaryAdA | tasmAd yatrAsya jIvasya niHsambodhasvasthatArUpaH svApaH -- upAdhijanitavisheShavij~nAnarahitaM svarUpam, yatastadbhraMsharUpamAgamanam, so.atra paramAtmA veditavyatayA shrAvita iti gamyate | api caivameke shAkhino vAjasaneyino.asminneva bAlAkyajAtashatrusaMvAde spaShTAM vij~nAnamayashabdena jIvamAmnAya tadvyatiriktaM paramAtmAnam Amananti ya eSha vij~nAnamayaH puruShaH kvaiSha tadAbhUtkuta etadAgAt iti prashne | prativacane.api ya eSho.antarhR^idaya AkAshastasmiJNshete iti | AkAshashabdashca paramAtmani prayuktaH daharo.asminnantarAkAshaH ityatra | sarva eta AtmAno vyuccaranti iti copAdhimatAmAtmanAmanyato vyuccaraNam AmanantaH paramAtmAnam eva kAraNatvenAmanantIti gamyate | prANanirAkaraNasyApi suShuptapuruShotthApanena prANAdivyatiriktopadesho.abhyuccayaH ||

5. vAkyAnvayAdhikaraNam

|| 1.4.19 ||

bR^ihadAraNyake maitreyIbrAhmaNe.abhidhIyate -- 

na vA are patyuH kAmAya ityupakramya, na vA are sarvasya kAmAya sarvaM priyaM bhavatyAtmanaH tu kAmAya sarvaM priyaM bhavatyAtmA vA are draShTavyaH shrotavyo mantavyo nididhyAsitavyo maitreyyAtmano vA are darshanena shravaNena matyA vij~nAnenedaM sarvaM viditam [bR^i.A.u. 4.5.6] iti

tatraitad vicikitsyate -- kiM vij~nAnAtmaivAyaM draShTavyashrotavyatvAdirUpeNopadishyate, Aho svit paramAtmeti ? kutaH punar eShA vicikitsA? priyasaMsUcitenAtmanA bhoktropakramAd vij~nAnAtmopadesha iti pratibhAti | tathAtmavij~nAnena sarvavij~nAnopadeshAt paramAtmopadesha iti | kiM tAvat prAptam? -- vij~nAnAtmopadesha iti | kasmAt? upakramasAmarthyAt | patijAyAputravittAdikaM hi bhogyabhUtaM sarvaM jagat AtmArthatayA priyaM bhavatIti priyasaMsUcitaM bhoktAram AtmAnam upakramyAnantaram idam Atmano darshanAdyupadishyamAnaM kasyAnyasyAtmanaH syAt? madhye.api idaM mahadbhUtam anantam apAraM vij~nAnaghana evaitebhyo bhUtebhyaH samutthAya tAnyevAnuvinashyati na pretya saMj~nAsti iti prakR^itasyaiva mahato bhUtasya draShTavyasya bhUtebhyaH samutthAnaM vij~nAnAtmabhAvena bruvan vij~nAnAtmana evedaM draShTavyatvaM darshayati | vij~nAtAram are kena vijAnIyAt iti kartR^ivacanena shabdenopasaMharan vij~nAnAtmAnam evehopadiShTAM darshayati | tasmAd Atmavij~nAnena sarvavij~nAnavacanaM bhoktrarthatvAd bhogyajAtasyaupacArikaM draShTavyam ityevaM prApte, brUmaH -- 

vAkyAnvayAt ||

paramAtmopadesha evAyam | kasmAt? vAkyAnvayAt | vAkyaM hIdaM paurvAparyeNa avekShyamANaM paramAtmAnaM pratyanvitAvayavaM lakShyate | katham iti tad upapAdyate --  amR^itatvasya tu nAshAsti vittena [bR^i.A.u. 4.5.3] iti yAj~navalkyAd upashrutya, yenAhaM nAmR^itA syAM kim ahaM tena kuryAM ? yad eva bhagavAn veda tad eva me brUhi [bR^i.A.u. 4.5.4] amR^itatvam AshAsAnAyai maitreyyai yAj~navalkya Atmavij~nAnam upadishati | na cAnyatra paramAtmavij~nAnAd amR^itatvam astIti shrutismR^itivAdA vadanti | tathA cAtmavij~nAnena sarvavij~nAnam ucyamAnaM nAnyatra paramakAraNavij~nAnAn mukhyam avakalpate | 

na caitad aupacArikam AshrayituM shakyam, yat kAraNam Atmavij~nAnena sarvavij~nAnaM pratij~nAyAnantareNa granthena tad evopapAdayati -- brahma taM parAd Adyo.anyatrAtmano brahma veda ityAdinA | yo hi brahmakShatrAdikaM jagad Atmano.anyatra svAtantryeNa labdhasadbhAvaM pashyati, taM mithyAdarshinaM tad eva mithyAdR^iShTAM brahmakShatrAdikaM jagat parAkarotIti bhedadR^iShTim apodya, idaM sarvaM yad ayam AtmA [bR^i.A.u. 2.4.6] iti sarvasya vastujAtasyAtmAvyatirekam avatArayati | dundubhyAdidR^iShTAntaishca tam evAvyatirekaM draDhayati -- asya mahato bhUtasya niHshvasitam etad yad R^igvedaH [bR^i.A.u. 2.4.10] ityAdinA ca prakR^itasyAtmano nAmarUpakarmaprapaJNcakAraNatAM vyAcakShANaH paramAtmAnam evainaM gamayati | tathaivaikAyanaprakriyAyAm api saviShayasya sendriyasya sAntaHkaraNasya prapaJNcasyaikAyanam anantaram abAhyaM kR^itsnaM praj~nAnaghanaM vyAcakShANaH paramAtmAnam evainaM gamayati | tasmAt paramAtmana evAyaM darshanAdyupadesha iti gamyate ||19|| 

|| 1.4.20 ||

yat punaruktaM priyasaMsUcitopakramAd vij~nAnAtmana evAyaM darshanAdyupadesha iti, atra brUmaH -- 

pratij~nAsiddher liN^gam AshmarathyaH ||

astyatra pratij~nA -- Atmani vij~nAte sarvam idaM vij~nAtaM bhavati idaM sarvaM yad ayam AtmA [bR^i.A.u. 2.4.6] iti ca | tasyAH pratij~nAyAH siddhiM sUcayatyetal liN^gam, yat priyasaMsUcitasyAtmano draShTavyAtvAdisaN^kIrtanam | yadi hi vij~nAnAtmA paramAtmano.anyaH syAt, tataH paramAtmavij~nAne.api vij~nAnAtmA na vij~nAyata ityekavij~nAnena sarvavij~nAnaM yat pratij~nAtam, tad dhIyeta | tasmAt pratij~nAsiddhyarthaM vij~nAnAtmaparamAtmanor abhedAMshenopakramaNam ityAshmarathya AcAryo manyate ||20||

|| 1.4.21 ||

utkramiShyata evambhAvAd ityauDulomiH ||

vij~nAnAtmana eva dehendriyamanobuddhisaMghAtopAdhisamparkAt kaluShIbhUtasya j~nAnadhyAnAdisAdhanAnuShThAnAt samprasannasya dehAdisaMghAtAd utkramiShyataH paramAtmanaikyopapatteH idam abhedenopakramaNam ityauDulomir AcAryo manyate | shrutishcaivaM bhavati -- eSha samprasAdo.asmAccharIrAt samutthAya paraM jyotir upasampadya svena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyate [chA.u. 8.3.4] iti | kvacicca jIvAshrayam api nAmarUpaM nadInidarshanena j~nApayati -- 

yathA nadyaH syandamAnAH sam upA.a
staM gacchanti nAmarUpe vihAya | 
tathA vidvAn nAmarUpAd vimuktaH 
parAt paraM puruSham upaiti divyam || [mu.u. 3.2.8] iti |

yathA loke nadyaH svAshrayam eva nAmarUpaM vihAya samudram upayanti, evaM jIvo.api svAshrayam eva nAmarUpaM vihAya paraM puruSham upaitIti hi tatrArthaH pratIyate -- dR^iShTAntadArShTAntikayoH tulyatAyai ||21||

|| 1.4.22 ||

avasthiteH iti kAshakR^itsnaH ||

asyaiva paramAtmano.anenApi vij~nAnAtmabhAvenAvasthAnAd upapannam idam abhedenopakramaNam iti kAshakR^itsna AcAryo manyate | tathA ca brAhmaNam -- anena jIvenAtmanAnupravishya nAmarUpe vyAkaravANi ityevaMjAtIyakaM parasyaivAtmano jIvabhAvenAvasthAnaM darshayati | mantravarNashca -- sarvANi rUpANi vicitya dhIro nAmAni kR^itvAbhivad anyad Aste [tai.A. 3.12.7] ityevaMjAtIyakaH | na ca tejaHprabhR^itInAM sR^iShTir jIvasya pR^ithaksR^iShTiH shrutA, yena parasmAd Atmano.anyastadvikAro jIvaH syAt | kAshakR^itsnasyAcAryasyAvikR^itaH parameshvaro jIvaH, nAnya iti matam | Ashmarathyasya tu yadyapi jIvasya parasmAd ananyatvam abhipretam, tathApi pratij~nAsiddhiH iti sApekShatvAbhidhAnAt kAryakAraNabhAvaH kiyAn apyabhipreta iti gamyate | 

auDulomipakShe punaH spaShTam evAvasthAntarApekShau bhedAbhedau gamyete | tatra kAshakR^itsnIyaM mataM shrutyanusArIti gamyate, pratipipAdayiShitArthAnusArAt tattvam asi ityAdi shrutibhyaH | evaM ca sati tajj~nAnAd amR^itatvam avakalpate | vikArAtmakatve hi jIvasyAbhyupagamyamAne vikArasya prakR^itisambandhe pralayaprasaN^gAn na tajj~nAnAd amR^itatvam avakalpeta | atashca svAshrayasya nAmarUpasyAsambhavAd upAdhyAshrayaM nAmarUpaM jIve upacaryate | ata evotpattir api jIvasya kvacid agnivisphuliN^godAharaNena shrAvyamANA upAdhyAshrayaiva veditavyA || 

yad apyuktaM prakR^itasyaiva mahato bhUtasya draShTavyasya bhUtebhyaH samutthAnaM vij~nAnAtmabhAvena darshayan vij~nAnAtmana evedaM draShTavyatvaM darshayatIti, tatrApIyam eva trisUtrI yojayitavyA | pratij~nAsiddher liN^gam AshmarathyaH [ve.sU. 1.4.20] | idam atra pratij~nAtam -- Atmani vidite sarvam idaM viditaM bhavati idaM sarvaM yad ayam AtmA [bR^i.A.u. 2.4.6] iti ca | upapAditaM ca sarvasya nAmarUpakarmaprapaJNcasyaikaprasavatvAd ekapralayatvAcca dundubhyAdidR^iShTAntaishca kAryakAraNayor avyatirekapratipAdanAt | tasyA eva pratij~nAyAH siddhiM sUcayatyetal liN^gam, yan mahato bhUtasya bhUtebhyaH samutthAnaM vij~nAnAtmabhAvena kathitam ityAshmarathya AcAryo manyate -- abhede hi satyekavij~nAnena sarvavij~nAnaM pratij~nAtam avakalpata iti | utkramiShyata evambhAvAd ityauDulomiH -- utkramiShyato vij~nAnAtmano j~nAnadhyAnAdisAmarthyAt samprasannasya pareNAtmanaikyasambhavAd idam abhedAbhidhAnam ityauDulomir AcAryo manyate | 

avasthiteH iti kAshakR^itsnaH -- asyaiva paramAtmano.anenApi vij~nAnAtmabhAvenAvasthAnAd upapannam idam abhedAbhidhAnam iti kAshakR^itsna AcAryo manyate | nanUcchedAbhidhAnam etat -- etebhyo bhUtebhyaH samutthAya tAnyevAnuvinashyati na pretya saMj~nAsti iti | katham etad abhedAbhidhAnam? naiSha doShaH | visheShavij~nAnavinAshAbhiprAyam etadvinAshAbhidhAnam, nAtmocchedAbhiprAyam | atraiva mA bhagavAn amUmuhan na pretya saMj~nAsti iti paryanuyujya, svayam eva shrutyA arthAntarasya darshitatvAt -- na vA are.ahaM mohaM bravImyavinAshI vA are.ayam AtmAnucchittidharmA [bR^i.A.u. 4.5.14], mAtrAsaMsargaH tu asya bhavati iti | 

etad uktaM bhavati -- kUTasthanitya evAyaM vij~nAnaghana AtmA | nAsyocchedaprasaN^go.asti | mAtrAbhiH tu asya bhUtendriyalakShaNAbhir avidyAkR^itAbhir asaMsargo vidyayA bhavati | saMsargAbhAve ca tatkR^itasya visheShavij~nAnasyAbhAvAt na pretya saMj~nAsti ityuktam iti | yad apyuktam -- vij~nAtAram are kena vijAnIyAt iti kartR^ivacanena shabdenopasaMhArAd vij~nAnAtmana evedaM draShTavyam iti, tad api kAshakR^itsnIyenaiva darshanena pariharaNIyam | 

api ca yatra hi dvaitam iva bhavati tad itara itaraM pashyati ityArabhyAvidyAviShaye tasyaiva darshanAdilakShaNaM visheShavij~nAnaM prapaJNcya, yatra tu asya sarvam AtmaivAbhUt tat kena kaM pashyet [bR^i.A.u. 4.5.15] ityAdinA vidyAviShaye tasyaiva darshanAdilakShaNasya visheShavij~nAnasyAbhAvam abhidadhAti | punashca viShayAbhAve.apyAtmAnaM vijAnIyAd ityAshaN^kya, vij~nAtAram are kena vijAnIyAt ityAha | tatashca visheShavij~nAnAbhAvopapAdanaparatvAd vAkyasya vij~nAnadhAtur eva kevalaH san bhUtapUrvagatyA kartR^ivacanena tR^icA nirdiShTA iti gamyate | darshitaM tu purastAt kAshakR^itsnIyasya pakShasya shrutimattvam | atashca vij~nAnAtmaparamAtmanor avidyApratyupasthApitanAmarUparacitadehAdyupAdhinimitto bhedaH, na pAramArthika ityeSho.arthaH sarvair vedAntavAdibhir abhyupagantavyaH -- sad eva somyedam agra AsId ekam evAdvitIyam AtmaivedaM sarvam [chA.u. 7.25.2], brahmaivedaM sarvam idaM sarvaM yad ayam AtmA [bR^i.A.u. 2.4.6] nAnyo.ato.asti draShTA nAnyad ato.asti draShTR^i ityevaMrUpAbhyaH shrutibhyaH | smR^itibhyashca -- vAsudevaH sarvam iti [gItA 7.19], kShetraj~naM cApi mAM viddhi sarvakShetreShu bhArata [gItA 13.2], samaM sarveShu bhUteShu tiShThantaM parameshvaram [gItA 13.26] ityevaMrUpAbhyaH | 

bhedadarshanApavAdAcca -- anyo.asAvanyo.aham asmIti na sa veda yathA pashuH mR^ityoH sa mR^ityum Apnoti ya iha nAneva pashyati ityevaMjAtIyakAt | sa vA eSha mahAn aja AtmAjaro.amaro.amR^ito.abhayo brahma [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.25] iti ca Atmani sarvavikriyApratiShedhAt | anyathA ca mumukShUNAM nirapavAdavij~nAnAnupapatteH, sunishcitArthatvAnupapatteshca | nirapavAdaM hi vij~nAnaM sarvAkAN^kShAnivartakam AtmaviShayam iShyate -- vedAntavij~nAnasunishcitArthAH iti ca shruteH | tatra ko mohaH kaH shoka ekatvam anupashyataH [Isho. 7] iti ca | sthitapraj~nalakShaNasmR^iteshca | sthite ca kShetraj~naparamAtmaikatvaviShaye samyagdarshane kShetraj~naH paramAtmeti nAmamAtrabhedAt, kShetraj~no.ayaM paramAtmano bhinnaH paramAtmAyaM kShetraj~nAd bhinna ityevaMjAtIyaka AtmabhedaviShayo.ayaM nirbandho nirarthakaH -- eko hyayam AtmA nAmamAtrabhedena bahudhAbhidhIyata iti | na hi satyaM j~nAnam anantaM brahma [tai.u. 2.3] | yo veda nihitaM guhAyAm iti kAMcid evaikAM guhAm adhikR^ityaitad uktam | na ca brahmaNo.anyo guhAyAM nihito.asti, tat sR^iShTvA tad evAnuprAvishat iti sraShTur eva praveshashravaNAt | ye tu nirbandhaM kurvanti, te vedAntArthaM bAdhamAnAH shreyoddhAraM samyagdarshanam eva bAdhante | kR^itakam anityaM ca mokShaM kalpayanti | nyAyena ca na saMgacchanta iti ||22||

6. prakR^ityadhikaraNam

|| 1.4.23 ||

yathAbhyudayahetutvAd dharmo jij~nAsyaH, evaM niHshreyasahetutvAd brahmApi jij~nAsyam ityuktam | brahma ca janmAdyasya yataH [ve.sU. 1.1.2] iti lakShitam | tacca lakShaNaM ghaTarucakAdInAM mR^itsuvarNAdivat prakR^ititve kulAlasuvarNakArAdivan nimittatve ca samAnam ityato bhavati vimarshaH -- kim AtmakaM punar brahmaNaH kAraNatvaM syAd iti | tatra nimittakAraNam eva tAvat kevalaM syAd iti pratibhAti | kasmAt? IkShApUrvakakartR^itvashravaNAt -- IkShApUrvakaM hi brahmaNaH kartR^itvam avagamyate -- sa IkShAM cakre sa prANam asR^ijata ityAdi shrutibhyaH | IkShApUrvakaM ca kartR^itvaM nimittakAraNeShv eva kulAlAdiShu dR^iShTam | anekakArakapUrvikA ca kriyAphalasiddhir loke dR^iShTA | sa ca nyAya Adikartaryapi yuktaH saMkramayitum | Ishvaratvaprasiddhashca -- IshvarANAM hi rAjavaivasvatAdInAM nimittakAraNatvam eva kevalaM pratIyate | tadvat parameshvarasyApi nimittakAraNatvam eva yuktaM pratipattum | kAryaM cedaM jagat sAvayavam acetanam ashuddhaM ca dR^ishyate, kAraNenApi tasya tAdR^ishenaiva bhavitavyam, kAryakAraNayoH sArUpyadarshanAt | brahma cAnevaMlakShaNam avagamyate -- niShkalaM niShkriyaM shAntaM niravadyaM niraJNjanam ityAdi shrutibhyaH | pArisheShyAd brahmaNo.anyad upAdAnakAraNam ashuddhyAdiguNakaM smR^itiprasiddham abhyupagantavyam, brahmakAraNatvashruter nimittatvamAtre paryavasAnAd ityevaM prApte -- 

prakR^itishca pratij~nAdR^iShTAntAnurodhAt ||

brUmaH -- prakR^itishcopAdAnakAraNaM ca brahmAbhyupagantavyam, nimittakAraNaM ca | na kevalaM nimittakAraNam eva | kasmAt? pratij~nAdR^iShTAntAnuparodhAt | evaM hi pratij~nAdR^iShTAntau shrautau noparudhyete | pratij~nA tAvat -- uta tam Adesham aprAkShyo yenAshrutaM shrutaM bhavatyamataM matam avij~nAtaM vij~nAtam [chA.u. 4.1.3] iti | tatra caikena vij~nAtena sarvam anyad avij~nAtam api vij~nAtaM bhavatIti pratIyate | taccopAdAnakAraNavij~nAne sarvavij~nAnaM sambhavati, upAdAnakAraNAvyatirekAt kAryasya | nimittakAraNAvyatirekaH tu kAryasya nAsti, loke takShNaH prAsAdavyatirekadarshanAt | dR^iShTAnto.api yathA somyaikena mR^itpiNDena sarvaM mR^inmayaM vij~nAtaM syAd vAcArambhaNaM vikAro nAmadheyaM mR^ittiketyeva satyam [chA.u. 6.1.4] ityupAdAnakAraNagocara evAmnAyate | tathA ekena lohamaNinA sarvaM lohamayaM vij~nAtaM syAt ekena nakhanikR^intanena sarvaM kArShNAyasaM vij~nAtaM syAt iti ca | tathAnyatrApi kasmin nu bhagavo vij~nAte sarvam idaM vij~nAtaM bhavati [mu.u. 1.1.3] iti pratij~nA | yathA pR^ithivyAm oShadhayaH sambhavanti iti dR^iShTAntaH | tathA Atmani khalvare dR^iShTo shrute mate vij~nAte idaM sarvaM viditam iti pratij~nA | sa yathA dundubher hanyamAnasya na bAhyAJNshabdAJNshaknuyAd grahaNAya dundubheH tu grahaNena dundubhyAghAtasya vA shabdo gR^ihItaH iti dR^iShTAntaH | 

evaM yathAsambhavaM prativedAntaM pratij~nAdR^iShTAntau prakR^ititvasAdhanau pratyetavyau | yata itIyam api paJNcamI -- yato vA imAni bhUtAni jAyante [tai.u. 3.1] ityatra janikartuH prakR^itiH iti visheShasmaraNAt prakR^itilakShaNa evApAdAne draShTavyA | nimittatvaM tu adhiShThAtrantarAbhAvAd adhigantavyam | yathA hi loke mR^itsuvarNAdikam upAdAnakAraNaM kulAlasuvarNakArAdIn adhiShThAtranapekShya pravartate, naivaM brahmaNa upAdAnakAraNasya sato.anyo.adhiShThAtApekShyo.asti, prAgutpatteH ekam evAdvitIyam ityavadhAraNAt | adhiShThAtrantarAbhAvo.api pratij~nAdR^iShTAntAnuparodhAM devodito veditavyaH -- adhiShThAtari hyupAdAnAd anyasminn abhyupagamyamAne punar apyekavij~nAnena sarvavij~nAnasyAsambhavAt pratij~nAdR^iShTAntoparodha eva syAt | tasmAd adhiShThAtrantarAbhAvAd AtmanaH kartR^itvam upAdAnAntarAbhAvAcca prakR^ititvam ||23|| 

|| 1.4.24 ||

kutashcAtmanaH kartR^itvaprakR^ititve? -- 

abhidhyopadeshAcca ||

abhidhyopadeshashcAtmanaH kartR^itvaprakR^ititve gamayati so.akAmayata bahu syAM prajAyeya [tai.u. 2.5.1] iti, tad aikShata bahu syAM prajAyeya iti ca | tatrAbhidhyAnapUrvikAyAH svAtantryapravR^itteH karteti gamyate | bahu syAm iti pratyagAtmaviShayatvAd bahubhavanAbhidhyAnasya prakR^itiH ityapi gamyate ||24||

|| 1.4.25 ||

sAkShAccobhayAmnAtAt ||

prakR^ititvasyAyam abhyuccayaH | itashca prakR^itir brahma, yat kAraNaM sAkShAd brahmaiva kAraNam upAdAya ubhau prabhavapralayAvamnAyete -- sarvANi ha vA imAni bhUtAnyAkAshAd eva sam utpadyante | AkAshaM pratyastaM yanti iti | yad dhi yasmAt prabhavati, yasmiMshca pralIyate tat tasyopAdAnaM prasiddham, yathA vrIhiyavAdInAM pR^ithivI | sAkShAt iti ca -- upAdAnAntarAnupAdAnaM sUcayati AkAshAd eva iti | pratyastamayashca nopAdAnAd anyatra kAryasya dR^iShTAH ||25||

|| 1.4.26 ||

AtmakR^iteH pariNAmAt ||

itashca prakR^itir brahma, yat kAraNaM brahmaprakriyAyAm, tad AtmAnaM svayam akuruta ityAtmanaH karmatvaM kartR^itvaM ca darshayati -- AtmAnam iti karmatvam, svayam akuruteti kartR^itvam | kathaM punaH pUrvasiddhasya sataH kartR^itvena vyavasthitasya kriyamANatvaM shakyaM sampAdayitum? pariNAmAd iti brUmaH -- pUrvasiddho.api hi sann AtmA visheSheNa vikArAtmanA pariNamayAmAsAtmAnam iti | vikArAtmanA ca pariNAmo mR^idAdyAsu prakR^itiShUpalabdhaH | svayam iti ca visheShaNAn nimittAntarAnapekShatvam api pratIyate |

pariNAmAt iti vA pR^ithak sUtram | tasyaiSho.arthaH -- itashca prakR^itir brahma, yat kAraNaM brahmaNa eva vikArAtmanA ca pariNAmaH sAmAnAdhikaraNyenAmnAyate sacca tyaccAbhavan niruktaM cAniruktaM ca [tai.u. 2.5.1] ityAdineti ||26||

|| 1.4.27 ||

yonishca hi gIyate ||

itashca prakR^itir brahma, yat kAraNaM brahma yoniH ityapi paThyate vedAnteShu -- kartAram IshaM puruShaM brahmayonim iti yad bhUtayoniM paripashyanti dhIrAH iti ca | yonishabdashca prakR^itivacanaH samadhigato loke -- pR^ithivI yonir oShadhivanaspatInAm iti | strIyoner apyastyevAvayavadvAreNa garbhaM pratyupAdAnakAraNatvam | 

kvacit sthAnavacano.api yonishabdo dR^iShTaH -- yoniShTA indra niShade akAri iti | vAkyasheShAt tu atra prakR^itivacanatA parigR^ihyate -- yathorNanAbhiH sR^ijate gR^ihNate ca [mu.u. 1.1.7] ityevaMjAtIyakAt | tad evaM prakR^ititvaM brahmaNaH prasiddham | yat punaH idamuktam, IkShApUrvakaM kartR^itvaM nimittakAraNeShv eva kulAlAdiShu loke dR^iShTAm, nopAdAneShvityAdi, tatpratyucyate -- na lokavadiha bhavitavyam | na hyayamanumAnagamyo.arthaH | shabdagamyatvAt tvasyArthasya yathAshabdam iha bhavitavyam | shabdashcekShitur Ishvarasya prakR^ititvaM pratipAdayatItyavocAma | punashcaitat sarvaM vistareNa prativakShyAmaH ||

7. sarvavyAkyAtAdhikaraNam

|| 1.4.28 ||

etena sarve vyAkhyAtA vyAkhyAtAH || 

IkShater nAshabdam ityArabhya pradhAnakAraNavAdaH sUtrair eva punaH punar AshaN^kya nirAkR^itaH -- tasya hi pakShasyopodbalakAni kAnicil liN^gAbhAsAni vedAnteShvapAtena mandamatIn prati bhAntIti | sa ca kAryakAraNAn anyatvAbhyupagamAt pratyAsanno vedAntavAd asya devalaprabhR^itibhishca kaishcid dharmasUtrakAraiH svagrantheShvashritaH, tena tatpratiShedhe eva yatno.atIva kR^itaH, nANvAdikAraNavAdapratiShedhe | te.api tu brahmakAraNavAdapakShasya pratipakShatvAt pratiSheddhavyAH | teShAm apyupodbalakaM vaidikaM kiMcil liN^gam ApAtena mandamatIn prati bhAyAd iti -- ataH pradhAnamallanibarhaNanyAyenAtidishati -- etena pradhAnakAraNavAdapratiShedhanyAyakalApena sarve.aNvAdikAraNavAdA api pratiShiddhatayA vyAkhyAtA veditavyAH, teShAm api pradhAnavadashabdatvAcchabdavirodhitvAcceti | vyAkhyAtA vyAkhyAtA iti padAbhyAso.adhyAyaparisamAptiM dyotayati || 
iti shrImatparamahaMsaparivrAjakAcAryasya shrIgovindabhagavatpUjyapAdashiShyasya shrImacchaMkarabhagavataH kR^itau 
shArIrakamImAMsAsUtrabhAShye prathamo.adhyAyaH || 


 
 || dvitIyo.adhyAye prathamaH pAdaH || 

dvitIye avirodhAkhyAdhyAye prathamapAde 
sAMkhyayogakANAdAdismR^itibhiH sAMkhyAdiprayuktatarkaishca 
vedAntasamanvayavirodhaparihAraH ||

1. smR^ityadhikaraNam 

|| 2.1.1 ||

prathame.adhyAye sarvaj~naH sarveshvaro jagadutpattikAraNaM mR^itsuvarNAdaya iva ghaTarucakAdInAM utpannasya jagato niyantR^itvena sthitikAraNaM mAyAvIva mAyAyAH, prasAritasya ca jagataH pnaH svAtmanyevopasaMhArakAraNaM avaniH iva caturvidhasya bhUtagrAmasya, sa eva ca sarveShAM na Atmetyetad vedAntavAkyasamanvayapratipAdanena pratipAditam | pradhAnAdikAraNavAdAshcAshabdena nirAkR^itAH | idAnIM svapakShe smR^itinyAyavirodhaparihAraH, pradhAnAdivAdAnAM ca nyAyAbhAsopabR^iMhitatvaM, prativedAntaM ca sR^iShTyAdiprakriyAyA aviItaatvaM ityasyArthajAtasya pratipAdanAya dvitIyo.adhyAya Arabhyate | tatra prathamaM tAvat smR^itivirodham upanyasya pariharati -- 

smR^ityanavakAshadoShaprasaN^ga iti cen 
nAnyasmR^ityavakAshadoShaprasaN^gAt ||

yad uktaM brahmaiva sarvaj~naM jagataH kAraNam iti, tad ayuktam | kutaH? smR^ityanavakAshadoShaprasaN^gAt -- smR^itishca tantrAkhyA paramarShipraNItA shiShTaparigR^ihItA anyAshca tadanusAriNyaH smR^itayaH, tA evaM satyanavakAshAH prasajyeran | tAsu hyacetanaM pradhAnaM svatantraM jagataH kAraNam upanibadhyate | manvAdismR^itayaH tAvaccodanAlakShaNenAgnihotrAdinA dharmajAtenApekShitam arthaM samarpayantyaH sAvakAshA bhavanti -- asya varNasyAsmin kAle.anena vidhAnenopanayanam, IdR^ishashcAcAraH, itthaM vedAdhyayanam, itthaM samAvartanam, itthaM sahadharmacAriNIsaMyoga iti | tathA puruShArthAMshcaturvarNAshramadharmAn nAnAvidhAn vidadhati | naivaM kApilAdismR^itInAm anuShTheye viShaye avakAsho.asti | mokShasAdhanam eva hi samyagdarshanam adhikR^itya tAH praNItAH | yadi tatrApyanavakAshAH syuH, Anarthakyam evAsAM prasajyeta | tasmAt tadavirodhena vedAntA vyAkhyAtavyAH | 

kathaM punar IkShatyAdibhyo hetubhyo brahmaiva sarvaj~naM jagataH kAraNam ityavadhAritaH shrutyarthaH smR^ityanavakAshadoShaprasaN^gena punar AkShipyate? bhaved ayam anAkShepaH svatantrapraj~nAnAm | paratantrapraj~nAH tu prAyeNa janAH svAtantryeNa shrutyartham avadhArayitum ashaknuvantaH prakhyAtapraNetR^ikAsu smR^itiShvavalamberan | tadbalena ca shrutyarthaM pratipitseran | asmatkR^ite ca vyAkhyAne na vishvasyuH, bahumAnAt smR^itInAM praNetR^iShu | kapilaprabhR^itInAM cArShaM j~nAnam apratihataM smaryate | shrutishca bhavati -- 

R^iShiM prasUtaM kapilaM yaH tam agre
j~nAnair bibharti jAyamAnaM ca pashyet || [shve.u. 5.2] iti |

tasmAn naiShAM matam ayathArthaM shakyaM sambhAvayitum | tarkAvaShTAmbhena ca te.arthaM pratiShThApayanti | tasmAd api smR^itibalena vedAntA vyAkhyeyA iti punar AkShepaH || 

tasya samAdhiH --  nAnyasmR^ityanavakAshadoShaprasaN^gAt iti | yadi smR^ityanavakAshadoShaprasaN^geneshvarakAraNavAda AkShipyeta, evam apyanyA IshvarakAraNavAdinyaH smR^itayo.anavakAshAH prasajyeran | tA udAhariShyAmaH --  yat tat sUkShmam avij~neyam [ma.bhA. 12.342.30] iti paraM brahma prakR^itya, sa hyantarAtmA bhUtAnAM kShetraj~nashceti kathyate [ma.bhA. 12.342.31] iti coktvA, tasmAd avyaktam utpannaM triguNaM dvijasattama [ma.bhA. 12.342.32] ityAha | tathAnyatrApi avyaktaM puruShe brahman nirguNe sampralIyate [ma.bhA. 12.347.31] ityAha | 

atashca saMkShepam imaM shR^iNudhvaM
nArAyaNaH sarvam idaM purANaH | 
sa sargakAle ca karoti sargaM 
saMhArakAle ca tad atti bhUyaH || [ma.bhA. 12.307.115] iti purANe | 

bhagavadgItAsu ca -- ahaM kR^itsnasya jagataH prabhavaH pralayaH tathA [gItA 7.6] iti | paramAtmAnam eva ca prakR^ityApastambaH paThati --  tasmAt kAyAH prabhavanti sarve sa mUlaM shAshvatikaH sa nityaH [dha.sU. 1.8.23.2] iti | evam anekashaH smR^itiShvapIshvaraH kAraNatvenopAdAnatvena ca prakAshyate || 

smR^itibalena pratyavatiShThamAnasya smR^itibalenaivottaraM pravakShyAmItyato.ayam anyasmR^ityanavakAshadoShopanyAsaH | darshitaM tu shrutInAm IshvarakAraNavAdaM prati tAt paryam | vipratipattau ca smR^itInAm avashyakartavye.anyataraparigrahe.anyataraparityAge ca shrutyanusAriNyaH smR^itayaH pramANam | anapekShyA itarAH | tad uktaM pramANalakShaNe -- virodhe tu anapekShaM syAd asati hyanumAnam [jai.sU. 1.3.3] iti | na cAtIndriyAnarthAn shrutim antareNa kashcid upalabhata iti shakyaM sambhAvayitum, nimittAbhAvAt | shakyaM kapilAdInAM siddhAnAm apratihataj~nAnatvAd iti cet, na | siddher api sApekShatvAt | dharmAnuShThAnApekShA hi siddhiH, sa ca dharmashcodanAlakShaNaH | tatashca pUrvasiddhAyAshcodanAyA artho na pashcimasiddhapuruShavacanavashenAtishaN^kituM shakyate | siddhavyapAshrayakalpanAyAm api bahutvAt siddhAnAM pradarshitena prakAreNa smR^itivipratipattau satyAM na shrutivyapAshrayAd anyan nirNayakAraNam asti | paratantrapraj~nasyApi nAkasmAt smR^itivisheShaviShayaH pakShapAto yuktaH, kasyacit kvacit pakShapAte sati puruSham ativaishvarUpyeNa tattvAvyavasthAnaprasaN^gAt | tasmAt tasyApi smR^itivipratipattyupanyAsena shrutyanusArAnanusAraviShayavivecanena ca sanmArge praj~nA saMgrahaNIyA | 

yA tu shrutiH kapilasya j~nAnAtishayaM pradarshayantI, pradarshitA na tayA shrutiviruddham api kApilaM mataM shraddhAtuM shakyam, kapilam iti shrutisAmAnyamAtratvAt, anyasya ca kapilasya sagaraputrANAM prataptur vAsudevanAmnaH smaraNAt, anyArthadarshanasya ca prAptirahitasyAsAdhakatvAt | bhavati cAnyA manor mAhAtmyaM prakhyApayantI shrutiH --  yad vai kiM ca manur avadat tadbheShajam [tai.saM. 2.2.10.2] iti | manunA ca, 

sarvabhUteShu cAtmAnaM sarvabhUtAni cAtmani | 
sampashyann AtmayAjI vai svArAjyam adhigacchati || [manu 12.91] iti |

sarvAtmatvadarshanaM prashaMsatA kApilaM mataM nindyata iti gamyate | kapilo hi na sarvAtmatvadarshanam anumanyate, AtmabhedAbhyupagamAt | mahAbhArate.api ca -- bahavaH puruShA brahmann utAho eka eva tu [ma.bhA. 12.360.1] iti vicArya, bahavaH puruShA rAjan sAN^khyayogavicAriNAm [ma.bhA. 12.360.2] iti parapakSham upanyasya tadvyudAsena -- 

bahUnAM puruShANAM hi yathaikA yonir ucyate | 
tathA taM puruShaM vishvam AkhyAsyAmi guNAdhikam || [ma.bhA. 12.360.3] ityupakramya, 

mamAntarAtmA tava ca ye cAnye dehisaMj~nitAH | 
sarveShAM sAkShibhUto.asau na grAhyaH kenacit kvacit || 
vishvamUrdhA vishvabhujo vishvapAdAkShinAsikaH | 
ekashcarati bhUteShu svairacArI yathAsukham || [ma.bhA. 12.360.45]

iti sarvAtmataiva nirdhAritA | shrutishca sarvAtmatAyAM bhavati -- 

yasmin sarvANi bhUtAnyAtmaivAbhUd vijAnataH | 
tatra ko mohaH kaH shoka ekatvam anupashyataH || [Isho. 7] ityevaMvidhA | 

atashca siddham AtmabhedakalpanayApi kApilasya tantrasya vedaviruddhatvaM vedAnusArimanuvacanaviruddhatvaM ca, na kevalaM svatantraprakR^itikalpanayaiveti | vedasya hi nirapekShaM svArthe prAmANyam, raveH iva rUpaviShaye | puruShavacasAM tu mUlAntarApekShaM vaktR^ismR^itivyavahitaM ceti viprakarShaH | tasmAd vedaviruddhA viShaye smR^ityanavakAshadoShaprasaN^go na doShaH ||1 || 

|| 2.1.2 ||

kutashca smR^ityanavakAshadoShaprasaN^go na doShaH? -- 

itareShAM cAnupalabdheH ||

pradhAnAd itarANi yAni pradhAnapariNAmatvena smR^itau kalpitAni mahadAdIni, na tAni vede loke copalabhyante | bhUtendriyANi tAval lokavedaprasiddhatvAcchakyante smartum | alokavedaprasiddhatvAt tu mahadAdInAM ShaShThasyevendriyArthasya na smR^itir avakalpate | yad api kvacit tatparam iva shravaNam avabhAsate, tad apyatatparaM vyAkhyAtam -- AnumAnikam apyekeShAm [ve.sU. 1.4.1] ityatra | kAryasmR^iter aprAmANyAt kAraNasmR^iter apyaprAmANyaM yuktam ityabhiprAyaH | tasmAd api na smR^ityanavakAshadoShaprasaN^go doShaH | tarkAvaShTambhaM, tu na vilakShaNatvAt [ve.sU. 2.1.4] ityArabhyonmathiShyati ||2||

|| iti smR^ityadhikaraNam ||

 -- o)0(o -- 

2. yogapratyuktyadhikaraNam
