|| 2.1.3 ||

etena yogaH pratyuktaH || 

etena sAN^khyasmR^itipratyAkhyAnena, yogasmR^itir api pratyAkhyAtA draShTavyetyatidishati | tatrApi shrutivirodhena pradhAnaM svatantram eva kAraNam, mahadAdIni ca kAryANyalokavedaprasiddhAni kalpyante | 

nanv evaM sati samAnanyAyatvAt pUrveNaivaitadgatam | kim arthaM punar atidishyate? asti hyatrAbhyadhikAshaN^kA -- samyagdarshanAbhyupAyo hi yogo vede vihitaH -- shrotavyo mantavyo nididhyAsitavyaH [bR^i.A.u 2.4.5] iti | trirunnataM sthApya samaM sharIram [shve.u. 2.8] ityAdinA cAsanAdikalpanApuraHsaraM bahuprapaJNcaM yogavidhAnaM shvetAshvataropaniShadi dR^ishyate | liN^gAni ca vaidikAni yogaviShayANi sahasrasha upalabhyante -- tAM yogam iti manyante sthirAm indriyadhAraNAm [kA. 2.3.11] iti, vidyAm etAM yogavidhiM ca kR^itsnam iti caivamAdIni | yogashAstre.api -- atha taddarshanAbhyupAyo yogaH iti samyagdarshanAbhyupAyatvenaiva yogo.aN^gIkriyate | ataH sampratipannArthaikadeshatvAd aShTakAdismR^itivad yogasmR^itir apyanapavadanIyA bhaviShyatIti -- iyam apyadhikA shaN^kAtideshena nivartyate, arthaikadeshasampratipattAvapyarthaikadeshavipratipatteH pUrvoktAyA darshanAt | 

satIShvapyadhyAtmaviShayAsu bahvIShu smR^itiShu sAN^khyayogasmR^ityor eva nirAkaraNe yatnaH kR^itaH | sAN^khyayogau hi paramapuruShArthasAdhanatvena loke prakhyAtau, shiShTaishca parigR^ihItau, liN^gena ca shrautenopabR^iMhitau --  tatkAraNaM sAN^khyayogAbhipannaM j~nAtvA devaM mucyate sarvapAshaiH [shve.u. 6.13] iti | nirAkaraNaM tu -- na sAN^khyasmR^itij~nAnena vedanirapekSheNa yogamArgeNa vA niHshreyasam adhigamyata iti | shrutir hi vaidikAd Atmaikatvavij~nAnAd anyan niHshreyasasAdhanaM vArayati -- tam eva viditvAt imR^ityum eti nAnyaH panthA vidyate.ayanAya [shve.u. 3.8] iti | dvaitino hi te sAN^khyA yogAshca nAtmaikatvadarshinaH | yat tu darshanam uktam, tatkAraNaM sAN^khyayogAbhipannam [shve.u. 6.13] iti, vaidikam eva tatra j~nAnaM dhyAnaM ca sAN^khyayogashabdAbhyAm abhilapyete pratyAsatteH ityavagantavyam | yena tu aMshena na virudhyete, teneShTam eva sAN^khyayogasmR^ityoH sAvakAshatvam | tad yathA -- asaN^go hyayaM puruShaH [bR^i.A.u 4.3.16] ityevam Adishrutiprasiddham eva puruShasya vishuddhatvaM nirguNapuruShanirUpaNena sAN^khyair abhyupagamyate | tathA ca yogair api -- atha parivrAD vivarNavAsA muNDo.aparigrahaH [jA.u. 5] ityevam Adi shrutiprasiddham eva nivR^ittiniShThatvaM pravrajyAdyupadeshenAnugamyate | 

etena sarvANi tarkasmaraNAni prativaktavyAni | tAnyapi tarkopapattibhyAM tattvaj~nAnAyopakurvantIti cet, upakurvantu nAma | tattvaj~nAnaM tu vedAntavAkyebhya eva bhavati -- nAvedavin manute taM bR^ihantam taM tu aupaniShadaM puruShaM pR^icchAmi [bR^i.A.u. 3.9.26] ityevam Adi shrutibhyaH ||3||

|| iti yogapratyuktyadhikaraNam ||

 -- o)0(o -- 
3. vilakShaNatvAdhikaraNam
|| 2.1.4 || 

na vilakShaNatvAd asya tathAtvaM ca shabdAt || 

brahmAsya jagato nimittakAraNaM prakR^itishcetyasya pakShasyAkShepaH smR^itinimittaH parihR^itaH | tarkanimitta idAnIm AkShepaH parihriyate | kutaH punar asminn avadhArite AgamArthe tarkanimittasyAkShepasyAvakAshaH? 

nanu dharma iva brahmaNyapyanapekSha Agamo bhavitum arhati | bhaved ayam avaShTambho yadi pramANAntarAn avagAhya AgamamAtraprameyo.ayam arthaH syAd anuShTheyarUpa iva dharmaH | pariniShpannarUpaM tu brahmAvagamyate | pariniShpanne ca vastuni pramANAntarANAm astyavakAsho yathA pR^ithivyAdiShu | yathA ca shrutInAM parasparavirodhe satyekavashenetarA nIyante, evaM pramANAntaravirodhe.api tadvashenaiva shrutir nIyeta | dR^iShTasAdharmyeNa cAdR^iShTam arthaM samarpayantI yuktir anubhavasya saMnikR^iShyate, viprakR^iShyate tu shrutiH, aitihyamAtreNa svArthAbhidhAnAt | anubhavAvasAnaM ca brahmavij~nAnam avidyAyA nivartakaM mokShasAdhanaM ca dR^iShTaphalatayeShyate | shrutir api -- shrotavyo mantavyaH [bR^i.A.u 2.4.5] iti shravaNavyatirekeNa mananaM vidadhatI tarkam apyatrAdR^itavyaM darshayati | ataH tarkanimittaH punar AkShepaH kriyate na vilakShaNatvAd asya iti || 

yad uktam cetanaM brahma jagataH kAraNaM prakR^itiH iti, tan nopapadyate | kasmAt ? vilakShaNatvAd asya vikArasya prakR^ityAH -- idaM hi brahmakAryatvenAbhipreyamANaM jagad brahmavilakShaNam acetanam ashuddhaM ca dR^ishyate | brahma ca jagadvilakShaNaM cetanaM shuddhaM ca shrUyate | na ca vilakShaNatve prakR^itivikArabhAvo dR^iShTAH | na hi rucakAdayo vikArA mR^itprakR^itikA bhavanti, sharAvAdayo vA suvarNaprakR^itikAH | mR^idaiva tu mR^idanvitA vikArAH prakriyante, suvarNena ca suvarNAnvitAH | tathedam api jagadacetanaM sukhadukhamohAnvitaM sat acetanasyaiva sukhaduHkhamohAtmakasya kAraNasya kAryaM bhavitum arhati, na vilakShaNasya brahmaNaH | brahmavilakShaNatvaM cAsya jagato.ashuddhyacetanatvadarshanAd avagantavyam -- ashuddhaM hIdaM jagat sukhaduHkhamohAtmakatayA pratIyate, prItiparitApaviShAdAdihetutvAt svarganarakAdyuccAvacaprapaJNcatvAcca | acetanaM cedaM jagat cetanaM prati kAryakAraNabhAvenopakaraNabhAvopagamAt | na hi sAmye satyupakAryopakArakabhAvo bhavati | na hi pradIpau parasparasyopakurutaH | 

nanu cetanam api kAryakAraNaM svAmibhR^ityanyAyena bhoktur upakariShyati | na, svAmibhR^ityayor apyacetanAMshasyaiva cetanaM pratyupakArakatvAt | yo hyekasya cetanasya parigraho buddhyAdir acetanabhAgaH sa evAnyasya cetanasyopakaroti, na tu svayam eva cetanashcetanAntarasyopakarotyapakaroti vA | niratishayA hyakartArashcetanA iti sAN^khyA manyante | tasmAd acetanaM kAryakAraNam | na ca kAShThaloShTAdInAM cetanatve kiMcit pramANam asti | prasiddhashcAyaM cetanAcetanavibhAgo loke | tasmAd brahmavilakShaNatvAn nedaM jagat tatprakR^itikam | 

yo.api kashcid AcakShIta -- shrutyA jagatashcetanaprakR^itikatAm, tadbalenaiva samastaM jagaccetanam avagamiShyAmi, prakR^itirUpasya vikAre.anvayadarshanAt | avibhAvanaM tu caitanyasya pariNAmavisheShAd bhaviShyati | yathA spaShTacaitanyAnAm apyAtmanAM svApamUrcchAdyavasthAsu caitanyaM na vibhAvyate, evaM kAShThaloShTAdInAm api caitanyaM na vibhAvayiShyate | etasmAd eva ca vibhAvitatvAvibhAvitatvakR^itAd visheShAd rUpAdibhAvAbhAvAbhyAM ca kAryakAraNAnAm AtmanAM ca cetanatvAvisheShe.api guNapradhAnabhAvo na virotsyate | yathA ca pArthivatvAvisheShe.api mAMsasUpaudanAdInAM pratyAtmavartino visheShAt parasparopakAritvaM bhavati, evam ihApi bhaviShyati | pravibhAgaprasiddhir apyata eva na virotsyata iti -- tenApi kathaMciccetanatvAcetanatvalakShaNaM vilakShaNatvaM parihriyeta | shuddhyashuddhitvalakShaNaM tu vilakShaNatvaM naiva parihriyate | 

na cetarad api vilakShaNatvaM parihartuM shakyata ityAha -- tathAtvaM ca shabdAd iti | anavagamyamAnam eva hIdaM loke samastasya vastunashcetanatvaM cetanaprakR^itikatvashravaNAcchabdasharaNatayA kevalayotprekSheta | tacca shabdenaiva virudhyate, yataH shabdAd api tathAtvam avagamyate | tathAtvam iti prakR^itivilakShaNatvaM kathayati | shabda eva vij~nAnaM cAvij~nAnaM ca [tai.u. 2.6] iti kasyacid vibhAgasyAcetanatAM shrAvayaMshcetanAd brahmaNo vilakShaNam acetanaM jagacchrAvayati ||4|| 

|| 2.1.5 ||

nanu cetanatvam api kvacid acetanatvAbhimatAnAM bhUtendriyANAM shrUyate, yathA -- mR^id abravIt Apo.abruvan [sha.brA. 6.1.3.2,4] iti tat teja aikShata tA Apa aikShanta [chA.u. 6.2.34] iti caivamAdyA bhUtaviShayA cetanatvashrutiH | indriyaviShayA api -- te heme prANA ahaMshreyase vivadamAnA brahma jagmuH [bR^i.A.u 6.1.7] iti, te ha vAcam UcuH tvaM na udgAyeti [bR^i.A.u 1.3.2] ityevamAdyendriyaviShayeti | ata uttaraM paThati -- 

abhimAnivyapadeshaH tu visheShAnugatibhyAm ||

tushabda AshaN^kAm apanudati | na khalu mR^id abravIt ityevaMjAtIyakayA shrutyA bhUtendriyANAM cetanatvam AshaN^kanIyam, yato.abhimAnivyapadesha eShaH | mR^idAdyabhimAninyo vAgAdyabhimAninyashca cetanAdevatA vadanasaMvadanAdiShu cetanociteShu vyavahAreShu vyapadishyante, na bhUtendriyamAtram | kasmAt? visheShAnugatibhyAm | visheSho hi bhoktNAM bhUtendriyANAM ca cetanAcetanapravibhAgalakShaNaH prAgabhihitaH | sarvacetanatAyAM cAsau nopapadyeta | 

api ca kauShItakinaH prANasaMvAde karaNamAtrAshaN^kAvinivR^ittaye.adhiShThAtR^icetanaparigrahAya devatAshabdena vishiMShanti -- etA ha vai devatA ahaMshreyase vivadamAnAH [kau.u. 2.14] iti, tA vA etAH sarvA devatAH prANe niHshreyasaM viditvA [kau.u. 2.14] iti ca | anugatAshca sarvatrAbhimAninyashcetanA devatA mantrArthavAdetihAsapurANAdibhyo.avagamyante -- agnir vAg bhUtvA mukhaM prAvishat [ai.A. 2.4.24] ityevamAdikA ca shrutiH karaNeShvanugrAhikAM devatAm anugatAM darshayati | prANasaMvAdavAkyasheShe ca -- te ha prANAH prajApatiM pitaram etyocuH [chA.u. 5.1.7] iti shreShThatvanirdhAraNAya prajApatigamanam, tadvacanAccaikaikotkramaNenAnvayavyatirekAbhyAM prANashraiShThyapratipattiH, tasmai baliharaNam [bR^i.A.u 6.1.13] iti caivaMjAtIyako.asmadAdiShviva vyavahAro.anugamyamAno.abhimAnivyapadeshaM draDhayati | tat teja aikShata [chA.u. 6.2.3] ityapi parasyA eva devatAyA adhiShThAtryAH svavikAreShvanugatAyA iyam IkShA vyapadishyata iti draShTavyam ||5|| 

|| 2.1.6 || 

tasmAd vilakShaNam evedaM brahmaNo jagat | vilakShaNatvAcca na brahmaprakR^itikam ityAkShipte, pratividhatte -- 

dR^ishyate tu ||

tushabdaH pakShaM vyAvartayati | yad uktam vilakShaNatvAn nedaM jagad brahmaprakR^itikam iti, nAyam ekAntaH | dR^ishyate hi loke -- cetanatvena prasiddhebhyaH puruShAdibhyo vilakShaNAnAM keshanakhAdInAm utpattiH, acetanatvena ca prasiddhebhyo gomayAdibhyo vR^ishcikAdInAm | 

nanvacetanAnyeva puruShAdisharIrANyacetanAnAM keshanakhAdInAM kAraNAni, acetanAnyeva ca vR^ishcikAdisharIrANyacetanAnAM gomayAdInAM kAryANIti | ucyate -- evam api kiJNcid acetanaM cetanasyAyatanabhAvam upagacchati kiMcin netyastyeva vailakShaNyam | mahAMshcAyaM pAriNAmikaH svabhAvaviprakarShaH puruShAdInAM keshanakhAdInAM ca rUpAdibhedAt, tathA gomayAdInAM vR^ishcikAdInAM ca | atyantasArUpye ca prakR^itivikArabhAva eva pralIyeta | athocyeta -- asti kashcit pArthivatvAdisvabhAvaH puruShAdInAM keshanakhAdiShvanuvartamAno gomayAdInAM ca vR^ishcikAdiShviti | brahmaNo.api tarhi sattAlakShaNaH svabhAva AkAshAdiShvanuvartamAno dR^ishyate | vilakShaNatvena ca kAraNena brahmaprakR^itikatvaM jagato dUShayatA kim asheShasya brahmasvabhAvasyAnanuvartanaM vilakShaNatvam abhipreyate, uta yasya kasyacit? atha caitanyasyeti vaktavyam -- prathame vikalpe samastaprakR^itivikArabhAvocchedaprasaN^gaH | na hyasatyatishaye prakR^itivikArabhAva iti bhavati | dvitIye cAsiddhatvam | dR^ishyate hi sattAlakShaNo brahmasvabhAva AkAshAdiShvanuvartamAna ityuktam | tR^itIye tu dR^iShTAntAbhAvaH | kiM hi yaccaitanyenAnanvitaM tad abrahmaprakR^itikaM dR^iShTam iti brahmakAraNavAdinaM pratyudAhriyeta, samastasyAsya vastujAtasya brahmaprakR^itikatvAbhyupagamAt | AgamavirodhaH tu prasiddha eva, cetanaM brahma jagataH kAraNaM prakR^itishcetyAgamatAt paryasya prasAdhitatvAt | 

yat tUktaM pariniShpannatvAd brahmaNi pramANAntarANi sambhaveyuH iti, tad api manorathamAtram | rUpAdyabhAvAd dhi nAyam arthaH pratyakShasya gocaraH | liN^gAdyabhAvAcca nAnumAnAdInAm | AgamamAtrasamadhigamya eva tu ayam artho dharmavat | tathA ca shrutiH -- naiShA tarkeNa matir ApaneyA proktAnyenaiva suj~nAnAya preShTha [ka.u. 1.2.9] iti | ko addhA veda ka iha pravocat | iyaM visR^iShTir yata AbabhUva [R^i.ve. 10.129.67] iti caite R^icau nijasiddhAnAm apIshvarANAM durbodhatAM jagatkAraNasya darshayataH | smR^itir api bhavati -- acintyAH khalu ye bhAvA na tAMH tarkeNa yojayet iti, avyakto.ayam acintyo.ayam avikAryo.ayam ucyate [gItA 2.25] iti ca, 

na me viduH suragaNAH prabhavaM na maharShayaH | 
aham Adir hi devAnAM maharShINAM ca sarvashaH | [gItA 10.2] iti caivaMjAtIyakA | 

yad api shravaNavyatirekeNa mananaM vidadhacchabda eva tarkam apyAdartavyaM darshayatItyuktam, nAnena miSheNa shuShkatarkasyAtrAtmalAbhaH sambhavati | shrutyanugR^ihIta eva hyatra tarko.anubhavAN^gatvenAshrIyate -- svapnAntabuddhAntayor ubhayoH itaretaravyabhicArAd Atmano.ananvAgatatvam, samprasAde ca prapaJNcaparityAgena sadAtmanA sampatter niShprapaJNcasadAtmakatvam, prapaJNcasya brahmaprabhavatvAt kAryakAraNAnanyatvanyAyena brahmAvyatireka ityevaMjAtIyakaH | tarkApratiShThAnAd [ve.sU. 2.1.11] iti ca kevalasya tarkasya vipralambhakatvaM darshayiShyati | 

yo.api cetanakAraNashravaNabalenaiva samastasya jagatashcetanatAm utprekSheta, tasyApi vij~nAnaM cAvij~nAnaM [tai.u. 2.6] ca iti cetanAcetanavibhAgashravaNaM vibhAvanAvibhAvanAbhyAM caitanyasya shakyata eva yojayitum | parasyaiva tvidam api vibhAgashravaNaM na yujyate | katham? paramakAraNasya hyatra samastajagadAtmanA samavasthAnaM shrAvyate -- vij~nAnaM cAvij~nAnaM cAbhavat [tai.u. 2.6] iti | tatra yathA cetanasyAcetanabhAvo nopapadyate vilakShaNatvAt, evam acetanasyApi cetanabhAvo nopapadyate | pratyuktatvAt tu vilakShaNatvasya yathA shrutyaiva cetanaM kAraNaM grahItavyaM bhavati ||6||

|| 2.1.7 || 

asad iti cen, na, pratiShedhamAtratvAt || 

yadi cetanaM shuddhaM shabdAdihInaM ca brahma tadviparItasyAcetanasyAshuddhasya shabdAdimatashca kAryasya kAraNam iShyeta, asat tarhi kAryaM prAgutpatteH iti prasajyeta | aniShTaM caitat satkAryavAdinaH taveti cet -- naiSha doShaH, pratiShedhamAtratvAt | pratiShedhamAtraM hIdam | nAsya pratiShedhasya pratiShedhyam asti | na hyayaM pratiShedhaH prAgutpatteH sattvaM kAryasya pratiShedhaM shaknoti | katham? yathaiva hIdAnIm apIdaM kAryaM kAraNAtmanA sat, evaM prAgutpatter apIti gamyate | na hIdAnIm apIdaM kAryaM kAraNAtmAnam antareNa svatantram evAsti -- sarvaM taM parAdAdyo.anyatrAtmanaH sarvaM veda [bR^i.A.u 2.4.6] ityAdi shravaNAt | kAraNAtmanA tu sattvaM kAryasya prAgutpatter avishiShTam | 

nanu shabdAdihInaM brahma jagataH kAraNam -- bADham -- na tu shabdAdimatkAryaM kAraNAtmanA hInaM prAgutpatteH idAnIM vA asti | tena na shakyate vaktuM prAgutpatter asatkAryam iti | vistareNa caitat kAryakAraNAnanyatvavAde [ve.sU. 2.1.14] vakShyAmaH ||7||

|| 2.1.8 || 

apItau tadvat prasaN^gAd asamaJNjasam || 

atrAha -- yadi sthaulyasAvayavattvAcetanatvaparicchinnatvAshuddhyAdidharmakaM kAryaM brahmakAraNakam abhyupagamyeta, tadApItau pralaye pratisaMsR^ijyamAnaM kAryaM kAraNAvibhAgam ApadyamAnaM kAraNam AtmIyena dharmeNa dUShayed iti -- apItau kAraNasyApi brahmaNaH kAryasyevAshuddhyAdirUpatAprasaN^gAt | sarvaj~naM brahma jagataH kAraNam ityasamaJNjasam idam aupaniShadaM darshanam | api ca samastasya vibhAgasyAvibhAgaprApteH punar utpattau niyamakAraNAbhAvAd bhoktR^ibhogyAdivibhAgenotpattir na prApnotItyasamaJNjasam | api ca bhoktNAM pareNa brahmaNA avibhAgaM gatAnAM karmAdinimittapralaye.api punar utpattAvabhyupagamyamAnAyAM muktAnAm api punar utpattiprasaN^gAd asamaJNjasam | athedaM jagad apItAvapi vibhaktam eva pareNa brahmaNAvatiShTheta, evam apyapItishca na sambhavati kAraNAvyatiriktaM ca kAryaM na sambhavatItyasamaJNjasam eveti ||8|| 

|| 2.1.9 ||

atrocyate -- 

na tu dR^iShTAntabhAvAt || 

naivAsmadIye darshane kiJNcid asAmaJNjasyam asti | yat tAvad abhihitam -- kAraNam api gacchatkAryaM kAraNam AtmIyena dharmeNa dUShayed iti, na tad dUShaNam | kasmAt? dR^iShTAntabhAvAt -- santi hi dR^iShTAntAH, yathA kAraNam api gacchat kAryaM kAraNam AtmIyena dharmeNa na dUShayati | tad yathA -- sharAvAdayo mR^itprakR^itikA vikArA vibhAgAvasthAyAm uccAvacamadhyamaprabhedAH santaH, punaH prakR^itim api gacchanto na tAm AtmIyena dharmeNa saMsR^ijanti | rucakAdayashca suvarNavikArA apItau na punaH suvarNam AtmIyena dharmeNa saMsR^ijanti | pR^ithivIvikArashcaturvidho bhUtagrAmo na pR^ithivIm apItAvatmIyena dharmeNa saMsR^ijati | tu atpakShasya tu na kashcid dR^iShTAnto.asti | apItir eva hi na sambhavet, yadi kAraNe kAryaM svadharmeNaivAvatiShTheta | ananyatve.api kAryakAraNayoH, kAryasya kAraNAtmatvam, na tu kAraNasya kAryAtmatvam -- ArambhaNashabdAdibhyaH ityatra vakShyAmaH | atyalpaM cedam ucyate -- kAryam apItAvatmIyena dharmeNa kAraNaM saMsR^ijed iti | sthitAvapi hi samAno.ayaM prasaN^gaH, kAryakAraNayor ananyatvAbhyupagamAt | idaM sarvaM yad ayam AtmA [bR^i.A.u. 2.4.6], AtmaivedaM sarvam [chA.u. 7.25.2], brahmaivedam amR^itaM purastAt [mu.u. 2.2.11], sarvaM khalvidaM brahma [chA.u. 3.14.1] ityevamAdyAbhir hi shrutibhir avisheSheNa triShvapi kAleShu kAryasya kAraNAd ananyatvaM shrAvyate | tatra yaH parihAraH kAryasya taddharmANAM cAvidyAdhyAropitatvAn na taiH kAraNaM saMsR^ijyata iti, apItAvapi sa samAnaH | 

asti cAyam aparo dR^iShTAntaH -- yathA svayaM prasAritayA mAyayA mAyAvI triShvapi kAleShu na saMspR^ishyate, avastutvAt | evaM paramAtmApi saMsAramAyayA na saMspR^ishyata iti | yathA ca svapnadR^ig ekaH svapnadarshanamAyayA na saMspR^ishyate, prabodhasamprasAdayor ananvAgatatvAt | evam avasthAtrayasAkShyeko.avyabhicAryavasthAtrayeNa vyabhicAriNA na saMspR^ishyate | mAyAmAtraM hyetat, yat paramAtmano.avasthAtrayAtmanAvabhAsanam, rajjvA iva sarpAdibhAveneti | atroktaM vedAntArthasampradAyavidbhir AcAryaiH -- 

anAdimAyayA supto yadA jIvaH prabudhyate | 
ajam anidram asvapnam advaitaM budhyate tadA || [gau.kA.  1.16] iti | 

tatra yad uktam apItau kAraNasyApi kAryasyeva sthaulyAdidoShaprasaN^ga iti, etad ayuktam | yat punar etad uktam -- samastasya vibhAgasyAvibhAgaprApteH punar vibhAgenotpattau niyamakAraNaM nopapadyata iti, ayam apyadoShaH, dR^iShTAntabhAvAd eva | yathA hi suShuptisamAdhyAdAvapi satyAM svAbhAvikyAm avibhAgaprAptau mithyAj~nAnasyAnapoditatvAt pUrvavat punaH prabodhe vibhAgo bhavati, evam ihApi bhaviShyati | shrutishcAtra bhavati -- 

imAH sarvAH prajAH sati sampadya na viduH sati sampadyAmaha [chA.u. 6.9.2] iti, ta iha vyAghro vA siMho vA vR^iko vA varAho vA kITo vA pataN^go vA daMsho vA mashako vA yad yad bhavanti tadA bhavanti [chA.u. 6.9.3] iti | 

yathA hyavibhAge.api paramAtmani mithyAj~nAnapratibaddho vibhAgavyavahAraH svapnavad avyAhataH sthitau dR^ishyate, evam apItAvapi mithyAj~nAnapratibaddhaiva vibhAgashaktir anumAsyate | etena muktAnAM punar utpattiprasaN^gaH pratyuktaH, samyagj~nAnena mithyAj~nAnasyApoditatvAt | yaH punar ayam ante.aparo vikalpa utprekShitaH -- athedaM jagadapItAvapi vibhaktam eva pareNa brahmaNAvatiShTheteti, so.apyanabhyupagamAd eva pratiShiddhaH | tasmAt samaJNjasam idam aupaniShadaM darshanam ||9||

|| 2.1.10 ||

svapakShadoShAcca ||

svapakShe caite prativAdinaH sAdhAraNA doShAH prAduHShyuH | katham ityucyate -- yat tAvad abhihitam, vilakShaNatvAn nedaM jagad brahmaprakR^itikam iti, pradhAnaprakR^itikatAyAm api samAnam etat, shabdAdihInAt pradhAnAcchabdAdimato jagata utpattyabhyupagamAt | ata eva ca vilakShaNakAryotpattyabhyupagamAt samAnaH prAgutpatter asatkAryavAdaprasaN^gaH | tathApItau kAryasya kAraNAvibhAgAbhyupagamAt tadvat prasaN^go.api samAnaH | tathA mR^iditasarvavisheSheShu vikAreShvapItAvavibhAgAtmatAM gateShu, idam asya puruShasyopAdAnam idam asyeti prAkpralayAt prati puruShaM ye niyatA bhedAH, na te tathaiva punar utpattau niyantuM shakyante, kAraNAbhAvAt | vinaiva ca kAraNena niyame.abhyupagamyamAne kAraNAbhAvasAmyAn muktAnAm api punar bandhaprasaN^gaH | 

atha kecid bhedA apItAvavibhAgam Apadyante, kecin neti cet -- ye nApadyante, teShAM pradhAnakAryatvaM na prApnoti | ityevam ete doShAH sAdhAraNatvAn nAnyatarasmin pakShe codayitavyA bhavantIti -- adoShatAm evaiShAM draDhayati --  avashyAshrayitavyatvAt ||10||

|| 2.1.11 ||

tarkApratiShThAnAd apy  anyathA.anumeyam iti ced 
evam apyavimokShaprasaN^gaH || 

itashca nAgamagamye.arthe kevalena tarkeNa pratyavasthAtavyam | yasmAn nirAgamAH puruShotprekShAmAtranibandhanAH tarkA apratiShThitA bhavanti, utprekShAyA niraN^kushatvAt | tathA hi -- kaishcid abhiyuktair yatnenotprekShitAH tarkA abhiyuktatarair anyair AbhAsyamAnA dR^ishyante | tair apyutprekShitAH santaH tato.anyair AbhAsyanta iti na pratiShThitatvaM tarkANAM shakyam Ashrayitum, puruShamativairUpyAt | 

atha kasyacit prasiddhamAhAtmyasya kapilasya anyasya vA saMmataH tarkaH pratiShThita ityAshrIyeta -- evam apyapratiShThitatvam eva, prasiddhamAhAtmyAbhimatAnAm api tIrthakarANAM kapilakaNabhukprabhR^itInAM parasparavipratipattidarshanAt | 

athocyeta -- anyathA vayam anumAsyAmahe, yathA nApratiShThAdoSho bhaviShyati | na hi pratiShThitaH tarka eva nAstIti shakyate vaktum | etad api hi tarkANAm apratiShThitatvaM tarkeNaiva pratiShThApyate, keShAMcit tarkANAm apratiShThitatvadarshanenAnyeShAm api tajjAtIyakAnAM tarkANAm apratiShThitatvakalpanAt | sarvatarkApratiShThAyAM ca lokavyavahArocchedaprasaN^gaH | atItavartamAnAdhvasAmyena hyanAgate.apyadhvani sukhaduHkhaprAptiparihArAya pravartamAno loko dR^ishyate | shrutyarthavipratipattau cArthAbhAsanirAkaraNena samyagarthanirdhAraNaM tarkeNaiva vAkyavR^ittinirUpaNarUpeNa kriyate | manur api caivam eva manyate -- 
pratyakShamanumAnaM ca shAstraM ca vividhAgamam | 
trayaM suviditaM kAryaM dharmashuddhim abhIpsatA || iti | 
ArShaM dharmopadeshaM ca vedashAstrAvirodhinA | yaH tarkeNAnusandhatte sa dharmaM veda netaraH iti ca bruvan | ayam eva ca tarkasyAlaMkAraH -- yad apratiShThitatvaM nAma | evaM hi sAvadyatarkaparityAgena niravadyaH tarkaH pratipattavyo bhavati | na hi pUrvajo mUDha AsId ityAtmanApi mUDhena bhavitavyam iti kiJNcid asti pramANam | tasmAn na tarkApratiShThAnaM doSha iti cet -- evam apyavimokShaprasaN^gaH | yadyapi kvacid viShaye tarkasya pratiShThitatvam upalakShyate, tathApi prakR^ite tAvad viShaye prasajyata evApratiShThitatvadoShAd anirmokShaH tarkasya | na hIdam atigambhIraM bhAvayAthAtmyaM muktinibandhanam Agamam antareNotprekShitum api shakyam | rUpAdyabhAvAd dhi nAyam arthaH pratyakShasya gocaraH, liN^gAdyabhAvAcca nAnumAnAdInAm iti cAvocAma | 
api ca samyagj~nAnAn mokSha iti sarveShAM mokShavAdinAm abhyupagamaH | tacca samyagj~nAnam ekarUpam, vastutantratvAt | ekarUpeNa hyavasthito yo.arthaH sa paramArthaH | loke tad viShayaM j~nAnaM samyagj~nAnam ityucyate -- yathAgnir uShNa iti | tatraivaM sati samyagj~nAne puruShANAM vipratipattir anupapannA | tarkaj~nAnAnAM tu anyonyavirodhAt prasiddhA vipratipattiH | yad dhi kenacit tArkikeNedam eva samyagj~nAnam iti pratiShThApitam, tad apareNa vyutthApyate | tenApi pratiShThApitaM tato.apareNa vyutthApyata iti ca prasiddhaM loke | katham ekarUpAnavasthitaviShayaM tarkaprabhavaM samyagj~nAnaM bhavet ? na ca pradhAnavAdI tarkavidAm uttama iti sarvaiH tArkikaiH parigR^ihItaH, yena tadIyaM mataM samyagj~nAnam iti pratipadyemahi | na ca shakyante.atItAn AgatavartamAnAH tArkikA ekasmin deshe kAle ca samAhartum, yena tanmatir ekarUpaikArthaviShayA samyaN^matiH iti syAt | vedasya tu nityatve vij~nAnotpattihetutve ca sati vyavasthitArthaviShayatvopapatteH, tajjanitasya j~nAnasya samyaktvam atItAn AgatavartamAnaiH sarvair api tArkikair apahnotum ashakyam | ataH siddham asyaivaupaniShadasya j~nAnasya samyagj~nAnatvam | ato.anyatra samyagj~nAnatvAnupapatteH saMsArAvimokSha eva prasajyeta | ata Agamavashena AgamAnusAritarkavashena ca cetanaM brahma jagataH kAraNaM prakR^itishceti sthitam ||11||

 -- o)0(o -- 

7. shiShTAparigrahAdhikaraNam
|| 2.1.12 || 

etena shiShTAparigrahA api vyAkhyAtAH || 

vaidikasya darshanasya pratyAsannatvAd gurutaratarkabalopetatvAd vedAnusAribhishca kaishcicchiShTaiH kenacid aMshena parigR^ihItatvAt pradhAnakAraNavAdaM tAvad vyapAshritya yaH tarkanimitta AkShepo vedAntavAkyeShUdbhAvitaH, sa parihR^itaH | idAnIm aNvAdivAdavyapAshrayeNApi kaishcin mandamatibhir vedAntavAkyeShu punaH tarkanimitta AkShepa AshaN^kyata ityataH pradhAnamallanibarhaNanyAyenAtidishati -- parigR^ihyanta iti parigrahAH | na parigrahAH aparigrahAH | shiShTAnAm aparigrahAH shiShTAparigrahAH | etena prakR^itena pradhAnakAraNavAdanirAkaraNakAraNena | shiShTair manuvyAsaprabhR^itibhiH kenacid apyaMshenAparigR^ihItA ye.aNvAdikAraNavAdAH, te.api pratiShiddhatayA vyAkhyAtA nirAkR^itA draShTavyAH | tulyatvAn nirAkaraNakAraNasya nAtra punar AshaN^kitavyaM kiJNcid asti | tulyam atrApi paramagambhIrasya jagatkAraNasya tarkAnavagAhyatvam, tarkasya cApratiShThitatvam, anyathAnumAne.apyavimokShaH, Agamavirodhashca -- ityevaMjAtIyakaM nirAkaraNakAraNam ||12||

 -- o)0(o -- 
8. bhoktrApattyadhikaraNam || 

|| 2.1.13 ||

bhoktrApatter avibhAgashcet syAl lokavat || 

anyathA punar brahmakAraNavAdaH tarkabalenaivAkShipyate | yadyapi shrutiH pramANaM svaviShaye bhavati, tathApi pramANAntareNa viShayApahAre.anyaparA bhavitum arhati, yathA mantrArthavAdau | tarko.api svaviShayAd anyatrApratiShThitaH syAt, yathA dharmAdharmayoH | kim ataH, yadyevam? ata idam ayuktam, yat pramANAntaraprasiddhArthabAdhanaM shruteH | kathaM punaH pramANAntaraprasiddho.arthaH shrutyA bAdhyata iti | 

atrocyate -- prasiddho hyayaM bhoktR^ibhogyavibhAgo loke -- bhoktA cetanaH shArIraH, bhogyAH shabdAdayo viShayA iti | yathA bhoktA devadattaH, bhogya odana iti | tasya ca vibhAgasyAbhAvaH prasajyeta, yadi bhoktA bhogyabhAvam Apadyeta bhogyaM vA bhoktR^ibhAvam Apadyeta | tayoshcetaretarabhAvApattiH paramakAraNAd brahmaNo.ananyatvAt prasajyeta | na cAsya prasiddhasya vibhAgasya bAdhanaM yuktam | yathA tu adyatve bhoktR^ibhogyayor vibhAgo dR^iShTAH, tathAtItAnAgatayor api kalpayitavyaH | tasmAt prasiddhasyAsya bhoktR^ibhogyavibhAgasyAbhAvaprasaN^gAd ayuktam idaM brahmakAraNatAvadhAraNam iti cet kashciccodayet, taM prati brUyAt -- syAl lokavad iti | upapadyata evAyam asmatpakShe.api vibhAgaH, evaM loke dR^iShTatvAt | tathA hi -- samudrAdudakAtmano.ananyatve.api tadvikArANAM phenavIcItaraN^gabudbudAdInAm itaretaravibhAga itaretarAsaMshleShAdilakShaNashca vyavahAra upalabhyate | na ca samudrAd udakAtmano.ananyatve.api tadvikArANAM phenataraN^gAdInAm itaretarabhAvApattir bhavati | na ca teShAm itaretarabhAvAnAm pattAvapi samudrAtmano.anyatvaM bhavati | evam ihApi -- na bhoktR^ibhogyayoH itaretarabhAvApattiH, na ca parasmAd brahmaNo.anyatvaM bhaviShyati | yadyapi bhoktA na brahmaNo vikAraH tat sR^iShTvA tad evAnuprAvishat iti sraShTair evAvikR^itasya kAryAnupraveshena bhoktR^itvashravaNAt, tathApi kAryam anupraviShTasyAstyupAdhinimitto vibhAga AkAshasyeva ghaTAdyupAdhinimittaH -- ityataH, paramakAraNAd brahmaNo.ananyatve.apyupapadyate bhoktR^ibhogyalakShaNo vibhAgaH samudrataraN^gAdinyAyenetyuktam ||13||

 -- o)0(o -- 
9. ArambhaNAdhikaraNam 

|| 2.1.14 || 

tad ananyatvam ArambhaNashabdAdibhyaH ||

abhyupagamya cemaM vyAvahArikaM bhoktR^ibhogyalakShaNaM vibhAgam syAl lokavat iti parihAro.abhihitaH | na tu ayaM vibhAgaH paramArthato.asti, yasmAt tayoH kAryakAraNayor ananyatvam avagamyate | kAryam AkAshAdikaM bahuprapaJNcaM jagat | kAraNaM paraM brahma | tasmAt kAraNAt paramArthato.ananyatvaM vyatirekeNAbhAvaH kAryasyAvagamyate | kutaH? ArambhaNashabdAdibhyaH | ArambhaNashabdaH tAvad ekavij~nAnena sarvavij~nAnaM pratij~nAya dR^iShTAntApekShAyAm ucyate -- yathA somyaikena mR^itpiNDena sarvaM mR^inmayaM vij~nAtaM syAd vAcArambhaNaM vikAro nAmadheyaM mR^ittiketyeva satyam [chA.u. 6.1.4] iti | etad uktaM bhavati -- ekena mR^itpiNDena paramArthato mR^idAtmanA vij~nAtena sarvaM mR^inmayaM ghaTasharAvodaJNcanAdikaM mR^idAtmakatvAvisheShAd vij~nAtaM bhavet | yato vAcArambhaNaM vikAro nAmadheyam -- vAcaiva kevalam astItyArabhyate -- vikAraH ghaTaH sharAva udaJNcanaM ceti | na tu vastuvR^ittena vikAro nAma kashcid asti | nAmadheyamAtraM hyetad anR^itam | mR^ittiketyeva satyam -- iti eSha brahmaNo dR^iShTAnta AmnAtaH | tatra shrutAd vAcArambhaNashabdAd dArShTAntike.api brahmavyatirekeNa kAryajAtasyAbhAva iti gamyate | punashca tejo.abannAnAM brahmakAryatAm uktvA tejobannakAryANAM tejobannavyatirekeNAbhAvaM bravIti apAgAd agner agnitvaM vAcArambhaNaM vikAro nAmadheyaM trINi rUpANItyeva satyam ityAdinA | ArambhaNashabdAdibhya ityAdi shabdAt aitadAtmyam idaM sarvaM tat satyaM sa AtmA tattvam asi idaM sarvaM yad ayam AtmA [bR^i.A.u. 2.4.6], brahmaivedaM sarvam AtmaivedaM sarvam [chA.u. 7.25.2], neha nAnAsti kiMcana ityevam AdyapyAtmaikatvapratipAdanaparaM vacanajAtam udAhartavyam | na cAnyathA ekavij~nAnena sarvavij~nAnaM sampadyate | tasmAd yathA ghaTakarakAdyAkAshAnAM mahAkAshAd ananyatvam, yathA ca mR^igatR^iShNikodakAdInAm USharAdibhyo.ananyatvam, dR^iShTanaShTasvarUpatvAt svarUpeNa tu anupAkhyatvAt | evam asya bhogyabhoktrAdiprapaJNcajAtasya brahmavyatirekeNAbhAva iti draShTavyam || 

nanvanekAtmakaM brahma | yathA vR^ikSho.anekashAkhaH, evam anekashaktipravR^ittiyuktaM brahma | ata ekatvaM nAnAtvaM cobhayam api satyam eva -- yathA vR^ikSha ityekatvaM shAkhA iti ca nAnAtvam | yathA ca samudrAtmanaikatvaM phenataraN^gAdyAtmanA nAnAtvam, yathA ca mR^idAtmanaikatvaM ghaTasharAvAdyAtmanA nAnAtvam | tatraikatvAMshena j~nAnAn mokShavyavahAraH setsyati | nAnAtvAMshena tu karmakANDAshrayau laukikavaidikavyavahArau setsyata iti | evaM ca mR^idAdidR^iShTAntA anurUpA bhaviShyantIti | naivaM syAt -- mR^ittiketyeva satyam iti prakR^itimAtrasya dR^iShTAnte satyatvAvadhAraNAt, vAcArambhaNashabdena ca vikArajAtasyAnR^itatvAbhidhAnAt, dArShTAntike.api aitadAtmyam idaM sarvaM tat satyam iti ca 
paramakAraNasyaivaikasya satyatvAvadhAraNAt, sa AtmA tattvam asi shvetaketo iti ca shArIrasya brahmabhAvopadeshAt | svayaM prasiddhaM hyetacchArIrasya brahmAtmatvam upadishyate, na yatnAntaraprasAdhyam | atashcedaM shAstrIyaM brahmAtmatvam abhyupagamyamAnaM svAbhAvikasya shArIrAtmatvasya bAdhakaM sampadyate, rajjvAdibuddhaya iva sarpAdibuddhInAm | bAdhite ca shArIrAtmatve tadAshrayaH samastaH svAbhAviko vyavahAro bAdhito bhavati, yat prasiddhaye nAnAtvAMsho.aparo brahmaNaH kalpyeta | darshayati ca -- yatra tu asya sarvam AtmaivAbhUt tat kena kaM pashyet [bR^i.A.u. 4.5.15] ityAdinA brahmAtmatvadarshinaM prati samastasya kriyAkArakaphalalakShaNasya vyavahArasyAbhAvam | na cAyaM vyavahArAbhAvo.a vasthAvisheShanibaddho.abhidhIyate iti yuktaM vaktum, tattvam asi iti brahmAtmabhAvasyAnavasthAvisheShanibandhanatvAt | taskaradR^iShTAntena cAnR^itAbhisandhasya bandhanaM satyAbhisandhasya ca mokShaM darshayan ekatvam evaikaM pAramArthikaM darshayati, mithyAj~nAnavijR^imbhitaM ca nAnAtvam | ubhayasatyatAyAM hi kathaM vyavahAragocaro.api jantur anR^itAbhisandha ityucyate? mR^ityoH sa mR^ityum Apnoti ya iha nAneva pashyati iti ca bhedadR^iShTim apavadann etad eva darshayati | na cAsmin darshane j~nAnAn mokSha ityupapadyate, samyagj~nAnApanodyasya kasyacin mithyAj~nAnasya saMsArakAraNatvenAnabhyupagamAt | ubhayasatyatAyAM hi katham ekatvaj~nAnena nAnAtvaj~nAnam apanudyata ityucyate | 

nanv ekatvaikAntAbhyupagame nAnAtvAbhAvAt pratyakShAdIni laukikAni pramANAni vyAhanyeran, nirviShayatvAt, sthANvAdiShviva puruShAdij~nAnAni | tathA vidhipratiShedhashAstram api bhedApekShatvAt tadabhAve vyAhanyeta | mokShashAstrasyApi shiShyashAsitrAdi bhedApekShatvAt tadabhAve vyAghAtaH syAt | kathaM cAnR^itena mokShashAstreNa pratipAditasyAtmaikatvasya satyatvam upapadyeteti | atrocyate -- naiSha doShaH, sarvavyavahArANAm eva prAgbrahmAtmatAvij~nAnAt satyatvopapatteH svapnavyavahArasyeva prAgbodhAt | yAvad dhi na satyAtmaikatvapratipattiH tAvatpramANaprameyaphalalakShaNeShu vikAreShvanR^itatvabuddhir na kasyacid utpadyate | vikArAn eva tu aham mama ityavidyayA AtmAtmIyena bhAvena sarvo jantuH pratipadyate svAbhAvikIM brahmAtmatAM hitvA | tasmAt prAgbrahmAtmatAprabodhAd upapannaH sarvo laukiko vaidikashca vyavahAraH -- yathA suptasya prAkR^itasya janasya svapne uccAvacAn bhAvAn pashyato nishcitam eva pratyakShAbhimataM vij~nAnaM bhavati prAkprabodhAt, na ca pratyakShAbhAsAbhiprAyaH tatkAle bhavati, tadvat | kathaM tu asatyena vedAntavAkyena satyasya brahmAtmatvasya pratipattir upapadyeta? na hi rajjusarpeNa daShTo dR^ishayate | nApi mR^igatR^iShNikAmbhasA pAnAvagAhanAdiprayojanaM kriyata iti | 

naiSha doShaH, shaN^kAviShAdinimittamaraNAdikAryopalabdheH, svapnadarshanAvasthasya ca sarpadaMshanodakasnAnAdikAryadarshanAt | tatkAryam apyanR^itam eveti ced brUyAt, tatra brUmaH -- yadyapi svapnadarshanAvasthasya sarpadaMshanodakasnAnAdikAryam anR^itam, tathApi tadavagatiH satyam eva phalam, pratibuddhasyApyabAdhyamAnatvAt | na hi svapnAd utthitaH svapnadR^iShTaM sarpadaMshanodakasnAnAdikAryaM mithyeti manyamAnaH tadavagatim api mithyeti manyate kashcit | etena svapnadR^isho.avagatyabAdhanena dehamAtrAtmavAdo dUShito veditavyaH | tathA ca shrutiH -- yadA karmasu kAmyeShu striyaM svapneShu pashyati | samR^iddhiM tatra jAnIyAt tasmin svapnanidarshane ityasatyena svapnadarshanena satyAyAH phalasamR^iddhiH prAptiM darshayati, tathA pratyakShadarshaneShu satyAyAH phalasamR^iddhiH prAptiM darshayati, tathA pratyakShadarshaneShu keShucid ariShTeShu jAteShu na ciram iva jIviShyatIti vidyAt ityuktvA atha yaH svapne puruShaM kR^iShNaM kR^iShNadantaM pashyati sa enaM hanti ityAdinA tenAsatyenaiva svapnadarshanena satyamaraNaM sUcyata iti darshayati | prasiddhaM cedaM loke.anvayavyatirekakushalAnAm IdR^ishena svapnadarshanena sAdhvAgamaH sUcyate, IdR^ishenAsAdhvAgama iti |
 
tathA akArAdisatyAkSharapratipattir dR^iShTA rekhAnR^itAkSharapratipatteH | api cAntyam idaM pramANam Atmaikatvasya pratipAdakam -- nAtaH paraM kiJNcid AkAN^kShyam asti | yathA hi loke yajetetyukte, kim? kena? katham? ityAkAN^kShyate | naivaM tattvam asi ahaM brahmAsmi [bR^i.A.u. 1.4.10] ityukte, kiJNcid anyad AkAN^kShyam asti -- sarvAtmaikatvaviShayatvAd avagateH | sati hyanyasminn avashiShyamANe.arthe AkAN^kShA syAt | na tvatmaikatvavyatirekeNAvashiShyamANo.anyo.artho.asti, ya AkAN^kShyeta | na ceyam avagatir notpadyata iti shakyaM vaktum, tad dhAsya vijaj~nau ityAdi shrutibhyaH, avagatisAdhanAnAM ca shravaNAdInAM vedAnuvacanAdInAM ca vidhIyamAnatvAt | na ceyam avagatir anarthikA bhrAntir veti shakyaM vaktum | avidyAnivR^ittiphaladarshanAt, bAdhakaj~nAnAntarAbhAvAcca | prAk cAtmaikatvAvagater avyAhataH sarvaH satyAnR^itavyavahAro laukiko vaidikashcetyavocAma | tasmAd antyena pramANena pratipAdite Atmaikatve samastasya prAcInasya bhedavyavahArasya bAdhitatvAt na anekAtmakabrahmakalpanAvakAsho.asti | 

nanu mR^idAdidR^iShTAntapraNayanAt pariNAmavad brahma shAstrasyAbhimatam iti gamyate | pariNAmino hi mR^idAdayo.arthA loke samadhigatA iti | netyucyate -- sa vA eSha mahAn aja AtmAjaro.amaro.amR^ito.abhayo brahma [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.25], sa eSha neti netyAtmA asthUlam anaNu ityAdyAbhyaH sarvavikriyApratiShedhashrutibhyaH brahmaNaH kUTasthatvAvagamAt | 
na hyekasya brahmaNaH pariNAmadharmatvaM tadrahitatvaM ca shakyaM pratipattum | sthitigativat syAd iti cet, na | kUTasthasyeti visheShaNAt | na hi kUTasthasya brahmaNaH sthitigativad anekadharmAshrayatvaM sambhavati | kUTasthaM ca nityaM brahma sarvavikriyApratiShedhAd ityavocAma | 

na ca, yathA brahmaNa AtmaikatvadarshanaM mokShasAdhanam, evaM jagadAkArapariNAmitvadarshanam api svatantram eva kasmaicit phalAyAbhipreyate, pramANAbhAvAt | kUTasthabrahmAtmaikatvavij~nAnAd eva hi phalaM darshayati shAstram -- sa eSha neti netyAtmA ityupakramya abhayaM vai janaka prApto.asi ityevaMjAtIyakam | tatraitat siddhaM bhavati -- brahmaprakaraNe sarvadharmavisheSharahitabrahmadarshanAd eva phalasiddhau satyAm, yat tatrAphalaM shrUyate brahmaNo jagadAkArapariNAmitvAdi, tad brahmadarshanopAyatvenaiva viniyujyate, phalavat saMnidhAvaphalaM tadaN^gam itivat | na tu svatantraM phalAya kalpyata iti | na hi pariNAmavattvavij~nAnAt pariNAmavattvam AtmanaH phalaM syAd iti vaktuM yuktam, kUTasthanityatvAn mokShasya | 

nanu kUTasthabrahmAtmavAdina ekatvaikAntyAt IshitrIshitavyAbhAve IshvarakAraNapratij~nAvirodha iti cet, na | avidyAtmakanAmarUpabIjavyAkaraNApekShatvAt sarvaj~natvasya | tasmAd vA etasmAd Atmana AkAshaH sambhUtaH ityAdi vAkyebhyaH nityashuddhabuddhamuktasvarUpAt sarvaj~nAt sarvashakter IshvarAjjagajjanisthitipralayAH, nAcetanAt pradhAnAd anyasmAd vA -- ityeSho.arthaH pratij~nAtaH -- janmAdyasya yataH iti | sA pratij~nA tadavasthaiva, na tadviruddho.arthaH punaH ihocyate | kathaM nocyate ? atyantam Atmana ekatvam advitIyatvaM ca bruvatA? sR^iNu yathA nocyate -- sarvaj~nasyeshvarasyAtmabhUte ivAvidyAkalpite nAmarUpe tattvAnyatvAbhyAm anirvacanIye saMsAraprapaJNcabIjabhUte sarvaj~nasyeshvarasya mAyAshaktiH prakR^itiH iti na shrutismR^ityor abhilapyete | tAbhyAm anyaH sarvaj~na IshvaraH, AkAsho vai nAma nAmarUpayor nirvahitA te yad antarA tad brahma iti shruteH, nAmarUpe vyAkaravANi sarvANi rUpANi vicitya dhIro nAmAni kR^itvAbhivad anyad Aste ekaM bIjaM bahudhA yaH karoti ityAdi shrutibhyashca | 

evam avidyAkR^itanAmarUpopAdhyanurodhIshvaro bhavati, vyom eva ghaTakarakAdyupAdhyanurodhi | sa ca svAtmabhUtAn eva ghaTAkAshasthAnIyAn avidyApratyupasthApitanAmarUpakR^itakAryakaraNasaMghAtAnurodhino jIvAkhyAn vij~nAnAtmanaH pratIShTo vyavahAraviShaye | tad evam avidyAtmakopAdhiparicchedApekSham eveshvarasyeshvaratvaM sarvaj~natvaM sarvashaktitvaM ca, na paramArthato vidyayA apAstasarvopAdhisvarUpe Atmani IshitrIshitavyasarvaj~natvAdivyavahAra upapadyate | tathA coktam -- yatra nAnyat pashyati nAnyacchR^iNoti nAnyad vijAnAti sa bhUmA iti | yatra tu asya sarvam AtmaivAbhUt tat kena kaM pashyet [bR^i.A.u. 4.5.15] ityAdinA ca | evaM paramArthAvasthAyAM sarvavyavahArAbhAvaM vadanti vedAntAH sarve | tatheshvaragItAsvapi -- 

na kartR^itvaM na karmANi lokasya sR^ijati prabhuH | 
na karmaphalasaMyogaM svabhAvaH tu pravartate ||
nAdatte kasyacit pApaM na caiva sukR^itaM vibhuH | 
aj~nAnenAvR^itaM j~nAnaM tena muhyanti jantavaH || [gItA 5.1415] iti |

paramArthAvasthAyAm IshitrIshitavyAdivyavahArAbhAvaH pradarshyate | vyavahArAvasthAyAM tUktaH shrutAvapIshvarAdivyavahAraH -- eSha sarveshvara eSha bhUtAdhipatir eSha bhUtapAla eSha setur vidharaNa eShAM lokAnAm asambhedAya [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.22] iti | tathA ceshvaragItAsvapi -- 

IshvaraH sarvabhUtAnAM hR^iddeshe.arjuna tiShThati | 
bhrAmayan sarvabhUtAni yantrArUDhAni mAyayA || [gItA 18.61] iti | 

sUtrakAro.api paramArthAbhiprAyeNa tad ananyatvam ityAha | vyavahArAbhiprAyeNa tu syAl lokavat iti mahAsamudrAdisthAnIyatAM brahmaNaH kathayati, apratyAkhyAyaiva kAryaprapaJNcaM pariNAmaprakriyAM cAshrayati -- saguNeShUpAsaneShUpayokShyata iti ||14||

|| 2.1.15 ||

bhAve copalabdheH ||

itashca kAraNAd ananyatvaM kAryasya, yat kAraNaM bhAva eva kAraNasya kAryam upalabhyate, nAbhAve | tad yathA -- satyAM mR^idi ghaTa upalabhyate, satsu ca tantuShu paTaH | na ca niyamenAnyabhAve.anyasyopalabdhir dR^iShTA | na hyashvo gor anyaH san gorbhAva evopalabhyate | na ca kulAlabhAva eva ghaTa upalabhyate, satyapi nimittanaimittikabhAve.anyatvAt | 

nanvanyasya bhAve.apyanyasyopalabdhir niyatA dR^ishyate, yathAgnibhAve dhUmasyeti | netyucyate -- uddhApite.apyagnau gopAlaghuTikAdidhAritasya dhUmasya dR^ishyamAnatvAt | atha dhUmaM kayAcid avasthayA vishiMShyAt -- IdR^isho dhUmo nAsatyagnau bhavatIti, naivam api kashcid doShaH | tadbhAvAnuraktAM hi buddhiM kAryakAraNayor ananyatve hetuM vayaM vadAmaH | na cAsAvagnidhUmayor vidyate | 

bhAvAccopalabdheH -- iti vA sUtram | na kevalaM shabdAd eva kAryakAraNayor ananyatvam, pratyakShopalabdhibhAvAcca tayor ananyatvam ityarthaH | bhavati hi pratyakShopalabdhiH kAryakAraNayor ananyatve | tad yathA -- tantusaMsthAne paTo tantuvyatirekeNa paTo nAma kAryaM naivopalabhyate, kevalAH tu tantava AtAnavitAnavantaH pratyakSham upalabhyante, tathA tantuShvaMshavaH, aMshuShu tadavayavAH | anayA pratyakShopalabdhyA lohitashuklakR^iShNAni trINi rUpANi, tato vAyumAtram AkAshamAtraM cetyanumeyam, tataH paraM brahmaikam evAdvitIyam | tatra sarvapramANAnAM niShThAm avocAma ||15||

|| 2.1.16 || 

sattvAccAvarasya || 

itashca kAraNAt kAryasyAnanyatvam, yat kAraNaM prAgutpatteH kAraNAtmanaiva kAraNe sattvam avarakAlInasya kAryasya shrUyate -- sad eva somyedam agra AsIt AtmA vA idam eka evAgra AsIt [chA.u. 6.2.2] ityAdAvidaM shabdagR^ihItasya kAryasya kAraNena sAmAnAdhikaraNyAt | yacca yad AtmanA yatra na vartate, na tat tata utpadyate, yathA sikatAbhyaH tailam | tasmAt prAgutpatter ananyatvAd utpannam apyananyad eva kAraNAt kAryam ityavagamyate | yathA ca kAraNaM brahma triShu kAleShu sattvaM na vyabhicarati, evaM kAryam api jagat triShu kAleShu sattvaM na vyabhicarati | ekaM ca punaH sattvam | ato.apyananyatvaM kAraNAt kAryasya ||16||

|| 2.1.17 || 

asadvyapadeshAn neti cen na dharmAntareNa vAkyasheShAt || 

nanu kvacid asattvam api prAgutpatteH kAryasya vyapadishati shrutiH -- asad evedam agra AsIt [chA.u. 6.2.1] iti, asad vA idam agra AsIt [chA.u. 6.2.2] iti ca | tasmAd asadvyapadeshAn na prAgutpatteH kAryasya sattvam iti cet -- neti brUmaH | na hyayam atyantAsattvAbhiprAyeNa prAgutpatteH kAryasyAsadvyapadeshaH | kiM tarhi, vyAkR^itanAmarUpatvAd dharmAd avyAkR^itanAmarUpatvaM dharmAntaram, tena dharmAntareNAyam asadvyapadeshaH prAgutpatteH sata eva kAryasya kAraNarUpeNAnanyasya | katham etad avagamyate? vAkyasheShAt | yad upakrame sandigdhArthaM vAkyaM taccheShAn nishcIyate | iha ca tAvat asad evedam agra AsIt ityasacchabdenopakrame nirdiShTaM yat, tad eva punaH tacchabdena parAmR^ishya, sad iti vishinaShTi -- tat sad AsIt iti -- asatashca pUrvAparakAlAsambandhAt AsIcchabdAnupapatteshca | asad vA idam agra AsIt ityatrApi tadAtmAnaM svayam akuruta iti vAkyasheShe visheShaNAn nAtyantAsattvam | tasmAd dharmAntareNaivAyam asadvyapadeshaH prAgutpatteH kAryasya | nAmarUpavyAkR^itaM hi vastu sacchabdArhaM loke prasiddham | ataH praN^nAmarUpavyAkaraNAd asad ivAsId ityupacaryate ||17||

|| 2.1.18 ||

yukteH shabdAntarAcca ||

yukteshca prAgutpatteH kAryasya sattvam ananyatvaM ca kAraNAd avagamyate, shabdAntarAcca | yuktiH tAvad varNyate -- dadhighaTarucakAdyarthibhiH pratiniyatAni kAraNAni kShIramR^ittikAsuvarNAdInyupAdIyamAnAni loke dR^ishyante | na hi dadhyarthibhir mR^ittikopAdIyate, na ghaTArthibhiH kShIram | tad asatkAryavAde nopapadyeta | avishiShTo hi prAgutpatteH sarvasya sarvatrAsattve kasmAt kShIrAd eva dadhyutpadyate, na mR^ittikAyAH? mR^ittikAyA eva ca ghaTa utpadyate, na kShIrAt? athAvishiShTo.api prAg asattve kShIra eva dadhnaH kashcid atishayo na mR^ittikAyAm, mR^ittikAyAm eva ca ghaTasya kashcid atishayo na kShIre -- ityucyeta -- ataH tarhyatishayavattvAt prAgavasthAyA asatkAryavAdahAniH, satkAryavAdasiddhishca | shaktishca kAraNasya kAryaniyamArthA kalpyamAnA nAnyA asatI vA kAryaM niyacchet, asattvAvisheShAd anyatvAvisheShAcca | tasmAt kAraNasyAtmabhUtA shaktiH, shakteshcAtmabhUtaM kAryam | api ca kAryakAraNayor dravyaguNAdInAM cAshvamahiShavad bhedabuddhyabhAvAt tAdAtmyam abhyupagantavyam | samavAyakalpanAyAm api, samavAyasya samavAyibhiH sambandhe.abhyupagamyamAne, tasya tasyAnyonyaH sambandhaH kalpayitavya ityanavasthAprasaN^gaH, anabhyupagamyamAne ca vicchedaprasaN^gaH |

atha samavAyaH svayaM sambandharUpatvAd anapekShyaivAparaM sambandhaM sambadhyeta, saMyogo.api tarhi svayaM sambandharUpatvAd anapekShyaivAparaM samavAyaM sambadhyeta | tAdAtmyapratIteshca dravyaguNAdInAM samavAyakalpanAnarthakyam | kathaM ca kAryam avayavidravyaM kAraNeShvavayavadravyeShu vartamAnaM vartate? kiM samasteShvavayaveShu varteta, uta pratyavayavam? yadi tAvat samasteShu varteta, tato.avayavyanupalabdhiH prasajyeta, samastAvayavasaMnikarShasyAshakyatvAt | na hi bahutvaM samasteShvashrayeShu vartamAnaM vyastAshrayagrahaNena gR^ihyate | athAvayavashaH samasteShu varteta, tadApyArambhakAvayavavyatirekeNAvayavino.avayavAH kalpyeran, yair ArambhakeShvavayaveShvavayavasho.avayavI varteta | koshAvayavavyatiriktair hyavayavairasiH koshaM vyApnoti | anavasthA caivaM prasajyeta, teShu teShvavayaveShu vartayitum anyeShAm anyeShAm avayavAnAM kalpanIyatvAt | 

atha pratyavayavaM varteta, tadaikatra vyApAre.anyatrAvyApAraH syAt | na hi devadattaH srughne saMnidhIyamAnaH tadahar eva pATAliputre.api saMnidhIyate | yugapad anekatra vR^ittAvanekatvaprasaN^gaH syAt, devadattayaj~nadattayoH iva srughnapATAliputranivAsinoH | gotvAd ivat pratyekaM parisamApter na doSha iti cet, na | tathA pratItyabhAvAt | yadi gotvAd ivat pratyekaM parisamApto.avayavI syAt, yathA gotvaM prativyaktipratyakShaM gR^ihyate, evam avayavyapi pratyavayavaM pratyakShaM gR^ihyeta | na caivaM niyataM gR^ihyate | pratyekaparisamAptau cAvayavinaH kAryeNAdhikArAt, tasya caikatvAt, sR^iN^geNApi stanakAryaM kuryAt, urasA ca pR^iShThakAryam | na caivaM dR^ishyate | prAgutpatteshca kAryasyAsattve, utpattir akartR^ikA nirAtmikA ca syAt | utpattishca nAma kriyA, sA sakartR^ikaiva bhavitum arhati, gatyAdivat | kriyA ca nAma syAt, akartR^ikA ca -- iti vipratiShidhyeta | ghaTasya cotpattir ucyamAnA ca ghaTakartR^ikA, kiM tarhyanyakartR^ikA -- iti kalpyA syAt | tathA kapAlAdInAm apyutpattir ucyamAnAnyakartR^ikaiva kalpyeta | tathA ca sati ghaTa utpadyate ityukte, kulAlAdIni kAraNAnyutpadyante ityuktaM syAt | na ca loke ghaTotpattiH ityukte kulAlAdInAm apyutpadyamAnatA pratIyate, utpannatApratIteH | 

atha svakAraNasattAsambandha evotpattir AtmalAbhashca kAryasyeti cet -- katham alabdhAtmakaM sambadhyeteti vaktavyam | sator hi dvayoH sambandhaH sambhavati, na sadasator asator vA | abhAvasya ca nirupAkhyatvAt prAgutpatteH iti maryAdAkaraNam anupapannam | satAM hi loke kShetragR^ihAdInAM maryAdA dR^iShTA nAbhAvasya | na hi, vandhyAputro rAjA babhUva prAkpUrNavarmaNo.abhiShekAd ityevaMjAtIyakena maryAdAkaraNena, nirupAkhyo vandhyAputraH -- rAjA babhUva bhavati bhaviShyatIti vA -- visheShyate | yadi ca vandhyAputro.api kArakavyApArAd Urdhvam abhaviShyat, tata idam apyupApatsyata -- kAryabhAvo.api kArakavyApArAd UrdhvaM bhaviShyatIti | vayaM tu pashyAmaH -- vandhyAputrasya kAryAbhAvasya cAbhAvatvAvisheShAt, yathA vandhyAputraH kArakavyApArAd UrdhvaM na bhaviShyati, evaM kAryAbhAvo.api kArakavyApArAd UrdhvaM na bhaviShyatIti | 

nanv evaM sati kArakavyApAro.anarthakaH prasajyeta | yathaiva hi prAksiddhatvAt kAraNasvarUpasiddhaye na kashcid vyApriyate, evaM prAksiddhatvAt tadananyatvAcca kAryasya svarUpasiddhaye.api na kashcid vyApriyeta | vyApriyate ca | ataH kArakavyApArArthavattvAya, manyAmahe, prAgutpatter abhAvaH kAryasyeti cet, naiSha doShaH | yataH kAryAkAreNa kAraNaM vyavasthApayataH kArakavyApArasyArthavattvam upapadyate | kAryAkAro.api kAraNasyAtmabhUta eva, anAtmabhUtasyAnArabhyatvAd ityabhANi | na ca visheShadarshanamAtreNa vastvanyatvaM bhavati | na hi devadattaH saMkucitahastapAdaH prasAritahastapAdashca visheSheNa dR^ishyamAno.api vastvanyatvaM gacchati, sa eveti pratyabhij~nAnAt | tathA pratidinam anekasaMsthAnAnAm api pitrAdInAM na vastvanyatvaM bhavati, mama pitA mama bhrAtA mama putra iti pratyabhij~nAnAt | janmocchedAnantaritatvAt tatra yuktam, nAnyatreti cet, na | kShIrAdInAm api dadhyAdyAkArasaMsthAnasya pratyakShatvAt | adR^ishyamAnAnAm api vaTadhAnAdInAM samAnajAtIyAvayavAntaropacitAnAm aN^kurAdibhAvena darshanagocaratApattau janmasaMj~nA | teShAm evAvayavAnAm apacayavashAd adarshanApattAv ucchedasaMj~nA | tatredR^igjanmocchedAntaritatvAcced asataH sattvApattiH, satashcAsattvApattiH, tathA sati garbhavAsina uttAnashAyinashca bhedaprasaN^gaH | 

tathA ca bAlyayauvanasthAvireShvapi bhedaprasaN^gaH, pitrAdivyavahAralopaprasaN^gashca | etena kShaNabhaN^gavAdaH prativaditavyaH | yasya tu punaH prAgutpatter asatkAryam, tasya nirviShayaH kArakavyApAraH syAt, abhAvasya viShayatvAnupapatteH -- AkAshahananaprayojanakhaDgAdyanekAyudhaprayuktivat | samavAyikAraNaviShayaH kArakavyApAraH syAd iti cet, na | anyaviShayeNa kArakavyApAreNAnyaniShpatter atiprasaN^gAt | samavAyikAraNasyaivAtmAtishayaH kAryam iti cet, na | satkAryatApatteH | tasmAt kShIrAdInyeva dravyANi dadhyAdibhAvenAvatiShThamAnAni kAryAkhyAM labhanta iti na kAraNAd anyat kAryaM varShashatenApi shakyaM kalpayitum | tathA mUlakAraNam eva A antyAt kAryAt tena tena kAryAkAreNa naTavat sarvavyavahArAspadatvaM pratipadyate | evaM yukteH, kAryasya prAgutpatteH sattvam, ananyatvaM ca kAraNAt, avagamyate ||18|| 

|| 2.1.19 ||

shabdAntarAccaitad avagamyate -- pUrvasUtre.asadvyapadeshinaH shabdasyodAhR^itatvAt tato.anyaH sadvyapadeshI shabdaH shabdAntaram -- sad eva somyedam agra AsId ekam evAdvitIyam [chA.u. 6.2.1] ityAdi | tad dhaika Ahur asad evedam agra AsIt iti cAsatpakSham upakShipya, katham asataH sajjAyeta ityAkShipya, sad eva somyedam agra AsIt ityavadhArayati | tatredaM shabdavAcyasya kAryasya prAgutpatteH sacchabdavAcyena kAraNena sAmAnAdhikaraNyasya shrUyamANatvAt, sattvAnanyatve prasidhyataH | yadi tu prAgutpatter asatkAryaM syAt, pashcAccotpadyamAnaM kAraNe samaveyAt, tad anyat kAraNAt syAt, tatra yenAshrutaM shrutaM bhavati [chA.u. 6.1.3] itIyaM pratij~nA pIDyeta | sattvAnanyatvAvagateH tviyaM pratij~nA samarthyate -- 

paTavacca ||

yathA ca saMveShTitaH paTo na vyaktaM gR^ihyate -- kim ayaM paTaH, kiM vAnyad dravyam iti | sa eva prasAritaH, yat saMveShTitaM dravyaM tatpaTa eveti prasAraNenAbhivyakto gR^ihyate | yathA ca saMveShTanasamaye paTa iti gR^ihyamANo.api na vishiShTAyAm avistAro gR^ihyate | sa eva prasAraNasamaye vishiShTAyAm avistAro gR^ihyate -- na saMveShTitarUpAd anyo.ayaM bhinnaH paTa iti, evaM tantvAdikAraNAvasthaM paTAdikAryam aspaShTaM sat, turIvemakuvindAdikArakavyApArAbhivyaktaM spaShTaM gR^ihyate | ataH saMveShTitaprasAritapaTanyAyenaivAnanyatkAraNAt kAryam ityarthaH ||19||

|| 2.1.20 || 

yathA ca prANAdi ||

yathA ca loke prANApAnAdiShu prANabhedeShu prANAyAmena nirurAShu kAraNamAtreNa rUpeNa vartamAneShu jIvanamAtraM kAryaM nirvartyate, nAkuJNcanaprasAraNAdikaM kAryAntaram | teShv eva prANabhedeShu punaH pravR^itteShu jIvanAd adhikam AkuJNcanaprasAraNAdikam api kAryAntaraM nirvartyate | na ca prANabhedAnAM prabhedavataH prANAd anyatvam, samIraNasvabhAvAvisheShAt -- evaM kAryasya kAraNAd ananyatvam | atashca kR^itsnasya jagato brahmakAryatvAt tadananyatvAcca siddhaiShA shrautI pratij~nA -- yenAshrutaM shrutaM bhavatyamataM matam avij~nAtaM vij~nAtam [chA.u. 6.1.1] iti ||20||

7. itaravyapadeshAdhikaraNam

|| 2.1.21 ||

itaravyapadeshAd dhitAkaraNAdidoShaprasaktiH ||

anyathA punashcetanakAraNavAda AkShipyate -- cetanAd dhi jagatprakriyAyAm AshrIyamANAyAM hitAkaraNAdayo doShAH prasajyante | kutaH? itaravyapadeshAt | itarasya shArIrasya brahmAtmatvaM vyapadishati shrutiH -- sa AtmA tat tvam asi shvetaketo [chA.u. 6.8.7] iti pratibodhanAt | yad vA -- itarasya ca brahmaNaH shArIrAtmatvaM vyapadishati -- tat sR^iShTvA tad evAnuprAvishat [tai.u. 2.6] iti sraShTur evAvikR^itasya brahmaNaH kAryAnupraveshena shArIrAtmatvadarshanAt | anena jIvenAtmanAnupravishya nAmarUpe vyAkaravANi [chA.u. 6.3.2] iti ca parA devatA jIvamAtmashabdena vyapadishantI, na brahmaNo bhinnaH shArIra iti darshayati | tasmAd yad brahmaNaH sraShTR^itvaM tacchArIrasyaiveti | atashca svatantraH kartA san hitam evAtmanaH saumanasyakaraM kuryAt, nAhitaM janmamaraNajarArogAdyanekAnarthajAlam | 

na hi kashcid aparatantro bandhanAgAram AtmanaH kR^itvAnupravishati | na ca svayam atyantanirmalaH san atyantamalinaM deham AtmatvenopeyAt | kR^itam api kathaMcid yad duHkhakaraM tadicchayA jahyAt | sukhakaraM copAdadIta | smarecca -- mayedaM jagad bimbaM vicitraM viracitam iti | sarvo hi lokaH spaShTAM kAryaM kR^itvA smarati -- mayedaM kR^itam iti | yathA ca mAyAvI svayaM prasAritAM mAyAm icchayA anAyAsenaivopasaMharati, evaM shArIro.apImAM sR^iShTim upasaMharet | svakIyam api tAvaccharIraM shArIro na shaknotyanAyAsenopasaMhartum | evaM hitakriyAdyadarshanAd anyAyyA cetanAjjagatprakriyeti gamyate ||21||

|| 2.1.22 || 

adhikaM tu bhedanirdeshAt ||

tushabdaH pakShaM vyAvartayati | yat sarvaj~naM sarvashakti brahma nityashuddhabuddhamuktasvabhAvaM shArIrAd adhikam anyat, tad vayaM jagataH sraShTR^i brUmaH | na tasmin hitAkaraNAdayo doShAH prasajyante | na hi tasya hitaM kiMcit kartavyam asti, ahitaM vA parihartavyam, nityamuktasvabhAvatvAt | na ca tasya j~nAnapratibandhaH shaktipratibandho vA kvacid apyasti, sarvaj~natvAt sarvashaktitvAcca | shArIraH tu anevaMvidhaH | tasmin prasajyante hitAkaraNAdayo doShAH | na tu taM vayaM jagataH sraShTAraM brUmaH | kuta etat? bhedanirdeshAt -- AtmA vA are draShTavyaH shrotavyo mantavyo nididhyAsitavyaH [bR^i.A.u. 2.4.5], so.anveShTavyaH sa vijij~nAsitavyaH [chA.u. 8.7.1], satA somya tadA sampanno bhavati [chA.u. 6.8.1], shArIra AtmA prAj~nenAtmanAnvArUDhaH [bR^i.A.u. 4.3.35]ityevaMjAtIyakaH kartR^ikarmAdibhedanirdesho jIvAd adhikaM brahma darshayati | 

nanvabhedanirdesho.api darshitaH -- tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7] ityevaMjAtIyakaH | kathaM bhedAbhedau viruddhau sambhaveyAtAm? naiSha doShaH, mahAkAshaghaTAkAshanyAyenobhayasambhavasya tatra tatra pratiShThApitatvAt | api ca yadA tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7] ityevaMjAtIyakenAbhedanirdeshenAbhedaH pratibodhito bhavati, apagataM bhavati tadA jIvasya saMsAritvaM brahmaNashca sraShTR^itvam, samastasya mithyAj~nAnavijR^imbhitasya bhedavyavahArasya samyagj~nAnena bAdhitatvAt | 

tatra kuta eva sR^iShTiH? kuto vA hitAkaraNAdayo doShAH? avidyApratyupasthApitanAmarUpakR^itakAryakaraNasaMghAtopAdhyavivekakR^itA hi bhrAntir hitAkaraNAdilakShaNaH saMsAraH, na tu paramArthato.astItyasakR^id avocAma -- janmamaraNacchedanabhedanAdyabhimAnavat | abAdhite tu bhedavyavahAre so.anveShTavyaH sa vijij~nAsitavyaH [chA.u. 8.7.1] ityevaMjAtIyakena bhedanirdeshenAvagamyamAnaM brahmaNo.adhikatvaM hitAkaraNAdidoShaprasaktiM niruNaddhi ||22||

|| 2.1.23 || 

ashmAdivacca tadanupapattiH ||

yathA ca loke pR^ithivItvasAmAnyAnvitAnAm apyashmanAM kecin mahArhA maNayo vajravaiDUryAdayaH, anye madhyamavIryAH sUryakAntAdayaH, anye prahINAH shvAyasaprakShepaNArhAH pAShANAH -- ityanekavidhaM vaicitryaM dR^ishyate | yathA caikapR^ithivIvyapAshrayANAm api bIjAnAM bahuvidhaM patrapuShpaphalagandharasAdivaicitryaM candanakimpAkacampakAdiShUpalakShyate | yathA caikasyApyannarasasya lohitAdIni keshalomAdIni ca vicitrANi kAryANi bhavanti -- evam ekasyApi brahmaNo jIvaprAj~napR^ithaktvaM kAryavaicitryaM copapadyata ityataH tadanupapattiH, paraparikalpitadoShAnupapattiH ityarthaH | shruteshca prAmANyAt, vikArasya ca vAcArambhaNamAtratvAt svapnadR^ishyabhAvavaicitryavacca -- ityabhyuccayaH ||23||

8. upasaMhAradarshanAdhikaramam ||

|| 2.1.24 ||

upasaMhAradarshanAn neti cen, na, kShIravad dhi || 

cetanaM brahmaikam advitIyaM jagataH kAraNam iti yad uktam, tan nopapadyate | kasmAt? upasaMhAradarshanAt | iha hi loke kulAlAdayo ghaTapaTAdInAM kartAro mR^iddaNDacakrasUtrasalilAdyanekakArakopasaMhAreNa saMgR^ihItasAdhanAH santaH tattatkAryaM kurvANA dR^ishyante | brahma cAsahAyaM tavAbhipretam | tasya sAdhanAntarAnupasaMgrahe sati kathaM sraShTR^itvam upapadyeta? tasmAn na brahma jagatkAraNam iti cet, naiSha doShaH | yataH kShIravad dravyasvabhAvavisheShAd upapadyate -- yathA hi loke kShIraM jalaM vA svayam eva dadhihimakarakAdibhAvena pariNamate.anapekShya bAhyaM sAdhanam, tathehApi bhaviShyati | 

nanu kShIrAdyapi dadhyAdibhAvena pariNamamAnam apekShata eva bAhyaM sAdhanam auShNyAdikam | katham ucyate kShIravad dhi iti? naiSha doShaH | svayam api hi kShIraM yAM ca yAvatIM ca pariNAmamAtrAm anubhavati, tAvatyeva tvAryate tu auShNyAdinA dadhibhAvAya | yadi ca svayaM dadhibhAvashIlatA na syAt, naivauShNyAdinApi balAd dadhibhAvam Apadyeta | na hi vAyur AkAsho vA auShNyAdinA balAd dadhibhAvam Apadyate | sAdhanasAmagryA ca tasya pUrNatA sampAdyate | paripUrNashaktikaM tu brahma | na tasyAnyena kenacit pUrNatA sampAdayitavyA | shrutishca bhavati -- 

na tasya kAryaM karaNaM ca vidyate 
na tatsamashcAbhyadhikashca dR^ishyate | 
parAsya shaktir vividhaiva shrUyate 
svAbhAvikI j~nAnabalakriyA ca || [shve.u. 6.2] iti | 

tasmAd ekasyApi brahmaNo vicitrashaktiyogAt kShIrAdivad vicitrapariNAma upapadyate ||24||

|| 2.1.25 ||

syAd etat | upapadyate kShIrAdInAm acetanAnAm anapekShyApi bAhyaM sAdhanaM dadhyAdibhAvaH, dR^iShTatvAt | cetanAH punaH kulAlAdayaH sAdhanasAmagrIm apekShyaiva tasmai tasmai kAryAya pravartamAnA dR^ishyante | kathaM brahma cetanaM sat asahAyaM pravarteta ? iti brUmaH -- 

devAdivad api loke ||

yathA loke devAH pitara R^iShaya ityevamAdayo mahAprabhAvAshcetanA api santo.anapekShyaiva kiJNcid bAhyaM sAdhanam aishvaryavisheShayogAd abhidhyAnamAtreNa svata eva bahUni nAnAsaMsthAnAni sharIrANi prAsAdAdIni rathAdIni ca nirmimANA upalabhyante, mantrArthavAdetihAsapurANaprAmANyAt | tantunAbhashca svata eva tantUn sR^ijati | balAkA cAntareNaiva shukraM garbhaM dhatte | padminI cAnapekShya kiMcit prasthAnasAdhanaM saro.antarAt saro.antaraM pratiShThate | evaM cetanam api brahma anapekShyaiva bAhyaM sAdhanaM svata eva jagat srakShyati | 

sa yadi brUyAt -- ya ete devAdayo brahmaNo dR^iShTAntA upAttAste dArShTAntikena brahmaNA na samAnA bhavanti | sharIram eva hyacetanaM devAdInAM sharIrAntarAdivibhUtyutpAdane upAdAnam, na tu cetana AtmA | tantunAbhasya ca kShudratarajantubhakShaNAl lAlA kaThinatAm ApadyamAnA tantur bhavati | balAkA ca stanayitnuravashravaNAd garbhaM dhatte | padminI ca cetanaprayuktA satI acetanenaiva sharIreNa saro.antarAt saro.antaram upasarpati, vallIva vR^ikSham, na tu svayam evAcetanA saro.antaropasarpaNe vyApriyate | tasmAn naite brahmaNo dR^iShTAntA iti | taM prati brUyAt -- nAyaM doShaH, kulAlAdidR^iShTAntavailakShaNyamAtrasya vivakShitatvAd iti | yathA hi kulAlAdInAM devAdInAM ca samAne cetanatve kulAlAdayaH kAryArambhe bAhyaM sAdhanam apekShante, na devAdayaH | tathA brahma cetanam api na bAhyaM sAdhanam apekShiShyata ityetAvad vayaM devAdyudAharaNena vivakShAmaH | tasmAd yathaikasya sAmarthyaM dR^iShTaM tathA sarveShAm eva bhavitum arhatIti nAstyekAnta ityabhiprAyaH ||25||

9. kR^itsnaprasaktyadhikaraNam 

|| 2.1.26 ||

kR^itsnaprasaktir niravayavatvashabdakopo vA || 

cetanam ekam advitIyaM brahma kShIrAdivad devAdivaccAnapekShya bAhyaM sAdhanaM svayaM pariNamamAnaM jagataH kAraNam iti sthitam | shAstrArthaparishuddhaye tu punar AkShipati | kR^itsnaprasaktiH kR^itsnasya brahmaNaH kAryarUpeNa pariNAmaH prApnoti, niravayavatvAt  -- yadi brahma pR^ithivyAdivat sAvayavam abhaviShyat, tato.asyaikadeshaH paryaNaMsyat, ekadeshashcAvasthAsyata | niravayavaM tu brahma shrutibhyo.avagamyate -- niShkalaM niShkriyaM shAntaM niravadyaM niraJNjanam [shve.u. 6.19], divyo hyamUrtaH puruShaH sa bAhyAbhyantaro hyajaH [mu.u. 2.1.2], idaM mahadbhUtam anantam apAraM vij~nAnaghana eva sa eSha neti netyAtmA asthUlam anaNu ityAdyAbhyaH sarvavisheShapratiShedhinIbhyaH | 

tatashcaikadeshapariNAmAsambhavAt kR^itsnapariNAmaprasaktau satyAM mUlocchedaH prasajyeta | draShTavyatopadeshAnarthakyaM ca Apadyeta, ayatnadR^iShTatvAt kAryasya, tadvyatiriktasya ca brahmaNo.asambhavAt | ajatvAdishabdavyAkopashca | athaitaddoShaparijihIrShayA sAvayavam eva brahmAbhyupagamyeta, tathApi ye niravayavatvasya pratipAdakAH shabdA udAhR^itAH te prakupyeyuH | sAvayavatve cAnityatvaprasaN^ga iti -- sarvathAyaM pakSho na ghaTayituM shakyata ityAkShipati ||26||

|| 2.1.27 || 

shruteH tu shabdamUlatvAt || 

tushabdenAkShepaM pariharati | na khalvasmatpakShe kashcid api doSho.asti | na tAvat kR^itsnaprasaktir asti | kutaH? shruteH -- yathaiva hi brahmaNo jagadutpattiH shrUyate, evaM vikAravyatirekeNApi brahmaNo.avasthAnaM shrUyate -- prakR^itivikArayor bhedena vyapadeshAt seyaM devataikShata hantAham imAH tisro devatA anena jIvenAtmanAnupravishya nAmarUpe vyAkaravANi iti, tAvAn asya mahimA tato jyAyAMshca pUruShaH | pAdo.asya vishvA bhUtAni tripAdasyAmR^itaM divi iti caivaMjAtIyakAt | tathA hR^idayAyatanatvavacanAt | satsampattivacanAcca -- yadi ca kR^itsnaM brahma kAryabhAvenopayuktaM syAt, satA somya tadA sampanno bhavati iti suShuptigataM visheShaNam anupapannaM syAt, vikR^itena brahmaNA nityasampannatvAd avikR^itasya ca brahmaNo.abhAvAt | tathendriyagocaratvapratiShedhAt -- brahmaNo vikArasya cendriyagocaratvopapatteH | tasmAd astyavikR^itaM brahma | na ca niravayavatvashabdavyAkopo.asti, shrUyamANatvAd eva niravayavatvasyApyabhyupagamyamAnatvAt | shabdamUlaM ca brahma shabdapramANakam, nendriyAdipramANakam | tad yathAshabdam abhyupagantavyam | shabdashcobhayam api brahmaNaH pratipAdayati --  akR^itsnaprasaktiM niravayavatvaM ca | laukikAnAm api maNimantrauShadhiprabhR^itInAM deshakAlanimittavaicitryavashAcchaktayo viruddhAnekakAryaviShayA dR^ishyante | tA api tAvan nopadesham antareNa kevalena tarkeNAvagantuM shakyante -- asya vastuna etAvatya etatsahAyA etadviShayA etatprayojanAshca shaktaya iti | kim utAcintyasvabhAvasya brahmaNo rUpaM vinA shabdena na nirUpyeta | tathA cAhuH paurANikAH -- 
 
acintyAH khalu ye bhAvA na tAMstarkeNa yojayet | 
prakR^itibhyaH paraM yacca tad acintyasya lakShaNam || iti | 

tasmAcchabdamUla evAtIndriyArthayAthAtmyAdhigamaH | 

nanu shabdenApi na shakyate viruddho.arthaH pratyAyayitum -- niravayavaM ca brahma pariNamate na ca kR^itsnam iti | yadi niravayavaM brahma syAt, naiva pariNam eta, kR^itsnam eva vA pariNam eta | atha kenacid rUpeNa pariNam eta kenaciccAvatiShTheteti, rUpabhedakalpanAt sAvayavam eva prasajyeta | kriyAviShaye hi atirAtre ShoDashinaM gR^ihNAti, nAtirAtre ShoDashinaM gR^ihNAti ityevaMjAtIyakAyAM virodhapratItAvapi vikalpAshrayaNaM virodhAparihArakAraNaM bhavati, puruShatantratvAccAnuShThAnasya | iha tu vikalpAshrayaNenApi na virodhaparihAraH sambhavati, apuruShatantratvAd vastunaH | tasmAd durghaTam etad iti -- naiSha doShaH, avidyAkalpitarUpabhedAbhyupagamAt | na hyavidyAkalpitena rUpabhedena sAvayavaM vastu sampadyate | na hi timiropahatanayanenAneka iva candramA dR^ishyamAno.aneka eva bhavati | avidyAkalpitena ca nAmarUpalakShaNena rUpabhedena vyAkR^itAvyAkR^itAtmakena tattvAnyatvAbhyAm anirvacanIyena brahma pariNAmAdisarvavyavahArAspadatvaM pratipadyate | pAramArthikena ca rUpeNa sarvavyavahArAtItam apariNatam avatiShThate, vAcArambhaNamAtratvAccAvidyAkalpitasya nAmarUpabhedasya -- iti na niravayavatvaM brahmaNaH kupyati | na ceyaM pariNAmashrutiH pariNAmapratipAdanArthA, tatpratipattau phalAnavagamAt | 

sarvavyavahArahInabrahmAtmabhAvapratipAdanArthA tv eShA, tatpratipattau phalAvagamAt | sa eSha neti netyAtmA ityupakramyAha -- abhayaM vai janaka prApto.asi iti | tasmAd asmatpakShe na kashcid api doShaprasaN^go.asti ||27||

|| 2.1.28 ||

Atmani ceva vicitrAshca hi ||

api ca naivAtra vivaditavyam --  katham ekasmin brahmaNi svarUpAnupamardena evAnekAkArA sR^iShTiH syAd iti | yata Atmanyapyekasmin svapnadR^ishi svarUpAnupamardenaivAnekAkArA sR^iShTiH paThante -- na tatra rathA na rathayogA na panthAno bhavantyatha rathAn rathayogAn pathaH sR^ijate ityAdinA | loke.api devAdiShu mAyAvyAdiShu ca svarUpAnupamardenaiva vicitrA hastyashvAdisR^iShTayo dR^ishyante | tathaikasminn api brahmaNi svarUpAnupamardenaivAnekAkArA sR^iShTir bhaviShyatIti ||29||

|| 2.1.29 ||

svapakShe doShAcca ||
 
pareShAm apyeSha samAnaH svapakShadoShaH -- pradhAnavAdino.api hi niravayavam aparicchinnaM shabdAdihInaM pradhAnaM sAvayavasya paricchinnasya shabdAdimataH kAryasya kAraNam iti svapakShaH | tatrApi kR^itsnaprasaktir niravayavatvAt pradhAnasya prApnoti, niravayavatvAbhyupagamakopo vA | 

nanu naiva tair niravayavaM pradhAnam abhyupagamyate | sattvarajastamAMsi hi trayo guNAH | teShAM sAmyAvasthA pradhAnam | tair evAvayavaiH tatsAvayavam iti -- naivaMjAtIyakena sAvayavatvena prakR^ito doShaH parihartuM pAryate, yataH sattvarajastamasAm apyekaikasya samAnaM niravayavatvam ekaikam eva cetaradvayAnugR^ihItaM sajAtIyasya prapaJNcasyopAdAnam iti -- samAnatvAt svapakShadoShaprasaN^gasya | tarkApratiShThAnAt sAvayavatvam eveti cet -- evam apyanityatvAdidoShaprasaN^gaH | atha shaktaya eva kAryavaicitryasUcitA avayavA ityabhiprAyaH, tAH tu brahmavAdino.apyavishiShTAH | tathA aNuvAdino.apyaNur aNvantareNa saMyujyamAno niravayavatvAd yadi kArtsnyena saMyujyeta, tataH prathimAnupapatter aNumAtratvaprasaN^gaH | athaikadeshena saMyujyeta, tathApi niravayavatvAbhyupagamakopa iti -- svapakShe.api samAna eSha doShaH | samAnatvAcca nAnyatarasminn eva pakShe upakSheptavyo bhavati | parihR^itaH tu brahmavAdinA svapakShe doShaH ||29||

 -- o)0(o -- 
10. sarvopetAdhikaraNam 

|| 2.1.30 ||

ekasyApi brahmaNo vicitrashaktiyogAd upapadyate vicitro vikAraprapaJNca ityuktam | tat punaH katham avagamyate -- vicitrashaktiyuktaM paraM brahmeti | tad ucyate -- 

sarvopetA ca taddarshanAt ||

sarvashaktiyuktA ca parA devatetyabhyupagantavyam | kutaH? taddarshanAt | tathA hi darshayati shrutiH sarvashaktiyogaM parasyA devatAyAH -- sarvakarmA sarvakAmaH sarvarasaH sarvam idam abhyAtto.avAkyanAdaraH satyakAmaH satyasaN^kalpaH yaH sarvaj~naH sarvavit etasya vA akSharasya prashAsane gArgi sUryAcandramasau vidhR^itau tiShThataH [bR^i.A.u. 3.8.9] ityevaMjAtIyakA ||30||

  -- o)0(o -- 

|| 2.1.31 ||

vikaraNatvAn neti cet tad uktam ||

syAd etat -- vikaraNAM parAM devatAM shAsti shAstram -- acakShuShkamashrotram avAgamanAH ityevaMjAtIyakam | kathaM sA sarvashaktiyuktApi satI kAryAya prabhavet? devAdayo hi cetanAH sarvashaktiyuktA api santa AdhyAtmikakAryakaraNasampannA eva tasmai tasmai kAryAya prabhavanto vij~nAyante | kathaM ca neti neti iti pratiShiddhasarvavisheShAyA devatAyAH sarvashaktiyogaH sambhavet, iti cet -- yad atra vaktavyaM tat purastAd evoktam | shrutyavagAhyam evedam atigambhIraM brahma na tarkAvagAhyam | na ca yathaikasya sAmarthyaM dR^iShTaM tathAnyasyApi sAmarthyena bhavitavyam iti niyamo.astIti | pratiShiddhasarvavisheShasyApi brahmaNaH sarvashaktiyogaH sambhavatItyetad apyavidyAkalpitarUpabhedopanyAsenoktam eva | tathA ca shAstram -- apANipAdo javano grahItA pashyatyacakShuH sa sR^iNotyakarNaH [shve.u. 3.19] ityakaraNasyapi brahmaNaH sarvasAmarthyayogaM darshayati ||31||

  -- o)0(o -- 

11. prayojanavattvAdhikaraNam

|| 2.1.32 || 

na prayojanavattvAt ||

anyathA punashcetanakartR^itvaM jagata AkShipati -- na khalu cetanaH paramAtmedaM jagadbimbaM viracayitum arhati | kutaH? prayojanavattvAt pravR^ittInAm | cetano hi loke buddhipUrvakArI puruShaH pravartamAno na mandopakramAm api tAvat pravR^ittim AtmaprayojanAnupayoginIm ArabhamANo dR^iShTaH, kim uta gurutarasaMrambhAm | bhavati ca lokaprasiddhyanuvAdinI shrutiH -- na vA are sarvasya kAmAya sarvam priyaM bhavatyAtmanaH tu kAmAya sarvam priyaM bhavati [bR^i.A.u. 2.4.5] iti gurutarasaMrambhA ceyaM pravR^ittiH -- yad uccAvacaprapaJNcaM jagadbimbaM viracayitavyam | yadIyam api pravR^ittishcetanasya paramAtmana AtmaprayojanopayoginI parikalpyeta, paritR^iptatvaM paramAtmanaH shrUyamANaM bAdhyeta | prayojanAbhAve vA pravR^ittyabhAvo.api syAt | 

atha cetano.api san unmatto buddhyaparAdhAd antareNaivAtmaprayojanaM pravartamAno dR^iShTAH, tathA paramAtmApi pravartiShyate ityucyeta -- tathA sati sarvaj~natvaM paramAtmanaH shrUyamANaM bAdhyeta | tasmAd ashliShTA cetanAt sR^iShTiH iti ||32||

 || 2.1.33 || 

lokavat tu lIlAkaivalyam || 

tushabdenAkShepaM pariharati | yathA loke kasyaci dAptaiShaNasya rAj~no rAjAmAtyasya vA vyatiriktaM kiMcit prayojanam anabhisandhAya kevalaM lIlArUpAH pravR^ittayaH krIDAvihAreShu bhavanti | yathA cocchvAsaprashvAsAdayo.anabhisandhAya bAhyaM kiMcit prayojanaM svabhAvAd eva sambhavanti | evam IshvarasyApyanapekShya kiMcit prayojanAntaraM svabhAvAd eva kevalaM lIlArUpA pravR^ittir bhaviShyati | na hIshvarasya prayojanAntaraM nirUpyamANaM nyAyataH shrutito vA sambhavati | na ca svabhAvaH paryanuyoktuM shakyate | yadyapyasmAkam iyaM jagadbimbaviracanA gurutarasaMrambhevAbhAti, tathApi parameshvarasya lIlaiva kevaleyam, aparimitashaktitvAt | yadi nAma loke lIlAsvapi kiMcit sUkShmaM prayojanam utprekShyeta, tathApi naivAtra kiMcit prayojanam utprekShituM shakyate, AptakAmashruteH | nApyapravR^ittir unmattapravR^ittir vA, sR^iShTishruteH, sarvaj~nashruteshca | na ceyaM paramArthaviShayA sR^iShTishrutiH | avidyAkalpitanAmarUpavyavahAragocaratvAt, brahmAtmabhAvapratipAdanaparatvAcca -- ityetad api naiva vismartavyam ||33||

  -- o)0(o -- 
12. vaiShamyanairghR^iNyAdhikaraNam 

|| 2.1.34 || 

punashca jagajjanmAdihetutvam IshvarasyAkShipyate, sthUNAnikhanananyAyena pratij~nAtasyArthasya dR^iDhIkaraNAya | neshvaro jagataH kAraNam upapadyate | kutaH? vaiShamyanairghR^iNyaprasaN^gAt -- kAMshcid atyantasukhabhAjaH karoti devAdIn, kAMshcid atyantaduHkhabhAjaH pashvAdIn, kAMshcin madhyamabhogabhAjo manuShyAdIn -- ityevaM viShamAM sR^iShTiM nirmimANasyeshvarasya pR^ithagjanasyeva rAgadveShopapatteH, shrutismR^ityavadhAritasvacchatvAd IshvarasvabhAvavilopaH prasajyeta | tathA khalajanair api jugupsitaM nirghR^iNatvam atikrUratvaM duHkhayogavidhAnAt sarvaprajopasaMhArAcca prasajyeta | tasmAd vaiShamyanairghR^iNyaprasaN^gAn neshvaraH kAraNam ityevaM prApte, brUmaH -- 

vaiShamyanairghR^iNye na sApekShatvAt tathAhi darshayati ||

vaiShamyanairghR^iNye neshvarasya prasajyete | kasmAt? sApekShatvAt | yadi hi nirapekShaH kevala Ishvaro viShamAM sR^iShTiM nirmimIte, syAtAm etau doShau -- vaiShamyaM nairghR^iNyaM ca | na tu nirapekShasya nirmAtR^itvam asti | sApekSho hIshvaro viShamAM sR^iShTiM nirmimIte | kim apekShate ? iti cet, dharmAdharmAvapekShata iti vadAmaH | ataH sR^ijyamAnaprANidharmAdharmApekShA viShamA sR^iShTiH iti nAyam IshvarasyAparAdhaH | IshvaraH tu parjanyavad draShTavyaH -- yathA hi parjanyo vrIhiyavAdisR^iShTau sAdhAraNaM kAraNaM bhavati, vrIhiyavAdivaiShamye tu tattadbIjagatAnyevAsAdhAraNAni sAmarthyAni kAraNAni bhavanti, evam Ishvaro devamanuShyAdisR^iShTau sAdhAraNaM kAraNaM bhavati, devamanuShyAdivaiShamye tu tattajjIvagatAnyevAsAdhAraNAni karmANi kAraNAni bhavanti | evam IshvaraH sApekShatvAn na vaiShamyanairghR^iNyAbhyAM duShyati | 

kathaM punar avagamyate sApekSha Ishvaro nIcamadhyamottamaM saMsAraM nirmimIta iti? tathA hi darshayati shrutiH -- eSha hyeva sAdhu karma kArayati taM yamebhyo lokebhya unninIShata eSha u evAsAdhu karma kArayati taM yamadho ninIShate iti [kau.u. 3.8], puNyo vai puNyena karmaNA bhavati pApaH pApena [bR^i.A.u. 3.2.13] iti ca | smR^itir api prANikarmavisheShApekSham eveshvarasyAnugrahItR^itvaM nigrahItR^itvaM ca darshayati -- ye yathA mAM prapadyante tAMH tathaiva bhajAmyaham [gItA 4.11] ityevaMjAtIyakA ||34||

|| 2.1.35 || 

na karmAvibhAgAd iti cen nAnAditvAt || 

sad eva somyedam agra AsId ekam evAdvitIyam iti prAksR^iShTer avibhAgAvadhAraNAn nAsti karma, yad apekShya viShamA sR^iShTiH syAt | sR^iShTyottarakAlaM hi sharIrAdivibhAgApekShaM karma, karmApekShashca sharIrAdivibhAgaH -- itItaretarAshrayatvaM prasajyeta | ato vibhAgAd UrdhvaM karmApekSha IshvaraH pravartatAM nAma | prAgvibhAgAd vaicitryanimittasya karmaNo.abhAvAt tulyaivAdyA sR^iShTiH prApnotIti cet, naiSha doShaH | anAditvAt saMsArasya | bhaved eSha doShaH, yadyAdimAn ayaM saMsAraH syAt | anAdau tu saMsAre bIjAN^kuravarAtuhetumadbhAvena karmaNaH sargavaiShamyasya ca pravR^ittir na virudhyate ||35|| 

|| 2.1.36 || 

kathaM punar avagamyate -- anAdir eSha saMsAra iti? ata uttaraM paThati -- 

upapadyate cApyupalabhyate ca || 

upapadyate ca saMsArasyAnAditvam -- Adimattve hi saMsArasyAkasmAd udbhUter muktAnAm api punaH saMsArodbhUtiprasaN^gaH, akR^itAbhyAgamakR^itavipraNAshaprasaN^gashca, sukhaduHkhAdivaiShamyasya nirnimittatvAt | na ceshvaro vaiShamyahetuH ityuktam | na cAvidyA kevalA vaiShamyasya kAraNam, ekarUpatvAt | rAgAdikleshavAsanAkShiptakarmApekShA tu avidyA vaiShamyakarI syAt | na ca karma antareNa sharIraM sambhavati, na ca sharIram antareNa karma sambhavati -- itItaretarAshrayatvaprasaN^gaH | anAditve tu bIjaN^kuranyAyenopapatter na kashcid doSho bhavati | upalabhyate ca saMsArasyAnAditvaM shrutismR^ityoH | shrutau tAvat -- anena jIvenAtmanA [chA.u. 6.3.2] iti sargapramukhe shArIram AtmAnaM jIvashabdena prANadhAraNanimittenAbhilapann anAdiH saMsAra iti darshayati | Adimattve tu prAganavadhAritaprANaH san kathaM prANadhAraNanimittena jIvashabdena sargapramukhe.abhilapyeta? na ca dhArayiShyatItyato.abhilapyeta -- anAgatAd dhi sambandhAd atItaH sambandho balIyAn bhavati, abhiniShpannatvAt | sUryAcandramasau dhAtA yathApUrvam akalpayat [R^i.ve. 10.190.3] iti ca mantravarNaH pUrvakalpasadbhAvaM darshayati | smR^itAvapyanAditvaM saMsArasyopalabhyate -- na rUpam asyeha tathopalabhyate nAnto na cAdir na ca sampratiShThA [gItA 15.3] iti | purANe cAtItAnAgatAnAM ca kalpAnAM na parimANam astIti sthApitam ||36||

  -- o)0(o -- 

13. sarvadharmopapattyadhikaraNam || 
|| 2.1.37 || 

sarvadharmopapatteshca || 

cetanaM brahma jagataH kAraNaM prakR^itishcetyasminn avadhArite vedArthe parair upakShiptAn vilakShaNatvAd In doShAn paryahArShId AcAryaH | idAnIM parapakShapratiShedhapradhAnaM prakaraNaM prAripsamANaH svapakShaparigrahapradhAnaM prakaraNam upasaMharati | yasmAd asmin brahmaNi kAraNe parigR^ihyamANe pradarshitena prakAreNa sarve kAraNadharmA upapadyante -- sarvaj~naM sarvashakti mahAmAyaM ca brahma iti, tasmAd anatishaN^kanIyam idam aupaniShadaM darshanam iti ||37|| 

iti shrImatparamahaMsaparivrAjakAcAryasya shrIgovindabhagavatpUjyapAdashiShyasya shrImacchaN^karabhagavataH kR^itau shArIrakamImAMsAsUtrabhAShye 
dvitIyAdhyAyasya prathamaH pAdaH 
|| 2.1 ||

o)0(o
 
(2.2)
 || dvitIyo.adhyAyaH || 
 || dvitIyaH pAdaH || 
1. racanAnupapattyadhikaraNam || 

|| 2.2.1 ||

yadyapIdaM vedAntavAkyAnAm aidamparyaM nirUpayituM shAstraM pravR^ittaM na tarkashAstravat devalAbhir yuktibhiH kaMcit siddhAntaM sAdhayituM dUShayituM vA pravR^ittam, tathApi vedAntavAkyam api vyAcakShANaiH samyagdarshanapratipakShabhUtAni sAMkhyAdidarshanAni nirAkaraNIyANIti tadarthaH paraH pAdaH pravartate |

vedAntArthanirNayasya ca samyagdarshanArthatvAt tannirNayena svapakShasthApanaM prathamaM kR^itaM tad dhyabhyarthitaM parapakShapratyAkhyAnAd iti |

nanu mumukShUNAM mokShasAdhanatvena samyagdarshananirUpaNAya svapakShasthApanam eva kevalaM kartuM yuktaM, kiM parapakShanirAkaraNena paradveShakareNa ? bADham evam, tathApi mahAjanaparigR^ihItAni mahAnti sAMkhyAditantrANi samyagdarshanApadeshena pravR^ittAnyupalabhya bhavet keShAMcin mandamatInAm etAnyapi samyagdarshanAyopadeyAnItyapekShA | tathA yuktagADhatvasambhavena sarvaj~nabhAShitatvAcca shraddhA ca teShvityataH tadasAratopapAdanAya prayatyate |

nanu IkShater nAshabdam [ve.sU. 1.1.5], kAmAcca nAnumAnApekShA [ve.sU. 1.1.18], etena sarve vyAkhyAtA vyAkhyAtAH [ve.sU. 1.4.28] iti ca pUrvatrApi sAMkhyAdipakShapratikShepaH kR^itaH, kiM punaH kR^itakaraNeneti ? tad ucyate -- sAN^khyAdayaH svapakShasthApanAya vedAntavAkyAnyapyudAhR^itya svapakShAnuguNenaiva yojayanto vyAcakShate, teShAM yad vyAkhyAnaM tad vyAkhyanAbhAsaM na samyagvyakhyAnam ityetAvat pUrvaM kR^itam | iha tu vAkyanirapekShaH svatantraH tadyuktipratiShedhaH kriyata ityeSha visheShaH |

racanAnupapatteshca nAnumAnam ||

tatra sAN^khyA manyante -- yathA ghaTasharAvAdayo bhedA mR^idAtmatayAnvIyamAnA mR^idAtmakasAmAnyapUrvakA loke dR^iShTAH, tathA sarva eva bAhyAdhyAtmikA bhedAH sukhaduHkhamohAtmatayAnvIyamAnAH sukhaduHkhamohAtmakasAmAnyapUrvakA bhavitum arhanti | yat sukhaduHkhamohAtmakaM sAmAnyaM tat triguNaM pradhAnaM mR^idvad acetanaM cetanasya puruShasyArthaM sAdhayituM svabhAvenaiva vicitreNa vikArAtmanA pravartata iti | tathA parimANAdibhir api liN^gaiH tad eva pradhAnam anumimate || 

tatra vadAmaH -- yadi dR^iShTAntabalenaivaitan nirUpyeta, nAcetanaM loke cetanAnadhiShThitaM svatantraM kiJNcid vishiShTapuruShArthanirvartanasamarthAn vikArAn viracayad dR^iShTam | gehaprAsAdashayanAsanavihArabhUmyAdayo hi loke praj~nAvadbhiH shilpibhir yathAkAlaM sukhaduHkhaprAptiparihArayogyA racitA dR^ishyante | tathedaM jagad akhilaM pR^ithivyAdi nAnAkarmaphalopabhogayogyaM bAhyam AdhyAtmikaM ca sharIrAdi nAnAjAtyanvitaM pratiniyatAvayavavinyAsam anekakarmaphalAnubhavAdhiShThAnaM dR^ishyamAnaM praj~nAvadbhiH sambhAvitatamaiH shilpibhir manasApyAlocayitum ashakyaM sat katham acetanaM pradhAnaM racayet? loShTapAShANAdiShvadR^iShTatvAt | mR^idAdiShvapi kumbhakArAdyadhiShThiteShu vishiShTAkArA racanA dR^ishyate, tadvat pradhAnasyApi cetanAntarAdhiShThitatvaprasaN^gaH | na ca mR^idAdyupAdAnasvarUpavyapAshrayeNaiva dharmeNa mUlakAraNam avadhAraNIyam, na bAhyakumbhakArAdivyapAshrayeNa -- iti kiMcin niyAmakam asti | na caivaM sati kiJNcid virudhyate, pratyuta shrutir anugR^ihyate, cetanakAraNasamarpaNAt | ato racanAnupapatteshca hetor nAcetanaM jagatkAraNam anumAtavyaM bhavati | anvayAdyanupapatteshceti cashabdena hetor asiddhiM samuccinoti | na hi bAhyAdhyAtmikAnAM bhedAnAM sukhaduHkhamohAtmakatayAnvaya upapadyate, sukhAdInAM cAntaratvapratIteH, shabdAdInAM cAtadrUpatvapratIteH, tannimittatvapratIteshca, shabdAdyavisheShe.api ca bhAvanAvisheShAt sukhAdivisheShopalabdheH | tathA parimitAnAM bhedAnAM mUlAN^kurAdInAM saMsargapUrvakatvaM dR^iShTvA bAhyAdhyAtmikAnAM bhedAnAM parimitatvAt saMsargapUrvakatvam anumimAnasya sattvarajastamasAm api saMsargapUrvakatvaprasaN^gaH, parimitatvAvisheShAt | kAryakAraNabhAvaH tu prekShApUrvakanirmitAnAM shayanAsanAdInAM dR^iShTA iti na kAryakAraNabhAvAd bAhyAdhyAtmikAnAM bhedAnAm acetanapUrvakatvaM shakyaM kalpayitum ||

|| 2.2.2 ||

pravR^itteshca || 

AstAM tAvad iyaM racanA | tatsiddhyarthA yA pravR^ittiH -- sAmyAvasthAnAt pracyutiH, sattvarajastamasAm aN^gAN^gibhAvarUpApattiH, vishiShTakAryAbhimukhapravR^ittitA -- sApi nAcetanasya pradhAnasya svatantrasyopapadyate, mR^idAdiShvadarshanAd rathAdiShu ca | na hi mR^idAdayo rathAdayo vA svayam acetanAH santashcetanaiH kulAlAdibhir ashvAdibhir vAnadhiShThitA vishiShTakAryAbhimukhapravR^ittayo dR^ishyante | dR^iShTAccAdR^iShTasiddhiH | ataH pravR^ittyanupapatter api hetor nAcetanaM jagatkAraNam anumAtavyaM bhavati | 

nanu cetanasyApi pravR^ittiH kevalasya na dR^iShTA -- satyam etat -- tathApi cetanasaMyuktasya rathAder acetanasya pravR^ittir dR^iShTA | na tu acetanasaMyuktasya cetanasya pravR^ittir dR^iShTA | kiM punar atra yuktam -- yasmin pravR^ittir dR^iShTA tasya sA, uta yat samprayuktasya dR^iShTA tasyaiva seti? 

nanu yasmin dR^ishyate pravR^ittiH tasyaiva seti yuktam, ubhayoH pratyakShatvAt | na tu pravR^ittyAshrayatvena kevalashcetano rathAdivat pratyakShaH | pravR^ittyAshrayadehAdisaMyuktasyaiva tu cetanasya sadbhAvasiddhiH -- kevalAcetanarathAdivailakShaNyaM jIvaddehasya dR^iShTam iti | ata eva ca pratyakShe dehe sati caitanyasya darshanAd asati cAdarshanAd dehasyaiva caitanyam apIti lokAyatikAH pratipannAH | tasmAd acetanasyaiva pravR^ittiH iti | 

tad abhidhIyate -- na brUmaH, yasminn acetane pravR^ittir dR^ishyate na tasya seti | bhavatu tasyaiva sA | sA tu cetanAd bhavatIti brUmaH, tadbhAve bhAvAt tadabhAve cAbhAvAt -- yathA kAShThAdivyapAshrayApi dAhaprakAshAdilakShaNA vikriyA, anupalabhyamAnApi ca kevale jvalane, jvalanAd eva bhavati, tatsaMyoge darshanAt tadviyoge cAdarshanAt, tadvat | lokAyatikAnAm api cetana eva deho.acetanAnAM rathAdInAM pravartako dR^iShTa ityavipratiShiddhaM cetanasya pravartakatvam | 

nanu tava dehAdisaMyuktasyApyAtmano vij~nAnasvarUpamAtravyatirekeNa pravR^ittyanupapatter anupapannaM pravartakatvam iti cet, na | ayaskAntavad rUpAdivacca pravR^ittirahitasyApi pravartakatvopapatteH | yathAyaskAnto maNiH svayaM pravR^ittirahito.apyayasaH pravartako bhavati, yathA ca rUpAdayo viShayAH svayaM pravR^ittirahitA api cakShurAdInAM pravartakA bhavanti, evaM pravR^ittirahito.apIshvaraH sarvagataH sarvAtmA sarvaj~naH sarvashaktishca san sarvaM pravartayed ityupapannam | ekatvAt pravartyAbhAve pravartakatvAnupapattiH iti cet, na | avidyApratyupasthApitanAmarUpamAyAveshavashenAsakR^itpratyuktatvAt | tasmAt sambhavati pravR^ittiH sarvaj~nakAraNatve, na tu acetanakAraNatve ||2||

|| 2.2.3 ||

payombuvaccet tatrApi ||

syAd etat -- yathA kShIram acetanaM svabhAvenaiva vatsavivR^iddhyarthaM pravartate, yathA ca jalam acetanaM svabhAvenaiva lokopakArAya syandate, evaM pradhAnam apyacetanaM svabhAvenaiva puruShArthasiddhaye pravartiShyata iti | naitat sAdhUcyate, yataH tatrApi payo.ambunoshcetanAdhiShThitayor eva pravR^ittiH ityanumimImahe, ubhayavAdiprasirA rathAdAvacetane kevale pravR^ittyadarshanAt | shAstraM ca -- yo.apsu tiShThan yo.apo.antaro yamayati [bR^i.A.u. 3.7.4], etasya vA akSharasya prashAsane gArgi prAcyo.anyA nadyaH syandante [bR^i.A.u. 3.8.9] ityevaMjAtIyakaM samastasya lokaparispanditasyeshvarAdhiShThitatAM shrAvayati | tasmAt sAdhyapakShanikShiptatvAt payo.ambuvad ityanupanyAsaH -- cetanAyAshca dhenvAH snehecchayA payasaH pravartakatvopapatteH, vatsacoShaNena ca payasa AkR^iShyamANatvAt | 

na cAmbuno.apyatyantam anapekShA, nimnabhUmyAdyapekShatvAt syandanasya | cetanApekShatvaM tu sarvatropadarshitam | upasaMhAradarshanAn neti cen na kShIravad dhi [ve.sU. 2.1.24] ityatra tu bAhyanimittanirapekSham api svAshrayaM kAryaM bhavatItyetallokadR^iShTyA nidarshitam | shAstradR^iShTyA punaH sarvatraiveshvarApekShatvam ApadyamAnaM na parANudyate ||3||

|| 2.2.4 || 

vyatirekAnavasthiteshcAnapekShatvAt ||

sAN^khyAnAM trayo guNAH sAmyenAvatiShThamAnAH pradhAnam | na tu tadvyatirekeNa pradhAnasya pravartakaM nivartakaM vA kiJNcid bAhyam apekShyam avasthitam asti | puruShaH tUdAsIno na pravartako na nivartakaH -- ityato.anapekShaM pradhAnam | anapekShatvAcca kadAcit pradhAnaM mahadAdyAkAreNa pariNamate, kadAcin na pariNamate, ityetad ayuktam | Ishvarasya tu sarvaj~natvAt sarvashaktitvAn mahAmAyatvAcca pravR^ittyapravR^ittI na virudhyete ||4||

|| 2.2.5 || 

anyatrAbhAvAcca ca tR^iNAdivat ||
