syAd etat -- yathA tR^iNapallavodakAdi nimittAntaranirapekShaM svabhAvAd eva kShIrAdyAkAreNa pariNamate, evaM pradhAnam api mahadAdyAkAreNa pariNaMsyata iti | kathaM ca nimittAntaranirapekShaM tR^iNAdIti gamyate? nimittAntarAnupalambhAt | yadi hi kiMcin nimittAntaram upalabhemahi, tato yathAkAmaM tena tena nimittena tR^iNAdyupAdAya kShIraM sampAdayemahi, na tu sampAdayAmahe | tasmAt svAbhAvikaH tR^iNAdeH pariNAmaH | tathA pradhAnasyApi syAd iti | atrocyate -- bhavet tR^iNAdivat svAbhAvikaH pradhAnasyApi pariNAmaH, yadi tR^iNAder api svAbhAvikaH pariNAmo.abhyupagamyeta, na tu abhyupagamyate, nimittAntaropalabdheH | kathaM nimittAntaropalabdhiH? anyatrAbhAvAt | dhenvaiva hyupabhuktaM tR^iNAdi kShIrIbhavati, na prahINam anaDuhAdyupabhuktaM vA | yadi hi nirnimittam etatsyAt, dhenusharIrasambandhAd anyatrApi tR^iNAdi kShIrIbhavet | 

na ca yathAkAmaM mAnuShair na shakyaM sampAdayitum ityetAvatA nirnimittaM bhavati | bhavati hi kiMcit kAryaM mAnuShasampAdyam, kiJNcid daivasampAdyam, manuShyA api shaknuvantyeva svocitenopAyena tR^iNAdyupAdAya kShIraM sampAdayitum | prabhUtaM hi kShIraM kAmayamAnAH prabhUtaM ghAsaM dhenuM cArayanti | tatashca prabhUtaM kShIraM labhante | tasmAn na tR^iNAdivat svAbhAvikaH pradhAnasya pariNAmaH ||5||

|| 2.2.6 ||

abhyupagame.apyarthAbhAvAt ||

svAbhAvikI pradhAnasya pravR^ittir na bhavatIti sthApitam | athApi nAma bhavataH shraddhAm anurudhyamAnAH svAbhAvikIm eva pradhAnasya pravR^ittim abhyupagacchema, tathApi doSho.anuShajyetaiva | kutaH? arthAbhAvAt | yadi tAvat svAbhAvikI pradhAnasya pravR^ittir na kiJNcid anyad ihApekShata ityucyeta, tato yathaiva sahakAri kiMcin nApekShate, evaM prayojanam api kiMcin nApekShiShyate -- ityataH pradhAnaM puruShasyArthaM sAdhayituM pravartata itIyaM pratij~nA hIyeta | sa yadi brUyAt -- sahakAryeva kevalaM nApekShate, na prayojanam apIti | tathApi pradhAnapravR^itteH prayojanaM vivektavyam -- bhogo vA syAt, apavargo vA, ubhayaM veti | bhogashcet -- kIdR^isho.anAdheyAtishayasya puruShasya bhogo bhavet? anirmokShaprasaN^gashca | apavargashcet -- prAg api pravR^itter apavargasya siddhatvAt pravR^ittir anarthikA syAt, shabdAdyanupalabdhiprasaN^gashca | ubhayArthatAbhyupagame.api bhoktavyAnAM pradhAnamAtrANAm AnantyAd anirmokShaprasaN^ga eva | na cautsukyanivR^ittyarthA pravR^ittiH | na hi pradhAnasyAcetanasyautsukyaM sambhavati | na ca puruShasya nirmalasya | dR^ikshaktisargashaktivaiyarthyabhayAccet pravR^ittiH, tarhi dR^ikshaktyanucchedavat sargashaktyanucchedAt saMsArAnucchedAd anirmokShaprasaN^ga eva | tasmAt pradhAnasya puruShArthA pravR^ittiH ityetad ayuktam ||6||

|| 2.2.7 ||

puruShAshmavad iti cet tathApi ||

syAd etat -- yathA kashcit puruSho dR^ikshaktisampannaH pravR^ittishaktivihInaH paN^guH aparaM puruShaM pravR^ittishaktisampannaM dR^ikshaktivihInam andham adhiShThAya pravartayati, yathA vA ayaskAnto.ashmA svayam apravartamAno.apyayaH pravartayati, evaM puruShaH pradhAnaM pravartayiShyati -- iti dR^iShTAntapratyayena punaH pratyavasthAnam | atrocyate -- tathApi naiva doShAn nirmokSho.asti | abhyupetahAnaM tAvad doSha Apatati, pradhAnasya svatantrasya pravR^ittyabhyupagamAt, puruShasya ca pravartakatvAnabhyupagamAt | kathaM codAsInaH puruShaH pradhAnaM pravartayet? paN^gur api hyandhaM puruShaM vAgAdibhiH pravartayati | naivaM puruShasya kashcid api pravartanavyApAro.asti, niShkriyatvAn nirguNatvAcca | nApyayaskAntavat saMnidhimAtreNa pravartayet, saMnidhinityatvena pravR^ittinityatvaprasaN^gAt | ayaskAntasya tu anityasaMnidher asti svavyApAraH saMnidhiH, parimArjanAdyapekShA cAsyAsti -- ityanupanyAsaH puruShAshmavad iti | tathA pradhAnasyAcaitanyAt puruShasya caudAsInyAt tR^itIyasya ca tayoH sambandhayitur abhAvAt sambandhAnupapattiH | yogyatAnimitte ca sambandhe yogyatAnucchedAd anirmokShaprasaN^gaH | pUrvavaccehApyarthAbhAvo vikalpayitavyaH | paramAtmanaH tu svarUpavyapAshrayam audAsInyam, mAyAvyapAshrayaM ca pravartakatvam -- ityastyatishayaH ||7||

|| 2.2.8 ||

aN^gitvAnupapatteshca ||

itashca na pradhAnasya pravR^ittir avakalpate -- yad dhi sattvarajastamasAm anyonyaguNapradhAnabhAvam utsR^ijya sAmyena svarUpamAtreNAvasthAnam, sA pradhAnAvasthA | tasyAm avasthAyAm anapekShasvarUpANAM svarUpapraNAshabhayAt parasparaM pratyaN^gAN^gibhAvAnupapatteH, bAhyasya ca kasyacit kShobhayitur abhAvAt, guNavaiShamyanimitto mahadAdyutpAdo na syAt ||8||

|| 2.2.9 ||

anyathA.anumitau ca j~nashaktiviyogAt || 

athApi syAt | anyathA vayam anumimImahe -- yathA nAyam anantaro doShaH prasajyeta | na hyanapekShasvabhAvAH kUTasthAshcAsmAbhir guNA abhyupagamyante, pramANAbhAvAt | kAryavashena tu guNAnAM svabhAvo.abhyupagamyate | yathA yathA kAryotpAda upapadyate, tathA tathaiteShAM svabhAvo.abhyupagantavyaH | calaM guNavR^ittam iti cAstyabhyupagamaH | tasmAt sAmyAvasthAyAm api vaiShamyopagamayogyA eva guNA avatiShThanta iti | evam api pradhAnasya j~nashaktiviyogAd racanAnupapattyAdayaH pUrvoktA doShAH tadavasthA eva | j~nashaktim api tu anumimAnaH prativAditvAn nivarteta, cetanam ekam anekaprapaJNcasya jagata upAdAnam iti brahmavAdaprasaN^gAt | vaiShamyopagamayogyA api guNAH sAmyAvasthAyAM nimittAbhAvAn naiva vaiShamyaM bhajeran, bhajamAnA vA nimittAbhAvAvisheShAt sarvadaiva vaiShamyaM bhajeran -- iti prasajyata evAyam anantaro.api doShaH ||9||

|| 2.2.10 ||

parasparaviruddhashcAyaM sAN^khyAnAm abhyupagamaH -- kvacit saptendriyANyanukrAmanti, kvacid ekAdasha | tathA kvacin mahataH tanmAtrasargam upadishanti, kvacid ahaMkArAt | tathA kvacit trINyantaHkaraNAni varNayanti, kvacid ekam iti | prasiddha eva tu shrutyeshvarakAraNavAdinyA virodhaH tadanuvartinyA ca smR^ityA | tasmAd apyasamaJNjasaM sAN^khyAnAM darshanam iti | atrAha -- 

vipratiShedhAccAsamaJNjasam ||

nanvaupaniShadAnAm apyasamaJNjasam eva darshanam, tapyatApakayor jAtyantarabhAvAn abhyupagamAt | ekaM hi brahma sarvAtmakaM sarvasya prapaJNcasya kAraNam abhyupagacchatAm | ekasyaivAtmano visheShau tapyatApakau, na jAtyantarabhUtau ityabhyupagantavyaM syAt | yadi caitau tapyatApakAv ekasyAtmano visheShau syAtAm, sa tAbhyAM tapyatApakAbhyAM na nirmucyeta, iti tApopashAntaye samyagdarshanam upadishacchAstram anarthakaM syAt | na hyauShNyaprakAshadharmasya pradIpasya tadavasthasyaiva tAbhyAM nirmokSha upapadyate | yo.api jalataraN^gavIcIphenAdyupanyAsaH, tatrApi jalAtmana ekasya vIcyAdayo visheShA AvirbhAvatirobhAvarUpeNa nityA eva -- iti samAno jalAtmano vIcyAdibhir anirmokShaH | prasiddhashcAyaM tapyatApakayor jAtyantarabhAvo loke | tathA hi -- arthI cArthashcAnyonyabhinnau lakShyete | yadyarthinaH svato.anyo.artho na syAt, yasyArthino yad viShayam arthitvaM sa tasyArtho nityasiddha eveti, na tasya tadviShayam arthitvaM syAt -- yathA prakAshAtmanaH pradIpasya prakAshAkhyo.artho nityasiddha eveti, na tasya tadviShayam arthitvaM bhavati -- aprApte hyarthe.arthino.arthitvaM syAd iti | tathArthasyApyarthatvaM na syAt | yadi syAt svArthatvam eva syAt | na caitad asti | sambandhishabdau hyetAvarthI cArthashceti | dvayoshca sambandhinoH sambandhaH syAt, naikasyaiva | tasmAd bhinnAv etAvarthArthinau | tathAnarthAnarthinAvapi | arthino.anukUlo.arthaH, pratikUlo.anarthaH | tAbhyAm ekaH paryAyeNobhAbhyAM sambadhyate | tatrArthasyAlpIyastvAt, bhUyastvAccAnarthasya ubhAvapyarthAnarthau anartha eveti -- tApakaH sa ucyate | tapyaH tu puruShaH -- ya ekaH paryAyeNobhAbhyAM sambadhyate -- iti tayoH tapyatApakayor ekAtmatAyAM mokShAnupapattiH | jAtyantarabhAve tu tatsaMyogahetuparihArAt syAd api kadAcin mokShopapattiH iti || 

atrocyate -- na, ekatvAd eva tapyatApakabhAvAnupapatteH -- bhaved eSha doShaH, yadyekAtmatAyAM tapyatApakAvanyonyasya viShayaviShayibhAvaM pratipadyeyAtAm | na tv etad asti, ekatvAd eva | na hyagnir ekaH san svam AtmAnaM dahati, prakAshayati vA, satyapyauShNyaprakAshAdidharmabhede pariNAmitve ca | kim u kUTasthe brahmaNyekasmiMH tapyatApakabhAvaH sambhavet? kva punar ayaM tapyatApakabhAvaH syAd iti | ucyate -- kiM na pashyasi -- karmabhUto jIvaddehaH tapyaH, tApakaH saviteti? 

nanu taptir nAma duHkham | sA cetayituH | nAcetanasya dehasya | yadi hi dehasyaiva taptiH syAt, sA dehanAshe svayam eva nashyatIti tannAshAya sAdhanaM naiShitavyaM syAd iti | ucyate -- dehAbhAve.api kevalasya cetanasya taptir na dR^iShTA | na ca tvayApi taptir nAma vikriyA cetayituH kevalasyeShyate | nApi dehacetanayoH saMhatatvam, ashuddhyAdidoShaprasaN^gAt | na ca tapter eva taptim abhyupagacchasi | kathaM tavApi tapyatApakabhAvaH? sattvaM tapyam, tApakaM rajaH -- iti cet, na | tAbhyAM cetanasya saMhatatvAnupapatteH | sattvAnurodhitvAccetano.api tapyata iveti cet -- paramArthataH tarhi naiva tapyata ityApatati ivashabdaprayogAt | na cet tapyate nevashabdo doShAya | na hi -- DuNDubhaH sarpa iva -- ityetAvatA saviSho bhavati, sarpo vA DuNDubha sarpa iva -- ityetAvatA nirviSho bhavati | atashcAvidyAkR^ito.ayaM tapyatApakabhAvaH, na pAramArthikaH -- ityabhyupagantavyam iti -- naivaM sati mamApi kiJNcid duShyati | atha pAramArthikam eva cetanasya tapyatvam abhyupagacchasi, tavaiva sutarAm anirmokShaH prasajyeta, nityatvAbhyupagamAcca tApakasya | tapyatApakashaktyor nityatve.api, sanimittasaMyogApekShatvAt tapteH, saMyoganimittAdarshananivR^ittau, AtyantikaH saMyogoparamaH, tatashcAtyantiko mokSha upapannaH -- iti cet, na | adarshanasya tamaso nityatvAbhyupagamAt | guNAnAM codbhavAbhibhavayor aniyatatvAd aniyataH saMyoganimittoparama iti viyogasyApyaniyatatvAt sAN^khyasyaivAnirmokSho.aparihAryaH syAt | aupaniShadasya tu AtmaikatvAbhyupagamAt, ekasya ca viShayaviShayibhAvAnupapatteH, vikArabhedasya ca vAcArambhaNamAtratvashravaNAt, anirmokShashaN^kA svapne.api nopajAyaMte | vyavahAre tu -- yatra yathA dR^iShTaH tapyatApakabhAvaH tatra tathaiva saH -- iti na codayitavyaH parihartavyo vA bhavati ||10||

2. mahaddIrghAdhikaraNam

|| 2.2.11 ||

pradhAnakAraNavAdo nirAkR^itaH, paramANukAraNavAda idAnIM nirAkartavyaH | tatrAdau tAvat -- yo.aNuvAdinA brahmavAdini doSha utprekShyate, sa pratisamAdhIyate | tatrAyaM vaisheShikANAm abhyupagamaH -- kAraNadravyasamavAyino guNAH kAryadravye samAnajAtIyaM guNAntaram Arabhante, shuklebhyaH tantubhyaH shuklasya paTasya prasavadarshanAt, tadviparyayAdarshanAcca | tasmAccetanasya brahmaNo jagatkAraNatve.abhyupagamyamAne, kArye.api jagati caitanyaM samaveyAt | tadadarshanAt tu na cetanaM brahma jagatkAraNaM bhavitum arhatIti | imam abhyupagamaM tadIyayaiva prakriyayA vyabhicArayati -- 

mahad dIrghavad vA hrasvaparimaNDalAbhyAm ||

eShA teShAM prakriyA -- paramANavaH kila kaMcit kAlam anArabdhakAryA yathAyogaM rUpAdimantaH pArimANDAlyaparimANAshca tiShThanti | te ca pashcAd adR^iShTAdipuraHsarAH saMyogasacivAshca santo dvyaNukAdikrameNa kR^itsnaM kAryajAtam Arabhante, kAraNaguNAshca kArye guNAntaram | yadA dvau paramANU dvyaNukam Arabhete, tadA paramANugatA rUpAdiguNavisheShAH shuklAdayo dvyaNuke shuklAdIn aparAn Arabhante | paramANuguNavisheShaH tu pArimANDAlyaM na dvyaNuke pArimANDAlyam aparam Arabhate, dvyaNukasya parimANAntarayogAbhyupagamAt | aNutvahrasvatve hi dvyaNukavartinI parimANe varNayanti | yadApi dve dvyaNuke caturaNukam Arabhete, tadApi samAnaM dvyaNukasamavAyinAM shuklAdInAm Arambhakatvam | aNutvahrasvatve tu dvyaNukasamavAyinI api naivArabhete, caturaNukasya mahattvadIrghatvaparimANayogAbhyupagamAt | yadApi bahavaH paramANavaH, bahUni vA dvyaNukAni, dvyaNukasahito vA paramANuH kAryam Arabhate, tadApi samAnaiShA yojanA | tad evaM yathA paramANoH parimaNDalAt sato.aNu hrasvaM ca dvyaNukaM jAyate, mahad dIrghaM ca tryaNukAdi, na parimaNDalam | yathA vA dvyaNukAd aNor hrasvAcca sato mahad dIrghaM ca tryaNukaM jAyate, nANu, no hrasvam | evaM cetanAd brahmaNo.acetanaM jagajjaniShyate -- ityabhyupagame kiM tava cchinnam || 

atha manyase -- virodhinA parimANAntareNAkrAntaM kAryadravyaM dvyaNukAdi -- ityato nArambhakANi kAraNagatAni pArimANDAlyAdIni -- ityabhyupagacchAmi | na tu cetanAvirodhinA guNAntareNa jagata AkrAntatvam asti, yena kAraNagatA cetanA kArye cetanAntaraM nArabheta | na hyacetanA nAma cetanAvirodhI kashcid guNo.asti, cetanApratiShedhamAtratvAt | tasmAt pArimANDAlyAdivaiShamyAt prApnoti cetanAyA Arambhakatvam iti | maivaM maMsthAH -- yathA kAraNe vidyamAnAnAm api pArimANDAlyAdInAm anArambhakatvam, evaM caitanyasyApi -- ityasyAMshasya samAnatvAt | na ca parimANAntarAkrAntatvaM pArimANDAlyAdInAm anArambhakatve kAraNam, prAkparimANAntarArambhAt pArimANDAlyAdInAm ArambhakatvopapatteH, Arabdham api kAryadravyaM prAgguNArambhAt kShaNamAtram aguNaM tiShThatItyabhyupagamAt | na ca parimANAntarArambhe vyagrANi pArimANDAlyAdInItyataH svasamAnajAtIyaM parimANAntaraM nArabhante, parimANAntarasyAnyahetutvAbhyupagamAt | kAraNabahutvAt kAraNamahattvAt pracayavisheShAcca mahat tadviparItam aNu etena dIrghatvahrasvatve vyAkhyAte iti hi kANabhujAni sUtrANi | na ca saMnidhAnavisheShAt kutashcit kAraNabahutvAd InyevArabhante, na pArimANDAlyAdInIti ucyeta, dravyAntare guNAntare vA ArabhyamANe sarveShAm eva kAraNaguNAnAM svAshrayasamavAyAvisheShAt | tasmAt svabhAvAd eva pArimANDAlyAdInAm anArambhakatvam, tathA cetanAyA apIti draShTavyam || 

saMyogAcca dravyAdInAM vilakShaNAnAm utpattidarshanAtsamAnajAtIyotpattivyabhicAraH | dravye prakR^ite guNodAharaNam ayuktam iti cet, na | dR^iShTAntena vilakShaNArambhamAtrasya vivakShitatvAt | na ca dravyasya dravyam evodAhartavyam, guNasya vA guNa eveti kashcin niyame hetur asti | sUtrakAro.api bhavatAM dravyasya guNam udAjahAra -- pratyakShApratyakShANAm apratyakShatvAt saMyogasya paJNcAtmakaM na vidyate iti | yathA pratyakShApratyakShayor bhUmyAkAshayoH samavayan saMyogo.apratyakShaH, evaM pratyakShApratyakSheShu paJNcasu bhUteShu samavayaccharIram apratyakShaM syAt | pratyakShaM hi sharIram, tasmAn na pAJNcabhautikam iti | 

etad uktaM bhavati -- guNashca saMyogo dravyaM sharIram | dR^ishyate tu iti cAtrApi vilakShaNotpattiH prapaJNcitA | nanv evaM sati tenaivaitadgatam | neti brUmaH -- tat sAN^khyaM pratyuktam etat tu vaisheShikaM prati | 

nanvatidesho.api samAnanyAyatayA kR^itaH -- etena shiShTaparigrahA api vyAkhyAtAH iti | satyam etat | tasyaiva tu ayaM vaisheShikaparIkShArambhe tatprakriyAnugatena nidarshanena prapaJNcaH kR^itaH ||11||

3. paramANujagadakAraNatvAdhikaraNam

|| 2.2.12 ||

ubhayathApi na karmAtaH tadabhAvaH ||

idAnIM paramANukAraNavAdaM nirAkaroti | sa ca vAda itthaM samuttiShThati -- paTAdIni hi loke sAvayavAni dravyANi svAnugatair eva saMyogasacivaiH tantvAdibhir dravyair ArabhyamANAni dR^iShTAni | tatsAmAnyena yAvat kiMcit sAvayavam, tat sarvaM svAnugatair eva saMyogasacivaiH taiH tair dravyair Arabdham iti gamyate | sa cAyam avayavAvayavivibhAgo yato nivartate, so.apakarShaparyantagataH paramANuH | sarvaM cedaM girisamudrAdikaM jagat sAvayavam | sAvayatvAccAdyantavat | na cAkAraNena kAryeNa bhavitavyam ityataH paramANavo jagataH kAraNam iti kaNabhugabhiprAyaH | tAnImAni catvAri bhUtAni bhUmyudakatejaHpavanAkhyAni sAvayavAnyupalabhya caturvidhAH paramANavaH parikalpyante | teShAM cApakarShaparyantagatatvena parato vibhAgAsambhavAd vinashyatAM pR^ithivyAdInAM paramANuparyanto vibhAgo bhavati | sa pralayakAlaH | tataH sargakAle ca vAyavIyeShvaNuShvadR^iShTApekShaM karmotpadyate | tat karma svAshrayam aNum aNvantareNa saMyunakti | tato dvyaNukAdikrameNa vAyur utpadyate | evam agniH | evam ApaH | evaM pR^ithivI | evam eva sharIraM sendriyam ityevaM sarvam idaM jagat aNubhyaH sambhavati | aNugatebhyashca rUpAdibhyo dvyaNukAdigatAni rUpAdIni sambhavanti, tantupaTanyAyena -- iti kANAdA manyante || 

tatredam abhidhIyate -- vibhAgAvasthAnAM tAvad aNUnAM saMyogaH karmApekSho.abhyupagantavyaH, karmavatAM tantvAdInAM saMyogadarshanAt | karmaNashca kAryatvAn nimittaM kim apyabhyupagantavyam | anabhyupagame nimittAbhAvAn nANuShvadyaM karma syAt | abhyupagame.api -- yadi prayatno.abhighAtAdir vA yathA dR^iShTaM kim api karmaNo nimittam abhyupagamyeta, tasyAsambhavAn naivANuShvadyaM karma syAt | na hi tasyAm avasthAyAm AtmaguNaH prayatnaH sambhavati, sharIrAbhAvAt | sharIrapratiShThe hi manasyAtmanaH saMyoge sati AtmaguNaH prayatno jAyate | etenAbhighAtAdyapi dR^iShTaM nimittaM pratyAkhyAtavyam | sargottarakAlaM hi tat sarvaM nAdyasya karmaNo nimittaM sambhavati | 

athAdR^iShTam Adyasya karmaNo nimittam ityucyeta -- tat punar AtmasamavAyi vA syAt? aNusamavAyi vA? ubhayathApi nAdR^iShTanimittam aNuShu karmAvakalpeta, adR^iShTasyAcetanatvAt | na hyacetanaM cetanenAnadhiShThitaM svatantraM pravartate pravartayati veti sAN^khyaparIkShAyAm abhihitam | AtmanashcAnutpannacaitanyasya tasyAm avasthAyAm acetanatvAt | AtmasamavAyitvAbhyupagamAcca nAdR^iShTam aNuShu karmaNo nimittaM syAt, asambandhAt | 

adR^iShTavatA puruSheNAstyaNUnAM sambandha iti cet -- sambandhasAtatyAt pravR^ittisAtatyaprasaN^gaH, niyAmakAntarAbhAvAt | tad evaM niyatasya kasyacit karmanimittasyAbhAvAn nANuShvadyaM karma syAt | karmAbhAvAt tannibandhanaH saMyogo na syAt | 

saMyogAbhAvAcca tannibandhanaM dvyaNukAdi kAryajAtaM na syAt | saMyogashcANor aNvantareNa sarvAtmanA vA syAt? ekadeshena vA? sarvAtmanA cet, upacayAnupapatter aNumAtratvaprasaN^gaH, dR^iShTaviparyayaprasaN^gashca, pradeshavato dravyasya pradeshavatA dravyAntareNa saMyogasya dR^iShTatvAt | ekadeshena cet, sAvayavatvaprasaN^gaH | paramANUnAM kalpitAH pradeshAH syuH iti cet, kalpitAnAm avastutvAd avastv eva saMyoga iti vastunaH kAryasyAsamavAyikAraNaM na syAt | asati cAsamavAyikAraNe dvyaNukAdikAryadravyaM notpadyeta | yathA cAdisarge nimittAbhAvAt saMyogotpattyarthaM karma nANUnAM sambhavati, evaM mahApralaye.api vibhAgotpattyarthaM karma naivANUnAM sambhavet | na hi tatrApi kiMcin niyataM tan nimittaM dR^iShTam asti | adR^iShTam api bhogaprasiddhyartham, na pralayaprasiddhyartham -- ityato nimittAbhAvAn na syAdaNUnAM saMyogotpattyarthaM vibhAgotpattyarthaM vA karma | atashca saMyogavibhAgAbhAvAttadAyattayoH sargapralayayor abhAvaH prasajyeta | tasmAd anupapanno.ayaM paramANukAraNavAdaH ||12||

 || 2.2.13 ||

samavAyAbhyupagamAcca sAmyAd anavasthiteH ||

samavAyAbhyupagamAcca tadabhAva iti prakR^itenANuvAdanirAkaraNena sambadhyate | dvAbhyAM cANubhyAM dvyaNukam utpadyamAnam atyantabhinnam aNubhyAm aNvoH samavaitItyabhyupagamyate bhavatA | na caivam abhyupagacchatA shakyate.aNukAraNatA samarthayitum | kutaH? sAmyAd anavasthiteH | yathaiva hyaNubhyAm atyantabhinnaM sad dvyaNukaM samavAyalakShaNena sambandhena tAbhyAM sambadhyate, evaM samavAyo.api samavAyibhyo.atyantabhinnaH san samavAyalakShaNenAnyenaiva sambandhena samavAyibhiH sambadhyeta, atyantabhedasAmyAt | tatashca tasya tasyAnyo.anyaH sambandhaH kalpayitavya ityanavasthaiva prasajyeta |

nanu iha pratyayagrAhyaH samavAyo nityasambaddha eva samavAyibhir gR^ihyate, nAsambaddhaH, sambandhAntarApekSho vA | tatashca na tasyAnyaH sambandhaH kalpayitavyaH yenAnavasthA prasajyeteti | netyucyate | saMyogo.apyevaM sati saMyogibhir nityasambaddha eveti samavAyavan nAnyaM sambandham apekSheta | athArthAntaratvAt saMyogaH sambandhAntaram apekSheta, samavAyo.api tarhyarthAntaratvAt sambandhAntaram apekSheta | 

na ca guNatvAt saMyogaH sambandhAntaram apekShate, na samavAyo.aguNatvAd iti yujyate vaktum | apekShAkAraNasya tulyatvAt, guNaparibhAShAyAshcAtantratvAt | tasmAd arthAntaraM samavAyam abhyupagacchataH prasajyetaivAnavasthA | prasajyamAnAyAM cAnavasthAyAm ekAsiddhau sarvAsiddher dvAbhyAm aNubhyAM dvyaNukaM naivotpadyeta | tasmAd apyanupapannaH paramANukAraNavAdaH ||13||

|| 2.2.14 ||

nityam eva ca bhAvAt ||

api cANavaH pravR^ittisvabhAvA vA, nivR^ittisvabhAvA vA, ubhayasvabhAvA vA, anubhayasvabhAvA vA abhyupagamyante -- gatyantarAbhAvAt | caturdhApi nopapadyate -- pravR^ittisvabhAvatve nityam eva pravR^itter bhAvAt pralayAbhAvaprasaN^gaH | nivR^ittisvabhAvatve.api nityam eva nivR^itter bhAvAt sargAbhAvaprasaN^gaH | ubhayasvabhAvatvaM ca virodhAd asamaJNjasam | anubhayasvabhAvatve tu nimittavashAt pravR^ittinivR^ittyor abhyupagamyamAnayor adR^iShTAder nimittasya nityasaMnidhAnAn nityapravR^ittiprasaN^gaH, atantratve.apyadR^iShTAder nityApravR^ittiprasaN^gaH | tasmAd apyanupapannaH paramANukAraNavAdaH ||14||

|| 2.2.15 ||

rUpAdimatvAcca viparyayo darshanAt ||

sAvayavAnAM dravyANAm avayavasho vibhajyamAnAnAM yataH paro vibhAgo na sambhavati te caturvidhA rUpAdimantaH paramANavashcaturvidhasya rUpAdimato bhUtabhautikasyArambhakA nityAshceti yad vaisheShikA abhyupagacchanti, sa teShAm abhyupagamo nirAlambana eva | yato rUpAdimattvAt paramANUnAm aNutvanityatvaviparyayaH prasajyeta | paramakAraNApekShayA sthUlatvam anityatvaM ca teShAm abhipretaviparItam ApadyetetyarthaH | kutaH? evaM loke dR^iShTatvAt  -- yad dhi loke rUpAdimad vastu tat svakAraNApekShayA sthUlam anityaM ca dR^iShTam | tad yathA -- paTaH tantUn apekShya sthUlo.anityashca bhavati | tantavashcAMshUn apekShya sthUlA anityAshca bhavanti -- tathA cAmI paramANavo rUpAdimantaH tair abhyupagamyante | tasmAt te.api kAraNavantaH tadapekShayA sthUlA anityAshca prApnuvanti | yacca nityatve kAraNaM tair uktam -- sadakAraNavan nityam iti, tad apyevaM sati aNuShu na sambhavati, uktena prakAreNANUnAm api kAraNavattvopapatteH | yad api nityatve dvitIyaM kAraNam uktam -- anityam iti ca visheShataH pratiShedhAbhAvaH iti, tad api nAvashyaM paramANUnAM nityatvaM sAdhayati | asati hi yasmin kasmiMshcin nitye vastuni nityashabdena naJNaH samAso nopapadyate | 

na punaH paramANunityatvam evApekShyate | taccAstyeva nityaM paramakAraNaM brahma | na ca shabdArthavyavahAramAtreNa kasyacid arthasya prasiddhir bhavati, pramANAntarasiddhayoH shabdArthayor vyavahArAvatArAt | yad api nityatve tR^itIyaM kAraNam uktam -- avidyA ca iti -- tad yadyevaM vivrIyeta -- satAM paridR^ishyamAnakAryANAM kAraNAnAM pratyakSheNAgrahaNam avidyeti, tato dvyaNukanityatApyApadyeta | 

athAdravyatve satIti visheShyeta, tathApyakAraNavattvam eva nityatAnimittam Apadyeta, tasya ca prAg evoktatvAt avidyA ca iti punar uktaM syAt | athApi kAraNavibhAgAt kAraNavinAshAccAnyasya tR^itIyasya vinAshahetor asambhavo.avidyA, sA paramANUnAM nityatvaM khyApayati -- iti vyAkhyAyeta -- nAvashyaM vinashyadvastu dvAbhyAm eva hetubhyAM vinaShTum arhatIti niyamo.asti | saMyogasacive hyanekasmiMshca dravye dravyAntarasyArambhake.abhyupagamyamAna etad evaM syAt | yadA tu apAstavisheShaM sAmAnyAtmakaM kAraNaM visheShavad avasthAntaram ApadyamAnam Arambhakam abhyupagamyate, tadA ghR^itakAThinyavilayanavan mUrtyavasthAvilayanenApi vinAsha upapadyate | tasmAd rUpAdimattvAt syAd abhipretaviparyayaH paramANUnAm | tasmAd apyanupapannaH paramANukAraNavAdaH ||15||

|| 2.2.16 ||

ubhayathA ca doShAt ||

gandharasarUpasparshaguNA sthUlA pR^ithivI, rUparasasparshaguNAH sUkShmA ApaH, rUpasparshaguNaM sUkShmataraM tejaH, sparshaguNaH sUkShmatamo vAyuH -- ityevam etAni catvAri bhUtAnyupacitApacitaguNAni sthUlasUkShmasUkShmatarasUkShmatamatAratamyopetAni ca loke lakShyante | tadvat paramANavo.apyupacitApacitaguNAH kalperan na vA | ubhayathApi ca doShAnuShaN^go.aparihArya eva syAt | kalpyamAne tAvad upacitApacitaguNatve, upacitaguNAnAM mUrtyupacayAd aparamANutvaprasaN^gaH | na cAntareNApi mUrtyupacayaM guNopacayo bhavatItyucyeta, kAryeShu bhUteShu guNopacaye mUrtyupacayadarshanAt | akalpyamAne tUpacitApacitaguNatve -- paramANutvasAmyaprasiddhaye yadi tAvat sarva ekaikaguNA eva kalpyeran, tataH tejasi sparshasyopalabdhir na syAt, apsu rUpasparshayoH, pR^ithivyAM ca rasarUpasparshAnAm, kAraNaguNapUrvakatvAt kAryaguNAnAm | atha sarve caturguNA eva kalpyeran, tato.apsvapi gandhasyopalabdhiH syAt, tejasi gandharasayoH, vAyau ca gandharUparasAnAm | na caivaM dR^ishyate | tasmAd apyanupapannaH paramANukAraNavAdaH ||16||

|| 2.2.17 ||

aparigrahAccAtyantam anapekShA ||

pradhAnakAraNavAdo vedavidbhir api kaishcin manvAdibhiH satkAryatvAdyaMshopajIvanAbhiprAyeNopanibaddhaH | ayaM tu paramANukAraNavAdo na kaishcid api shiShTaiH kenacid apyaMshena parigR^ihIta ityatyantam evAnAdaraNIyo vedavAdibhiH | api ca vaisheShikAH tantrArthabhUtAn ShaTpadArthAn dravyaguNakarmasAmAnyavisheShasamavAyAkhyAn atyantabhinnAn bhinnalakShaNAn abhyupagacchanti -- yathA manuShyo.ashvaH shasha iti | tathAtvaM cAbhyupagamya tadviruddhaM dravyAdhInatvaM sheShANAm abhyupagacchanti | tan nopapadyate | katham? yathA hi loke shashakushapalAshaprabhR^itInAm atyantabhinnAnAM satAM netaretarAdhInatvaM bhavati, evaM dravyAdInAm apyatyantabhinnatvAt, naiva dravyAdhInatvaM guNAdInAM bhavitum arhati | atha bhavati dravyAdhInatvaM guNAdInAm, tato dravyabhAve bhAvAd dravyAbhAve.abhAvAd dravyam eva saMsthAnAdibhedAd anekashabdapratyayabhAg bhavati -- yathA devadatta eka eva san avasthAntarayogAd anekashabdapratyayabhAg bhavati, tadvat | tathA sati sAN^khyasiddhAntaprasaN^gaH svasiddhAntavirodhashcApadyeyAtAm | 

nanvagner anyasyApi sato dhUmasyAgnyadhInatvaM dR^ishyate | satyaM dR^ishyate | bhedapratItestu tatrAgnidhUmayor anyatvaM nishcIyate | iha tu shuklaH kambalaH, rohiNI dhenuH, nIlam utpalam -- iti dravyasyaiva tasya tasya tena tena visheShaNena pratIyamAnatvAt, naiva dravyaguNayor agnidhUmayoH iva bhedapratItir asti | tasmAd dravyAtmakatA guNasya | etena karmasAmAnyavisheShasamavAyAnAM dravyAtmakatA vyAkhyAtA || 

guNAnAM dravyAdhInatvaM dravyaguNayor ayutasiddhatvAd iti yadyucyeta, tat punar ayutasiddhatvam apR^ithagdeshatvaM vA syAt, apR^ithakkAlatvaM vA, apR^ithaksvabhAvatvaM vA | sarvathApi nopapadyate -- apR^ithagdeshatve tAvat svAbhyupagamo virudhyeta | katham? tantvArabdho hi paTaH tantudesho.abhyupagamyate, na paTadeshaH | paTasya tu guNAH shuklatvAd ayaH paTadeshA abhyupagamyante, na tantudeshAH | tathA cAhuH -- dravyANi dravyAntaram Arabhante guNAshca guNAntaram iti | tantavo hi kAraNadravyANi kAryadravyaM paTam Arabhante, tantugatAshca guNAH shuklAdayaH kAryadravye paTo shuklAdiguNAntaram Arabhante -- iti hi te.abhyupagacchanti | so.abhyupagamo dravyaguNayor apR^ithagdeshatve.abhyupagamyamAne bAdhyeta | atha apR^ithakkAlatvam ayutasiddhatvam ucyeta, savyadakShiNayor api goviShANayor ayutasiddhatvaM prasajyeta | tathA apR^ithaksvabhAvatve tu ayutasiddhatve, na dravyaguNayor AtmabhedaH sambhavati, tasya tAdAtmyenaiva pratIyamAnatvAt || 

yutasiddhayoH sambandhaH saMyogaH, ayutasiddhayoH tu samavAyaH -- ityayam abhyupagamo mR^iShaiva teShAm, prAksiddhasya kAryAt kAraNasyAyutasiddhatvAnupapatteH | athAnyatarApekSha evAyam abhyupagamaH syAt -- ayutasiddhasya kAryasya kAraNena sambandhaH samavAya iti, evam api prAgasiddhasyAlabdhAtmakasya kAryasya kAraNena sambandho nopapadyate, dvayAyattatvAt sambandhasya | siddhaM bhUtvA sambadhyata iti cet, prAkkAraNasambandhAt kAryasya siddhAvabhyupagamyamAnAyAm ayutasiddhyabhAvAt, kAryakAraNayoH saMyogavibhAgau na vidyete itIdam uktaM duruktaM syAt | yathA cotpannamAtrasyAkriyasya kAryadravyasya vibhubhir AkAshAdibhir dravyAntaraiH sambandhaH saMyoga evAbhyupagamyate, na samavAyaH, evaM kAraNadravyeNApi sambandhaH saMyoga eva syAt, na samavAyaH | nApi saMyogasya samavAyasya vA sambandhasya sambandhivyatirekeNAstitve kiMcit pramANam asti | sambandhishabdapratyayavyatirekeNa saMyogasamavAyashabdapratyayadarshanAt tayor astitvam iti cet, na | ekatve.api svarUpabAhyarUpApekShayA anekashabdapratyayadarshanAt | yathaiko.api san devadatto loke svarUpaM sambandhirUpaM cApekShya anekashabdapratyayabhAg bhavati -- manuShyo brAhmaNaH shrotriyo vadAnyo bAlo yuvA sthaviraH pitA putraH pautro bhrAtA jAmAteti, yathA caikApi satI rekhA sthAnAnyatvena nivishamAnA ekadashashatasahasrAdishabdapratyayabhedam anubhavati, tathA sambandhinor eva sambandhishabdapratyayavyatirekeNa saMyogasamavAyashabdapratyayArhatvam, na vyatiriktavastvastitvena -- ityupalabdhilakShaNaprAptasyAnupalabdheH abhAvaH vastvantarasya | 

nApi sambandhiviShayatve sambandhashabdapratyayayoH saMtatabhAvaprasaN^gaH | svarUpabAhyarUpApekShayeti -- uktottaratvAt | tathANvAtmamanasAmapradeshatvAn na saMyogaH sambhavati, pradeshavato dravyasya pradeshavatA dravyAntareNa saMyogadarshanAt | kalpitAH pradeshA aNvAtmamanasAM bhaviShyantIti cet, na | avidyamAnArthakalpanAyAM sarvArthasiddhiprasaN^gAt, iyAnevAvidyamAno viruddho.aviruddho vA arthaH kalpanIyaH, nAto.adhikaH -- iti niyamahetvabhAvAt, kalpanAyAshca svAyattatvAt prabhUtatvasambhavAcca -- na ca vaisheShikaiH kalpitebhyaH ShaDabhyaH padArthebhyo.anye.adhikAH shataM sahasraM vA arthA na kalpayitavyA iti nivArako hetur asti | tasmAd yasmai yasmai yadyadrocate tat tat sidhyet | kashcitkR^ipAluH prANinAM duHkhabahulaH saMsAra eva mA bhUd iti kalpayet | anyo vA vyasanI muktAnAm api punar utpattiM kalpayet | kaH tayor nivArakaH syAt | 

kiM cAnyat | dvAbhyAM paramANubhyAM niravayavAbhyAM sAvayavasya dvyaNukasyAkAsheneva saMshleShAnupapattiH | na hyAkAshasya pR^ithivyAdInAM ca jatukAShThavatsaMshleSho.asti | kAryakAraNadravyayor AshritAshrayabhAvo.anyathA nopapadyata ityavashyaM kalpyaH samavAya iti cet, na | itaretarAshrayatvAt  -- kAryakAraNayor hi bhedasiddhAvAshritAshrayabhAvasiddhiH, AshritAshrayabhAvasiddhau ca tayor bhedasiddhiH -- kuNDabadaravat -- itItaretarAshrayatA syAt | na hi kAryakAraNayor bheda AshritAshrayabhAvo vA vedAntavAdibhir abhyupagamyate, kAraNasyaiva saMsthAnamAtraM kAryam ityabhyupagamAt || 

kiM cAnyat | paramANUnAM paricchinnatvAt, yAvatyo dishaH -- ShaT aShTau dasha vAtAvadbhir avayavaiH sAvayavAste syuH, sAvayavatvAd anityAshca -- iti nityatvaniravayavatvAbhyupagamo bAdhyeta | yAMstvaM digbhedabhedino.avayavAnkalpayasi, ta eva paramANava iti cet, na | sthUlasUkShmatAratamyakrameNa A paramakAraNAdvinAshopapatteH -- yathA pR^ithivI dvyaNukAdyapekShayA sthUlatamA vastubhUtApi vinashyati, tataH sUkShmaM sUkShmataraM ca pR^ithivyekajAtIyakaM vinashyati, tataH dvyaNukam, tathA paramANavo.api pR^ithivyekajAtIyakatvAd vinashyeyuH | vinashyanto.apyavayavavibhAgenaiva vinashyantIti cet, nAyaM doShaH | yato ghR^itakAThinyavilayanavad api vinAshopapattimavocAma -- yathA hi ghR^itasuvarNAdInAmavibhajyamAnAvayavAnAm apyagnisaMyogAt dravabhAvApattyA kAThinyavinAsho bhavati, evaM paramANUnAm api paramakAraNabhAvApattyA mUrtyAdivinAsho bhaviShyati | tathA kAryArambho.api nAvayavasaMyogenaiva kevalena bhavati, kShIrajalAdInAmantareNApyavayavasaMyogAntaraM dadhihimAdikAryArambhadarshanAt | tad evam asArataratarkasandR^ibdhatvAd IshvarakAraNashrutiviruddhatvAcchrutipravaNaishca shiShTair manvAdibhir aparigR^ihItatvAd atyantam evAnapekShA asmin paramANukAraNavAde kAryAkAryaiH shreyo.arthibhiH iti vAkyasheShaH ||17||

3. samudAyAdhikaraNam

|| 2.2.18 ||

samudAya ubhayahetuke.api tadaprAptiH ||

vaisheShikarAddhAnto duryuktiyogAd vedavirodhAcchiShTaparigrahAcca nApekShitavya ityuktam | so.ardhavainAshika iti vainAshikatvasAmyAt sarvavainAshikarAddhAnto natarAm apekShitavya itIdam idAnIm upapAdayAmaH | sa ca bahuprakAraH, pratipattibhedAd vineyabhedAd vA | tatraite trayo vAdino bhavanti -- kecit sarvAstitvavAdinaH | kecid vij~nAnAstitvamAtravAdinaH | anye punaH sarvashUnyatvavAdina iti | tatra ye sarvAstitvavAdino bAhyam AntaraM ca vastu abhyupagacchanti, bhUtaM bhautikaM ca, cittaM caittaM ca, tAMH tAvat prati brUmaH | tatra bhUtaM pR^ithivIdhAtvAdayaH, bhautikaM rUpAdayashcakShurAdayashca, catuShTaye ca pR^ithivyAdiparamANavaH kharasnehoShNeraNasvabhAvAH, te pR^ithivyAdibhAvena saMhanyante -- iti manyante | tathA rUpavij~nAnavedanAsaMj~nAsaMskArasaMj~nakAH paJNcaskandhAH, te.apyAdhyAtmaM sarvavyavahArAspadabhAvena saMhanyante -- iti manyante || 

tatredam abhidhIyate -- yo.ayam ubhayahetuka ubhayaprakAraH samudAyaH pareShAm abhipretaH -- aNuhetukashca bhUtabhautikasaMhatirUpaH, skandhahetukashca paJNcaskandhI rUpaH -- tasminn ubhayahetuke.api samudAye.abhipreyamANe, tadaprAptiH syAt -- samudAyAprAptiH samudAyabhAvAnupapattiH ityarthaH | kutaH? samudAyinAm acetanatvAt, cittAbhijvalanasya ca samudAyasiddhyadhInatvAt, anyasya ca kasyaciccetanasya bhoktuH prashAsitur vA sthirasya saMhantur anabhyupagamAt, nirapekShapravR^ittyabhyupagame ca pravR^ittyanuparam aprasaN^gAt, AshayasyApyanyatvAnanyatvAbhyAm anirUpyatvAt, kShaNikatvAbhyupagamAcca nirvyApAratvAt pravR^ittyanupapatteH | tasmAt samudAyAnupapattiH | samudAyAnupapattau ca tadAshrayA lokayAtrA lupyeta ||18||

|| 2.2.19 ||

itaretarapratyayatvAd iti cen notpattimAtranimittatvAt ||

yadyapi bhoktA prashAsitA vA kashciccetanaH saMhantA sthiro nAbhyupagamyate, tathApyavidyAdInAm itaretarakAraNatvAd upapadyate lokayAtrA | tasyAM copapadyamAnAyAM na kiJNcid aparam apekShitavyam asti | te cAvidyAdayaH -- avidyA saMskAraH vij~nAnaM nAma rUpaM ShaDAyatanaM sparshaH vedanA tR^iShNA upAdAnaM bhavaH jAtiH jarA maraNaM shokaH paridevanA duHkhaM durmanastA -- ityevaMjAtIyakA itaretarahetukAH saugate samaye kvacit saMkShiptA nirdiShTaH, kvacit prapaJNcitAH | sarveShAm apyayam avidyAdikalApo.apratyAkhyeyaH | 

tad evam avidyAdikalApe parasparanimittanaimittikabhAvena ghaTI yantravad anisham AvartamAne.arthAkShipta upapannaH saMghAta iti cet, tan na | kasmAt? utpattimAtranimittatvAt | bhaved upapannaH saMghAtaH, yadi saMghAtasya kiMcin nimittam avagamyeta | na tu avagamyate | yata itaretarapratyayatve.apyavidyAdInAM pUrvapUrvam uttarottarasyotpattimAtranimittaM bhavat bhavet, na tu saMghAtotpatteH kiMcin nimittaM sambhavati | 

nanvavidyAdibhir arthAd AkShipyate saMghAta ityuktam | atrocyate -- yadi tAvad ayam abhiprAyaH -- avidyAdayaH saMghAtam antareNAtmAnam alabhamAnA apekShante saMghAtam iti, tataH tasya saMghAtasya kiMcin nimittaM vaktavyam | tacca nityeShvapyaNuShvabhyugamyamAneShvashrayAshrayibhUteShu ca bhoktR^iShu satsu na sambhavatItyuktaM vaisheShikaparIkShAyAm | kim aN^ga punaH kShaNikeShvapyaNuShu bhoktR^irahiteShvashrayAshrayishUnyeShu vAbhyupagamyamAneShu sambhavet? 

athAyam abhiprAyaH -- avidyAdaya eva saMghAtasya nimittam iti, kathaM tam evAshrityAtmAnaM labhamAnAH tasyaiva nimittaM syuH? atha manyase -- saMghAtA evAnAdau saMsAre saMtatyAnuvartante, tadAshrayAshcAvidyAdaya iti, tadApi saMghAtAt saMghAtAntaram utpadyamAnaM niyamena vA sadR^isham evotpadyeta, aniyamena vA sadR^ishaM visadR^ishaM votpadyeta | niyamAbhyupagame manuShyapudgalasya devatiryagyoninArakaprAptyabhAvaH prApnuyAt | aniyamAbhyupagame.api manuShyapudgalaH kadAcit kShaNena hastI bhUtvA devo vA punar manuShyo vA bhaved iti prApnuyAt | ubhayam apyabhyupagamaviruddham | 

api ca yad bhogArthaH saMghAtaH syAt, sa jIvo nAsti sthiro bhoktA iti tavAbhyupagamaH | tatashca bhogo bhogArtha eva, sa nAnyena prArthanIyaH | tathA mokSho mokShArtha eveti mumukShuNA nAnyena bhavitavyam | anyena cet prArthyetobhayam, bhogamokShakAlAvasthAyinA tena bhavitavyam | avasthAyitve kShaNikatvAbhyupagamavirodhaH | tasmAd itaretarotpattimAtranimittatvam avidyAdInAM yadi bhavet, bhavatu nAma | na tu saMghAtaH sidhyet, bhoktrabhAvAt -- ityabhiprAyaH ||19||

|| 2.2.20 ||

uttarotpAde ca pUrvanirodhAt ||

uktam etat -- avidyAdInAm utpattimAtranimittatvAn na saMghAtasiddhir astIti | tad api tu utpattimAtranimittatvaM na sambhavatItIdam idAnIm upapAdyate | kShaNabhaN^gavAdino.ayam abhyupagamaH -- uttarasmin kShaNe utpadyamAne pUrvaH kShaNo nirudhyata iti | na caivam abhyupagacchatA pUrvottarayoH kShaNayor hetuphalabhAvaH shakyate sampAdayitum, nirudhyamAnasya niruddhasya vA pUrvakShaNasyAbhAvagrastatvAd uttarakShaNahetutvAnupapatteH | atha bhAvabhUtaH pariniShpannAvasthaH pUrvakShaNa uttarakShaNasya hetuH ityabhiprAyaH, tathApi nopapadyate, bhAvabhUtasya punar vyApArakalpanAyAM kShaNAntarasambandhaprasaN^gAt | 

atha bhAva evAsya vyApAra ityabhiprAyaH, tathApi naivopapadyate, hetusvabhAvAnuparaktasya phalasyotpattyasambhavAt | svabhAvoparAgAbhyupagame ca, hetusvabhAvasya phalakAlAvasthAyitve sati, kShaNabhaN^gAbhyupagamatyAgaprasaN^gaH | vinaiva vA svabhAvoparAgeNa hetuphalabhAvam abhyupagacchataH sarvatra tatprApter atiprasaN^gaH | api cotpAdanirodhau nAma vastunaH svarUpam eva vA syAtAm, avasthAntaraM vA, vastvantaram eva vA -- sarvathApi nopapadyate | yadi tAvad vastunaH svarUpam evotpAdanirodhau syAtAm, tato vastushabda utpAdanirodhashabdau ca paryAyAH prApnuyuH | 

athAsti kashcid visheSha iti manyeta -- utpAdanirodhashabdAbhyAM madhyavartino vastuna AdyantAkhye avasthe abhilapyete iti, evam apyAdyantamadhyakShaNatrayasambandhitvAd vastunaH kShaNikatvAbhyupagamahAniH | athAtyantavyatiriktAv evotpAdanirodhau vastunaH syAtAm -- ashvamahiShavat, tato vastu utpAdanirodhAbhyAm asaMspR^iShTam iti vastunaH shAshvatatvaprasaN^gaH | yadi ca darshanAdarshane vastuna utpAdanirodhau syAtAm, evam api draShTR^idharmau tau na vastudharmAviti vastunaH shAshvatatvaprasaN^ga eva | tasmAd apyasaN^gataM saugataM matam ||20||

|| 2.2.21 ||

asati pratij~noparodho yaugapadyam anyathA ||

kShaNabhaN^gavAde pUrvakShaNo nirodhagrastatvAn nottarasya kShaNasya hetur bhavatItyuktam | athAsatyeva hetau phalotpattiM brUyAt, tataH pratij~noparodhaH syAt -- caturvidhAn hetUn pratItya cittacaittA utpadyanta itIyaM pratij~nA hIyeta | nirhetukAyAM cotpattAvapratibandhAt sarvaM sarvatrotpadyeta | athottarakShaNotpattir yAvat tAvad avatiShThate pUrvakShaNa iti brUyAt, tato yaugapadyaM hetuphalayoH syAt | tathApi pratij~noparodha eva syAt -- kShaNikAH sarve saMskArA itIyaM pratij~noparudhyeta ||21||


|| 2.2.22 ||

pratisaN^khyApratisaN^khyAnirodhA prAptir avicchedAt ||

api ca vainAshikAH kalpayanti -- buddhibodhyaM trayAd anyat saMskR^itaM kShaNikaM ca iti | tad api ca trayam -- pratisaMkhyApratisaMkhyAnirodhau AkAshaM cetyAcakShate | trayam api caitat avastu abhAvamAtraM nirupAkhyam iti manyante | buddhipUrvakaH kila vinAsho bhAvAnAM pratisaMkhyAnirodho nAma bhAShyate | tadviparIto.apratisaMkhyAnirodhaH | AvaraNAbhAvamAtram AkAsham iti | teShAm AkAshaM parastAt pratyAkhyAsyati | nirodhadvayam idAnIM pratyAcaShTe -- pratisaMkhyApratisaMkhyAnirodhayoH aprAptir asambhava ityarthaH | kasmAt? avicchedAt -- etau hi pratisaMkhyApratisaMkhyAnirodhau santAnagocarau vA syAtAm, bhAvagocarau vA | na tAvat santAnagocarau sambhavataH, sarveShvapi santAneShu santAninAm avicchinnena hetuphalabhAvena santAnavicchedasyAsambhavAt | 

nApi bhAvagocarau sambhavataH -- na hi bhAvAnAM niranvayo nirupAkhyo vinAshaH sambhavati, sarvAsvapyavasthAsu pratyabhij~nAnabalenAnvayyavicchedadarshanAt, aspaShTapratyabhij~nAnAsvapyavasthAsu kvacid dR^iShTenAnvayyavicchedenAnyatrApi tadanumAnAt | tasmAt paraparikalpitasya nirodhadvayasyAnupapattiH ||22||

|| 2.2.23 || 

ubhayathA ca doShAt ||

yo.ayam avidyAdinirodhaH pratisaMkhyAnirodhAntaHpAtI paraparikalpitaH, sa samyagj~nAnAd vA saparikarAt syAt | svayam eva vA -- pUrvasmin vikalpe nirhetukavinAshAbhyupagamahAniprasaN^gaH | uttarasmiMH tu mArgopadeshAnarthakyaprasaN^gaH | evam ubhayathApi doShaprasaN^gAd asamaJNjasam idaM darshanam ||23||

|| 2.2.24 ||

AkAshe cAvisheShAt || 

yacca teShAm evAbhipretaM nirodhadvayam AkAshaM ca nirupAkhyam iti -- tatra nirodhadvayasya nirupAkhyatvaM purastAn nirAkR^itam | AkAshasyedAnIM nirAkriyate | AkAshe cAyukto nirupAkhyatvAbhyupagamaH, pratisaMkhyApratisaMkhyAnirodhayoH iva vastutvapratipatter avisheShAt | AgamaprAmANyAt tAvat Atmana AkAshaH sambhUtaH ityAdi shrutibhya AkAshasya ca vastutvaprasiddhiH | vipratipannAn prati tu shabdaguNAnumeyatvaM vaktavyam -- gandhAdInAM guNAnAM pR^ithivyAdivastvAshrayatvadarshanAt | 

api ca AvaraNAbhAvamAtram AkAsham icchatAm, ekasmin suparNe patatyAvaraNasya vidyamAnatvAt suparNAntarasyotpitsato.anavakAshatvaprasaN^gaH | yatrAvaraNAbhAvaH tatra patiShyatIti cet -- yenAvaraNAbhAvo visheShyate, tat tarhi vastubhUtam evAkAshaM syAt, na AvaraNAbhAvamAtram | api ca AvaraNAbhAvamAtram AkashaM manyamAnasya saugatasya svAbhyupagamavirodhaH prasajyeta | saugate hi samaye pR^ithivI bhagavaH kiMsaMnishrayA ityasmin prashnaprativacanapravAhe pR^ithivyAdInAm ante vAyuH kiMsaMnishrayaH ityasya prashnasya prativacanaM bhavati -- vAyur AkAshasaM nishrayaH iti | tad AkAshasyAvastutve na samaJNjasaM syAt | tasmAd apyayuktam AkAshasyAvastutvam | api ca nirodhadvayam AkAshaM ca trayam apyetannirupAkhyam avastu nityaM ceti vipratiShiddham | na hyavastuno nityatvam anityatvaM vA sambhavati, vastvAshrayatvAd dharmadharmivyavahArasya | dharmadharmibhAve hi ghaTAdivad vastutvam eva syAt, na nirupAkhyatvam ||24||

|| 2.2.25 || 

anusmR^iteshca || 

api ca vainAshikaH sarvasya vastunaH kShaNikatAm abhyupayan upalabdhur api kShaNikatAm abhyupeyAt | na ca sA sambhavati | anusmR^iteH -- anubhavam upalabdhim anutpadyamAnaM smaraNam eva anusmR^itiH | sA copalabdhyekakartR^ikA satI sambhavati, puruShAntaropalabdhiviShaye puruShAntarasya smR^ityadarshanAt | kathaM hi aham ado.adrAkSham -- idam idAnIM pashyAmi iti ca pUrvottaradarshinyekasminn asati pratyayaH syAt | api ca darshanasmaraNayoH kartaryekasmin pratyakShaH pratyabhij~nApratyayaH sarvasya lokasya prasiddhaH -- aham ado.adrAkSham -- idaM pashyAmi iti | yadi hi tayor bhinnaH kartA syAt, tato.ahaM smarAmi -- adrAkShId anyaH iti pratIyAt | na tv evaM pratyeti kashcit | yatraivaM pratyayaH tatra darshanasmaraNayor bhinnam eva kartAraM sarvaloko.avagacchati -- smarAmyaham -- asAvado.adrAkShIt iti | iha tu aham ado.adrAkSham iti darshanasmaraNayor venAshiko.apyAtmAnam evaikaM kartAram avagacchati | na nAham ityAtmano darshanaM nirvR^ittaM nihnute -- yathA agnir anuShNo.aprakAsha iti vA | tatraivaM satyekasya darshanasmaraNalakShaNakShaNadvayasambandhe kShaNikatvAbhyupagamahAnir aparihAryA vainAshikasya syAt | tathA anantarAm anantarAm Atmana eva pratipattiM pratyabhijAnann ekakartR^ikAm A uttamAd ucchvAsAt, atItAshca pratipattIH A janmana AtmaikakartR^ikAH, pratisandadhAnaH, kathaM kShaNabhaN^gavAdI vainAshiko nApatrapeta? sa yadi brUyAt sAdR^ishyAd etat sampatsyata iti, taM pratibrUyAt -- tenedaM sadR^isham iti dvayAyattatvAt sAdR^ishyasya, kShaNabhaN^gavAdinaH sadR^ishayor ubhayor vastunor grahItur ekasyAbhAvAt, sAdR^ishyanimittaM pratisandhAnam iti mithyApralApa eva syAt | syAccet pUrvottarayoH kShaNayoH sAdR^ishyasya grahItaikaH, tathA satyekasya kShaNadvayAvasthAnAtkShaNikatvapratij~nA pIDAAta | tenedaM sadR^isham iti pratyayAntaram evedam, na pUrvottarakShaNadvayagrahaNanimittam iti cet, na | tena idam iti bhinnapadArthopAdAnAt | pratyayAntaram eva cetsAdR^ishyaviShayaM syAt, tenedaM sadR^isham iti vAkyaprayogo.anarthakaH syAt, sAdR^ishyam ityeva prayogaH prApnuyAt | yadA hi loke prasiddhaH padArthaH parIkShakair na parigR^ihyate, tadA svapakShasiddhiH parapakShadoSho vA ubhayam apyucyamAnaM parIkShakANAm Atmanashca yathArthatvena na buddhisantAnam Arohati | evam evaiSho.arthaH iti nishcitaM yat, tad eva vaktavyam | tato.anyad ucyamAnaM bahupralApitvam AtmanaH kevalaM prakhyApayet | na cAyaM sAdR^ishyAt saMvyavahAro yuktaH | tadbhAvAvagamAt, tatsadR^ishabhAvAnavagamAcca | bhaved api kadAcid bAhyavastuni vipralambhasambhavAt tad evedaM syAt, tat sadR^ishaM vA iti sandehaH | upalabdhari tu sandeho.api na kadAcid bhavati -- sa evAhaM syAM tatsadR^isho vA iti, ya evAhaM pUrvedyur adrAkShaM sa evAham adya smarAmi iti nishcitatadbhAvopalambhAt | tasmAd apyanupapanno vainAshikasamayaH ||25||

|| 2.2.26 ||

nAsato.adR^iShTatvAt ||

itashcAnupapanno vainAshikasamayaH, yataH sthiram anuyAyikAraNam anabhyupagacchatAm abhAvAd bhAvotpattiH ityetad Apadyeta | darshayanti cAbhAvAd bhAvotpattim -- nAnupamR^idya prAdurbhAvAt iti | vinaShTAd dhi kila bIjAd aN^kura utpadyate, tathA vinaShTAt kShIrAd dadhi, mR^itpiNDAcca ghaTaH | kUTasthAccet kAraNAt kAryam utpadyeta, avisheShAt sarvaM sarvata utpadyeta | tasmAd abhAvagrastebhyo bIjAdibhyo.aN^kurAdInAm utpadyamAnatvAd abhAvAd bhAvotpattiH -- iti manyante | 

tatredam ucyate -- nAsato.adR^iShTatvAt iti | nAbhAvAd bhAva utpadyate | yadyabhAvAd bhAva utpadyeta, abhAvatvAvisheShAt kAraNavisheShAbhyupagamo.anarthakaH syAt | na hi bIjAdInAm upamR^iditAnAM yo.abhAvaH tasyAbhAvasya shashaviShANAdInAM ca, niHsvabhAvatvAvisheShAd abhAvatve kashcid visheSho.asti, yena bIjAd evAN^kuro jAyate kShIrAd eva dadhi ityevaMjAtIyakaH kAraNavisheShAbhyupagamo.arthavAn syAt | nirvisheShasya tu abhAvasya kAraNatvAbhyupagame shashaviShANAdibhyo.apyaN^kurAdayo jAyeran | na caivaM dR^ishyate | yadi punar abhAvasyApi visheSho.abhyupagamyeta -- utpalAdInAm iva nIlatvAdiH, tato visheShavattvAd evAbhAvasya bhAvatvam utpalAdivat prasajyeta | 

nApyabhAvaH kasyacid utpattihetuH syAt, abhAvatvAd eva shashaviShANAdivat | abhAvAcca bhAvotpattAvabhAvAnvitam eva sarvaM kAryaM syAt | na caivaM dR^ishyate, sarvasya ca vastunaH svena svena rUpeNa bhAvAtmanaivopalabhyamAnatvAt | na ca mR^idanvitAH sharAvAdayo bhAvAH tantvAdivikArAH kenacid abhyupagamyante | mR^idvikArAneva tu mR^idanvitAn bhAvAn lokaH pratyeti | yat tUktam -- svarUpopamardam antareNa kasyacit kUTasthasya vastunaH kAraNatvAnupapatter abhAvAd bhAvotpattir bhavitum arhatIti, tad duruktam, sthirasvabhAvAnAm eva suvarNAdInAM pratyabhij~nAyamAnAnAM rucakAdikAraNabhAvadarshanAt | yeShvapi bIjAdiShu svarUpopamardo lakShyate, teShvapi nAsAv upamR^idyamAnA pUrvAvasthA uttarAvasthAyAH kAraNam abhyupagamyate, anupamR^idyamAnAnAm evAnuyAyinAM bIjAdyavayavAnAm aN^kurAdikAraNabhAvAbhyupagamAt | tasmAd asadbhyaH shashaviShANAdibhyaH sadutpattyadarshanAt, sadbhyashca suvarNAdibhyaH sadutpattidarshanAt, anupapanno.ayam abhAvAd bhAvotpattyabhyupagamaH | api ca caturbhishcittacaittA utpadyante paramANubhyashca bhUtabhautikalakShaNaH samudAya utpadyate -- ityabhyupagamya, punar abhAvAd bhAvotpattiM kalpayadbhir abhyupagamam apahnuvAnair vainAshikaiH sarvo loka AkulIkriyate ||26||

|| 2.2.27 ||

udAsInAnAm api caivaM siddhiH ||

yadi cAbhAvAd bhAvotpattir abhyupagamyeta, evaM satyudAsInAnAm anIhamAnAnAm api janAnAm abhimatasiddhiH syAt, abhAvasya sulabhatvAt | kR^iShIvalasya kShetrakarmaNyaprayatamAnasyApi sasyaniShpattiH syAt | kulAlasya ca mR^itsaMskriyAyAm aprayatamAnasyApi amatrotpattiH | tantuvAyasyApi tantUn atanvAnasyApi tanvAnasyeva vastralAbhaH | svargApavargayoshca na kashcit kathaMcit samIheta | na caitad yujyate abhyupagamyate vA kenacit | tasmAd anupapanno.ayam abhAvAd bhAvotpattyabhyupagamaH ||27||

|| iti samudAyAdhikaraNam ||

  -- o)0(o -- 

5. abhAvAdhikaraNam 

|| 2.2.28 ||

evaM bAhyArthavAdam Ashritya samudAyAprAptyAdiShu dUShaNeShUdbhAviteShu vij~nAnavAdI bauddha idAnIM pratyavatiShThate -- keShAMcit kila vineyAnAM bAhye vastunyabhinivesham AlakShya tadanurodhena bAhyArthavAdaprakriyeyaM viracitA | nAsau sugatAbhiprAyaH | tasya tu vij~nAnaikaskandhavAda evAbhipretaH | tasmiMshca vij~nAnavAde buddhyArUDhena 
rUpeNAntastha eva pramANaprameyaphalavyavahAraH sarva upapadyate, satyapi bAhyArthe buddhyAroham antareNa pramANAdivyavahArAnavatArAt | kathaM punar avagamyate -- antastha evAyaM sarvavyavahAraH, na vij~nAnavyatirikto bAhyo.artho.astIti | tadasambhavAd ityAha -- sa hi bAhyo.artho.abhyupagamyamAnaH paramANavo vA syuH, tatsamUhA vA stambhAdayaH syuH | tatra na tAvat paramANavaH stambhAdipratyayaparicchedyA bhavitum arhanti, paramANvAbhAsaj~nAnAnupapatteH | 

nApi tatsamUhAH stambhAdayaH, teShAM paramANubhyo.anyatvAnanyatvAbhyAM nirUpayitum ashakyatvAt | evaM jAtyAdIn api pratyAcakShIta | 

api ca anubhavamAtreNa sAdhAraNAtmano j~nAnasya jAyamAnasya yo.ayaM prativiShayaM pakShapAtaH -- stambhaj~nAnaM kuDyaj~nAnaM ghaTaj~nAnaM paTaj~nAnam iti, nAsau j~nAnagatavisheSham antareNopapadyata ityavashyaM viShayasArUpyaM j~nAnasyAN^gIkartavyam | aN^gIkR^ite ca tasmin viShayAkArasya j~nAnenaivAvaruddhatvAd apArthikA bAhyArthasadbhAvakalpanA | 

api ca sahopalambhaniyamAd abhedo viShayavij~nAnayor Apatati | na hyanayor ekasyAnupalambhe.anyasyopalambho.asti | na caitat svabhAvaviveke yuktam, pratibandhakAraNAbhAvAt | tasmAd apyarthAbhAvaH | svapnAdivaccedaM draShTavyam -- yathA hi svapnamAyAmarIcyudakagandharvanagarAdipratyayA vinaiva bAhyenArthena grAhyagrAhakAkArA bhavanti | evaM jAgaritagocarA api stambhAdipratyayA bhavitum arhantItyavagamyate, pratyayatvAvisheShAt | kathaM punar asati bAhyArthe pratyayavaicitryam upapadyate? vAsanAvaicitryAd ityAha -- anAdau hi saMsAre bIjAN^kuravad vij~nAnAnAM vAsanAnAM cAnyonyanimittanaimittikabhAvena vaicitryaM na vipratiShidhyate | api ca anvayavyatirekAbhyAM vAsanAnimittam eva j~nAnavaicitryam ityavagamyate, svapnAdiShvantareNApyarthaM vAsanAnimittasya j~nAnavaicitryasya ubhAbhyAm apyAvAbhyAm abhyupagamyamAnatvAt, antareNa tu vAsanAm arthanimittasya j~nAnavaicitryasya mayA anabhyupagamyamAnatvAt | tasmAd apyabhAvo bAhyArthasyeti | evaM prApte, brUmaH -- 

nAbhAva upalabdheH ||

na khalvabhAvo bAhyasyArthasyAdhyavasAtuM shakyate | kasmAt? upalabdheH -- upalabhyate hi pratipratyayaM bAhyo.arthaH -- stambhaH kuDyaM ghaTaH paTa iti | na copalabhyamAnasyaivAbhAvo bhavitum arhati | yathA hi kashcid bhuJNjAno bhujisAdhyAyAM tR^iptau svayam anubhUyamAnAyAm evaM brUyAt -- nAhaM bhuJNje na vA tR^ipyAmi iti -- tadvad indriyasaMnikarSheNa svayam upalabhamAna eva bAhyam artham, nAham upalabhe na ca so.asti iti bruvan, katham upAdeyavacanaH syAt | 

nanu nAham evaM bravImi -- na kaMcid artham upalabhe iti | kiM tu upalabdhivyatiriktaM nopalabhe iti bravImi | bADham evaM bravIShi niraN^kushatvAt te tuNDasya, na tu yuktyupetaM bravIShi, yata upalabdhivyatireko.api balAd arthasyAbhyupagantavyaH, upalabdher eva | na hi kashcid upalabdhim eva stambhaH kuDyaM cetyupalabhate | upalabdhiviShayatvenaiva tu stambhakuDyAdIn sarve laukikA upalabhante | atashcaivam eva sarve laukikA upalabhante, yat pratyAcakShANA api bAhyam artham evam AcakShate -- yad antarj~neyarUpaM tad bahirvad avabhAsate iti -- te.api hi sarvalokaprasiddhAM bahiravabhAsamAnAM saMvidaM pratilabhamAnAH, pratyAkhyAtukAmAshca bAhyam artham, bahirvat iti vatkAraM kurvanti | itarathA hi kasmAt bahirvat iti brUyuH | na hi viShNumitro vandhyAputravad avabhAsate iti kashcid AcakShIta | tasmAt yathAnubhavaM tattvam abhyupagacchadbhiH bahir evAvabhAsate iti yuktam abhyupagantum, na tu bahirvad avabhAsata iti | 

nanu bAhyasyArthasyAsambhavAt bahirvad avabhAsate ityadhyavasitam | nAyaM sAdhur adhyavasAyaH, yataH pramANapravR^ittyam pravR^ittipUrvakau sambhavAsambhavAvavadhAryete, na punaH sambhavAsambhavapUrvake pramANapravR^ittyapravR^ittI | yad dhi pratyakShAdInAm anyatamenApi pramANenopalabhyate, tat sambhavati | yat tu na kenacid api pramANenopalabhyate, tan na sambhavati | iha tu yathAsvaM sarvair eva pramANair bAhyo.artha upalabhyamAnaH kathaM vyatirekAvyatirekAdivikalpair na sambhavatItyucyeta -- upalabdher eva? na ca j~nAnasya viShayasArUpyAd viShayanAsho bhavati, asati viShaye viShayasArUpyAnupapatteH, bahir upalabdheshca viShayasya | ata eva sahopalambhaniyamo.api pratyayaviShayayor upAyopeyabhAvahetukaH, na abhedahetuka ityabhyupagantavyam | 

api ca ghaTaj~nAnaM paTaj~nAnam iti visheShaNayor eve ghaTapaTayor bhedaH, na visheShyasya j~nAnasya -- yathA shuklo gauH kR^iShNo gauH iti shauklyakArShNyayor eva bhedaH, na gotvasya | dvAbhyAM ca bheda ekasya siddho bhavati, ekasmAcca dvayoH | tasmAd arthaj~nAnayor bhedaH | tathA ghaTadarshanaM ghaTasmaraNam ityatrApi pratipattavyam | atrApi hi visheShyayor eva darshanasmaraNayor bhedaH, na visheShaNasya ghaTasya -- yathA kShIragandhaH kShIrarasa iti visheShyayor eva gandharasayor bhedaH, na visheShaNasya kShIrasya, tadvat | api ca dvayor vij~nAnayoH pUrvottarakAlayoH svasaMvedanenaiva upakShINayoH itaretaragrAhyagrAhakatvAnupapattiH | tatashca -- vij~nAnabhedapratij~nA kShaNikatvAdidharmapratij~nA svalakShaNasAmAnyalakShaNavAsyavAsakatvAvidyopaplavasadasaddharmabandhamokShAdipratij~nAshca svashAstragatAH -- tA hIyeran | 

kiM cAnyat -- vij~nAnaM vij~nAnam ityabhyupagacchatA, bAhyArthaH stambhaH kuDyam ityevaMjAtIyakaH kasmAn nAbhyupagamyata iti vaktavyam? vij~nAnam anubhUyata iti cet, bAhyo.apyartho.anubhUyata eveti yuktam abhyupagantum | atha vij~nAnaM prakAshAtmakatvAt pradIpavat svayam evAnubhUyate, na tathA bAhyo.apyartha iti cet -- atyantaviruddhAM svAtmani kriyAm abhyupagacchasi -- agnir AtmAnaM dahatItivat | aviruddhaM tu lokaprasiddham -- svAtmavyatiriktena vij~nAnena bAhyArtho.anubhUyata iti necchasi | aho pANDityaM mahad darshitam | na cArthavyatiriktam api vij~nAnaM svayam evAnubhUyate, svAtmani kriyAvirodhAd eva | 

nanu vij~nAnasya svarUpavyatiriktagrAhyatve, tad apyanyena grAhyaM tad apyanyena -- ityanavasthA prApnoti | api ca pradIpavad avabhAsAtmakatvAjj~nAnasya j~nAnAntaraM kalpayataH samatvAd avabhAsyAvabhAsakabhAvAnupapatteH kalpanAnarthakyam iti tad ubhayam apyasat, vij~nAnagrahaNamAtra eva vij~nAnasAkShiNo grahaNAkAN^kShAnutpAdAd anavasthAshaN^kAnupapatteH, sAkShipratyayayoshca svabhAvavaiShamyAd upalabdher upalabhyabhAvopapatteH, svayaMsiddhasya ca sAkShiNo.apratyAkhyeyatvAt | 

kiM cAnyat -- pradIpavadvij~nAnam avabhAsakAntaranirapekShaM svayam eva prathate -- iti bruvatA apramANagamyaM vij~nAnam anavagantR^ikam ityuktaM syAt -- shilAghanamadhyasthapradIpasahasraprathanavat | bADham evam -- anubhavarUpatvAt tu vij~nAnasyeShTo naH pakShaH tvayA anuj~nAyata iti cet, na | anyasyAvagantushcakShuHsAdhanasya pradIpAdiprathanadarshanAt | ato vij~nAnasyApyavabhAsyatvAvisheShAt satyevAnyasminn avagantari prathanaM pradIpavad ityavagamyate | sAkShiNo.avagantuH svayaMsiddhatAm upakShipatA, svayaM prathate vij~nAnam ityeSha eva mama pakShaH tvayA vAcoyuktyantareNAshrita iti cet, na | vij~nAnasyotpattipradhvaMsAnekatvAdivisheShavattvAbhyupagamAt | ataH pradIpavad vij~nAnasyApi vyatiriktAvagamyatvam asmAbhiH prasAdhitam ||28||

|| 2.2.29 ||

vaidharmyAcca na svapnAdivat ||

yad uktaM bAhyArthApalApinA -- svapnAdipratyayavajjAgaritagocarA api stambhAdipratyayA vinaiva bAhyenArthena bhaveyuH, pratyayatvAvisheShAd iti, tat prativaktavyam | atrocyate -- na svapnAdipratyayavajjAgratpratyayA bhavitum arhanti | kasmAt? vaidharmyAt -- vaidharmyaM hi bhavati svapnajAgaritayoH | kiM punar vaidharmyam? bAdhAbAdhAviti brUmaH -- bAdhyate hi svapnopalabdhaM vastu pratibuddhasya -- mithyA mayopalabdho mahAjanasamAgama iti, na hyasti mama mahAjanasamAgamaH, nidrAglAnaM tu me mano babhUva, tenaiShA bhrAntir udbabhUveti | evaM mAyAdiShvapi bhavati yathAyathaM bAdhaH | naivaM jAgaritopalabdhaM vastu stambhAdikaM kasyAMcid apyavasthAyAM bAdhyate | api ca smR^itir eShA, yat svapnadarshanam | upalabdhiH tu jAgaritadarshanam | smR^ityupalabdhyoshca pratyakSham antaraM svayam anubhUyate arthaviprayogasamprayogAtmakam -- iShTaM putraM smarAmi, nopalabhe, upalabdhum icchAmIti | tatraivaM sati na shakyate vaktum -- mithyA jAgaritopalabdhiH, upalabdhitvAt, svapnopalabdhivad iti -- ubhayor antaraM svayam anubhavatA | na ca svAnubhavApalApaH prAj~namAnibhir yuktaH kartum | api ca anubhavavirodhaprasaN^gAjjAgaritapratyayAnAM svato nirAlambanatAM vaktum ashaknuvatA svapnapratyayasAdharmyAd vaktum iShyate | na ca, yo yasya svato dharmo na sambhavati so.anyasya sAdharmyAt tasya sambhaviShyati | na hyagnir uShNo.anubhUyamAna udakasAdharmyAcchIto bhaviShyati | darshitaM tu vaidharmyaM svapnajAgaritayoH ||29||

|| 2.2.30 ||

na bhAvo.anupalabdheH ||

yad apyuktam -- vinApyarthena j~nAnavaicitryaM vAsanAvaicitryAd evAvakalpata iti, tat prativaktavyam | atrocyate -- na bhAvo vAsanAnAm upapadyate, tvatpakShe.anupalabdher bAhyAnAm arthAnAm | arthopalabdhinimittA hi pratyarthaM nAnArUpA vAsanA bhavanti | anupalabhyamAneShu tu artheShu kiMnimittA vicitrA vAsanA bhaveyuH? anAditve.apyandhaparamparAnyAyenApratiShThaivAnavasthA vyavahAralopinI syAt, nAbhiprAyasiddhiH | yAvapyanvayavyatirekAvarthApalApinopanyastau -- vAsanAnimittam evedaM j~nAnajAtaM nArthanimittam iti, tAvapyevaM sati pratyuktau draShTavyau, vinArthopalabdhyA vAsanAnupapatteH | api ca vinApi vAsanAbhir arthopalabdhyupagamAt, vinA tu arthopalabdhyA vAsanotpattyanabhyupagamAt arthasadbhAvam evAnvayavyatirekAvapi pratiShThApayataH | api ca vAsanA nAma saMskAravisheShAH | saMskArAshca nAshrayam antareNAvakalpante, evaM loke dR^iShTatvAt | na ca tava vAsanAshrayaH kashcid asti, pramANato.anupalabdheH ||30||

|| 2.2.31 || 

kShaNikatvAcca || 

yad apyAlayavij~nAnaM nAma vAsanAshrayatvena parikalpitam, tad api kShaNikatvAbhyupagamAd anavasthitasvarUpaM sat, pravR^ittivij~nAnavan na vAsanAnAm adhikaraNaM bhavitum arhati | na hi kAlatrayasambandhinyekasminn anvayinyasati kUTasthe vA sarvArthadarshini deshakAlanimittApekShavAsanAdhIn asmR^itipratisandhAn AdivyavahAraH sambhavati | sthirasvarUpatve tvalayavij~nAnasya siddhAntahAniH | api ca vij~nAnavAde.api kShaNikatvAbhyupagamasya samAnatvAt, yAni bAhyArthavAde kShaNikatvanibandhanAni dUShaNAnyudbhAvitAni -- uttarotpAde ca pUrvanirodhAt ityevam AdIni, tAnIhApyanusandhAtavyAni | evam etau dvAvapi vainAshikapakShau nirAkR^itau -- bAhyArthavAdipakSho vij~nAnavAdipakShashca | shUnyavAdipakShaH tu sarvapramANavipratiShiddha iti tannirAkaraNAya nAdaraH kriyate | na hyayaM sarvapramANasiddho lokavyavahAro.anyat tattvam anadhigamya shakyate.apahnotum, apavAdAbhAve utsargaprasiddhiH ||31||

|| 2.2.32 ||

sarvathA.anupapatteshca || 

kiM bahunA? sarvaprakAreNa -- yathA yathAyaM vainAshikasamaya upapattimattvAya parIkShyate tathA tathA -- sikatAkUpavad vidIryata eva | na kAMcid apyatropapattiM pashyAmaH | atashcAnupapanno vainAshikatantravyavahAraH | api ca bAhyArthavij~nAnashUnyavAdatrayam itaretaraviruddham upadishatA sugatena spaShTIkR^itam Atmano.asambaddhapralApitvam, pradveSho vA prajAsu -- viruddhArthapratipattyA vimuhyeyuH imAH prajA iti | sarvathApyanAdaraNIyo.ayaM sugatasamayaH shreyaskAmaiH ityabhiprAyaH ||32||

 -- o)0(o -- 
6. ekasminn asambhavAdhikaraNam

|| 2.2.33 ||

naikasminn asambhavAt ||

nirastaH sugatasamayaH | vivasanasamaya idAnIM nirasyate | sapta caiShAM padArthAH saMmatAH -- jIvAjIvAsravasaMvaranirjarabandhamokShA nAma | saMkShepataH tu dvAv eva padArthau jIvAjIvAkhyau, yathAyogaM tayor evetarAntarbhAvAd iti manyante | tayoH imam aparaM prapaJNcam AcakShate, paJNcAstikAyA nAma -- jIvAstikAyaH pudgalAstikAyo dharmAstikAyo.adharmAstikAya AkAshAstikAyashceti | sarveShAm apyeShAm avAntarabhedAn bahuvidhAn svasamayaparikalpitAn varNayanti | sarvatra cemaM saptabhaN^gInayaM nAma nyAyam avatArayanti -- syAd asti, syAn nAsti, syAd asti ca nAsti ca, syAd avaktavyaH, syAd asti cAvaktavyashca, syAn nAsti cAvaktavyashca, syAd asti ca nAsti cAvaktavyashceti | evam evaikatvanityatvAdiShvapImaM saptabhaN^gInayaM yojayanti || 

atrAcakShmahe -- nAyam abhyupagamo yukta iti | kutaH? ekasminn asambhavAt | na hyekasmin dharmiNi yugapat sadasattvAdiviruddhadharmasamAveshaH sambhavati, shItoShNavat | ya ete saptapadArthA nirdhAritA etAvanta evaMrUpAshceti, te tathaiva vA syuH, naiva vA tathA syuH | itarathA hi, tathA vA syur atathA vetyanirdhAritarUpaM j~nAnaM saMshayaj~nAnavad apramANam eva syAt | 

nanvanekAtmakaM vastviti nirdhAritarUpam eva j~nAnam utpadyamAnaM saMshayaj~nAnavan nApramANaM bhavitum arhati | neti brUmaH -- niraN^kushaM hyanekAntatvaM sarvavastuShu pratijAnAnasya nirdhAraNasyApi vastutvAvisheShAt, syAd asti syAn nAsti ityAdi vikalpopanipAtAd anirdhAraNAtmakataiva syAt | evaM nirdhArayitur nirdhAraNaphalasya ca syAtpakShe.astitA, syAcca pakShe nAstiteti | evaM sati kathaM pramANabhUtaH san tIrthakaraH pramANaprameyapramAtR^ipramitiShvanirdhAritAsu upadeShTuM shaknuyAt? kathaM vA tadabhiprAyAnusAriNaH tadupadiShTe.arthe.anirdhAritarUpe pravarteran? aikAntikaphalatvanirdhAraNe hi sati tatsAdhanAnuShThAnAya sarvo loko.anAkulaH pravartate, nAnyathA | atashcAnirdhAritArthaM shAstraM praNayan mattonmattavad anupAdeyavacanaH syAt | tathA paJNcAnAm astikAyAnAM paJNcatvasaMkhyA asti vA nAsti vA iti vikalpyamAnA, syAt tAvad ekasmin pakShe, pakShAntare tu na syAt -- ityato nyUnasaMkhyAtvam adhikasaMkhyAtvaM vA prApnuyAt | 

na caiShAM padArthAnAm avaktavyatvaM sambhavati | avaktavyAshcen nocyeran | ucyante cAvaktavyAshceti vipratiShiddham | ucyamAnAshca tathaivAvadhAryante nAvadhAryanta iti ca | tathA tadavadhAraNaphalaM samyagdarshanam asti vA nAsti vA -- evaM tadviparItam asamyagdarshanam apyasti vA nAsti vA -- iti pralapan mattonmattapakShasyaiva pakShaH syAt, na pratyayitavyapakShasya | svargApavargayoshca pakShe bhAvaH pakShe cAbhAvaH, tathA pakShe nityatA pakShe cAnityatAityanavadhAraNAyAM pravR^ittyanupapattiH | anAdisiddhajIvaprabhR^itInAM ca svashAstrAvadhR^itasvabhAvAnAm ayathAvadhR^itasvabhAvatvaprasaN^gaH | evaM jIvAdiShu padArtheShv ekasmin dharmiNi sattvAsattvayor viruddhayor dharmayor asambhavAt, sattve caikasmin dharme.asattvasya dharmAntarasyAsambhavAt, asattve caivaM sattvasyAsambhavAt, asaN^gatam idam ArhataM matam | 

etenaikAnekanityAnityavyatiriktAvyatiriktAdyanekAntAbhyupagamA nirAkR^itA mantavyAH | yat tu pudgalasaMj~nakebhyo.aNubhyaH saMghAtAH sambhavantIti kalpayanti, tatpUrveNaivANuvAdanirAkaraNena nirAkR^itaM bhavatItyato na pR^ithaktannirAkaraNAya prayatyate ||33||

|| 2.2.34 ||

evaM cAtmAkArtsnyam ||

yathaikasmin dharmiNi viruddhadharmAsambhavo doShaH syAdvAde prasaktaH, evam Atmano.api jIvasya akArtsnyam aparo doShaH prasajyeta | katham? sharIraparimANo hi jIva ityArhatA manyante | sharIraparimANatAyAM ca satyAm, akR^itsno.asarvagataH paricchinna Atmetyato ghaTAdivad anityatvam AtmanaH prasajyeta | sharIrANAM cAnavasthitaparimANatvAt manuShyajIvo manuShyasharIraparimANo bhUtvA punaH kenacit karmavipAkena hastijanma prApnuvan na kR^itsnaM hastisharIraM vyApnuyAt | puttikAjanma ca prApnuvan na kR^itsnaH puttikAsharIre saMmIyeta | samAna eSha ekasminn api janmani kaumArayauvanasthAvireShu doShaH | syAd etat -- anantAvayavo jIvaH | tasya ta evAvayavA alpe sharIre saN^kuceyuH | mahati ca vikaseyuH iti | teShAM punar anantAnAM jIvAvayavAnAM samAnadeshatvaM prativihanyate vA, na veti vaktavyam | pratighAte tAvat nAnantAvayavAH paricchinne deshe saMmIyeran | pratighAte.apyekAvayavadeshatvopapatteH sarveShAm avayavAnAM prathimAnupapatter jIvasyANumAtratvaprasaN^gaH syAt | api ca sharIramAtraparicchinnAnAM jIvAvayavAnAm AnantyaM notprekShitum api shakyam ||34||

|| 2.2.35 || 

atha paryAyeNa bR^ihaccharIrapratipattau kecijjIvAvayavA upagacchanti, tanusharIrapratipattau ca kecid apagacchantItyucyeta | tatrApyucyate -- 

na ca paryAyAd apyavirodho vikArAdibhyaH ||

na ca paryAyeNApyavayavopagamApagamAbhyAm etad dehaparimANatvaM jIvasyAvirodhenopapAdayituM shakyate | kutaH? vikArAdidoShaprasaN^gAt -- avayavopagamApagamAbhyAM hyanisham ApUryamANasyApakShIyamANasya ca jIvasya vikriyAvattvaM tAvad aparihAryam | vikriyAvattve ca carmAdivad anityatvaM prasajyeta | tatashca bandhamokShAbhyupagamo bAdhyeta -- karmAShTakapariveShTitasya jIvasya alAbUvatsaMsArasAgare nimagnasya bandhanocchedAd UrdhvagAmitvaM bhavatIti | 

kiM cAnyat -- AgacchatAm apagacchatAM ca avayavAnAm AgamApAyadharmavattvAd eva anAtmatvaM sharIrAdivat | tatashcAvasthitaH kashcid avayava Atmeti syAt | na ca sa nirUpayituM shakyate -- ayam asAviti | 

kiM cAnyat -- Agacchantashcaite jIvAvayavAH kutaH prAdurbhavanti, apagacchantashca kva vA lIyanta iti vaktavyam | na hi bhUtebhyaH prAdurbhaveyuH, bhUteShu ca nilIyeran, abhautikatvAjjIvasya | nApi kashcid anyaH sAdhAraNo.asAdhAraNo vA jIvAnAm avayavAdhAro nirUpyate, pramANAbhAvAt | 

kiM cAnyat -- anavadhR^itasvarUpashcaivaM sati AtmA syAt, AgacchatAm apagacchatAM ca avayavAnAm aniyataparimANatvAt | ata evamAdidoShaprasaN^gAt na paryAyeNApyavayavopagamApagamAvatmana AshrayituM shakyete | athavA pUrveNa sUtreNa sharIraparimANasyAtmana upacitApacitasharIrAntarapratipattAvakArtsnyaprasaJNjanadvAreNAnityatAyAM coditAyAm, punaH paryAyeNa parimANAnavasthAne.api srotaHsantAnanityatAnyAyena Atmano nityatA syAt -- yathA raktapaTAnAM vij~nAnAnavasthAne.api tatsantAnanityatA, tadvad visicAm api -- ityAshaN^kya, anena sUtreNottaram ucyate -- santAnasya tAvad avastutve nairAtmyavAdaprasaN^gaH, vastutve.apyAtmano vikArAdidoShaprasaN^gAd asya pakShasyAnupapattiH iti ||35||

|| 2.2.36 ||

antyAvasthiteshcobhayanityatvAd avisheShAt ||

api ca antyasya mokShAvasthAbhAvino jIvaparimANasya nityatvam iShyate jainaiH | tadvat pUrvayor apyAdyamadhyamayor jIvaparimANayor nityatvaprasaN^gAd avisheShaprasaN^gaH syAt | ekasharIraparimANataiva syAt, na upacitApacitasharIrAntaraprAptiH | athavA antyasya jIvaparimANasya avasthitatvAt pUrvayor apyavasthayor avasthitaparimANa eva jIvaH syAt | tatashcAvisheSheNa sarvadaiva aNur mahAn vA jIvo.abhyupagantavyaH, na sharIraparimANaH | atashca saugatavad Arhatam api matam asaN^gatam ityupekShitavyam ||36||

7. patyadhikaraNam

|| 2.2.37 ||

idAnIM kevalAdhiShThAtr IshvarakAraNavAdaH pratiShidhyate | tat katham avagamyate? prakR^itishca pratij~nAdR^iShTAntAnuparodhAt abhidhyopadeshAcca ityatra prakR^itibhAvena adhiShThAtR^ibhAvena ca ubhayasvabhAvasyeshvarasya svayam eva AcAryeNa pratiShThApitatvAt | yadi punar avisheSheNeshvarakAraNavAdamAtramiha pratiShidhyeta, pUrvottaravirodhAdvyAhatAbhivyAhAraH sUtrakAra ityetadApadyeta | tasmAd aprakR^itiradhiShThAtA kevalaM nimittakAraNam IshvaraH -- ityeSha pakSho vedAntavihitabrahmaikatvapratipakShatvAt yatnenAtra pratiShidhyate | sA ceyaM vedabAhyeshvarakalpanA anekaprakArA -- kecittAvatsAN^khyayogavyapAshrayAH kalpayanti -- pradhAnapuruShayor adhiShThAtA kevalaM nimittakAraNam IshvaraH | itaretaravilakShaNAH pradhAnapuruSheshvarA iti | mAheshvarAH tu manyante -- kAryakAraNayogavidhiduHkhAntAH paJNca padArthAH pashupatineshvareNa pashupAshavimokShaNAyopadiShTAH | pashupatir Ishvaro nimittakAraNam iti | tathA vaisheShikAdayo.api kecitkathaMcitsvaprakriyAnusAreNa nimittakAraNam Ishvaram iti | ata uttaram ucyate -- 

patyur asAmaJNjasyAt ||

patyur Ishvarasya pradhAnapuruShayor adhiShThAtR^itvena jagatkAraNatvaM nopapadyate | kasmAt? asAmaJNjasyAt | kiM punar asAmaJNjasyam? hInamadhyamottamabhAvena hi prANibhedAn vidadhata Ishvarasya rAgadveShAdidoShaprasakteH asmadAdivad anIshvaratvaM prasajyeta | prANikarmApekShitatvAd adoSha iti cet, na | karmeshvarayoH pravartyapravartayitR^itve itaretarAshrayadoShaprasaN^gAt | na, anAditvAt, iti cet, na | vartamAnakAlavadatIteShvapi kAleShvitaretarAshrayadoShAvisheShAd andhaparamparAnyAyApatteH | api ca pravartanAlakShaNA doShAH iti nyAyavitsamayaH | na hi kashcid adoShaprayuktaH svArthe parArthe vA pravartamAno dR^ishyate | svArthaprayukta eva ca sarvo janaH parArthe.api pravartata ityevam apyasAmaJNjasyam, svArthavattvAd IshvarasyAnIshvaratvaprasaN^gAt | puruShavisheShatvAbhyupagamAcceshvarasya, puruShasya caudAsInyAbhyupagamAd asAmaJNjasyam ||37||

|| 2.2.38 ||

sambandhAnupapatteshca ||

punar apyasAmaJNjasyam eva -- na hi pradhAnapuruShavyatirikta Ishvaro.antareNa sambandhaM pradhAnapuruShayor IshitA | na tAvat saMyogalakShaNaH sambandhaH sambhavati, pradhAnapuruSheshvarANAM sarvagatatvAn niravayavatvAcca | nApi samavAyalakShaNaH sambandhaH, AshrayAshrayibhAvAnirUpaNAt | nApyanyaH kashcit kAryagamyaH sambandhaH shakyate kalpayitum, kAryakAraNabhAvasyaivAdyApyasiddhatvAt | brahmavAdinaH katham iti cet, na | tasya tAdAtmyalakShaNasambandhopapatteH | api ca Agamabalena brahmavAdI kAraNAdisvarUpaM nirUpayatIti nAvashyaM tasya yathAdR^iShTam eva sarvam abhyupagantavyam iti niyamo.asti | parasya tu dR^iShTAntabalena kAraNAdisvarUpaM nirUpayataH yathAdR^iShTam eva sarvam abhyupagantavyam ityayam astyatishayaH | parasyApi sarvaj~napraNItAgamasadbhAvAt samAnam Agamabalam iti cet, na | itaretarAshrayaprasaN^gAt -- AgamapratyayAt sarvaj~natvasiddhiH sarvaj~natvapratyayAccAgamasiddhiH iti | tasmAd anupapannA sAN^khyayogavAdinAm IshvarakalpanA | evam anyAsvapi vedabAhyAsv IshvarakalpanAsu yathAsambhavam asAmaJNjasyaM yojayitavyam ||38||

|| 2.2.39 ||

adhiShThAnAnupapatteshca ||

itashcAnupapattiH tArkikaparikalpitasyeshvarasya -- sa hi parikalpyamAnaH, kumbhakAra iva mR^idAdIni, pradhAnAdInyadhiShThAya pravartayet | na caivam upapadyate | na hyapratyakShaM rUpAdihInaM ca pradhAnam IshvarasyAdhiShTheyaM sambhavati, mR^idAdivailakShaNyAt ||39||

|| 2.2.40 ||

karaNavaccen na bhogAdibhyaH ||

syAd etat -- yathA karaNagrAmaM cakShurAdikam apratyakShaM rUpAdihInaM ca puruSho.adhitiShThati, evaM pradhAnam Ishvaro.adhiShThAsyatIti | tathApi nopapadyate | bhogAdidarshanAd dhi karaNagrAmasya adhiShThitatvaM gamyate | na cAtra bhogAdayo dR^ishyante | karaNagrAmasAmye ca abhyupagamyamAne saMsAriNAm iva IshvarasyApi bhogAdayaH prasajyeran ||40|| 

 -- o)0(o -- 

|| 2.2.41 ||

anyathA vA sUtradvayaM vyAkhyAyate -- adhiShThAnAnupapatteshca -- itashcAnupapattiH tArkikaparikalpitasyeshvarasya | sAdhiShThAno hi loke sasharIro rAjA rAShTrasyeshvaro dR^ishyate | na niradhiShThAnaH | atashca taddR^iShTAntavashenAdR^iShTam IshvaraM kalpayitum icchataH IshvarasyApi kiMciccharIraM karaNAyatanaM varNayitavyaM syAt | na ca tad varNayituM shakyate, sR^iShTyuttarakAlabhAvitvAccharIrasya, prAksR^iShTeH tadanupapatteH | niradhiShThAnatve ceshvarasya pravartakatvAnupapattiH, evaM loke dR^iShTatvAt | karaNavaccen na bhogAdibhyaH -- atha lokadarshanAnusAreNa IshvarasyApi kiMcitkaraNAnAm AyatanaM sharIraM kAmena kalpyeta -- evam api nopapadyate | sasharIratve hi sati saMsArivad bhogAdiprasaN^gAt IshvarasyApyanIshvaratvaM prasajyeta ||

antavatvam asarvaj~natA vA ||

itashcAnupapattiH tArkikaparikalpitasyeshvarasya -- sa hi sarvaj~naH tair abhyupagamyate.anantashca | anantaM ca pradhAnam, anantAshca puruShA mitho bhinnA abhyupagamyante | tatra sarvaj~neneshvareNa pradhAnasya puruShANAm AtmanashceyattA paricchidyeta vA, na vA paricchidyeta | ubhayathApi doSho.anuShakta eva | katham? pUrvasmiMH tAvad vikalpe, iyattAparicchinnatvAt pradhAnapuruSheshvarANAm antavattvam avashyambhAvi, evaM loke dR^iShTatvAt | yad dhi loke iyattAparicchinnaM vastu ghaTAdi, tadantavad dR^iShTam -- tathA pradhAnapuruSheshvaratrayam apIyattAparicchinnatvAd antavat syAt | saMkhyAparimANaM tAvat pradhAnapuruSheshvaratrayarUpeNa paricchinnam | svarUpaparimANam api tadgatam IshvareNa paricchidyeta, puruShagatA ca mahAsaMkhyA | tatashceyattAparicchinnAnAM madhye ye saMsArAn mucyante, teShAM saMsAro.antavAn, saMsAritvaM ca teShAm antavat | evam itareShvapi krameNa mucyamAneShu saMsArasya saMsAriNAM ca antavattvaM syAt | pradhAnaM ca savikAraM puruShArtham Ishvarasya adhiShTheyaM saMsAratvenAbhimatam | tacchUnyatAyAm IshvaraH kim adhitiShThet? kiMviShaye vA sarvaj~nateshvarate syAtAm? pradhAnapuruSheshvarANAm caivam antavattve sati AdimattvaprasaN^gaH | Adyantavattve ca shUnyavAdaprasaN^gaH | atha mA bhUd eSha doSha ityuttaro vikalpo.abhyupagamyeta -- na pradhAnasya puruShANAm Atmanashca iyattA IshvareNa paricchidyata iti | tata Ishvarasya sarvaj~natvAbhyupagamahAnir aparo doShaH prasajyeta | tasmAd apyasaN^gataH tArkikaparigR^ihIta IshvarakAraNavAdaH ||41||

 -- o)0(o -- 

8. utpattyasambhavAdhikaraNam

|| 2.2.42 ||

yeShAm aprakR^itir adhiShThAtA kevalanimittakAraNam Ishvaro.abhimataH, teShAM pakShaH pratyAkhyAtaH | yeShAM punaH prakR^itishcAdhiShThAtA ca ubhayAtmakaM kAraNam Ishvaro.abhimataH, teShAM pakShaH pratyAkhyAyate | 

nanu shrutisamAshrayaNenApyevaMrUpa eveshvaraH prAN^nirdhAritaH -- prakR^itishcAdhiShThAtA ceti | shrutyanusAriNI ca smR^itiH pramANam iti sthitiH | tat kasya hetor eSha pakShaH pratyAcikhyAsita iti -- ucyate -- yadyapyevaMjAtIyako.aMshaH samAnatvAn na visaMvAdagocaro bhavati, asti tu aMshAntaraM visaMvAdasthAnam ityataH tatpratyAkhyAnAyArambhaH || 

tatra bhAgavatA manyate -- bhagavAn evaiko vAsudevo niraJNjanaj~nAnasvarUpaH paramArthatattvam | sa caturdhAtmAnaM pravibhajya pratiShThitaH -- vAsudevavyUharUpeNa, saN^karShaNavyUharUpeNa, pradyumnavyUharUpeNa, aniruddhavyUharUpeNa ca | vAsudevo nAma paramAtmA ucyate | saN^karShaNo nAma jIvaH | pradyumno nAma manaH | aniruddho nAma ahaMkAraH | teShAM vAsudevaH parA prakR^itiH, itare saN^karShaNAdayaH kAryam | tam itthambhUtaM parameshvaraM bhagavantam abhigamanopAdAnejyAsvAdhyAyayogair varShashatam iShTavA kShINaklesho bhagavantam eva pratipadyata iti | tatra yat tAvad ucyate -- yo.asau nArAyaNaH paro.avyaktAt prasiddhaH paramAtmA sarvAtmA, sa AtmanAtmAnam anekadhA vyUhyAvasthita iti -- tan na nirAkriyate, sa ekadhA bhavati tridhA bhavati ityAdi shrutibhyaH paramAtmano.anekadhAbhAvasyAdhigatatvAt | yad api tasya bhagavato.abhigamanAdilakShaNam ArAdhanam ajasram ananyacittatayAbhipreyate, tad api na pratiShidhyate, shrutismR^ityor IshvarapraNidhAnasya prasiddhatvAt | 

yat punaH idam ucyate -- vAsudevAt saN^karShaNa utpadyate, saN^karShaNAcca pradyumnaH, pradyumnAccAniruddha iti, atra brUmaH -- na vAsudevasaMj~nakAt paramAtmanaH saN^karShaNasaMj~nakasya jIvasyotpattiH sambhavati, anityatvAdidoShaprasaN^gAt | utpattimattve hi jIvasya anityatvAdayo doShAH prasajyeran | tatashca naivAsya bhagavatprAptir mokShaH syAt, kAraNaprAptau kAryasya pravilayaprasaN^gAt | pratiShedhiShyati ca AcAryo jIvasyotpattim -- nAtmAshruter nityatvAcca tAbhyaH iti | tasmAd asaN^gataiShA kalpanA ||

|| 2.2.43 ||

na ca kartuH karaNam || 

itashcAsaN^gataiShA kalpanA -- yasmAn na hi loke kartur devadattAdeH karaNaM parashvAdyutpadyamAnaM dR^ishyate | varNayanti ca bhAgavatAH kartur jIvAt saN^karShaNasaMj~nakAt karaNaM manaH pradyumnasaMj~nakam utpadyate, kartR^ijAcca tasmAd aniruddhasaMj~nako.ahaMkAra utpadyata iti | na caitaddR^iShTAntam antareNAdhyavasAtuM shaknumaH | na caivambhUtAM shrutim upalabhAmahe ||43||

|| 2.2.44 ||

vij~nAnAdi bhAve vA tadapratiShedhaH ||

athApi syAt -- na caite saN^karShaNAdayo jIvAdibhAvenAbhipreyante | kiM tarhi, IshvarA evaite sarve j~nAnaishvaryashaktibalavIryatejobhir aishvaryadharmair anvitA abhyupagamyante -- vAsudevA evaite sarve nirdoShA niradhiShThAnA niravadyAshceti | tasmAn nAyaM yathAvarNita utpattyasambhavo doShaH prApnotIti | atrocyate -- evam api, tadapratiShedhaH utpattyasambhavasyApratiShedhaH, prApnotyevAyam utpattyasambhavo doShaH prakArAntareNetyabhiprAyaH | katham? yadi tAvad ayam abhiprAyaH -- parasparabhinnA evaite vAsudevAdayashcatvAra IshvarAH tulyadharmANaH, naiShAm ekAtmakatvam astIti -- tato.anekeshvarakalpanAnarthakyam, ekenaiveshvareNeshvarakAryasiddhiH | siddhAntahAnishca, bhagavAn evaiko vAsudevaH paramArthatattvam ityabhyupagamAt | 

athAyam abhiprAyaH -- ekasyaiva bhagavata ete catvAro vyUhAH tulyadharmANa iti, tathApi tadavastha evotpattyasambhavaH | na hi vAsudevAt saN^karShaNasyotpattiH sambhavati, saN^karShaNAcca pradyumnasya, pradyumnAccAniruddhasya, atishayAbhAvAt | bhavitavyaM hi kAryakAraNayor atishayena, yathA mR^idghaTayoH | na hyasatyatishaye, kAryaM kAraNam ityavakalpate | na ca paJNcarAtrasiddhAntibhir vAsudevAdiShu ekasmin sarveShu vA j~nAnaishvaryAditAratamyakR^itaH kashcid bhedo.abhyupagamyate | vAsudevA eva hi sarve vyUhA nirvisheShA iShyante | na caite bhagavadvyUhAshcatuHsaMkhyAyAm evAvatiShTheran, brahmAdistambaparyantasya samastasyaiva jagato bhagavadvyUhatvAvagamAt ||

|| 2.2.45 ||

vipratiShedhAcca ||

vipratiShedhashca asmin shAstre bahuvidha upalabhyate -- guNaguNitvakalpanAdilakShaNaH | j~nAnaishvaryashaktibalavIryatejAMsi guNAH, AtmAna evaite bhagavanto vAsudevA ityAdidarshanAt | vedavipratiShedhashca bhavati -- caturShu vedeShu paraM shreyo.alabdhvA shANDilya idaM shAstram adhigatavAn ityAdi vedanindAdarshanAt | tasmAt asaN^gataiShA kalpaneti siddham ||45|| 

iti shrImatparamahaMsaparivrAjakAcAryasya shrIgovindabhagavatpUjyapAdashiShyasya shrImacchaN^karabhagavataH kR^itau shArIrakamImAMsAsUtrabhAShye 
dvitIyAdhyAyasya dvitIyaH pAdaH || 
||2.2||

 
(2.3)

|| dvitIyAdhyAye tR^itIyaH pAdaH ||

atra pAde paJNcamahAbhUtajIvAdishrutInAM virodhaparihAraH ||
 
1. viyadadhikaraNam 

|| 2.3.1 || 

vedAnteShu tatra tatra bhinnaprasthAnA utpattishrutaya upalabhyante | kecid AkAshasyotpattim Amananti, kecin na | tathA kecid vAyor utpattim Amananti, kecin na | evaM jIvasya prANAnAM ca | evam eva kramAdidvArako.api vipratiShedhaH shrutyantareShUpalakShyate | vipratiShedhAcca parapakShANAm anapekShitatvaM sthApitaM tadvat svapakShasyApi vipratiShedhAd evAnapekShitatvam AshaN^kyetetyataH sarvavedAntagatasR^iShTishrutyarthanirmalatvAya paraH papraJNca Arabhyate | tadarthanirmalatve ca phalaM yathoktAshaN^kAnivR^ittir eva | tatra prathamaM tAvad AkAsham Ashritya cintyate -- kim asyAkAshasyotpattir asti, uta nAstIti ? tatra tAvat pratipadyate -- 

na viyadashruteH ||

na khalvakAsham utpadyate | kasmAt? ashruteH -- na hyasyotpattiprakaraNe shravaNam asti | chAndogye hi sad eva somyedam agra AsId ekam evAdvitIyam iti sacchabdavAcyaM brahma prakR^itya, tad aikShata tat tejo.asR^ijata iti ca paJNcAnAM mahAbhUtAnAM madhyamaM teja Adi kR^itvA trayANAM tejo.abannAnAm utpattiH shrAvyate | shrutishca naH pramANam atIndriyArthavij~nAnotpattau | na ca atra shrutir astyAkAshasyotpattipratipAdinI | tasmAn nAkAshasyotpattiH iti ||

|| 2.3.2 ||

asti tu || 

tushabdaH pakShAntaraparigrahe | mA nAmAkAshasya chAndogye.abhUd utpattiH | shrutyantare tu asti | taittirIyakA hi samAmananti -- satyaM j~nAnam anantaM brahma [tai.u. 2.1.1] iti prakR^itya, tasmAd vA etasmAd Atmana AkAshaH sambhUtaH iti | tatashca shrutyor vipratiShedhaH -- kvacit tejaHpramukhA sR^iShTiH, kvacid AkAshapramukheti | nanvekavAkyatA anayoH shrutyoryuktA | satyaM sA yuktA, na tu sA avagantuM shakyate | kutaH? tattejo.asR^ijata iti sakR^icchrutasya sraShTuH sraShTavyadvayena sambandhAnupapatteH -- tattejo.asR^ijata tadAkAshamasR^ijata iti | 

nanu sakR^icchrutasyApi kartuH kartavyadvayena sambandho dR^ishyate -- yathA saH sUpaM paktvA odanaM pacatIti, evaM tadAkAshaM sR^iShTvA tattejo.asR^ijata iti yojayiShyAmi | naivaM yujyate | prathamajatvaM hi chAndogye tejaso.avagamyate | taittirIyake ca AkAshasya | na ca ubhayoH prathamajatvaM sambhavati | etena itarashrutyakSharavirodho.api vyAkhyAtaH -- tasmAd vA etasmAd Atmana AkAshaH sambhUtaH ityatrApi -- tasmAd AkAshaH sambhUtaH, tasmAt tejaH sambhUtam -- iti sakR^icchrutasyApAdAnasya sambhavanasya ca viyattejobhyAM yugapatsambandhAnupapatteH, vAyor agniH iti ca pR^ithagAmnAnAt ||2|| 

|| 2.3.3 ||

asmin vipratiShedhe kashcid Aha -- 

gauNyasambhavAt || 

nAsti viyata utpattiH, ashruter eva | yA tvitarA viyadutpattivAdinI shrutir udAhR^itA, sA gauNI bhavitum arhati | kasmAt? asambhavAt | na hyAkAshasyotpattiH sambhAvayituM shakyA, shrImatkaNabhugabhiprAyAnusAriShu jIvatsu | te hi kAraNasAmagryasambhavAd AkAshasyotpattiM vArayanti | samavAyyasamavAyinimittakAraNebhyo hi kila sarvam utpadyamAnaM samutpadyate | dravyasya caikajAtIyakam anekaM ca dravyaM samavAyikAraNaM bhavati | na cAkAshasyaikajAtIyakam anekaM ca dravyam Arambhakam asti | yasmin samavAyikAraNe sati, asamavAyikAraNe ca tatsaMyoge, AkAsha utpadyeta | tadabhAvAt tu tadanugrahapravR^ittaM nimittakAraNaM dUrApetam eva AkAshasya bhavati | utpattimatAM ca tejaHprabhR^itInAM 
pUrvottarakAlayor visheShaH sambhAvyate -- prAgutpatteH prakAshAdikAryaM na babhUva, pashcAcca bhavatIti | AkAshasya punar na pUrvottarakAlayor visheShaH sambhAvayituM shakyate | kiM hi prAgutpatter anavakAsham asuShiram acchidraM babhUveti shakyate.adhyavasAtum? pR^ithivyAdivaidharmyAcca vibhutvAdilakShaNAt AkAshasya ajatvasiddhiH | tasmAd yathA loke -- AkAshaM kuru, AkAsho jAtaH ityevaMjAtIyako gauNaH prayogo bhavati, yathA ca ghaTAkAshaH, karakAkAshaH gR^ihAkAshaH -- ityekasyApyAkAshasya evaMjAtIyako bhedavyapadesho gauNo bhavati -- vede.api AraNyAnAkAsheShvalabheran iti | evam utpattishrutir api gauNI draShTavyA ||3||

|| 2.3.4 || 

shabdAcca || 

shabdaH khalvapyAkAshasya ajatvaM khyApayati, yata Aha -- vAyushcAntarikShaM caitad amR^itam [bR^i.A.u. 2.3.3] iti | na hyamR^itasyotpattir upapadyate | AkAshavat sarvagatashca nityaH iti ca AkAshena brahma sarvagatatvanityatvAbhyAM dharmAbhyAm upamimAnaH AkAshasyApi tau dharmau sUcayati | na ca tAdR^ishasyotpattir upapadyate | sa yathA -- ananto.ayam AkAsha evam ananta AtmA veditavyaH iti ca udAharaN, AkAshasharIraM brahma [tai.u. 1.6.2], AkAsha AtmA [tai.u. 1.7.1] iti ca | na hyAkAshasyotpattimattve brahmaNaH tena visheShaNaM sambhavati -- nIlenevotpalasya | tasmAn nityam evAkAshena sAdhAraNaM brahmeti gamyate ||4||

 || 2.3.5 || 

idaM padottaraM sUtram | syAd etat | kathaM punar ekasya sambhUtashabdasya -- tasmAd vA etasmAd Atmana AkAshaH sambhUtaH [tai.u. 2.1] ityasminn adhikAre pareShu tejaHprabhR^itiShvanuvartamAnasya mukhyatvaM sambhavati, AkAshe ca gauNatvam iti | ata uttaram ucyate -- 

syAccaikasya brahmashabdavat ||

syAccaikasyApi sambhUtashabdasya viShayavisheShavashAd gauNo mukhyashca prayogaH -- brahmashabdavat | yathaikasyApi brahmashabdasya tapasA brahma vijij~nAsasva tapo brahma [tai.u. 3.2] ityasminn adhikAre.annAdiShu gauNaH prayogaH, Anande ca mukhyaH | yathA ca tapasi brahmavij~nAnasAdhane brahmashabdo bhaktyA prayujyate, aJNjasA tu vij~neye brahmaNi, tadvat | kathaM punar anutpattau nabhasaH ekam evAdvitIyam [chA.u. 6.2.1] itIyaM pratij~nA samarthyate?
