nanu nabhasA dvitIyena sadvitIyaM brahma prApnoti | kathaM ca brahmaNi vidite sarvaM viditaM syAt ? iti, tad ucyate -- ekam eva iti tAvat svakAryApekShayopapadyate | yathA loke kashcit kumbhakArakule pUrvedyur mR^iddaNDacakrAdIni ca upalabhya aparedyushca nAnAvidhAnyamatrANi prasAritAnyupalabhya brUyAt -- mR^id evaikAkinI pUrvedyur AsIt iti, sa ca tayAvadhAraNayA mR^itkAryajAtam eva pUrvedyur nAsId ityabhipreyAt, na daNDacakrAdi -- tadvad advitIyashrutir adhiShThAtrantaraM vArayati -- yathA mR^ido.amatraprakR^iteH kumbhakAro.adhiShThAtA dR^ishyate, naivaM brahmaNo jagatprakR^iter anyo.adhiShThAtA astIti | na ca nabhasApi dvitIyena sadvitIyaM brahma prasajyate | lakShaNAnyatvanimittaM hi nAnAtvam | na ca prAgutpatter brahmanabhasor lakShaNAnyatvam asti -- kShIrodakayoH iva saMsR^iShTayoH -- vyApitvAmUrtatvAdidharmasAmAnyAt | sargakAle tu brahma jagad utpAdayituM yatate, stimitam itarat tiShThati, tenAnyatvam avasIyate | tathA ca AkAshasharIraM brahma ityAdishrutibhyo.api brahmAkAshayor abhedopacArasiddhiH | ata eva ca brahmavij~nAnena sarvavij~nAnasiddhiH | 

api ca sarvaM kAryam utpadyamAnam AkAshenAvyatiriktadeshakAlam evotpadyate, brahmaNA ca avyatiriktadeshakAlam evAkAshaM bhavatIti -- ato brahmaNA tatkAryeNa ca vij~nAtena saha vij~nAtam evAkAshaM bhavati -- yathA kShIrapUrNe ghaTo katicid abbindavaH prakShiptAH santaH kShIragrahaNenaiva gR^ihItA bhavanti | na hi kShIragrahaNAd abbindugrahaNaM parishiShyate | evaM brahmaNA tatkAryaishcAvyatiriktadeshakAlatvAt gR^ihItam eva brahmagrahaNena nabho bhavati | tasmAd bhAktaM nabhasaH sambhavashravaNam iti ||5|| 

|| 2.3.6 || 

evaM prApte, idam Aha -- 

pratij~nA.ahAnir avyatirekAcchabdebhyaH ||

yenAshrutaM shrutaM bhavatyamataM matam avij~nAtaM vij~nAtam [chA.u. 6.1.3] iti, Atmani khalvare dR^iShTe shrute mate vij~nAte idaM sarvaM viditam iti, kasmin nu bhagavo vij~nAte sarvam idaM vij~nAtaM bhavati [mu.u. 1.1.3] iti, na kAcana madbahirdhA vidyAsti iti caivaMrUpA prativedAntaM pratij~nA vij~nAyate | tasyAH pratij~nAyA evam ahAnir anuparodhaH syAt, yadyavyatirekaH kR^itsnasya vastujAtasya vij~neyAd brahmaNaH syAt | vyatireke hi sati ekavij~nAnAnena sarvaM vij~nAyata itIyaM pratij~nA hIyeta | sa cAvyatireka evam upapadyate, yadi kR^itsnaM vastujAtam ekasmAd brahmaNa utpadyeta | shabdebhyashca prakR^itivikArAvyatirekanyAyenaiva pratij~nAsiddhir avagamyate | tathA hi -- yenAshrutaM shrutaM bhavati [chA.u. 6.1.3] iti pratij~nAya, mR^idAdidR^iShTAntaiH kAryakAraNAbhedapratipAdanaparaiH pratij~naiShA samarthyate | tatsAdhanAyaiva cottare shabdAH -- sad eva somyedam agra AsId ekam evAdvitIyam [chA.u. 6.2.1], tad aikShata tat tejo.asR^ijata ityevaM kAryajAtaM brahmaNaH pradarshya, avyatirekaM pradarshayanti -- aitadAtmyam idaM sarvam ityArabhya AprapAThakaparisamApteH | tad yadyAkAshaM na brahmakAryaM syAt, na brahmaNi vij~nAte AkAshaM vij~nAyeta | tatashca pratij~nAhAniH syAt | na ca pratij~nAhAnyA vedasyAprAmANyaM yuktaM kartum | tathA hi prativedAntaM te te shabdAH tena tena dR^iShTAntena tAm eva pratij~nAM j~nApayanti -- idaM sarvaM yad ayam AtmA [bR^i.A.u. 2.4.6], brahmaivedam amR^itaM purastAt [mu.u. 2.2.11] ityevamAdayaH | tasmAjjvalanAdivad eva gaganam apyutpadyate || 

yad uktam -- ashruter na viyad utpadyata iti, tad ayuktam, viyadutpattiviShayashrutyantarasya darshitatvAt -- tasmAd vA etasmAd Atmana AkAshaH sambhUtaH iti | satyaM darshitam, viruddhaM tu tat tejo.asR^ijata ityanena shrutyantareNa | na, ekavAkyatvAt sarvashrutInAm | bhavatv ekavAkyatvam aviruddhAnAm | iha tu virodha uktaH -- sakR^icchrutasya sraShTuH sraShTavyadvayasambandhAsambhavAd dvayoshca prathamajatvAsambhavAd vikalpAsambhavAcceti -- naiSha doShaH, tejaHsargasya taittirIyake tR^itIyatvashravaNAt -- tasmAd vA etasmAd Atmana AkAshaH sambhUtaH, AkAshAd vAyuH, vAyor agniH iti | ashakyA hIyaM shrutir anyathA pariNetum | shakyA tu pariNetuM chAndogyashrutiH -- tad AkAshaM vAyuM ca sR^iShTvA tat tejo.asR^ijata iti | na hIyaM shrutiH tejojanipradhAnA satI shrutyantaraprasiddhAm AkAshasyotpattiM vArayituM shaknoti, ekasya vAkyasya vyApAradvayAsambhavAt | sraShTA tv eko.api krameNAnekaM sraShTavyaM sR^ijet -- ityekavAkyatvakalpanAyAM sambhavantyAM na viruddhArthatvena shrutir hAtavyA | na cAsmAbhiH sakR^icchrutasya sraShTuH sraShTavyadvayasambandho.abhipreyate, shrutyantaravashena sraShTavyAntaropasaMgrahAt | yathA ca sarvaM khalvidaM brahma tajjalAn [chA.u. 3.14.1] ityatra sAkShAd eva sarvasya vastujAtasya brahmajatvaM shrUyamANaM na pradeshAntaravihitaM tejaHpramukham utpattikramaM vArayati, evaM tejaso.api brahmajatvaM shrUyamANaM na shrutyantaravihitaM nabhaHpramukham utpattikramaM vArayitum arhati | 

nanu shamavidhAnArtham etad vAkyam -- tajjalAn iti shAnta upAsIta [chA.u. 3.14.1] iti shruteH | naitat sR^iShTivAkyam | tasmAd etan na pradeshAntaraprasiddhaM kramam anuroddhum arhatIti | tat tejo.asR^ijata [chA.u. 6.2.3] ityetat sR^iShTivAkyam | tasmAd atra yathAshruti kramo grahItavya iti | netyucyate | na hi tejaHprAthamyAnurodhena shrutyantaraprasiddho viyatpadArthaH parityaktavyo bhavati, padArthadharmatvAt kramasya | 

api ca tat tejo.asR^ijata [chA.u. 6.2.3] iti nAtra kramasya vAcakaH kashcicchabdo.asti | arthAt tu kramo gamyate | sa ca vAyor agniH ityanena shrutyantaraprasiddhena krameNa nivAryate | vikalpasamuccayau tu viyattejasoH prathamajatvaviShayAvasambhavAnabhyupagamAbhyAM nivAritau | tasmAn nAsti shrutyor vipratiShedhaH | api ca chAndogye yenAshrutaM shrutaM bhavati [chA.u. 6.1.3] ityetAM pratij~nAM vAkyopakrame shrutAM samarthayitum asamAmnAtam api viyadutpattAv upasaMkhyAtavyam | kim aN^ga punaH taittirIyake samAmnAtaM nabho na saMgR^ihyate | yaccoktam -- AkAshasya sarveNAnanyad eshakAlatvAd brahmaNA tatkAryaishca saha viditam eva tad bhavati | ato na pratij~nA hIyate | na ca ekam evAdvitIyam [chA.u. 6.2.1] iti shrutikopo bhavati, kShIrodakavad brahmanabhasor avyatirekopapatteH iti | 

atrocyate -- na kShIrodakanyAyenedam ekavij~nAnena sarvavij~nAnaM netavyam | mR^idAdidR^iShTAntapraNayanAd dhi prakR^itivikAranyAyenaivedaM sarvavij~nAnaM netavyam iti gamyate | kShIrodakanyAyena ca sarvavij~nAnaM kalpyamAnaM na samyagvij~nAnaM syAt | na hi kShIraj~nAnagR^ihItasyodakasya samyagvij~nAnagR^ihItatvam asti | na ca vedasya puruShANAm iva mAyAlIkavaJNcanAdibhir arthAvadhAraNam upapadyate | sAvadhAraNA ceyam ekam evAdvitIyam [chA.u. 6.2.1] iti shrutiH kShIrodakanyAyena nIyamAnA pIDyata | na ca svakAryApekShayedaM vastvekadeshaviShayaM sarvavij~nAnam evAdvitIyatAvadhAraNaM ceti nyAyyam, mR^idAdiShvapi hi tatsambhavAt -- na tad apUrvavad upanyasitavyaM bhavati -- shvetaketo yan nu somyedaM mahAmanA anUcAnamAnI stabdho.asyuta tam Adesham aprAkShyaH yenAshrutaM shrutaM bhavati [chA.u. 6.1.3] ityAdinA | tasmAd asheShavastuviShayam evedaM sarvavij~nAnaM sarvasya brahmakAryatApekShayopanyasyata iti draShTavyam ||6|| 

|| 2.3.7 ||

yat punar etad uktam -- asambhavAd gauNI gaganasyotpattishrutiH iti, atra brUmaH -- 

yAvad vikAraM tu vibhAgo lokavat ||

tushabdo.asambhavAshaN^kAvyAvR^ittyarthaH | na khalvakAshotpattAvasambhavAshaN^kA kartavyA | yato yAvat kiMcid vikArajAtaM dR^ishyate -- ghaTaghaTikodaJNcanAdi vA, kaTakakeyUrakuNDalAdi vA, sUcInArAcanistriMshAdi vA -- tAvAn eva vibhAgo loke lakShyate | na tu avikR^itaM kiMcit kutashcid vibhaktam upalabhyate | vibhAgashcAkAshasya pR^ithivyAdibhyo.avagamyate | tasmAt so.api vikAro bhavitum arhati | etena dikkAlamanaHparamANvAdInAM kAryatvaM vyAkhyAtam | 

nanvatmApyAkAshAdibhyo vibhakta iti tasyApi kAryatvaM ghaTAdivat prApnoti | na, Atmana AkAshaH sambhUtaH iti shruteH | yadi hyAtmApi vikAraH syAt, tasmAt param anyan na shrutam ityAkAshAdi sarvaM kAryaM nirAtmakam AtmanaH kAryatve syAt | tathA ca shUnyavAdaH prasajyeta | AtmatvAccAtmano nirAkaraNashaN^kAnupapattiH na hyAtmAgantukaH kasyacit, svayaMsiddhatvAt | na hyAtmA AtmanaH pramANam apekShya sidhyati | tasya hi pratyakShAdIni pramANAnyasiddhaprameyasiddhaye upAdIyante | na hyAkAshAdayaH padArthAH pramANanirapekShAH svayaM siddhAH kenacid abhyupagamyante | AtmA tu pramANAdivyavahArAshrayatvAt prAg eva pramANAdivyavahArAt sidhyati | na cedR^ishasya nirAkaraNaM sambhavati | AgantukaM hi vastu nirAkriyate, na svarUpam | ya eva hi nirAkartA, tad eva tasya svarUpam | na hyagner auShNyam agninA nirAkriyate | tathA aham evedAnIM jAnAmi vartamAnaM vastu, aham evAtItam atItataraM cAj~nAsiSham, aham evAnAgatam anAgatataraM ca j~nAsyAmi, ityatItAn AgatavartamAnabhAvenAnyathAbhavatyapi j~nAtavye na j~nAtur anyathAbhAvo.asti, sarvadA vartamAnasvabhAvatvAt | tathA bhasmIbhavatyapi dehe nAtmana ucchedaH | vartamAnasvabhAvAd anyasvabhAvatvaM vA na sambhAvayituM shakyam | evam apratyAkhyeyasvabhAvatvAd akAryatvam AtmAnaH, kAryatvaM ca AkAshasya || 

yat tUktaM samAnajAtIyam anekaM kAraNadravyaM vyomno nAstIti, tat pratyucyate -- na tAvat samAnajAtIyam evArabhate, na bhinnajAtIyam iti niyamo.asti | na hi tantUnAM tatsaMyogAnAM ca samAnajAtIyatvam asti, dravyaguNatvAbhyupagamAt | na ca nimittakAraNAnAm api turIvemAdInAM samAnajAtIyatvaniyamo.asti | syAd etat -- samavAyikAraNaviShaya eva samAnajAtIyatvAbhyupagamaH, na kAraNAntaraviShaya iti | tad apyanaikAntikam | sUtragobAlair hyanekajAtIyair ekA rajjuH sR^ijyamAnA dR^ishyate | tathA sUtrair UrNAdibhishca vicitrAn kambalAn vitanvate | sattvadravyatvAdyapekShayA vA samAnajAtIyatve kalpyamAne niyamAn arthakyam, sarvasya sarveNa samAnajAtIyakatvAt | 

nApyanekam evArabhate, naikam -- iti niyamo.asti | aNumanasor AdyakarmArambhAbhyupagamAt | ekaiko hi paramANur manashcAdyaM karmArabhate, na dravyAntaraiH saMhatya -- ityabhyupagamyate | dravyArambha evAnekArambhakatvaniyama iti cet, na | pariNAmAbhyupagamAt | bhaved eSha niyamaH -- yadi saMyogasacivaM dravyaM dravyAntarasyArambhakam abhyupagamyeta | tad eva tu dravyaM visheShavad avasthAntaram ApadyamAnaM kAryaM nAmAbhyupagamyate | tacca kvacid anekaM pariNamate mR^id bIjAdi, aN^kurAdibhAvena | kvacid ekaM pariNamate kShIrAdi, dadhyAdibhAvena | neshvarashAsanam iti -- anekam eva kAraNaM kAryaM janayatIti | ataH shrutiprAmANyAd ekasmAd brahmaNa AkAshAdimahAbhUtotpattikrameNa jagajjAtam iti nishcIyate | tathA coktam -- upasaMhAradarshanAn neti cen na kShIravad dhi iti || 

yaccoktam AkAshasyotpattau na pUrvottarakAlayor visheShaH sambhAvayituM shakyata iti, tad ayuktam | yenaiva visheSheNa pR^ithivyAdibhyo vyatiricyamAnaM nabhaH svarUpavadidAnImadhyavasIyate, sa eva visheShaH prAgutpatter nAsId iti gamyate | yathA ca brahma na sthUlAdibhiH pR^ithivyAdisvabhAvaiH svabhAvavat -- asthUlamanaNu ityAdishrutibhyaH, evamAkAshasvabhAvenApi na svabhAvavadanAkAsham iti shruteravagamyate | tasmAt prAgutpatter anAkAsham iti sthitam | yadapyuktaM pR^ithivyAdivaidharmyAdAkAshasyAjatvam iti, tadapyasat, shrutivirodhe satyutpattyasambhavAnumAnasyAbhAsatvopapatteH, utpattyanumAnasya ca darshitatvAt | anityamAkAsham, anityaguNAshrayatvAt, ghaTAdivadityAdiprayogasambhavAcca | AtmanyanaikAntikam iti cet, na | tasyaupaniShadaM pratyanityaguNAshrayatvAsiddhiH | vibhutvAd InAM ca AkAshasyotpattivAdinaM pratyasiddhatvAt | yaccoktam etat -- shabdAcceti -- tatrAmR^itatvashrutistAvadviyati amR^itA divaukasaH itivaddraShTavyA | utpattipralayayor upapAditatvAt | AkAshavat sarvagatashca nityaH ityapi 
prasiddhamahattvenAkAshopamAnaM kriyate niratishayamahattvAya, na AkAshasamatvAya -- yathA iShuriva savitA dhAvati iti kShipragatitvAyocyate, na iShutulyagatitvAya, tadvat | etenAnantatvopamAnashrutir vyAkhyAtA | jyAyAnAkAshAt ityAdishrutibhyashca brahmaNaH sakAshAdAkAshasyonaparimANatvasiddhiH na tasya pratimAsti iti ca brahmaNo.anupamAnatvaM darshayati | ato.anyadArtam iti ca brahmaNo.anyeShAmAkAshAdInAmArtatvaM darshayati | tapasi brahmashabdavadAkAshasya janmashruter gauNatvam ityetad AkAshasambhavashrutyanumAnAbhyAM parihR^itam | tasmAd brahmakAryaM viyad iti siddham ||

mAtarishvAdhikaraNam

|| 2.3.8 || 

etena mAtarishvA vyAkhyAtaH ||

atidesho.ayam | etena viyadvyAkhyAnena mAtarishvApi viyadAshrayo vAyur vyAkhyAtaH | tatrApyete yathAyogaM pakShA racayitavyAH -- na vAyur utpadyate, chandogAnAm utpattiprakaraNe.anAmnAnAd ityekaH pakShaH, asti tu taittirIyANAm utpattiprakaraNe AmnAnam AkAshAd vAyuH -- iti pakShAntaram | tatashca shrutyor vipratiShedhe sati gauNI vAyor utpattishrutiH, asambhavAt ityaparo.abhiprAyaH | asambhavashca saiShAnastamitA devatA yad vAyuH ityastamayapratiShedhAd amR^itatvAdishravaNAcca | pratij~nAnuparodhAd yAvadvikAraM ca vibhAgAbhyupagamAd utpadyate vAyuH iti siddhAntaH | astamayapratiShedho.aparavidyAviShaya ApekShikaH, agnyAdInAm iva vAyor astamayAbhAvAt | kR^itapratividhAnaM ca amR^itatvAd ishravaNam | 

nanu vAyor AkAshasya ca tulyayor utpattiprakaraNe shravaNAshravaNayor ekam evAdhikaraNam ubhayaviShayam astu kim atideshenAsati visheSha iti, ucyate -- satyam evam etat | tathApi mandadhiyAM shabdamAtrakR^itAshaN^kAnivR^ittyartho.ayam atideshaH kriyate -- saMvargavidyAdiShu hyupAsyata vAyor mahAbhAgatvashravaNAt astamayapratiShedhAdibhyashca bhavati nityatvAshaN^kA kasyacid iti ||38||

asambhavAdhikaraNam

|| 2.3.9 || 

asambhavaH tu sato.anupapatteH ||

viyatpavanayor asambhAvyamAnajanmanor apyutpattim upashrutya, brahmaNo.api bhavet kutashcid utpattiH iti syAt kasyacin matiH | tathA vikArebhya evAkAshAdibhya uttareShAM vikArANAm utpattim upashrutya, AkAshasyApi vikArAd eva brahmaNa utpattiH iti kashcin manyeta | tAm AshaN^kAm apanetum idaM sUtram -- asambhavaH tviti | na khalu brahmaNaH sadAtmakasya kutashcid anyataH sambhava utpattir AshaN^kitavyA | kasmAt? anupapatteH | sanmAtraM hi brahma | na tasya sanmAtrAd evotpattiH sambhavati, asatyatishaye prakR^itivikArabhAvAnupapatteH | nApi sadvisheShAt, dR^iShTaviparyayAt -- sAmAnyAd visheShA utpadyamAnA dR^ishyante, mR^idAder ghaTAdayaH, na tu visheShebhyaH sAmAnyam | nApyasataH, nirAtmakatvAt | katham asataH sajjAyeta iti ca AkShepashravaNAt | sa kAraNaM karaNAdhipAdhipo na cAsya kashcijjanitA na cAdhipaH [shve.u. 6.9] iti ca brahmaNo janayitAraM vArayati | viyatpavanayoH punar utpattiH pradarshitA, na tu brahmaNaH sA astIti vaiShamyam | na ca vikArebhyo vikArAntarotpattidarshanAd brahmaNo.api vikAratvaM bhavitum arhati, mUlaprakR^ityanabhyupagame.anavasthAprasaN^gAt | yA mUlaprakR^itir abhyupagamyate, tad eva ca no brahmetyavirodhaH ||9||

tejo.adhikaraNam

|| 2.3.10 ||

chAndogye sanmUlatvaM tejasaH shrAvitam, taittirIyake tu vAyumUlatvam | tatra tejoyoniM prati shrutivipratipattau satyAm, prAptaM tAvad brahmayonikaM teja iti | kutaH? sad eva ityupakramya tat tejo.asR^ijata [chA.u. 6.2.3] ityupadeshAt | sarvavij~nAnapratij~nAyAshca, brahmaprabhavatve sarvasya, sambhavAt | tajjalAn iti ca avisheShashruteH | etasmAjjAyate prANaH [mu.u. 2.1.3] iti ca upakramya shrutyantare sarvasyAvisheSheNa brahmajatvopadeshAt | taittirIyake ca sa tapaH taptvA | idaM sarvam asR^ijata | yad idaM kiMca ityavisheShashravaNAt | tasmAt -- vAyor agniH iti kramopadesho draShTavyaH | vAyor anantaram agniH sambhUta iti | evaM prApte, ucyate -- 

tejo.ataH tathA hyAha || 

tejo.ataH mAtarishvanaH jAyata iti | kasmAt? tathA hyAha -- vAyor agniH iti | 
avyavahite hi tejaso brahmajatve sati, asati vAyujatve vAyor agniH itIyaM shrutiH kadarthitA syAt | 

nanu kramArthaiShA bhaviShyatItyuktam | neti brUmaH -- tasmAd vA etasmAd Atmana AkAshaH sambhUtaH iti purastAt sambhavatyapAdAnasya AtmanaH paJNcamInirdeshAt, tasyaiva ca sambhavaterihAdhikArAt, parastAd api tadadhikAre pR^ithivyA oShadhayaH ityapAdAnapaJNcamIdarshanAt, vAyor agniH ityapAdAnapaJNcamyevaiSheti gamyate | api ca, vAyor UrdhvamagniH sambhUtaH -- iti kalpyaH upapadArthayogaH, kptastu kArakArthayogaH -- vAyor agniH sambhUtaH iti | tasmAd eShA shrutir vAyuyonitvaM tejaso.avagamayati | nanvitarApi shrutir brahmayonitvaM tejaso.avagamayati -- tattejo.asR^ijata iti | na, tasyAH pAramparyajatve.apyavirodhAt | yadApi hyAkAshaM vAyuM ca sR^iShTvA vAyubhAvApannaM brahma tejo.asR^ijateti kalpyate, tadApi brahmajatvaM tejaso na virudhyate, yathA -- tasyAH sR^itam, tasyA dadhi, tasyA AmikShetyAdi | darshayati ca brahmaNo vikArAtmanAvasthAnam -- tadAtmAnaMsvayamakuruta iti | tathA ca IshvarasmaraNaM bhavati -- buddhir j~nAnamasaMmohaH ityAdyanukramya bhavanti bhAvA bhUtAnAM matta eva pR^ithagvidhAH iti | yadyapi buddhyAdayaH svakAraNebhyaH pratyakShaM bhavanto dR^ishyante, tathApi sarvasya bhAvajAtasya sAkShAt praNADAa vA IshvaravaMshyatvAt | etenAkramasR^iShTivAdinyaH shrutayo vyAkhyAtAH, tAsAM sarvathopapatteH, kramavatsR^iShTivAdinInAM tu anyathAnupapatteH | pratij~nApi sauMshyatvamAtramapekShate, na avyavahitajanyatvam -- ityavirodhaH ||10||

7. abadhikaraNam

|| 2.3.11 ||

ApaH ||

 atastathA hyAha ityanuvartate | ApaH, ataH tejasaH, jAyante | kasmAt? tathA hyAha -- tadapo.asR^ijata iti, agnerApaH iti ca | sati vacane nAsti saMshayaH | tejasaH tu sR^iShTiM vyAkhyAya pR^ithivyA vyAkhyAsyan, apo.antariyAm iti ApaH iti sUtrayAm babhUva ||11||

8. pR^ithivyadhikArAdhikaraNam

|| 2.3.12 || 

tA Apa aikShanta bahvyaH syAma prajAyemahIti tA annam asR^ijanta [chA.u. 6.2.4] iti shrUyate | tatra saMshayaH -- kim anenAnnashabdena vrIhiyavAdyabhyavahAryaM vA odanAdyucyate, kiM vA pR^ithivIti | tatra prAptaM tAvat -- vrIhiyavAdi odanAdi vA parigrahItavyam iti | tatra hyannashabdaH prasiddho loke | vAkyasheSho.apyetam artham upodvalayati -- tasmAd yatra kvacana varShati tad eva bhUyiShTham annaM bhavati iti -- vrIhiyavAdyeva hi sati varShaNe bahu bhavati, na pR^ithivIti || evaM prApte, 

pR^ithivyadhikArarUpashabdAntarebhyaH ||

brUmaH -- pR^ithivyeveyam annashabdenAdbhyo jAyamAnA vivakShyata iti | kasmAt? adhikArAt, rUpAt, shabdAntarAcca | adhikAraH tAvat -- tat tejo.asR^ijata tad apo.asR^ijata [chA.u. 6.2.3] iti mahAbhUtaviShayo vartate | tatra kramaprAptAM pR^ithivIM mahAbhUtaM vilaN^ghya nAkasmAd vrIhyAdiparigraho nyAyyaH | tathA rUpam api vAkyasheShe pR^ithivyanuguNaM dR^ishyate -- yat kR^iShNaM tad annasya iti | na hy odanAder abhyavahAryasya kR^iShNatvaniyamo.asti, nApi vrIhyAdInAm | 

nanu pR^ithivyA api naiva kR^iShNatvaniyamo.asti, payaHpANDurasyAN^gArarohitasya ca kShetrasya darshanAt | nAyaM doShaH -- bAhulyApekShatvAt | bhUyiShThaM hi pR^ithivyAH kR^iShNaM rUpam, na tathA shvetarohite | paurANikA api pR^ithivIcchAyAM sharvarIm upadishanti, sA ca kR^iShNAbhAsA -- ityataH kR^iShNaM rUpaM pR^ithivyA iti shliShyate | shrutyantaram api samAnAdhikAram -- adabhyaH pR^ithivI iti bhavati, tad yad apAM shara AsIt tat samahanyata sA pR^ithivyabhavat iti ca | pR^ithivyAH tu vrIhyAder utpattiM darshayati -- pR^ithivyA oShadhaya oShadhIbhyo.annam iti ca | evam adhikArAdiShu pR^ithivyAH pratipAdakeShu satsu kuto vrIhyAdipratipattiH? prasiddhir apyadhikArAdibhir eva bAdhyate | vAkyasheSho.api pArthivatvAd annAdyasya taddvAreNa pR^ithivyA evAdbhyaH prabhavatvaM sUcayatIti draShTavyam | tasmAt pR^ithivIyam annashabdeti ||12||

9. tadabhidhyAnAdhikaraNam

|| 2.3.13 ||

kim imAni viyadAdIni bhUtAni svayam eva svavikArAn sR^ijanti, Aho svit parameshvara eva tena tena AtmanAvatiShThamAno.abhidhyAyan taM taM vikAraM sR^ijatIti sandehe sati, prAptaM tAvat -- svayam eva sR^ijantIti | kutaH? AkAshAd vAyur vAyor agniH ityAdisvAtantryashravaNAt | 

nanu acetanAnAM svatantrANAM pravR^ittiH pratiShiddhA | naiSha doShaH -- tat teja aikShata tA Apa IkShanta iti ca bhUtAnAm api cetanatvashravaNAd iti || evaM prApte, 

tadabhidhyAnAd eva tu talliN^gAt saH ||

abhidhIyate -- sa eva parameshvarastena tena AtmanA avatiShThamAno.abhidhyAyan taM taM vikAraM sR^ijatIti | kutaH? talliN^gAt | tathA hi shAstram -- yaH pR^ithivyAM tiShThan yaH pR^ithivyA antaro yaM pR^ithivI na veda yasya pR^ithivI sharIraM yaH pR^ithivI mantaro yamayati [bR^i.A.u. 3.7.3] ityevaMjAtIyakam -- sAdhyakShANAm eva bhUtAnAM pravR^ittiM darshayati | tathA so.akAmayata bahu syAM prajAyeyeti [tai.u. 2.6] iti prastutya, sacca tyaccAbhavat, tadAtmAnaM svayamakuruta iti ca tasyaiva ca sarvAtmabhAvaM darshayati | yat tu IkShaNashravaNamaptejasoH, tatparameshvarAveshavashAd eva draShTavyam -- nAnyo.ato.asti draShTA itIkShitrantarapratiShedhAt, prakR^itatvAcca sata IkShituH tadaikShata bahu syAM prajAyeyeti ityatra ||13||

 -- o)0(o -- 
viparyayAdhikaraNam 

|| 2.3.14 || 

bhUtAnAm utpattikramashcintitaH | athedAnIm apyayakramashcintyate -- kim aniyatena krameNApyayaH, uta utpattikrameNa, athavA tadviparItena ? iti | trayo.api ca utpattisthitipralayA bhUtAnAM brahmAyattAH shrUyante -- yato vA imAni bhUtAni jAyante, yena jAtAni jIvanti, yat prayantyabhisaMvishanti [tai.u. 3.1] iti | tatrAniyamo.avisheShAd iti prAptam | athavA utpatteH kramasya shrutatvAt pralayasyApi kramAkAN^kShiNaH sa eva kramaH syAd iti || evaM prAptaM -- 

viparyayeNa tu kramo.ata upapadyate ca ||

 tato brUmaH -- viparyayeNa tu pralayakramaH, ataH utpattikramAt, bhavitum arhati | tathA hi loke dR^ishyate -- yena krameNa sopAnamArUDhaH, tato viparItena krameNAvarohatIti | api ca dR^ishyate -- mR^ido jAtaM ghaTasharAvAdi apyayakAle mR^idbhAvamapyeti, adbhyashca jAtaM himakarakAdi abbhAvamapyetIti | atashcopapadyata etat -- yatpR^ithivI adbhyo jAtA satI sthitikAlavyatikrAntau apo.apIyAt | Apashca tejaso jAtAH satyaH tejo.apIyuH | evaM krameNa sUkShmaM sUkShmataraM ca anantaram anantarataraM kAraNam apItya sarvaM kAryajAtaM paramakAraNaM paramasUkShmaM ca brahmApyetIti veditavyam | na hi svakAraNavyatikrameNa kAraNakAraNe kAryApyayo nyAyyaH | smR^itAvapyutpattikramaviparyayeNaivApyayakramastatra tatra darshitaH -- jagatpratiShThA devarShe pR^ithivyapsu pralIyate | jyotiShyApaH pralIyante jyotirvAyau pralIyate ityevamAdau | utpattikramastu utpattAveva shrutatvAnnApyaye bhavitum arhati | na ca asau ayogyatvAd apyayenAkAN^kShyate | na hi kArye dhrIyamANe kAraNasyApyayo yuktaH, kAraNApyaye kAryasyAvasthAnAnupapatteH | kAryApyaye tu kAraNasyAvasthAnaM yuktam -- mR^idAdiShvevaM dR^iShTatvAt ||14||

 -- o)0(o -- 

antarAvij~nAnAdhikaraNam 

|| 2.3.15 ||

antarA vij~nAnamanasI krameNa talliN^gAd iti cen nAvisheShAt |

 
bhUtAnAm utpattipralayAvanulomapratilomakramAbhyAM bhavata ityuktam | AtmAdir utpattiH pralayashcAtmAntaH -- ityapyuktam | sendriyasya tu manaso buddhishca sadbhAvaH prasiddhaH shrutismR^ityoH -- 

buddhiM tu sArathiM viddhi manaH pragraham eva ca | 
indriyANi hayAn AhuH ityAdiliN^gebhyaH | 

tayor api kasmiMshcid antarAle krameNotpattipralayAv upasaMgrAhyau, sarvasya vastujAtasya brahmajatvAbhyupagamAt | api ca AtharvaNe utpattiprakaraNe bhUtAnAm AtmanashcAntarAle karaNAnyanukramyante -- 

etasmAjjAyate prANo manaH sarvendriyANi ca | 
khaM vAyur jyotir ApaH pR^ithivI vishvasya dhAriNI || [mu.u. 2.1.3] iti |

tasmAt pUrvoktotpattipralayakramabhaN^gaprasaN^go bhUtAnAm iti cet, na | avisheShAt -- yadi tAvad bhautikAni karaNAni, tato bhUtotpattipralayAbhyAm evaiShAm utpattipralayau bhavata iti naitayoH kramAntaraM mR^igyam | bhavati ca bhautikatve liN^gaM karaNAnAm -- annamayaM hi somya mana ApomayaH prANaH tejomayI vAk [chA.u. 6.6.6] ityevaMjAtIyakam | vyapadesho.api kvacid bhUtAnAM karaNAnAM ca brAhmaNaparivrAjakanyAyena netavyaH | atha tu abhautikAni karaNAni, tathApi bhUtotpattikramo na karaNair vishiShyate -- prathamaM karaNAnyutpadyante caramaM bhUtAni, prathamaM vA bhUtAnyutpadyante caramaM karaNAnIti | AtharvaNe tu samAmnAyakramamAtraM karaNAnAM bhUtAnAM ca, na tatrotpattikrama ucyate | tathA anyatrApi pR^ithag eva bhUtakramAt karaNakrama AmnAyate -- prajApatir vA idam agra AsIt sa AtmAnam aikShata sa mano.asR^ijata tan mana evAsIt tad AtmAnam aikShata tad vAcam asR^ijata ityAdinA | tasmAn nAsti bhUtotpattikramasya bhaN^gaH ||15||

 -- o)0(o -- 
carAcaravyapAshrayAdhikaraNam

|| 2.3.16 ||

carAcaravyapAshrayaH tu syAt tadvyapadesho.abhAktaH tadbhAvabhAvitatvAt ||

#sto jIvasyApyutpattipralayau, jAto devadatto mR^ito devadatta ityevaMjAtIyakAl laukikavyapadeshAt jAtakarmAdisaMskAravidhAnAcca -- iti syAt kasyacid bhrAntiH | tAm apanudAmaH | na jIvasyotpattipralayau staH, shAstraphalasambandhopapatteH | sharIrAnuvinAshini hi jIve sharIrAntaragateShTAniShTaprAptiparihArArthau vidhipratiShedhAvanarthakau syAtAm | shrUyate ca -- jIvApetaM vAva kiledaM mriyate na jIvo mriyate iti | 

nanu laukiko janmamaraNavyapadesho jIvasya darshitaH | satyaM darshitaH | bhAktaH tv eSha jIvasya janmamaraNavyapadeshaH | kim AshrayaH punar ayaM mukhyaH, yadapekShayA bhAkta iti? ucyate -- carAcaravyapAshrayaH | sthAvarajaN^gamasharIraviShayau janmamaraNashabdau | sthAvarajaN^gamAni hi bhUtAni jAyante ca mriyante ca | ataH tadviShayau janmamaraNashabdau mukhyau santau tatsthe jIvAtmanyupacaryete, tadbhAvabhAvitvAt |

sharIraprAdurbhAvatirobhAvayor hi sator janmamaraNashabdau bhavataH, nAsatoH | na hi sharIrasambandhAd anyatra jIvo jAto mR^ito vA kenacil lakShyate | sa vA ayaM puruSho jAyamAnaH sharIram abhisampadyamAnaH sa utkrAman mriyamANaH iti ca sharIrasaMyogaviyoganimittAv eva janmamaraNashabdau darshayati | jAtakarmAdividhAnam api dehaprAdurbhAvApekSham eva draShTavyam, abhAvAjjIvaprAdurbhAvasya | jIvasya parasmAd Atmana utpattir viyadAdInAm ivAsti nAsti vetyetad uttareNa sUtreNa vakShyati | dehAshrayau tAvajjIvasya sthUlAv utpattipralayau na staH ityetad anena sUtreNAvocat ||16||

11. AtmAdhikaraNam

|| 2.3.17 ||

nAtmAshruter nityatvAcca tAbhyaH ||

astyAtmA jIvAkhyaH sharIrendriyapaJNjarAdhyakShaH karmaphalasambandhI | sa kiM vyomAdivad utpadyate brahmaNaH, Aho svid brahmavad eva notpadyate, iti shrutivipratipatter viShayaH | kAsucicchrutiShu agnivisphuliN^gAdinidarshanair jIvAtmanaH parasmAd brahmaNa utpattir AmnAyate | kAsucittu avikR^itasyaiva parasya brahmaNaH kAryapraveshena jIvabhAvo vij~nAyate, na ca utpattir AmnAyata iti | tatra prAptaM tAvat -- utpadyate jIva iti | kutaH? pratij~nAnuparodhAd eva | ekasmin vidite sarvam idaM viditam itIyaM pratij~nA sarvasya vastujAtasya brahmaprabhavatve sati noparudhyeta, tattvAntaratve tu jIvasya pratij~neyam uparudhyeta | na ca avikR^itaH paramAtmaiva jIva iti shakyate vij~nAtum, lakShaNabhedAt -- apahatapApmatvAdidharmako hi paramAtmA, tadviparIto hi jIvaH | vibhAgAccAsya vikAratvasiddhiH -- yAvAn hi AkAshAdiH pravibhaktaH, sa sarvo vikAraH | tasya ca AkAshAderutpattiH samadhigatA | jIvAtmApi puNyApuNyakarmA sukhaduHkhayuk pratisharIraM pravibhakta iti, tasyApi prapaJNcotpattyavasare utpattir bhavitum arhati | api ca yathAgneH kShudrA visphuliN^gA vyuccarantyevam evAsmAdAtmanaH sarve prANAH iti prANAder bhogyajAtasya sR^iShTiM shiShTavA sarva eta AtmAno vyuccaranti iti bhoktNAm AtmanAM pR^ithaksR^iShTiM shAsti | yathA sudIptAt pAvakAdvisphuliN^gAH sahasrashaH prabhavante sarUpAH | tathAkSharAd vividhAH somya bhAvAH prajAyante tatra caivApi yanti iti ca jIvAtmanAm utpattipralayAv ucyete, sarUpavacanAt -- jIvAtmAno hi paramAtmanA sarUpA bhavanti, caitanyayogAt | na ca kvacid ashravaNam anyatra shrutaM vArayitum arhati, shrutyantaragatasyApyaviruddhasyAdhikasyArthasya sarvatropasaMhartavyatvAt | praveshashrutir apyevaM sati vikArabhAvApattyaiva vyAkhyAtavyA -- tad AtmAnaM svayam akuruta ityAdivat | tasmAd utpadyate jIva iti || 

evaM prApte, brUmaH -- nAtmA jIva utpadyata iti | kasmAt? ashruteH | na hyasyotpattiprakaraNe shravaNam asti bhUyaHsu pradesheShu | 

nanu kvacid ashravaNam anyatra shrutaM na vArayatItyuktam | satyam uktam | utpattir eva tu asya na sambhavatIti vadAmaH | kasmAt? nityatvAcca tAbhyaH -- cashabdAd ajatvAdibhyashca -- nityatvaM hyasya shrutibhyo.avagamyate, tathA ajatvam avikAritvam avikR^itasyaiva brahmaNo jIvAtmanAvasthAnaM brahmAtmanA ceti | na caivaMrUpasyotpattir upapadyate | tAH kAH shrutayaH? -- na jIvo mriyate sa vA eSha mahAn aja AtmAjaro.amaro.amR^ito.abhayo brahma [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.25], na jAyate mriyate vA vipashcit ajo nityaH shAshvato.ayaM purANaH [ka.u. 1.2.18], tat sR^iShTvA tad evAnuprAvishat anena jIvenAtmanAnupravishya nAmarUpe vyAkaravANi sa eSha iha praviShTA A nakhAgrebhyaH tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7], ahaM brahmAsmi [bR^i.A.u. 1.4.10], ayam AtmA brahma sarvAnubhUH [bR^i.A.u. 2.5.19] ityevamAdyA nityatvavAdinyaH satyaH jIvasyotpattiM pratibadhnanti | 

nanu pravibhaktatvAd vikAraH, vikAratvAccotpadyate -- ityuktam | atrocyate -- nAsya pravibhAgaH svato.asti, 

eko devaH sarvabhUteShu gUDhaH 
sarvavyApI sarvabhUtAntarAtmA [shve.u. 6.11] iti shruteH | 

buddhyAdyupAdhinimittaM tu asya pravibhAgapratibhAnam, AkAshasyeva ghaTAdisambandhanimittam | tathA ca shAstram -- sa vA ayam AtmA brahma vij~nAnamayo manomayaH prANamayashcakShurmayaH shrotramayaH ityevamAdi -- brahmaNa evAvikR^itasya sato.asyaikasyAnekabuddhyAdimayatvaM darshayati | tanmayatvaM ca asya tadviviktasvarUpAnabhivyaktyA taduparaktasvarUpatvam -- strImayo jAlma ityAdivad draShTavyam | yad api kvacid asyotpattipralayashravaNam, tad apyata evopAdhisambandhAn netavyam -- upAdhyutpattyA asyotpattiH, tatpralayena ca pralaya iti | tathA ca darshayati -- praj~nAnaghana evaitebhyo bhUtebhyaH samutthAya tAnyevAnu vinashyati na pretya saMj~nAsti iti | tathopAdhipralaya evAyam, nAtmavilayaH -- ityetad api -- atraiva mA bhagavAn mohAntam ApIpadan na vA aham imaM vijAnAmi -- na pretya saMj~nAsti -- iti prashnapUrvakaM pratipAdayati -- na vA are.ahaM mohaM bravImyavinAshI vA are.ayam AtmAnucchittidharmA -- mAtrAsaMsargaH tu asya bhavati -- iti | pratij~nAnuparodho.apyavikR^itasyaiva brahmaNo jIvabhAvAbhyupagamAt | lakShaNabhedo.apyanayor upAdhinimitta eva, ata UrdhvaM vimokShAyaiva brUhi iti ca prakR^itasyaiva vij~nAnamayasyAtmanaH sarvasaMsAradharmapratyAkhyAnena paramAtmabhAvapratipAdanAt | tasmAt naivAtmotpadyate pravilIyate ceti ||17||


j~nAdhikaraNam 

|| 2.3.18 ||

sa kiM kANabhujAnAm ivAgantukacaitanyaH, svato.acetanaH, Aho svit sAN^khyAnAm iva nityacaitanyasvarUpa eva, iti vAdivipratipatteH saMshayaH | kiM tAvat prAptam? Agantukam Atmanashcaitanyam AtmamanaHsaMyogajam, agnighaTasaMyogajarohitAdiguNavad iti prAptam | nityacaitanyatve hi suptamUrcchitagrahAviShTAnAm api caitanyaM syAt | te pR^iShTAH santaH na kiJNcid vayaM cetayemahi iti jalpanti | svasthAshca cetayamAnA dR^ishyante | ataH kAdAcitkacaitanyatvAd Agantukacaitanya Atmeti || 

evaM prApte, abhidhIyate -- 

j~no.ata eva ||

j~no nityacaitanyo.ayam AtmA | ata eva yasmAd eva notpadyate, param eva brahma avikR^itam upAdhisamparkAjjIvabhAvenAvatiShThate | parasya hi brahmaNashcaitanyasvarUpatvam AmnAtam --  vij~nAnam AnandaM brahma [bR^i.A.u. 3.9.7], satyaM j~nAnam anantaM brahma [tai.u. 2.1.1], anantaro.abAhyaH kR^itsnaH praj~nAnaghana eva ityAdiShu shrutiShu | tad eva cet paraM brahma jIvaH, tasmAjjIvasyApi nityacaitanyasvarUpatvam agnyauShNyaprakAshavad iti gamyate | vij~nAnamayaprakriyAyAM ca shrutayo bhavanti -- asuptaH suptAn abhicAkashIti atrAyaM puruShaH svayaMjyotir bhavati iti, na hi vij~nAtur vij~nAter viparilopo vidyate [bR^i.A.u. 4.3.30] ityevaMrUpAH | atha yo vededaM jighrANIti sa AtmA iti ca -- sarvaiH karaNadvAraiH idaM veda, idaM veda iti vij~nAnenAnusandhAnAt tadrUpatvasiddhiH | nityacaitanyasvarUpatve ghrANAdyAnarthakyam iti cet, na, gandhAdiviShayavisheShaparicchedArthatvAt | tathA hi darshayati -- gandhAya ghrANam ityAdi | yat tu suptAdayo na cetayanta iti, tasya shrutyaiva parihAro.abhihitaH suShuptaM prakR^itya -- yad vai tan na pashyati pashyan vai tan na pashyati | na hi draShTur dR^iShTer viparilopo vidyate.avinAshitvAt | na tu tad dvitIyam asti tato.anyad vibhaktaM yat pashyet [bR^i.A.u. 4.3.23] ityAdinA | etad uktaM bhavati -- viShayAbhAvAd iyam acetayamAnatA, na caitanyAbhAvAd iti -- yathA viyad Ashrayasya prakAshasya prakAshyAbhAvAd anabhivyaktiH, na svarUpAbhAvAt, tadvat | vaisheShikAditarkashca shrutivirodha AbhAsI bhavati | tasmAn nityacaitanyasvarUpa eva Atmeti nishcinumaH ||18||

  -- o)0(o -- 
utkrAntigatyadhikaraNam

|| 2.3.19 || 

utkrAntigatyAgatInAm || 

idAnIM tu kimparimANo jIva iti cintyate -- kim aNuparimANaH, uta madhyamaparimANaH, Aho svit mahAparimANa iti | 

nanu ca nAtmotpadyate nityacaitanyashcAyam ityuktam | atashca para eva AtmA jIva ityApatati | parasya ca Atmano.anantatvam AmnAtam | tatra kuto jIvasya parimANacintAvatAra iti | ucyate -- satyam etat | utkrAntigatyAgatishravaNAni tu jIvasya paricchedaM prApayanti | svashabdena ca asya kvacid aNuparimANatvam AmnAyate | tasya sarvasya anAkulatvopapAdanAya ayam ArambhaH | tatra prAptaM tAvat -- utkrAntigatyAgatInAM shravaNAt paricchinno.aNuparimANo jIva iti | utkrAntiH tAvat -- sa yadAsmAccharIrAd utkrAmati sahaivaitaiH sarvair utkrAmati iti | gatir api -- ye vai ke cAsmAl lokAt prayanti candramasam eva te sarve gacchanti iti | Agatir api -- tasmAl lokAt punar aityasmai lokAya karmaNe iti | AsAm utkrAntigatyAgatInAM shravaNAt paricchinnaH tAvajjIva iti prApnoti -- na hi vibhoshcalanam avakalpata iti | sati paricchede, sharIraparimANatvasyArhataparIkShAyAM nirastatvAt aNur Atmeti gamyate ||19||

|| 2.3.20 || 

svAtmanA cottarayoH || 

utkrAntiH kadAcid acalato.api grAmasvAmyanivR^ittivad dehasvAmyanivR^ittyA karmakShayeNAvakalpeta | uttare tu gatyAgatI nAcalataH sambhavataH | svAtmanA hi tayoH sambandho bhavati, gameH kartR^isthakriyAtvAt | amadhyamaparimANasya ca gatyAgatI aNutve eva sambhavataH | satyoshca gatyAgatyor utkrAntir apyapasR^iptir eva dehAd iti pratIyate | na hi anapasR^iptasya dehAd gatyAgatI syAtAm -- dehapradeshAnAM ca utkrAntAvapAdAnatvavacanAt -- cakShuShTo vA mUrdhno vAnyebhyo vA sharIradeshebhyaH iti | sa etAH tejomAtrAH samabhyAdadAno hR^idayam evAnvavakrAmati shukram AdAya punar aiti sthAnam iti cAntare.api sharIre shArIrasya gatyAgatI bhavataH | tasmAd apyasyANutvasiddhiH ||20||

|| 2.3.21 ||

nANur atacchruteH iti cen netarAdhikArAt ||

athApi syAt --  nANur ayam AtmA | kasmAt? atacchruteH | aNutvaviparItaparimANashravaNAd ityarthaH | sa vA eSha mahAn aja AtmA, yo.ayaM vij~nAnamayaH prANeShu [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.22], AkAshavat sarvagatashca nityaH, satyaM j~nAnam anantaM brahma [tai.u. 2.1.1] ityevaMjAtIyakA hi shrutir Atmano.aNutve vipratiShidhyeteti cet, naiSha doShaH | kasmAt? itarAdhikArAt -- parasya hi AtmanaH prakriyAyAm eShA parimANAntarashrutiH, parasyaivAtmanaH prAdhAnyena vedAnteShu veditavyatvena prakR^itatvAt, virajaH para AkAshAt ityevaMvidhAcca parasyaivAtmanaH tatra tatra visheShAdhikArAt | 

nanu yo.ayaM vij~nAnamayaH prANeShu [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.22] iti shArIra eva mahattvasambandhitvena pratinirdishyate --  shAstradR^iShTyA tu eSha nirdesho vAmadevavad draShTavyaH | tasmAt prAj~naviShayatvAt parimANAntarashravaNasya na jIvasyANutvaM virudhyate ||21||

|| 2.3.22 ||

svashabdonmAnAbhyAM ca ||

itashcANur AtmA, yataH sAkShAd evAsyANutvavAcI shabdaH shrUyate -- eSho.aNur AtmA cetasA veditavyo yasmin prANaH paJNcadhA saMvivesha [mu.u. 3.1.9] iti | prANasambandhAcca jIva evAyam aNur abhihita iti gamyate | tathonmAnam api jIvasyANimAnaM gamayati -- bAlAgrashatabhAgasya shatadhA kalpitasya ca | bhAgo jIvaH sa vij~neyaH [shve.u. 5.9] iti | ArAgramAtro hyavaro.api dR^iShTAH iti ca unmAnAntaram ||22|| 

|| 2.3.23 ||

nanvaNutve sati ekadeshasthasya sakaladehagatopalabdhir virudhyate | dR^ishyate ca jAhnavIhradanimagnAnAM sarvAN^gashaityopalabdhiH, nidAghasamaye ca sakalasharIraparitApopalabdhiH iti | ata uttaraM paThati -- 

avirodhashcandanavat ||

yathA hi haricandanabinduH sharIraikadeshasambaddho.api san sakaladehavyApinam AhlAdaM karoti, evam AtmApi dehaikadeshasthaH sakaladehavyApinIm upalabdhiM kariShyati | tvaksambandhAccAsya sakalasharIragatA vedanA na virudhyate | tu agAtmanor hi sambandhaH kR^itsnAyAM tu aci vartate | tvak ca kR^itsnasharIravyApinIti ||23|| 

|| 2.3.24 ||

avasthitivaisheShyAd iti cen nAbhyupagamAt hR^idi hi ||

atrAha -- yad uktam avirodhashcandanavad iti, tad ayuktam, dR^iShTAntadArShTAntikayor atulyatvAt | siddho hi Atmano dehaikadeshasthatve candanadR^iShTAnto bhavati, pratyakShaM tu candanasyAvasthitivaisheShyam ekadeshasthatvaM sakaladehAhlAdanaM ca | AtmanaH punaH sakaladehopalabdhimAtraM pratyakSham, naikadeshavartitvam | anumeyaM tu tad iti yad apyucyeta -- na ca atrAnumAnaM sambhavati -- kim AtmanaH sakalasharIragatA vedanA tu agindriyasyeva sakaladehavyApinaH sataH, kiM vA vibhor nabhasa iva, Aho sviccandanabindoH ivANor ekadeshasthasya iti saMshayAnativR^itteH iti | 

atrocyate -- nAyaM doShaH | kasmAt? abhyupagamAt | abhyupagamyate hi Atmano.api candanasyeva dehaikadeshavR^ittitvam avasthitivaisheShyam | katham iti, ucyate -- hR^idi hyeSha AtmA paThyate vedAnteShu, hR^idi hyeSha AtmA [pra.u. 3.6], sa vA eSha AtmA hR^idi katama Atmeti yo.ayaM vij~nAnamayaH prANeShu hR^idyantarjyotiH puruShaH [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.22] ityAdyupadeshebhyaH | tasmAd dR^iShTAntadArShTAntikayor avaiShamyAt yuktam evaitat -- avirodhashcandanavat iti ||24||

|| 2.3.25 ||

guNAd vA Alokavat ||

caitanyaguNavyApter vA aNor api sato jIvasya sakaladehavyApi kAryaM na virudhyate -- yathA loke maNipradIpaprabhR^itInAm apavarakaikadeshavartinAm api prabhA apavarakavyApinI satI kR^itsne.apavarake kAryaM karoti, tadvat | syAt kadAciccandanasya sAvayavatvAt sUkShmAvayavavisarpaNenApi sakaladeha AhlAdayitR^itvam | na tu aNor jIvasyAvayavAH santi, yair ayaM sakaladehaM visarpet -- ityAshaN^kya guNAd vA lokavat ityuktam ||25|| 

|| 2.3.26 || 

kathaM punar guNo guNivyatirekeNAnyatra varteta? na hi paTasya shuklo guNaH paTavyatirekeNAnyatra vartamAno dR^ishyate | pradIpaprabhAvad bhaved iti cet, na | tasyA api dravyatvAbhyupagamAt -- niviDAvayavaM hi tejodravyaM pradIpaH, praviralAvayavaM tu tejodravyam eva prabhA iti, ata uttaraM paThati -- 

vyatireko gandhavat ||

yathA guNasyApi sato gandhasya gandhavaddravyavyatirekeNa vR^ittir bhavati, aprApteShvapi kusumAdiShu gandhavatsu kusumagandhopalabdheH | evam aNor api sato jIvasya caitanyaguNavyatireko bhaviShyati | atashcAnaikAntikam etat -- guNatvAd rUpAdivad AshrayavishleShAnupapattiH iti, guNasyaiva sato gandhasya AshrayavishleShadarshanAt | gandhasyApi sahaivAshrayeNa vishleSha iti cet, na | yasmAn mUladravyAd vishleShaH tasya kShayaprasaN^gAt | akShIyamANam api tatpUrvAvasthAto gamyate | anyathA tatpUrvAvasthair gurutvAdibhir hIyeta | syAd etat -- gandhAshrayANAM vishliShTAnAm avayavAnAm alpatvAt sann api vishleSho nopalakShyate | sUkShmA hi gandhaparamANavaH sarvato viprasR^itA gandhabuddhim utpAdayanti nAsikApuTam anupravishanta iti cet, na | atIndriyatvAt paramANUnAm, sphuTagandhopalabdheshca nAgakesarAdiShu | na ca loke pratItiH -- gandhavad dravyam AghrAtam iti | gandha eva AghrAta iti tu laukikAH pratiyanti | rUpAdiShvashrayavyatirekAnupalabdher gandhasyApyayukta Ashrayavyatireka iti cet, na | pratyakShatvAd anumAnApravR^itteH | tasmAt yat yathA loke dR^iShTam, tat tathaiva anumantavyaM nirUpakaiH, nAnyathA | na hi raso guNo jihvayopalabhyata ityato rUpAdayo.api guNA jihvayaivopalabhyerann iti niyantuM shakyate ||26||

|| 2.3.27 ||

tathA ca darshayati || 

hR^idayAyatanatvam aNuparimANatvaM ca Atmano.abhidhAya tasyaiva A lomabhya A nakhAgrebhyaH iti caitanyena guNena samastasharIravyApitvaM darshayati ||27|| 

|| 2.3.28 || 

pR^ithagupadeshAt || 

praj~nayA sharIraM samAruhya iti ca Atmapraj~nayoH kartR^ikaraNabhAvena pR^ithagupadeshAt caitanyaguNenaiva asya sharIravyApitA gamyate | tad eShAM prANAnAM vij~nAnena vij~nAnam AdAya iti ca kartuH shArIrAt pR^ithagvij~nAnasyopadeshaH etam evAbhiprAyam upodbalayati | tasmAd aNur Atmeti ||28|| 

|| 2.3.29 ||

evaM prApte, brUmaH -- 

tadguNasAratvAt tu tadvyapadeshaH prAj~navat ||

tushabdaH pakShaM vyAvartayati | naitad asti -- aNur Atmeti | utpattyashravaNAt parasyaiva tu brahmaNaH praveshashravaNAt tAdAtmyopadeshAcca param eva brahma jIva ityuktam | param eva ced brahma jIvaH, tasmAd yAvat paraM brahma tAvAn eva jIvo bhavitum arhati | parasya ca brahmaNo vibhutvam AmnAtam | tasmAd vibhur jIvaH | tathA ca sa vA eSha mahAn aja AtmA yo.ayaM vij~nAnamayaH prANeShu [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.22] ityevaMjAtIyakA jIvaviShayA vibhutvavAdAH shrautAH smArtAshca samarthitA bhavanti | na ca aNor jIvasya sakalasharIragatA vedanopapadyate | tvaksambandhAt syAd iti cet, na | kaNTakatodane.api sakalasharIragataiva vedanA prasajyeta -- tvakkaNTakayor hi saMyogaH kR^itsnAyAM tvaci vartate -- tvak ca kR^itsnasharIravyApinIti | pAdatala eva tu kaNTakanunno vedanAM pratilabhate | na ca aNor guNavyAptir upapadyate, guNasya guNideshatvAt | guNatvam eva hi guNinam anAshritya guNasya hIyeta | pradIpaprabhAyAshca dravyAntaratvaM vyAkhyAtam | gandho.api guNatvAbhyupagamAt sAshraya eva saMcaritum arhati, anyathA guNatvahAniprasaN^gAt | tathA coktaM bhagavatA dvaipAyanena -- 

upalabhyApsu ced gandhaM kecid brUyur anaipuNAH | 
pR^ithivyAm eva taM vidyAd apo vAyuM ca saMshritam || iti | 

yadi ca caitanyaM jIvasya samastasharIraM vyApnuyAt, nANur jIvaH syAt | caitanyam eva hi asya svarUpam, agneH ivauShNyaprakAshau -- nAtra guNaguNivibhAgo vidyata iti | sharIraparimANatvaM ca pratyAkhyAtam | parisheShAd vibhur jIvaH || 

kathaM tarhi aNutvAdivyapadesha ityata Aha -- tadguNasAratvAt tu tadvyapadesha iti | tasyA buddhiH guNAH tadguNAH -- icchA dveShaH sukhaM duHkham ityevamAdayaH -- tadguNAH sAraH pradhAnaM yasyAtmanaH saMsAritve sambhavati, sa tadguNasAraH, tasya bhAvaH tadguNasAratvam | na hi buddhir guNair vinA kevalasya AtmanaH saMsAritvam asti | buddhyupAdhidharmAdhyAsanimittaM hi kartR^itvabhoktR^itvAdilakShaNaM saMsAritvam akartur abhoktushcAsaMsAriNo nityamuktasya sata AtmanaH | tasmAt tadguNasAratvAd buddhiparimANenAsya parimANavyapadeshaH, tadutkrAntyAdibhishca asyotkrAntyAdivyapadeshaH, na svataH | tathA ca -- 

bAlAgrashatabhAgasya shatadhA kalpitasya ca | 
bhAgo jIvaH sa vij~neyaH sa cAnantyAya kalpate || [shve.u. 5.9] 

ityaNutvaM jIvasyoktvA tasyaiva punar Anantyam Aha | taccaivam eva samaJNjasaM syAt -- yadyaupacArikam aNutvaM jIvasya bhavet, pAramArthikaM ca Anantyam | na hi ubhayaM mukhyam avakalpeta | na ca Anantyam aupacArikam iti shakyaM vij~nAtum, sarvopaniShatsu brahmAtmabhAvasya pratipipAdayiShitatvAt | tathetarasminn apyunmAne buddhir guNenAtmaguNena caiva ArAgramAtro hyavaro.api dR^iShTaH iti ca buddhiguNasambandhenaiva ArAgramAtratAM shAsti, na svenaivAtmanA | eSho.aNur AtmA cetasA veditavyaH [mu.u. 3.1.9] ityatrApi na jIvasya aNuparimANatvaM shiShyate, parasyaivAtmanashcakShurAdyanavagrAhyatvena j~nAnaprasAdagamyatvena ca prakR^itatvAt, jIvasyApi ca mukhyANuparimANatvAnupapatteH | tasmAd dur j~nAnatvAbhiprAyam idam aNutvavacanam, upAdhyabhiprAyaM vA draShTavyam | tathA praj~nayA sharIraM samAruhya ityevaMjAtIyakeShvapi bhedopadesheShu -- buddhyaivopAdhibhUtayA jIvaH sharIraM samAruhya -- ityevaM yojayitavyam, vyapadeshamAtraM vA -- shilAputrakasya sharIram ityAdivat | na hyatra guNaguNivibhAgo.api vidyata ityuktam | hR^idayAyatanatvavacanam api buddher eva tadAyatanatvAt | tathA utkrAntyAdInAm apyupAdhyAyattatAM darshayati -- kasmin nu aham utkrAnta utkrAnto bhaviShyAmi ? kasmin vA pratiShThite pratiShThAsyAmIti sa prANam asR^ijata iti | utkrAntyabhAve hi gatyAgatyor apyabhAvo vij~nAyate | na hi anapasR^iptasya dehAd gatyAgatI syAtAm | evam upAdhiguNasAratvAjjIvasyANutvAdivyapadeshaH, prAj~navat | yathA prAj~nasya paramAtmanaH saguNeShUpAsaneShu upAdhiguNasAratvAd aNIyastvAdivyapadeshaH -- aNIyAn vrIher vA yavAd vA manomayaH 
prANamayaH prANasharIraH sarvagandhaH sarvarasaH satyakAmaH satyasaN^kalpaH ityevamprakAraH, tadvat ||29|| 

|| 2.3.30 ||

syAd etat -- yadi buddhiguNasAratvAd AtmanaH saMsAritvaM kalpyeta, tato buddhyAtmanor bhinnayoH saMyogAvasAnam avashyambhAvItyato buddhiviyoge sati Atmano vibhaktasyAnAlakShyatvAd asattvam asaMsAritvaM vA prasajyeteti -- ata uttaraM paThati -- 

yAvad AtmabhAvitvAcca na doShaH taddarshanAt || 

neyam anantaranirdiShTadoShaprAptir AshaN^kanIyA | kasmAt? yAvadAtmabhAvitvAd buddhisaMyogasya -- yAvad ayam AtmA saMsArI bhavati, yAvad asya samyagdarshanena saMsAritvaM na nivartate, tAvad asya buddhyA saMyogo na shAmyati | yAvad eva cAyaM buddhyupAdhisambandhaH, tAvad evAsya jIvatvaM saMsAritvaM ca | paramArthataH tu na jIvo nAma buddhyupAdhiparikalpitasvarUpavyatirekeNAsti | na hi nityamuktasvarUpAt sarvaj~nAdIshvarAd anyashcetano dhAtur dvitIyo vedAntArthanirUpaNAyAm upalabhyate -- nAnyo.ato.asti draShTA shrotA mantA vij~nAtA nAnyad ato.asti draShTR^i shrotR^i mantR^i vij~nAtR^i tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7], ahaM brahmAsmi [bR^i.A.u. 1.4.10] ityAdi shrutishatebhyaH | 

kathaM punar avagamyate yAvad AtmabhAvI buddhisaMyoga iti ? taddarshanAd ityAha | tathA hi shAstraM darshayati -- yo.ayaM vij~nAnamayaH prANeShu hR^idyantarjyotiH puruShaH sa samAnaH sann ubhau lokAvanusaMcarati dhyAyatIva lelAyatIva [bR^i.A.u. 4.3.7] ityAdi | tatra vij~nAnamaya iti buddhimaya ityetad uktaM bhavati, pradeshAntare vij~nAnamayo manomayaH prANamayashcakShurmayaH shrotramayaH iti vij~nAnamayasya manaAdibhiH sahapAThAt | buddhimayatvaM ca tadguNasAratvam evAbhipreyate -- yathA loke strImayo devadatta iti strIrAgAdipradhAno.abhidhIyate, tadvat | sa samAnaH sann ubhau lokAvanusaMcarati iti ca lokAntaragamane.apyaviyogaM buddhyA darshayati | kena samAnaH? tayaiva buddhyeti gamyate, saMnidhAnAt | tacca darshayati -- dhyAyatIva lelAyatIva iti | 

etad uktaM bhavati -- nAyaM svato dhyAyati, nApi calati, dhyAyantyAM buddhau dhyAyatIva, calantyAM buddhau calatIveti | api ca mithyAj~nAnapuraHsaro.ayam Atmano buddhyupAdhisambandhaH | na ca mithyAj~nAnasya samyagj~nAnAd anyatra nivR^ittir astItyato yAvad brahmAtmatAnavabodhaH, tAvad ayaM buddhyupAdhisambandho na shAmyati | darshayati ca -- 

vedAham etaM puruShaM mahAntam 
AdityavarNaM tamasaH parastAt | 
tam eva viditvAtimR^ityum eti 
nAnyaH panthA vidyate.ayanAya || [shve.u. 3.8] iti || 


|| 2.3.31 ||

nanu suShuptapralayayor na shakyate buddhisambandha Atmano.abhyupagantum, satA somya tadA sampanno bhavati svam apIto bhavati iti vacanAt, kR^itsnavikArapralayAbhyupagamAcca | tat kathaM yAvadAtmabhAvitvaM buddhisambandhasyeti, atrocyate -- 

puMstvAdivat tu asya sato.abhivyaktiyogAt || 

yathA loke puMstvAdIni bIjAtmanA vidyamAnAnyeva bAlyAdiShvanupalabhyamAnAnyavidyamAnavad abhipreyamANAni yauvanAdiShvavirbhavanti | na avidyamAnAnyutpadyante, ShaNDAdInAm api tadutpattiprasaN^gAt -- evam ayam api buddhisambandhaH shaktyAtmanA vidyamAna eva suShuptapralayayoH punaH prabodhaprasavayor Avirbhavati | evaM hi etad yujyate | na hi AkasmikI kasyacid utpattiH sambhavati, atiprasaN^gAt | darshayati ca suShuptAd utthAnam avidyAtmakabIjasadbhAvakAritam -- sati sampadya na viduH sati sampadyAmaha iti ta iha vyAghro vA diMho vA ityAdinA | tasmAt siddham etat -- yAvadAtmabhAvI buddhyAdyupAdhisambandha iti ||3||

|| 2.3.32 ||

nityopalabdhyanupalabdhiprasaN^go.anyataraniyamo vA.anyathA || 

taccAtmana upAdhibhUtam -- antaHkaraNaM mano buddhir vij~nAnaM cittam iti ca anekadhA tatra tatrAbhilapyate | kvacicca vR^ittivibhAgena -- saMshayAdivR^ittikaM mana ityucyate, nishcayAdivR^ittikaM buddhiH iti | taccaivaM bhUtam antaHkaraNam avashyam astItyabhyupagantavyam, anyathA hyanabhyupagamyamAne tasmin nityopalabdhyanupalabdhiprasaN^gaH syAt | AtmendriyaviShayANAm upalabdhisAdhanAnAM saMnidhAne sati nityam evopalabdhiH prasajyeta | 

atha satyapi hetusamavadhAne phalAbhAvaH, tato nityam evAnupalabdhiH prasajyeta | na caivaM dR^ishyate | athavA anyatarasyAtmana indriyasya vA shaktipratibandho.abhyupagantavyaH | na ca AtmanaH shaktipratibandhaH sambhavati, avikriyatvAt | nApi indriyasya | na hi tasya pUrvottarayoH kShaNayor apratibaddhashaktikasya sato.akasmAcchaktiH pratibadhyeta | tasmAt yasyAvadhAnAnavadhAnAbhyAm upalabdhyanupalabdhI bhavataH, tan manaH | tathA ca shrutiH -- anyatra manA abhUvaM nAdarsham anyatra manA abhUvaM nAshrauSham iti, manasA hyeva pashyati manasA sR^iNoti iti ca | 

kAmAdayashcAsya vR^ittaya iti darshayati -- kAmaH saN^kalpo vicikitsA shraddhAshraddhA dhR^itir adhR^itir hrIr dhIr bhIH ityetat sarvaM mana eva iti | tasmAd yuktam etat -- tadguNasAratvAt tadvyapadesha iti ||

5. kartradhikaraNam 

|| 2.3.33 || 

kartA shAstrArthavattvAt || 

tadguNasAratvAd hikAreNaivAparo.api jIvadharmaH prapaJNcyate | kartA ca ayaM jIvaH syAt | kasmAt? shAstrArthavattvAt  -- evaM ca yajeta juhuyAt dadyAt ityevaMvidhaM vidhishAstram arthavad bhavati | anyathA tadanarthakaM syAt | tad dhi kartuH sataH kartavyavisheSham upadishati | na ca asati kartR^itve tad upapadyeta | tathedam api shAstram arthavad bhavati -- eSha hi draShTA shrotA mantA boddhA kartA vij~nAnAtmA puruShaH [pra.u. 4.9] iti ||

|| 2.3.34 || 

vihAropadeshAt ||

itashca jIvasya kartR^itvam, yajjIvaprakriyAyAM sandhye sthAne vihAram upadishati -- sa Iyate.amR^ito yatra kAmam iti, sve sharIre yathAkAmaM parivartate iti ca ||34||

upAdAnAt || 2.3.35 || 

 || 2.3.35 || 

itashcAsya kartR^itvam, yajjIvaprakriyAyAm eva karaNAnAm upAdAnaM saN^kIrtayati -- tadeShAM prANAnAM vij~nAnena vij~nAnamAdAya iti, prANAngR^ihItvA iti ca ||

vyapadeshAcca kriyAyAM na cennirdeshaviparyayaH || 2.3.36 || 

 || 2.3.36 || 

itashca jIvasya kartR^itvam, yadasya laukikIShu vaidikIShu ca kriyAsu kartR^itvaM vyapadishati shAstram -- vij~nAnaM yaj~naM tanute karmANi tanute.api ca iti | 

nanu vij~nAnashabdo buddhau samadhigataH, katham anena jIvasya kartR^itvaM sUcyata iti, netyucyate -- jIvasyaivaiSha nirdeshaH, na buddhiH | na cejjIvasya syAt, nirdeshaviparyayaH syAt -- vij~nAnenetyevaM niradekShyat | tathA hi anyatra buddhivivakShAyAM vij~nAnashabdasya karaNavibhaktinirdesho dR^ishyate -- tadeShAM prANAnAM vij~nAnena vij~nAnamAdAya iti | iha tu vij~nAnaM yaj~naM tanute iti kartR^isAmAnAdhikaraNyanirdeshAdbuddhivyatiriktasyaivAtmanaH kartR^itvaM sUcyata ityadoShaH || 

atrAha -- yadi buddhivyatirikto jIvaH kartA syAt, sa svatantraH san priyaM hitaM caiva Atmano niyamena sampAdayet, na viparItam | viparItam api tu sampAdayannupalabhyate | na ca svatantrasyAtmanaH IdR^ishI pravR^ittiraniyamenopapadyata iti, ata uttaraM paThati -- 

upalabdhivadaniyamaH || 2.3.37 || 

 || 2.3.37 || 

yathAyam AtmopalabdhiM prati svatantro.api aniyameneShTAmaniShTAM ca upalabhate, evamaniyamenaiveShTAmaniShTAM ca sampAdayiShyati | upalabdhAvapyasvAtantryam, upalabdhihetUpAdAnopalambhAd iti cet, na, viShayaprakalpanAmAtraprayojanatvAd upalabdhihetUnAm | upalabdhau tu ananyApekShatvamAtmanaH, caitanyayogAt | api ca 
arthakriyAyAm api nAtyantamAtmanaH svAtantryam asti, deshakAlanimittavisheShApekShatvAt | na ca sahAyApekShasya kartuH kartR^itvaM nivartate | bhavati hyedhodakAdyapekShasyApi paktuH paktR^itvam | sahakArivaicitryAcca iShTAniShTArthakriyAyAmaniyamena pravR^ittirAtmano na virudhyate ||

shaktiviparyayAt || 2.3.38 || 

 || 2.3.38 || 

itashca vij~nAnavyatirikto jIvaH kartA bhavitum arhati | yadi punar vij~nAnashabdavAcyA buddhir eva kartrI syAt, tataH shaktiviparyayaH syAt -- karaNashaktir buddhir hIyeta, kartR^ishaktishcApadyeta | satyAM ca buddheH kartR^ishaktau, tasyA eva ahampratyayaviShayatvam abhyupagantavyam, ahaMkArapUrvikAyA eva pravR^itteH sarvatra darshanAt -- ahaM gacchAmi, aham AgacchAmi, ahaM bhuJNje, ahaM pibAmi iti ca | tasyAshca kartR^ishaktiyuktAyAH sarvArthakAri karaNam anyat kalpayitavyam | shakto.api hi san kartA karaNam upAdAya kriyAsu pravartamAno dR^ishyate | tatashca saMj~nAmAtre vivAdaH syAt, na vastubhedaH kashcit, karaNavyatiriktasya kartR^itvAbhyupagamAt ||38||

|| 2.3.39 || 

samAdhyabhAvAcca ||

yo.apyayam aupaniShadAtmapratipattiprayojanaH samAdhir upadiShTo vedAnteShu -- AtmA vA are draShTavyaH shrotavyo mantavyo nididhyAsitavyaH so.anveShTavyaH sa vijij~nAsitavyaH om ityevaM dhyAyatha AtmAnam ityevaMlakShaNaH, so.apyasatyAtmanaH kartR^itve nopapadyeta | tasmAd apyasya kartR^itvasiddhiH ||39||

takShAdhikaraNam 

|| 2.3.40 ||

evaM tAvacchAstrArthavattvAdibhir hetubhiH kartR^itvaM shArIrasya pradarshitam | tat punaH svAbhAvikaM vA syAt, upAdhinimittaM veti cintyate | tatraitair eva shAstrArthavattvAdibhir hetubhiH svAbhAvikaM kartR^itvam, apavAdahetvabhAvAd iti | evaM prApte, brUmaH -- 

yathA ca takShobhayathA ||

na svAbhAvikaM kartR^itvam AtmanaH sambhavati, anirmokShaprasaN^gAt | kartR^itvasvabhAvatve hyAtmano na kartR^itvAn nirmokShaH sambhavati -- agneH ivauShNyAt | na ca kartR^itvAd anirmuktasyAsti puruShArthasiddhiH, kartR^itvasya duHkharUpatvAt | 

nanu sthitAyAm api kartR^itvashaktau kartR^itvakAryaparihArAt puruShArthaH setsyati | tatparihArashca nimittaparihArAt -- yathAgner dahanashaktiyuktasyApi kAShThaviyogAd dahanakAryAbhAvaH, tadvat, na, nimittAnAm api shaktilakShaNena sambandhena sambaddhAnAm atyantaparihArAsambhAvAt | 

nanu mokShasAdhanavidhAnAn mokShaH setsyati -- na, sAdhanAyattasya anityatvAt | api ca nityashuddhamuktAtmapratipAdanAt mokShasiddhir abhimatA | tAdR^igAtmapratipAdanaM ca na svAbhAvike kartR^itve.avakalpeta | tasmAt upAdhidharmAdhyAsenaivAtmanaH kartR^itvam, na svAbhAvikam | tathA ca shrutiH -- dhyAyatIva lelAyatIva iti AtmendriyamanoyuktaM bhoktetyAhur manIShiNaH iti ca -- upAdhisampR^iktasyaivAtmano bhoktR^itvAdivisheShalAbhaM darshayati | na hi vivekinAM parasmAd anyo jIvo nAma kartA bhoktA vA vidyate, nAnyo.ato.asti draShTA ityAdishravaNAt | para eva tarhi saMsArI kartA bhoktA ca prasajyeta | parasmAd anyashceccitimAJNjIvaH kartA, buddhyAdisaMghAtavyatirikto na syAt -- na, avidyApratyupasthApitatvAt kartR^itvabhoktR^itvayoH | tathA ca shAstram -- yatra hi dvaitam iva bhavati taditara itaraM pashyati ityavidyAvasthAyAM kartR^itvabhoktR^itve darshayitvA, vidyAvasthAyAM te eva kartR^itvabhoktR^itve nivArayati -- yatra tu asya sarvam AtmaivAbhUt tat kena kaM pashyet [bR^i.A.u. 4.5.15] iti | tathA svapnajAgaritayor Atmana upAdhisamparkakR^itaM shramaM shyenasyevAkAshe viparipatataH shrAvayitvA, tadabhAvaM suShuptau prAj~nenAtmanA sampariShvaktasya shrAvayati -- tad vA asyaitad AptakAmam AtmakAmam akAmaM rUpaM shokAntaram ityArabhya eShAsya paramA gatir eShAsya paramA sampad eSho.asya paramo loka eSho.asya parama AnandaH ityupasaMhArAt || 

tad etad AhAcAryaH -- yathA ca takShobhayathA iti | tu arthe cAyaM caH paThitaH | naivaM mantavyam -- svAbhAvikam evAtmanaH kartR^itvam, agneH ivauShNyam iti | yathA tu takShA loke vAsyAdikaraNahastaH kartA duHkhI bhavati, sa eva svagR^ihaM prApto vimuktavAsyAdikaraNaH svastho nirvR^ito nirvyApAraH sukhI bhavati | evam avidyApratyupasthApitadvaitasampR^ikta AtmA svapnajAgaritAvasthayoH kartA duHkhI bhavati, sa taccharmApanuttaye svam AtmAnaM paraM brahma pravishya vimuktakAryakaraNasaMghAto.akartA sukhI bhavati samprasAdAvasthAyAm -- tathA muktyavasthAyAm apyavidyAdinA taM vidyApradIpena vidhUya Atmaiva kevalo nirvR^ittaH sukhI bhavati | takShadR^iShTAntashcaitAvatAMshena draShTavyaH -- takShA hi vishiShTeShu takShaNAdivyApAreShvapekShyaiva pratiniyatAni karaNAni vAsyAdIni kartA bhavati, svasharIreNa tu akarteva | evam ayam AtmA sarvavyApAreShvapekShyaiva manAdIni karaNAni kartA bhavati, svAtmanA tu karteveti | na tu AtmanaH takShNa ivAvayavAH santi, yaiH hastAdibhiH iva vAsyAdIni takShA, manaAdIni karaNAnyAtmopAdadIta nyasyed vA || 

yat tUktam, shAstrArthavattvAdibhir hetubhiH svAbhAvikam AtmanaH kartR^itvam iti, tan na -- vidhishAstraM tAvad yathAprAptaM kartR^itvam upAdAya kartavyavisheSham upadishati, na kartR^itvam AtmanaH pratipAdayati | na ca svAbhAvikam asya kartR^itvam asti, brahmAtmatvopadeshAt -- ityavocAma | tasmAd avidyAkR^itaM kartR^itvam upAdAya vidhishAstraM pravartiShyate | kartA vij~nAnAtmA puruShaH [pra.u. 4.9] ityevaMjAtIyakam api shAstram anuvAdarUpatvAd yathAprAptam evAvidyAkR^itaM kartR^itvam anuvadiShyati | etena vihAropAdAne parihR^ite, tayor apyanuvAdarUpatvAt | 

nanu sandhye sthAne prasupteShu karaNeShu sve sharIre yathAkAmaM parivartate -- iti vihAra upadishyamAnaH kevalasyAtmanaH kartR^itvam Avahati | tathopAdAne.api tad eShAM prANAnAM vij~nAnena vij~nAnam AdAya iti karaNeShu karmakaraNavibhaktI shrUyamANe kevalasyAtmanaH kartR^itvaM gamayata iti | 

atrocyate -- na tAvat sandhye sthAne.atyantam AtmanaH karaNaviramaNam asti, sadhIH svapno bhUtvemaM lokam atikrAmati iti tatrApi dhIsambandhashravaNAt | tathA ca smaranti -- 

indriyANAm uparame mano.anuparataM yadi | 
sevate viShayAn eva tad vidyAt svapnadarshanam || iti | 

kAmAdayashca manaso vR^ittayaH iti shrutiH | tAshca svapne dR^ishyante | tasmAt samanA eva svapte viharati | vihAro.api ca tatratyo vAsanAmaya eva, na tu pAramArthiko.asti | tathA ca shrutiH ivakArAnubaddham eva svapnavyApAraM varNayati -- uteva strIbhiH saha modamAno jakShad utevApi bhayAni pashyan iti | laukikA api tathaiva svapnaM kathayanti -- ArukSham iva girisR^iN^gam, adrAkSham iva vanarAjim iti | tathopAdAne.api yadyapi karaNeShu karmakaraNavibhaktinirdeshaH, tathApi tatsampR^iktasyaivAtmanaH kartR^itvaM draShTavyam, kevale kartR^itvAsambhavasya darshitatvAt | bhavati ca loke.anekaprakArA vivakShA -- yodhA yudhyante, yodhai rAjA yudhyata iti | 

api ca asminn upAdAne karaNavyApAroparamamAtraM vivakShyate, na svAtantryaM kasyacit, abuddhipUrvakasyApi svApe karaNavyApAroparamasya dR^iShTatvAt | yaH tu ayaM vyapadesho darshitaH, vij~nAnaM yaj~naM tanute iti, sa buddher eva kartR^itvaM prApayati -- vij~nAnashabdasya tatra prasiddhatvAt, mano.anantaraM pAThAcca, tasya shraddhaiva shiraH iti ca vij~nAnamayasyAtmanaH shraddhAdyavayavatvasaN^kIrtanAt -- shraddhAdInAM ca buddhidharmatvaprasiddhiH, vij~nAnaM devAH sarve brahma jyeShTham upAsate iti ca vAkyasheShAt -- jyeShThatvasya ca prathamajatvasya buddhau prasiddhatvAt, sa eSha vAcashcittasyottarottarakramo yadyaj~naH iti ca shrutyantare yaj~nasya vAgbuddhisAdhyatvAvadhAraNAt | na ca buddhiH shaktiviparyayaH karaNAnAM kartR^itvAbhyupagame bhavati, sarvakArakANAm eva svasvavyApAreShu kartR^itvasyAvashyambhAvitvAt | upalabdhyapekShaM tv eShAM karaNAnAM karaNatvam | sA cAtmanaH | na ca tasyAm apyasya kartR^itvam asti, nityopalabdhisvarUpatvAt | ahaMkArapUrvakam api kartR^itvaM nopalabdhur bhavitum arhati, ahaMkArasyApyupalabhyamAnatvAt | na caivaM sati karaNAntarakalpanAprasaN^gaH, buddheH karaNatvAbhyupagamAt | samAdhyabhAvaH tu shAstrArthavattvenaiva parihR^itaH, yathAprAptam eva kartR^itvam upAdAya samAdhividhAnAt | tasmAt kartR^itvam apyAtmana upAdhinimittam eveti sthitam ||40||

 -- o)0(o -- 

parAyattAdhikaraNam 

|| 2.3.41 ||

parAt tu tacchruteH || 

yad idam avidyAvasthAyAm upAdhinibandhanaM kartR^itvaM jIvasyAbhihitam, tat kim anapekShyeshvaraM bhavati, Aho svid IshvarApekSham iti bhavati vicAraNA | tatra prAptaM tAvat -- neshvaram apekShate jIvaH kartR^itva iti | kasmAt? apekShAprayojanAbhAvAt | ayaM hi jIvaH svayam eva rAgadveShAdidoShaprayuktaH kArakAntarasAmagrIsampannaH kartR^itvam anubhavituM shaknoti | tasya kim IshvaraH kariShyati? na ca loke prasiddhir asti -- kR^iShyAdikAsu kriyAsvanaDuhAdivat Ishvaro.aparo.apekShitavya iti | kleshAtmakena ca kartR^itvena jantUn saMsR^ijata Ishvarasya nairghR^iNyaM prasajyeta | viShamaphalaM ca eShAM kartR^itvaM vidadhato vaiShamyam | 

nanu vaiShamyanairghR^iNye na sApekShatvAt ityuktam -- satyam uktam, sati tu Ishvarasya sApekShatvasambhave | sApekShatvaM ca Ishvarasya sambhavati sator jantUnAM dharmAdharmayoH | tayoshca sadbhAvaH sati jIvasya kartR^itve | tad eva cet kartR^itvam IshvarApekShaM syAt, kiMviShayam Ishvarasya sApekShatvam ucyeta | akR^itAbhyAgamashcaivaM jIvasya prasajyeta | tasmAt svata evAsya kartR^itvam iti -- etAM prAptiM tushabdena vyAvartya pratijAnIte -- parAd iti | avidyAvasthAyAM kAryakaraNasaMghAtAvivekadarshino jIvasyAvidyAtimirAndhasya sataH parasmAd AtmanaH karmAdhyakShAt sarvabhUtAdhivAsAt sAkShiNashcetayitur IshvarAt tadanuj~nayA kartR^itvabhoktR^itvalakShaNasya saMsArasya siddhiH | tadanugrahahetukenaiva ca vij~nAnena mokShasiddhir bhavitum arhati | kutaH? tacchruteH | yadyapi doShaprayuktaH sAmagrIsampannashca jIvaH, yadyapi ca loke kR^iShyAdiShu karmasu neshvarakAraNatvaM prasiddham, tathApi sarvAsv eva pravR^ittiShv Ishvaro hetukarteti shruter avasIyate | tathA hi shrutir bhavati -- eSha hyeva sAdhu karma kArayati taM yamebhyo lokebhya unninIShate | eSha hyevAsAdhu karma kArayati taM yam adho ninIShate [kau.u. 3.8] iti, ya Atmani tiShThann AtmAnam antaro yamayati [bR^i.A.u. 3.7.5] iti ca evaMjAtIyakA ||41||

|| 2.3.42 ||

nanu evam Ishvarasya kArayitR^itve sati vaiShamyanairghR^iNye syAtAm, akR^itAbhyAgamashca jIvasyeti | netyucyata -- 

kR^itaprayatnApekShaH tu vihitapratiShiddhAvaiyarthyAdibhyaH ||

tushabdashcoditadoShavyAvartanArthaH | kR^ito yaH prayatno jIvasya dharmAdharmalakShaNaH, tadapekSha evainam IshvaraH kArayati | atashcaite coditA doShA na prasajyante -- jIvakR^itadharmAdharmavaiShamyApekSha eva tattatphalAni viShamaM vibhajet parjanyavat Ishvaro nimittatvamAtreNa -- yathA loke nAnAvidhAnAM gucchagulmAdInAM vrIhiyavAdInAM ca asAdhAraNebhyaH svasvabIjebhyo jAyamAnAnAM sAdhAraNaM nimittaM bhavati parjanyaH -- na hi asati parjanye rasapuShpaphalapalAshAdivaiShamyaM teShAM jAyate, nApyasatsu svasvabIjeShu -- evaM jIvakR^itaprayatnApekSha IshvaraH teShAM shubhAshubhaM vidadhyAd iti shliShyate | 

nanu kR^itaprayatnApekShatvam eva jIvasya parAyatte kartR^itve nopapadyate -- naiSha doShaH | parAyatte.api hi kartR^itve, karotyeva jIvaH, kurvantaM hi tam IshvaraH kArayati | api ca pUrvaprayatnam apekShya idAnIM kArayati, pUrvataraM ca prayatnam apekShya pUrvam akArayad iti -- anAditvAt saMsArasyeti -- anavadyam | kathaM punar avagamyate -- kR^itaprayatnApekSha Ishvara iti? vihitapratiShiddhAvaiyarthyAdibhyaH ityAha | evaM hi svargakAmo yajeta brAhmaNo na hantavyaH ityevaMjAtIyakasya vihitasya pratiShiddhasya ca avaiyarthyaM bhavati | anyathA tad anarthakaM syAt | Ishvara eva vidhipratiShedhayor niyujyeta, atyantaparatantratvAjjIvasya | tathA vihitakAriNam apyanarthena saMsR^ijet, pratiShiddhakAriNam apyarthena | tatashca prAmANyaM vedasyAstamiyAt | Ishvarasya ca atyantAnapekShatve laukikasyApi puruShakArasya vaiyarthyam, tathA deshakAlanimittAnAm | pUrvoktadoShaprasaN^gashca -- ityevaMjAtIyakaM doShajAtam AdigrahaNena darshayati ||42||

 -- o)0(o -- 
17. aMshAdhikaraNam 
|| 2.3.43 || 

svAmibhR^ityayoH, yathA vA agnivisphuliN^gayoH | tatashca jIveshvarayor apyupakAryopakArakabhAvAbhyupagamAt kiM svAmibhR^ityavatsambandhaH, Aho svid agnivisphuliN^gavat? ityasyAM vicikitsAyAm aniyamo vA prApnoti | athavA svAmibhR^ityaprakAreShv eva IshitrIshitavyabhAvasya prasiddhatvAt tadvidha eva sambandha iti prApnoti || ato bravIti -- 

aMsho nAnAvyapadeshAd anyathA cApi dAsakitavAditvam adhIyata eke ||

jIveshvarayor upakAryopakArakabhAva uktaH | sa ca sambaddhayor eva loke dR^iShTAH -- yathA jIva IshvarasyAMsho bhavitum arhati, yathAgner visphuliN^gaH | aMsha ivAMshaH | na hi niravayavasya mukhyoM.ashaH sambhavati | kasmAt punaH niravayavatvAt sa eva na bhavati? nAnAvyapadeshAt | so.anveShTavyaH sa vijij~nAsitavyaH etam eva viditvA munir bhavati ya Atmani tiShThann AtmAnam antaro yamayati [bR^i.A.u. 3.7.5] iti ca evaMjAtIyako bhedanirdesho nAsati bhede yujyate | 

nanu ca ayaM nAnAvyapadeshaH sutarAM svAmibhR^ityasArUpye yujyata iti, ata Aha -- anyathA cApIti | na ca nAnAvyapadeshAd eva kevalAd aMshatvapratipattiH | kiM tarhi, anyathA cApi vyapadesho bhavatyanAnAtvasya pratipAdakaH | tathA hyeke shAkhino dAshakitavAdibhAvaM brahmaNa AmanantyAtharvaNikAbrahmasUkte -- brahma dAshA brahma dAsA brahmaiveme kitavAH ityAdinA | dAshA ya ete kaivartAH prasiddhAH, ye ca amI dAsAH svAmiShvatmAnam upakShapayanti, ye ca anye kitavA dyUtakR^itaH, te sarve brahmaiva -- iti hInajantUdAharaNena sarveShAm eva nAmarUpakR^itakAryakaraNasaMghAtapraviShTAnAM jIvAnAM brahmatvam Aha | tathA anyatrApi brahmaprakriyAyAm evAyam arthaH prapaJNcyate -- tvaM strI tvaM pumAn asi tvaM kumAra uta vA kumArI | tvaM jINo daNDona vaJNcasi tvaM jAto bhavati vishvatomukhaH iti, sarvANi rUpANi vicitya dhIro nAmAni kR^itvAbhivadan yad Aste iti ca | nAnyo.ato.asti draShTA ityAdi shrutibhyashca asyArthasya siddhiH | caitanyaM ca avishiShTaM jIveshvarayoH, yathAgnivisphuliN^gayor auShNyam | ato bhedAbhedAvagamAbhyAm aMshatvAvagamaH || 

|| 2.3.44 ||

kutashca aMshatvAvagamaH? -- 
mantravarNAcca || 

mantravarNashcaitam artham avagamayati --  tAvAn asya mahimA | tato jyAyAMshca puruShaH | pAdo.asya sarvA bhUtAni | tripAdasyAmR^itaM divi iti | atra bhUtashabdena jIvapradhAnAni sthAvarajaN^gamAni nirdishati, ahiMsan sarvabhUtAnyanyatra tIrthebhyaH iti prayogAt | aMshaH pAdo bhAga ityanarthAntaram | tasmAd apyaMshatvAvagamaH ||44|| 

|| 2.3.45 || 

kutashca aMshatvAvagamaH? -- 

api ca smaryate || 

IshvaragItAsvapi ca IshvarAMshatvaM jIvasya smaryate -- mamaivAMsho jIvaloke jIvabhUtaH sanAtanaH [gItA 15.7] iti | tasmAd apyaMshatvAvagamaH | yat tUktam, svAmibhR^ityAdiShv eva IshitrIshitavyabhAvo loke prasiddha iti --  yadyapyeShA loke prasiddhiH, tathApi shAstrAt tu atra aMshAMshitvam IshitrIshitavyabhAvashca nishcIyate | niratishayopAdhisampannashceshvaro nihInopAdhisampannAJNjIvAn prashAstIti na kiJNcid vipratiShidhyate || 

atrAha -- nanu jIvasyeshvarAMshatvAbhyupagame tadIyena saMsAraduHkhopabhogenAMshina IshvarasyApi duHkhitvaM syAt -- yathA loke hastapAdAdyanyatamAN^gatena duHkhena aN^gino devadattasya duHkhitvam, tadvat | tatashca tatprAptAnAM mahattaraM duHkhaM prApnuyAt | ato varaM pUrvAvasthaH saMsAra evAstu -- iti samyagdarshanAnarthakyaprasaN^gaH syAd iti || 

|| 2.3.46 || 

atrocyate -- 
prakAshAdivan naivaM paraH ||

yathA jIvaH saMsAraduHkham anubhavati, naivaM para Ishvaro.anubhavatIti pratijAnImahe | jIvo hi avidyAveshavashAt dehAdyAtmabhAvam iva gatvA, tatkR^itena duHkhena duHkhI aham iti avidyayA kR^itaM duHkhopabhogam abhimanyate | naivaM parameshvarasya dehAdyAtmabhAvo duHkhAbhimAno vAsti |

jIvasyApyavidyAkR^itanAmarUpanirvR^ittadehendriyAdyupAdhyavivekabhramanimitta eva duHkhAbhimAnaH, na tu pAramArthiko.asti | yathA ca svadehagatadAhacchedAdinimittaM duHkhaM tadabhimAnabhrAntyAnubhavati, tathA putramitrAdigocaram api duHkhaM tadabhimAnabhrAntyaivAnubhavati -- aham eva putraH, aham eva mitram ityevaM snehavashena putramitrAdiShvabhinivishamAnaH | tatashca nishcitam etad avagamyate -- mithyAbhimAnabhramanimitta eva duHkhAnubhava iti | vyatirekadarshanAcca evam avagamyate | tathA hi -- putramitrAdimatsu bahuShUpaviShTeShu tatsambandhAbhimAniShvitareShu ca, putro mR^ito mitraM mR^itam ityevam AghoShite, yeShAm eva putramitrAdimattvAbhimAnaH teShAm eva tannimittaM duHkham utpadyate, na abhimAnahInAnAM parivrAjakAdInAm | atashca laukikasyApi puMsaH samyagdashanArthavattvaM dR^iShTam, kim uta viShayashUnyAd Atmano.anyad vastvantaram apashyato nityacaitanyamAtrasvarUpasyeti | tasmAn nAsti samyagdarshanAnarthakyaprasaN^gaH | 

prakAshAdivad iti nidarshanopanyAsaH -- prakAshaH saurashcAndramaso vA viyad vyApya avatiShThamAno.aN^gulyAdyupAdhisambandhAt teShu R^ijuvakrAdibhAvaM pratipadyamAneShu tattadbhAvam iva pratipadyamAno.api na paramArthataH tadbhAvaM pratipadyate, yathA cAkAsho ghaTAdiShu gacchatsu gacchann iva vibhAvyamAno.api na paramArthato gacchati, yathA ca udasharAvAdikampanAt tadgate sUryapratibimbe kampamAne.api na tadvAn sUryaH kampate -- evam avidyApratyupasthApite buddhyAdyupahite jIvAkhye aMshe duHkhAyamAne.api na tadvAn Ishvaro duHkhAyate | jIvasyApi duHkhaprAptir avidyAnimittaivetyuktam | tathA ca avidyAnimittajIvabhAvavyudAsena brahmabhAvam eva jIvasya pratipAdayanti vedAntAH -- tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7] ityevamAdayaH | tasmAn nAsti jaivena duHkhena paramAtmano duHkhitvaprasaN^gaH ||46||

|| 2.3.47 ||

smaranti ca || 

smaranti ca vyAsAdayaH -- yathA jaivena duHkhena na paramAtmA duHkhAyata iti | tatra yaH paramAtmA hi sa nityo nirguNaH smR^itaH | na lipyate phalaishcApi paspatramivAmbhasA | karmAtmA tu aparo yo.asau mokShabandhaiH sa yujyate | sa saptadashakenApi rAshinA yujyate punaH iti | cashabdAt -- sam Amananti ca -- iti vAkyasheShaH -- tayor anyaH pippalaM svAdvattyanashnann anyo abhicAkashIti [mu.u. 3.1.1] iti, ekaH tathA sarvabhUtAntarAtmA na lipyate lokaduHkhena bAhyaH iti ca ||47|| 

|| 2.3.48 || 

atrAha -- yadi tarhyeka eva sarveShAM bhUtAnAm antarAtmA syAt, katham anuj~nAparihArau syAtAM laukikau vaidikau ceti | 

nanu ca aMsho jIva Ishvarasya ityuktam | tadbhedAccAnuj~nAparihArau tadAshrayAvavyatikIrNAvupapadyete | kim atra codyata iti, ucyate -- naitad evam | anaMshatvam api hi jIvasyAbhedavAdinyaH shrutayaH pratipAdayanti -- tat sR^iShTvA tad evAnuprAvishat nAnyo.ato.asti draShTA mR^ityoH sa mR^ityum Apnoti ya iha nAneva pashyati tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7], ahaM brahmAsmi [bR^i.A.u. 1.4.10] ityevaMjAtIyakAH | 

nanu bhedAbhedAvagamAbhyAm aMshatvaM sidhyatItyuktam -- syAd etad evam, yadyubhAvapi bhedAbhedau pratipipAdayiShitau syAtAm | abheda eva tu atra pratipipAdayiShitaH, brahmAtmatvapratipattau puruShArthasiddhiH | svabhAvaprAptaH tu bhedo.anUdyate | na ca niravayavasya brahmaNo mukhyo.aMsho jIvaH sambhavatItyuktam | tasmAt para evaikaH sarveShAM bhUtAnAm antarAtmA jIvabhAvenAvasthita ityato vaktavyA anuj~nAparihAropapattiH | tAM brUmaH -- 

anuj~nAparihArau dehasambandhAjjyotirAdivat || 

R^itau bhAryAm upeyAt ityanuj~nA, gurvaN^ganAM nopagacchet iti parihAraH | tathA agnIShomIyaM pashuM saMj~napayet ityanuj~nA, na hiMsyAt sarvA bhUtAni iti parihAraH |  evaM loke.api mitram upasevitavyam ityanuj~nA, shatruH parihartavya iti parihAraH -- evamprakArAvanuj~nAparihArau ekatve.apyAtmanaH dehasambandhAt syAt | dehaiH sambandho dehasambandhaH | kaH punar dehasambandhaH? dehAdirayaM saMghAto.aham eva -- ityAtmani viparItapratyayotpattiH | dR^iShTA ca sA sarvaprANinAm -- ahaM gacchAmi ahamAgacchAmi, ahamandho.ahamanandhaH, ahaM mUDho.ahamamUDhaH ityevamAtmikA | na hi asyAH samyagdarshanAdanyannivArakam asti | prAktu samyagdarshanAt pratataiShA bhrAntiH sarvajantuShu | tad evam avidyAnimittadehAdyupAdhisambandhakR^itAd visheShAd aikAtmyAbhyupagame.apyanuj~nAparihArAvavakalpete | samyagdarshinaH tarhyanuj~nAparihArAnarthakyaM prAptam -- na, tasya kR^itArthatvAn niyojyatvAnupapatteH -- heyopAdeyayor hi niyojyo niyoktavyaH syAt | AtmanaH tu atiriktaM heyam upAdeyaM vA vastu apashyan kathaM niyujyeta | na ca AtmA Atmanyeva niyojyaH syAt | sharIravyatirekadarshina eva niyojyatvam iti cet, na | tatsaMhatatvAbhimAnAt -- satyaM vyatirekadarshino niyojyatvam | tathApi vyomAdivad dehAdyasaMhatatvam apashyata eva Atmano niyojyatvAbhimAnaH | na hi dehAdyasaMhatatvadarshinaH kasyacid api niyogo dR^iShTAH, kim utaikAtmyadarshinaH | na ca niyogAbhAvAt samyagdarshino yatheShTaceShTAprasaN^gaH, sarvatrAbhimAnasyaiva pravartakatvAt, abhimAnAbhAvAcca samyagdarshinaH | tasmAd dehasambandhAd evAnuj~nAparihArau -- jyotir Adivat -- yathA jyotiSha ekatve.apyagniH kravyAt parihriyate, netaraH | yathA ca prakAsha ekasyApi savitur amedhyadeshasambaddhaH parihriyate, netaraH shucibhUmiShThaH | tathA bhaumAH pradeshA vajravaiDUryAdaya upAdIyante, bhaumA api santo narakalevarAdayaH parihriyante | tathA mUtrapurIShaM gavAM pavitratayA parigR^ihyate, tad eva jAtyantare parivarjyate, tadvat ||48||

asantateshcAvyatikaraH || 2.3.49 || 

 || 2.3.49 || 

syAtAM nAma anuj~nAparihArAvekasyAtmano dehavisheShayogAt | yastvayaM karmaphalasambandhaH, sa ca IkAtmyAbhyupagame vyatikIryeta, svAmyekatvAd iti cet, naitad evam, asaMtateH | na hi karturbhoktushcAtmanaH saMtataH sarveH sharIraiH sambandho.asti | upAdhitantro hi jIva ityuktam | upAdhyasantAnAcca nAsti jIvasantAnaH -- tatashca karmavyatikaraH phalavyatikaro vA na bhaviShyati ||

|| 2.3.50 || 

AbhAsa eva ca || 

AbhAsa eva ca eSha jIvaH parasyAtmano jalasUryakAdivat pratipattavyaH, na sa eva sAkShAt, nApi vastvantaram | atashca yathA naikasmiJNjalasUryake kampamAne jalasUryakAntaraM kampate, evaM naikasmiJNjIve karmaphalasambandhini jIvAntarasya tatsambandhaH | evam avyatikara eva karmaphalayoH | AbhAsasya ca avidyAkR^itatvAt tadAshrayasya saMsArasyAvidyAkR^itatvopapattiH iti, tadvyudAsena ca pAramArthikasya brahmAtmabhAvasyopadeshopapattiH | yeShAM tu bahava AtmAnaH, te ca sarve sarvagatAH, teShAm evaiSha vyatikaraH prApnoti | katham? bahavo vibhavashcAtmAnashcaitanyamAtrasvarUpA nirguNA niratishayAshca | tadarthaM sAdhAraNaM pradhAnam | tannimittaiShAM bhogApavargasiddhiH iti sAN^khyAH | sati bahutve vibhutve ca ghaTakuDyAdisamAnA dravyamAtrasvarUpAH svato.acetanA AtmAnaH, tadupakaraNAni ca aNUni manAMsyacetanAni, tatra AtmadravyANAM manodravyANAM ca saMyogAt nava icchAdayo vaisheShikA AtmaguNA utpadyante, te ca avyatirekeNa pratyekam Atmasu samavayanti, sa saMsAraH | teShAM navAnAm AtmaguNAnAm atyantAnutpAdo mokSha iti kANAdAH | tatra sAN^khyAnAM tAvaccaitanyasvarUpatvAt sarvAtmanAM saMnidhAnAdyavisheShAcca ekasya sukhaduHkhasambandhe sarveShAM sukhaduHkhasambandhaH prApnoti | syAd etat -- pradhAnapravR^itteH puruShakaivalyArthatvAd vyavasthA bhaviShyati | anyathA hi svavibhUtikhyApanArthA pradhAnapravR^ittiH syAt | tathA ca anirmokShaH prasajyeteti -- naitat sAram -- na hi abhilaShitasiddhinibandhanA vyavasthA shakyA vij~nAtum | upapattyA tu kayAcid vyavasthocyeta | asatyAM punar upapattau kAmaM mA bhUd abhilaShitaM puruShakaivalyam | prApnoti tu vyavasthAhetvabhAvAd vyatikaraH | kANAdAnAm api -- yadA ekenAtmanA manaH saMyujyate, tadA AtmAntarair api nAntarIyakaH saMyogaH syAt, saMnidhAnAdyavisheShAt | tatashca hetu avisheShAt phalAvisheSha ityekasyAtmanaH sukhaduHkhayoge sarvAtmanAm api samAnaM sukhaduHkhitvaM prasajyeta ||50|| 

|| 2.3.51 ||

syAd etat -- adR^iShTanimitto niyamo bhaviShyatIti | netyAha -- 

adR^iShTAniyamAt ||

bahuShvatmasvakAshavat sarvagateShu pratisharIraM bAhyAbhyantarAvisheSheNa saMnihiteShu manovAkkAyair dharmAdharmalakShaNam adR^iShTam upArjyate | sAN^khyAnAM tAvat tadanAtmasamavAyi pradhAnavarti | pradhAnasAdhAraNyAn na pratyAtmaM sukhaduHkhopabhogasya niyAmakam upapadyate | kANAdAnAm api pUrvavat sAdhAraNenAtmamanaHsaMyogena nirvartitasyAdR^iShTasyApi asyaivAtmana idam adR^iShTam iti niyame hetvabhAvAd eSha eva doShaH ||51|| 

|| 2.3.52 || 

syAd etat -- aham idaM phalaM prApnavAni, idaM pariharANi, itthaM prayatai, itthaM karavANi -- ityevaMvidhA abhisandhyAdayaH pratyAtmaM pravartamAnA adR^iShTasyAtmanAM ca svasvAmibhAvaM niyaMsyantIti | netyAha -- 

abhisandhyAdiShvapi caivam || 

abhisandhyAdInAm api sAdhAraNenaivAtmamanaHsaMyogena sarvAtmasaMnidhau kriyamANAnAM niyamahetutvAnupapatter uktadoShAnuShaN^ga eva ||52||

|| 2.3.53 || 

pradeshAd iti cen nAntarbhAvAt || 

athocyeta -- vibhutve.apyAtmanaH sharIrapratiShThena manasA saMyogaH sharIrAvacchinna eva Atmapradeshe bhaviShyati | ataH pradeshakR^itA vyavasthA abhisandhyAdInAm adR^iShTasya sukhaduHkhayoshca bhaviShyatIti, tad api nopapadyate | kasmAt? antarbhAvAt | vibhutvAvisheShAd dhi sarva evAtmAnaH sarvasharIreShvantarbhavanti | tatra na vaisheShikaiH sharIrAvacchinno.apyAtmanaH pradeshaH kalpayituM shakyaH | kalpyamAno.apyayaM niShpradeshasyAtmanaH pradeshaH kAlpanikatvAd eva na pAramArthikaM kAryaM niyantuM shaknoti | sharIram api sarvAtmasaMnidhAv utpadyamAnam -- asyaiva AtmanaH, netareShAm -- iti na niyantuM shakyam | pradeshavisheShAbhyupagame.api ca dvayor AtmanoH samAnasukhaduHkhabhAjoH kadAcid ekenaiva tAvaccharIreNopabhogasiddhiH syAt, samAnapradeshasyApi dvayor Atmanor adR^iShTasya sambhavAt | tathA hi -- devadatto yasmin pradeshe sukhaduHkham anvabhUt, tasmAt pradeshAd apakrAnte taccharIre, yaj~nadattasharIre ca taM pradesham anuprApte, tasyApi itareNa samAnaH sukhaduHkhAnubhavo dR^ishyate | sa na syAt, yadi devadattayaj~nadattayoH samAnapradesham adR^iShTaM na syAt | svargAdyanupabhogaprasaN^gashca pradeshavAdinaH syAt, brAhmaNAdisharIrapradesheShvadR^iShTaniShpatteH pradeshAntaravartitvAcca svargAdyupabhogasya | sarvagatatvAnupapattishca bahUnAm AtmanAm, dR^iShTAntAbhAvAt | vada tAvat tvam -- ke bahavaH samAnadeshAshceti | rUpAdaya iti cet, na | teShAm api dharmyaMshenAbhedAt, lakShaNabhedAcca -- na tu bahUnAm AtmanAM lakShaNabhedo.asti | antyavisheShavashAd bhedopapattiH iti cet, na | bhedakalpanAyA antyavisheShakalpanAyAshca itaretarAshrayatvAt | AkAshAdInAm api vibhutvaM brahmavAdino.asiddham, kAryatvAbhyupagamAt | tasmAd AtmaikatvapakSha eva sarvadoShAbhAva iti siddham ||53|| 

iti shrImatparamahaMsaparivrAjakAcAryasya shrIgovindabhagavatpUjyapAdashiShyasya shrImacchaN^karabhagavataH kR^itau 
shArIrakamImAMsAsUtrabhAShye dvitIyAdhyAyasya tR^itIyaH pAdaH || 

 
(2.4)
|| dvitIyo.adhyAye caturthaH pAdaH ||

atra pAde liN^gasharIrashrutInAM virodhaparihAraH ||
1. prANotpattyadhikaraNam 

|| 2.4.1 ||

viyadAdiviShayaH shrutivipratiShedhaH tR^itIyena pAdena parihR^itaH | caturthenedAnIM prANaviShayaH parihriyate | tatra tAvat tat tejo.asR^ijata [chA.u. 6.2.3] iti, tasmAd vA etasmAd Atmana AkAshaH sambhUtaH [tai.u. 2.1.1] iti caivamAdiShUtpattiprakaraNeShu prANAnAm utpattir nAmnAyate | kvaciccAnutpattir evaiShAm AmnAyate -- asad vA idam agra AsIt | tad AhuH kiM tad asad AsId ity R^iShayo vAva te.agre.asad AsIt | tad AhuH ke te R^iShaya iti | prANA vAva R^iShayaH [tai.u. 2.7], ityatra prAgutpatteH prANAnAM sadbhAvashravaNAt | 

anyatra tu prANAnAm apyutpattiH paThyate -- yathAgner jvalataH kShudrA visphuliN^gA vyuccarantyevam evaitasmAd AtmanaH sarve prANAH iti, etasmAjjAyate prANo manaH sarvendriyANi ca [mu.u. 2.1.3] iti, sapta prANAH prabhavanti tasmAt [mu.u.  2.1.8] iti, sa prANam asR^ijata prANAcchraddhAM khaM vAyur jyotir ApaH pR^ithivIndriyaM mano.annam [pra.u. 6.4] iti caivamAdipradesheShu |

tatra tatra shrutivipratiShedhAd anyataranirdhAraNakAraNAnirUpaNAccApratipattiH prApnoti |
athavA prAgutpatteH sadbhAvashravaNAd gauNI prANAnAm utpattiH iti prApnoti | ata uttaram idaM paThati -- 

tathA prANAH ||

kathaM punar atra tathA ityakSharAnulomyam, prakR^itopamAnAbhAvAt -- sarvagatAtmabahutvavAdidUShaNam atItAnantarapAdAnte prakR^itam | tat tAvan nopamAnaM sambhavati, sAdR^ishyAbhAvAt | sAdR^ishye hi sati upamAnaM syAt, yathA diMhaH tathA balavarmeti | adR^iShTasAmyapratipAdanArtham iti yadyucyeta -- yathA adR^iShTasya sarvAtmasaMnidhAv utpadyamAnasyAniyatatvam, evaM prANAnAm api sarvAtmanaH pratyaniyatatvam iti -- tad api dehAniyamenaivoktatvAt punar uktaM bhavet | na ca jIvena prANA upamIyeran, siddhAntavirodhAt -- jIvasya hi anutpattir AkhyAtA, prANAnAM tu utpattir AcikhyAsitA | tasmAt tathA ityasambaddham iva pratibhAti -- na, udAharaNopAttenApyupamAnena sambandhopapatteH | atra prANotpattivAdivAkyajAtam udAharaNam -- etasmAd AtmanaH sarve prANAH sarve lokAH sarve devAH sarvANi bhUtAni vyuccaranti ityevaMjAtIyakam | tatra yathA lokAdayaH parasmAd brahmaNa utpadyante, tathA prANA apItyarthaH | tathA -- 

etasmAjjAyate prANo manaH sarvendriyANi ca |
khaM vAyur jyotir ApaH pR^ithivI vishvasya dhAriNI || [mu.u. 2.1.3]

ityevamAdiShvapi khAdivatprANAnAm utpattiH iti draShTavyam | athavA pAnavyApacca tadvat ityevamAdiShu vyavahitopamAnasambandhasyApyAshritatvAt  -- yathA atItAnantarapAdAdAv uktA viyadAdayaH parasya brahmaNo vikArAH samadhigatAH, tathA prANA api parasya brahmaNo vikArA iti yojayitavyam | kaH punaH prANAnAM vikAratve hetuH? shrutatvam eva | 

nanu keShucit pradesheShu na prANAnAm utpattiH shrUyata ityuktam -- tad ayuktam, pradeshAntareShu shravaNAt | na hi kvacid ashravaNam anyatra shrutaM nivArayitum utsahate | tasmAcchrutatvAvisheShAd AkAshAdivat prANA apyutpadyanta iti sUktam ||1||

|| 2.4.2 ||

yat punar uktaM prAgutpatteH sadbhAvashravaNAd gauNI prANAnAm utpattishrutiH iti, tat pratyAha -- 
gauNyasambhavAt || 

gauNyA asambhavo gauNyasambhavaH -- na hi prANAnAm utpattishrutir gauNI sambhavati, pratij~nAhAniprasaN^gAt -- kasmin nu bhagavo vij~nAte sarvam idaM vij~nAtaM bhavati [mu.u. 1.1.3] iti hi ekavij~nAnena sarvavij~nAnaM pratij~nAya tatsAdhanAyedam AmnAyate etasmAjjAyate prANaH [mu.u. 2.1.3] ityAdi | sA ca pratij~nA prANAdeH samastasya jagato brahmavikAratve sati prakR^itivyatirekeNa vikArAbhAvAt sidhyati | gauNyAM tu prANAnAm utpattishrutau pratij~nA iyaM hIyeta | tathA ca pratij~nAtArtham upasaMharati -- puruSha evedaM vishvaM karma tapo brahma parAmR^itam iti, brahmaivedaM vishvam idaM variShTham iti ca | tathA Atmano vA 
are darshanena shravaNena matyA vij~nAnenedaM sarvaM viditam ityevaMjAtIyakAsu shrutiShu eShaiva pratij~nA yojayitavyA | kathaM punaH prAgutpatteH prANAnAM sadbhAvashravaNam? naitanmUlaprakR^itiviShayam, aprANo hyamanAH shubhro hyakSharAt parataH paraH [mu.u. 2.1.2] iti mUlaprakR^iteH prANAdisamastavisheSharahitatvAvadhAraNAt | avAntaraprakR^itiviShayaM tv etat svavikArApekShaM prAgutpatteH prANAnAM sadbhAvAvadhAraNam iti draShTavyam, vyAkR^itaviShayANAm api bhUyasInAm avasthAnAM shrutismR^ityoH prakR^itivikArabhAvaprasiddhiH | viyadadhikaraNe hi -- gauNyasambhavAt iti pUrvapakShasUtratvAt  -- gauNIjanmashrutiH, asambhavAt -- iti vyAkhyAtam | pratij~nAhAnyA ca tatra siddhAnto.abhihitaH | iha tu siddhAntasUtratvAt  -- gauNyA janmashruter asambhavAt -- iti vyAkhyAtam | tadanurodhena tu ihApi -- gauNI janmashrutiH, asambhavAt -- iti vyAcakShANaiH pratij~nAhAnir upekShitA syAt ||2||

|| 2.4.3 ||

tat prAk shruteshca ||
