itashca AkAshAdInAm iva prANAnAm api mukhyaiva janmashrutiH -- yat jAyate ityekaM janmavAcipadaM prANeShu prAkshrutaM sat uttareShvakAshAdiShvanuvartate -- etasmAjjAyate prANaH [mu.u. 2.1.3] ityatra | AkAshAdiShu mukhyaM janmeti pratiShThApitam | tatsAmAnyAt prANeShvapi mukhyam eva janma bhavitum arhati | na hi ekasmin prakaraNe ekasmiMshca vAkye ekaH shabdaH sakR^iduccarito bahubhiH sambadhyamAnaH kvacin mukhyaH kvacid gauNa ityadhyavasAtuM shakyam, vairUpyaprasaN^gAt | tathA sa prANam asR^ijata prANAccharddhAm ityatrApi prANeShu shrutaH sR^ijatiH pareShvapyutpattimatsu shraddhAdiShvanuShajyate | yatrApi pashcAcchruta utpattivacanaH shabdaH pUrveH sambadhyate, tatrApyeSha eva nyAyaH -- yathA sarvANi bhUtAni vyuccaranti ityayam ante paThito vyuccarantishabdaH pUrvair api prANAdibhiH sambadhyate ||

|| 2.4.4 ||

tat pUrvakatvAd vAcaH ||

yadyapi tat tejo.asR^ijata [chA.u. 6.2.3] ityetasmin prakaraNe prANAnAm utpattir na paThyate, tejo.abannAnAm eva trayANAM bhUtAnAm utpattishravaNAt | tathApi brahmaprakR^itikatejo.abannapUrvakatvAbhidhAnAd vAkprANamanasAm, tatsAmAnyAcca sarveShAm eva prANAnAM brahmaprabhavatvaM siddhaM bhavati | tathA hi -- asminn eva prakaraNe tejo.abannapUrvakatvaM vAkprANamanasAm AmnAyate -- annamayaM hi somya mana ApomayaH prANaH tejomayI vAk iti | tatra yadi tAvanmukhyam evaiShAm annAdimayatvam, tato vartata eva brahmaprabhavatvam | atha bhAktam, tathApi brahmakartR^ikAyAM nAmarUpavyAkriyAyAM shravaNAt, yenAshrutaM shrutaM bhavati [chA.u. 6.1.3] iti copakramAt aitadAtmyam idaM sarvam iti copasaMhArAt, shrutyantaraprasiddhishca brahmakAryatvaprapaJNcanArtham eva manaAdInAm annAdimayatvavacanam iti gamyate | tasmAd api prANAnAM brahmavikAratvasiddhiH ||4||

 -- o)0(o -- 

2. saptagatyadhikaraNam

|| 2.4.5 ||

sapta gater visheShitatvAcca ||

utpattiviShayaH shrutivipratiShedhaH prANAnAM parihR^itaH | saMkhyAviShaya idAnIM parihriyate | tatra mukhyaM prANam upariShTAd vakShyati | samprati tu kati itare prANA iti sampradhArayati | shrutivipratipatteshcAtra viShayaH | kvacit sapta prANAH saN^kIrtyante -- sapta prANAH prabhavanti tasmAt [mu.u. 2.1.8] iti | kvacid aShTau prANA grahatvena guNena saN^kIrtyante -- aShTau grahA aShTAvatigrahAH [bR^i.A.u. 3.1.1] iti | kvacin nava -- sapta vai shIrShiNyAH prANA dvAvavAJNcau  iti | kvacid dasha -- nava vai puruShe prANA nAbhir dashamI iti | kvacid ekAdasha -- dasheme puruShe prANA AtmaikAdashaH [bR^i.A.u. 3.9.4] iti | kvacid dvAdasha -- sarveShAM sparshAnAM tvag ekAyanam ityatra | kvacit trayodasha -- cakShushca draShTavyaM ca ityatra -- evaM hi vipratipannAH prANeyattAM prati shrutayaH | kiM tAvat prAptam ? saptaiva prANA iti | kutaH? gateH | yataH tAvanto.avagamyante sapta prANAH prabhavanti tasmAt ityevaMvidhAsu shrutiShu, visheShitAshcaite sapta vai shIrShiNyAH prANAH ityatra | 

nanu prANA guhAshayA nihitAH sapta sapta iti vIpsA shrUyate | sA saptabhyo.atiriktAn prANAn gamayatIti -- naiSha doShaH | puruShabhedAbhiprAyeyaM vIpsA -- pratipuruShaM sapta sapta prANA iti | na tattvabhedAbhiprAyA -- sapta sapta anye.anye prANA iti | 

nanvaShTatvAdikApi saMkhyA prANeShu udAhR^itA | kathaM saptaiva syuH? satyam udAhR^itA | virodhAttvanyatamA saMkhyA adhyavasAtavyA | tatra stokakalpanAnurodhAt saptasaMkhyAdhyavasAnam | vR^ittibhedApekShaM ca saMkhyAntarashravaNam iti manyate ||5|| 

|| 2.4.6 || 

atrocyate -- 

hastAdayaH tu sthite.ato naivam || 

hastAdayaH tu apare saptabhyo.atiriktAH prANAH shrUyante -- hastau vai grahaH sa karmaNAtigraheNa gR^ihIto hastAbhyAM hi karma karoti [bR^i.A.u. 3.2.8] ityevamAdyAsu shrutiShu | sthite ca saptatvAtireke saptatvam antarbhAvAcchakyate sambhAvayitum | hInAdhikasaMkhyAvipratipattau hi adhikA saMkhyA saMgrAhyA bhavati | tasyAM hInA antar bhavati, na tu hInAyAm adhikA | atashca naivaM mantavyam -- stokakalpanAnurodhAt saptaiva prANAH syuH iti | uttarasaMkhyAnurodhAt tu ekAdashaiva te prANAH syuH | tathA ca udAhR^itA shrutiH -- dasheme puruShe prANA AtmaikAdashaH [bR^i.A.u. 3.9.4] iti | Atmashabdena ca atra antaHkaraNaM parigR^ihyate, karaNAdhikArAt | 

nanv ekAdashatvAd apyadhike dvAdashatrayodashatve udAhR^ite -- satyam udAhR^ite | na tv ekAdashabhyaH kAryajAtebhyo.adhikaM kAryajAtam asti, yadartham adhikaM karaNaM kalpyeta | shabdasparsharUparasagandhaviShayAH paJNca buddhibhedAH, tadarthAni paJNca buddhIndriyANi | vacanAdAnaviharaNotsargAnandAH paJNca karmabhedAH, tadarthAni ca paJNca karmendriyANi | sarvArthaviShayaM traikAlyavR^itti manaH tu ekam anekavR^ittikam | tad eva vR^ittibhedAt kvacid bhinnavad vyapadishyate -- mano buddhir ahaMkArashcittaM ceti | tathA ca shrutiH kAmAdyA nAnAvidhA vR^ittIr anukramyAha -- etat sarvaM mana eva iti | api ca saptaiva shIrShaNyAn prANAn abhimanyamAnasya catvAra eva prANA abhimatAH syuH | sthAnabhedAd dhyete catvAraH santaH sapta gaNyante -- dve shrotre dve cakShuShI dve nAsike ekA vAk iti | 

na ca tAvatAm eva vR^ittibhedA itare prANA iti shakyate vaktum, hastAdivR^ittInAm atyantavijAtIyatvAt | tathA nava vai puruShe prANA nAbhir dashamI ityatrApi dehacchidrabhedAbhiprAyeNaiva dasha prANA ucyante, na prANatattvabhedAbhiprAyeNa, nAbhir dashamI iti vacanAt | na hi nAbhir nAma kashcit prANaH prasiddho.asti | mukhyasya tu prANasya bhavati nAbhir apyekaM visheShAyatanam iti -- ato nAbhir dashamI ityucyate | kvacid upAsanArthaM katicit prANA gaNyante, kvacit pradarshanArtham | tad evaM vicitre prANeyattAmnAne sati, kva kiM param AmnAnam iti vivektavyam | kAryajAtavashAt tv ekAdashatvAmnAnaM prANaviShayaM pramANam iti sthitam || 

iyam aparA sUtradvayayojanA -- saptaiva prANAH syuH, yataH saptAnAm eva gatiH shrUyate -- tam utkrAmantaM prANo.anUtkrAmati prANam anUtkrAmantaM sarve prANA anUtkrAmanti [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.2] ityatra | 

nanu sarvashabdo.atra paThyate, tat kathaM saptAnAm eva gatiH pratij~nAyata iti | visheShitatvAd ityAha -- saptaiva hi prANAshcakShurAdayaH tvakparyantA visheShitA iha prakR^itAH sa yatraiva cAkShuShaH puruShaH parAN^ paryAvartate.athArUpaj~no bhavati ekIbhavati na pashyatItyAhuH ityevamAdinA anukramaNena | prakR^itagAmI ca sarvashabdo bhavati | yathA sarve brAhmaNA bhojayitavyA iti ye nimantritAH prakR^itA brAhmaNAH ta eva sarvashabdenocyante, nAnye | evam ihApi ye prakR^itAH sapta prANAH ta eva sarvashabdenocyante, nAnya iti | 

nanvatra vij~nAnam aShTamam anukrAntam | kathaM saptAnAm evAnukramaNam? naiSha doShaH | manovij~nAnayoH tattvAbhedAd vR^ittibhede.api saptatvopapatteH | tasmAt saptaiva prANA iti -- evaM prApte, brUmaH -- hastAdayaH tu apare saptabhyo.atiriktAH prANAH pratIyante hastau vai grahaH [bR^i.A.u. 3.2.8] ityAdi shrutiShu | grahatvaM ca bandhanabhAvaH, gR^ihyate badhyate kShetraj~no.anena grahasaMj~nakena bandhaneneti | sa ca kShetraj~no naikasminn eva sharIre badhyate, sharIrAntareShvapi tulyatvAd bandhanasya | tasmAccharIrAntarasaMcAri idaM grahasaMj~nakaM bandhanam ityarthAd uktaM bhavati | tathA ca smR^itiH -- 

puryaShTakena liN^gena prANAdyena sa yujyate | 
tena baddhasya vai bandho mokSho muktasya tena ca || iti |

prAN^mokShAt grahasaMj~nakena bandhanena aviyogaM darshayati | AtharvaNe ca viShayendriyAnukramaNe cakShushca draShTavyaM ca ityatra tulyavad dhastAdInIndriyANi saviShayANyanukrAmati -- hastau cAdAtavyaM copasthashcAnandayitavyaM ca pAyushca visarjayitavyaM ca pAdau ca gantavyaM ca iti | tathA dasheme puruShe prANA AtmaikAdashaH te yadAsmAccharIrAn martyAd utkrAmantyatha rodayanti [bR^i.A.u. 3.9.4] ityekAdashAnAM prANAnAm utkrAntir darshayati | sarvashabdo.api ca prANashabdena sambadhyamAno.asheShAn prANAn abhidadhAno na prakaraNavashena saptasv evAvasthApayituM shakyate, prakaraNAcchabdasya balIyastvAt | sarve brAhmaNA bhojayitavyAH ityatrApi sarveShAm eva avanivartinAM brAhmaNAnAM grahaNaM nyAyyam, sarvashabdasAmarthyAt | sarvabhojanAsambhavAt tu tatra nimantritamAtraviShayA sarvashabdasya vR^ittir AshritA | iha tu na kiMcit sarvashabdArthasaMkocane kAraNam asti | tasmAt sarvashabdena atra asheShANAM prANAnAM parigrahaH | pradarshanArthaM ca saptAnAm anukramaNam ityanavadyam | tasmAd ekAdashaiva prANAH -- shabdataH kAryatashceti siddham ||6||

 -- o)0(o -- 
3. prANANutvAdhikaraNam 

|| 2.4.7 || 

aNavashca || 

adhunA prANAnAm eva svabhAvAntaram abhyuccinoti | aNavashcaite prakR^itAH prANAH pratipattavyAH | aNutvaM caiShAM saukShmyaparicchedau, na paramANutulyatvam, kR^itsnadehavyApikAryAnupapattiprasaN^gAt -- sUkShmA ete prANAH, sthUlAshcet syuH -- maraNakAle sharIrAn nirgacchantaH, bilAd ahiH iva, upalabhyeran mriyamANasya pArshvasthaiH | paricchinnAshcaite prANAH, sarvagatAshcet syuH -- utkrAntigatyAgatishrutivyAkopaH syAt, tadguNasAratvaM ca jIvasya na sidhyet | sarvagatAnAm api vR^ittilAbhaH sharIradeshe syAd iti cet, na, vR^ittimAtrasya karaNatvopapatteH | yad eva hi upalabdhisAdhanam -- vR^ittiH anyad vA -- tasyaiva naH karaNatvam, saMj~nAmAtre vivAdaH iti karaNAnAM vyApitvakalpanA nirarthikA | tasmAt sUkShmAH paricchinnAshca prANA ityadhyavasyAmaH ||7||

 -- o)0(o -- 
4. prANashraiShThyAdhikaraNam

|| 2.4.8 || 

shreShThashca ||

mukhyashca prANa itaraprANavad brahmavikAraH -- ityatidishati | tacca avisheSheNaiva sarvaprANAnAM brahmavikAratvam AkhyAtam -- etasmAjjAyate prANo manaH sarvendriyANi ca [mu.u. 2.1.3] iti sendriyamanovyatirekeNa prANasyotpattishravaNAt, sa prANam asR^ijata ityAdi shravaNebhyashca | kimarthaH punar atideshaH? adhikAshaN^kAvAraNArthaH -- nAsadAsIye hi brahmapradhAne sUkte mantravarNo bhavati -- 

na mR^ityur AsId amR^itaM na tarhi 
na rAtryA ahna AsIt praketaH | 
AnId avAtaM svadhayA tad ekaM 
tasmAd dhAnyanna paraH kiMca nAsa || [R^igveda 8.7.17] iti | 

AnIt iti prANakarmopAdAnAt prAgutpatteH santam iva prANaM sUcayati | tasmAd ajaH prANa iti jAyate kasyacin matiH | tAm atideshenApanudati | AnIcchabdo.api na prAgutpatteH prANasadbhAvaM sUcayati, avAtam iti visheShaNAt, aprANo hyamanAH shubhraH [mu.u. 2.1.2] iti ca mUlaprakR^iteH prANAdisamastavisheSharahitatvasya darshitatvAt | tasmAt kAraNasadbhAvapradarshanArtha evAyam AnIcchabda iti | shreShThaH iti ca mukhyaM prANam abhidadhAti, prANo vAva jyeShThashca shreShThashca iti shrutinirdeshAt | jyeShThashca prANaH, shukraniShekakAlAd Arabhya tasya vR^ittilAbhAt -- na cet tasya tadAnIM vR^ittilAbhaH syAt, yonau niShiktaM shukraM pUyeta, na sambhaved vA | shrotrAdInAM tu karNashaShkulyAdisthAnavibhAganiShpattau vR^ittilAbhAn na jyeShThatvam | shreShThashca prANaH, guNAdhikyAt, na vai shakShyAmaH tvadR^ite jIvitum iti shruteH ||8||

 -- o)0(o -- 
5. vAyukriyAdhikaraNam ||

|| 2.4.9 || 

na vAyukriye pR^ithagupadeshAt ||

sa punar mukhyaH prANaH kiMsvarUpaH ? itIdAnIM jij~nAsyate | tatra prAptaM tAvat -- shruteH vAyuH prANa iti | evaM hi shrUyate -- yaH prANaH sa vAyuH sa eSha vAyuH paJNcavidhaH prANo.apAno vyAna udAnaH samAnaH [bR^i.A.u. 3.1.5] iti | athavA tantrAntarIyAbhiprAyAt samastakaraNavR^ittiH prANa iti prAptam | evaM hi tantrAntarIyA AcakShate -- sAmAnyA karaNavR^ittiH prANAdyA vAyavaH paJNceti || 

atrocyate -- na vAyuH prANaH, nApi karaNavyApAraH | kutaH? pR^ithagupadeshAt | vAyoH tAvat prANasya pR^ithagupadesho bhavati -- prANa eva brahmaNashcaturthaH pAdaH sa vAyunA jyotiShA bhAti ca tapati ca iti | na hi vAyur eva san vAyoH pR^ithag upadishyeta | tathA karaNavR^itter api pR^ithagupadesho bhavati, vAgAdIni karaNAnyanukramya tatra tatra pR^ithakprANasyAnukramaNAt, vR^ittivR^ittimator abhedAt | na hi karaNavyApAra eva san karaNebhyaH pR^ithag upadishyeta | tathA etasmAjjAyate prANo manaH sarvendriyANi ca | khaM vAyuH [mu.u. 2.1.3] ityevamAdayo.api vAyoH karaNebhyashca prANasya pR^ithagupadeshA anusartavyAH | na ca samastAnAM karaNAnAm ekA vR^ittiH sambhavati, pratyekam ekaikavR^ittitvAt, samudAyasya ca akArakatvAt | 

nanu paJNjaracAlananyAyena etad bhaviShyati -- yathA ekapaJNjaravartina ekAdashapakShiNaH pratyekaM pratiniyatavyApArAH santaH sambhUya ekaM paJNjaraM cAlayanti, evam ekasharIravartina ekAdashaprANAH pratyekaM pratiniyatavR^ittayaH santaH sambhUya ekAM prANAkhyAM vR^ittiM pratilapsyanta iti | netyucyate -- yuktaM tatra -- pratyekavR^ittibhir avAntaravyApAraiH paJNjaracAlanAnurUpair evopetAH pakShiNaH sambhUya ekaM paJNjaraM cAlayeyuH iti, tathA dR^iShTatvAt | iha tu -- shravaNAdyavAntaravyApAropetAH prANA na sambhUya prANyuH iti yuktam, pramANAbhAvAt, atyantavijAtIyatvAcca shravaNAdibhyaH prANanasya | tathA prANasya shreShThatvAd yuddhoShaNam, guNabhAvopagamashca taM prati vAgAdInAm, na karaNavR^ittimAtre prANe.avakalpate | tasmAd anyo vAyukriyAbhyAM prANaH | kathaM tarhIyaM shrutiH -- yaH prANaH sa vAyuH iti? ucyate -- vAyur evAyam adhyAtmam ApannaH paJNcavyUho visheShAtmanAvatiShThamAnaH prANo nAma bhaNyate, na tattvAntaram, nApi vAyumAtram | atashcobhe api bhedAbhedashrutI na virudhyete ||9|| 


 || 2.4.10 || 

syAd etat -- prANo.api tarhi jIvavat asmin sharIre svAtantryaM prApnoti, shreShThatvAt, guNabhAvopagamAcca, taM prati vAgAdInAm indriyANAm | tathA hyanekavidhA vibhUtiH prANasya shrAvyate -- supteShu vAgAdiShu prANa evaiko jAgarti, prANa evaiko mR^ityunA anAptaH, prANaH saMvargo vAgAdIn saMvR^iN^kte [chA.u. 4.3.3], prANa itarAn prANAn rakShati mAteva putrAn  iti | tasmAt prANasyApi jIvavat svAtantryaprasaN^gaH | taM pariharati -- 
cakShurAdivat tu tat saha shiShTyAdibhyaH ||

tushabdaH prANasya jIvavat svAtantryaM vyAvartayati | yathA cakShurAdIni, rAjaprakR^itivat, jIvasya kartR^itvaM bhoktR^itvaM ca prati upakaraNAni, na svatantrANi | tathA mukhyo.api prANaH, rAjamantrivat, jIvasya sarvArthakaratvena upakaraNabhUtaH, na svatantraH | kutaH? tat saha shiShTyAdibhyaH | taishcakShurAdibhiH sahaiva prANaH shiShyate prANasaMvAdAdiShu | samAnadharmaNAM ca saha shAsanaM yuktaM bR^ihadrathantarAdivat | Adishabdena saMhatatvAcetanatvAdIn prANasya svAtantryanirAkaraNahetUn darshayati ||10|| 

|| 2.4.11 || 

syAd etat -- yadi cakShurAdivat prANasya jIvaM prati karaNabhAvo.abhyupagamyeta, viShayAntaraM rUpAdivat prasajyeta -- rUpAlocanAdibhir vR^ittibhir yathAsvaM cakShurAdInAM jIvaM prati karaNabhAvo bhavati | api ca ekAdashaiva kAryajAtAni rUpAlocanAdIni parigaNitAni, yadartham ekAdasha prANAH saMgR^ihItAH | na tu dvAdasham aparaM kAryajAtam avagamyate, yadartham ayaM dvAdashaH prANaH pratij~nAyata iti | ata uttaraM paThati -- 

akaraNatvAcca na doShaH tathA hi darshayati ||

na tAvad viShayAntaraprasaN^go doShaH, akaraNatvAt prANasya | na hi cakShurAdivat prANasya viShayaparicchedena karaNatvam abhyupagamyate | na cAsya etAvatA kAryAbhAva eva | kasmAt? tathA hi shrutiH prANAntareShvasambhAvyamAnaM mukhyaprANasya vaisheShikaM kAryaM darshayati prANasaMvAdAdiShu -- atha ha prANA ahaM shreyasi vyUdire [chA.u. 5.1.6] ityupakramya, yasminn utkrAnte sharIraM pApiShThataram iva dR^ishyeta sa vaH shreShThaH [chA.u. 5.1.7] iti ca upanyasya, pratyekaM vAgAdyutkramaNena tadvR^ittimAtrahInaM yathApUrvaM jIvanaM darshayitvA, prANoccikramiShAyAM vAgAdishaithilyApattiM sharIrapAtaprasaN^gaM ca darshayantI shrutiH prANanimittAM sharIrendriyasthitiM darshayati -- tAn variShThaH prANa uvAca mA moham Apad yathAham evaitat paJNcadhAtmAnaM pravibhajyaitadbANam avaShTabhya vidhArayAmi iti ca | 

etam evArthaM shrutir Aha -- prANena rakShann avaraM kulAyam [bR^i.A.u. 4.3.12] iti ca | supteShu cakShurAdiShu prANanimittAM sharIrarakShAM darshayati -- yasmAt kasmAccAN^gAt prANa utkrAmati tad eva tacchuShyati, iti tena yad ashnAti yat pibati tenetarAn prANAn avati [bR^i.A.u. 1.3.19] iti ca | prANanimittAM sharIrendriyapuShTiM darshayati -- kasmin nvaham utkrAnta utkrAnto bhaviShyAmi kasmin vA pratiShThite pratiShThAsyAmi iti, sa prANam asR^ijata... iti ca prANanimitte jIvasyotkrAntipratiShThe darshayati ||11||

|| 2.4.12 ||

paJNcavR^ittir manovad vyapadishyate ||

itashcAsti mukhyasya prANasya vaisheShikaM kAryam, yatkAraNaM paJNcavR^ittir ayaM vyapadishyate shrutiShu -- prANo.apAno vyAna udAnaH samAnaH iti | vR^ittibhedashcAyaM kAryabhedApekShaH -- prANaH prAgvR^ittiH ucchvAsAdikarmA, apAno.avAgvR^ittir nishvAsAdikarmA, vyAnaH tayoH sandhau vartamAno vIryavatkarmahetuH, udAnaH UrdhvavR^ittir utkrAntyAdihetuH, samAnaH samaM sarveShvaN^geShu yo.annarasAn nayati -- ityevaM paJNcavR^ittiH prANaH, manovat -- yathA manasaH paJNca vR^ittayaH, evaM prANasyApItyarthaH | shrotrAdinimittAH shabdAdiviShayA manasaH paJNca vR^ittayaH prasiddhAH | na tu kAmaH saN^kalpaH ityAdyAH paripaThitA gR^ihyeran, paJNcasaMkhyAtirekAt | 

nanvatrApi shrotrAdinirapekShA bhUtabhaviShyadAdiviShayA aparA manaso vR^ittir astIti samAnaH paJNcasaMkhyAtirekaH | evaM tarhi paramatamapratiShiddham anumataM bhavati iti nyAyAt ihApi yogashAstraprasiddhA manasaH paJNca vR^ittayaH parigR^ihyante -- pramANaviparyayavikalpanidrAsmR^itayaH nAma | bahuvR^ittitvamAtreNa vA manaH prANasya nidarshanam iti draShTavyam | jIvopakaraNatvam api prANasya paJNcavR^ittitvAt, manovat -- iti vA yojayitavyam ||12||

 -- o)0(o -- 

shreShThANutvAdhikaraNam

|| 2.4.13 ||

aNushca ||

aNushcAyaM mukhyaH prANaH pratyetavyaH, itaraprANavat | aNutvaM ca ihApi saukShmyaparicchedau, na paramANutulyatvam, paJNcabhir vR^ittibhiH kR^itsnasharIravyApitvAt | sUkShmaH prANaH, utkrAntau pArshvasthena anupalabhyamAnatvAt | paricchinnashca, utkrAntigatyAgatishrutibhyaH | 

nanu vibhutvam api prANasya samAmnAyate -- samaH pluShiNA samo mashakena samo nAgena sama ebhiH tribhir lokaiH samo.anena sarveNa ityevamAdiShu pradesheShu | tad ucyate -- Adhidaivikena samaShTivyaShTirUpeNa hairaNyagarbheNa prANAtmanaiva etadvibhutvam AmnAyate, nAdhyAtmikena | api ca samaH pluShiNA ityAdinA sAmyavacanena pratiprANivartinaH prANasya pariccheda eva pradarshyate | tasmAd adoShaH ||13||

 -- o)0(o -- 


jyotirAdyadhikaraNam 

|| 2.4.14 || 

te punaH prakR^itAH prANAH kiM svamahimnaiva svasmai svasmai kAryAya prabhavanti, Aho svid devatAdhiShThitAH prabhavanti iti vicAryate | tatra prAptaM tAvat -- yathAsvaM kAryashaktiyogAt svamahimnaiva prANAH pravarterann iti | api ca devatAdhiShThitAnAM prANAnAM pravR^ittAvabhyugamyamAnAyAM tAsAm evAdhiShThAtNAM devatAnAM bhoktR^itvaprasaN^gAt shArIrasya bhoktR^itvaM pralIyeta | ataH svamahimnaiva eShAM pravR^ittiH iti | evaM prApte -- 

jyotirAdyadhiShThAnaM tu tadAmananAt || 

tushabdena pUrvapakSho vyAvartyate | jyotirAdibhir agnyAdyabhimAninIbhir devatAbhir adhiShThitaM vAgAdikaraNajAtaM svakAryeShu pravartata iti pratijAnIte | hetuM ca vyAcaShThe -- tadAmananAd iti | tathA hi Amananti -- agnir vAg bhUtvA mukhaM prAvishat ityAdi | agneshcAyaM vAgbhAvo mukhapraveshashca devatAtmanA adhiShThAtR^itvam aN^gIkR^itya ucyate | na hi devatAsambandhaM pratyAkhyAya agneH vAci mukhe vA kashcid visheShasambandho dR^ishyate | tathA vAyuH prANo bhUtvA nAsike prAvishat ityevam Adyapi yojayitavyam | tathA anyatrApi vAg eva brahmaNashcaturthaH pAdaH so.agninA jyotiShA bhAti ca tapati ca ityevamAdinA vAgAdInAm agnyAdijyotiShTavAdivacanena etam evArthaM draDhayati | sa vai vAcam eva prathamAm atyavahat sA yadA mR^ityum atyamucyata so.agnir abhavat iti ca evamAdinA vAgAdInAm agnyAdibhAvApattivacanena etam evArthaM dyotayati | sarvatra ca adhyAtmAdhidaivatavibhAgena vAgAdyagnyAdyanukramaNam anayaiva pratyAsattyA bhavati | smR^itAvapi -- 

vAg adhyAtmam iti prAhur brAhmaNAH tattvadarshinaH | 
vaktavyam adhibhUtaM tu vahniH tatrAdhidaivatam || 

ityAdinA vAgAdInAm agnyAdidevatAdhiShThitatvaM saprapaJNcaM pradarshitam | yad uktam -- svakAryashaktiyogAt svamahimnaiva prANAH pravarterann iti, tad ayuktam, shaktAnAm api shakaTAdInAm anaDuhAdyadhiShThitAnAM pravR^ittidarshanAt | ubhayathopapattau ca AgamAt vAgAdInAM devatAdhiShThitatvam eva nishcIyate ||14|| 

|| 2.4.15 ||

yad apyuktam -- devatAnAm evAdhiShThAtrINAM bhoktR^itvaprasaN^gaH, na shArIrasyeti, tat parihriyate -- 

prANavatA shabdAt || 

satIShvapi prANAnAm adhiShThAtrIShu devatAsu prANavatA kAryakaraNasaMghAtasvAminA shArIreNaiva eShAM prANAnAM sambandhaH shruter avagamyate | tathA hi shrutiH -- atha yatraitad AkAsham anu viShaNNaM cakShuH sa cAkShuShaH puruSho darshanAya cakShur atha yo vededaM jighrANIti sa AtmA gandhAya ghrANam ityevaMjAtIyakA shArIreNaiva prANAnAM sambandhaM shrAvayati | api ca anekatvAt pratikaraNam adhiShThAtrINAM devatAnAM na bhoktR^itvam asmin sharIre.avakalpate | eko hyayam asmin sharIre shArIro bhoktA pratisandhAnAdisambhavAd avagamyate ||15||

|| 2.4.16 ||

tasya ca nityatvAt || 

tasya ca shArIrasyAsmin sharIre bhoktR^itvena nityatvam -- puNyapApopalepasambhavAt sukhaduHkhopabhogasambhavAcca, na devatAnAm | tA hi parasminn aishvarye pade.avatiShThamAnA na hIne.asmin sharIre bhoktR^itvaM pratilabdhum arhanti | shrutishca bhavati -- puNyam evAmuM gacchati na ha vai devAn pApaM gacchati iti | shArIreNaiva ca nityaH prANAnAM sambandhaH, utkrAntyAdiShu tadanuvR^ittidarshanAt -- tam utkrAmantaM prANo.anUtkrAmati prANam anUtkrAmantaM sarve prANA anUtkrAmanti [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.2] ityAdi shrutibhyaH | tasmAt satIShvapi karaNAnAM niyantrIShu devatAsu na shArIrasya bhoktR^itvam apagacchati | karaNapakShasyaiva hi devatA, na bhoktR^ipakShasyeti ||16||

 -- o)0(o -- 

10. indriyAdhikaraNam 

|| 2.4.17 ||

mukhyashcaikaH itare caikAdasha prANA anukrAntAH | tatredam aparaM sandihyate -- kiM mukhyasyaiva prANasya vR^ittibhedA itare prANAH, Aho svit tattvAntarANIti | kiM tAvat prAptam -- mukhyasyaivetare vR^ittibhedA iti | kutaH? shruteH | tathA hi shrutiH mukhyam itarAMshca prANAn saMnidhApya, mukhyAtmatAm itareShAM khyApayati -- hantAsyaiva sarve rUpam asAmeti ta etasyaiva sarve rUpam abhavan iti | prANaikashabdatvAcca ekatvAd hyavasAyaH | itarathA hyanyAyyam anekArthatvaM prANashabdasya prasajyeta, ekatra vA mukhyasyetaratra lAkShaNikatvam Apadyeta | tasmAd yathaikasyaiva prANasya prANAdyAH paJNca vR^ittayaH, evaM vAgAdyA apyekAdasheti | evaM prApte -- 

ta indriyANi tadvyapadeshAd anyatra shreShThAt ||

brUmaH -- tattvAntarANyeva prANAd vAgAdInIti | kutaH? vyapadeshabhedAt | ko.ayaM vyapadeshabhedaH? te prakR^itAH prANAH, shreShThaM varjayitvA avashiShTA ekAdashendriyANItyucyante, shrutAvevaM vyapadeshabhedadarshanAt -- etasmAjjAyate prANo manaH sarvendriyANi ca [mu.u. 2.1.3] iti hyevaMjAtIyakeShu pradesheShu pR^ithak prANo vyapadishyate, pR^ithak ca indriyANi | 

nanu manaso.apyevaM sati varjanam indriyatvena, prANavat, syAt -- manaH sarvendriyANi ca iti pR^ithag vyapadeshadarshanAt | satyam etat -- smR^itau tu ekAdashendriyANIti mano.api indriyatvena shrotrAdivat saMgR^ihyate | prANasya tu indriyatvaM na shrutau smR^itau vA prasiddham asti | vyapadeshabhedashcAyaM tattvabhedapakShe upapadyate | tattvaikatve tu, sa evaikaH san prANa indriyavyapadeshaM labhate na labhate ca -- iti vipratiShiddham | tasmAt tattvAntarabhUtA mukhyAd itare ||17|| 

|| 2.4.18 ||

kutashca tattvAntarabhUtAH? -- 

bhedashruteH || 

bhedena vAgAdibhyaH prANaH sarvatra shrUyate -- te ha vAcam UcuH ityupakramya, vAgAdIn asurapApmavidhvastAn upanyasya, upasaMhR^itya vAgAdiprakaraNam, atha hemamAsanyaM prANam UcuH ityasuravidhvaMsino mukhyasya prANasya pR^ithagupakramaNAt | tathA mano vAcaM prANaM tAnyAtmane.akuruta ityevamAdyA api bhedashrutaya udAhartavyAH | tasmAd api tattvAntarabhUtA mukhyAd itare ||18|| 

|| 2.4.19 ||

kutashca tattvAntarabhUtAH? -- 

vailakShaNyAcca ||

vailakShaNyaM ca bhavati, mukhyasya itareShAM ca -- supteShu vAgAdiShu mukhya eko jAgarti | sa eva ca eko mR^ityunA anAptaH, AptAH tvitare, tasyaiva ca sthityutkrAntibhyAM dehadhAraNapatanahetutvam, na indriyANAm | viShayAlocanahetutvaM ca indriyANAm, na prANasya -- ityevaMjAtIyako bhUyAMl lakShaNabhedaH prANendriyANAm | tasmAd apyeShAM tattvAntarabhAvasiddhiH | yad uktam -- ta etasyaiva sarve rUpam abhavan iti shruteH prANa evendriyANIti, tad ayuktam, tatrApi paurvAparyAlocanAd bhedapratIteH | tathA hi -- vadiShyAmyevAham iti vAg dadhre iti vAgAdInIndriyANyanukramya, tAni mR^ityuH shramo bhUtvopayeme tasmAccharamyatyeva vAk iti ca shramarUpeNa mR^ityunA grastatvaM vAgAdInAm abhidhAya, athemam eva nApnodyo.ayaM madhyamaH prANaH iti pR^ithak prANaM mR^ityunA anabhibhUtaM tam anukrAmati | ayaM vai naH shreShThaH iti ca shreShThatAm asyAvadhArayati, tasmAt tadavirodhena, vAgAdiShu parispandalAbhasya prANAyattatvam -- tadrUpabhavanaM vAgAdInAm -- iti mantavyam, na tu tAdAtmyam | ata eva ca prANashabdasyendriyeShu lAkShaNikatvasiddhiH | tathA ca shrutiH -- ta etasyaiva sarve rUpam abhavan | tasmAd eta etenAkhyAyante prANAH iti mukhyaprANaviShayasyaiva prANashabdasyendriyeShu lAkShaNikIM vR^ittiM darshayati | tasmAt tattvAntarANi prANAt vAgAdIni indriyANIti ||19||

saMj~nAmUrtikptyadhikaraNam 

|| 2.4.20 ||

satprakriyAyAM tejo.abannAnAM sR^iShTim abhidhAyopadishyate -- 

seyaM devataikShata hantAham imAH tisro devatA anena jIvenAtmanAnupravishya nAmarUpe vyAkaravANIti | tAsAM trivR^itaM trivR^itam ekaikAM karavANi [chA.u. 6.3.23] iti |

tatra saMshayaH -- kiM jIvakartR^ikam idaM nAmarUpavyAkaraNam, Aho svit parameshvarakartR^ikam iti | tatra prAptaM tAvat -- jIvakartR^ikam evedaM nAmarUpavyAkaraNam iti | kutaH? anena jIvenAtmanA iti visheShaNAt -- yathA loke cAreNAhaM parasainyam anupravishya saMkalayAni ityevaMjAtIyake prayoge, cArakartR^ikam eva sat sainyasaMkalanaM hetukartR^itvAt rAjA Atmanyad hyAropayati saMkalayAnItyuttamapuruShaprayogeNa | evaM jIvakartR^ikam eva sat nAmarUpavyAkaraNaM hetukartR^itvAt devatA Atmanyad hyAropayati vyAkaravANItyuttamapuruShaprayogeNa | api ca DitthaDAvitthAdiShu nAmasu ghaTasharAvAdiShu ca rUpeShu jIvasyaiva vyAkartR^itvaM dR^iShTAm | tasmAjjIvakartR^ikam evedaM nAmarUpavyAkaraNam ityevaM prApte -- 

saMj~nAmUrtikptiH tu trivR^it kurvata upadeshAt ||

abhidhatte -- saMj~nAmUrtikptiH tviti | tushabdena pakShaM vyAvartayati | saMj~nAmUrtikptiH iti -- nAmarUpavyAkriyetyetat | trivR^it kurvata iti parameshvaraM lakShayati, trivR^itkaraNe tasya nirapavAdakartR^itvanirdeshAt -- yeyaM saMj~nAkptiH mUrtikptishca, agniH AdityaH candramAH vidyud iti, tathA kushakAshapalAshAdiShu pashumR^igamanuShyAdiShu ca, pratyAkR^iti prativyakti ca anekaprakArA, sA khalu parameshvarasyaiva tejo.abannAnAM nirmAtuH kR^itir bhavitum arhati | kutaH? upadeshAt | tathA hi -- seyaM devatA ityupakramya vyAkaravANi ityuttamapuruShaprayogeNa parasyaiva brahmaNo vyAkartR^itvam ihopadishyate | 

nanu jIvena iti visheShaNAt jIvakR^irtR^ikatvaM vyAkaraNasyAdhyavasitam -- naitad evam | jIvena ityetat anupravishya ityanena sambadhyate, AnantaryAt | na vyAkaravANi ityanena -- tena hi sambandhe vyAkaravANi ityayaM devatAviShaya uttamapuruSha aupacArikaH kalpyeta | na ca girinadIsamudrAdiShu nAnAvidheShu nAmarUpeShu anIshvarasya jIvasya vyAkaraNasAmarthyam asti | yeShvapi ca asti sAmarthyam, teShvapi parameshvarAyattam eva tat | na ca jIvo nAma parameshvarAd atyantabhinnaH -- cAra iva rAj~naH, AtmanA iti visheShaNAt, upAdhimAtranibandhanatvAcca jIvabhAvasya | tena tatkR^itam api nAmarUpavyAkaraNaM parameshvarakR^itam eva bhavati | parameshvara eva ca nAmarUpayor vyAkarteti sarvopaniShatsiddhAntaH, AkAsho ha vai nAma nAmarUpayor nirvahitA ityAdishrutibhyaH | tasmAt parameshvarasyaiva trivR^itkurvataH karma nAmarUpavyAkaraNam | trivR^itkaraNapUrvakam evedam iha nAmarUpavyAkaraNaM vivakShyate, pratyekaM nAmarUpavyAkaraNasya tejo.abannotpattivacanenaivoktatvAt | tacca trivR^itkaraNam agnyAdityacandravidyutsu shrutir darshayati -- yad agne rohitaM rUpaM tejasaH tad rUpaM yacchuklaM tad apAM yat kR^iShNaM tad annasya ityAdinA | tatrAgniH iti idaM rUpaM vyAkriyate, sati ca rUpavyAkaraNe viShayapratilambhAd agniH iti idaM nAma vyAkriyate |
 
evam evAdityacandravidyutsvapi draShTavyam | anena ca agnyAdyudAharaNena bhaumAmbhasataijaseShu triShvapi dravyeShvavisheSheNa trivR^itkaraNam uktaM bhavati, upakramopasaMhArayoH sAdhAraNatvAt | tathA hi --  avisheSheNaiva upakramaH -- imAH tisro devatAH trivR^it trivR^id ekaikA bhavati iti, avisheSheNaiva ca upasaMhAraH -- yad u rohitam ivAbhUd iti tejasaH tad rUpam ityevamAdiH, yad vavij~nAtam ivAbhUd ityetAsAm eva devatAnAM samAsaH ityevam antaH || 

|| 2.4.21 ||

tAsAM tisR^iNAM devatAnAm, bahiH trivR^itkR^itAnAM satInAm, adhyAtmam aparaM trivR^itkaraNam uktam -- imAH tisro devatAH puruShaM prApya trivR^it trivR^id ekaikA bhavati iti | tad idAnIm AcAryo yathAshrutyevopadarshayati, AshaN^kitaM kaMcid doShaM parihariShyan -- 

mAMsAdi bhaumaM yathAshabdam itarayoshca || 

bhUmeH trivR^itkR^itAyAH puruSheNopabhujyamAnAyA mAMsAdikAryaM yathAshabdaM niShpadyate | tathA hi shrutiH -- annam ashitaM tredhA vidhIyate tasya yaH sthaviShTho dhAtuH tatpurIShaM bhavati yo madhyamaH tan mAMsaM yo.aNiShThaH tan manaH iti | trivR^itkR^itA bhUmir evaiShA vrIhiyavAdyannarUpeNa adyata ityabhiprAyaH | tasyAshca sthaviShThaM rUpaM purIShabhAvena bahir nirgacchati | madhyamam adhyAtmaM mAMsaM vardhayati | aNiShThaM tu manaH | evam itarayor aptejasor yathAshabdaM kAryam avagantavyam -- mUtraM lohitaM prANashca apAM kAryam, asthi majjA vAk tejasa iti ||21|| 

|| 2.4.22 ||

atrAha -- yadi sarvam eva trivR^itkR^itaM bhUtabhautikam, avisheShashruteH -- tAsAM trivR^itaM trivR^itam ekaikAm akarot iti, kiMkR^itaH tarhyayaM visheShavyapadeshaH -- idaM tejaH, imA ApaH, idam annam iti? tathA adhyAtmam -- idam annasyAshitasya kAryaM mAMsAdi, idam apAM pItAnAM kAryaM lohitAdi, idaM tejaso.ashitasya kAryam asthyAdi iti? atrocyate -- 

vaisheShyAt tu tadvAdaH tadvAdaH ||

tushabdena coditaM doSham apanudati | visheShasya bhAvo vaisheShyam, bhUyastvam iti yAvat | satyapi trivR^itkaraNe kvacit kasyacid bhUtadhAtor bhUyastvam upalabhyate -- agneH tejobhUyastvam, udakasyAbbhUyastvam, pR^ithivyA annabhUyastvam iti | vyavahAraprasiddhyarthaM cedaM trivR^itkaraNam | vyavahArashca trivR^itkR^itarajjuvad ekatvApattau satyAm, na bhedena bhUtatrayagocaro lokasya prasidhyet | tasmAt satyapi trivR^itkaraNe vaisheShyAd eva tejo.abannavisheShavAdo bhUtabhautikaviShaya upapadyate | tadvAdaH tadvAdaH iti padAbhyAso.adhyAyaparisamAptiM dyotayati ||22||

iti shrImatparamahaMsaparivrAjakAcAryasya shrIgovindabhagavatpUjyapAdashiShyasya shrImacchaN^karabhagavataH kR^itau 
shArIrakamImAMsAsUtrabhAShye dvitIyo.adhyAyaH || 
|| 2.4 ||
 
(3)
|| tR^itIyo.adhyAyaH || 

(3.1)
|| prathamaH pAdaH ||

tR^itIye sAdhanAkhyAdhyAye prathamapAde 
gatyAgaticintAvairAgyanirUpaNavicArashca ||

1. tadantarapratipattyadhikaraNam

|| 3.1.1 ||

dvitIye.adhyAye smR^itinyAyavirodho vedAntavihite brahmadarshane parihR^itaH | parapakShANAM cAnapekShatvaM prapaJNcitaM | shrutivipratiShedhashca parihR^itaH | tatra ca jIvavyatiriktAni tattvAni jIvopakaraNAni brahmaNo jAyanta ityuktam | athedAnIm upakaraNopahitasya jIvasya saMsAragatiprakAraH tadavasthAntarANi brahmasatattvaM vidyAbhedAbhedau guNopasaMhArAnupasaMhArau samyagdarshanAt puruShArthasiddhiH samyagdarshanopAyavidhiprabhedo muktiphalAniyamashceti | etad arthajAtaM tR^itIye.adhyAye nirUpayiShyate prasaN^gAgataM ca kim apyanyat | tatra prathame tAvat pAde paJNcAgnividyAm  Ashritya saMsAragatiprabhedaH pradarshyate vairAgyahetoH | tasmAjjugupset iti cAnte shravaNAt | jIvo mukhyuaprANasacivaH sendriyaH samanasko.avidyAkarmapUrvapraj~nAparigrahaH pUrvadehaM vihAya dehAntaraM pratipadyata ityetad avagatam | athainam ete prANA abhisamAyanti [bR^i.A.u 4.4.1] ityevam AdeH anyan navataraM kalyANataraM rUpaM kurute [bR^i.A.u 4.4.4] ityevam antAt saMsAraprakaraNasthAcchabdAt | dharmAdharmaphalopabhogasambhavAcca | sa kiM dehabIjair bhUtasUkShmair asampariShvakto gacchatyAho svit sampariShvakta iti cintyate | 

kiM tAvat prAptam ? asampariShvakta iti | kutaH ? karaNopAdAnavad bhUtopAdAnasyAshrutatvAt | sa etAH tejomAtrAH [bR^i.A.u 4.4.1] iti hyatra tejomAtrAshabdena karaNAnAM upAdAnaM saN^kIrtayati | vAkyasheShe cakShurAdisaN^kIrtanAt | naivaM bhUtamAtropAdAnasaN^kIrtanam asti | sulabhAshca sarvatra bhUtamAtrAH | yatraiva deha ArabdhavyaH tatraiva santi, tatashca tAsAM nayanaM niShprayojanam | tasmAd asampariShvakto yAtIti | evaM prApte paThatyAcAryaH -- 

tadantara pratipattau raMhati sampariShvaktaH prashnanirUpaNAbhyAm |

tadantarapratipattau dehAntarapratipattau, dehabIjair bhUtasUkShmaiH sampariShvaktaH, raMhati gacchati ityavagantavyam | kutaH? prashnanirUpaNAbhyAm | tathA hi prashnaH -- vettha yathA paJNcamyAm AhutAvapaH puruShavacaso bhavanti [chA.u. 5.3.3] iti | nirUpaNaM ca prativacanam, dyuparjanyapR^ithivIpuruShayoShitsu paJNcasvagniShu shraddhAsomavR^iShTyannaretorUpAH paJNca AhutIr darshayitvA, -- iti tu paJNcamyAm AhutAvapaH puruShavacaso bhavanti [chA.u. 5.9.1] iti | tasmAd adbhiH pariveShTito jIvo raMhati vrajatIti gamyate | 

nanvanyA shrutiH jalUkAvat pUrvadehaM na muJNcati yAvan na dehAntaram AkramatIti darshayati -- tad yathA tR^iNajalAyukA iti | tatrApyappariveShTitasyaiva jIvasya karmopasthApitapratipattavyadehaviShayabhAvanAdIrghIbhAvamAtraM jalUkayopamIyata ityavirodhaH | evaM shrutyukte dehAntarapratipattiprakAre sati, yAH puruSham atiprabhavAH kalpanAH -- vyApinAM karaNAnAm Atmanashca dehAntarapratipattau karmavashAd vR^ittilAbhaH tatra bhavati, -- kevalasyaivAtmano vR^ittilAbhaH tatra bhavati, indriyANi tu dehavad abhinavAnyeva tatra tatra bhogasthAne utpadyante, -- mana eva vA kevalaM bhogasthAnam abhipratiShThate, -- jIva eva vA utplutya dehAd dehAntaraM pratipadyate, shuka iva vR^ikShAd vR^ikShAntaram -- ityevam AdyAH, tAH sarvA eva anAdartavyAH, shrutivirodhAt ||1||

|| 3.1.2 || 

nanu udAhR^itAbhyAM prashnaprativacanAbhyAM kevalAbhir adbhiH sampariShvakto raMhatIti prApnoti, apshabdashravaNasAmarthyAt | tatra kathaM sAmAnyena pratij~nAyate -- sarvair eva bhUtasUkShmaiH sampariShvakto raMhatIti? ata uttaraM paThati --  

tryAtmakatvAt tu bhUyastvAt || 

tushabdena coditAm AshaN^kAm ucchinatti | tryAtmikA hi ApaH, trivR^itkaraNashruteH | tAsvarambhikAsvabhyupagatAsvitarad api bhUtadvayam avashyam abhyupagantavyaM bhavati | tryAtmakashca dehaH, trayANAm api tejo.abannAnAM tasmin kAryopalabdheH | punashca tryAtmakaH, tridhAtutvAt -- tribhir vAtapittashleShmabhiH | na sa bhUtAntarANi pratyAkhyAya kevalAbhir adbhir ArabdhuM shakyate | tasmAd bhUyastvApekSho.ayam -- ApaH puruShavacasaH iti -- prashnaprativacanayor apshabdaH, na kaivalyApekShaH | sarvadeheShu hi rasalohitAdidravabhUyastvaM dR^ishyate | 

nanu pArthivo dhAtur bhUyiShTho deheShUpalabhyate | naiSha doShaH -- itarApekShayA apAM bAhulyaM bhaviShyati | dR^ishyate ca shukrashoNitalakShaNe.api dehabIje dravabAhulyam | karma ca nimittakAraNaM dehAntarArambhe | karmANi ca agnihotrAdIni somAjyapayaHprabhR^itidravadravyavyapAshrayANi | karmasamavAyinyashca ApaH shraddhAshabdoditAH saha karmabhir dyulokAkhye.agnau hUyanta iti vakShyati | tasmAd apyapAM bAhulyaprasiddhiH | bAhulyAcca apshabdena sarveShAm eva dehabIjAnAM bhUtasUkShmANAm upAdAnam iti niravadyam ||2||

|| 3.1.3 || 

prANagateshca ||

prANAnAM ca dehAntarapratipattau gatiH shrAvyate -- tam utkrAmantaM prANo.anUtkrAmati prANam anUtkrAmantaM sarve prANA anUtkrAmanti [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.2] ityAdi shrutibhiH | sA ca prANAnAM gatir nAshrayam antareNa sambhavatItyataH, prANagatiprayuktA tadAshrayabhUtAnAm apAm api bhUtAntaropasR^iShTAnAM gatir arthAd avagamyate | na hi nirAshrayAH prANAH kvacid gacchanti tiShThanti vA, jIvato darshanAt ||3||

|| 3.1.4 ||

agnyAdigatishruteH iti cen na bhAktatvAt ||

syAd etat -- naiva prANA dehAntarapratipattau saha jIvena gacchanti, agnyAdigatishruteH | tathA hi shrutiH maraNakAle vAgAdayaH prANA agnyAdIn devAn gacchantIti darshayati -- yatrAsya puruShasya mR^itasyAgniM vAg apyeti vAtaM prANaH [bR^i.A.u. 3.2.13] ityAdinA iti cet, na, bhAktatvAt | vAgAdInAm agnyAdigatishrutir gauNI, lomasu kesheShu ca adarshanAt -- oShadhIr lomAni vanaspatIn keshAH iti hi tatrAmnAyate, na hi lomAni keshAshcotplutya oShadhIr vanaspatIMshca gacchantIti sambhavati | na ca jIvasya prANopAdhipratyAkhyAne gamanam avakalpate | nApi prANair vinA dehAntare upabhoga upapadyate | vispaShTaM ca prANAnAM saha jIvena gamanam anyatra shrAvitam | ato vAgAdyadhiShThAtNAm agnyAdidevatAnAM vAgAdyupakAriNInAM maraNakAle upakAranivR^ittimAtram apekShya -- vAgAdayo.agnyAdIn gacchantItyupacaryate ||4||

|| 3.1.5 || 

syAd etat -- kathaM punaH paJNcamyAm AhutAvapaH puruShavacaso bhavanti ityetat nirdhArayituM pAryate, yAvatA naiva prathame.agnAvapAM shravaNam asti? -- iha hi dyulokaprabhR^itayaH paJNcAgnyaH paJNcAnAm AhutInAm AdhAratvenAdhItAH | teShAM ca pramukhe asau vAva loko gautamAgniH [chA.u. 5.4.1] ityupanyasya, tasminn etasminn agnau devAH shraddhAM juhvati [chA.u. 5.4.2] iti shraddhA homyadravyatvena AveditA | na tatra Apo homyadravyatayA shrutAH | yadi nAma parjanyAdiShUttareShu caturShvagniShvapAM homyadravyatA parikalpyeta, parikalpyatAM nAma, teShu hotavyatayopAttAnAM somAdInAm abbahulatvopapatteH | prathame tu agnau shrutAM shraddhAM parityajya ashrutA ApaH parikalpyanta iti sAhasam etat | shraddhA ca nAma pratyayavisheShaH, prasiddhisAmarthyAt | tasmAd ayuktaH paJNcamyAm AhutAvapAM puruShabhAva iti cet -- 

prathame.ashravaNAd iti cen, na, tA eva hyupapatteH ||

naiSha doShaH | hi yataH tatrApi prathame.agnau tA evApaH shraddhAshabdenAbhipreyante | kutaH? upapatteH | evaM hyAdimadhyAvasAnasaMgAnAt anAkulam etad ekavAkyam upapadyate | itarathA punaH, paJNcamyAm Ahutau apAM puruShavacastvaprakAre pR^iShTo, prativacanAvasare prathamAhutisthAne yadyanapo homyadravyaM shraddhAM nAmAvatArayet -- tato.anyathA prashno.anyathA prativacanam ityekavAkyatA na syAt | iti tu paJNcamyAm AhutAvapaH puruShavacaso bhavanti iti ca upasaMharan etad eva darshayati | shraddhAkAryaM ca somavR^iShTyAdi sthUlIbhavadabbahulaM lakShyate | sA ca shraddhAyA aptve yuktiH | kAraNAnurUpaM hi kAryaM bhavati | na ca shraddhAkhyaH pratyayaH, manaso jIvasya vA dharmaH san dharmiNo niShkR^iShya homAyopAdAtuM shakyate -- pashvAdibhya iva hR^idayAdIni iti, Apa eva shraddhAshabdA bhaveyuH | shraddhAshabdashcApsUpapadyate, vaidikaprayogadarshanAt -- shraddhA vA ApaH iti | tanutvaM shraddhAsArUpyaM gacchanti Apo dehabIjabhUtA ityataH, shraddhAshabdAH syuH -- yathA siMhaparAkramo naraH siMhashabdo bhavati | shraddhApUrvakakarmasamavAyAcca apsu shraddhAshabda upapadyate, maJNcashabda iva puruSheShu | shraddhAhetutvAcca shraddhAshabdopapattiH, Apo hAsmai shraddhAM saMnamante puNyAya karmaNe iti shruteH ||

|| 3.1.6 ||

ashrutatvAd iti cen neShTAdikAriNAM pratIteH ||

athApi syAt -- prashnaprativacanAbhyAM nAma ApaH shraddhAdikrameNa paJNcamyAm Ahutau puruShAkAraM pratipadyeran | na tu tatsampariShvaktA jIvA raMheyuH, ashrutatvAt  -- na hyatra apAm iva jIvAnAM shrAvayitA kashcicchabdo.asti | tasmAt raMhati sampariShvaktaH ityayuktam -- iti cet, naiSha doShaH | kutaH? iShTAdikAriNAM pratIteH -- atha ya ime grAma iShTApUrte dattam ityupAsate te dhUmam abhisambhavanti [chA.u. 5.10.3] ityupakramya iShTAdikAriNAM dhUmAdinA pitR^iyANena pathA candraprAptiM kathayati -- AkAshAccandramasam eSha somo rAjA [chA.u. 5.10.4] iti | ta evehApi pratIyante, tasminn etasminn agnau devAH shraddhAM juhvati tasyA AhuteH somo rAjA sambhavati iti shrutisAmAnyAt | teShAM ca agnihotradarshapUrNamAsAdikarmasAdhanabhUtA dadhipayaHprabhR^itayo dravadravyabhUyastvAt pratyakSham eva ApaH santi | tA AhavanIye hutAH sUkShmA Ahutyo.apUrvarUpAH satyaH tAn iShTAdikAriNa Ashrayanti -- teShAM ca sharIraM naidhanena vidhAnenAntye.agnAv R^itvijo juhvati -- asau svargAya lokAya svAhA iti | tataH tAH shraddhApUrvakakarmasamavAyinya Ahutimayya Apo.apUrvarUpAH satyaH tAn iShTAdikAriNo jIvAn pariveShTya amuM lokaM phaladAnAya nayantIti yat, tad atra juhotinA abhidhIyate -- shraddhAM juhvatIti | tathA ca agnihotre ShaTprashnInirvacanarUpeNa vAkyasheSheNa te vA ete AhutI hute utkrAmataH ityevamAdinA agnihotrAhutyoH phalArambhAya lokAntaraprAptir darshitA | tasmAd AhutImayIbhir adbhiH sampariShvaktA jIvA raMhanti svakarmaphalopabhogAyeti shliShyate ||6||

|| 3.1.7 ||

kathaM punaH idam iShTAdikAriNAM svakarmaphalopabhogAya raMhaNaM pratij~nAyate, yAvatA teShAM dhUmapratIkena vartmanA candramasam adhirUDhAnAm annabhAvaM darshayati -- eSha somo rAjA tad devAnAm annaM taM te vA bhakShayanti iti, te can draM prApyAnnaM bhavanti tAMH tatra devA yathA somaM rAjAnam ApyAyasvApakShIyasvetyevam etAMH tatra bhakShayanti iti ca samAnaviShayaM shrutyantaram? na ca vyAghrAdibhiH iva devair bhakShyamANAnAm upabhogaH sambhavatIti | ata uttaraM paThati -- 

bhAktaM vAnAtmavittvAt tathA hi darshayati ||

vAshabdashcoditadoShavyAvartanArthaH | bhAktam eShAm annatvam, na mukhyam | mukhye hyannatve svargakAmo yajeta ityevaMjAtIyakAdhikArashrutir uparudhyeta | candramaNDale ced iShTAdikAriNAm upabhogo na syAt, kimartham adhikAriNa iShTAdi AyAsabahulaM karma kuryuH ? annashabdashcopabhogahetutvasAmAnyAt ananne.apyupacaryamANo dR^ishyate, yathA -- visho.annaM rAj~nAM pashavo.annaM vishAm iti | tasmAd iShTastrIputramitrabhR^ityAdibhiH iva guNabhAvopagataiH iShTAdikAribhir yat sukhaviharaNaM devAnAm, tad evaiShAM bhakShaNam abhipretam, na modakAdivaccarvaNaM nigaraNaM vA | na ha vai devA ashnanti na pibantyetad evAmR^itaM dR^iShTvA tR^ipyanti [chA.u. 3.6.1] iti ca devAnAM carvaNAdivyApAraM vArayati | teShAM ca iShTAdikAriNAM devAn prati guNabhAvopagatAnAm apyupabhoga upapadyate, rAjopajIvinAm iva parijanAnAm | anAtmavittvAcca iShTAdikAriNAM devopabhogyabhAva upapadyate | tathA hi shrutir anAtmavidAM devopabhogyatAM darshayati -- atha yo.anyAM devatAm upAste.anyo.asAvanyo.aham asmIti na sa veda yathA pashur evaM sa devAnAm [bR^i.A.u. 1.4.10] iti | sa cAsminn api loke iShTAdibhiH karmabhiH prINayan pashuvad devAnAm upakaroti, amuShminn api loke tadupajIvI tadAdiShTaM phalam upabhuJNjAnaH pashuvad eva devAnAm upakarotIti gamyate || 

anAtmavittvAt tathA hi darshayati ityasya aparA vyAkhyA -- anAtmavido hyete kevalakarmiNa iShTAdikAriNaH, na j~nAnakarmasamuccayAnuShThAyinaH paJNcAgnividyAm iha Atmavidyetyupacaranti, prakaraNAt | paJNcAgnividyAvihInatvAccedam iShTAdikAriNAM guNavAdenAnnatvam udbhAvyate paJNcAgnivij~nAnaprashaMsAyai | paJNcAgnividyeha vidhitsitA, vAkyatAt paryAvagamAt | tathA hi shrutyantaraM candramaNDale bhogasadbhAvaM darshayati -- sa somaloke vibhUtim anubhUya punar Avartate iti | tathA anyad api shrutyantaram -- atha ye shataM pitNAM jitalokAnAm AnandAH sa ekaH karma devAnAm Anando ye karmaNA devatvam abhisampadyante iti iShTAdikAriNAM devaiH saha saMvasatAM bhogaprAptiM darshayati | evaM bhAktatvAd annabhAvavacanasya, iShTAdikAriNo.atra jIvA raMhantIti pratIyate | tasmAt raMhati sampariShvaktaH iti yuktam evoktam ||7||

 -- o)0(o -- 
2. kR^itAtyayAdhikaraNam

|| 3.1.8 ||

iShTAdikAriNAM dhUmAdinA vartmanA candramaNDalam adhirUDhAnAM bhuktabhogAnAM tataH pratyavaroha AmnAyate -- tasmin yAvat sampAtam uShitvAthaitam evAdhvAnaM punar nivartante yathetam [chA.u. 5.10.5] ityArabhya, yAvat ramaNIyacaraNA brAhmaNAdiyonim Apadyante kapUyacaraNAH shvAdiyonim [chA.u. 5.10.7] iti | 

tatredaM vicAryate -- kiM niranushayA bhuktakR^itsnakarmANo.avarohanti, Aho svit sAnushayA ? iti | kiM tAvat prAptam? niranushayA iti | kutaH? yAvat sampAtam iti visheShaNAt -- sampAtashabdenAtra karmAshaya ucyate, sampatanti anena asmAl lokAt amuM lokaM phalopabhogAyeti | yAvat sampAtam uShitvA iti ca kR^itsnasya tasya kR^itasya tatraiva bhuktatAM darshayati | teShAM yadA tatparyavaiti iti ca shrutyantareNaiva evArthaH pradarshyate | syAd etat -- yAvad amuShmiMl loke upabhoktavyaM karma tAvad upabhuN^kta iti kalpayiShyAmIti | naivaM kalpayituM shakyate, yat kiM ca ityanyatra parAmarshAt -- 

prApyAntaM karmaNaH tasya yat kiM ceha karotyayam | 
tasmAl lokAt punar aityasmai lokAya karmaNe || [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.6]

iti hi aparA shrutiH yat kiM ca ityavisheShaparAmarshena kR^itsnasyeha kR^itasya karmaNaH tatra kShayitatAM darshayati | api ca prAyaNam anArabdhaphalasya karmaNo.abhivyaJNjakam | prAk prAyaNAt Arabdhaphalena karmaNA pratibaddhasyAbhivyaktyanupapatteH | tacca avisheShAd yAvat kiMcid anArabdhaphalaM tasya sarvasyAbhivyaJNjakam | na hi sAdhAraNe nimitte naimittikam asAdhAraNaM bhavitum arhati | na hyavishiShTo pradIpasaMnidhau, ghaTo.abhivyajyate na paTa ityupapadyate | tasmAn niranushayA avarohantItyevaM prApte -- 

kR^itAtyaye.anushayavAn dR^iShTasmR^itibhyAM yathetaman evaM ca ||

brUmaH -- kR^itAtyaye.anushayavAn iti | yena karmavR^indena candramasam ArUDhAH phalopabhogAya, tasminn upabhogena kShayite, teShAM yad ammayaM sharIraM candramasyupabhogAyArabdham, tad upabhogakShayadarshanashokAgnisamparkAt pravilIyate -- savitR^ikiraNasamparkAdivahimakarakAH, hutabhugarciHsamparkAd iva ca ghR^itakAThinyam | tataH kR^itAtyaye kR^itasyeShTAdeH karmaNaH phalopabhogenopakShaye sati, sAnushayA evemam avarohanti | kena hetunA? dR^iShTasmR^itibhyAm ityAha | tathA hi pratyakShA shrutiH sAnushayAnAm avarohaM darshayati -- tad ya iha ramaNIyacaraNA abhyAsho ha yat te ramaNIyAM yonim Apadyeran brAhmaNayoniM vA kShatriyayoniM vA vaishyayoniM vAtha ya iha kapUyacaraNA abhyAsho ha yat te kapUyAM yonim ApadyeraJNshvayoniM vA sUkarayoniM vA cANDAlayoniM vA [chA.u. 5.10.34] iti | caraNashabdenAnushayaH sUcyata iti varNayiShyati | dR^iShTashcAyaM janmanaiva pratiprANyuccAvacarUpa upabhogaH pravibhajyamAna AkasmikatvAsambhavAd anushayasadbhAvaM sUcayati, abhyudayapratyavAyayoH sukR^itaduShkR^itahetutvasya sAmAnyataH shAstreNAvagamitatvAt | smR^itir api -- varNA AshramAshca svakarmaniShThAH pretya karmaphalam anubhUya tataH sheSheNa vishiShTadeshajAtikularUpAyuHshrutavR^ittavittasukhamedhaso janma pratipadyante iti sAnushayAnAm evAvarohaM darshayati || 

kaH punar anushayo nAmeti -- kecit tAvad AhuH -- svargArthasya karmaNo bhuktaphalasyAvasheShaH kashcid anushayo nAma, bhANDAnusArisnehavat -- yathA hi snehabhANDaM ricyamAnaM na sarvAtmanA ricyate, bhANDAnusAryeva kashcit snehasheSho.avatiShThate, tathA anushayo.apIti | 

nanu kAryavirodhitvAd adR^iShTasya na bhuktaphalasyAvasheShAvasthAnaM nyAyyam | nAyaM doShaH | na hi sarvAtmanA bhuktaphalatvaM karmaNaH pratijAnImahe | 

nanu niravasheShakarmaphalopabhogAya candramaNDalam ArUDhAH | bADham -- tathApi svalpakarmAvasheShamAtreNa tatrAvasthAnaM na labhyate | yathA kila kashcit sevakaH sakalaiH sevopakaraNaiH rAjakulam upasR^iptashcirapravAsAt parikShINabahUpakaraNashchatrapAdukAdimAtrAvasheSho na rAjakule.avasthAtuM shaknoti, evam anushayamAtraparigraho na candramaNDale.avasthAtuM shaknotIti || 

na caitad yuktam iva | na hi svargArthasya karmaNo bhuktaphalasyAvasheShAnuvR^ittir upapadyate, kAryavirodhitvAd ityuktam | 

nanv etad apyuktam -- na svargaphalasya karmaNo nikhilasya bhuktaphalatvaM bhaviShyatIti | tad etad apeshalam -- svargArthaM kila karma svargasthasyaiva svargaphalaM nikhilaM na janayati, svargacyutasyApi kaMcit phalaleshaM janayatIti | na shabdapramANakAnAm IdR^ishI kalpanA avakalpate | snehabhANDe tu snehaleshAnuvR^ittir dR^iShTatvAd upapadyate | tathA sevakasyopakaraNaleshAnuvR^ittishca dR^ishyate | na tviha tathA svargaphalasya karmaNo leshAnuvR^ittir dR^ishyate | nApi kalpayituM shakyate, svargaphalatvashAstravirodhAt | avashyaM caitad evaM vij~neyam -- na svargaphalasyeShTAdeH karmaNo bhANDAnusArisnehavad ekadesho.anuvartamAno.anushaya iti | yadi hi yena sukR^itena karmaNA iShTAdinA svargam anvabhUvan, tasyaiva kashcid ekadesho.anushayaH kalpyeta, tato ramaNIya evaiko.anushayaH syAt, na viparItaH | tatreyam anushayavibhAgashrutir uparudhyeta -- tadya iha ramaNIyacaraNAH ... atha ya iha kapUyacaraNAH iti | tasmAd AmuShmikaphale karmajAte upabhukte.avashiShTAm aihikaphalaM karmAntarajAtam anushayaH, tadvanto.avarohantIti || 

yad uktam -- yat kiM ca ityavisheShaparAmarshAt sarvasyeha kR^itasya karmaNaH phalopabhogenAntaM prApya niranushayA avarohantIti, naitad evam | anushayasadbhAvasyAvagamitatvAt, yat kiMcid iha kR^itam AmuShmikaphalaM karma Arabdhabhogam, tat sarvaM phalopabhogena kShapayitvA -- iti gamyate | yad apyuktam -- prAyaNam avisheShAd anArabdhaphalaM kR^itsnam eva karmAbhivyanakti | tatra kenacit karmaNAmuShmiMl loke phalam Arabhyate, kenacid asmin ityayaM vibhAgo na sambhavatIti -- tad apyanushayasadbhAvapratipAdanenaiva pratyuktam | 

api ca kena hetunA prAyaNam anArabdhaphalasya karmaNo.abhivyaJNjakaM pratij~nAyata iti vaktavyam | Arabdhaphalena karmaNA pratibaddhasyetarasya vR^ittyudbhavAnupapatteH, tadupashamAt prAyaNakAle vR^ittyudbhavo bhavatIti yadyucyeta -- tato vaktavyam -- yathaiva tarhi prAk prAyaNAt Arabdhaphalena karmaNA pratibaddhasya itarasya vR^ittyudbhavAnupapattiH, evaM prAyaNakAle.api viruddhaphalasyAnekasya karmaNo yugapatphalArambhAsambhavAt balavatA pratibaddhasya durbalasya vR^ittyudbhavAnupapattiH iti | na hi anArabdhaphalatvasAmAnyena jAtyantaropabhogyaphalam apyanekaM karma ekasmin prAyaNe yugapad abhivyaktaM sat ekAM jAtim Arabhata iti shakyaM vaktum, pratiniyataphalatvavirodhAt | 

nApi kasyacit karmaNaH prAyaNe.abhivyaktiH kasyacid uccheda iti shakyate vaktum, aikAntikaphalatvavirodhAt | na hi prAyashcittAdibhir hetubhir vinA karmaNAmucchedaH sambhAvyate | smR^itir api viruddhaphalena karmaNA pratibaddhasya karmAntarasya ciram avasthAnaM darshayati -- kadAcit sukR^itaM karma kUTastham iha tiShThati | majjamAnasya saMsAre yAvad duHkhAd vimucyate ityevaMjAtIyAkA | 

yadi ca kR^itsnam anArabdhaphalaM karma ekasmin prAyaNe.abhivyaktaM sat ekAM jAtim Arabheta, tataH svarganarakatiryagyoniShvadhikArAnavagamAt dharmAdharmAnutpattau nimittAbhAvAt nottarA jAtir upapadyeta, brahmahatyAdInAM ca ekaikasya karmaNo.anekajanmanimittatvaM smaryamANam uparudhyeta | 

na ca dharmAdharmayoH svarUpaphalasAdhanAdisamadhigame shAstrAd atiriktaM kAraNaM shakyaM sambhAvayitum | 

na ca dR^iShTaphalasya karmaNaH kArIryAdeH prAyaNam abhivyaJNjakaM sambhavatIti, avyApikApIyaM prAyaNasyAbhivyaJNjakatvakalpanA | pradIpopanyAso.api karmabalAbalapradarshanenaiva pratinItaH | sthUlasUkShmarUpAbhivyaktivaccedaM draShTavyam -- yathA hi pradIpaH samAne.api saMnidhAne sthUlaM rUpam abhivyanakti, na sUkShmam -- evaM prAyaNaM samAne.apyanArabdhaphalasya karmajAtasya prAptAvasaratve balavataH karmaNo vR^ittim udbhAvayati, na durbalasyeti | tasmAcchrutismR^itinyAyavirodhAd ashliShTo.ayam asheShakarmAbhivyaktyabhyupagamaH | sheShakarmasadbhAve.anirmokShaprasaN^ga ityayam apyasthAne sambhramaH, samyagdarshanAd asheShakarmakShayashruteH | tasmAt sthitam etad eva -- anushayavanto.avarohantIti | te ca avarohanto yathetam anevaM ca avarohanti | yathetam iti yathAgatam ityarthaH | anevam iti tadviparyayeNetyarthaH | dhUmAkAshayoH pitR^iyANe.adhvanyupAttayor avarohe saN^kIrtanAt yathetaMshabdAcca yathAgatam iti pratIyate | rAtryAdyasaN^kIrtanAd abhrAdyupasaMkhyAnAcca viparyayo.api pratIyate ||8||

|| 3.1.9 || 


caraNAd iti cen nopalakShaNArtheti kArShNAjiniH ||

athApi syAt -- yA shrutir anushayasadbhAvapratipAdanAyodAhR^itA -- tad ya iha ramaNIyacaraNAH iti, sA khalu caraNAt yonyApattiM darshayati, nAnushayAt | anyaccaraNam, anyo.anushayaH -- caraNaM cAritram AcAraH shIlam ityanarthAntaram, anushayaH tu bhuktaphalAt karmaNo.atiriktaM karma abhipretam | shrutishca karmacaraNe bhedena vyapadishati -- yathAkArI yathAcArI tathA bhavati iti yAnyanavadyAni karmANi tAni sevitavyAni no itarANi yAnyasmAkaM sucaritAni tAni tvayopAsyAni iti ca | tasmAt caraNAd yonyApattishruteH nAnushayasiddhiH iti cet, naiSha doShaH -- yato.anushayopalakShaNArthaivaiShA caraNashrutiH iti kArShNAjinir AcAryo manyate ||9||

|| 3.1.10 || 

Anarthakyam iti cen na tadapekShatvAt || 

syAd etat -- kasmAt punashcaraNashabdena shrautaM shIlaM vihAya lAkShaNiko.anushayaH pratyAyyate? nanu shIlasyaiva shrautasya vihitapratiShiddhasya sAdhvasAdhurUpasya shubhAshubhayonyApattiH phalaM bhaviShyati | avashyaM ca shIlasyApi kiMcitphalam abhyupagantavyam, anyathA hyAnarthakyam eva shIlasya prasajyeta -- iti cet, naiSha doShaH | kutaH? tadapekShatvAt | iShTAdi hi karmajAtaM caraNApekSham | na hi sadAcArahInaH kashcid adhikR^itaH syAt -- AcArahInaM na punanti vedAH ityAdismR^itibhyaH | puruShArthatve.apyAcArasya na Anarthakyam | iShTAdau hi karmajAte phalam ArabhamANe tadapekSha evAcAraH tatraiva kaMcid atishayam Arapsyate | karma ca sarvArthakAri -- iti shrutismR^itiprasiddhiH | tasmAt karmaiva shIlopalakShitam anushayabhUtaM yonyApattau kAraNam iti kArShNAjiner matam | na hi karmaNi sambhavati shIlAt yonyApattir yuktA | na hi padbhyAM palAyituM pArayamANo jAnubhyAM raMhitum arhatIti ||10||

|| 3.1.11 || 

sukR^itaduShkR^ite eveti tu bAdariH ||

bAdariH tvacAryaH sukR^itaduShkR^ite eva caraNashabdena pratyAyyete iti manyate | caraNam anuShThAna karmetyanarthAntaram | tathA hi avisheSheNa karmamAtre caratiH prayujyamAno dR^ishyate -- yo hi iShTAdilakShaNaM puNyaM karma karoti, taM laukikA AcakShate -- dharmaM caratyeSha mahAtmeti | AcAro.api ca dharmavisheSha eva | bhedavyapadeshaH tu karmacaraNayor brAhmaNaparivrAjakanyAyenApyupapadyate | tasmAt ramaNIyacaraNAH prashastakarmANaH, kapUyacaraNA ninditakarmANaH iti nirNayaH ||11||

aniShTAdikAryadhikaraNam

|| 3.1.12 || 

aniShTAdikAriNAm api ca shrutam || 

iShTAdikAriNashcandramasaM gacchantItyuktam | ye tvitare.aniShTAdikAriNaH, te.api kiM candramasaM gacchanti, uta na gacchantIti cintyate | tatra tAvad Aha -- iShTAdikAriNa eva candramasaM gacchantItyetat na | kasmAt? yato.aniShTAdikAriNAm api candramaNDalaM gantavyatvena shrutam | tathA hi avisheSheNa kauShItakinaH samAmananti -- ye vai ke cAsmAl lokAt prayanti candramasam eva te sarve gacchanti iti | dehArambho.api ca punar jAyamAnAnAM na antareNa candraprAptim avakalpate, paJNcamyAm Ahutau ityAhutisaMkhyAniyamAt | tasmAt sarva eva candramasam AsIdeyuH | iShTAdikAriNAm itareShAM ca samAnagatitvaM na yuktam iti cet, na, itareShAM candramaNDale bhogAbhAvAt ||12||

|| 3.1.13 || 

saMyamane tu anubhUyetareShAm ArohAvarohau tadgatidarshanAt ||

tushabdaH pakShaM vyAvartayati | naitad asti -- sarve candramasaM gacchantIti | kasmAt? bhogAyaiva hi candrArohaNam, na niShprayojanam | nApi pratyavarohAyaiva, -- yathA kashcid vR^ikSham Arohati puShpaphalopAdAnAya, na niShprayojanam, nApi patanAyaiva | bhogashca aniShTAdikAriNAM candramasi nAstItyuktam | tasmAd iShTAdikAriNa eva candramasam Arohanti, netare | te tu saMyamanaM yamAlayam avagAhya svaduShkR^itAnurUpA yAmIr yAtanA anubhUya punar eva imaM lokaM pratyavarohanti | evambhUtau teShAm ArohAvarohau bhavataH | kutaH? tadgatidarshanAt | tathA hi yamavacanasarUpA shrutiH prayatAm aniShTAdikAriNAM yamavashyatAM darshayati -- 

na sAmparAyaH pratibhAti bAlaM 
pramAdyantaM vittamohena mUDham | 
ayaM loko nAsti para iti mAnI 
punaH punar vasham Apadyate me || [ka.u. 1.2.6] iti |

vaivasvataM saMgamanaM janAnAm ityevaMjAtIyakaM ca bahv eva yamavashyatAprAptiliN^gaM bhavati ||13||

|| 3.1.14 ||

smaranti ca ||

api ca manuvyAsaprabhR^itayaH shiShTAH saMyamane pure yamAyattaM kapUyakarmavipAkaM smaranti nAciketopAkhyAnAdiShu ||14||

|| 3.1.15 || 

api sapta ||

api ca sapta narakA rauravapramukhA duShkR^itaphalopabhogabhUmitvena smaryante paurANikaiH | tAn aniShTAdikAriNaH prApnuvanti | kutaH te candraM prApnuyuH ? ityabhiprAyaH ||15|| 

|| 3.1.16 ||

nanu viruddham idam -- yam AyattA yAtanAH pApakarmANo.anubhavantIti, yAvatA teShu rauravAdiShu anye citraguptAdayo nAnAdhiShThAtAraH smaryanta iti | netyAha -- 

tatrApi ca tadvyApArAd avirodhaH ||

teShvapi saptasu narakeShu tasyaiva yamasyAdhiShThAtR^itvavyApArAbhyupagamAd avirodhaH | yamaprayuktA eva hi te citraguptAdayo.adhiShThAtAraH smaryante ||16||


 
|| 3.1.17 ||

vidyAkarmaNoH iti tu prakR^itatvAt ||

paJNcAgnividyAyAm vettha yathAsau loko na sampUryate [chA.u. 5.3.3] ityasya prashnasya prativacanAvasare shrUyate -- athaitayoH pathor na katareNacana tAnImAni kShudrANyasakR^idAvartIni bhUtAni bhavanti | jAyasva mriyasvetyetat tR^itIyaM sthAnaM tenAsau loke na sampUryate [chA.u. 5.10.8] iti | tatra etayoH pathoH iti vidyAkarmaNoH ityetat | kasmAt? prakR^itatvAt | vidyAkarmaNI hi devayAnapitR^iyANayoH pathoH pratipade prakR^ite -- tad ya itthaM viduH iti vidyA, tayA pratipattavyo devayAnaH panthAH prakIrtitaH | iShTApUrte dattam iti karma, tena pratipattavyaH pitR^iyANaH panthAH prakIrtitaH -- tatprakriyAyAm athaitayoH pathor na katareNacana iti shrutam | 

etad uktaM bhavati -- ye na vidyAsAdhanena devayAne pathyadhikR^itAH, nApi karmaNA pitR^iyANe, teShAm eSha kShudrajantulakShaNo.asakR^idAvartI tR^itIyaH panthA bhavatIti | tasmAd api na aniShTAdikAribhishcandramAH prApyate | syAd etat -- te.api candrabimbam Aruhya tato.avaruhya kShudrajantutvaM pratipatsyanta iti | tad api nAsti, ArohAnarthakyAt | api ca sarveShu prayatsu candralokaM prApnuvatsu asau lokaH prayadbhiH sampUryeta -- ityataH prashnaviruddhaM prativacanaM prasajyeta | tathA hi prativacanaM dAtavyam, yathA asau loko na sampUryate | avarohAbhyupagamAd asampUraNopapattiH iti cet, na, ashrutatvAt | satyam avarohAd apyasampUraNam upapadyate | shrutiH tu tR^itIyasthAnasaN^kIrtanena asampUraNaM darshayati -- etat tR^itIyaM sthAnaM tenAsau loko na sampUryate iti | tena anArohAd eva asampUraNam iti yuktam | avarohasyeShTAdikAriShvapyavishiShTatve sati tR^itIyasthAnoktyAnarthakyaprasaN^gAt | tushabdaH tu shAkhAntarIyavAkyaprabhavAm asheShagamanAshaN^kAm ucchinatti | evaM sati adhikR^itApekShaH shAkhAntarIye vAkye sarvashabdo.avatiShThate -- ye vai kecid adhikR^itA asmAl lokAt prayanti candramasam eva te sarve gacchanti iti ||17|| 

|| 3.1.18 || 

yat punar uktam -- dehalAbhopapattaye sarve candramasaM gantum arhanti, paJNcamyAm Ahutau ... ityAhutisaMkhyAniyamAd iti, tat pratyucyate -- 

na tR^itIye tathopalabdheH ||

na tR^itIye sthAne dehalAbhAya paJNcasaMkhyAniyama AhutInAm AdartavyaH | kutaH? tathopalabdheH | tathA hi antareNaivAhutisaMkhyAniyamaM varNitena prakAreNa tR^itIyasthAnaprAptir upalabhyate -- jAyasva mriyasvetyetat tR^itIyaM sthAnam iti | 

api ca paJNcamyAm AhutAvapaH puruShavacaso bhavanti iti manuShyasharIrahetutvena AhutisaMkhyA kIrtyate, na kITapataN^gAdisharIrahetutvena, puruShashabdasya manuShyajAtivacanatvAt | 

api ca paJNcamyAm AhutAvapAM puruShavacastvam upadishyate, na apaJNcamyAm Ahutau puruShavacastvaM pratiShidhyate, vAkyasya dvyarthatAdoShAt | tatra yeShAm ArohAvarohau sambhavataH, teShAM paJNcamyAm Ahutau deha udbhaviShyati | anyeShAM tu vinaivAhutisaMkhyayA bhUtAntaropasR^iShTAbhir adbhir deha Arapsyate ||18||

|| 3.1.19 || 

smaryate.api ca loke ||

api ca smaryate loke, droNadhR^iShTAdyumnaprabhR^itInAM sItAdraupadIprabhR^itInAM ca ayonijatvam | tatra droNAdInAM yoShidviShayA ekA Ahutir nAsti | dhR^iShTAdyumnAdInAM tu yoShitpuruShaviShaye dve apyAhutI na staH | yathA ca tatra AhutisaMkhyAniyamAnAdaro bhavati, evam anyatrApi bhaviShyati | balAkApi antareNaiva retaHsekaM garbhaM dhatta iti lokarUDhiH ||19||

|| 3.1.20 ||

darshanAcca ||

api ca caturvidhe bhUtagrAme jarAyujANDajasvedajodbhijjalakShaNe svedajodbhijjayoH antareNaiva grAmyadharmam utpattidarshanAt AhutisaMkhyAnAdaro bhavati | evam anyatrApi bhaviShyati ||20||

|| 3.1.21 ||

nanu teShAM khalv eShAM bhUtAnAM trINyeva bIjAni bhavanti ANDAjaM jIvajamudbhijjam ityatra trividha eva bhUtagrAmaH shrUyate | kathaM caturvidhatvaM bhUtagrAmasya pratij~nAtam iti, atrocyate -- 

tR^itIyashabdAvarodhaH saMshokajasya ||

aNDajaM jIvajam udbhijjam ityatra tR^itIyenodbhijjashabdenaiva svedajopasaMgrahaH kR^itaH pratyetavyaH, ubhayor api svedajodbhijjayoH bhUmyudakodbhedaprabhavatvasya tulyatvAt | sthAvarodbhedAt tu vilakShaNo jaN^gamodbheda ityanyatra svedajodbhijjayor bhedavAda ityavirodhaH ||

4. sAbhAvyApattyadhikaraNam

|| 3.1.22 ||

iShTAdikAriNashcandramasam Aruhya tasmin yAvatsampAtam uShitvA tataH sAnushayA avarohantItyuktam | athAvarohaprakAraH parIkShyate | tatreyam avarohashrutir bhavati -- 

athaitam evAdhvAnaM punar nivartante yathetam AkAsham AkAshAd vAyuM vAyur bhUtvA dhUmo bhavati dhUmo bhUtvAbhraM bhavatyabhraM bhUtvA megho bhavati megho bhUtvA pravarShati [chA.u. 5.10.5] iti | 

tatra saMshayaH -- kim AkAshAdisvarUpam evAvarohantaH pratipadyante, kiM vA AkAshAdisAmyam iti | tatra prAptaM tAvat AkAshAdisvarUpam eva pratipadyanta iti | kutaH? evaM hi shrutir bhavati | itarathA lakShaNA syAt | shrutilakShaNAviShaye ca shrutir nyAyyA, na lakShaNA | tathA ca vAyur bhUtvA dhUmo bhavati ityevamAdInyakSharaNi tattatsvarUpApattau AJNjasyena avakalpante | tasmAd AkAshAdisvarUpapratipattiH iti | evaM prApte,

sAbhAvyApattir upapatteH || 

brUmaH -- AkAshAdisAmyaM pratipadyanta iti | candramaNDale yat ammayaM sharIram upabhogArtham Arabdham, tat upabhogakShaye sati pravilIyamAnaM sUkShmam AkAshasamaM bhavati | tato vAyor vasham eti | tato dhUmAdibhiH sampR^icyata iti | tad etad ucyate -- yathetam AkAsham AkAshAd vAyum ityevamAdinA | kuta etat? upapatteH | evaM hi etad upapadyate | na hi anyasyAnyabhAvo mukhya upapadyate | AkAshasvarUpapratipattau ca vAyvAdikrameNAvaroho nopapadyate | vibhutvAcca AkAshena nityasambaddhatvAt na tatsAdR^ishyApatter anyaH tatsambandho ghaTate | shrutyasambhave ca lakShaNAshrayaNaM nyAyyam eva | ata AkAshAditulyatApattir eva | atra AkAshAdibhAva ityupacaryate ||22||

 -- o)0(o -- 

5. nAticireNAdhikaraNam

|| 3.1.23 ||

tatra akAshAdipratipattau prAgvrIhyAdibhAvApatteH bhavati viShayaH -- kiM dIrghaM dIrghaM kAlaM pUrvapUrvasAdR^ishyenAvasthAyottarottarasAdR^ishyaM gacchanti, utAlpam alpam iti | tatrAniyamaH, niyamakAriNaH shAstrasyAbhAvAd ityevaM prApte, idam Aha -- 

nAticireNa visheShAt ||

alpam alpaM kAlam AkAshAdibhAvenAvasthAya varShadhArAbhiH saha imAM bhuvam Apatanti | kuta etat? visheShadarshanAt | tathA hi vrIhyAdibhAvApatter anantaraM vishinaShTi -- ato vai khalu durniShprapataram iti | takAra ekashchAndasyAM prakriyAyAM lupto mantavyaH | durniShprapatataraM durniShkramataram -- duHkhataram asmAd vrIhyAdibhAvAn niHsaraNaM bhavatItyarthaH | tatra duHkhaM niShprapatanaM pradarshayan pUrveShu sukhaM niShprapatanaM darshayati | sukhaduHkhatAvisheShashcAyaM niShprapatanasya kAlAlpatvadIrghatvanimittaH, tasminn avadhau sharIrAniShpatter upabhogAsambhavAt | tasmAd vrIhyAdibhAvApatteH prAk alpenaiva kAlenAvarohaH syAd iti ||23||

6. anyAdhiShThitAdhikaraNam


|| 3.1.24 ||

tasminn evAvarohe pravarShaNAnantaraM paThyate -- ta iha vrIhiyavA oShadhivanaspatayaH tilamAShA iti jAyante [chA.u. 5.10.6] iti | tatra saMshayaH -- kim asminn avadhau sthAvarajAtyApannAH sthAvarasukhaduHkhabhAjo.anushayino bhavanti, Aho svit kShetraj~nAntarAdhiShThiteShu sthAvarasharIreShu saMshleShamAtraM gacchantIti | kiM tAvat prAptam? sthAvarajAtyApannAH tatsukhaduHkhabhAjo.anushayino bhavantIti | kuta etat? janer mukhyArthatvopapatteH, sthAvarabhAvasya ca shrutismR^ityor upabhogasthAnatvaprasiddhiH, pashuhiMsAdiyogAccaiShTAdeH karmajAtasyAniShTaphalatvopapatteH | tasmAn mukhyam evedam anushayinAM vrIhyAdijanma, shvAdijanmavat -- yathA shvayoniM vA sUkarayoniM vA cANDAlayoniM vA iti mukhyam evAnushayinAM shvAdijanma tatsukhaduHkhAnvitaM bhavati, evaM vrIhyAdijanmApIti | evaM prApte -- 

anyAdhiShThite pUrvavad abhilAShAt ||

brUmaH -- anyair jIvair adhiShThiteShu vrIhyAdiShu saMsargamAtram anushayinaH pratipadyante, na tatsukhaduHkhabhAjo bhavanti, pUrvavat -- yathA vAyudhUmAdibhAvo.anushayinAM tatsaMshleShamAtram, evaM vrIhyAdibhAvo.api jAtisthAvaraiH saMshleShamAtram | kuta etat? tadvad evehApyabhilApAt | ko.abhilApasya tadvad bhAvaH? karmavyApAram antareNa saN^kIrtanam -- yathA AkAshAdiShu pravarShaNAnteShu na kiMcit karmavyApAraM parAmR^ishati, evaM vrIhyAdijanmanyapi | tasmAn nAstyatra sukhaduHkhabhAktvam anushayinAm | yatra tu sukhaduHkhabhAktvam abhipraiti, parAmR^ishati tatra karmavyApAram -- ramaNIyacaraNAH ... kapUyacaraNAH iti | api ca mukhye.anushayinAM vrIhyAdijanmani, vrIhyAdiShu lUyamAneShu kaNDyamAneShu pacyamAneShu bhakShyamANeShu ca tadabhimAnino.anushayinaH pravaseyuH | yo hi jIvo yaccharIram abhimanyate, sa tasmin pIDyamAne pravasatIti prasiddham | tatra vrIhyAdibhAvApAtaHsigbhAvo.anushayinAM nAbhilapyeta | ataH saMsargamAtram anushayinAm anyAdhiShThiteShu vrIhyAdiShu bhavati | etena janer mukhyArthatvaM pratibrUyAt, upabhogasthAnatvaM ca sthAvarabhAvasya | na ca vayam upabhogasthAnatvaM sthAvarabhAvasyAvajAnImahe | bhavatu anyeShAM jantUnAm apuNyasAmarthyena sthAvarabhAvam upagatAnAm etat upabhogasthAnam | candramasaH tu avarohanto.anushayino na sthAvarabhAvam upabhuJNjata ityAcakShmahe ||24||

|| 3.1.25 ||

ashuddham iti cen na shabdAt ||

yat punar uktam -- pashuhiMsAdiyogAd ashuddham AdhvarikaM karma, tasyAniShTam api phalam avakalpata ityato mukhyam evAnushayinAM vrIhyAdijanma astu | tatra gauNI kalpanA anarthiketi -- tat parihriyate -- na, shAstrahetutvAd dharmAdharmavij~nAnasya | ayaM dharmo.ayam adharma iti shAstram eva vij~nAne kAraNam, atIndriyatvAt tayoH | aniyatadeshakAlanimittatvAcca -- yasmin deshe kAle nimitte ca yo dharmo.anuShThIyate, sa eva deshakAlanimittAntareShvadharmo bhavati | tena na shAstrAd R^ite dharmAdharmaviShayaM vij~nAnaM kasyacidasti | shAstrAcca hiMsAnugrahAdyAtmako jyotiShTomo dharma ityavadhAritaH, sa katham ashuddha iti shakyate vaktum | 

nanu na hiMsyAt sarvA bhUtAni iti shAstram eva bhUtaviShayAM hiMsAm adharma ityavagamayati | bADham -- utsargastu saH | apavAdo.ayaM ca agnIShomIyaM pashum Alabheta iti | utsargApavAdayoshca vyavasthitaviShayatvam | tasmAd vishuddhaM karma vaidikam, shiShTairanuShThIyamAnatvAt anindyamAnatvAcca | tena na tasya pratirUpaM phalam jAtisthAvaratvam | na ca shvAdijanmavadapi vrIhyAdijanma bhavitum arhati | tad dhi kapUyacaraNAnadhikR^itya ucyate | naivamiha vaisheShikaH kashcidadhikAro.asti | atashcandrasthalaskhalitAnAmanushayinAM vrIhyAdisaMshleShamAtraM tadbhAva ityupacaryate ||25||

|| 3.1.26 || 

retaHsigyogo.atha ||

itashca vrIhyAdisaMshleShamAtraM tadbhAvaH, yatkAraNaM vrIhyAdibhAvasyAnantaram anushayinAM retaHsigbhAva AmnAyate -- yo yo hyannam atti yo retaH siJNcati tad bhUya eva bhavati [chA.u. 5.10.6] iti | na cAtra mukhyo retaHsigbhAvaH sambhavati | cirajAto hi prAptayauvano retaHsigbhavati | katham iva anupacaritaM tadbhAvam adyamAnAn nAnugato.anushayI pratipadyate? tatra tAvad avashyaM retaHsigyoga eva retaHsigbhAvo.abhyupagantavyaH | tadvat vrIhyAdibhAvo.api vrIhyAdiyoga evetya virodhaH ||26||

|| 3.1.27 ||

yoneH sharIram ||

atha retaHsigbhAvasyAnantaraM yonau niShikte retasi, yoner adhi sharIram anushayinAm anushayaphalopabhogAya jAyata ityAha shAstram -- tad ya iha ramaNIyacaraNAH [chA.u. 5.10.7] ityAdi | tasmAd apyavagamyate -- nAvarohe vrIhyAdibhAvAvasare taccharIram eva sukhaduHkhAnvitaM bhavatIti | tasmAt vrIhyAdisaMshleShamAtram anushayinAM tajjanmeti siddham ||27||

iti shrImatparamahaMsaparivrAjakAcAryasya shrIgovindabhagavatpUjyapAdashiShyasya shrImacchaN^karabhagavataH kR^itau shArIrakamImAMsAsUtrabhAShye
tR^itIyAdhyAyasya prathamaH pAdaH || 
|| 3.1 ||

 

(3.2)

|| tR^itIyo.adhyAye dvitIyaH pAdaH || 

atra pAde tattvaMpadArthaparishodhanavicAraH ||

1. sandhyadhikaraNam

|| 3.2.1 ||

atikrAnte pAde paJNcAgnividyAm udAhR^itya jIvasya saMsAragatiprabhedaH prapaJNcitaH | idAnIM tu tasyaivAvasthAbhedaH prapaJNcyate | idam Amananti -- sa yatra prasvapiti [bR^i.A.u. 4.3.9] ityupakramya na tatra rathA na rathayogA na panthAno bhavantyatha rathAn rathayogAn pathaH sR^ijate [bR^i.A.u. 4.3.10] ityAdi | tatra saMshayaH -- kiM prabodha iva svapne'pi pAramArthikI sR^iShTir Aho svin mAyAmayIti | tatra tAvat pratipadyate -- 
 
sandhye sR^iShTir Aha hi ||

sandhye tathyarUpA sR^iShTiH iti | sandhyam iti svapnasthAnam AcaShTe, vede prayogadarshanAt -- sandhyaM tR^itIyaM svapnasthAnam iti | dvayor lokasthAnayoH prabodhasamprasAdasthAnayor vA sandhau bhavatIti sandhyam | tasmin sandhye sthAne tathyarUpaiva sR^iShTir bhavitum arhati | kutaH? yataH pramANabhUtA shrutir evam Aha -- atha rathAn rathayogAn pathaH sR^ijate [bR^i.A.u. 4.3.10] ityAdi | sa hi kartA iti ca upasaMhArAt evam evAvagamyate ||1||

|| 3.2.2 ||

nirmAtAraM caike putrAdayashca ||

api ca eke shAkhino.asminn eva sandhye sthAne kAmAnAM nirmAtAram AtmAnam Amananti -- ya eSha supteShu jAgarti kAmaM kAmaM puruSho nirmimANaH [ka.u. 2.2.8] iti | putrAdayashca tatra kAmA abhipreyante -- kAmyanta iti | 

nanu kAmashabdenecchAvisheSho evocyeran | na, shatAyuShaH putrapautrAn vR^iNIShva [ka.u. 1.1.25] iti prakR^itya ante kAmAnAM tvA kAmabhAjaM karomi [ka.u. 1.1.24] iti prakR^iteShu tatra tatra putrAdiShu kAmashabdasya prayuktatvAt | prAj~naM cainaM nirmAtAraM prakaraNavAkyasheShAbhyAM pratImaH -- prAj~nasya hIdaM prakaraNam -- anyatra dharmAd anyatrAdharmAt ityAdi | tadviShaya eva ca vAkyasheSho.api -- 

tad eva shukraM tad brahma tad evAmR^itam ucyate | 
tasmiMl lokAH shritAH sarve tadu nAtyeti kashcana || [ka.u. 2.2.8] iti | 

prAj~nakartR^ikA ca sR^iShTiH tathyarUpA samadhigatA jAgaritAshrayA, tathA svapnAshrayApi sR^iShTir bhavitum arhati | tathA ca shrutiH -- atho khalvahur jAgaritadesha evAsyaiSha [bR^i.A.u. 4.3.14] iti yAnyeva jAgrat pashyati tAni suptaH iti svapnajAgaritayoH samAnanyAyatAM shrAvayati | tasmAt tathyarUpaiva sandhye sR^iShTiH iti ||2||

|| 3.2.3 || 

evaM prApte, pratyAha -- 

mAyAmAtraM tu kArtsnyenAnabhivyaktasvarUpatvAt ||

tushabdaH pakShaM vyAvartayati | naitad asti -- yad uktam, sandhye sR^iShTiH pAramArthikIti | mAyaiva sandhye sR^iShTiH, na paramArthagandho.apyasti | kutaH? kArtsnyenAnabhivyaktasvarUpatvAt | na hi kArtsnyena paramArthavastudharmeNa abhivyaktasvarUpaH svapnaH | kiM punar atra kArtsnyam abhipretam? deshakAlanimittasampattiH abAdhashca | na hi paramArthavastuviShayANi deshakAlanimittAni abAdhashca svapne sambhAvyante | 

na tAvat svapne rathAdInAm ucito deshaH sambhavati | na hi saMvR^ite dehadeshe rathAdayo.avakAshaM labheran | syAd etat -- bahirdehAt svapnaM drakShyati, deshAntaritadravyagrahaNAt | darshayati ca shrutiH bahirdehAt svapnam -- bahiShkulAyAd amR^itashcaritvA | sa Iyate.amR^ito yatra kAmam iti | sthitigatipratyayabhedashca na aniShkrAnte jantau sAmaJNjasyam ashnuvIta -- iti | netyucyate -- na hi suptasya jantoH kShaNamAtreNa yojanashatAntaritaM deshaM paryetuM viparyetuM ca tataH sAmarthyaM sambhAvyate | kvacicca pratyAgamanavarjitaM svapnaM shrAvayati -- kuruShvaham adya shayAno nidrayAbhiplutaH, svapne paJNcAlA nabhigatashca asmin pratibuddhashca -- iti | dehAcced apeyAt, paJNcAleShv eva pratibudhyeta | tAn asAvabhigata iti | kuruShv eva tu pratibudhyate | yena cAyaM dehena deshAntaram ashnuvAno manyate, tam anye pArshvasthAH shayanadesha eva pashyanti | yathAbhUtAni ca ayaM deshAntarANi svapne pashyati, na tAni tathAbhUtAnyeva bhavanti | 

paridhAvaMshcet pashyet, jAgradvat vastubhUtam artham Akalayet | darshayati ca shrutir antar eva dehe svapnam -- sa yatraitat svapnyayA carati ityupakramya sve sharIre yathAkAmaM parivartate iti | atashca shrutyupapattivirodhAd bahiShkulAyashrutiH gauNI vyAkhyAtavyA -- bahiH iva kulAyAt amR^itashcaritveti -- yo hi vasann api sharIre na tena prayojanaM karoti, sa bahiH iva sharIrAd bhavati -- iti | sthitigatipratyayabhedo.apyevaM sati vipralambha evAbhyupagantavyaH || 

kAlavisaMvAdo.api ca svapne bhavati -- rajanyAM supto vAsaraM bhArate varShe manyate | tathA muhUrtamAtravartini svapne kadAcit bahUn varShapUgAn ativAhayati | nimittAnyapi ca svapne na buddhaye karmaNe vA ucitAni vidyante | karaNopasaMhArAd dhi nAsya ashvarathAdigrahaNAya cakShurAdIni santi | rathAdinirvartane.api kuto.asya nimeShamAtreNa sAmarthyaM dArUNi vA | bAdhyante caite rathAshvAdayaH svapnadR^iShTAH prabodhe | svapna eva ca ete sulabhabAdhA bhavanti, Adyantayor vyabhicAradarshanAt -- ratho.ayam iti hi kadAcit svapne nirdhAritaH kShaNena manuShyaH sampadyate, manuShyo.ayam iti nirdhAritaH kShaNena vR^ikShaH | spaShTaM cAbhAvaM rathAdInAM svapne shrAvayati shAstram -- na tatra rathA na rathayogA na panthAno bhavanti ityAdi | tasmAn mAyAmAtraM svapnadarshanam ||3||

|| 3.2.4 ||

sUcakashca hi shruter AcakShate ca tadvidaH ||

mAyAmAtratvAt tarhi na kashcit svapne paramArthagandho.astIti -- netyucyate -- sUcakashca hi svapno bhavati bhaviShyatoH sAdhvasAdhunoH | tathA hi shrUyate -- yadA karmasu kAmyeShu striyaM svapneShu pashyati | samR^iddhiM tatra jAnIyAt tasmin svapnanidarshane iti | tathA puruShaM kR^iShNaM kR^iShNadantaM pashyati sa enaM hanti ityevamAdibhiH svapnair acirajIvitvam Avedyata iti shrAvayati | AcakShate ca svapnAdhyAyavidaH -- kuJNjarArohaNAdIni svapne dhanyAni, kharayAnAdInyadhanyAni iti | mantradevatAdravyavisheShanimittAshca kecit svapnAH satyArthagandhino bhavantIti manyante | tatrApi bhavatu nAma sUcyamAnasya vastunaH satyatvam | sUcakasya tu strIdarshanAder bhavatyeva vaitathyam, bAdhyamAnatvAd ityabhiprAyaH | tasmAd upapannaM svapnasya mAyAmAtratvam || 

yad uktam -- Aha hi iti tad evaM sati bhAktaM vyAkhyAtavyam -- yathA lAN^galaM gavAdIn udvahati iti nimittamAtratvAd evam ucyate, na tu pratyakSham eva lAN^galaM gavAdIn udvahati | evaM nimittamAtratvAt  -- supto rathAdIn sR^ijate, sa hi kartA -- iti ca ucyate | na tu pratyakSham eva supto rathAdIn sR^ijati | nimittatvaM tu asya rathAdipratibhAnanimittamodatrAsAdidarshanAt tannimittabhUtayoH sukR^itaduShkR^itayoH kartR^itveneti vaktavyam | api ca jAgarite viShayendriyasaMyogAt AdityAdijyotir vyatikarAcca AtmanaH svayaMjyotiShTvaM durvivecanam iti tadvivecanAya svapna upanyastaH | tatra yadi rathAdisR^iShTivacanaM shrutyA nIyeta, tataH svayaMjyotiShTavM na nirNItaM syAt | tasmAd rathAdyabhAvavacanaM shrutyA, rathAdisR^iShTivacanaM tu bhaktyeti vyAkhyeyam | etena nirmANashravaNaM vyAkhyAtam | yad apyuktam -- prAj~namenaM nirmAtAram Amananti iti, tadapyasat, shrutyantare svayaM vihatya svayaM nirmAya svena bhAsA svena jyotiShA prasvapiti iti jIvavyApArashravaNAt | ihApi ya eSha supteShu jAgarti iti prasiddhAnuvAdAjjIva evAyaM kAmAnAM nirmAtA saN^kIrtyate | tasya tu vAkyasheSheNa tad eva shukraM tad brahma iti jIvabhAvaM vyAvartya brahmabhAva upadishyate -- tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7] ityAdivat -- iti na brahmaprakaraNaM virudhyate | na cAsmAbhiH svapne.api prAj~navyApAraH pratiShidhyate, tasya sarveshvaratvAt sarvAsvapyavasthAsvadhiShThAtR^itvopapatteH | pAramArthikastu nAyaM sandhyAshrayaH sargaH viyadAdisargavat -- ityetAvat pratipAdyate | na ca viyadAdisargasyApyAtyantikaM satyatvam asti | pratipAditaM hi tad ananyatvam ArambhaNashabdAdibhyaH ityatra samastasya prapaJNcasya mAyAmAtratvam | prAk tu brahmAtmatvadarshanAt viyadAdiprapaJNco vyavasthitarUpo bhavati | sandhyAshrayaH tu prapaJNcaH pratidinaM bAdhyate -- ityato vaisheShikam idaM sandhyasya mAyAmAtratvam uditam ||24||


|| 3.2.5 ||

parAbhidhyAnAt tu tirohitaM tato hyasya bandhaviparyayau ||

athApi syAt -- parasyaiva tAvad Atmano.aMshaH jIvaH -- agneH iva visphuliN^gaH | tatraivaM sati yathA agnivisphuliN^gayoH samAne dahanaprakAshanashaktI bhavataH, evaM jIveshvarayor api j~nAnaishvaryashaktI | tatashca jIvasya j~nAnaishvaryavashAt sAMkalpikI svapne rathAdisR^iShTir bhaviShyatIti | atrocyate -- satyapi jIveshvarayor aMshAMshibhAve pratyakSham eva jIvasyeshvaraviparItadharmatvam | kiM punar jIvasya IshvarasamAnadharmatvaM nAstyeva? na nAstyeva | vidyamAnam api tat tirohitam avidyAdivyavadhAnAt | tat punaH tirohitaM sat parameshvaram abhidhyAyato yatamAnasya jantor vidhUtadinA tasya -- timiratiraskR^iteva dR^ikshaktiH auShadhavIryAt -- IshvaraprasAdAt saMsiddhasya kasyacid evAvirbhavati, na svabhAvata eva, sarveShAM jantUnAm | kutaH? tato hi IshvarArAtoH, asya jIvasya, bandhamokShau bhavataH -- IshvarasvarUpAparij~nAnAt bandhaH, tatsvarUpaparij~nAnAt tu mokShaH | tathA ca shrutiH -- 

j~nAtvA devaM sarvapAshApahAniH 
kShINaiH kleshair janmamR^ityuprahANiH | 
tasyAbhidhyAnAt tR^itIyaM dehabhede 
vishvaishvaryaM kevala AptakAmaH || [shve.u. 1.11] ityevamAdyA ||5||

|| 3.2.6 ||

dehayogAd vA so.api || 

kasmAt punar jIvaH paramAtmAMsha eva san tiraskR^itaj~nAnaishvaryo bhavati? yuktaM tu j~nAnaishvaryayor atiraskR^itatvam, visphuliN^gasyeva dahanaprakAshanayoH -- iti | ucyate -- satyam evaitat | so.api tu jIvasya j~nAnaishvaryatirobhAvaH, dehayogAt dehendriyamanobuddhiviShayavedanAdiyogAt bhavati | asti ca atropamA -- yathA agner dahanaprakAshanasampannasyApyaraNigatasya dahanaprakAshane tirohite bhavataH, yathA vA bhasmacchannasya -- evam avidyApratyupasthApitanAmarUpakR^itadehAdyupAdhiyogAt tadavivekabhramakR^ito jIvasya j~nAnaishvaryatirobhAvaH | vAshabdo jIvasya IshvarAt anyatvashaN^kAvyAvR^ittyarthaH | 

nanvanya eva jIvaH IshvarAd astu, tiraskR^itaj~nAnaishvaryatvAt | kiM dehayogakalpanayA? netyucyate -- na hi anyatvaM jIvasya IshvarAd upapadyate -- seyaM devataikShata ityupakramya anena jIvenAtmanAnupravishya ityAtmashabdena jIvasya parAmarshAt | tat satyaM sa AtmA tat tvam asi shvetaketo [chA.u. 6.8.7] iti ca jIvAya upadishati IshvarAtmatvam | ato.ananya eva IshvarAjjIvaH san dehayogAt tirohitaj~nAnaishvaryo bhavati | atashca na sAMkalpikI jIvasya svapne rathAdisR^iShTir ghaTate | yadi ca sAMkalpikI svapne rathAdisR^iShTiH syAt, naivAniShTAM kashcit svapnaM pashyet, na hi kashcid aniShTaM saN^kalpayate | yat punar uktam -- jAgaritadeshashrutiH svapnasya satyatvaM khyApayatIti, na tatsAmyavacanaM satyatvAbhiprAyam, svayaMjyotiShTavavirodhAt, shrutyaiva ca svapne rathAdyabhAvasya darshitatvAt | jAgaritaprabhavavAsanAnirmitatvAt tu svapnasya tattulyanirbhAsatvAbhiprAyaM tat | tasmAd upapannaM svapnasya mAyAmAtratvam ||6||

  -- o)0(o -- 
tadabhAvAdhikaraNam

|| 3.2.7 ||

svapnAvasthA parIkShitA | suShuptAvasthedAnIM parIkShyate | tatraitAH suShuptaviShayAH shrutayo bhavanti | kvacicchrUyate -- tad yatraitat suptaH samastaH samprasannaH svapnaM na vijAnAtyAsu tadA nADIShu sR^ipto bhavati [chA.u. 8.6.1] iti | anyatra tu nADIr evAnukramya shrUyate -- tAbhiH pratyavasR^ipya purItati shete [bR^i.A.u. 2.1.19] iti | tathAnyatra nADIr evAnukramya -- tAsu tadA bhavati yadA suptaH svapnaM na kaMcana pashyatyathAsmin prANa evaikadhA bhavati iti | tathAnyatra -- ya eSho.antar hR^idaya AkAshaH tasmiJNshete [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.22] iti | tathAnyatra -- satA somya tadA sampanno bhavati svam apIto bhavati iti | tathA -- prAj~nenAtmanA sampariShvakto na bAhyaM kiMcana veda nAntaram iti ca | 

tatra saMshayaH -- kim etAni nADyAdIni parasparanirapekShatayA bhinnAni suShuptisthAnAni, Aho svit parasparApekShatayA ekaM suShuptisthAnam iti | kiM tAvat prAptam? bhinnAnIti | kutaH? ekArthatvAt  -- na hi ekArthAnAM kvacit parasparApekShatvaM dR^ishyate vrIhiyavAdInAm | nADyAdInAM ca ekArthatA suShuptau dR^ishyate, nADIShu sR^ipto bhavati purItati shete iti ca tatra tatra saptamInirdeshasya tulyatvAt | 

nanu naivaM sati saptamInirdesho dR^ishyate -- satA somya tadA sampanno bhavati iti | naiSha doShaH, tatrApi saptamyarthasya gamyamAnatvAt  -- vAkyasheSho hi tatra AyatanaiShI jIvaH sat upasarpatItyAha -- anyatrAyatanamalabdhvA prANam evopashrayate iti | prANashabdena tatra prakR^itasya sata upAdAnAt | AyatanaM ca saptamyarthaH, saptamInirdesho.api tatra vAkyasheShe dR^ishyate -- sati sampadya na viduH sati sampadyAmahe iti | sarvatra ca visheShavij~nAnoparamalakShaNaM suShuptaM na vishiShyate | tasmAd ekArthatvAt nADyAdInAM vikalpena kadAcit kiMcitsthAnaM svApAyopasarpatIti | evaM prApte, 

tadabhAvo nADIShu tacchruter Atmani ca || 

pratipAdyate -- tadabhAvo nADIShvatmani ceti | tadabhAva iti, tasya prakR^itasya svapnadarshanasya abhAvaH suShuptam ityarthaH | nADIShvatmani ceti samuccayena etAni nADyAdIni svApAyopasarpati, na vikalpena -- ityarthaH | kutaH? tacchruteH | tathA hi sarveShAm eva nADyAdInAM tatra tatra suShuptisthAnatvaM shrUyate | tacca samuccaye saMgR^ihItaM bhavati | vikalpe hyeShAm, pakShe bAdhaH syAt | 

nanu ekArthatvAd vikalpo nADyAdInAM vrIhiyavAdivad ityuktam | netyucyate -- na hi ekavibhaktinirdeshamAtreNa ekArthatvaM vikalpashca Apatati, nAnArthatvasamuccayayor apyekavibhaktinirdeshadarshanAt -- prAsAde shete paryaN^ke shete ityevamAdiShu, tathA ihApi nADIShu purItati brahmaNi ca svapitIti upapadyate samuccayaH | tathA ca shrutiH -- tAsu tadA bhavati yadA suptaH svapnaM na kaMcana pashyatyathAsmin prANa evaikadhA bhavati iti samuccayaM nADInAM prANasya ca suShuptau shrAvayati, ekavAkyopAdAnAt | prANasya ca brahmatvaM samadhigatam -- prANaH tathAnugamAt ityatra | yatrApi nirapekShA iva nADIH suShuptisthAnatvena shrAvayati -- Asu tadA nADIShu sR^ipto bhavati iti, tatrApi pradeshAntaraprasiddhasya brahmaNo.apratiShedhAt nADIdvAreNa brahmaNyevAvatiShThata iti pratIyate | 

na caivam api nADIShu saptamI virudhyate, nADIbhir api brahmopasarpan sR^ipta eva nADIShu bhavati -- yo hi gaN^gayA sAgaraM gacchati, gata eva sa gaN^gAyAM bhavati | bhavati ca atra rashminADIdvArAtmakasya brahmalokamArgasya vivakShitatvAt nADIstutyarthaM sR^iptisaN^kIrtanam -- nADIShu sR^ipto bhavati ityuktvA taM na kashcana pApmA spR^ishati iti bruvan nADIH prashaMsati | bravIti ca pApmasparshAbhAve hetum tejasA hi tadA sampanno bhavati iti -- tejasA nADIgatena pittAkhyena abhivyAptakaraNo na bAhyAn viShayAnIkShata ityarthaH |
