athavA tejaseti brahmaNa evAyaM nirdeshaH, shrutyantare brahmaiva teja eva iti tejaHshabdasya brahmaNi prayuktatvAt | brahmaNA hi tadA sampanno bhavati nADIdvAreNa, ataH taM na kashcana pApmA spR^ishatItyarthaH -- brahmasampattishca pApmasparshAbhAve hetuH samadhigataH sarve pApmAno.ato nivartante.apahatapApmA hyeSha brahmalokaH ityAdishrutibhyaH | evaM ca sati pradeshAntaraprasiddhena brahmaNA suShuptisthAnenAnugato nADInAM samuccayaH samadhigato bhavati | tathA purItato.api brahmaprakriyAyAM saN^kIrtanAt tadanuguNam eva suShuptisthAnatvaM j~nAyate -- ya eSho.antarhR^idaya AkAshaH tasmiJNshete iti hR^idayAkAshe suShuptisthAne prakR^ite idam ucyate -- purItati shete iti | purItad iti hR^idayapariveShTanam ucyate | tadantarvartinyapi hR^idayAkAshe shayAnaH shakyate purItati shete iti vaktum -- prAkAraparikShipte.api hi pure vartamAnaH prAkAre vartata ityucyate | hR^idayAkAshasya ca brahmatvaM samadhigatam dahara uttarebhyaH ityatra | tathA nADIpurItatsamuccayo.api tAbhiH pratyavasR^ipya purItati shete ityekavAkyopAdAnAt avagamyate | satprAj~nayoshca prasiddham eva brahmatvam | 

evam etAsu shrutiShu trINyeva suShuptisthAnAni saN^kIrtitAni -- nADyAH purItat brahma ceti | tatrApi dvAramAtraM nADyAH purItacca, brahmaiva tu ekam anapAyi suShuptisthAnam | api ca nADyAH purItad vA jIvasyopAdhyAdhAra eva bhavati -- tatrAsya karaNAni vartanta iti | na hi upAdhisambandham antareNa svata eva jIvasyAdhAraH kashcit sambhavati, brahmAvyatirekeNa svamahimapratiShThitatvAt | brahmAdhAratvam apyasya suShupte naiva AdhArAdheyabhedAbhiprAyeNa ucyate | kathaM tarhi? tAdAtmyAbhiprAyeNa | yata Aha -- satA somya tadA sampanno bhavati svam apIto bhavati iti -- svashabdena AtmA abhilapyate, svarUpam ApannaH supto bhavatItyarthaH | api ca na kadAcijjIvasya brahmaNA sampattir nAsti, svarUpasyAnapAyitvAt | svapnajAgaritayoH tUpAdhisamparkavashAt pararUpApattim ivApekShya tadupashamAt suShupteH svarUpApattir vivakShyate -- svam apIto bhavati iti | 

atashca suptAvasthAyAM kadAcit satA sampadyate, kadAcin na sampadyate -- ityayuktam | api ca sthAnavikalpAbhyupagame.api visheShavij~nAnopashamalakShaNaM tAvat suShuptaM na kvacid vishiShyate | tatra sati sampannaH tAvat ekatvAt na vijAnAtIti yuktam, tat kena kaM vijAnIyAt iti shruteH | nADIShu purItati ca shayAnasya na kiMcit avij~nAne kAraNaM shakyaM vij~nAtum, bhedaviShayatvAt, yatra vA anyad iva syAt tatrAnyo.anyat pashyet iti shruteH | 

nanu bhedaviShayasyApyatidUrAdikAraNam avij~nAne syAt | bADham evaM syAt, yadi jIvaH svataH paricchinno.abhyupagamyeta -- yathA viShNumitraH pravAsI svagR^ihAn na pashyatIti | na tu jIvasyopAdhivyatirekeNa paricchedo vidyate | upAdhigatam evAtidUrAdikAraNam avij~nAne iti yadyucyeta, tathApyupAdher upashAntatvAt satyeva sampannaH na vijAnAtIti yuktam | na ca vayam iha tulyavat nADyAdisamuccayaM pratipAdayAmaH | na hi nADyaH suptisthAnaM purItacca ityanena vij~nAnena kiMcit prayojanam asti | na hyetadvij~nAnapratibaddhaM kiMcit phalaM shrUyate | nApyetadvij~nAnaM phalavataH kasyacid aN^gam upadishyate | brahma tu anapAyi suptisthAnam -- ityetat pratipAdayAmaH | tena tu vij~nAnena prayojanam asti jIvasya brahmAtmatvAvadhAraNaM svapnajAgaritavyavahAravimuktatvAvadhAraNaM ca | tasmAd Atmaiva suptisthAnam ||7||

|| 3.2.8 ||

ataH prabodho.asmAt ||

yasmAcca Atmaiva suptisthAnam, ata eva ca kAraNAt nityavad eva asmAd AtmanaH prabodhaH svApAdhikAre shiShyate, kuta etad AgAt ityasya prashnasya prativacanAvasare -- yathAgneH kShudrA visphuliN^gA vyuccarantyevam evAsmAd AtmanaH sarve prANAH ityAdinA, sata Agamya na viduH sata AgacchAmahe ... [chA.u. 6.10.2] iti ca | vikalpyamAneShu tu suShuptisthAneShu, kadAcin nADIbhyaH pratibudhyate kadAcit purItataH kadAcid AtmanaH -- ityashAsiShyat | tasmAd apyAtmaiva suptisthAnam iti ||8||

  -- o)0(o -- 
karmAnusmR^itishabdavidhyadhikaraNam

|| 3.2.9 || 

tasyAH punaH satsampatteH pratibudhyamAnaH kiM ya eva satsampannaH sa eva pratibudhyate, uta sa vA anyo vA iti cintyate | tatra prAptaM tAvat -- aniyama iti | kutaH? yadA hi jalarAshau kashcijjalabinduH prakShipyate, jalarAshir eva sa tadA bhavati, punar uddharaNe ca sa eva jalabindur bhavati -- iti duHsampAdam, tadvat suptaH pareNaikatvam ApannaH samprasIdatIti na sa eva punar utthAtum arhati | tasmAt sa eva Ishvaro vA anyo vA jIvaH pratibudhyate iti || evaM prApte, idam Aha -- 

sa eva tu karmAnusmR^itishabdavidhibhyaH ||

sa eva tu jIvaH suptaH svAsthyaM gataH punar uttiShThati, nAnyaH | kasmAt? karmAnusmR^itishabdavidhibhyaH | vibhajya hetuM darshayiShyAmi -- karmasheShAnuShThAnadarshanAt tAvat sa evotthAtum arhati nAnyaH | tathA hi -- pUrvedyuranuShThitasya karmaNo.aparedyuH sheSham anutiShThan dR^ishyate | na cAnyena sAmikR^itasya karmaNo.anyaH sheShakriyAyAM pravartitum utsahate, atiprasaN^gAt | tasmAd eka eva pUrvedyuraparedyushca ekasya karmaNaH karteti gamyate | itashca sa evottiShThati, yatkAraNam atIte.ahani aham ado.adrAkSham iti pUrvAnubhUtasya pashcAt smaraNam anyasyotthAne nopapadyate | na hyanyadR^iShTam anyo.anusmartum arhati | so.aham asmIti ca AtmAnusmaraNam AtmAntarotthAne nAvakalpate | shabdebhyashca tasyaivotthAnam avagamyate | tathA hi -- punaH pratinyAyaM pratiyonyAdravati buddhAntAyaiva imAH sarvAH prajA aharahar gacchantya etaM brahmalokaM na vindanti ta iha vyAghro vA siMho vA vR^iko vA varAho vA kITo vA pataN^go vA daMsho vA mashako vA yad yad bhavanti tadA bhavanti [chA.u. 6.10.2] ityevamAdayaH shabdAH svApaprabodhAdhikArapaThitA na AtmAntarotthAne sAmaJNjasyam IyuH | karmavidyAvidhibhyashcaivam evAvagamyate | anyathA hi karmavidyAvidhayo.anarthakAH syuH | anyotthAnapakShe hi suptamAtro mucyata ityApadyeta | evaM cet syAt, vada kiM kAlAntaraphalena karmaNA vidyayA vA kR^itaM syAt | api ca anyotthAnapakShe yadi tAvaccharIrAntare vyavaharamANo jIva uttiShThet, tatratyavyavahAralopaprasaN^gaH syAt | atha tatra supta uttiShThet, kalpanAnarthakyaM syAt -- yo hi yasmin sharIre suptaH saH tasmin nottiShThati, anyasmin sharIre supto.anyasminn uttiShThatIti ko.asyAM kalpanAyAM lAbhaH syAt? 

atha mukta uttiShThet, antavAn mokSha Apadyeta | nivR^ittAvidyasya ca punar utthAnam anupapannam | etena IshvarasyotthAnaM pratyuktam, nityanivR^ittAvidyatvAt | akR^itAbhyAgamakR^itavipraNAshau ca durnivArAvanyotthAnapakShe syAtAm | tasmAt sa evottiShThati, nAnya iti | yat punar uktam -- yathA jalarAshau prakShipto jalabindur noddhartuM shakyate, evaM sati sampanno jIvo notpatitum arhatIti, tat parihriyate -- yuktaM tatra vivekakAraNAbhAvAt jalabindor anuddharaNam, iha tu vidyate vivekakAraNam -- karma ca avidyA ca, iti vaiShamyam | dR^ishyate ca durvivecayor apyasmajjAtIyaiH kShIrodakayoH saMsR^iShTayoH haMsena vivecanam | api ca na jIvo nAma kashcit parasmAd anyo vidyate, yo jalabinduH iva jalarAsheH sato vivicyeta | sad eva tu upAdhisamparkAjjIva ityupacaryate ityasakR^itprapaJNcitam | evaM sati yAvad ekopAdhigatA bandhAnuvR^ittiH, tAvad ekajIvavyavahAraH | upAdhyantaragatAyAM tu bandhAnuvR^ittau jIvAntaravyavahAraH | sa evAyam upAdhiH svApaprabodhayoH bIjAN^kuranyAyena -- ityataH sa eva jIvaH pratibudhyata iti yuktam ||9||

  -- o)0(o -- 
mugdhAdhikaraNam

|| 3.2.10 || 


asti mugdho nAma, yaM mUrchita iti laukikAH kathayanti | sa tu kim avastha iti parIkShAyAm, ucyate -- tisrastAvadavasthAH sharIrasthasya jIvasya prasiddhAH -- jAgaritaM svapnaH suShuptam iti | caturthI sharIrAd apasR^iptiH | na tu paJNcamI kAcidavasthA jIvasya shrutau smR^itau vA prasiddhA asti | tasmAccatasR^iNAm evAvasthAnAmanyatamAvasthA mUrccheti || evaM prApte, 

mugdhe.ardhasampattiH parisheShAt ||

brUmaH -- na tAvan mugdho jAgaritAvastho bhavitum arhati | na hyayam indriyair viShayAn IkShate | syAd etat -- iShukAranyAyena mugdho bhaviShyati -- yathA iShukAro jAgrad api iShvAsaktamanastayA nAnyAn viShayAn IkShate, evaM mugdho musalasampAtAdijanitaduHkhAnubhavavyagramanastayA jAgrad api nAnyAn viShayAn IkShata iti | na, acetayamAnatvAt | iShukAro hi vyApR^itamanA bravIti -- iShum evAham etAvantaM kAlam upalabhamAno.abhUvam iti, mugdhaH tu labdhasaMj~no bravIti -- andhe tamasyaham etAvantaM kAlaM prakShipto.abhUvam, na kiMcin mayA cetitam iti | jAgratashcaikaviShayaviShaktacetaso.api deho vidhrIyate | mugdhasya tu deho dharaNyAM patati | tasmAn na jAgarti | nApi svapnAn pashyati, niHsaMj~nakatvAt | nApi mR^itaH, prANoShmaNor bhAvAt -- mugdhe hi jantau mR^ito.ayaM syAn na vA mR^ita iti saMshayAnAH, UShmAsti nAstIti, hR^idayadesham Alabhante, nishcayArtham, prANo.asti nAstIti ca, nAsikAdesham | yadi prANoShmaNor astitvaM nAvagacchanti, tato mR^ito.ayam ityadhyavasAya dahanAyAraNyaM nayanti | atha tu prANam UShmANaM vA pratipadyante, tato nAyaM mR^ita ityadhyavasAya saMj~nAlAbhAya bhiShajyanti | punarutthAnAcca na diShTaM gataH | na hi yamaM gataH yamarAShTrAt pratyAgacchati | astu tarhi suShuptaH, niHsaMj~natvAt, amR^itatvAcca | na, vailakShaNyAt -- mugdhaH kadAcicciram api nocchvasiti, savepathur asya deho bhavati, bhayAnakaM ca vadanam, visphArite netre | suShuptaH tu prasannavadanaH tulyakAlaM punaH punar ucchvasiti, nimIlite asya netre bhavataH, na cAsya deho vepate | pANipeShaNamAtreNa ca suShuptam utthApayanti, na tu mugdhaM mudgaraghAtenApi | nimittabhedashca bhavati mohasvApayoH -- musalasampAtAdinimittatvAn mohasya, shramanimittatvAcca svApasya | na ca loke.asti prasiddhiH -- mugdhaH supta iti | parisheShAd ardhasampattir mugdhatetyavagacchAmaH -- niHsaMj~natvAt sampannaH, itarasmAcca vailakShaNyAd asampannaH iti ||

kathaM punar ardhasampattir mugdhateti shakyate vaktum? -- yAvatA suptaM prati tAvad uktaM shrutyA -- satA somya tadA sampanno bhavati iti, atra steno.asteno bhavati naitaM setum ahorAtre tarato na jarA na mR^ityur na shoko na sukR^itaM na duShkR^itam ityAdi | jIve hi sukR^itaduShkR^itayoH prAptiH sukhitvaduHkhitvapratyayotpAdanena bhavati | na ca sukhitvapratyayo duHkhitvapratyayo vA suShupte vidyate | mugdhe.api tau pratyayau naiva vidyete | tasmAt upAdhyupashamAt suShuptavan mugdhe.api kR^itsnasampattir eva bhavitum arhati, nArdhasampattiH iti | atrocyate -- na brUmaH, mugdhe.ardhasampattir jIvasya brahmaNA bhavatIti | kiM tarhi, ardhena suShuptapakShasya bhavati mugdhatvam, ardhenAvasthAntarapakShasya -- iti brUmaH | darshite ca mohasya svApena sAmyavaiShamye | dvAraM caitat maraNasya | yadAsya sAvasheShaM karma bhavati, tadA vAN^manase pratyAgacchataH | yadA tu niravasheShaM karma bhavati, tadA prANoShmANAvapagacchataH | tasmAd ardhasampattiM brahmavida icchanti | yat tUktam -- na paJNcamI kAcid avasthA prasiddhAstIti, naiSha doShaH | kAdAcitkIyam avastheti na prasiddhA syAt | prasiddhA caiShA lokAyurvedayoH | ardhasampattyabhyupagamAcca na paJNcamI gaNyata ityanavadyam ||10||

  -- o)0(o -- 
ubhayaliN^gAdhikaraNam ||

|| 3.2.11 || 

na sthAnato.api parasyobhayaliN^gaM sarvatra hi ||

yena brahmaNA suShuptyAdiShu jIva upAdhyupashamAtsampadyate, tasyedAnIM svarUpaM shrutivashena nirdhAryate | santyubhayaliN^gAH shrutayo brahmaviShayAH -- sarvakarmA sarvakAmaH sarvagandhaH sarvarasaH ityevamAdyAH savisheShaliN^gAH | asthUlam anaNvahrasvam adIrgham [bR^i.A.u. 3.8.8] ityevamAdyAshca nirvisheShaliN^gAH | kim Asu shrutiShu ubhayaliN^gaM brahma pratipattavyam, uttAnyataraliN^gam | yadApyanyataraliN^gam, tadApi savisheSham, uta nirvisheSham -- iti mImAMsyate | tatra ubhayaliN^gashrutyanugrahAt ubhayaliN^gam eva brahma ityevaM prApte, brUmaH -- na tAvat svata eva parasya brahmaNa ubhayaliN^gatvam upapadyate | na hyekaM vastu svata eva rUpAdivisheShopetaM tadviparItaM ca ityavadhArayituM shakyam, virodhAt | astu tarhi sthAnataH, pR^ithivyAdyupAdhiyogAd iti | tad api nopapadyate -- na hi upAdhiyogAd apyanyAdR^ishasya vastuno.anyAdR^ishaH svabhAvaH sambhavati | na hi svacchaH san sphaTiko.alaktakAdyupAdhiyogAd asvaccho bhavati, bhramamAtratvAd asvacchatAbhiniveshasya | upAdhInAM ca avidyApratyupasthApitatvAt | atashca anyataraliN^gaparigrahe.api samastavisheSharahitaM nirvikalpakam eva brahma pratipattavyam, na tad viparItam | sarvatra hi brahmasvarUpapratipAdanapareShu vAkyeShu ashabdam asparsham arUpam avyayam ityevamAdiShu apAstasamastavisheSham eva brahma upadishyate ||11||

|| 3.2.12 ||

na bhedAd iti cen, na, pratyekam atadvacanAt ||

athApi syAt -- yad uktam, nirvikalpam ekaliN^gam eva brahma nAsya svataH sthAnato vA ubhayaliN^gatvam astIti, tan nopapadyate | kasmAt? bhedAt | bhinnA hi pratividyaM brahmaNa AkArA upadishyante, catuShpAt brahma, ShoDashakalaM brahma, vAmanItvAdilakShaNaM brahma, trailokyasharIravaishvAnarashabdoditaM brahma, ityevaMjAtIyakAH | tasmAt savisheShatvam api brahmaNo.abhyupagantavyam | 

nanu uktaM nobhayaliN^gatvaM brahmaNaH sambhavatIti | ayam apyavirodhaH, upAdhikR^itatvAd AkArabhedasya | anyathA hi nirviShayam eva bhedashAstraM prasajyeta -- iti cet, neti brUmaH | kasmAt? pratyekam atadvacanAt | pratyupAdhibhedaM hi abhedam eva brahmaNaH shrAvayati shAstram -- yashcAyam asyAM pR^ithivyAM tejomayo.amR^itamayaH puruSho yashcAyam adhyAtmaM shArIraH tejomayo.amR^itamayaH puruSho.ayam eva sa yo.ayam AtmA ityAdi | atashca na bhinnAkArayogo brahmaNaH shAstrIya iti shakyate vaktum, bhedasya upAsanArthatvAt, abhede tAtparyAt ||12||

|| 3.2.13 ||

api caivam eke || 

api caivaM bhedadarshananindApUrvakam abhedadarshanam eva eke shAkhinaH samAmananti -- 

manasaivedam AptavyaM neha nAnAsti kiMcana | 
mR^ityoH sa mR^ityum Apnoti ya iha nAneva pashyati || [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.19] iti | 

tathAnye.api -- bhoktA bhogyaM preritAraM ca matvA sarvaM proktaM trividhaM brahma me tat iti samastasya bhogyabhoktR^iniyantR^ilakShaNasya prapaJNcasya brahmaikasvabhAvatAm adhIyate ||13|| 


|| 3.2.14 ||

kathaM punaH AkAravad upadeshinIShu anAkAropadeshinIShu ca brahmaviShayAsu shrutiShu satIShu, anAkAram eva brahma avadhAryate, na punar viparItam? ityata uttaraM paThati -- 

arUpavad eva hi tatpradhAnatvAt ||

rUpAdyAkArarahitam eva hi brahma avadhArayitavyam, na rUpAdimat | kasmAt? tatpradhAnatvAt | asthUlam anaNvahrasvam adIrgham ashabdam asparsham arUpam avyayam AkAsho vai nAma nAmarUpayor nirvahitA te yad antarA tad brahma, divyo hyamUrtaH puruShaH sa bAhyAbhyantaro hyajaH [mu.u. 2.1.2], tad etad brahmApUrvam anaparam anantaram abAhyam ayam AtmA brahma sarvAnubhUH [bR^i.A.u. 2.5.19] ityevamAdIni vAkyAni niShprapaJNcabrahmAtmatattvapradhAnAni, na arthAntarapradhAnAni -- ityetat pratiShThApitam tat tu samanvayAt ityatra | tasmAd evaMjAtIyakeShu vAkyeShu yathAshrutaM nirAkAram eva brahma avadhArayitavyam | itarANi tu AkAravad brahmaviShayANi vAkyAni na tatpradhAnAni | upAsanAvidhipradhAnAni hi tAni | teShvasati virodhe yathAshrutam Ashrayitavyam | sati tu virodhe tatpradhAnAni atatpradhAnebhyo balIyAMsi bhavanti -- ityeSha vinigamanAyAM hetuH, yena ubhayIShvapi shrutiShu satIShu anAkAram eva brahma avadhAryate, na punar viparItam iti ||14|| 

|| 3.2.15 || 

kA tarhyAkAravad viShayANAM shrutInAM gatiH? ityata Aha -- 

prakAshavaccAvaiyarthyAt ||

yathA prakAshaH saurashcAndramaso vA viyad vyApya avatiShThamAno.aN^gulyAdyupAdhisambandhAt teShu R^ijuvakrAdibhAvaM pratipadyamAneShu tadbhAvam iva pratipadyate, evaM brahmApi pR^ithivyAdyupAdhisambandhAt tadAkAratAm iva pratipadyate | tadAlambano brahmaNa AkAravisheShopadesha upAsanArtho na virudhyate | evam avaiyarthyam AkAravadbrahmaviShayANAm api vAkyAnAM bhaviShyati | na hi vedavAkyAnAM kasyacid arthavattvam kasyacid anarthavattvam iti yuktaM pratipattum, pramANatvAvisheShAt | 

nanv evam api yat purastAt pratij~nAtam -- nopAdhiyogAd apyubhayaliN^gatvaM brahmaNo.astIti, tad virudhyate | neti brUmaH -- upAdhinimittasya vastudharmatvAnupapatteH | upAdhInAM ca avidyApratyupasthApitatvAt | satyAm eva ca naisargikyAm avidyAyAM lokavedavyavahArAvatAra iti tatra tatra avocAma ||15||

|| 3.2.16 || 

Aha ca tanmAtram ||

Aha ca shrutiH caitanyamAtraM vilakShaNarUpAntararahitaM nirvisheShaM brahma -- sa yathA saindhavaghano.anantaro.abAhyaH kR^itsno rasaghana evaivaM vA are.ayam AtmAnantaro.abAhyaH kR^itsnaH praj~nAnaghana eva [bR^i.A.u. 4.5.13] iti | etad uktaM bhavati -- nAsya Atmano.antar bahir vA caitanyAd anyad rUpam asti, caitanyam eva tu nirantaram asya svarUpam -- yathA saindhavaghanasyAntar bahishca lavaNarasa eva nirantaro bhavati, na rasAntaram, tathaiveti ||16||

|| 3.2.17 || 

darshayati cAtho api smaryate || 

darshayati ca shrutiH pararUpapratiShedhenaiva brahma -- nirvisheShatvAt | athAta Adesho neti neti anyad eva tadviditAdatho aviditAdadhi [ke.u. 1.3], yato vAco nivartante aprApya manasA saha [tai.u. 2.8] ityevamAdyA | bAShkalinA ca bAdhvaH pR^iShTaH san avacanenaiva brahma provAceti shrUyate -- sa hovAcAdhIhi bho iti sa tUShNIM babhUva taM ha dvitIye tR^itIye vA vacana uvAca brUmaH khalu tvaM tu na vijAnAsi | upashAnto.ayam AtmA iti | tathA smR^itiShvapi parapratiShedhenaivopadishyate -- 

j~neyaM yat tat pravakShyAmi yajj~nAtvAmR^itam ashnute | 
anAdimat paraM brahma na sat tan nAsad ucyate || [gItA 13.12] ityevamAdyAsu, 

tathA vishvarUpadharo nArAyaNo nAradam uvAceti smaryate -- 

mAyA hyeShA mayA sR^iShTA yanmAM pashyasi nArada | 
sarvabhUtaguNair yuktaM naivaM mAM j~nAtum arhasi || iti ||17||

|| 3.2.18 ||

ata eva copamA sUryakAdivat ||

yata eva ca ayam AtmA caitanyarUpo nirvisheSho vAN^manasAtItaH parapratiShedhopadeshyaH, ata eva ca asyopAdhinimittAm apAramArthikIM visheShavattAm abhipretya jalasUryakAdivad ityupamA upAdIyate mokShashAstreShu -- 

yathA hyayaM jyotir AtmA vivasvAn 
apo bhinnA bahudhaiko.anugacchan | 
upAdhinA kriyate bhedarUpo 
devaH kShetreShv evam ajo.ayam AtmA || iti | 

eka eva hi bhUtAtmA bhUte bhUte vyavasthitaH | 
ekadhA bahudhA caiva dR^ishyate jalacandravat || iti caivamAdiShu ||18|| 
 
|| 3.2.19 || 

atra pratyavasthIyate -- 

ambuvad agrahaNAt tu na tathAtvam ||

na jalasUryakAditulyatvam ihopapadyate, tadvad agrahaNAt | sUryAdibhyo hi mUrtebhyaH pR^ithagbhUtaM viprakR^iShTadeshaM mUrtaM jalaM gR^ihyate | tatra yuktaH sUryAdipratibimbodayaH | na tu AtmA mUrtaH, na cAsmAt pR^ithagbhUtA viprakR^iShTadeshAshcopAdhayaH, sarvagatatvAt sarvAnanyatvAcca | tasmAd ayukto.ayaM dR^iShTAnta iti ||19||

|| 3.2.20 ||

atra pratividhIyate -- 

vR^iddhihrAsabhAktvam antarbhAvAd ubhayasAmaJNjasyAd evam ||

yukta eva tu ayaM dR^iShTAntaH, vivakShitAMshasambhavAt | na hi dR^iShTAntadArShTAntikayoH kvacit kaMcit vivakShitam aMshaM muktvA sarvasArUpyaM kenacit darshayituM shakyate | sarvasArUpye hi dR^iShTAntadArShTAntikabhAvoccheda eva syAt | na cedaM svamanIShayA jalasUryakAdidR^iShTAntapraNayanam | shAstrapraNItasya tu asya prayojanamAtram upanyasyate | kiM punar atra vivakShitaM sArUpyam iti, tad ucyate -- vR^iddhihrAsabhAktvam iti | jalagataM hi sUryapratibimbaM jalavR^iddhau vardhate, jalahrAse hrasati, jalacalane calati, jalabhede bhidyate -- ityevaM jaladharmAnuvidhAyi bhavati, na tu paramArthataH sUryasya tathAtvam asti | evaM paramArthato.avikR^itam ekarUpam api sat brahma dehAdyupAdhyantarbhAvAt bhajata ivopAdhidharmAn vR^iddhihrAsAdIn | evam ubhayor dR^iShTAntadArShTAntikayoH sAmaJNjasyAd avirodhaH ||20||

|| 3.2.21 ||

darshanAcca ||

darshayati ca shrutiH parasyaiva brahmaNo dehAdiShUpAdhiShvantar anupravesham -- purashcakre dvipadaH purashcakre catuShpadaH | puraH sa pakShI bhUtvA puraH puruSha Avishat iti | anena jIvenAtmanAnupravishya iti ca | tasmAd yuktam etat ata eva copamA sUryakAdivat iti | tasmAt nirvikalpakaikaliN^gam eva brahma, na ubhayaliN^gaM viparItaliN^gaM vA iti siddham || 

atra kecit dve adhikaraNe kalpayanti -- prathamaM tAvat kiM pratyastamitAsheShaprapaJNcam ekAkAraM brahma, uta prapaJNcavad anekAkAropetam iti | dvitIyaM tu pratyastamitaprapaJNcatve kiM sallakShaNaM brahma, uta bodhalakShaNam, uta ubhayalakShaNam iti | atra vayaM vadAmaH -- sarvathApyAnarthakyam adhikaraNAntaram Arambhasyeti | yadi tAvad anekaliN^gatvaM parasya brahmaNo nirAkartavyam ityayaM prayAsaH, tat pUrveNaiva na sthAnato.api ityanenAdhikaraNena nirAkR^itam iti, uttaram adhikaraNam prakAshavacca ityetad vyartham eva bhavet | na ca sallakShaNam eva brahma na bodhalakShaNam -- iti shakyaM vaktum, vij~nAnaghana eva ityAdishrutivaiyarthyaprasaN^gAt | kathaM vA nirastacaitanyaM brahma cetanasya jIvasyAtmatvenopadishyeta? nApi bodhalakShaNam eva brahma na sallakShaNam iti shakyaM vaktum, astItyevopalabdhavyaH ityAdishrutivaiyarthyaprasaN^gAt | kathaM vA nirastasattAko bodho.abhyupagamyeta | 

nApyubhayalakShaNam eva brahma -- iti shakyaM vaktum, pUrvAbhyupagamavirodhaprasaN^gAt | sattAvyAvR^ittena ca bodhena bodhavyAvR^ittayA ca sattayA upetaM brahma pratijAnAnasya tad eva pUrvAdhikaraNapratiShiddhaM saprapaJNcatvaM prasajyeta | shrutatvAd adoSha iti cet, na, ekasya anekasvabhAvatvAnupapatteH | atha sattaiSha bodhaH, bodha eva ca sattA, nAnayoH parasparavyAvR^ittir astIti yadyucyeta, tathApi kiM sallakShaNaM brahma, uta bodhalakShaNam, utobhayalakShaNam -- ityayaM vikalpo nirAlambana eva syAt | sUtrANi tv ekAdhikaraNatvenaivAsmAbhir nItAni | api ca brahmaviShayAsu shrutiShu AkAravad anAkArapratipAdanena vipratipannAsu, anAkAre brahmaNi parigR^ihIte, avashyaM vaktavyA itarAsAM shrutInAM gatiH | tAdarthyena prakAshavacca ityAdIni sUtrANyarthavattarANi sampadyante || 

yad apyAhuH -- AkAravAdinyo.api shrutayaH prapaJNcavilayamukhena anAkArapratipattyarthA eva, na pR^ithagarthA iti, tad api na samIcInam iva lakShyate | katham? ye hi paravidyAdhikAre kecit prapaJNcA ucyante, yathA -- yuktA hyasya harayaH shatA dasheti, ayaM vai harayo.ayaM vai dasha ca sahasrANi bahUni cAnantAni ca [bR^i.A.u. 2.5.19] ityevamAdayaH, te bhavantu pravilayArthAH | tad etad brahmApUrvam anaparam anantaram abAhyam [bR^i.A.u. 2.5.19] ityupasaMhArAt | 

ye punar upAsanAvidhAnAdhikAre prapaJNcA ucyante, yathA -- manomayaH prANasharIro bhArUpaH [chA.u. 3.14.2] ityevamAdayaH -- na teShAM pravilayArthatvaM nyAyyam | sa kratuM kurvIta ityevaMjAtIyakena prakR^itenaiva upAsanavidhinA teShAM sambandhAt | shrutyA ca evaMjAtIyakAnAM guNAnAm upAsanArthatve.avakalpamAne na lakShaNayA pravilayArthatvam avakalpate | sarveShAM ca sAdhAraNe pravilayArthatve sati arUpavad eva hi tatpradhAnatvAt iti vinigamanakAraNavacanam anavakAshaM syAt | phalam apyeShAM yathopadeshaM kvacid duritakShayaH, kvacid aishvairyaprAptiH, kvacit kramamuktiH ityavagamyata eva | ityataH pArthagarthyam eva upAsanAvAkyAnAM brahmavAkyAnAM ca nyAyyam, na ekavAkyatvam || 

kathaM ca eShAm ekavAkyatotprekShyata iti vaktavyam -- ekaniyogapratIteH, prayAjadarshapUrNamAsavAkyavad iti cet, na, brahmavAkyeShu niyogAbhAvAt -- vastumAtraparyavasAyIni hi brahmavAkyAni, na niyogopadeshIni ityetadvistareNa pratiShThApitam tat tu samanvayAt ityatra | kiMviShayashcAtra niyogo.abhipreyata iti vaktavyam | puruSho hi niyujyamAnaH kuru iti svavyApAre kasmiMshcin niyujyate | 

nanu dvaitaprapaJNcapravilayo niyogaviShayo bhaviShyati -- apravilApite hi dvaitaprapaJNce brahmatattvAbodho na bhavatItyato brahmatattvAvabodhapratyanIkabhUto dvaitaprapaJNcaH pravilApyaH -- yathA svargakAmasya yAgo.anuShThAtavya upadishyate, evam apavargakAmasya prapaJNcapravilayaH | yathA ca tamasi vyavasthitaM ghaTAditattvam avabubhutsamAnena tatpratyanIkabhUtaM tamaH pravilApyate, evaM brahmatattvam avabubhutsamAnena tatpratyanIkabhUtaH prapaJNcaH pravilApayitavyaH | brahmasvabhAvo hi prapaJNcaH, na prapaJNcasvabhAvaM brahma | tena nAmarUpaprapaJNcapravilApanena brahmatattvAvabodho bhavati -- iti | atra vayaM pR^icchAmaH -- ko.ayaM prapaJNcapravilayo nAma? -- kim agnipratApasamparkAt ghR^itakAThinyapravilaya iva prapaJNcapravilayaH kartavyaH, Aho svid ekasmiMshca timirakR^itAnekacandraprapaJNcavat avidyAkR^ito brahmaNi nAmarUpaprapaJNco vidyayA pravilApayitavyaH -- iti | tatra yadi tAvad vidyamAno.ayaM prapaJNcaH dehAdilakShaNa AdhyAtmikaH bAhyashca pR^ithivyAdilakShaNaH pravilApayitavya ityucyeta, sa puruShamAtreNAshakyaH pravilApayitum iti tatpravilayopadesho.ashakyaviShaya eva syAt | ekena ca Adimuktena pR^ithivyAdipravilayaH kR^ita iti idAnIM pR^ithivyAdishUnyaM jagad abhaviShyat | 

atha avidyAdhyasto brahmaNyekasmin ayaM prapaJNco vidyayA pravilApyata iti brUyAt, tato brahmaiva avidyAdhyastaprapaJNcapratyAkhyAnena Avedayitavyam -- ekam evAdvitIyaM [chA.u. 6.2.1], brahma tat satyaM sa AtmA tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7] iti -- tasminn Avedite, vidyA svayam evotpadyate | tayA ca avidyA bAdhyate, tatashca avidyAdhyastaH sakalo.ayaM nAmarUpaprapaJNcaH svapnaprapaJNcavat pravilIyate -- anAvedite tu brahmaNi brahmavij~nAnaM kuru prapaJNcapravilayaM ca iti shatakR^itvo.apyukte na brahmavij~nAnaM prapaJNcapravilayo vA jAyeta | 

nanvavedite brahmaNi tadvij~nAnaviShayaH prapaJNcavilayaviShayo vA niyogaH syAt | na, niShprapaJNcabrahmAtmatvAvedanenaiva ubhayasiddhiH -- rajjusvarUpaprakAshanenaiva 
hi tatsvarUpavij~nAnam avidyAdhyastasarpAdiprapaJNcapravilayashca bhavati | na ca kR^itam eva punaH kriyate || 

niyojyo.api ca prapaJNcAvasthAyAM yo.avagamyate jIvo nAma, sa prapaJNcapakShasyaiva vA syAt, brahmapakShasyaiva vA -- prathame vikalpe niShprapaJNcabrahmatattvapratipAdanena pR^ithivyAdivat jIvasyApi pravilApitatvAt kasya prapaJNcavilaye niyoga ucyeta? kasya vA niyoganiShThatayA mokSho.avAptavya ucyeta? dvitIye.api brahmaiva aniyojyasvabhAvaM jIvasya svarUpam, jIvatvaM tu, avidyAkR^itam eva -- iti pratipAdite brahmaNi niyojyAbhAvAt niyogAbhAva eva | draShTavyAdishabdA api paravidyAdhikArapaThitAH tattvAbhimukhIkaraNapradhAnAH, na tattvAvabodhavidhipradhAnA bhavanti | loke.api -- idaM pashya, idam AkarNayeti ca evaMjAtIyakeShu nirdesheShu praNidhAnamAtraM kurvityucyate, na sAkShAjj~nAnam eva kurviti | j~neyAbhimukhasyApi j~nAnaM kadAcijjAyate, kadAcin na jAyate | tasmAt taM prati j~nAnaviShaya eva darshayitavyo j~nApayitukAmena | tasmin darshite svayam eva yathAviShayaM yathApramANaM ca j~nAnam utpadyate | na ca pramANAntareNa anyathAprasiddhe.arthe anyathAj~nAnaM niyuktasyApyupapadyate | yadi punar niyukto.aham iti anyathA j~nAnaM kuryAt, na tu tat j~nAnam, kiM tarhi, mAnasI sA kriyA | svayam eva ced anyathotpadyeta, bhrAntir eva syAt | j~nAnaM tu pramANajanyaM yathAbhUtaviShayaM ca | na tat niyogashatenApi kArayituM shakyate, na ca pratiShedhashatenApi vArayituM shakyate | na hi tat puruShatantram, vastutantram eva hi tat | ato.api niyogAbhAvaH | 

kiM cAnyat -- niyoganiShThatayaiva paryavasyatyAmnAye, yad abhyupagatam aniyojyabrahmAtmatvaM jIvasya, tad apramANakam eva syAt | atha shAstram eva aniyojyabrahmAtmatvam AcakShIta, tadavabodhe ca puruShaM niyuJNjIta, tato brahmashAstrasyaikasya dvyarthaparatA viruddhArthaparatA ca prasajyeyAtAm | niyogaparatAyAM ca, shrutahAniH ashrutakalpanA karmaphalavan mokShasyAdR^iShTaphalatvam anityatvaM ca -- ityevamAdayo doShA na kenacit parihartuM shakyAH | tasmAd avagatiniShThAnyeva brahmavAkyAni, na niyoganiShThAni | atashca ekaniyogapratIter ekavAkyatetyayuktam || 

abhyupagamyamAne.api ca brahmavAkyeShu niyogasadbhAve, tad ekatvaM niShprapaJNcopadesheShu saprapaJNcopadesheShu cAsiddham | na hi shabdAntarAdibhiH pramANair niyogabhede.avagamyamAne, sarvatra eko niyoga iti shakyam Ashrayitum | prayAjadarshapUrNamAsavAkyeShu tu adhikArAMshenAbhedAt yuktam ekatvam | na tviha saguNanirguNacodanAsu kashcid ekatvakaro.aMsho.asti | na hi bhArUpatvAdayo guNAH prapaJNcapravilayopakAriNaH, nApi prapaJNcavilayo bhArUpatvAdiguNopakArI, parasparavirodhitvAt | na hi kR^itsnaprapaJNcapravilApanaM prapaJNcaikadeshApekShaNaM ca ekasmin dharmiNi yuktaM samAveshayitum | tasmAt asmadukta eva vibhAgaH AkAravadanAkAropadeshAnAM yuktatara iti ||21||

prakR^itaitAvattvAdhikaraNam 
|| 3.2.22 ||

dve vAva brahmaNo rUpe mUrtaM caivAmUrtaM [bR^i.A.u. 2.3.1] ca ityupakramya, paJNcamahAbhUtAni dvairAshyena pravibhajya, amUrtarasasya ca puruShashabdoditasya mAhArajanAdIni rUpANi darshayitvA, punaH paThyate -- athAta Adesho neti neti na hyetasmAd iti netyanyat param asti [bR^i.A.u. 2.3.6] iti | tatra ko.asya pratiShedhasya viShaya iti jij~nAsAmahe | na hyatra idaM tad iti visheShitaM kiMcitpratiShedhyam upalabhyate | itishabdena tu atra pratiShedhyaM kim api samarpyate, neti neti iti itiparatvAt naJNprayogasya | itishabdashcAyaM saMnihitAlambanaH evaMshabdasamAnavR^ittiH prayujyamAno dR^ishyate -- iti ha smopAdhyAyaH kathayati ityevamAdiShu | saMnihitaM cAtra prakaraNasAmarthyAd rUpadvayaM saprapaJNcaM brahmaNaH, tacca brahma, yasya te dve rUpe | tatra naH saMshaya upajAyate -- kim ayaM pratiShedho rUpe rUpavacca ubhayam api pratiShedhati, Aho svid ekataram | yadApyekataram, tadApi kiM brahma pratiShedhati, rUpe parishinaShTi, Aho svid rUpe pratiShedhati, brahma parishinaShTIti || 

tatra prakR^itatvAvisheShAd ubhayam api pratiShedhatItyAshaN^kAmahe -- dvau caitau pratiShedhau, dviH netishabdaprayogAt | tayor ekena saprapaJNcaM brahmaNo rUpaM pratiShidhyate, apareNa rUpavad brahma -- iti bhavati matiH | athavA brahmaiva rUpavat pratiShidhyate | tad dhi vAN^manasAtItatvAd asambhAvyamAnasadbhAvaM pratiShedhArham | na tu rUpaprapaJNcaH pratyakShAdigocaratvAt pratiShedhArhaH | abhyAsastvAd arArthaH ityevaM prApte, brUmaH -- 

prakR^itaitAvattvaM hi pratiShedhati tato bravIti ca bhUyaH ||

na tAvad ubhayapratiShedha upapadyate, shUnyavAdaprasaN^gAt -- kaMcid dhi paramArtham Alambya aparamArthaH pratiShidhyate, yathA rajjvAdiShu sarpAdayaH | tacca parishiShyamANe kasmiMshcid bhAve avakalpate | kR^itsnapratiShedhe tu ko.anyo bhAvaH parishiShyeta ? aparishiShyamANe cAnyasmin, ya itaraH pratiSheddhum Arabhyate pratiSheddhum ashakyatvAt tasyaiva paramArthatvApatteH pratiShedhAnupapattiH | 

nApi brahmapratiShedha upapadyate -- brahma te bravANi [bR^i.A.u. 2.1.1] ityAdyupakramavirodhAt, asann eva sa bhavati | asad brahmeti veda cet [tai.u. 2.6.1] ityAdinindAvirodhAt, astItyevopalabdhavyaH [ka.u. 2.3.13] ityAdyavadhAraNavirodhAt, sarvavedAntavyAkopaprasaN^gAcca | vAN^manasAtItatvam api brahmaNo na abhAvAbhiprAyeNAbhidhIyate | na hi mahatA parikarabandhena brahmavid Apnoti param satyaM j~nAnam anantaM brahma [tai.u. 2.1.1] ityevamAdinA vedAnteShu brahma pratipAdya tasyaiva punar abhAvo.abhilapyeta | prakShAlanAd dhi paN^kasya dUrAd asparshanaM varam iti hi nyAyaH | pratipAdanaprakriyA tu eShA -- yato vAco nivartante | aprApya manasA saha [tai.u. 2.4.1] iti | 

etad uktaM bhavati -- vAN^manasAtItam aviShayAntaHpAtipratyagAtmabhUtaM nityashuddhabuddhamuktasvabhAvaM brahmeti | tasmAd brahmaNo rUpaprapaJNcaM pratiShedhati, parishinaShTi brahmetyavagantavyam || 

tad etad ucyate -- prakR^itaitAvattvaM hi pratiShedhatIti | prakR^itaM yad etAvat iyattAparicchinnaM mUrtAmUrtalakShaNaM brahmaNo rUpaM tad eSha shabdaH pratiShedhati | tad dhi prakR^itaM prapaJNcitaM ca pUrvasmin granthe adhidaivatam adhyAtmaM ca | tajjanitam eva ca vAsanAlakShaNam aparaM rUpam amUrtarasabhUtaM puruShashabdoditaM liN^gAtmavyapAshrayaM mAhArajanAdyupamAbhir darshitam -- amUrtarasasya puruShasya cakShurgrAhyarUpayogitvAnupapatteH | tad etat saprapaJNcaM brahmaNo rUpaM saMnihitAlambanena itikaraNena pratiShedhakaM naJNaM prati upanIyata iti gamyate | brahma tu rUpavisheShaNatvena ShaShThyA nirdiShTaM pUrvasmin granthe, na svapradhAnatvena | prapaJNcite ca tadIye rUpadvaye rUpavataH svarUpajij~nAsAyAm idam upakrAntam -- athAta Adesho neti neti iti | tatra kalpitarUpapratyAkhyAnena brahmaNaH svarUpAvedanam iti nirNIyate | tadAspadaM hi idaM samastaM kAryam neti neti iti pratiShiddham | yuktaM ca kAryasya, vAcArambhaNashabdAdibhyo.asattvam iti, neti netIti pratiShedhanam | 

na tu brahmaNaH, sarvakalpanAmUlatvAt | na ca atra iyam AshaN^kA kartavyA -- kathaM hi shAstraM svayam eva brahmaNo rUpadvayaM darshayitvA, svayam eva punaH pratiShedhati -- prakShAlanAd dhi paN^kasya dUrAd asparshanaM varam iti, yataH nedaM shAstraM pratipAdyatvena brahmaNo rUpadvayaM nirdishati, lokaprasiddhaM tu idaM rUpadvayaM brahmaNi kalpitaM parAmR^ishati pratiShedhyatvAya shuddhabrahmasvarUpapratipAdanAya ca -- iti niravadyam | dvau ca etau pratiShedhau yathAsaMkhyanyAyena dve api mUrtAmUrte pratiShedhataH | 

yad vA, pUrvaH pratiShedho bhUtarAshiM pratiShedhati, uttaro vAsanArAshim | athavA neti neti iti vIpsA iyam -- iti iti yAvat kiMcit utprekShyate, tat sarvaM na bhavatItyarthaH -- parigaNitapratiShedhe hi kriyamANe, yadi naitad brahma, kim anyad brahma bhaved iti jij~nAsA syAt | vIpsAyAM tu satyAM samastasya viShayajAtasya pratiShedhAt aviShayaH pratyagAtmA brahmeti, jij~nAsA nivartate | tasmAt prapaJNcam eva brahmaNi kalpitaM pratiShedhati, parishinaShTi brahmeti nirNayaH || 

itashca eSha eva nirNayaH, yataH -- tataH prapaJNcapratiShedhAt, bhUyo brahma bravIti, anyat param asti iti | abhAvAvasAne hi pratiShedhe kriyamANe, kim anyat param astIti brUyAt | tatraiShA akSharayojanA -- neti netIti brahmAdishya, tam evAdeshaM punar nirvakti -- neti netItyasya ko.arthaH ? na hyetasmAd brahmaNo vyatiriktam astIti, ataH neti netItyucyate, na punaH svayam eva nAstItyarthaH | tacca darshayati -- anyat param apratiShiddhaM brahmAstIti | yadA punar evam akSharANi yojyante -- na hi, etasmAt iti na iti na iti prapaJNcapratiShedharUpAt AdeshanAt, anyat paramAdeshanaM brahmaNo.astIti -- tadA, tato bravIti ca bhUyaH ityetat nAmadheyaviShayaM yojayitavyam -- atha nAmadheyaM satyasya satyam iti prANA vai satyaM teShAm eSha satyam iti hi bravIti -- iti | tacca brahmAvasAne pratiShedhe samaJNjasaM bhavati | abhAvAvasAne tu pratiShedhe, kim satyasya satyam ityucyeta? tasmAd brahmAvasAno.ayaM pratiShedhaH, nAbhAvAvasAnaH -- ityadhyavasyAmaH ||22||

|| 3.2.23 ||

tad avyaktam Aha hi ||

yat tat pratiShiddhAt prapaJNcajAtAd anyat paraM brahma, tad asti cet, kasmAn na gR^ihyata iti, ucyate -- tat avyaktam anindriyagrAhyam, sarvadR^ishyasAkShitvAt | Aha hyevaM shrutiH -- 

na cakShuShA gR^ihyate nApi vAcA 
nAnyair devaiH tapasA karmaNA vA || [mu.u. 3.1.8]

sa eSha neti netyAtmA gR^ihyo na hi gR^ihyate yat tad apAshyam agrAhyam yadA hyevaiSha etasminn adR^ishye.anAtmye.anirukte.anilayane [bR^i.A.u. 3.9.26] ityAdyA | smR^itir api -- avyakto.ayam acintyo.ayam avikAryo.ayam ucyate [gItA 2.29] ityAdyA ||23||


|| 3.2.24 ||

api ca saMrAdhane pratyakShAnumAnAbhyAm ||

api ca enam AtmAnaM nirastasamastaprapaJNcam avyaktaM saMrAdhanakAle pashyanti yoginaH | saMrAdhanaM ca bhaktidhyAnapraNidhAnAdyanuShThAnam | kathaM punar avagamyate -- saMrAdhanakAle pashyantIti? pratyakShAnumAnAbhyAm, shrutismR^itibhyAm ityarthaH | tathA hi shrutiH -- 

parAJNci khAni vyatR^iNat svayambhUs
tasmAt parAM pashyati nAntarAtman | 
kashcid dhIraH pratyag AtmAnam aikShad
AvR^ittacakShur amR^itatvam icchan || [ka.u. 2.1.1] iti | 

j~nAnaprasAdena vishuddhasattvaH 
tataH tu taM pashyate niShkalaM dhyAyamAnaH || [mu.u. 3.1.8] iti caivamAdyA | 

smR^itir api -- 
ye vinidrA jitashvAsAH saMtuShTAH saMyatendriyAH | 
jyotiH pashyanti yuJNjAnAH tasmai yogAtmane namaH || 
yoginaH taM prapashyanti bhagavantaM sanAtanam || iti caivamAdyA ||24|| 

|| 3.2.25 ||

nanu saMrAdhyasaMrAdhakabhAvAbhyupagamAt parAparAtmanor anyatvaM syAd iti | netyucyate -- 

prakAshAdivaccAvaisheShyaM, prakAshashca karmaNyabhyAsAt || 

yathA prakAshAkAshasavitR^iprabhR^itayo.aN^gulikarakodakaprabhR^itiShu karmasu upAdhibhUteShu savisheShA ivAvabhAsante, na ca svAbhAvikIm avisheShAtmatAM jahati | evam upAdhinimitta evAyam AtmabhedaH, svataH tu aikAtmyam eva | tathA hi vedAnteShu abhyAsena asakR^it jIvaprAj~nayor abhedaH pratipAdyate ||25||

|| 3.2.26 ||

ato.anantena tathA hi liN^gam ||

atashca svAbhAvikatvAd abhedasya, avidyAkR^itatvAcca bhedasya, vidyayA avidyAM vidhUya jIvaH pareNa anantena prAj~nena AtmanA ekatAM gacchati | tathA hi liN^gam -- sa yo ha vai tat paramaM brahma veda brahmaiva bhavati [mu.u. 3.2.9], brahmaiva san brahmApyeti [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.7] ityAdi ||26||

|| 3.2.27 ||

ubhayavyapadeshAt tu ahikuNDalavat ||

tasminn eva saMrAdhyasaMrAdhakabhAve matAntaram upanyasyati, svamatavishuddhaye | kvacit jIvaprAj~nayor bhedo vyapadishyate -- tataH tu taM pashyate niShkalaM dhyAyamAnaH [mu.u. 3.1.8] iti dhyAtR^idhyAtavyatvena draShTR^idraShTavyatvena ca | parAt paraM puruSham upaiti divyam [mu.u. 3.2.8] iti gantR^igantavyatvena | yaH sarvANi bhUtAnyantaro yamayati iti niyantR^iniyantavyatvena ca | kvacit tu tayor evAbhedo vyapadishyate -- tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7], ahaM brahmAsmi [bR^i.A.u. 1.4.10], eSha ta AtmA sarvAntaraH eSha ta AtmAntaryAmyamR^itaH iti | tatraivam ubhayavyapadeshe sati, yadyabheda eva ekAntato gR^ihyate, bhedavyapadesho nirAlambana eva syAt | ata ubhayavyapadeshadarshanAt ahikuNDalavad atra tattvaM bhavitum arhati -- yathA ahiH ityabhedaH, kuNDalAbhogaprAMshutvAdInIti ca bhedaH, evam ihApIti ||

|| 3.2.28 || 

prakAshAshrayavad vA tejastvAt ||

athavA prakAshAshrayavad etat pratipattavyam -- yathA prakAshaH sAvitraH tadAshrayashca savitA nAtyantabhinnau, ubhayor api tejastvAvisheShAt | atha ca bhedavyapadeshabhAjau bhavataH -- evam ihApIti ||28||

|| 3.2.29 || 

pUrvavad vA ||

yathA vA pUrvam upanyastam -- prakAshAdivaccAvaisheShyam iti, tathaiva etad bhavitum arhati | tathA hi avidyAkR^itatvAd bandhasya vidyayA mokSha upapadyate | yadi punaH paramArthata eva baddhaH kashcid AtmA ahikuNDalanyAyena parasya AtmanaH saMsthAnabhUtaH, prakAshAshrayanyAyena ca ekadeshabhUto.abhyupagamyeta | tataH pAramArthikasya bandhasya 
tiraskartum ashakyatvAt mokShashAstravaiyarthyaM prasajyeta | na cAtra ubhAvapi bhedAbhedau shrutiH tulyavad vyapadishati | abhedam eva hi pratipAdyatvena nirdishati, bhedaM tu pUrvaprasiddham evAnuvadati arthAntaravivakShayA | tasmAt prakAshAdivaccAvaisheShyam ityeSha eva siddhAntaH ||29||

|| 3.2.30 ||

pratiShedhAcca ||

itashca eSha eva siddhAntaH, yat kAraNaM parasmAd Atmano.anyaM cetanaM pratiShedhati shAstram -- nAnyo.ato.asti draShTA ityevamAdi | athAta Adesho neti neti tad etad brahmApUrvam anaparam anantaram abAhyam iti ca brahmavyatiriktaprapaJNcanirAkaraNAt brahmamAtraparisheShAcca eSha eva siddhAnta iti gamyate ||30|| 

|| 3.2.31 || 

yadetat nirastasamastaprapaJNcaM brahma nirdhAritam, asmAt param anyat tattvam asti nAstIti shrutivipratipatteH saMshayaH | kAnicid dhi vAkyAni ApAtenaiva pratibhAsamAnAni brahmaNo.api param anyat tattvaM pratipAdayantIva | teShAM hi parihAram abhidhAtum ayam upakramaH kriyate -- 

paramataH setUnmAnasambandhabhedavyapadeshebhyaH ||

param ato brahmaNo.anyat tattvaM bhavitum arhati | kutaH? setuvyapadeshAt unmAnavyapadeshAt sambandhavyapadeshAt bhedavyapadeshAcca | setuvyapadeshaH tAvat -- atha ya AtmA sa setur vidhR^itiH [chA.u. 8.4.1] ityAtmashabdAbhihitasya brahmaNaH setutvaM saN^kIrtayati | setushabdashca hi loke jalasantAnavicchedakare mR^iddArvAdipracaye prasiddhaH | iha ca setushabdaH Atmani prayukta iti laukikasetoH iva Atmasetor anyasya vastuno.astitvaM gamayati | setu tIrtvA [chA.u. 8.4.2] iti ca taratishabdaprayogAt -- yathA laukikaM setuM tIrtvA jAN^galam asetuM prApnoti, evam AtmAnaM setuM tIrtvA anAtmAnam asetuM prApnotIti gamyate | 

unmAnavyapadeshashca bhavati -- tad etad brahma catuShpAt  aShTAshaphaM  ShoDashakalam  iti | yacca loke unmitam etAvad idam iti paricchinnaM kArShApaNAdi, tato.anyad vastu astIti prasiddham | tathA brahmaNo.apyunmAnAt tato.anyena vastunA bhavitavyam iti gamyate | tathA sambandhavyapadesho bhavati -- satA somya tadA sampanno bhavati [chA.u. 6.8.1] iti, shArIra AtmA prAj~nenAtmanA sampariShvaktaH [bR^i.A.u 4.3.21] iti ca | mitAnAM ca mitena sambandho dR^iShTAH, yathA narANAM nagareNa | jIvAnAM ca brahmaNA sambandhaM vyapadishati suShuptau | ataH tataH paramanyad amitamastIti gamyate | bhedavyapadeshashca enamarthaM gamayati | tathA hi -- atha ya eSho.antarAditye hiraNmayaH puruSho dR^ishyate ityAdityAdhAram IshvaraM vyapadishya, tato bhedena akShyAdhAram IshvaraM vyapadishati -- atha ya eSho.akShiNi puruSho dR^ishyate iti | atideshaM ca asya amunA rUpAdiShu karoti -- tasyaitasya tad eva rUpaM yadamuShya rUpaM yAvamuShya geShNau tau geShNau yannAma tannAma iti | sAvadhikaM ca Ishvaratvam ubhayor vyapadishati -- ye cAmuShmAt parAJNco lokAsteShAM ceShTo devakAmAnAM ca ityekasya, ye caitasmAd arvAJNco lokAsteShAM ceShTo manuShyakAmAnAM ca ityekasya, yathA idaM mAgadhasya rAjyam, idaM vaidehasyeti | evam etebhyaH setvAdivyapadeshebhyo brahmaNaH paramastIti || 

|| 3.2.32 ||

evaM prApte, pratipAdyate -- 

sAmAnyAt tu ||

tushabdena pradarshitAM prAptiM niruNaddhi | na brahmaNo.anyat kiMcid bhavitum arhati, pramANAbhAvAt -- na hyanyasyAstitve kiMcit pramANam upalabhAmahe | sarvasya hi janimato vastujAtasya janmAdi brahmaNo bhavatIti nirdhAritam, ananyatvaM ca kAraNAt kAryasya | na ca brahmavyatiriktaM kiMcit ajaM sambhavati, sad eva somyedam agra AsId ekam evAdvitIyam ityavadhAraNAt | ekavij~nAnena ca sarvavij~nAnapratij~nAnAt na brahmavyatiriktavastvastitvam avakalpate | 

nanu setvAdivyapadeshAH brahmavyatiriktaM tattvaM sUcayantItyuktam | netyucyate -- setu -- vyapadeshaH tAvat na brahmaNo bAhyasya sadbhAvaM pratipAdayituM kShamate | setur Atmeti hi Aha, na ataH paramastIti | tatra parasmin asati setutvaM nAvakalpata iti paraM kim api kalpyeta | na caitat nyAyyam | haTaho hi aprasiddhakalpanA | api ca setuvyapadeshAd Atmano laukikasetunidarshanena sabAhyavastutAM prasaJNjayatA mR^iddArumayatApi prAsaN^kShyata | na caitan nyAyyam, ajatvAdishrutivirodhAt | setusAmAnyAt tu setushabda Atmani prayukta iti shliShyate | jagataH tanmaryAdAnAM ca vidhArakatvaM setusAmAnyam AtmanaH | ataH setuH iva setuH -- iti prakR^ita AtmA stUyate | setuM tIrtvA ityapi taratiH atikramAsambhavAt prApnotyartha eva vartate -- yathA vyAkaraNaM tIrNa iti prAptaH ucyate, na atikrAntaH, tadvat ||32||

|| 3.2.33 || 

buddhyarthaH pAdavat ||

yad apyuktam -- unmAnavyapadeshAd asti param iti, tatrAbhidhIyate -- unmAnavyapadesho.api na brahmavyatiriktavastvastitvapratipattyarthaH | kim arthaH tarhi? buddhyarthaH, upAsanArtha iti yAvat | catuShpAd aShTAshaphaM ShoDashakalam ityevaMrUpA -- buddhiH kathaM nu nAma brahmaNi sthirA syAt ? iti -- vikAradvAreNa brahmaNa unmAnakalpanaiva kriyate | na hi avikAre.anante brahmaNi sarveH pumbhiH shakyA buddhiH sthApayitum, mandamadhyamottamabuddhitvAt puMsAm iti | pAdavat -- yathA manAkAshayor adhyAtmam adhidaivataM ca brahmapratIkayor AmnAtayoH, catvAro vAgAdayo manaHsambandhinaH pAdAH kalpyante, catvArashca agnyAdaya AkAshasambandhinaH -- AdhyAnAya, tadvat | athavA pAdavad iti -- yathA kArShApaNe pAdavibhAgo vyavahAraprAcuryAya kalpyate -- na hi sakalenaiva kArShApaNena sarvadA sarve janA vyavahartum Ishate, krayavikraye parimANAniyamAt, tadvad ityarthaH ||33||

|| 3.2.34 ||

sthAnavisheShAt prakAshAdivat ||

iha sUtre dvayor api sambandhabhedavyapadeshayoH parihAro.abhidhIyate | yad apyuktam -- sambandhavyapadeshAt bhedavyapadeshAcca paramataH syAditi, tadapyasat | yata ekasyApi sthAnavisheShApekShayA etau vyapadeshAv upapadyete | sambandhavyapadeshe tAvad ayam arthaH -- buddhyAdyupAdhisthAnavisheShayogAd udbhUtasya visheShavij~nAnasya upAdhyupashame ya upashamaH, sa paramAtmanA sambandhaH -- ityupAdhyapekShayA upacaryate, na parimitatvApekShayA | tathA bhedavyapadesho.api brahmaNa upAdhibhedApekShayaiva upacaryate, na svarUpabhedApekShayA | prakAshAdivad iti upamopAdAnam -- yathA ekasya prakAshasya sauryasya cAndramasasya vA upAdhiyogAd upajAtavisheShasya upAdhyupashamAt sambandhavyapadesho bhavati, upAdhibhedAcca bhedavyapadeshaH | yathA vA, sUcIpAshAkAshAdiShUpAdhyapekShayaivaitau sambandhabhedavyapadeshau bhavataH, tadvat ||24||

|| 3.2.35 ||

upapatteshca ||

upapadyate ca atra IdR^isha eva sambandhaH, nAnyAdR^ishaH -- svam apIto bhavati iti hi svarUpasambandham enam Amananti | svarUpasya ca anapAyitvAt na naranagaranyAyena sambandho ghaTate | upAdhikR^itasvarUpatirobhAvAt tu svam apIto bhavati ityupapadyate | tathA bhedo.api nAnyAdR^ishaH sambhavati, bahutarashrutiprasiddhaikeshvaratvavirodhAt | tathA ca shrutir ekasyApyAkAshasya sthAnakR^itaM bhedavyapadesham upapAdayati -- yo.ayaM bahirdhA puruShAd AkAshaH yo.ayam antaH puruSha AkAshaH yo.ayam antarhR^idaya AkAshaH [chA.u. 3.12.7] iti ||35||

|| 3.2.36 ||

tathAnyapratiShedhAt ||

evaM setvAdivyapadeshAn parapakShahetUn unmathya samprati svapakShaM hetvantareNopasaMharati | tathAnyapratiShedhApi na brahmaNaH paraM vastvantaram astIti gamyate | tathA hi -- sa evAdhastAt... aham evAdhastAt [chA.u. 7.25.1], AtmaivAdhastAt sarvaM taM parAd Adyo.anyatrAtmanaH sarvaM veda [bR^i.A.u 1.4.7], brahmaivedaM sarvam [bR^i.A.u 2.5.1], AtmaivedaM sarvam neha nAnAsti kiMcana [chA.u. 7.25.2], yasmAt paraM nAparam asti kiMcit tad etad brahmApUrvam anaparam anantaram abAhyam ityevamAdIni vAkyAni svaprakaraNasthAni anyArthatvena pariNetum ashakyAni brahmavyatiriktaM vastvantaraM vArayanti | sarvAntarashruteshca na paramAtmano.anyo.antarAtmA astItyavagamyate ||36||

|| 3.2.37 ||

anena sarvagatatvamAyAmashabdAdibhyaH ||

anena setvAdivyapadeshanirAkaraNena anyapratiShedhasamAshrayaNena ca sarvagatatvam apyAtmanaH siddhaM bhavati | anyathA hi tan na sidhyet | setvAdivyapadesheShu hi mukhyeShvaN^gIkriyamANeShu pariccheda AtmanaH prasajyeta, setvAdInAm evam AtmakatvAt | tathA anyapratiShedhe.apyasati, vastu vastvantarAd vyAvartata iti pariccheda eva AtmanaH prasajyeta | sarvagatatvaM ca asya AyAmashabdAdibhyo.avagamyate | AyAmashabdaH vyAptivacanaH shabdaH | yAvAn vA ayam AkAshaH tAvAn eSho.antarhR^idaya AkAshaH AkAshavat sarvagatashca nityaH jyAyAn divaH jyAyAn AkAshAt -- nityaH sarvagataH sthANur acalo.ayaM sanAtanaH [gItA 2.24] ityevamAdayo hi shrutismR^itinyAyAH sarvagatatvam Atmano.avabodhayanti ||27||

  -- o)0(o -- 
phalAdhikaraNam

|| 3.2.38 || 

tasyaiva brahmaNo vyAvahArikyAm IshitrIshitavyavibhAgAvasthAyAm, ayam anyaH svabhAvo varNyate | yad etat iShTAniShTavyAmishralakShaNaM karmaphalaM saMsAragocaraM trividhaM prasiddhaM jantUnAm, kim etat karmaNo bhavati, Aho svid IshvarAd iti bhavati vicAraNA | 

phalam ata upapatteH ||

tatra tAvat pratipAdyate -- phalam ata IshvarAt bhavitum arhati | kutaH? upapatteH | sa hi sarvAdhyakShaH sR^iShTisthitisaMhArAn vicitrAn vidadhat deshakAlavisheShAbhij~natvAt karmiNAM karmAnurUpaM phalaM sampAdayatItyupapadyate | karmaNaH tu anukShaNavinAshinaH kAlAntarabhAvi phalaM bhavatItyanupapannam, abhAvAd bhAvAnutpatteH | syAd etat -- karma vinashyat svakAlam eva svAnurUpaM phalaM janayitvA vinashyati, tat phalaM kAlAntaritaM kartrA bhokShyata iti | tad api na parishudhyati, prAgbhoktR^isambandhAt phalatvAnupapatteH -- yatkAlaM hi yat sukhaM duHkhaM vA AtmanA bhujyate, tasyaiva loke phalatvaM prasiddham | na hi asambaddhasyAtmanA sukhasya duHkhasya vA phalatvaM pratiyanti laukikAH | athocyeta -- mA bhUt karmAnantaraM phalotpAdaH, karmakAryAd apUrvAt phalam utpatsyata iti, tad api nopapadyate, apUrvasyAcetanasya kAShThaloShTAsamasya cetanenApravartitasya pravR^ittyanupapatteH, tadastitve eva pramANAbhAvAt | arthApattiH pramANam iti cet, na, Ishvarasiddher arthApattikShayAt ||38||

|| 3.2.39 || 

shrutatvAcca || 
 
na kevalam upapatter eva IshvaraM phalahetuM kalpayAmaH, kiM tarhi shrutatvAd api Ishvaram eva phalahetuM manyAmahe, tathA ca shrutir bhavati -- sa vA eSha mahAn ajaH, AtmAnnAdo vasudAnaH [bR^i.A.u 4.4.24] ityevaMjAtIyakA ||39||

|| 3.2.40 || 

dharmaM jaiminir ata eva ||

jaiminiH tvacAryo dharmaM phalasya dAtAraM manyate, ata eva hetoH -- shruteH upapatteshca | shrUyate tAvad ayam arthaH -- svargakAmo yajeta [ya.ve. 2.5.5] ityevamAdiShu vAkyeShu | tatra ca vidhishruter viShayabhAvopagamAt yAgaH svargasyotpAdaka iti gamyate | anyathA hi ananuShThAtR^iko yAga Apadyeta | tatra asya upadeshavaiyarthyaM syAt |

nanu anukShaNavinAshinaH karmaNaH phalaM nopapadyata iti, parityakto.ayaM pakShaH | naiSha doShaH, shrutiprAmANyAt -- shrutishcet pramANam, yathAyaM karmaphalasambandhaH shruta upapadyate, tathA kalpayitavyaH | na ca anutpAdya kim apyapUrvaM karma vinashyat kAlAntaritaM phalaM dAtuM shaknoti | ataH karmaNo vA sUkShmA kAcid uttarAvasthA phalasya vA pUrvAvasthA apUrvaM nAma astIti tarkyate | upapadyate ca ayam artha uktena prakAreNa | IshvaraH tu phalaM dadAtItyanupapannam, avicitrasya kAraNasya vicitrakAryAnupapatteH vaiShamyanairghR^iNyaprasaN^gAt, tadanuShThAnavaiyarthyApatteshca | tasmAt dharmAd eva phalam iti ||40||

|| 3.2.41 || 

pUrvaM tu bAdarAyaNo hetuvyapadeshAt ||

bAdarAyaNaH tvacAryaH pUrvoktam eva IshvaraM phalahetuM manyate | kevalAt karmaNo.apUrvAd vA kevalAt phalam ityayaM pakShaH tushabdena vyAvartyate | karmApekShAt apUrvApekShAd vA yathA tathAstu IshvarAt phalam iti siddhAntaH | kutaH? hetuvyapadeshAt | dharmAdharmayor api hi kArayitR^itvena Ishvaro hetuH vyapadishyate, phalasya ca dAtR^itvena -- eSha hyeva sAdhu karma kArayati taM yamebhyo lokebhya unninIShate | eSha u evAsAdhu karma kArayati taM yam adho ninIShate [kau.u. 3.8] iti | smaryate ca ayam artho bhagavadgItAsu -- 

yo yo yAM yAM tanuM bhaktaH shraddhayArcitum icchati | 
tasya tasyAcalAM shraddhAM tAm eva vidadhAmyaham || 
sa tayA shraddhayA yuktaH tasyArAdhanam Ihate | 
labhate ca tataH kAmAn mayaiva vihitAn hitAn || [gItA 7.2122] iti | 

sarvavedAnteShu ca IshvarahetukA eva sR^iShTayo vyapadishyante | tad eva ca Ishvarasya phalahetutvam, yat svakarmAnurUpAH prajAH sR^ijati | vicitrakAryAnupapattyAdayo.api doShAH kR^itaprayatnApekShatvAd Ishvarasya na prasajyante ||41||

iti shrImatparamahaMsaparivrAjakAcAryasya shrIgovindabhagavatpUjyapAdashiShyasya shrImacchaN^karabhagavataH kR^itau shArIrakamImAMsAsUtrabhAShye
tR^itIyAdhyAyasya dvitIyaH pAdaH ||
|| 3.2 ||

  -- o)0(o -- 
 
(3.3)
|| tR^itIyo.adhyAye tR^itIyaH pAdaH || 

atra parAparabrahmavidyAguNopasaMhAravivaraNam ||

1. sarvavedAntapratyayAdhikaraNam

|| 3.3.1 ||

vyAkhyAtaM vij~neyasya brahmaNaH tattvam | idAnIM tu prativedAntaM vij~nAnAni bhidyante na veti vicAryate |

nanu vij~neyaM brahma pUrvAparAdibhedarahitam ekarasaM saindhavaghanavad avadhAritam | tatra kuto vij~nAnabhedAbhedacintAvatAraH ? na hi karmabahutvavad brahmabahutvam api vedAnteShu pratipipAdayiShitam iti shakyaM vaktum | brahmaNa ekavAkyatvAd ekarUpatvAcca | na caikarUpe brahmaNyanekarUpANi vij~nAnAni sambhavanti | na hyanyathArtho.anyathA j~nAnam ityabhrAntaM bhavati | yadi punar ekasmin brahmaNi bahUni vij~nAnAni vedAntAntareShu pratipipAdayiShitAni, teShAm ekam abhrAntaM bhrAntAnItarANItyanAshvAsaprasaN^go vedAnteShu | tasmAn na tAvat prativedAntaM brahmavij~nAnabheda AshaN^kituM shakyate | nApyasya codanAdyavisheShAd abheda ucyate | brahmavij~nAnasyAcodanAlakShaNatvAt | avidhipradhAnair hi vastuparyavasAyibhir brahmavAkyair brahmavij~nAnaM janyata ityavocadAcAryaH -- tat tu samanvayAt [ve.sU. 1.1.4] ityatra |

tat katham imAM bhedAbhedacintAmArabhate ? iti | tad ucyate -- saguNabrahmaviShayA prANAdiviShayA ceyaM vij~nAnabhedAbhedacintetyadoShaH | 

atra hi karmavad upAsanAnAM bhedAbhedau sambhavataH karmavad eva, copAsanAni dR^iShTaphalAni cocyante | kramamuktiphalAni ca kAnicit samyagj~nAnotpattidvAreNa | teShv eShA cintA sambhavati | kiM prativedAntaM vij~nAnabheda Aho svin na ? iti | 

tatra pUrvapakShahetavaH tAvad upanyasyante | nAmnAH tAvad bhedapratipattihetutvaM prasiddhaM jyotirAdiShu | asti cAtra vedAntAntaravihiteShu vij~nAneShvanyad anyan nAma taittirIyakaM vAjasaneyakaM kauthumakaM shATyAyanakam ityevam Adi | tathA rUpabhedo.api karmabhedasya pratipAdakaH prasiddho vaishvadevyAmikShA vAjibhyo vAjinam ityevamAdiShu | asti cAtra rUpabhedaH | tad yathA -- kecicchAkhinaH paJNcAgnividyAyAM ShaShTham aparam agnim Amananti, pare punaH paJNcaiva paThanti | tathA prANasaMvAdAdiShu kecid UnAn vAgAdIn Amananti, kecid adhikAn | tathA dharmavisheSho 'pi karmabhedasya pratipAdaka AshaN^kitaH kArIryAdiShu | asti cAtra dharmavisheShaH | yathAtharvaNikAnAM shirovratam iti | evaM punaruktyAdayo.api bhedahetavo yathAsambhavaM vedAntAntareShu yojayitavyAH | tasmAt prativedAntaM vij~nAnabheda iti | evaM prApte brUmaH -- 

sarvavedAntapratyayaM codanAdyavisheShAt ||

sarvavedAntapratyayAni vij~nAnAni tasmin tasmin vedAnte tAni tAnyeva bhavitum arhanti | kutaH? codanAdyavisheShAt | AdigrahaNena shAkhAntarAdhikaraNasiddhAntasUtroditA abhedahetava ihAkR^iShyante -- saMyogarUpacodanAkhyAvisheShAd ityarthaH | yathA ekasminn agnihotre shAkhAbhede.api puruShaprayatnaH tAdR^isha eva codyate -- juhuyAd iti, evam yo ha vai jyeShThaM ca shreShThaM ca veda iti vAjasaneyinAM chandogAnAM ca tAdR^ishyeva codanA | prayojanasaMyogo.apyavishiShTa eva -- jyeShThashca shreShThashca svAnAM bhavati iti | rUpam apyubhayatra tad eva vij~nAnasya, yad uta jyeShThashreShThAdivisheShaNAnvitaM prANatattvam -- yathA ca dravyadevate yAgasya rUpam, evaM vij~neyaM rUpaM vij~nAnasya | tena hi tat rUpyate | samAkhyApi saiva -- prANavidyeti | tasmAt sarvavedAntapratyayatvaM vij~nAnAnAm | evaM paJNcAgnividyA vaishvAnaravidyA shANDilyavidyetyevam AdiShvapi yojayitavyam | ye tu nAmarUpAdayo bhedahetvAbhAsAH, te prathama eva kANDe na nAmnA syAd acodanAbhidhAnatvAt ityArabhya parihR^itAH ||1||

|| 3.3.2 || 

ihApi kaMcid visheSham AshaN^kya pariharati -- 

bhedAn neti cen naikasyAm api ||

syAd etat -- sarvavedAntapratyayatvaM vij~nAnAnAM guNabhedAt nopapadyate | tathA hi -- vAjasaneyinaH paJNcAgnividyAM prastutya ShaShTham aparam agnim Amananti -- tasyAgnir evAgnir bhavati ityAdinA | chandogAH tu taM na Amananti, paJNcasaMkhyayaiva ca te upasaMharanti -- atha ha ya etAn evaM paJNcAgnIn veda iti | yeShAM ca sa guNo.asti, yeShAM ca nAsti, katham ubhayeShAm ekA vidyopapadyeta ? na ca atra guNopasaMhAraH shakyate pratyetum, paJNcasaMkhyAvirodhAt | tathA prANasaMvAde shreShThAt anyAn caturaH prANAn vAkcakShuHshrotramanAMsi chandogA Amananti | vAjasaneyinaH tu paJNcamam apyAmananti -- reto vai prajApatiH prajAyate ha prajayA pashubhir ya evaM veda iti | AvApodvApabhedAcca vedyabhedo bhavati, vedyabhedAcca vidyAbhedaH, dravyadevatAbhedAd iva yAgasyeti cet -- naiSha doShaH | yata ekasyAm api vidyAyAm evaMjAtIyako guNabheda upapadyate | yadyapi ShaShThasyAgner upasaMhAro na sambhavati, tathApi dyuprabhR^itInAM paJNcAnAm agnInAm ubhayatra pratyabhij~nAyamAnatvAt na vidyAbhedo bhavitum arhati | na hi ShoDashigrahaNAgrahaNayor atirAtro bhidyate | paThyate.api ca ShaShTho.agniH chandogaiH -- taM pretaM diShTam ito.agnaya eva haranti iti | vAjasaneyinaH tu sAmpAdikeShu paJNcasvagniShu anuvR^ittAyAH samirmAdikalpanAyA nivR^ittaye tasyAgnir evAgnir bhavati samit samit ityAdi samAmananti | sa nityAnuvAdaH | athApyupAsanArtha eSha vAdaH, tathApi sa guNaH shakyate chandogair apyupasaMhartum | na cAtra paJNcasaMkhyAvirodha AshaN^kyaH | sAmpAdikAgnyabhiprAyA hi eShA paJNcasaMkhyA nityAnuvAdabhUtA, na vidhisamavAyinI -- ityadoShaH | evaM prANasaMvAdAdiShvapi adhikasya guNasya itaratropasaMhAro na virudhyate | na ca AvApodvApabhedAd vedyabhedo vidyAbhedashcAshaN^kyaH, kasyacid vedyAMshasya AvApodvApayor api bhUyaso vedyarAsher abhedAvagamAt | tasmAd aikavidyam eva ||

|| 3.3.3 ||

svAdhyAyasya tathAtvena hi samAcAre.adhikArAcca, 
savavacca tanniyamaH ||

yad apyuktam -- AtharvaNikAnAM vidyAM prati shirovratAdyapekShaNAt anyeShAM ca tadanapekShaNAt vidyAbheda iti, tat pratyucyate | svAdhyAyasya eSha dharmaH, na vidyAyAH | katham idam avagamyate? yataH, tathAtvena svAdhyAyadharmatvena, samAcAre vedavratopadeshapare granthe, AtharvaNikAH idam api vedavratatvena vyAkhyAtam iti samAmananti | naitad acIrNavrato.adhIte iti ca adhikR^itaviShayAd etacchabdAt adhyayanashabdAcca svopaniShadadhyayanadharma eva eSha iti nirdhAryate | 

nanu teShAm evaitAM brahmavidyAM vadeta shirovrataM vidhivad yaiH tu cIrNam iti brahmavidyAsaMyogashravaNAt, ekaiva sarvatra brahmavidyeti, saN^kIryeta eSha dharmaH -- na, tatrApi etAm iti prakR^itapratyavamarshAt | prakR^itatvaM ca brahmavidyAyAH granthavisheShApekSham -- iti granthavisheShasaMyogyeva eSha dharmaH | savavacca tanniyama iti nidarshananirdeshaH -- yathA ca savAH sapta sauryAdayaH shataudanaparyantAH vedAntaroditatretAgnyanabhisambandhAt AtharvaNoditaikAgnyabhisambandhAcca AtharvaNikAnAm eva niyamyante, tathaiva ayam api dharmaH svAdhyAyavisheShasambandhAt tatraiva niyamyate | tasmAd apyanavadyaM vidyaikatvam ||3||

|| 3.3.4 || 

darshayati ca ||

darshayati ca vedo.api vidyaikatvaM sarvavedAnteShu vedyaikatvopadeshAt -- sarve vedA yat padam Amananti [ka.u. 1.2.15] iti, tathaitaM hyeva bahvR^icA mahatyukthe mImAMsanta etam agnAvadhvaryava etaM mahAvrate chandogAH iti ca | tathA mahad bhayaM vajram udyatam, iti kAThake uktasya IshvaraguNasya bhayahetutvasya taittirIyake bhedadarshananindAyai parAmarsho dR^ishyate -- yadA hyevaiSha etasminn udaram antaraM kurute | atha tasya bhayaM bhavati | tat tv eva bhayaM viduSho.amanvAnasya iti | tathA vAjasaneyake prAdeshamAtrasampAditasya vaishvAnarasya cchAndogye siddhavad upAdAnam -- yaH tv etam evaM prAdeshamAtram abhivimAnam AtmAnaM vaishvAnaram upAste iti | tathA sarvavedAntapratyayatvena anyatra vihitAnAm ukthAdInAm anyatropAsanavidhAnAya upAdAnAt prAyadarshananyAyena upAsanAnAm api sarvavedAntapratyayatvasiddhiH ||4||

 -- o)0(o -- 
2. upasaMhArAdhikaraNam

|| 3.3.5 ||

upasaMhAro.arthAbhedAd vidhisheShavat samAne ca ||
 
idaM prayojanasUtram | sthite caivaM sarvavedAntapratyayatve sarvavij~nAnAnAm, anyatroditAnAM vij~nAnaguNAnAm, anyatrApi samAne vij~nAne upasaMhAro bhavati | arthAbhedAt -- ya eva hi teShAM guNAnAm ekatra artho vishiShTAvij~nAnopakAraH, sa eva anyatrApi | ubhayatrApi hi tad evaikaM vij~nAnam | tasmAd upasaMhAraH | vidhisheShavat -- yathA vidhisheShANAm agnihotrAdidharmANAm, tad eva ekam agnihotrAdi karma sarvatreti, arthAbhedAt upasaMharaNam | evam ihApi | yadi hi vij~nAnabhedo bhavet, tato vij~nAnAntaranibaddhatvAd guNAnAm, prakR^itivikR^itibhAvAbhAvAcca na syAd upasaMhAraH | vij~nAnaikatve tu naivam iti | asyaiva tu prayojanasUtrasya prapaJNcaH sarvAbhedAt ityArabhya bhaviShyati ||5||

 -- o)0(o -- 
3. anyathAtvAdhikaraNam 

|| 3.3.6 || 

anyathAtvaM shabdAd iti cen nAvisheShAt ||

vAjasaneyake -- te ha devA Ucur hantAsurAn yaj~na udgIthenAtyayAm eti | te ha vAcam UcuH tvaM na udgAya [bR^i.A.u. 1.2.12] iti prakramya, vAgAdIn prANAn asurapApmaviddhatvena ninditvA, mukhyaprANaparigrahaH paThyate -- atha hemam AsanyaM prANam UcuH tvaM na udgAyeti tatheti tebhya eSha prANa udagAyat [bR^i.A.u. 1.2.7] iti | tathA chAndogye.api, tad dha devA udgItham Ajahrur anenainAn abhibhaviShyAmaH [chA.u. 1.2.1] iti prakramya, itarAn prANAn asurapApmaviddhatvena ninditvA, tathaiva mukhyaprANaparigrahaH paThyate -- atha ha ya evAyaM mukhyaH prANaH tam udgItham upAsAMcakrire [chA.u. 1.5.3] iti | ubhayatrApi ca prANaprashaMsayA prANavidyAvidhir adhyavasIyate | 

tatra saMshayaH -- kim atra vidyAbhedaH syAt, Aho svit vidyaikatvam iti | kiM tAvat prAptam pUrveNa nyAyena vidyaikatvam iti | 

nanu na yuktaM vidyaikatvam, prakramabhedAt | anyathA hi prakramante vAjasaneyinaH, anyathA chandogAH -- tvaM na udgAya [bR^i.A.u. 1.2.2] iti vAjasaneyina udgIthasya kartR^itvena prANam Amananti, chandogAH tu udgIthatvena tam udgItham upAsAMcakrire [chA.u. 1.2.7] iti, tat kathaM vidyaikatvaM syAd iti cet -- naiSha doShaH | na hi etAvatA visheSheNa vidyaikatvam apagacchati, avisheShasyApi bahutarasya pratIyamAnatvAt | tathA hi -- devAsurasaMgrAmopakramatvam, asurAtyayAbhiprAyaH, udgIthopanyAsaH, vAgAdisaN^kIrtanam, tannindayA mukhyaprANavyapAshrayaH, tadvIryAcca asuravidhvaMsanam ashmaloShTAnidarshanena -- ityevaM bahavo.arthA ubhayatrApyavishiShTAH pratIyante | vAjasaneyake.api ca udgIthasAmAnAdhikaraNyaM prANasya shrutam -- eSha u vA udgIthaH iti | tasmAcchAndogye.api kartR^itvaM lakShayitavyam | tasmAcca vidyaikatvam iti ||6||

|| 3.3.7 || 

na vA prakaraNabhedAt parovarIyastvAdivat ||

na vA vidyaikatvam atra nyAyyam | vidyAbheda eva atra nyAyyaH | kasmAt? prakaraNabhedAt, prakramabhedAd ityarthaH | tathA hi iha prakramabhedo dR^ishyate, chAndogye tAvat -- om ityetad akSharam udgItham upAsIta [chA.u. 1.1.1] ityevam udgIthAvayavasya oMkArasya upAsyatvaM prastutya, rasatamatvAdiguNopavyAkhyAnaM tatra kR^itvA, atha khalv etasyaivAkSharasyopavyAkhyAnaM bhavati [chA.u. 1.1.10] iti punar api tam eva udgIthAvayavam oMkAram anuvartya, devAsurAkhyAyikAdvAreNa tam prANam udgItham upAsAMcakrire ityAha | tatra yadi udgIthashabdena sakalA bhaktir abhipreyeta, tasyAshca kartA udgAtA R^itvik, tata upakramashcoparudhyeta, lakShaNA ca prasajyeta | upakramatantreNa ca ekasmin vAkye upasaMhAreNa bhavitavyam | tasmAt atra tAvat udgIthAvayave oMkAre prANadR^iShTir upadishyate | 

vAjasaneyake tu udgIthashabdena avayavagrahaNe kAraNAbhAvAt sakalaiva bhaktir Avedyate | tvaM na udgAya ityapi tasyAH kartA udgAtA R^itvik prANatvena nirUpyata iti -- prasthAnAntaram | yad api tatra udgIthasAmAnAdhikaraNyaM prANasya, tad api udgAtR^itvenaiva didarshayiShitasya prANasya sarvAtmatvapratipAdanArtham iti na vidyaikatvam Avahati | sakalabhaktiviShaya eva ca tatrApi udgIthashabda iti vaiShamyam | na ca prANasyodgAtR^itvam asambhavena hetunA parityajyate, udgIthabhAvavat udgAtR^ibhAvasyApi upAsanArthatvena upadishyamAnatvAt | prANavIryeNaiva ca udgAtA audgAtraM karotIti nAstyasambhavaH | 

tathA ca tatraiva shrAvitam -- vAcA ca hyeva sa prANena codagAyat [bR^i.A.u. 1.2.24] iti | na ca vivakShitArthabhede.avagamyamAne vAkyacchAyAnukAramAtreNa samAnArthatvam adhyavasAtuM yuktam | tathA hi -- abhyudayavAkye pashukAmavAkye ca tredhA taNDulAn vibhajed ye madhyamAH syuH tAn agnaye dAtre puroDAsham aShTakapAlaM kuryAt ityAdi nirdeshasAmye.api, upakramabhedAt abhyudayavAkye devatApanayo.adhyavasitaH, pashukAmavAkye tu yAgavidhiH -- tathA ihApi upakramabhedAt vidyAbhedaH | parovarIyastvAdivat -- yathA paramAtmadR^iShTyAdhyAsasAmye.api, AkAsho hyevaibhyo jyAyAn AkAshaH parAyaNam sa eSha parovarIyAn udgIthaH sa eSho.anantaH iti parovarIyastvaguNavishiShTAm udgIthopAsanam akShyAdityAdigatahiraNyashmashrutvAdiguNavishiShTodgIthopAsanAt bhinnam | na ca itaretaraguNopasaMhAra ekasyAm api shAkhAyAm, tadvat shAkhAntarastheShvapi evaMjAtIyakeShu upAsaneShviti ||7||

|| 3.3.8 ||

saMj~nAtashcettad uktam asti tu tad api || 

athocyeta -- saMj~naikatvAt vidyaikatvam atra nyAyyam, udgIthavidyetyubhayatrApi ekA saMj~neti, tad api nopapadyate | uktaM hyetat -- na vA prakaraNabhedAt parovarIyastvAdivat iti | tad eva ca atra nyAyyataraM shrutyakSharAnugataM hi | tat saMj~naikatvaM tu shrutyakSharabAhyam udgIthashabdamAtrayogAt laukikair vyavahartR^ibhir upacaryate | asti ca etat saMj~naikatvaM prasiddhabhedeShvapi parovarIyastvAdyupAsaneShu -- udgIthavidyeti | tathA prasiddhabhedAnAm api agnihotradarshapUrNamAsAdInAM kAThakaikagranthaparipaThitAnAM kAThakasaMj~naikatvaM dR^ishyate, tathehApi bhaviShyati | yatra tu nAsti kashcit evaMjAtIyako bhedahetuH, tatra bhavatu saMj~naikatvAt vidyaikatvam -- yathA saMvargavidyAdiShu ||8||

 -- o)0(o -- 

vyAptyadhikaraNam

|| 3.3.9 ||

om ityetad akSharam udgItham upAsIta ityatra akSharodgIthashabdayoH sAmAnAdhikaraNye shrUyamANe adhyAsApavAdaikatvavisheShaNapakShANAM pratibhAsanAt katamo.atra pakSho nyAyyaH syAd iti vicAraH | tatra adhyAso nAma -- dvayor vastunoH anivartitAyAm eva anyatarabuddhau anyatarabuddhir adhyasyate | yasmin itarabuddhir adhyasyate, anuvartata eva tasmin tadbuddhiH, adhyastetarabuddhAvapi -- yathA nAmni brahmabuddhAvadhyasyamAnAyAm api anuvartata eva nAmabuddhiH, na brahmabuddhyA nivartate -- yathA vA pratimAdiShu viShNvAdibuddhyadhyAsaH -- evam ihApi akShare udgIthabuddhir adhyasyeta, udgIthe vA akSharabuddhiH iti | apavAdo nAma -- yatra kasmiMshcid vastuni pUrvaniviShTAyAM mithyAbuddhau nishcitAyAm, pashcAd upajAyamAnA yathArthA buddhiH pUrvaniviShTAyA mithyAbuddhiH nivartikA bhavati -- yathA dehendriyasaMghAte AtmabuddhiH, Atmanyeva AtmabuddhyA pashcAdbhAvinyA tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7] ityanayA yathArthabuddhyA nivartyate -- yathA vA digbhrAntibuddhiH digyAthAtmyabuddhyA nivartyate -- evam ihApi akSharabuddhyA udgIthabuddhir nivartyeta, udgIthabuddhyA vA akSharabuddhiH iti | ekatvaM tu akSharodgIthashabdayor anatiriktArthavR^ittitvam -- yathA dvijottamo brAhmaNo bhUmideva iti | visheShaNaM punaH sarvavedavyApina om ityetasyAkSharasya grahaNaprasaN^ge audgAtravisheShasya samarpaNam -- yathA nIlaM yad utpalam tad Anayeti, evam ihApi udgItho ya oMkAraH tam upAsIteti | evam etasmin sAmAnAdhikaraNyavAkye vimR^ishyamAne, ete pakShAH pratibhAnti | tatrAnyatamanirdhAraNakAraNAbhAvAt anirdhAraNaprAptau, idam ucyate -- 

vyApteshca samaJNjasam ||

cashabdo.ayaM tushabdasthAnaniveshI pakShatrayavyAvartanaprayojanaH | tad iha trayaH pakShAH sAvadyA iti paryudasyante | visheShaNapakSha evaiko niravadya ityupAdIyate | tatrAdhyAse tAvat -- yA buddhiH itaratra adhyasyate, tacchabdasya lakShaNAvR^ittitvaM prasajyeta, tatphalaM ca kalpyeta | shrUyata eva phalam, ApayitA ha vai kAmAnAM bhavati ityAdi, iti cet -- tan na, tasya anyaphalatvAt | AptyAdidR^iShTiphalaM hi tat, nodgIthAdhyAsaphalam | apavAde.api samAnaH phalAbhAvaH | mithyAj~nAnanivR^ittiH phalam iti cet, na | puruShArthopayogAnavagamAt | na ca kadAcid api oMkArAt okArabuddhir nivarteta, udgIthAd vA udgIthabuddhiH | na cedaM vAkyaM vastutattvapratipAdanaparam, upAsanAvidhiparatvAt | nApi ekatvapakShaH saMgacchate | niShprayojanaM hi tadA shabdadvayoccAraNaM syAt, ekenaiva vivakShitArthasamarpaNAt | na ca hautraviShaye AdhvaryavaviShaye vA akShare oMkArashabdavAcye udgIthashabdaprasiddhir asti, nApi sakalAyAm sAmno dvitIyAyAM bhaktau udgIthashabdavAcyAyAm oMkArashabdaprasiddhiH, yenAnatiriktArthatA syAt | parisheShAd visheShaNapakShaH parigR^ihyate, vyApteH sarvavedasAdhAraNyAt | sarvavyApyakSharam iha mA prasaJNji -- ityata udgIthashabdena akSharaM visheShyate -- kathaM nAma udgIthAvayavabhUta oMkAro gR^ihyeteti | 

nanvasminn api pakShe samAnA lakShaNA, udgIthashabdasya avayavalakShaNArthatvAt | satyam evam etat | lakShaNAyAm api tu saMnikarShaviprakarShau bhavata eva | adhyAsapakShe hi arthAntarabuddhir arthAntare nikShipyata iti viprakR^iShTA lakShaNA, visheShaNapakShe tu avayavivacanena shabdena avayavaH samarpyata iti saMnikR^iShTA | samudAyeShu hi pravR^ittAH shabdA avayaveShvapi vartamAnA dR^iShTAH paTagrAmAdiShu | atashca vyApter hetoH om ityetad akSharam [chA.u. 1.4.1] ityetasya udgItham ityetad visheShaNam iti samaJNjasam etat, niravadyam ityarthaH ||9||

  -- o)0(o -- 

5. sarvAbhedAdhikaraNam

|| 3.3.10 ||

vAjinAM chandogAnAM ca prANasaMvAde shraiShThyaguNAnvitasya prANasya upAsyatvam uktam | vAgAdayo.api hi tatra vasiShThatvAdiguNAnvitA uktAH | te ca guNAH prANe punaH pratyarpitAH -- yad vA ahaM vasiShThAsmi tvaM tad vasiShTho.asi [cha.u. 6.1.14] ityAdinA | anyeShAm api tu shAkhinAM kauShItakiprabhR^itInAM prANasaMvAdeShu athAto niHshreyasAdAnam etA ha vai devatA ahaM shreyase vivadamAnAH ityevaMjAtIyakeShu prANasya shraiShThyam uktam, na tvime vasiShThatvAdayo.api guNA uktAH | 

tatra saMshayaH -- kim ime vasiShThatvAdayo guNAH kvacid uktA anyatrApi asyeran, uta nAsyerann iti | tatra prAptaM tAvat -- nAsyerann iti | kutaH? evaMshabdasaMyogAt | atho ya evaM vidvAn prANe niHshreyasaM viditvA iti hi tatra tatra evaMshabdena vedyaM vastu nivedyate | evaMshabdashca saMnihitAvalambanaH na shAkhAntaraparipaThitam evaMjAtIyakaM guNajAtaM shaknoti nivedayitum | tasmAt svaprakaraNasthair eva guNair nirAkAN^kShatvam ityevaM prApte -- 

sarvAbhedAd anyatreme ||

pratyAha -- asyeran ime guNAH kvacid uktA vasiShThatvAdayo.anyatrApi | kutaH? sarvAbhedAt -- sarvatraiva tad eva ekaM prANavij~nAnam abhinnaM pratyabhij~nAyate, prANasaMvAdAdisArUpyAt | abhede ca vij~nAnasya katham ime guNAH kvacid uktA anyatra na asyeran | 

nanu evaMshabdaH tatra tatra bhedena evaMjAtIyakaM guNajAtaM vedyatvAya samarpayatItyuktam | atrocyate -- yadyapi kauShItakIbrAhmaNagatena evaMshabdena vAjasaneyibrAhmaNagataM guNajAtam asaMshabditam asaMnihitatvAt, tathApi tasminn eva vij~nAne vAjasaneyibrAhmaNagatena evaMshabdena tat saMshabditam iti -- na parashAkhAgatam api abhinnavij~nAnAvabaddhaM guNajAtaM svashAkhAgatAd vishiShyate | na caivaM sati shrutahAniH ashrutakalpanA vA bhavati | ekasyAm api hi shAkhAyAM shrutA guNAH shrutA eva sarvatra bhavanti, guNavato bhedAbhAvAt | na hi devadattaH shauryAdiguNatvena svadeshe prasiddhaH deshAntaraM gataH taddeshyair avibhAvitashauryAdiguNo.api atadguNo bhavati | yathA ca tatra paricayavisheShAt deshAntare.api devadattaguNA vibhAvyante | evam abhiyogavisheShAt shAkhAntare.apyupAsyA guNAH shAkhAntare.apyasyeran | tasmAd ekapradhAnasambaddhA dharmA ekatrApyucyamAnAH sarvatraiva upasaMhartavyA iti ||10||

  -- o)0(o -- 

6. AnandAdyadhikaraNam

|| 3.3.11 ||

brahmasvarUpapratipAdanaparAsu shrutiShu AnandarUpatvaM vij~nAnaghanatvaM sarvagatatvaM sarvAtmatvam ityevaMjAtIyakA brahmaNo dharmAH kvacit kecit shrUyante | teShu saMshayaH -- kim AnandAdayo brahmadharmAH yatra yAvantaH shrUyante tAvanta eva tatra pratipattavyAH, kiM vA sarve sarvatreti | tatra yathAshrutivibhAgaM dharmapratipattau prAptAyAm -- 
AnandAdayaH pradhAnasya ||

idam ucyate -- AnandAdayaH pradhAnasya brahmaNo dharmAH sarve sarvatra pratipattavyAH | kasmAt? sarvAbhedAd eva -- sarvatra hi tad eva ekaM pradhAnaM visheShyaM brahma na bhidyate | tasmAt sArvatrikatvaM brahmadharmANAm -- tenaiva pUrvAdhikaraNoditena devadattashauryAdinidarshanena ||11|| 

|| 3.3.12 ||

nanu evaM sati priyashirastvAdayo.api dharmAH sarve sarvatra saN^kIryeran | tathA hi taittirIyake Anandamayam AtmAnaM prakramya AmnAyate -- tasya priyam eva shiraH | modo dakShiNaH pakShaH | pramoda uttaraH pakShaH | Ananda AtmA | brahma pucchaM pratiShThA [tai.u. 2.5.2] iti | ata uttaraM paThati -- 

priyashirastvAdyaprAptir upacayApacayau hi bhede || 

priyashirastvAd InAM dharmANAM taittirIyake AmnAtAnAM nAsti anyatra prAptiH, yat kAraNam -- priyaM modaH pramoda Ananda ityete -- parasparApekShayA bhoktrantarApekShayA ca upacitApacitarUpA upalabhyante | upacayApacayau ca sati bhede sambhavataH | nirbhedaM tu brahma ekam evAdvitIyam ityAdi shrutibhyaH | na ca ete priyashirastvAdayo brahmadharmAH | koshadharmAH tu ete ityupadiShTam asmAbhiH Anandamayo.abhyAsAt ityatra | api ca parasmin brahmaNi cittAvatAropAyamAtratvena ete parikalpyante, na draShTavyatvena | evam api sutarAm anyatrAprAptiH priyashirastvAd InAm | brahmadharmAMH tu etAn kR^itvA nyAyamAtram idam AcAryeNa pradarshitam -- priyashirastvAd yaprAptiH iti | sa ca nyAyo.anyeShu nishciteShu brahmadharmeShu upAsanAyopadishyamAneShu netavyaH -- saMyadvAmatvAd iShu satyakAmatvAd iShu ca | teShu hi satyapi upAsyasya brahmaNa ekatve, prakramabhedAd upAsanAbhede sati, na anyonyadharmANAm anyonyatra prAptiH | yathA ca dve nArryau ekaM nR^ipatim upAsAte -- chatreNa anyA cAmareNa anyA -- tatropAsyaikatve.api upAsanabhedo dharmavyavasthA ca bhavati -- evam ihApIti | upacitApacitaguNatvaM hi sati bhedavyavahAre saguNe brahmaNyupapadyate, na nirguNe parasmin brahmaNi | ato na satyakAmatvAd InAM dharmANAM kvacicchrutAnAM sarvatra prAptiH ityarthaH ||13||

|| 3.3.13 ||

itare tu arthasAmAnyAt ||

itare tu AnandAdayo dharmA brahmasvarUpapratipAdanAyaiva ucyamAnAH, arthasAmAnyAt pratipAdyasya brahmaNo dharmiNa ekatvAt, sarve sarvatra pratIyerann iti vaiShamyam -- pratipattimAtraprayojanA hi te iti ||13||

 -- o)0(o -- 

|| 3.3.14 ||

kAThake hi paThyate -- 

indriyebhyaH parA hyarthA arthebhyashca paraM manaH | manasaH tu parA buddhiH [ka.u. 1.3.10] ityArabhya, puruShAn na paraM kiMcit sA kAShThA sA parA gatiH [ka.u. 1.3.11] iti | 

tatra saMshayaH -- kim ime sarva eva arthAdayaH tataH tataH paratvena pratipAdyante, uta puruSha eva ebhyaH sarvebhyaH paraH pratipAdyata iti | tatra tAvat sarveShAm evaiShAM paratvena pratipAdanam iti bhavati matiH | tathA hi shrUyate -- idam asmAt param, idam asmAt param iti | 

nanu bahuShvartheShu paratvena pratipipAdayiShiteShu vAkyabhedaH syAt | naiSha doShaH, vAkyabahutvopapatteH | bahUnyeva hi etAni vAkyAni prabhavanti bahUn arthAn paratvopetAn pratipAdayitum | tasmAt pratyekam eShAM paratvapratipAdanam ityevaM prApte, brUmaH -- 

AdhyAnAya prayojanAbhAvAt ||
 
puruSha eva hi ebhyaH sarvebhyaH paraH pratipAdyata iti yuktam -- na pratyekam eShAM paratvapratipAdanam | kasmAt? prayojanAbhAvAt | na hi itareShu paratvena pratipanneShu kiMcit prayojanaM dR^ishyate, shrUyate vA | puruShe tu indriyAdibhyaH parasmin sarvAn arthavrAtAtIte pratipanne dR^ishyate prayojanam, mokShasiddhiH | tathA ca shrutiH -- nicAyya tanmR^ityumukhAt pramucyate iti | api ca parapratiShedhena kAShThAshabdena ca puruShaviShayam AdaraM darshayan puruShapratipattyarthaiva pUrvAparapravAhoktiH iti darshayati | AdhyAnAyeti -- AdhyAnapUrvakAya samyagdarshanAyetyarthaH | samyagdarshanArtham eva hi iha AdhyAnam upadishyate, na tu AdhyAnam eva svapradhAnam ||14||

|| 3.3.15 || 

AtmashabdAcca ||

itashca puruShapratipattyartha eva iyam indriyAdipravAhoktiH, yatkAraNam eSha sarveShu bhUteShu gUDhAtmA na prakAshate | dR^ishyate tu agryayA buddhyA sUkShmayA sUkShmadarshibhiH iti prakR^itaM puruSham AtmetyAha | atashca anAtmatvam itareShAM vivakShitam iti gamyate | tasyaiva ca durvij~nAnatAM saMskR^itam atigamyatAM ca darshayati | tadvij~nAnAyaiva ca -- yacched vAN^manasI prAj~naH iti AdhyAnaM vidadhAti | tat vyAkhyAtam AnumAnikam apyekeShAm ityatra | evam anekaprakAra AshayAtishayaH shruteH puruShe lakShyate, netareShu | api ca so.adhvanaH pAram Apnoti tadviShNoH paramaM padam ityukte, kiM tat adhvanaH pAraM viShNoH paramaM padam ityasyAm AkAN^kShAyAm indriyAdyanukramaNAt paramapadapratipattyartha evAyam AmnAya ityavasIyate ||15||

AtmagR^ihItyadhikaraNam

|| 3.3.16 || 

aitareyake shrUyate -- 

AtmA vA idam eka evAgra AsIn nAnyat kiMcana miShat sa aikShata lokAn nu sR^ijA iti sa imAMl lokAn asR^ijatAmbho marIcIr maram ApaH ityAdi | 

tatra saMshayaH -- kiM para evAtmA iha AtmashabdenAbhilapyate, uta anyaH kashcid iti | kiM tAvat prAptam? na paramAtmA iha AtmashabdAbhilapyo bhavitum arhatIti | kasmAt? vAkyAnvayadarshanAt | 

nanu vAkyAnvayaH sutarAM paramAtmaviShayo dR^ishyate, prAgutpatteH AtmaikatvAvadhAraNAt, IkShaNapUrvakasraShTR^itvavacanAcca | netyucyate, lokasR^iShTivacanAt -- paramAtmani hi sraShTAri parigR^ihyamANe, mahAbhUtasR^iShTiH Adau vaktavyA | lokasR^iShTiH tu iha AdAvucyate | lokAshca mahAbhUtasaMniveshavisheShAH | tathA ca ambhaHprabhR^itIn lokatvenaiva nirbravIti -- ado.ambhaH pareNa divam ityAdinA | lokasR^iShTishca parameshvarAdhiShThitena apareNa kenacid IshvareNa kriyata iti shrutismR^ityor upalabhyate | tathA hi shrutir bhavati -- Atmaivedam agra AsIt puruShavidhaH ityAdyA | smR^itir api -- 

sa vai sharIrI prathamaH sa vai puruSha ucyate | 
AdikartA sa bhUtAnAM brahmAgre samavartata || iti | 

aitareyiNo.api athAto retasaH sR^iShTiH prajApate reto devAH ityatra pUrvasmin prakaraNe prajApatikartR^ikAM vicitrAM sR^iShTim Amananti | Atmashabdo.api tasmin prayujyamAno dR^ishyate -- Atmaivedam agra AsIt puruShavidhaH ityatra | ekatvAvadhAraNam api prAgutpatteH svavikArApekSham upapadyate | IkShaNam api tasya cetanatvAbhyupagamAd upapannam | api ca tAbhyo gAmAnayat tAbhyo.ashvam Anayat tAbhyaH puruSham Anayat tA abruvan ityevaMjAtIyako bhUyAn vyApAravisheShaH laukikeShu visheShavatsu Atmasu prasiddhaH ihAnugamyate | tasmAt visheShavAn eva kashcid iha AtmA syAd ityevaM prApte -- 

AtmagR^ihItiH itaravad uttarAt ||

brUmaH -- para eva AtmA iha Atmashabdena gR^ihyate | itaravat -- yathA itareShu sR^iShTishravaNeShu tasmAd vA etasmAd Atmana AkAshaH sambhUtaH ityevamAdiShu parasyAtmano grahaNam, yathA ca itarasmin laukikAtmashabdaprayoge pratyagAtmaiva mukhya Atmashabdena gR^ihyate -- tathA ihApi bhavitum arhati | yatra tu Atmaivedamagra AsIt ityevamAdau puruShavidhaH ityevamAdi visheShaNAntaraM shrUyate, bhavet tatra visheShavata Atmano grahaNam | atra punaH paramAtmagrahaNAnuguNam eva visheShaNam api uttaram upalabhyate -- sa aikShata lokAn nu sR^ijA iti sa imAMl lokAn asR^ijata ityevam Adi | tasmAt tasyaiva grahaNam iti nyAyyam||

|| 3.3.17 ||

anvayAd iti cet syAd avadhAraNAt ||

vAkyAnvayadarshanAt na paramAtmagrahaNam iti punaH yad uktam, tat parihartavyam iti -- atrocyate -- syAd avadhAraNAd iti | bhaved upapannaM paramAtmano grahaNam | kasmAt? avadhAraNAt | paramAtmagrahaNe hi prAgutpatter AtmaikatvAvadhAraNam AJNjasam avakalpate | anyathA hi anAJNjasaM tat parikalpyeta | lokasR^iShTivacanaM tu shrutyantaraprasiddhamahAbhUtasR^iShTyanantaram iti yojayiShyAmi | yathA tat tejo.asR^ijata [chA.u. 6.2.3] ityetat shrutyantaraprasiddhaviyadvAyusR^iShTyanantaram iti ayUyujam, evam ihApi | shrutyantaraprasiddho hi samAnaviShayo visheShaH shrutyantareShu upasaMhartavyo bhavati | 

yo.apyayaM vyApAravisheShAnugamaH tAbhyo gAm Anayat ityevamAdiH, so.api vivakShitArthAvadhAraNAnuguNyenaiva grahItavyaH | na hyayaM sakalaH kathAprabandho vivakShita iti shakyate vaktum, tat pratipattau puruShArthAbhAvAt | brahmAtmatvaM tu iha vivakShitam | tathA hi -- ambhaHprabhR^itInAM lokAnAM lokapAlAnAM cAgnyAdInAM sR^iShTiM shiShTvA, karaNAni karaNAyatanaM ca sharIram upadishya, sa eva sraShTA kathaM nvidaM madR^ite syAt iti vIkShya, idaM sharIraM pravivesheti darshayati -- sa etam eva sImAnaM vidAryaitayA dvArA prApadyata iti | punashca yadi vAcAbhivyAhR^itaM yadi prANenAbhiprANitam ityevamAdinA karaNavyApAravivecanapUrvakam atha ko.aham iti vIkShya, sa etam eva puruShaM brahma tatamam apashyat iti brahmAtmatvadarshanam avadhArayati | tathopariShTAt -- eSha brahmaiSha indraH ityAdinA samastaM bhedajAtaM saha mahAbhUtair anukramya, sarvaM tatpraj~nAnetraM praj~nAne pratiShThitaM praj~nAnetro lokaH praj~nA pratiShThA praj~nAnaM brahma iti brahmAtmatvadarshanam eva avadhArayati | tasmAt iha AtmagR^ihItiH ityanapavAdam || 

aparA yojanA -- AtmagR^ihItiH itaravad uttarAt | vAjasaneyake katama Atmeti yo.ayaM vij~nAnamayaH prANeShu hR^idyantarjyotiH puruShaH ityAtmashabdenopakramya, tasyaiva sarvasaN^gavinirmuktatvapratipAdanena brahmAtmatAm avadhArayati | tathA hi upasaMharati -- sa vA eSha mahAn aja AtmAjaro.amaro.amR^ito.abhayo brahma [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.25] iti | chAndogye tu, sad eva somyedam agra AsId ekam evAdvitIyam [chA.u. 6.2.1] iti antareNaivAtmashabdam upakramya, udarke sa AtmA tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7] iti tAdAtmyam upadishati | 

tatra saMshayaH -- tulyArthatvaM kim anayor AmnAnayoH syAt, atulyArthatvaM veti | atulyArthatvam iti tAvat prAptam, atulyatvAd AmnAnayoH | na hi AmnAnavaiShamye sati arthasAmyaM yuktaM pratipattum, AmnAnatantratvAd arthaparigrahasya | vAjasaneyake ca AtmashabdopakramAt Atmatattvopadesha iti gamyate | chAndogye tu upakramaviparyayAt upadeshaviparyayaH | 

nanu chandogAnAm api astyudarke tAdAtmyopadesha ityuktam | satyam uktam, upakramatantratvAd upasaMhArasya, tAdAtmyasampattiH sA -- iti manyate | tathA prApte, abhidhIyate -- AtmagR^ihItiH sad eva somyedam agra AsIt [chA.u. 6.2.1] ityatra cchandogAnAm api bhavitum arhati | itaravat -- yathA katama AtmA ityatra vAjasaneyinAm AtmagR^ihItiH, tathaiva | kasmAt? uttarAt tAdAtmyopadeshAt | anvayAd iti ced avadhAraNAt -- yad uktam, upakramAnvayAt upakrame ca AtmashabdashravaNAbhAvAt na AtmagR^ihItiH iti, tasya kaH parihAra iti cet, so.abhidhIyate -- syAd avadhAraNAd iti | bhaved upapannA iha AtmagR^ihItiH, avadhAraNAt | tathA hi -- yenAshrutaM shrutaM bhavatyamataM matam avij~nAtaM vij~nAtam [chA.u. 6.1.3] ityekavij~nAnena sarvavij~nAnam avadhArya, tatsampipAdayiShayA sad eva ityAha | tacca AtmagR^ihItau satyAM sampadyate | anyathA hi, yo.ayaM mukhya AtmA sa na vij~nAta iti, naiva sarvavij~nAnaM sampadyeta | tathA prAgutpatteH ekatvAd hAraNam, jIvasya ca Atmashabdena parAmarshaH, svApAvasthAyAM ca tatsvabhAvasampattikathanam, paricodanApUrvakaM ca punaH punaH tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7] ityavadhAraNam -- iti ca sarvam etat tAdAtmyapratipAdanAyAm eva avakalpate, na tAdAtmyasampAdanAyAm | na ca atra upakramatantratvopanyAso nyAyyaH | na hi upakrame AtmatvasaN^kIrtanam anAtmatvasaN^kIrtanaM vA asti | sAmAnyopakramashca na vAkyasheShagatena visheSheNa virudhyate, visheShAkaN^kShitvAt sAmAnyasya | sacchabdArtho.api ca paryAlocyamAnaH na mukhyAd Atmano.anyaH sambhavati, ato.anyasya vastujAtasya ArambhaNashabdAdibhyo.anR^itatvopapatteH | AmnAnavaiShamyam api nAvashyam arthavaiShamyam Avahati, Ahara pAtram pAtram Ahara ityevamAdiShu arthasAmye.api taddarshanAt | tasmAt evaMjAtIyakeShu vAkyeShu pratipAdanaprakArabhede.api pratipAdyArthAbheda iti siddham ||17||

  -- o)0(o -- 
kAryAkhyAnAdhikaraNam

|| 3.3.18 ||
