chandogA vAjasaneyinashca prANasaMvAde shvAdimaryAdaM prANasya annam AmnAya, tasyaiva Apo vAsa Amananti | anantaraM ca cchandogA Amananti -- tasmAd vA etad ashiShyantaH purastAccopariShTAccAdbhiH paridadhati [chA.u. 5.2.2] iti | vAjasaneyinashcAmananti -- tadvidvAMsaH shrotriyA ashiShyanta AcAmantyashitvA cAcAmantyetam eva tad anam anagnaM kurvanto manyante tasmAd evaMvid ashiShyann AcAmed ashitvA cAcAmed etam eva tad anam anagnaM kurute [bR^i.A.u. 6.1.14] iti | tatra ca Acamanam anagnatAcintanaM ca prANasya pratIyate | tat kim ubhayam api vidhIyate, uta Acamanam eva, uta anagnatAcintanam eveti vicAryate | kiM tAvat prAptam? ubhayam api vidhIyata iti | kutaH? ubhayasyApyavagamyamAnatvAt | ubhayam api ca etat apUrvatvAt vidhyarham | athavA Acamanam eva vidhIyate | vispaShTA hi tasmin vidhivibhaktiH -- tasmAd evaMvid ashiShyann AcAmed ashitvA cAcAmet iti | tasyaiva stutyartham anagnatAsaN^kIrtanam ityevaM prApte, brUmaH -- 

kAryAkhyAnAdapUrvam ||

na Acamanasya vidheyatvam upapadyate, kAryAkhyAnAt -- prAptam eva hi idaM kAryatvena AcamanaM prAyatyArthaM smR^itiprasiddham anvAkhyAyate | 

nanu iyaM shrutiH tasyAH smR^iter mUlaM syAt | netyucyate, viShayanAnAtvAt | sAmAnyaviShayA hi smR^itiH puruShamAtrasambaddhaM prAyatyArtham AcamanaM prApayati | shrutiH tu prANavidyAprakaraNapaThitA tadviShayam eva AcamanaM vidadhatI vidadhyAt | na ca bhinnaviShayayoH shrutismR^ityoH mUlamUlibhAvo.avakalpate | na ca iyaM shrutiH prANavidyAsaMyogi apUrvam AcamanaM vidhAsyatIti shakyam Ashrayitum, pUrvasyaiva puruShamAtrasaMyogina Acamanasya iha pratyabhij~nAyamAnatvAt | ata eva ca nobhayavidhAnam | ubhayavidhAne ca vAkyaM bhidyeta | tasmAt prAptam eva ashishiShatAm ashitavatAM ca ubhayata Acamanam anUdya, etam eva tadanam anagnaM kurvanto manyante iti prANasya anagnatAkaraNasaN^kalpo.anena vAkyena AcamanIyAsvapsu prANavidyAsambandhitvena apUrva upadishyate | na ca ayam anagnatAvAdaH Acamanastutyartha iti nyAyyam, AcamanasyAvidheyatvAt | svayaM ca anagnatAsaN^kalpasya vidheyatvapratIteH | na ca evaM sati ekasya Acamanasya ubhayArthatA abhyupagatA bhavati -- prAyatyArthatA paridhAnArthatA ceti, kriyAntaratvAbhyupagamAt -- kriyAntaram eva hi AcamanaM nAma prAyatyArthaM puruShasya abhyupagamyate | tadIyAsu tu apsu vAsaH saN^kalpanaM nAma kriyAntaram eva paridhAnArthaM prANasya abhyupagamyata ityanavadyam | api ca yad idaM kiM cAshvabhya A kR^imibhya A kITApataN^gebhyaH tat te.annam ityatra tAvat na sarvAn nAbhyavahArashcodyata iti shakyaM vaktum, ashabdatvAd ashakyatvAcca | sarvaM tu prANasyAnnam iti iyamann adR^iShTishcodyate | tatsAhacaryAcca Apo vAsaH ityatrApi na apAm AcamanaM codyate | prasiddhAsv eva tu AcamanIyAsvapsu paridhAnadR^iShTishcodyata iti yuktam | na hi ardhavaishasaM sambhavati | api ca AcAmantIti vartamAnApadeshitvAt nAyaM shabdo vidhikShamaH | 

nanu manyanta ityapi samAnaM vartamAnApadeshitvam | satyam eva tat | avashyavidheye tu anyatarasmin vAsaHkAryAkhyAnAt apAM vAsaHsaN^kalpanam eva apUrvaM vidhIyate | na Acamanam | pUrvavad dhi tat -- ityupapAditam | yad apyuktam -- vispaShTA ca Acamane vidhivibhaktiH iti, tad api pUrvavattvenaiva Acamanasya pratyuktam | ata eva AcamanasyAvidhitsitatvAt etam eva tadanam anagnaM kurvanto manyante ityatraiva kANvAH paryavasyanti, na Amananti tasmAd evaMvit ityAdi | tasmAt mAdhyaMdinAnAm api pAThe AcamanAnuvAdena evaMvittvam eva prakR^itaprANavAsovittvaM vidhIyata iti pratipattavyam | yo.apyayam abhyupagamaH -- kvacid AcamanaM vidhIyatAm, kvacid vAsovij~nAnam iti -- so.api na sAdhuH, Apo vAsaH ityAdikAyA vAkyapravR^itteH sarvatraikarUpyAt | tasmAt vAsovij~nAnam eva iha vidhIyate, na Acamanam iti nyAyyam ||18||

samAnAdhikaraNam

|| 3.3.19 ||

vAjasaneyishAkhAyAm agnirahasye shANDilyanAmAN^kitA vidyA vij~nAtA | tatra ca guNAH shrUyante -- sa AtmAnam upAsIta manomayaM prANasharIraM bhArUpam [chA.u. 3.14.2] ityevamAdayaH | tasyAm eva shAkhAyAM bR^ihadAraNyake punaH paThyate -- manomayo.ayaM puruSho bhAH satyaH tasminn antarhR^idaye yathA vrIhir vA yavo vA sa eSha sarvasyeshAnaH sarvasyAdhipatiH sarvam idaM prashAsti yad idaM kiM ca iti | tatra saMshayaH -- kim iyam ekA vidyA agnirahasyabR^ihadAraNyakayoH guNopasaMhArashca, uta dve ime vidye guNAnupasaMhArashceti | kiM tAvat prAptam? vidyAbhedaH guNavyavasthA ceti | kutaH? paunaruktyaprasaN^gAt -- bhinnAsu hi shAkhAsu adhyetR^iveditR^ibhedAt paunaruktyaparihAramAlocya vidyaikatvamadhyavasAya ekatrAtiriktA guNA itaratropasaMhriyante prANasaMvAdAdiShu -- ityuktam | ekasyAM punaH shAkhAyAm 
adhyetR^iveditR^ibhedAbhAvAt ashakyaparihAre paunaruktye na viprakraShTAdeshasthA ekA vidyA bhavitum arhati | na ca atra ekamAmnAnaM vidyAvidhAnArtham, aparaM guNavidhAnArtham -- iti vibhAgaH sambhavati | tadA hi atiriktA eva guNA itaratretaratra ca AmnAyeran, na samAnAH | samAnA api tu ubhayatrAmnAyante manomayatvAd ayaH | tasmAt nAnyonyaguNopasaMhAra ityevaM prApte -- 

samAna evaM cAbhedAt ||

brUmahe -- yathA bhinnAsu shAkhAsu vidyaikatvaM guNopasaMhArashca bhavati evam ekasyAm api shAkhAyAM bhavitum arhati, upAsyAbhedAt | tad eva hi brahma manomayatvAd iguNakam ubhayatrApi upAsyam abhinnaM pratyabhijAnImaH | upAsyaM ca rUpaM vidyAyAH | na ca vidyamAne rUpAbhede vidyAbhedamadhyavasAtuM shaknumaH | nApi vidyAbhede guNavyavasthAnam | 

nanu paunaruktyaprasaN^gAt vidyAbhedo.adhyavasitaH | netyucyate, arthavibhAgopapatteH -- ekaM hi AmnAnaM vidyAvidhAnArtham, aparaM guNavidhAnArtham -- iti na kiMcinnopapadyate | 

nanu evaM sati yadapaThitamagnirahasye, tad eva bR^ihadAraNyake paThitavyam -- sa eSha sarvasyeshAnaH ityAdi | yat tu paThitam eva manomayaH ityAdi, tan na paThitavyam -- naiSha doShaH, tadbalenaiva pradeshAntarapaThitavidyApratyabhij~nAnAt | samAnaguNAmnAnena hi viprakR^iShTAdeshAM shANDilyavidyAM pratyabhij~nApya tasyAm IshAnatvAdi upadishyate | anyathA hi kathaM tasyAm ayaM guNavidhirabhidhIyate | api ca aprAptAMshopadeshena arthavati vAkye saMjAte, prAptAMshaparAmarshasya nityAnuvAdatayApi upapadyamAnatvAt na tadbalena pratyabhij~nA upekShituM shakyate | tasmAd atra samAnAyAm api shAkhAyAM vidyaikatvaM guNopasaMhArashcetyupapannam||


|| 3.3.20|| 

sambandhAdhikaraNam

|| 3.3.20 || 

bR^ihadAraNyake satyaM brahma ityupakramya, tad yat tat satyam asau sa Adityo ya eSha etasmin maNDale puruSho yashcAyaM dakShiNe.akShan puruShaH iti tasyaiva satyasya brahmaNo.adhidaivatamadhyAtmaM ca AyatanavisheSham upadishya, vyAhR^itisharIratvaM ca sampAdya, dve upaniShadAvAdishyete -- tasyopaniShadahaH iti -- adhidaivatam, tasyopaniShadaham iti -- adhyAtmam | 

tatra saMshayaH -- kim avibhAgenaiva ubhe api upaniShadAv ubhayatrAnusandhAtavye, uta vibhAgena -- ekA adhidaivatam, ekA adhyAtmam iti | tatra sUtreNaivopakramate -- 

sambandhAd evam anyatrApi ||

yathA shANDilyavidyAyAM vibhAgenApyadhItAyAM guNopasaMhAra uktaH, evam anyatrApi evaMjAtIyake viShaye bhavitum arhati, ekavidyAbhisambandhAt -- ekA hi iyaM satyavidyA adhidaivatam adhyAtmaM ca adhItA, upakramAbhedAt vyatiShaktapAThAcca | kathaM tasyAmudito dharmaH tasyAm eva na syAt | yo hyAcArye kashcidanugamanAdirAcArashcoditaH, sa grAmagate.araNyagate ca tulyavad eva bhavati | tasmAt ubhayor apyupaniShadoH ubhayatra prAptiH iti ||20|| 

|| 3.3.21 ||

evaM prApte, pratividhatte -- 

na vA visheShAt ||

naiva ubhayoH ubhayatra prAptiH | kasmAt? visheShAt, upAsanasthAnavisheShopanibandhAd ityarthaH | kathaM sthAnavisheShopanibandha iti, ucyate -- ya eSha etasmin maNDale puruShaH iti hi AdhidaivikaM puruShaM prakR^itya, tasyopaniShadahaH iti shrAvayati | yo.ayaM dakShiNe.akShan puruShaH iti ca AdhyAtmikaM puruShaM prakR^itya, tasyopaniShadaham iti | tasyeti ca etat saMnihitAvalambanaM sarvanAma | tasmAt AyatanavisheShavyapAshrayeNaiva ete upaniShadAvupadishyete | kuta ubhayorubhayatra prAptiH | 

nanu eka evAyam adhidaivatam adhyAtmaM ca puruShaH, ekasyaiva satyasya brahmaNa AyatanadvayapratipAdanAt | satyam evam etat | ekasyApi tu avasthAvisheShopAdAnenaiva upaniShadvisheShopadeshAt tadavasthasyaiva sA bhavitum arhati | asti cAyaM dR^iShTAntaH -- satyapi AcAryasvarUpAnapAye, yat AcAryasya AsInasya anuvartanam uktam, na tat tiShThato bhavati | yacca tiShThata uktam, na tadAsInasyeti | grAmAraNyayoH tu AcAryasvarUpAnapAyAt tatsvarUpAnubaddhasya ca dharmasya grAmAraNyakR^itavisheShAbhAvAt ubhayatra tulyavadbhAva iti adR^iShTAntaH saH | tasmAt vyavasthA anayor upaniShadoH ||21||

|| 3.3.22 || 

darshayati ca ||

api ca evaMjAtIyakAnAM dharmANAM vyavastheti liN^gadarshanaM bhavati -- tasyaitasya tad eva rUpaM yad amuShya rUpaM yAvamuShya geShNau tau geShNau yan nAma tan nAma iti | katham asya liN^gatvam iti, tad ucyate -- akShyAdityasthAnabhedabhinnAn dharmAn anyonyasminn anupasaMhAryAn pashyan iha atideshena AdityapuruShagatAn rUpAdIn akShipuruShe upasaMharati -- tasyaitasya tad eva rUpam ityAdinA | tasmAd vyavatiShThete eva ete upaniShadAviti nirNayaH ||22||

  -- o)0(o -- 

sambhR^ityadhikaraNam

|| 3.3.23 || 

sambhR^itidyuvyAptyapi cAtaH ||

brahmajyeShThA vIryA sambhR^itAni brahmAgre jyeShThaM divam AtatAna ityevaM rANAyanIyAnAM khileShu vIryasambhR^itidyuniveshaprabhR^itayo brahmaNo vibhUtayaH paThyante | teShAm eva ca upaniShadi shANDilyavidyAprabhR^itayo brahmavidyAH paThyante | tAsu brahmavidyAsu tA brahmavibhUtaya upasaMhriyeran, na veti vicAraNAyAm, brahmasambandhAd upasaMhAraprAptau evaM paThati | sambhR^itidyuvyAptiprabhR^itayo vibhUtayaH shANDilyavidyAprabhR^itiShu nopasaMhartavyAH, ata eva ca AyatanavisheShayogAt | tathA hi shANDilyavidyAyAM hR^idayAyatanatvaM brahmaNa uktam -- eSha ma AtmAntarhR^idaye [chA.u. 3.14.3] iti | tadvad eva daharavidyAyAm api -- daharaM puNDarIkaM veshma daharo.asminn antar AkAshaH [chA.u. 8.1.1] iti | upakosalavidyAyAM tu akShyAyatanatvam -- ya eSho.akShiNi puruSho dR^ishyate iti | evaM tatra tatra tattat AdhyAtmikamAyatanam etAsu vidyAsu pratIyate | Adhidaivikyastu etA vibhUtayaH sambhR^itidyuvyAptiprabhR^itayaH | tAsAM kuta etAsu prAptiH | nanvetAsvapi Adhidaivikyo vibhUtayaH shrUyante -- jyAyAndivo jyAyAnebhyo lokebhyaH eSha u eva bhAmanIreSha hi sarveShu lokeShu bhAti yAvAnvAyamAkAshastAvAneSho.antarhR^idaya AkAsha ubhe asmindyAvApR^ithivI antar eva samAhite ityevamAdyAH | santi ca anyA AyatanavisheShahInA api iha brahmavidyAH ShoDashakalAdyAH -- satyam evam etat | tathApyatra vidyate visheShaH sambhR^ityAdyanupasaMhArahetuH -- samAnaguNAmnAnena hi pratyupasthApitAsu viprakR^iShTAdeshAsvapi vidyAsu viprakR^iShTAdeshaguNA upasaMhriyerann itiyuktam | sambhR^ityAdayastu shANDilyAdivAkyagocarAshca guNAH parasparavyAvR^ittasvarUpatvAt na pradeshAntaravartividyApratyupasthApanakShamAH | na ca brahmasambandhamAtreNa pradeshAntaravartividyApratyupasthApanamityucyate, vidyAbhede.api tadupapatteH | ekam api hi brahma vibhUtibhedairanekadhA upAsyata iti sthitiH, parovarIyastvAd ivadbhedadarshanAt | tasmAt vIryasambhR^ityAdInAM shANDilyavidyAdiShu anupasaMhAra iti ||23||

  -- o)0(o -- 

puruShavidyAdhikaraNam ||

|| 3.3.24 || 

puruShavidyAyAm iva cetareShAm anAmnAnAt ||

asti tANDinAM paiN^ginAM ca rahasyabrAhmaNe puruShavidyA | tatra puruSho yaj~naH kalpitaH | tadIyam AyuH tredhA vibhajya savanatrayaM kalpitam | ashishiShAdIni ca dIkShAdibhAvena kalpitAni | anye ca dharmAH tatra samadhigatA AshIr mantraprayogAdayaH | taittirIyakA api kaMcit puruShayaj~naM kalpayanti -- tasyaivaMviduSho yaj~nasyAtmA yajamAnaH shraddhA patnI ityetenAnuvAkena | 

tatra saMshayaH -- kim itaratra uktAH puruShayaj~nasya dharmAH taittirIyakeShu upasaMhartavyAH, kiM vA nopasaMhartavyA iti | puruShayaj~natvAvisheShAt upasaMhAraprAptau, AcakShmahe -- nopasaMhartavyA iti | kasmAt? tadrUpapratyabhij~nAnAbhAvAt | tad AhAcAryaH puruShavidyAyAm iveti -- yathA ekeShAM shAkhinAM tANDinAM paiN^ginAM ca puruShavidyAyAm AmnAnam, naivam itareShAM taittirIyANAm AmnAnam asti | teShAM hi itaravilakShaNam eva yaj~nasampAdanaM dR^ishyate, patnIyajamAnavedivedabarhiryUpAjyapashvR^itvigAdyanukramaNAt | yad api savanasampAdanam, tad api itaravilakShaNam eva -- yat prAtar madhyaMdinaM sAyaM ca tAni iti | yad api kiMcit, maraNAvabhR^ithatvAdisAmAnyam, tad api alpIyastvAt bhUyasA vailakShaNyena abhibhUyamAnaM na pratyabhij~nApanakShamam | na ca taittirIyake puruShasya yaj~natvaM shrUyate | viduShaH yaj~nasya iti hi na ca ete samAnAdhikaraNe ShaShThyai -- vidvAn eva yo yaj~naH tasyeti | na hi puruShasya mukhyaM yaj~natvam asti | vyadhikaraNe tu ete ShaShThyai -- viduSho yo yaj~naH tasyeti | bhavati hi puruShasya mukhyo yaj~nasambandhaH | satyAM ca gatau, mukhya evArtha AshrayitavyaH, na bhAktaH | AtmA yajamAnaH iti ca yajamAnatvaM puruShasya nirbruvan vaiyadhikaraNyenaiva asya yaj~nasambandhaM darshayati | api ca tasyaivaMviduShaH iti siddhavad anuvAdashrutau satyAm, puruShasya yaj~nabhAvam AtmAdInAM ca yajamAnAdibhAvaM pratipitsamAnasya vAkyabhedaH syAt | api ca sasaMnyAsAm AtmavidyAM purastAd upadishya anantaram tasyaivaMviduShaH ityAdyanukramaNaM pashyantaH -- pUrvasheSha eva eSha AmnAyaH, na svatantra iti pratImaH | tathA ca ekam eva phalam ubhayor apyanuvAkayor upalabhAmahe -- brahmaNo mahimAnam Apnoti iti | itareShAM tu ananyasheShaH puruShavidyAmnAyaH | AyurabhivR^iddhiphalo hyasau, praha ShoDashaM varShashataM jIvati ya evaM veda iti samabhivyAhArAt | tasmAt shAkhAntarAdhItAnAM puruShavidyAdharmANAm AshIrmantrAdInAm aprAptiH taittirIyake ||24||

  -- o)0(o -- 

vedhAdyadhikaraNam

|| 3.3.25 ||

astyAtharvaNikAnAm upaniShadArambhe mantrasamAmnAyaH -- sarvaM pravidhya hR^idayaM pravidhya dhamanIH pravR^ijya shiro.abhipravR^ijya tridhA vipR^iktaH ityAdiH | tANDinAm -- deva savitaH prasuva yaj~nam ityAdiH | shATAayaninAm -- shvetAshvo haritanIlo.asi ityAdiH | kaTahAnAM taittirIyANAM ca -- shaM no mitraH shaM varuNaH ityAdiH | vAjasaneyinAM tu upaniShadArambhe pravagryabrAhmaNaM paThyate -- devA ha vai satraM niSheduH ityAdi | kauShItakinAm api agniShTomabrAhmaNam -- brahma vA agniShTomo brahmaiva tadaharbrahmaNaiva te brahmopayanti te.amR^itatvamApnuvanti ya etadaharupayanti iti | kimime sarve pravidhyAdayo mantrAH pravagryAdIni ca karmANi vidyAsu upasaMhriyeran, kiM vA na upasaMhriyeran -- iti mImAMsAmahe | kiM tAvat naH pratibhAti? upasaMhAra eva eShAM vidyAsviti | kutaH? vidyApradhAnAnAm upaniShadgranthAnAM samIpe pAThAt | 

nanu eShAM vidyArthatayA vidhAnaM nopalabhAmahe -- bADham, anupalabhamAnA api tu anumAsyAmahe, saMnidhisAmarthyAt | na hi saMnidheH arthavattve sambhavati, akasmAd asAvanAshrayituM yuktaH | 

nanu naiShAM mantrANAM vidyAviShayaM kiMcitsAmarthyaM pashyAmaH | kathaM ca pravagryAdIni karmANi anyArthatvenaiva viniyuktAni santi vidyArthatvenApi pratipadyemahIti -- naiSha doShaH | sAmarthyaM tAvat mantrANAM vidyAviShayam api kiMcit shakyaM kalpayitum, hR^idayAdisaN^kIrtanAt | hR^idayAdIni hi prAyeNa upAsaneShu AyatanAdibhAvenopadiShTAni | taddvAreNa ca hR^idayaM pravidhya ityevaMjAtIyakAnAM mantrANAm upapannam upAsanAN^gatvam | dR^iShTAshca upAsaneShvapi mantraviniyogaH -- bhUH prapadye.amunAmunAmunA ityevamAdiH | tathA pravagryAdInAM karmaNAm anyatrApi viniyuktAnAM satAm aviruddho vidyAsu viniyogaH -- vAjapeya iva bR^ihaspatisavasya -- ityevaM prApte -- 

vedhAdyarthabhedAt ||

brUmaH -- naiShAm upasaMhAro vidyAsviti | kasmAt? vedhAdyarthabhedAt -- hR^idayaM pravidhya ityevaMjAtIyakAnAM hi mantrANAM ye.arthA hR^idayavedhAdayaH, bhinnAH anabhisambaddhAH te upaniShaduditAbhir vidyAbhiH | na teShAM tAbhiH saMgantuM sAmarthyam asti | 

nanu hR^idayasya upAsaneShvapyupayogAt taddvAraka upAsanAsambandha upanyastaH -- netyucyate | hR^idayamAtrasaN^kIrtanasya hyevam upayogaH kathaMcidutprekShyeta | na ca hR^idayamAtramatra mantrArthaH | hR^idayaM pravidhya dhamanIH pravR^ijya ityevaMjAtIyako hi na sakalo mantrArtho vidyAbhir abhisambadhyate | abhicAraviShayo hyeSho.arthaH | tasmAd AbhicArikeNa karmaNA sarvaM pravidhya ityetasya mantrasyAbhisambandhaH | tathA deva savitaH prasuva yaj~nam ityasya yaj~naprasavaliN^gatvAt yaj~nena karmaNA abhisambandhaH | tadvisheShasambandhastu pramANAntarAdanusartavyaH | evam anyeShAm api mantrANAm -- keShAMcit liN^gena, keShAMcidvacanena, keShAMcitpramANAntareNetyevam -- arthAntareShu viniyuktAnAm, rahasyapaThitAnAm api satAm, na saMnidhimAtreNa vidyAsheShatvopapattiH | durbalo hi saMnidhiH shrutyAdibhya ityuktaM prathame tantre -- shrutiliN^gavAkyaprakaraNasthAnasamAkhyAnAM samavAye pAradaurbalyamarthaviprakarShAt ityatra | tathA karmaNAm api pravagryAdInAm anyatra viniyuktAnAM na vidyAsheShatvopapattiH | na hyeShAM vidyAbhiH saha IkArthyaM kiMcidasti | vAjapeye tu bR^ihaspatisavasya spaShTAM viniyogAntaram -- vAjapeyeneShTavA bR^ihaspatisavena yajeta iti | api ca eko.ayaM pravagryaH sakR^idutpanno balIyasA pramANena anyatra viniyuktaH na durbalena pramANena anyatrApi viniyogam arhati | agR^ihyamANavisheShatve hi pramANayoH evaM syAt | na tu balavadabalavatoH pramANayor agR^ihyamANavisheShatA sambhavati, balavadabalavattvavisheShAd eva | tasmAt evaMjAtIyakAnAM mantrANAM karmaNAM vA na saMnidhipAThamAtreNa vidyAsheShatvamAshaN^kitavyam | araNyAnuvacanAdidharmasAmAnyAt tu saMnidhipATha iti saMtoShTavyam ||25||

  -- o)0(o -- 
15. hAnyadhikaraNam

|| 3.3.26 ||

hAnau tUpAyanashabdasheShatvAt kushAcchandastutyupagAnavat tad uktam ||

asti tANDinAM shrutiH -- ashva iva romANi vidhUya pApaM candra iva rAhor mukhAt pramucya dhUtvA sharIram akR^itaM kR^itAtmA brahmalokam abhisambhavAmi [chA.u. 8.13.1] iti | tathA AtharvaNikAnAm -- tathA vidvAn nAmarUpAd vimuktaH parAt paraM puruSham upaiti divyam [mu.u. 3.2.8] iti | tathA shATyAyaninaH paThanti -- tasya putrA dAyam upayanti suhR^idaH sAdhukR^ityAM dviShantaH pApakR^ityAm iti | tathaiva kauShItakinaH -- tatsukR^itaduShkR^ite vidhUnute tasya priyA j~nAtayaH sukR^itam upayantyapriyA duShkR^itam [kau.u. 1.4] iti | 

tad iha kvacit sukR^itaduShkR^itayor hAnaM shrUyate | kvacit tayor eva vibhAgena priyair apriyaishcopAyanam | kvacit tu ubhayam api hAnam upAyanaM ca | tad yatrobhayaM shrUyate tatra tAvat na kiMcid vaktavyam asti | yatrApyupAyanam eva shrUyate, na hAnam, tatrApyarthAd eva hAnaM saMnipatati, anyair AtmIyayoH sukR^itaduShkR^itayor upeyamAnayoH AvashyakatvAt taddhAnasya | yatra tu hAnam eva shrUyate, nopAyanam -- tatropAyanaM saMnipated vA, na veti vicikitsAyAm -- ashravaNAd asaMnipAtaH, vidyAntaragocaratvAcca shAkhAntarIyasya shravaNasya | api ca AtmakartR^ikaM sukR^itaduShkR^itayor hAnam | parakartR^ikaM tu upAyanam | tayor asatyAvashyakabhAve, kathaM hAnenopAyanam AkShipyeta? tasmAd asaMnipAto hAnAv upAyanasyeti || 

asyAM prAptau paThati -- hAnAviti | hAnau tu etasyAM kevalAyAm api shrUyamANAyAm upAyanaM saMnipatitum arhati | taccheShatvAt  -- hAnashabdasheSho hi upAyanashabdaH samadhigataH kauShItakirahasye | tasmAd anyatra kevalahAnashravaNe.apyupAyanAnuvR^ittiH | yad uktam -- ashravaNAt vidyAntaragocaratvAt anAvashyakatvAcca asaMnipAta iti, tad ucyate -- bhaved eShA vyavasthoktiH, yadyanuShTheyaM kiMcid anyatra shrutam anyatra ninIShyeta | 

na tviha hAnam upAyanaM vA anuShTheyatvena saN^kIrtyate | vidyAstutyarthaM tu anayoH saN^kIrtanam -- itthaM mahAbhAgA vidyA, yat sAmarthyAd asya viduShaH sukR^itaduShkR^ite saMsArakAraNabhUte vidhUyete, te ca asya suhR^iddurhR^itsu nivishete iti | stutyarthe ca asmin saN^kIrtane, hAnAnantarabhAvitvenopAyanasya, kvacicchrutatvAt anyatrApi hAnashrutAv upAyanAnuvR^ittiM manyate -- stutiprakarShalAbhAya | prasiddhA ca arthavAdAntarApekShA arthavAdAntarapravR^ittiH -- ekaviMsho vA ito.asAvadityaH [chA.u. 2.10.5] ityevamAdiShu | kathaM hi iha ekaviMshatA AdityasyAbhidhIyeta, anapekShyamANe.arthavAdAntare -- dvAdasha mAsAH paJNcartavaH traya ime lokA asAvaditya ekaviMshaH ityasmin? tathA triShTubhau bhavataH sendriyatvAya ityevamAdivAdeShu indriyaM vai triShTup ityevamAdyarthavAdAntarApekShA dR^ishyate | vidyAstutyarthatvAcca asyopAyanavAdasya, katham anyadIye sukR^itaduShkR^ite anyair upeyete iti nAtIvAbhiniveShTavyam | upAyanashabdasheShatvAd iti ca shabdashabdaM samuccArayan stutyarthAm eva hAnAv upAyanAnuvR^ittiM sUcayati | guNopasaMhAravivakShAyAM hi upAyanArthasyaiva hAnAvanuvR^ittiM brUyAt | tasmAt guNopasaMhAravicAraprasaN^gena stutyupasaMhArapradarshanArtham idaM sUtram | kushAcchandastutyupagAnavad iti upamopAdAnam | tad yathA -- bhAllavinAm kushA vAnaspatyAH sthatA mA pAta ityetasmin nigame kushAnAm avisheSheNa vanaspatiyonitvashravaNe, shATyAyaninAm audumbarAH iti visheShavacanAt audumbaryaH kushA AshrIyante | yathA ca kvacit devAsuracchandasAm avisheSheNa paurvAparyaprasaN^ge, devacchandAMsi pUrvANIti paiN^gyAmnAnAt pratIyate | yathA ca ShoDashistotre keShAMcit kAlAvisheShaprAptau, samayAdhyuShite sUrye ityArcashruteH kAlavisheShapratipattiH | yathaiva ca avisheSheNopagAnaM kecit samAmananti visheSheNa bhAllavinaH -- yathA eteShu kushAdiShu shrutyantaragatavisheShAnvayaH, evaM hAnAvapyupAyanAnvaya ityarthaH | shrutyantarakR^itaM hi visheShaM shrutyantare.anabhyupagacchataH sarvatraiva vikalpaH syAt | sa ca anyAyyaH satyAM gatau | tad uktaM dvAdashalakShaNyAm -- api tu vAkyasheShatvAd itaraparyudAsaH syAt pratiShedhe vikalpaH syAt iti || 

athavA etAsv eva vidhUnanashrutiShu etena sUtreNa etaccintayitavyam -- kim anena vidhUnanavacanena sukR^itaduShkR^itayor hAnam abhidhIyate, kiM vA arthAntaram iti | tatra ca evaM prApayitavyam -- na hAnaM vidhUnanam abhidhIyate, dhUJNkampane iti smaraNAt, dodhUyante dhvajAgrANi iti ca vAyunA cAlyamAneShu dhvajAgreShu prayogadarshanAt | tasmAt cAlanaM vidhUnanam abhidhIyate | cAlanaM tu sukR^itaduShkR^itayoH kaMcit kAlaM phalapratibandhanAt -- ityevaM prApayya, prativaktavyam -- hAnAv eva eSha vidhUnanashabdo vartitum arhati, upAyanashabdasheShatvAt | na hi paraparigrahabhUtayoH sukR^itaduShkR^itayoH aprahINayoH parair upAyanaM sambhavati | yadyapi idaM parakIyayoH sukR^itaduShkR^itayoH parair upAyanaM na AJNjasaM sambhAvyate, tathApi tatsaN^kIrtanAt tAvat tadAnuguNyena hAnam eva vidhUnanaM nAmeti nirNetuM shakyate | kvacid api ca idaM vidhUnanasaMnidhAv upAyanaM shrUyamANaM kushAcchandastutyupagAnavat vidhUnanashrutyA sarvatrApekShyamANaM sArvatrikaM nirNayakAraNaM sampadyate | na ca cAlanaM dhvajAgravat sukR^itaduShkR^itayor mukhyaM sambhavati, adravyatvAt | ashvashca romANi vidhUnvAnaH tyajan rajaH sahaiva tena romANyapi jIrNAni shAtayati -- ashva iva romANi vidhUya pApam iti ca brAhmaNam | anekArthatvAbhyupagamAcca dhAtUnAM na smaraNavirodhaH | tad uktam iti vyAkhyAtam ||26||

  -- o)0(o -- 
16. sAmparAyAdhikaraNam

|| 3.3.27 || 

sAmparAye tartavyAbhAvAttathA hyanye ||

devayAnena pathA paryaN^kasthaM brahma abhiprasthitasya vyadhvani sukR^itaduShkR^itayor viyogaM kauShItakinaH paryaN^kavidyAyAm Amananti -- sa etaM devayAnaM panthAnam AsAdyAgnilokam Agacchati [kau.brA. 1.3] ityupakramya, sa Agacchati virajAM nadIM tAM manasaivAtyeti tatsukR^itaduShkR^ite vidhUnute [kau.brA. 1.4] iti | tat kiM yathAshrutaM vyadhvanyeva viyogavacanaM pratipattavyam, Aho svit AdAv eva dehAd apasarpaNe -- iti vicAraNAyAm, shrutiprAmANyAt yathAshruti pratipattiprasaktau, paThati -- sAmparAya iti | sAmparAye gamana eva dehAd apasarpaNe, idaM vidyAsAmarthyAt sukR^itaduShkR^itahAnaM bhavati -- iti pratijAnIte | 

hetuM cAcaShTe -- tartavyAbhAvAd iti | na hi viduShaH samparetasya vidyayA brahma samprepsato.antarAle sukR^itaduShkR^itAbhyAM kiMcit prAptavyam asti, yadarthaM katicit kShaNAn akShINe te kalpeyAtAm | vidyAviruddhaphalatvAcca vidyAsAmarthyena tayoH kShayaH | sa ca yadaiva vidyA phalAbhimukhI tadaiva bhavitum arhati | tasmAt prAg eva san ayaM sukR^itaduShkR^itakShayaH pashcAt paThyate | tathA hi anye.api shAkhinaH tANDinaH shATyAyaninashca prAgavasthAyAm eva sukR^itaduShkR^itahAnam Amananti -- ashva iva romANi vidhUya pApam iti, tasya putrA dAyam upayanti suhR^idaH sAdhukR^ityAM dviShantaH pApakR^ityAm iti ca ||27||

|| 3.3.28 ||

chandata ubhayAvirodhAt ||

yadi ca dehAd apasR^iptasya devayAnena pathA prasthitasya ardhapathe sukR^itaduShkR^itakShayo.abhyupagamyeta, tataH patite dehe yamaniyam avidyAbhyAsAtmakasya sukR^itaduShkR^itakShayahetoH puruShayatnasya icchAto.anuShThAnAnupapatteH anupapattir eva tarAtukasya sukR^itaduShkR^itakShayasya syAt | tasmAt pUrvam eva sAdhakAvasthAyAM chandato.anuShThAnaM tasya syAt, tatpUrvakaM ca sukR^itaduShkR^itahAnam iti draShTavyam | evaM nimittanaimittikayor upapattiH tANDishATyAyanishrutyoshca saN^gatiH iti ||28||

  -- o)0(o -- 
17. gater arthavattvAdhikaraNam 

|| 3.3.29 ||

gater arthavattvam ubhayathA.anyathA hi virodhaH || 

kvacit puNyapApAhAnasaMnidhau devayAnaH panthAH shrUyate, kvacin na | tatra saMshayaH -- kiM hAnAvavisheSheNaiva devayAnaH panthAH saMnipatet, uta vibhAgena kvacit saMnipatet kvacin neti | yathA tAvat hAnAvavisheSheNaiva upAyanAnuvR^ittir uktA evaM devayAnAnuvR^ittir api bhavitum arhatItyasyAM prAptau, AcakShmahe -- gateH devayAnasya pathaH, arthavattvam, ubhayathA vibhAgena bhavitum arhati -- kvacid arthavatI gatiH kvacin neti | na avisheSheNa | anyathA hi avisheSheNaiva etasyAM gatAvaN^gIkriyamANAyAM virodhaH syAt -- puNyapApe vidhUya niraJNjanaH paramaM sAmyam upaiti ityasyAM shrutau deshAntaraprApaNI gatir virudhyeta | kathaM hi niraJNjano.agantA deshAntaraM gacchet | gantavyaM ca paramaM sAmyaM na deshAntaraprAptyAyattam -- ityAnarthakyam evAtra gater manyAmahe ||29||

|| 3.3.30 || 

upapannaH tallakShaNArthopalabdher lokavat ||

upapannashcAyam ubhayathAbhAvaH -- kvacid arthavatI gatiH kvacin neti | tallakShaNArthopalabdheH -- gatikAraNabhUto.arthaH paryaN^kavidyAdiShu saguNeShu upAsaneShu upalabhyate | tatra hi paryaN^kArohaNam, paryaN^kasthena brahmaNA saha saMvadanam, vishiShTAgandhAdiprAptishca -- ityevamAdi bahudeshAntaraprAptyAyattaM phalaM shrUyate | tatra arthavatI gatiH | na tu samyagdarshane tallakShaNArthopalabdhir asti | na hi AtmaikatvadarshinAm AptakAmAnAm ihaiva dagdhAsheShakleshabIjAnAm ArabdhabhogakarmAshayakShapaNavyatirekeNa apekShitavyaM kiMcid asti | tatra anarthikA gatiH | lokavacca eSha vibhAgo draShTavyaH -- yathA loke grAmaprAptau deshAntaraprApaNaH panthA apekShyate, na ArogyaprAptau, evam ihApIti | bhUyashca enaM vibhAgaM caturthAdhyAye nipuNataram upapAdayiShyAmaH ||

  -- o)0(o -- 

18. aniyamAdhikaraNam

|| 3.3.31 ||

saguNAsu vidyAsu gatir arthavatI, na nirguNAyAM paramAtmavidyAyAm ityuktam | saguNAsvapi vidyAsu kAsucid gatiH shrUyate -- yathA paryaN^kavidyAyAm upakosalavidyAyAM paJNcAgnividyAyAM daharavidyAyAm iti | na anyAsu -- yathA madhuvidyAyAM shANDilyavidyAyAM ShoDashakalavidyAyAM vaishvAnaravidyAyAm iti | tatra saMshayaH -- kiM yAsv eShA gatiH shrUyate, tAsv eva niyamyeta, uta aniyamena sarvAbhir eva evaMjAtIyakAbhir vidyAbhir abhisambadhyeta ? iti | 

kiM tAvat prAptam? niyama iti | yatraiva shrUyate, tatraiva bhavitum arhati, prakaraNasya niyAmakatvAt | yadyanyatra ashrUyamANApi gatiH vidyAntaraM gacchet, shrutyAdInAM prAmANyaM hIyeta, sarvasya sarvArthatvaprasaN^gAt | api ca arcirAdikA ekaiva gatiH upakosalavidyAyAM paJNcAgnividyAyAM ca tulyavat paThyate | tatsarvArthatve.anarthakaM punar vacanaM syAt | tasmAn niyama ityevaM prApte, paThati -- 

aniyamaH sarvAsAm avirodhaH shabdAnumAnAbhyAm ||

sarvAsAm eva abhyudayaprAptiphalAnAM saguNAnAM vidyAnAm avisheSheNa eShA devayAnAkhyA gatir bhavitum arhati | 

nanu aniyamAbhyupagame prakaraNavirodha uktaH -- naiSho.asti virodhaH | shabdAnumAnAbhyAM shrutismR^itibhyAm ityarthaH | tathA hi shrutiH -- tad ya itthaM viduH [chA.u. 5.10.1] iti paJNcAgnividyAvatAM devayAnaM panthAnam avatArayantI ye ceme.araNye shraddhA tapa ityupAsate [chA.u. 5.10.1] iti vidyAntarashIlinAm api paJNcAgnividyAvidbhiH samAnamArgatAM gamayati | kathaM punar avagamyate -- vidyAntarashIlinAm iyaM gatiH iti? 

nanu shraddhAtapaHparAyaNAnAm eva syAt, tanmAtrashravaNAt -- naiSha doShaH | na hi kevalAbhyAM shraddhAtapobhyAm antareNa vidyAbalam eShA gatir labhyate -- vidyayA tad Arohanti yatra kAmAH parAgatAH | na tatra dakShiNA yanti nAvidvAMsaH tapasvinaH iti shrutyantarAt | tasmAt iha shraddhAtapobhyAM vidyAntaropalakShaNam | vAjasaneyinaH tu paJNcAgnividyAdhikAre.adhIyate -- ya evam etadvidurye cAmI araNye shraddhAM satyam upAsate [bR^i.A.u. 6.2.15] iti | tatra shraddhAlavo ye satyaM brahmopAsate iti vyAkhyeyam, satyashabdasya brahmaNi asakR^itprayuktatvAt | paJNcAgnividyAvidAM ca itthaMvittayaiva upAttatvAt, vidyAntaraparAyaNAnAm eva etadupAdAnaM nyAyyam | atha ya etau panthAnau na viduH te kITAH pataN^gA yad idaM dandashUkam [bR^i.A.u. 6.2.16] iti ca mArgadvayabhraShTAnAM kaShTam adhogatiM gamayantI shrutiH devayAnapitR^iyANayor eva enAn antar bhAvayati | tatrApi vidyAvisheShAd eShAM devayAnapratipattiH | smR^itir api -- 

shuklakR^iShNe gatI hyete jagataH shAshvate mate | 
ekayA yAtyanAvR^ittim anyayAvartate punaH || [gItA 8.23] iti | 

yat punaH devayAnasya patho dvirAmnAnam upakosalavidyAyAM paJNcAgnividyAyAM ca, tat ubhayatrApi anucintanArtham | tasmAd aniyamaH ||31||

  -- o)0(o -- 
19. yAvadadhikArAdhikaraNam

|| 3.3.32 ||

yAvad adhikAram avasthitir AdhikArikANAm ||

viduSho vartamAnadehapAtAnantaraM dehAntaram utpadyate, na vA -- iti cintyate | 

nanu vidyAyAH sAdhanabhUtAyAH sampattau kaivalyanirvR^ittiH syAt, na veti neyaM cintA upapadyate | na hi pAkasAdhanasampattau, odano bhavet, na veti cintA sambhavati | nApi bhuJNjAnaH tR^ipyet, na veti cintyate -- upapannA tu iyaM cintA, brahmavidAm api keShAMcit itihAsapurANayor dehAntarotpattidarshanAt | tathA hi -- apAntaratamA nAma vedAcAryaH purANarShiH viShNuniyogAt kalidvAparayoH sandhau kR^iShNadvaipAyanaH sambabhUveti smaranti | vasiShThashca brahmaNo mAnasaH putraH san nimishApAd apagatapUrvadehaH punar brahmAdeshAn mitrAvaruNAbhyAM sambabhUveti | bhR^igvAdInAm api brahmaNa eva mAnasaputrANAM vAruNe yaj~ne punar utpattiH smaryate | sanatkumAro.api brahmaNa eva mAnasaH putraH svayaM rudrAya varapradAnAt skandatvena prAdurbabhUva | 

evam eva dakShanAradaprabhR^itInAM bhUyasI dehAntarotpattiH kathyate tena tena nimittena smR^itau | shrutAvapi mantrArthavAdayoH prAyeNopalakShyate | te ca kecit patite pUrvadehe dehAntaram Adadate, kecit tu sthita eva tasmin yogaishvaryavashAt anekadehAdAnanyAyena | sarve ca ete samadhigatasakalavedArthAH smaryante | tad eteShAM dehAntarotpattidarshanAt prAptaM brahmavidyAyAH pAkShikaM mokShahetutvam, ahetutvaM veti || 

ata uttaram ucyate -- na, teShAm apAntaratamaHprabhR^itInAM vedapravartanAdiShu lokasthitihetuShvadhikAreShu niyuktAnAm adhikAratantratvAt sthiteH | yathAsau bhagavAn savitA sahasrayugaparyantaM jagato.adhikAraM caritvA tadavasAne udayAstamayavarjitaM kaivalyam anubhavati -- atha tata Urdhva udetya naivodetA nAstam etaikala eva madhye sthAtA [chA.u. 3.11.1] iti shruteH | yathA ca vartamAnA brahmavidaH ArabdhabhogakShaye kaivalyam anubhavanti -- tasya tAvad eva ciraM yAvanna vimokShye.atha sampatsye [chA.u. 6.14.2] iti shruteH | 

evam apAntaratamaHprabhR^itayo.apIshvarAH parameshvareNa teShu teShvadhikAreShu niyuktAH santaH satyapi samyagdarshane kaivalyahetau akShINakarmANo yAvad adhikAram avatiShThante, tadavasAne ca apavR^ijyanta ityaviruddham | sakR^itpravR^ittam eva hi te phalAdAnAya karmAshayam ativAhayantaH, svAtantryeNaiva gR^ihAd iva gR^ihAntaram anyam anyaM dehaM saMcarantaH svAdhikAranirvartanAya, aparimuShitasmR^itaya eva dehendriyaprakR^itivashitvAt nirmAya dehAn yugapat krameNa vA adhitiShThanti | na ca ete jAtismarA ityucyante -- ta evaite iti smR^itiprasiddhiH -- yathA hi sulabhA nAma brahmavAdinI janakena vivaditukAmA vyudasya svaM deham, jAnakaM deham Avishya, vyudya tena, pashcAt svam eva deham Avivesha -- iti smaryate | 

yadi hyupayukte sakR^itpravR^itte karmaNi karmAntaraM dehAntarArambhakAraNam Avirbhavet, tato.anyad apyadagdhabIjaM karmAntaraM tadvad eva prasajyeteti brahmavidyAyAH pAkShikaM mokShahetutvam ahetutvaM vA shaN^kyeta | na tviyam AshaN^kA yuktA, j~nAnAt karmabIjadAhasya shrutismR^itiprasiddhatvAt | tathA hi shrutiH -- 

bhidyate hR^idayagranthishchidyante sarvasaMshayAH | 
kShIyante cAsya karmANi tasmin dR^iShTe parAvare || [mu.u. 2.2.8] iti,

smR^itilambhe sarvagranthInAM vipramokShaH [chA.u. 7.26.2] iti caivamAdyA | smR^itir api -- 

yathaidhAMsi samiddho.agnir bhasmasAt kurute.arjuna | 
j~nAnAgniH sarvakarmANi bhasmasAt kurute tathA || [gItA 4.37] iti |

bIjAnyagnyupadagdhAni na rohanti yathA punaH | 
j~nAnadagdhaiH tathA kleshair nAtmA sampadyate punaH || iti caivamAdyA | 

na ca avidyAdikleshadAhe sati kleshabIjasya karmAshayasya ekadeshadAhaH ekadeshaprarohashca ityupapadyate | na hi agnidagdhasya shAlibIjasya ekadeshapraroho dR^ishyate | pravR^ittaphalasya tu karmAshayasya mukteShoH iva vegakShayAt nivR^ittiH, tasya tAvad eva ciram [chA.u. 6.14.2] iti sharIrapAtAvadhikShepakaraNAt | tasmAd upapannA yAvadadhikAram AdhikArikANAm avasthitiH | na ca j~nAnaphalasya anaikAntikatA | tathA ca shrutiH avisheSheNaiva sarveShAM j~nAnAn mokShaM darshayati -- tad yo yo devAnAM pratyabudhyata sa eva tad abhavat tatha rShINAM tathA manuShyANAm [bR^i.A.u. 1.4.10] iti | j~nAnAntareShu ca aishvaryAdiphaleShvasaktAH syur maharShayaH | te pashcAd aishvaryakShayadarshanena nirviNNAH paramAtmaj~nAne pariniShThAya kaivalyaM prApuH ityupapadyate -- 

brahmaNA saha te sarve samprApte pratisaMcare | 
parasyAnte kR^itAtmAnaH pravishanti paraM padam || iti smaraNAt | 

pratyakShaphalatvAcca j~nAnasya phalavirahAshaN^kAnupapattiH | karmaphale hi svargAdAvanubhavAnArUDhe syAd AshaN^kA, bhaved vA na veti | anubhavArUDhaM tu j~nAnaphalam -- yat sAkShAd aparokShAd brahma [bR^i.A.u. 3.4.1] iti shruteH, tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7] iti siddhavadupadeshAt | 

na hi tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7] ityasya vAkyasya arthaH -- tat tvaM mR^ito bhaviShyasIti -- evaM pariNetuM shakyaH | tad dhaitat pashyann R^iShir vAmadevaH pratipede.ahaM manur abhavaM sUryashca [bR^i.A.u. 1.4.10] iti ca samyagdarshanakAlam eva tat phalaM sarvAtmatvaM darshayati | tasmAt aikAntikI viduShaH kaivalyasiddhiH ||32||

 -- o)0(o -- 
15. akSharAdhikaraNam

|| 3.3.33 ||

vAjasaneyake shrUyate -- etad vai tad akSharaM gArgi brAhmaNA abhivadantyasthUlam anaNvahrasvam adIrgham alohitam asneham [bR^i.A.u. 3.8.8] ityAdi | tathA AtharvaNe shrUyate -- atha parA yayA tad akSharam adhigamyate yat tad apAshyam agrAhyam agotram avarNam [mu.u. 1.1.5] ityAdi | tathaiva anyatrApi visheShanirAkaraNadvAreNa akSharaM paraM brahma shrAvyate | tatra ca kvacit kecit atiriktA visheShAH pratiShidhyante | tAsAM visheShapratiShedhabuddhInAM kiM sarvAsAM sarvatra prAptiH, uta vyavastheti saMshaye, shrutivibhAgAt vyavasthAprAptau -- 

akSharadhiyAM tu avarodhaH sAmAnyatadbhAvAbhyAm 
aupasadavat, tad uktam || 

ucyate -- akSharaviShayAH tu visheShapratiShedhabuddhayaH sarvAH sarvatrAvaroddhavyAH, sAmAnyatadbhAvAbhyAm -- samAno hi sarvatra visheShanirAkaraNarUpo brahmapratipAdanaprakAraH | tad eva ca sarvatra pratipAdyaM brahma abhinnaM pratyabhij~nAyate | tatra kim iti anyatra kR^itA buddhayo.anyatra na syuH | tathA ca AnandAdayaH pradhAnasya [ve.sU. 3.3.11] ityatra vyAkhyAtam | tatra vidhirUpANi visheShaNAni cintitAni, iha pratiShedharUpANIti visheShaH | prapaJNcArthashcAyaM cintAbhedaH | aupasadavad iti nidarshanam | yathA jAmadagnye.ahIne puroDAshinIShUpasatsu coditAsu, puroDAshapradAnamantrANAm agner verhotraM veradhvaram ityevam AdInAm udgAtR^ivedotpannAnAm api adhvaryubhir abhisambandho bhavati, adhvaryukartR^ikatvAt puroDashapradAnasya, pradhAnatantratvAccAN^gAnAm | 

evam ihApi akSharatantratvAt tadvisheShaNAnAM yatra kvacid apyutpannAnAm akShareNa sarvatrAbhisambandha ityarthaH | tad uktaM prathame kANDe -- guNamukhyavyatikrame tadarthatvAn mukhyena vedasaMyogaH [jai. sU. 3.3.8] ityatra ||33||

  -- o)0(o -- 
16. iyadadhikaraNam

|| 3.3.34 || 

dvA suparNA sayujA sakhAyA 
samAnaM vR^ikShaM pariShasvajAte | 
tayor anyaH pippalaM svAdvatty 
anashnann anyo abhicAkashIti || [mu.u. 3.1.1]

ityadhyAtmAdhikAre mantram AtharvaNikAH shvetAshvatarAshca paThanti | tathA kaThAH -- 

R^itaM pibantau sukR^itasya loke 
guhAM praviShTau parame parArdhye | 
chAyAtapau brahmavido vadanti 
paJNcAgnayo ye ca triNAciketAH || [ka.u. 1.3.1] iti | 

kim atra vidyaikatvam, uta vidyAnAnAtvam iti saMshayaH | kiM tAvat prAptam? vidyAnAnAtvam iti | kutaH? visheShadarshanAt -- dvA suparNA ityatra hi ekasya bhoktR^itvaM dR^ishyate, ekasya ca abhoktR^itvaM dR^ishyate | R^itaM pibantau ityatra ubhayor api bhoktR^itvam eva dR^ishyate | tat vedyarUpaM bhidyamAnaM vidyAM bhindyAd ityevaM prApte -- 

iyad AmananAt ||

bravIti -- vidyaikatvam iti | kutaH? yataH ubhayor apyanayor mantrayoH iyattAparicchinnaM dvitvopetaM vedyaM rUpam abhinnam Amananti | 

nanu darshito rUpabhedaH -- netyucyate | ubhAvapyetau mantrau jIvadvitIyam IshvaraM pratipAdayataH, nArthAntaram | dvA suparNA ityatra tAvat -- anashnann anyo abhicAkashIti ityashanAyAdyatItaH paramAtmA pratipAdyate | vAkyasheShe.api ca sa eva pratipAdyamAno dR^ishyate, juShTaM yadA pashyatyanyam Isham asya mahimAnam iti | R^itaM pibantau ityatra tu jIve pibati, ashanAyAdyatItaH paramAtmApi sAhacaryAt chatrinyAyena pibatItyupacaryate | paramAtmaprakaraNaM hi etat, anyatra dharmAd anyatrAdharmAt ityupakramAt | tadviShaya eva ca atrApi vAkyasheSho bhavati -- yaH setur IjAnAnAm akSharaM brahma yat param iti | guhAM praviShTAvatmAnau hi [ve.sU. 1.2.11] ityatra ca etat prapaJNcitam | tasmAn nAsti vedyabhedaH | tasmAcca vidyaikatvam | api ca triShvapyeteShu vedAnteShu paurvAparyAlocane paramAtmavidyaiva avagamyate | tAdAtmyavivakShayaiva jIvopAdAnam, nArthAntaravivakShayA | na ca paramAtmavidyAyAM bhedAbhedavicArAvatAro.astItyuktam | tasmAt prapaJNcArtha eva eSha prayogaH | tasmAccAdhikadharmopasaMhAra iti ||34||

  -- o)0(o -- 
antaratvAdhikaraNam

|| 3.3.35 || 

antarA bhUtagrAmavat svAtmanaH ||

yat sAkShAd aparokShAd brahma ya AtmA sarvAntaraH [bR^i.A.u. 3.4.1] ityevaM dviH UShastakaholaprashnayoH nairantaryeNa vAjasaneyinaH samAmananti | tatra saMshayaH -- vidyaikatvaM vA syAt, vidyAnAnAtvaM veti | vidyAnAnAtvam iti tAvat prAptam, abhyAsasAmarthyAt | anyathA hi anUnAnatiriktArthe dvir AmnAnam anarthakam eva syAt | tasmAt yathA abhyAsAt karmabhedaH, evam abhyAsAd vidyAbheda ityevaM prApte, pratyAha -- antarA AmnAnAvisheShAt svAtmanaH vidyaikatvam iti | sarvAntaro hi svAtmA ubhayatrApyavishiShTaH pR^icchyate, pratyucyate ca | na hi dvAvatmAnau ekasmin dehe sarvAntarau sambhavataH | tadA hi ekasya AJNjasaM sarvAntaratvam avakalpeta, ekasya tu bhUtagrAmavat naiva sarvAntaratvaM syAt | yathA ca paJNcabhUtasamUhe dehe -- pR^ithivyA Apo.antarAH, adbhyaH tejo.antaram iti -- satyapyApekShike.antaratve, naiva mukhyaM sarvAntaratvaM bhavati, tathehApItyarthaH | athavA bhUtagrAmavad iti shrutyantaraM nidarshayati | yathA -- 

eko devAH sarvabhUteShu gUDhaH 
sarvavyApI sarvabhUtAntarAtmA [shve.u. 6.11]

ityasmin mantre samasteShu bhUtagrAmeShv eka eva sarvAntara AtmA AmnAyate -- evam anayor api brAhmaNayoH ityarthaH | tasmAt vedyaikyAt vidyaikatvam iti ||35||

|| 3.3.36 || 

anyathA bhedAnupapattiH iti cen nopadeshAntaravat || 

atha yad uktam -- anabhyupagamyamAne vidyAbhede AmnAnabhedAnupapattiH iti, tat parihartavyam | atrocyate -- nAyaM doShaH | upadeshAntaravad upapatteH | yathA tANDinAm upaniShadi ShaShThe prapAThake -- sa AtmA tattvam asi shvetaketo iti navakR^itvo.apyupadeshe na vidyAbhedo bhavati, evam ihApi bhaviShyati | kathaM ca navakR^itvo.apyupadeshe vidyAbhedo na bhavati? upakramopasaMhArAbhyAm ekArthatAvagamAt -- bhUya eva mA bhagavAn vij~nApayatu iti ca ekasyaivArthasya punaH punaH pratipipAdayiShitatvena upakShepAt AshaN^kAntaranirAkaraNena ca asakR^idupadeshopapatteH | evam ihApi prashnarUpAbhedAt, ato.anyad Artam iti ca parisamAptyavisheShAt upakramopasaMhArau tAvad ekArthaviShayau dR^ishyete | yad eva sAkShAd aparokShAd brahma iti dvitIye prashne evakAraM prayuJNjAnaH pUrvaprashnagatam evArtham uttaratrAnukR^iShyamANaM darshayati | pUrvasmiMshca brAhmaNe kAryakaraNavyatiriktasya AtmanaH sadbhAvaH kathyate | uttarasmiMH tu tasyaiva ashanAyAdisaMsAradharmAtItatvaM visheShaH kathyate -- ityekArthatopapattiH | tasmAt ekA vidyeti ||36||

  -- o)0(o -- 

vyatihArAdhikaraNam 

|| 3.3.37 ||

vyatihAro vishiMShanti hItaravat ||

yathA -- tadyo.ahaM so.asau yo.asau so.aham ityAdityapuruShaM prakR^ityaitareyiNaH samAmananti, tathA jAbAlAH -- tvaM vA ahamasmi bhagavo devate.ahaM vai tu amasi iti | tatra saMshayaH -- kim iha vyatihAreNa ubhayarUpA matiH kartavyA, uta ekarUpaiveti | ekarUpaiveti tAvadAha | na hi atra Atmana IshvareNaikatvaM muktvA anyat kiMciccintayitavyam asti | yadi caivaM cintayitavyavisheShaH parikalpyeta, saMsAriNashca IshvarAtmatvam, Ishvarasya saMsAryAtmatvam iti -- tatra saMsAriNastAvadIshvarAtmatve utkarSho bhavet | Ishvarasya tu saMsAryAtmatve nikarShaH kR^itaH syAt | tasmAt aikarUpyam eva mateH | vyatihArAmnAyastu ekatvadR^iDhIkArArtha ityevaM prApte, pratyAha -- vyatihAro.ayam AdhyAnAyAmnAyate | itaravat -- yathA itare guNAH sarvAtmatvaprabhR^itayaH AdhyAnAya AmnAyante, tadvat | tathA hi vishiMShanti samAmnAtAraH ubhayoccAraNena -- tvamahamasmyahaM ca tu amasi iti | tacca ubhayarUpAyAM matau kartavyAyAm arthavadbhavati | anyathA hi idaM visheSheNobhayAmnam anarthakaM syAt, ekenaiva kR^itatvAt | 

nanu ubhayAmnAnasya arthavisheShe parikalpyamAne devatAyAH saMsAryAtmatvApatteH nikarShaH prasajyetetyuktam -- naiSha doShaH | aikAtmyasyaivAnena prakAreNAnucintyamAnatvAt | 

nanu, evaM sati sa eva ekatvadR^iDhIkAra Apadyeta -- na vayam ekatvadR^iDhIkAraM vArayAmaH | kiM tarhi, vyatihAreNa iha dvirUpA matiH kartavyA vacanaprAmANyAt, naikarUpetyetAvat upapAdayAmaH | phalataH tu ekatvam api dR^iDhIbhavati | yathA AdhyAnArthe.api satyakAmAdiguNopadeshe tadguNa IshvaraH prasidhyati, tadvat | tasmAd ayam AdhyAtavyo vyatihAraH samAne ca viShaye upasaMhartavyo bhavatIti ||37||

 -- o)0(o -- 

satyAdyadhikaraNam 

|| 3.3.38 || 

saiva hi satyAdayaH ||

sa yo haitaM mahadyakShaM prathamajaM veda satyaM brahma ityAdinA vAjasaneyake satyavidyAM sanAmAkSharopAsanAM vidhAya, anantaramAmnAyate -- tadyattatsatyamasau sa Adityo ya eSha etasmin maNDale puruSho yashcAyaM dakShiNe.akShan puruShaH ityAdi | tatra saMshayaH -- kiM dve ete satyavidye, kiM vA ekaiveti | dve iti tAvat prAptam | bhedena hi phalasaMyogo bhavati -- jayatImAlMlokAn iti purastAt, hanti pApmAnaM jahAti ca ityupariShTAt | prakR^itAkarShaNaM tu upAsyaikatvAd ityevaM prApte -- 

brUmaH -- ekaiveyaM satyavidyeti | kutaH? tadyattatsatyam iti prakR^itAkarShaNAt | 

nanu vidyAbhede.api prakR^itAkarShaNam upAsyaikatvAd upapadyata ityuktam -- naitad evam | yatra tu vispaShTAt kAraNAntarAt vidyAbhedaH pratIyate, tatra etad evaM syAt | atra tu ubhayathA sambhave tadyattatsatyam iti prakR^itAkarShaNAt pUrvavidyAsambaddham eva satyam uttaratra AkR^iShyata iti ekavidyAtvanishcayaH | yat punar uktam -- phalAntarashravaNAdvidyAntaram iti, atrocyate -- tasyopaniShadahaH ... aham iti ca aN^gAntaropadeshasya stAvakamidaM phalAntarashravaNam ityadoShaH | api ca arthavAdAd eva phale kalpayitavye sati, vidyaikatve ca avayaveShu shrUyamANAni bahUnyapi phalAni avayavinyAm eva vidyAyAm upasaMhartavyAni bhavanti | tasmAt saiveyam ekA satyavidyA tena tena visheSheNopetA AmnAtA -- ityataH sarva eva satyAdayo guNA ekasmin prayoge upasaMhartavyAH || 

kecit punar asmin sUtre idaM ca vAjasaneyakam akShyAdityapuruShaviShayaM vAkyam, chAndogye ca atha ya eSho.antarAditye hiraNmayaH puruSho dR^ishyate ya eSho.akShiNi puruSho dR^ishyate [chA.u. 1.6.6] ityudAhR^itya, saiveyam akShyAdityapuruShaviShayA vidyA ubhayatra ekaiveti kR^itvA, satyAdIn guNAn vAjasaneyibhyashchandogAnAm upasaMhAryAn manyante | tan na sAdhu lakShyate | chAndogye hi karmasambandhinI udgIthavyapAshrayA vidyA vij~nAyate | tatra hi AdimadhyAvasAneShu karmasambandhicihnAni bhavanti -- iyam eva rgagniH sAma [chA.u. 1.6.1] ityupakrame, tasya rk ca sAma ca geShNau tasmAd udgIthaH [chA.u. 1.6.8] iti madhye, ya evaM vidvAn sAma gAyati [chA.u. 1.7.9] ityupasaMhAre | naivaM vAjasaneyake kiMcit karmasambandhi cihnam asti | tatra prakramabhedAt vidyAbhede sati guNavyavasthaiva yukteti ||38||

  -- o)0(o -- 

kAmAdyadhikaraNam

|| 3.3.39 || 

kAmAdItaratra tatra cAyatanAdibhyaH ||

atha yad idam asmin brahmapure daharaM puNDarIkaM veshma daharo.asminn antar AkAshaH [chA.u. 8.1.1] iti prastutya, chandogA adhIyate -- eSha AtmApahatapApmA vijaro vimR^ityur vishoko vijighatso.apipAsaH satyakAmaH satyasaN^kalpaH [chA.u. 8.1.5] ityAdi | tathA vAjasaneyinaH -- sa vA eSha mahAn aja AtmA yo.ayaM vij~nAnamayaH prANeShu ya eSho.antarhR^idaya AkAshaH tasmiJNshete sarvasya vashI ityAdi | tatra vidyaikatvaM parasparaguNayogashca, kiM vA neti saMshaye -- vidyaikatvam iti | tatredam ucyate -- kAmAdIti, satyakAmAdItyarthaH -- yathA devadatto dattaH, satyabhAmA bhAmeti | yadetat chAndogye hR^idayAkAshasya satyakAmatvAd iguNajAtam upalabhyate, tad itaratra vAjasaneyake sa vA eSha mahAn aja AtmA ityatra sambadhyeta | yacca vAjasaneyake vashitvAdi upalabhyate, tad api itaratra chAndogye eSha AtmApahatapApmA [chA.u. 8.1.5] ityatra sambadhyeta | kutaH? AyatanAdisAmAnyAt | samAnaM hi ubhayatrApi hR^idayamAyatanam, samAnashca vedya IshvaraH, samAnaM ca tasya setutvaM lokAsambhedaprayojanam -- ityevamAdi bahusAmAnyaM dR^ishyate | 

nanu visheSho.api dR^ishyate -- chAndogye hR^idayAkAshasya guNayogaH, vAjasaneyake tu AkAshAshrayasya brahmaNa iti -- na, dahara uttarebhyaH ityatra cchAndogye.api AkAshashabdaM brahmaiveti pratiShThApitatvAt | ayaM tu atra vidyate visheShaH -- saguNA hi brahmavidyA chAndogye upadishyate -- atha ya ihAtmAnamanuvidya vrajantyetAMshca satyAnkAmAn ityAtmavat kAmAnAm api vedyatvashravaNAt, vAjasaneyake tu nirguNam eva brahma upadishyamAnaM dR^ishyate -- atha urdhvaM vimokShAya brUhi asaN^go hyayaM puruShaH ityAdiprashnaprativacanasamanvayAt | vashitvAdi tu stutyartham eva guNajAtaM vAjasaneyake saN^kIrtyate | tathA ca upariShTAt sa eSha neti netyAtmA ityAdinA nirguNam eva brahma upasaMharati | guNavatastu brahmaNa ekatvAt vibhUtipradarshanAya ayaM guNopasaMhAraH sUtritaH, nopAsanAya -- iti draShTavyam ||39||

  -- o)0(o -- 

AdarAdhikaraNam

|| 3.3.40 || 

chAndogye vaishvAnaravidyAM prakR^itya shrUyate -- tad yad bhaktaM prathamam Agacchet tad dhomIyaM sa yAM prathamAm AhutiM juhuyAt tAM juhuyAt prANAya svAhA [chA.u. 5.19.1] ityAdi | tatra paJNca prANAhutayo vihitAH | tAsu ca parastAd agnihotrashabdaH prayuktaH, ya etad evaM vidvAn agnihotraM juhoti [chA.u. 5.24.2] iti, yatheha kShudhitA bAlA mAtaraM paryupAsate | evaM sarvANi bhUtAnyagnihotram upAsate [chA.u. 5.24.5] iti ca | 

tatredaM vicAryate -- kiM bhojanalope lopaH prANAgnihotrasya, uta alopa iti | tad yad bhaktam iti bhaktAgamanasaMyogashravaNAt, bhaktAgamanasya ca bhojanArthatvAt, bhojanalope lopaH prANAgnihotrasyetyevaM prApte,

AdarAd alopaH ||

na lupyeteti tAvad Aha | kasmAt? AdarAt | tathA hi vaishvAnaravidyAyAm eva jAbAlAnAM shrutiH -- pUrvo.atithibhyo.ashnIyAt | yathA ha vai svayam ahutvAgnihotraM parasya juhuyAd evaM tat iti atithibhojanasya prAthamyaM ninditvA, svAmibhojanaM prathamaM prApayantI prANAgnihotre AdaraM karoti | yA hi na prAthamyalopaM sahate, natarAM sA prAthamyavato.agnihotrasya lopaM saheteti manyate | 

nanu bhojanArthabhaktAgamanasaMyogAd bhojanalope lopaH prApitaH -- na, tasya dravyavisheShavidhAnArthatvAt | prAkR^ite hi agnihotre payaHprabhR^itInAM dravyANAM niyatatvAt ihApi agnihotrashabdAt kauNDapAyinAm ayanavat taddharmaprAptau satyAm, bhaktadravyatAguNavisheShavidhAnArtham idaM vAkyam tad yad bhaktam iti | ato guNalope na mukhyasyetyevaM prAptam | bhojanalope.api adbhir vA anyena vA dravyeNAviruddhena pratinidhAnanyAyena prANAgnihotrasyAnuShThAnam iti ||40|| 

|| 3.3.41 ||

ata uttaraM paThati -- 

upasthite.ataH tadvacanAt ||

+++upasthite bhojane ataH tasmAd eva bhojanadravyAt prathamopanipatitAt prANAgnihotraM nirvartayitavyam | kasmAt? tadvacanAt | tathA hi -- tad yad bhaktaM prathamam Agacchet tad dhomIyam iti siddhavad bhaktopanipAtaparAmarshena parArthadravyasAdhyatAM prANAhutInAM vidadhAti | tAH aprayojakalakShaNApannAH satyaH, kathaM bhojanalope dravyAntaraM pratinidhApayeyuH | na ca atra prAkR^itAgnihotradharmaprAptir asti | kuNDapAyinAm ayane hi mAsam agnihotraM juhoti iti vidhyuddeshagato.agnihotrashabdaH tadvad bhAvaM vidhApayed iti yuktA taddharmaprAptiH | iha punar arthavAdagato.agnihotrashabdaH na tadvad bhAvaM vidhApayitum arhati | taddharmaprAptau ca abhyupagamyamAnAyAm, agnyuddharaNAdayo.api prApyeran | na ca asti sambhavaH | agnyuddharaNaM tAvat homAdhikaraNabhAvAya | na ca ayam agnau homaH, bhojanArthatAvyAghAtaprasaN^gAt | bhojanArthopanItadravyasambandhAccAsya eva eSha homaH | tathA ca jAbAlashrutiH pUrvo.atithibhyo.ashnIyAt iti AsyAdhArAm eva imAM homanirvR^ittiM darshayati | ata eva ca ihApi sAmpAdikAnyevAgnihotrAN^gAni darshayati -- ura eva vedir lomAni barhir hR^idayaM gArhapatyo mano.anvAhAryapacana Asyam AhavanIyaH iti | vedishrutishcAtra sthaNDilamAtropalakShaNArthA draShTavyA, mukhyAgnihotre vedyabhAvAt, tadaN^gAnAM ca iha sampipAdayiShitatvAt | bhojanenaiva ca kR^itakAlena saMyogAt na agnihotrakAlAvarodhasambhavaH | evam anye.api upasthAnAdayo dharmAH kecit kathaMcit virudhyante | tasmAd bhojanapakSha eva ete mantradravyadevatAsaMyogAt paJNca homA nirvartayitavyAH | yat tu Adaradarshanavacanam, tat bhojanapakShe prAthamyavidhAnArtham | na hyasti vacanasya atibhAraH | na tu anena asya nityatA shakyate darshayitum | tasmAt bhojanalope lopa eva prANAgnihotrasyeti ||41||

  -- o)0(o -- 
tannirdhAraNAdhikaraNam

|| 3.3.42||

+++santi karmAN^gavyapAshrayANi vij~nAnAni -- om ityetad akSharam udgItham upAsIta [chA.u. 1.4.1] ityevamAdIni | kiM tAni nityAnyeva syuH karmasu, parNamayItvAd ivat | uta anityAni, godohanAdivad iti vicArayAmaH | kiM tAvat prAptam? nityAnIti | kutaH? prayogavacanaparigrahAt -- anArabhyAdhItAnyapi hi etAni udgIthAdidvAreNa kratusambandhAt kratuprayogavacanenaiva aN^gAntaravat saMspR^ishyante | yat tu eShAM svavAkyeShu phalashravaNam -- ApayitA ha vai kAmAnAM bhavati ityAdi, tadvartamAnApadesharUpatvAd arthavAdamAtram eva, apApashlokashravaNAdivat, na phalapradhAnam | tasmAt yathA yasya parNamayI 
juhUr bhavati na sa pApaM shlokaM sR^iNoti ityevamAdInAm aprakaraNapaThitAnAm api juhvAdidvAreNa kratupraveshAt prakaraNapaThitavat nityatA, evamudgIthAdyupAsanAnAmapItyevaM prApte -- 

tannirdhAraNAniyamaH taddR^iShTeH pR^ithag ghyapratibandhaH phalam ||

brUmaH -- tannirdhAraNAniyama iti | yAnyetAni udgIthAdikarmaguNayAthAtmyanirdhAraNAni -- rasatamaH, AptiH, samR^iddhiH, mukhyaprANaH, AdityaH -- ityevamAdIni, naitAni nityavat karmasu niyamyeran | kutaH? taddR^iShTeH | tathA hi anityatvam evaMjAtIyakAnAM darshayati shrutiH -- tenobhau kuruto yashcaitad evaM veda yashca na veda ityaviduSho.api kriyAbhyanuj~nAnAt | prastAvAdidevatAvij~nAnavihInAnAm api prastotrAdInAM yAjanAdhyavasAnadarshanAt -- prastotaryA devatA prastAvam anvAyattA tAM ced avidvAn prastoShyasi tAM ced avidvAn udgAsyasi tAM ced avidvAn pratihariShyasi iti ca | 

api ca evaMjAtIyakasya karmavyapAshrayasya vij~nAnasya pR^ithag eva karmaNaH phalam upalabhyate -- karmaphalasiddhyapratibandhaH tatsamR^iddhiH atishayavisheShaH kashcit -- tenobhau kuruto yashcaitad evaM veda yashca na veda | nAnA tu vidyA cAvidyA ca yad eva vidyayA karoti shraddhayopaniShadA tad eva vIryavattaraM bhavati iti | tatra nAnA tu iti vidvadavidvatprayogayoH pR^ithakkaraNAt, vIryavattaram iti ca tarappratyayaprayogAt vidyAhInam api vIryavad iti gamyate | tacca anityatve vidyAyA upapadyate | nityatve tu kathaM tadvihInaM karma vIryavad ityanuj~nAyeta | sarvAN^gopasaMhAre hi vIryavatkarmeti sthitiH | tathA lokasAmAdiShu pratiniyatAni pratyupAsanaM phalAni shiShyante -- kalpante hAsmai lokA UrdhvAshcAvR^ittAshca ityevamAdIni | na cedaM phalashravaNam arthavAdamAtraM yuktaM pratipattum | tathA hi guNavAda Apadyeta | phalopadeshe tu mukhyavAdopapattiH | prayAjAdiShu tu itikartavyatAkAN^kShasya kratoH prakR^itatvAt tAdarthye sati yuktaM phalashruter arthavAdatvam | tathA anArabhyAdhIteShvapi parNamayItvAdiShu -- na hi parNamayItvAdInAm akriyAtmakAnAm Ashrayam antareNa phalasambandho.avakalpate | godohanAdInAM hi prakR^itAppraNayanAdyAshrayalAbhAd upapannaH phalavidhiH | tathA bailvAdInAm api prakR^itayUpAdyAshrayalAbhAd upapannaH phalavidhiH | na tu parNamayItvAdiShu evaMvidhaH kashcid AshrayaH prakR^ito.asti | vAkyenaiva tu juhvAdyAshrayatAM vivakShitvA phale.api vidhiM vivakShato vAkyabhedaH syAt | upAsanAnAM tu kriyAtmakatvAt vishiShTavidhAnopapatteH udgIthAdyAshrayANAM phale vidhAnaM na virudhyate | tasmAt yathA kratvAshrayANyapi godohanAdIni phalasaMyogAd anityAni, evam udgIthAdyupAsanAnyapi iti draShTavyam | ata eva ca kalpasUtrakArA naivaMjAtIyakAnyupAsanAni kratuShu kalpayAMcakruH ||44||

20. pradAnAdhikaraNam

|| 3.3.45 ||
+++
vAjasaneyake vadiShyAmyevAham iti vAg dadhre ityatra adhyAtmaM vAgAdInAM prANaH shreShTho.avadhAritaH, adhidaivatam agnyAdInAM vAyuH | tathA chAndogye -- 
vAyur vAva saMvargaH ityatra adhidaivatam agnyAdInAM vAyuH saMvargo.avadhAritaH, prANo vAva saMvargaH ityatra adhyAtmaM vAgAdInAM prANaH | tatra saMshayaH -- kiM pR^ithag evemau vAyuprANAv upagantavyau syAtAm, uta apR^ithag iti | apR^ithag iti tAvat prAptam, tattvAbhedAt | na hi abhinne tattve pR^ithag anucintanaM nyAyyam | darshayati ca shrutiH adhyAtmam adhidaivataM ca tattvAbhedam -- agnir vAg bhUtvA mukhaM prAvishat ityArabhya | tathA ta ete sarva eva samAH sarve.anantAH iti AdhyAtmikAnAM prANAnAm AdhidaivikIM vibhUtim AtmabhUtAM darshayati | tathA anyatrApi tatra tatra adhyAtmam adhidaivataM ca bahudhA tattvAbhedadarshanaM bhavati | kvacicca yaH prANaH sa vAyuH iti spaShTam eva vAyuM prANaM ca ekaM karoti | tathA udAhR^ite.api vAjasaneyibrAhmaNe yatashcodeti sUryaH ityasmin upasaMhArashloke, prANAd vA eSha udeti prANe.astam eti iti prANenaiva upasaMharan ekatvaM darshayati | tasmAd ekam eva vrataM caret prANyAccaivApAnyAcca iti ca prANavratenaiva ekenopasaMharan etad eva draDhayati | tathA chAndogye.api parastAt mahAtmanashcaturo deva ekaH kaH sa jagAra bhuvanasya gopAH ityekam eva saMvargaM gamayati | na bravIti -- eka eva eShAM caturNAM saMvargaH, aparo.apareShAm iti | tasmAd apR^ithaktvam upagamanasyetyevaM prApte -- 

pradAnavad eva tad uktam ||

brUmaH -- pR^ithag eva vAyuprANAv upagantavyAviti | kasmAt? pR^ithag upadeshAt | AdhyAnArtho hi ayam adhyAtmAdhidaivavibhAgopadeshaH | so.asatyAdhyAnapR^ithaktve anarthaka eva syAt | nanu uktam, apR^ithaganucintanaM tattvAbhedAditi -- naiSha doShaH | tattvAbhede.apyavasthAbhedAt upadeshabhedavashena anucintanabhedopapatteH, shlokopanyAsasya ca tattvAbhedAbhiprAyeNApi upapadyamAnasya pUrvoditadhyeyabhedanirAkaraNasAmarthyAbhAvAt, sa yathaiShAM prANAnAM madhyamaH prANa evam etAsAM devatAnAM vAyuH iti ca upamAnopameyakaraNAt | etena vratopanyAso vyAkhyAtaH | 
 ekam eva vratam iti ca evakAraH vAgAdivratanivartanena prANavratapratipattyarthaH | bhagnavratAni hi vAgAdInyuktAni, tAni mR^ityuH shramo bhUtvopayeme iti shruteH | na vAyuvratanivR^ittyarthaH, athAto vratamImAMsA iti prastutya tulyavat vAyuprANayor abhagnavratatvasya nirdhAritatvAt | ekam eva vrataM caret iti ca uktvA, teno etasyai devatAyai sAyujyaM salokatAM jayati iti vAyuprAptiM phalaM bruvan vAyuvratamanivartitaM darshayati | devatetyatra vAyuH syAt, aparicchinnAtmakatvasya propsatatvAt, purastAt prayogAcca -- saiShAnastamitA devatA yadvAyuH iti | tathA tau vA etau dvau saMvargau vAyur eva deveShu prANaH prANeShu iti bhedena vyapadishati | te vA ete paJNcAnye paJNcAnye dasha santastatkR^itam iti ca bhedenaiva upasaMharati | tasmAt pR^ithageva upagamanam | pradAnavat -- yathA indrAya rAj~ne puroDAshamekAdashakapAlam indrAyAdhirAjAyendrAya svarAj~ne ityasyAM tripuroDAshinyAmiShTau, sarveShAm abhigamayannavadyatyachambaTakAram ityato vacanAt, indrAbhedAcca, sahapradAnAshaN^kAyAm -- rAjAdiguNabhedAt yAjyAnuvAkyAvyatyAsavidhAnAcca yathAnyAsam eva devatApR^ithaktvAt pradAnapR^ithaktvaM bhavati | evaM tattvAbhede.api AdhyeyAMshapR^ithaktvAt AdhyAnapR^ithaktvamityarthaH | tad uktaM saMkarShe -- nAnA vA devatA pR^ithagj~nAnAt iti | tatra tu dravyadevatAbhedAt yAgabhedo vidyate | naivamiha vidyAbhedo.asti, upakramopasaMhArAbhyAm adhyAtmAdhidaivopadesheShu ekavidyAvidhAnapratIteH | vidyaikye.api tu adhyAtmAdhidaivabhedAt pravR^ittibhedo bhavati -- agnihotra iva sAyamprAtaHkAlabhedAt -- ityetAvadabhipretya pradAnavadityuktam ||43||
+++
liN^gabhUyastvAdhikaraNam

|| 3.3.44 ||

liN^gabhUyastvAt tad dhi balIyastad api ||

vAjasaneyino.agnirahasye naiva vA idam agre sadAsIt ityetasminbrAhmaNe mano.adhikR^itya adhIyate -- tatShaTtriMshataM sahasrANyapashyadAtmano.agnInarkAnmanomayAnmanashcitaH ityAdi | tathaiva vAk citaH prANacitashcakShushcitaH shrotracitaH karmacito.agnicitaH iti pR^ithagagnIn Amananti sAmpAdikAn | teShu saMshayaH -- kimete manashcidAdayaH kriyAnupraveshinaH taccheShabhUtAH, uta svatantrAH kevalavidyAtmakA iti | tatra prakaraNAt kriyAnupraveshe prApte, svAtantryaM tAvatpratijAnIte -- liN^gabhUyastvAd iti | bhUyAMsi hi liN^gAni asminbrAhmaNe kevalavidyAtmakatvameShAm upodbalayanti dR^ishyante -- tadyatkiMcemAni bhUtAni manasA saN^kalpayanti teShAm eva sA kR^itiH iti, tAnhaitAnevaMvide sarvadA sarvANi bhUtAni cinvantyapi svapate iti ca evaMjAtIyakAni | tad dhi liN^gaM prakaraNAd balIyaH | tad apyuktaM pUrvasmin kANDe -- shrutiliN^gavAkyaprakaraNasthAnasamAkhyAnAM samavAye pAradaurbalyam arthaviprakarShAt iti ||44||

pUrvavikalpaH prakaraNAtsyAt kriyA mAnasavat|| 3.3.45|| 

|| 3.3.45|| 

naitadyuktam -- svatantrA ete.agnayo.ananyasheShabhUtA iti | pUrvasya kriyAmayasya agneH prakaraNAt tadviShaya eva ayaM vikalpavisheShopadeshaH syAt, na svatantraH | 

nanu prakaraNAl liN^gaM balIyaH -- satyam evam etat | liN^gam api tu evaMjAtIyakaM na prakaraNAd balIyo bhavati | anyArthadarshanaM hi etat, sAmpAdikAgniprashaMsArUpatvAt | anyArthadarshanaM ca asatyAmanyasyAM prAptau guNavAdenApyupapadyamAnaM na prakaraNaM bAdhitum utsahate | tasmAt sAmpAdikA apyete.agnayaH prakaraNAt kriyAnupraveshina eva syuH | mAnasavat -- yathA dasharAtrasya dashame.ahani avivAkye pR^ithivyA pAtreNa samudrasya somasya prajApataye devatAyai gR^ihyamANasya grahaNAsAdanahavanAharaNopahvAnabhakShaNAni mAnasAnyeva AmnAyante, sa ca mAnaso.api grahakalpaH kriyAprakaraNAt kriyAsheSha eva bhavati -- evam ayam apyagnikalpa ityarthaH ||45||

|| 3.3.46 || 

atideshAcca ||

atideshashca eShAm agnInAM kriyAnupravesham upodbalayati -- ShaTtriMshatsahasrANyagnayo.arkAH teShAm ekaika eva tAvAn yAvAn asau pUrvaH iti | sati hi sAmAnye atideshaH pravartate | tatashca pUrveNa iShTakAcitena kriyAnupraveshinA agninA sAmpAdikAn agnIn atidishan kriyAnupravesham eva eShAM dyotayati ||46||

|| 3.3.47 || 

vidyaiva tu nirdhAraNAt ||

tushabdaH pakShaM vyAvartayati | vidyAtmakA eva ete svatantrA manashcidAdayo.agnayaH syuH, na kriyAsheShabhUtAH | tathA hi nirdhArayati -- te haite vidyAcita eva iti, vidyayA haivaita evaMvidashcitA bhavanti iti ca ||47||

|| 3.3.48 ||

darshanAcca ||

dR^ishyate ca eteShAM svAtantrye liN^gam | tatpurastAd darshitam -- liN^gabhUyastvAt ityatra ||48|| 



|| 3.3.49 ||

nanu liN^gam api asatyAmanyasyAM prAptau asAdhakaM kasyacid arthasyeti, apAsya tat, prakaraNasAmarthyAt kriyAsheShatvamadhyavasitam -- ityata uttaraM paThati -- 

shrutyAdibalIyastvAcca na bAdhaH ||

naivaM prakaraNasAmarthyAt kriyAsheShatvam adhyavasAya svAtantryapakSho bAdhitavyaH, shrutyAder balIyastvAt | balIyAMsi hi prakaraNAt shrutiliN^gavAkyAnIti sthitaM shrutiliN^gasUtre | tAni ca iha svAtantryapakShaM sAdhayanti dR^ishyante | katham? shrutiH tAvat -- te haite vidyAcita eva iti | tathA liN^gam -- sarvadA sarvANi bhUtAni cinvantyapi svapate iti | tathA vAkyam api -- vidyayA haivaita evaMvidashcitA bhavanti iti | vidyAcita eva iti hi sAvadhAraNAm iyaM shrutiH kriyAnupraveshe.amIShAm abhyupagamyamAne pIDitA syAt | 

nanu abAhyasAdhanatvAbhiprAyam idam avadhAraNaM bhaviShyati -- netyucyate | tadabhiprAyatAyAM hi vidyAcitaH iti iyatA svarUpasaN^kIrtanenaiva kR^itatvAt, anarthakam avadhAraNaM bhavet -- svarUpam eva hi eShAm abAhyasAdhanatvam iti | abAhyasAdhanatve.api tu mAnasagrahavat kriyAnupraveshashaN^kAyAM tannivR^ittiphalam avadhAraNam arthavad bhaviShyati | tathA svapate jAgrate caivaMvide sarvadA sarvANi bhUtAnyetAn agnIMshcinvanti iti sAtatyadarshanam eShAM svAtantrye.avakalpate -- yathA sAmpAdike vAkprANamaye.agnihotre prANaM tadA vAci juhoti ... vAcaM tadA prANe juhoti iti ca uktvA ucyate -- ete anante amR^ite AhutI jAgracca svapaMshca satataM juhoti iti, tadvat | kriyAnupraveshe tu kriyAprayogasya alpakAlatvAt na sAtatyena eShAM prayogaH kalpeta | na ca idam arthavAdamAtram iti nyAyyam | yatra hi vispaShTo vidhAyako liN^AdiH upalabhyate, yuktaM tatra saN^kIrtanamAtrasyArthavAdatvam | iha tu vispaShTavidhyantarAnupalabdheH saN^kIrtanAd eva eShAM vij~nAnavidhAnaM kalpanIyam | tacca yathAsaN^kIrtanam eva kalpayituM shakyata iti, sAtatyadarshanAt tathAbhUtam eva kalpyate | tatashca sAmarthyAd eShAM svAtantryasiddhiH | etena tad yat kiM cemAni bhUtAni manasA saN^kalpayanti teShAm eva sA kR^itiH ityAdi vyAkhyAtam | tathA vAkyam api evaMvide iti puruShavisheShasambandham eva eShAm AcakShANaM na kratusambandhaM mR^iShyate | tasmAt svAtantryapakSha eva jyAyAn iti ||49||

|| 3.3.50 ||

anubandhAdibhyaH praj~nAntarapR^ithaktvavad dR^iShTAshca tad uktam || 

itashca prakaraNam upamR^idya svAtantryaM manashcidAdInAM pratipattavyam, yat kriyAvayavAn manaAdivyApAreShvanubadhnAti -- te manasaivAdhIyanta manasAcIyanta manasaiva grahA agR^ihyanta manasAstuvan manasAshaMsan yat kiM ca yaj~ne karma kriyeta yat kiM ca yaj~niyaM karma manasaiva teShu tan manomayeShu manashcitsu manomayam eva kriyate ityAdinA | sampatphalo hi ayam anubandhaH | na ca pratyakShAH kriyAvayavAH santaH sampadA lipsitavyAH | na ca atra udgIthAdyupAsanavat kriyAN^gasambandhAt tadanupraveshitvamAshaN^kitavyam, shrutivairUpyAt | na hi atra kriyAN^gaM kiMcid AdAya tasmin ado nAmAdhyavasitavyam iti vadati | ShaTtriMshatsahasrANi tu manovR^ittibhedAn AdAya teShvagnitvaM grahAdIMshca kalpayati, puruShayaj~nAdivat | saMkhyA ca iyaM puruShAyuShasyAhaHsudR^iShTA satI tatsambandhinIShu manovR^ittiShvaropyata iti draShTavyam | evam anubandhAt svAtantryaM manashcidAdInAm | AdishabdAt atideshAdyapi yathAsambhavaM yojayitavyam | tathA hi -- teShAm ekaika eva tAvAn yAvAn asau pUrvaH iti kriyAmayasyAgner mAhAtmyaM j~nAnamayAnAm ekaikasya atidishan kriyAyAm anAdaraM darshayati | na ca satyeva kriyAsambandhe vikalpaH pUrveNottareShAm iti shakyaM vaktum | na hi, yena vyApAreNa AhavanIyadhAraNAdinA pUrvaH kriyAyAm upakaroti, tena uttare upakartuM shaknuvanti | yat tu pUrvapakShe.apyatidesha upodbalaka ityuktam -- sati hi sAmAnye.atideshaH pravartata iti, tat asmatpakShe.apyagnitvasAmAnyenAtideshasambhavAt pratyuktam -- asti hi sAmpAdikAnAm apyagnInAm agnitvam iti | 

shrutyAdIni ca kAraNAni darshitAni | evam anubandhAdibhyaH kAraNebhyaH svAtantryaM manashcidAdInAm | praj~nAntarapR^ithaktvavat -- yathA praj~nAntarANi shANDilyavidyAprabhR^itIni svena svena anubandhena anubadhyamAnAni pR^ithag eva karmabhyaH praj~nAntarebhyashca svatantrANi bhavanti, evam iti | dR^iShTashca aveShTeH rAjasUyaprakaraNapaThitAyAH prakaraNAd utkarShaH -- varNatrayAnubandhAt | rAjayaj~natvAcca rAjasUyasya | tad uktaM prathame kANDe -- kratvarthAyAm iti cen na varNatrayasaMyogAt [jai.sU. 11.4.7] iti ||50||

|| 3.3.51 || 

na sAmAnyAd apyupalabdher mR^ityuvan na hi lokApattiH || 

yad uktaM mAnasavad iti, tat pratyucyate | na mAnasagrahasAmAnyAd api manashcidAdInAM kriyAsheShatvaM kalpyam, pUrvoktebhyaH shrutyAdihetubhyaH kevalapuruShArthatvopalabdheH | na hi kiMcit kasyacit kenacit sAmAnyaM na sambhavati | na ca tAvatA yathAsvaM vaiShamyaM nivartate | mR^ityuvat, yathA -- sa vA eSha eva mR^ityur ya eSha etasmin maNDale puruShaH iti, agnir vai mR^ityuH [bR^i.A.u. 3.2.10] iti ca agnyAdityapuruShayoH samAne.api mR^ityushabdaprayoge, na atyantasAmyApattiH | yathA ca -- asau vAva loko gautamAgniH tasyAditya eva samit [chA.u. 5.4.1] ityatra na samidAdisAmAnyAt lokasyAgnibhAvApattiH, tadvat ||51||

|| 3.3.52 ||

pareNa ca shabdasya tAdvidhyaM bhUyastvAt tu anubandhaH ||

parastAd api ayaM vAva loka eSho.agnishcitaH ityasmin anantare brAhmaNe, tAdvidhyaM kevalavidyAvidhitvam shabdasya prayojanaM lakShyate, na shuddhakarmAN^gavidhitvam | tatra hi -- 

vidyayA tad Arohanti yatra kAmAH parAgatAH | 
na tatra dakShiNA yanti nAvidvAMsaH tapasvaniH ||

ityanena shlokena kevalaM karma nindan vidyAM ca prashaMsan idaM gamayati | tathA purastAd api yad etan maNDalaM tapati ityasmin brAhmaNe vidyApradhAnatvam eva lakShyate -- so.amR^ito bhavati mR^ityur hyasyAtmA bhavati iti vidyAphalenaiva upasaMhArAt na karmapradhAnatA | tatsAmAnyAt ihApi tathAtvam | bhUyAMH tu agnyavayavAH sampAdayitavyA vidyAyAm -- ityetasmAt kAraNAt agninA anubadhyate vidyA, na karmAN^gatvAt | tasmAt manashcidAdInAM kevalavidyAtmakatvasiddhiH ||52||

  -- o)0(o -- 
30. aikAtmyAdhikaraNam  

|| 3.3.53 ||

eka AtmanaH sharIre bhAvAt || 

iha dehavyatiriktasya AtmanaH sadbhAvaH samarthyate, bandhamokShAdhikArasiddhaye | na hi asati dehavyatirikta Atmani paralokaphalAshcodanA upapadyeran | kasya vA brahmAtmatvam upadishyeta | 

nanu shAstrapramukha eva prathame pAde shAstraphalopabhogayogyasya dehavyatiriktasya Atmano.astitvam uktam -- satyam uktaM bhAShyakR^itA | na tu tatrAtmAstitve sUtram asti | iha tu svayam eva sUtrakR^itA tadastitvam AkShepapuraHsaraM pratiShThApitam | ita eva ca AkR^iShya AcAryeNa shabarasvAminA pramANalakShaNe varNitam | ata eva ca bhagavatA upavarSheNa prathame tantre AtmAstitvAbhidhAnaprasaktau shArIrake vakShyAma ityuddhAraH kR^itaH | iha ca idaM codanAlakShaNeShu upAsaneShu vicAryamANeShu AtmAstitvaM vicAryate, kR^itsnashAstrasheShatvapradarshanAya | api ca pUrvasminn adhikaraNe prakaraNotkarShAbhyupagamena manashcidAdInAM puruShArthatvaM varNitam | ko.asau puruShaH, yadarthA ete manashcidAdayaH ? ityasyAM prasaktau idaM dehavyatiriktasya Atmano.astitvam ucyate | tadastitvAkShepArtham idam AdimaM sUtram -- AkShepapUrvikA hi parihAroktiH vivakShite.arthe sthUNAnikhanananyAyena dR^iDhAM buddhim utpAdayed iti || 

atra eke dehamAtrAtmadarshino lokAyatikAH dehavyatiriktasya Atmano.abhAvaM manyamAnAH, samastavyasteShu bAhyeShu pR^ithivyAdiShvadR^iShTam api caitanyaM sharIrAkArapariNateShu bhUteShu syAd iti -- sambhAvayantaH tebhyashcaitanyam, madashaktivat vij~nAnam caitanyavishiShTaH kAyaH puruShaH -- iti ca AhuH | na svargagamanAya apavargagamanAya vA samartho dehavyatirikta AtmA asti, yatkR^itaM caitanyaM dehe syAt | deha eva tu cetanashca AtmA ca iti pratijAnate | 

hetuM cAcakShate -- sharIre bhAvAd iti yad dhi yasmin sati bhavati, asati ca na bhavati, tattaddharmatvenAdhyavasIyate -- yathA agnidharmAvauShNyaprakAshau | prANaceShTAcaitanyasmR^ityAdayashca AtmadharmatvenAbhimatA AtmavAdinAm -- te.api antar eva dehe upalabhyamAnAH bahishcAnupalabhyamAnAH asiddhe dehavyatirikte dharmiNi dehadharmA eva bhavitum arhanti | tasmAd avyatireko dehAd Atmana iti ||53||

|| 3.3.54 ||

evaM prApte, brUmaH -- 

vyatirekaH tadbhAvAbhAvitvAn na tUpalabdhivat || 

na tv etad asti -- yad uktam avyatireko dehAd Atmana iti | vyatireka eva asya dehAd bhavitum arhati | tadbhAvAbhAvitvAt | yadi dehabhAve bhAvAt dehadharmatvam AtmadharmANAM manyeta -- tato dehabhAve.api abhAvAt ataddharmatvam eva eShAM kiM na manyeta? dehadharmavailakShaNyAt | ye hi dehadharmA rUpAdayaH, te yAvaddehaM bhavanti | prANaceShTAdayaH tu satyapi dehe mR^itAvasthAyAM na bhavanti | dehadharmAshca rUpAdayaH parair apyupalabhyante, na tvAtmadharmAshcaitanyasmR^ityAdayaH | api ca sati hi tAvat dehe jIvadavasthAyAm eShAM bhAvaH shakyate nishcetum, na tu asatyabhAvaH | patite.api kadAcid asmin dehe dehAntarasaMcAreNa AtmadharmA anuvarteran | saMshayamAtreNApi parapakShaH pratiShidhyate | kimAtmakaM ca punaH idaM caitanyaM manyate, yasya bhUtebhya utpattim icchati -- iti paraH paryanuyoktavyaH, na hi bhUtacatuShTayavyatirekeNa lokAyatikaH kiMcit tattvaM pratyeti | yad anubhavanaM bhUtabhautikAnAm, tat caitanyam iti cet, tarhi viShayatvAt teShAm na taddharmatvam ashnuvIta, svAtmani kriyAvirodhAt | na hi agnir uShNaH san svAtmAnaM dahati, na hi naTAH shikShitaH san svaskandham adhirokShyati | na hi bhUtabhautikadharmeNa satA caitanyena bhUtabhautikAni viShayIkriyeran | na hi rUpAdibhiH svarUpaM pararUpaM vA viShayIkriyate | viShayIkriyante tu bAhyAdhyAtmikAni bhUtabhautikAni caitanyena | atashca yathaiva asyA bhUtabhautikaviShayAyA upalabdher bhAvo.abhyupagamyate, evaM vyatireko.api asyAstebhyo.abhyupagantavyaH | upalabdhisvarUpa eva ca na Atmeti Atmano dehavyatiriktatvam | nityatvaM ca upalabdheH, aikarUpyAt, aham idam adrAkSham iti ca avasthAntarayoge.apyupalabdhR^itvena pratyabhij~nAnAt, smR^ityAdyupapatteshca | yat tUktam -- sharIre bhAvAccharIradharma upalabdhiH iti, tad varNitena prakAreNa pratyuktam | api ca satsu pradIpAdiShu upakaraNeShu upalabdhir bhavati asatsu na bhavatIti -- na ca etAvatA pradIpAdidharma eva upalabdhir bhavati | evaM sati dehe upalabdhir bhavati, asati ca na bhavatIti -- na dehadharmo bhavitum arhati | upakaraNatvamAtreNApi pradIpAdivat dehopayogopapatteH | na cAtyantaM dehasya upalabdhAv upayogo.api dR^ishyate, nishceShTe.apyasmin dehe svapne nAnAvidhopalabdhidarshanAt | tasmAd anavadyaM dehavyatiriktasya Atmano.astitvam ||54||

  -- o)0(o -- 

31. aN^gAvabaddhAdhikaraNam

 || 3.3.55 ||

aN^gAvabaddhAH tu na shAkhAsu hi prativedam || 

samAptA prAsaN^gikI kathA | samprati prakR^itAm evAnuvartAmahe | om ityetadakSharamudgItham upAsIta lokeShu paJNcavidhaM sAmopAsIta ukthamuktham iti vai prajA vadanti tadidam evoktham iyam eva pR^ithivI ayaM vAva lokaH eSho.agnishcitaH ityevamAdyA ye udgIthAdikarmAN^gAvabaddhAH pratyayAH prativedaM shAkhAbhedeShu vihitAH, te tacchAkhAgateShv eva udgIthAdiShu bhaveyuH, athavA sarvashAkhAgateShu -- iti viShayaH | pratishAkhaM ca svarAdibhedAt udgIthAdibhedAnupAdAya ayam upanyAsaH | kiM tAvat prAptam? svashAkhAgateShv eva udgIthAdiShu vidhIyerann iti| kutaH? saMnidhAnAt -- udgItham upasIta iti hi sAmAnyavihitAnAM visheShAkAN^kShAyAM saMnikR^iShTenaiva svashAkhAgatena visheSheNa AkAN^kShAdinivR^itteH, tadatilaN^ghanena shAkhAntaravihitavisheShopAdAne kAraNaM nAsti | tasmAt pratishAkhaM vyavasthetyevaM prApte, bravIti -- aN^gAvabaddhAstviti | tushabdaH pakShaM vyAvartayati | naite prativedaM svashAkhAsveva vyavatiShTheran api tu sarvashAkhAsvanuvarteran | kutaH? udgIthAdishrutyavisheShAt | svashAkhAvyavasthAyAM hi udgItham upAsIta iti sAmAnyashrutir avisheShapravR^ittA satI saMnidhAnavashena visheShe vyavasthApyamAnA pIDitA syAt | na caitannyAyyam | saMnidhAnAddhi shrutir balIyasI | na ca sAmAnyAshrayaH pratyayo nopapadyate | tasmAt svarAdibhede satyapi udgIthatvAd yavisheShAt sarvashAkhAgateShv eva udgIthAdiShu evaMjAtIyakAH pratyayAH syuH ||55||

|| 3.3.56 ||

mantrAdivad vA.avirodhaH || 

athavA naivAtra virodhaH shaN^kitavyaH -- katham anyashAkhAgateShu udgIthAdiShu anyashAkhAvihitAH pratyayA bhaveyuH iti, mantrAdivat avirodhopapatteH | tathA hi -- mantrANAM karmaNAM guNAnAM ca shAkhAntarotpannAnAm api shAkhAntare upasaMgraho dR^ishyate | yeShAm api hi shAkhinAm kuTArurasi ityashmAdAnamantro nAmnAtaH, teShAm api asau viniyogo dR^ishyate -- kukkuTo.asItyashmAnamAdatte, kuTArurasIti vA iti | yeShAm api samidAdayaH prayAjA nAmnAtAH, teShAm api teShu guNavidhirAmnAyate -- R^itavo vai prayAjAH samAnatra hotavyAH iti | tathA yeShAm api ajo.agnIShomIyaH iti jAtivisheShopadesho nAsti, teShAm api tadviShayo mantravarNa upalabhyate -- chAgasya vapAyA medaso.anubrUhi iti | tathA vedAntarotpannAnAm api agnerverhotraM veradhvaram ityevamAdimantrANAM vedAntare parigraho dR^iShTAH | tathA bahvR^icapaThitasya sUktasya yo jAta eva prathamo manasvAn ityasya, adhvaryave sajanIyaM shasyam ityatra parigraho dR^iShTAH | tasmAt yathA AshrayANAM karmAN^gAnAM sarvatrAnuvR^ittiH, evam AshritAnAm api pratyayAnAm -- ityavirodhaH ||

bhUmajyAyastvAdhikaraNam

|| 3.3.57 ||

prAcInashAla aupamanyavaH [chA.u. 5.11.1] ityasyAm AkhyAyikAyAM vyastasya samastasya ca vaishvAnarasya upAsanaM shrUyate | vyastopAsanaM tAvat -- aupamanyava kaM tu amAtmAnam upAssa iti divam eva bhagavo rAjann iti hovAcaiSha vai sutejA AtmA vaishvAnaro yaM tu amAtmAnam upAsse [chA.u. 5.12.1] ityAdi | tathA samastopAsanam api -- tasya ha vA etasyAtmano vaishvAnarasya mUrdhaiva sutejAshcakShur vishvarUpaH prANaH pR^ithagvartmAtmA sandeho bahulo vastir eva rayiH pR^ithivyeva pAdau [chA.u. 5.18.2] ityAdi | tatra saMshayaH -- kim iha ubhayathApi upAsanaM syAt vyastasya samastasya ca, uta samastasyaiveti | kiM tAvat prAptam? pratyavayavaM sutejaH -- prabhR^itiShu upAsse iti kriyApadashravaNAt, tasmAt tava sutaM prasutam AsutaM kule dR^ishyate ityAdi phalabhedashravaNAcca, vyastAnyapyupAsanAni syuH iti prAptam | tato.abhidhIyate -- 

bhUmnaH kratuvajjyAyastvaM tathA hi darshayati ||

bhUmnaH padArthopacayAtmakasya samastasya vaishvAnaropAsanasya jyAyastvaM prAdhAnyena asmin vAkye vivakShitaM bhavitum arhati, na pratyekam avayavopAsanAnAm api | kratuvat -- yathA kratuShu darshapUrNamAsaprabhR^itiShu sAmastyena sAN^gapradhAnaprayoga eva eko vivakShyate, na vyastAnAm api prayogaH prayAjAdInAm, nApyekadeshAN^gayuktasya pradhAnasya, tadvat | kuta etat -- bhUmaiva jyAyAn iti? tathA hi shrutiH bhUmno jyAyastvaM darshayati, ekavAkyatAvagamAt | ekaM hi idaM vAkyaM vaishvAnaravidyAviShayaM paurvAparyAlocanAt pratIyate | tathA hi -- prAcInashAlaprabhR^itaya uddAlakAvasAnAH ShaT R^iShayaH vaishvAnaravidyAyAM pariniShThAm apratipadyamAnAH ashvapatiM kaikeyaM rAjAnam abhyAjagmuH ityupakramya, ekaikasya R^iSher upAsyaM dyuprabhR^itInAm ekaikaM shrAvayitvA, mUrdhA tv eSha Atmana [chA.u. 5.12.2] iti hovAca ityAdinA mUrdhAdibhAvaM teShAM vidadhAti | mUrdhA te vyapatiShyad yan mAM nAgamiShyaH [chA.u. 5.12.2] ityAdinA ca vyastopAsanam apavadati | punashca vyastopAsanaM vyAvartya, samastopAsanam evAnuvartya, sa sarveShu lokeShu sarveShu bhUteShu sarveShvatmasvannam atti [chA.u. 5.18.1] iti bhUmAshrayam eva phalaM darshayati | yat tu pratyekaM sutejaHprabhR^itiShu phalabhedashravaNam, tat evaM sati aN^gaphalAni pradhAna evAbhyuccinotIti draShTavyam | tathA upAsse ityapi pratyavayavam AkhyAtashravaNaM parAbhiprAyAnuvAdArtham, na vyastopAsanavidhAnArtham | tasmAt samastopAsanapakSha eva shreyAn iti ||

kecit tu atra samastopAsanapakShaM jyAyAMsaM pratiShThApya, jyAyastvavacanAd eva kila vyastopAsanapakSham api sUtrakAro.anumanyata iti kalpayanti | tad ayuktam, ekavAkyatAvagatau satyAM vAkyabhedakalpanasyAnyAyyatvAt, mUrdhA te vyapatiShyat iti ca evamAdinindAvirodhAt, spaShTe ca upasaMhArasthe samastopAsanAvagame tadabhAvasya pUrvapakShe vaktum ashakyatvAt, sautrasya ca jyAyastvavacanasya pramANavattvAbhiprAyeNApi upapadyamAnatvAt ||57||

  -- o)0(o -- 

33. shabdAdibhedAdhikaraNam

|| 3.3.58 ||

pUrvasminn adhikaraNe satyAm api sutejaHprabhR^itInAM phalabhedashrutau samastasyopAsanaM jyAya ityuktam | ataH prAptA buddhiH -- anyAnyapi bhinnashrutInyupAsanAni samasya upAsiShyante iti | api ca naiva vedyAbhede vidyAbhedo vij~nAtuM shakyate | vedyaM hi rUpaM vidyAyAH, dravyadaivatam iva yAgasya | vedyashca eka eva IshvaraH shrutinAnAtve.apyavagamyate --  manomayaH prANasharIraH [chA.u. 3.14.2], kaM brahma khaM brahma [chA.u. 4.10.5], satyakAmaH satyasaN^kalpaH [chA.u. 8 1.5] ityevamAdiShu -- tathA eka eva prANaH prANo vAva saMvargaH [chA.u. 4.3.3], prANo vAva jyeShThashca shreShThashca [chA.u. 5.1.1], prANo ha pitA prANo mAtA [chA.u. 7.15.1] ityevamAdiShu | vedyaikatvAcca vidyaikatvam | shrutinAnAtvam api asmin pakShe guNAntaraparatvAt na anarthakam | tasmAt svaparashAkhAvihitam ekavedyavyapAshrayaM guNajAtam upasaMhartavyaM vidyAkArtsnyAya ityevaM prApte, pratipAdyate --  

nAnA shabdAdibhedAt ||

vedyAbhede.api evaMjAtIyakA vidyA bhinnA bhavitum arhati | kutaH? shabdAdibhedAt | bhavati hi shabdabhedaH -- veda upAsIta sa kratuM kurvIta [chA.u. 3.14.1] ityevamAdiH | shabdabhedashca karmabhedahetuH samadhigataH purastAt shabdAntare karmabhedaH kR^itAnubandhatvAt iti | AdigrahaNAt guNAdayo.api yathAsambhavaM bhedahetavo yojayitavyAH | 

nanu veda ityAdiShu shabdabheda eva avagamyate, na yajati ityAdivat arthabhedaH, sarveShAm evaiShAM manovR^ittyarthatvAbhedAt, arthAntarAsambhavAcca | tat kathaM shabdabhedAd vidyAbhedaH ? iti | naiSha doShaH, manovR^ittyarthatvAbhede.api anubandhabhedAd vedyabhede sati vidyAbhedopapatteH | ekasyApIshvarasya upAsyasya pratiprakaraNaM vyAvR^ittA guNAH shiShyante | tathA ekasyApi prANasya tatra tatra upAsyasya abhede.apyanyAdR^igguNo.anyatropAsitavyo.anyAdR^igguNashcAnyatra -- ityevam anubandhabhedAd vidhibhede sati vidyAbhedo vij~nAyate | 

na cAtra eko vidyAvidhiH, itare guNavidhaya iti shakyaM vaktum -- vinigamanAyAM hetvabhAvAt, anekatvAcca pratiprakaraNaM guNAnAM prAptavidyAnuvAdena vidhAnAnupapatteH | na ca asmin pakShe samAnAH santaH satyakAmAdayo guNA asakR^icchravayitavyAH | pratiprakaraNaM ca -- idaM kAmenedam upAsitavyam, idaM kAmena cedam iti nairAkAN^kShyAvagamAt naikavAkyatApattiH | na ca atra vaishvAnaravidyAyAm iva samastacodanA aparA asti, yad balena pratiprakaraNavartInyavayavopAsanAni bhUtvA ekavAkyatAm iyuH | vedyaikatvanimitte ca vidyaikatve sarvatra niraN^kushe pratij~nAyamAne, samastaguNopasaMhAro.ashakyaH pratij~nAyeta | tasmAt suShThu ucyate -- nAnA shabdAdibhedAd iti | sthite ca etasminn adhikaraNe, sarvavedAntapratyayam ityAdi draShTavyam ||58||

  -- o)0(o -- 
34. vikalpAdhikaraNam

|| 3.3.59 || 

vikalpo.avishiShTAphalatvAt || 

sthite vidyAbhede vicAryate -- kim AsAm icchayA samuccayo vikalpo vA syAt, athavA vikalpa eva niyameneti | tatra sthitatvAt tAvadvidyAbhedasya na samuccayaniyame kiMcit kAraNam asti | 

nanu bhinnAnAm apyagnihotradarshapUrNamAsAdInAM samuccayaniyamo dR^ishyate -- naiSha doShaH | nityatAshrutir hi tatra kAraNam | naivaM vidyAnAM kAcin nityatAshrutir asti | tasmAn na samuccayaniyamaH | nApi vikalpaniyamaH, vidyAntarAdhikR^itasya vidyAntarApratiShedhAt | pArisheShyAt yAthAkAmyam Apadyate | 

nanu avishiShTaphalatvAd AsAM vikalpo nyAyyaH | tathA hi -- manomayaH prANasharIraH [chA.u. 3.14.2], kaM brahma khaM brahma [chA.u. 4.10.5], satyakAmaH satyasaN^kalpaH [chA.u. 8 1.5] ityevamAdyAH tulyavat IshvaratvaprAptiphalA lakShyante -- naiSha doShaH, samAnaphaleShvapi svargAdisAdhaneShu karmasu yAthAkAmyadarshanAt | tasmAt yAthAkAmyaprAptau, ucyate -- vikalpa eva AsAM bhavitum arhati, na samuccayaH | kasmAt? avishiShTaphalatvAt | avishiShTaM hyAsAM phalam upAsyaviShayasAkShAtkaraNam | ekena ca upAsanena sAkShAtkR^ite upAsye viShaye IshvarAdau, dvitIyam anarthakam | api ca asambhava eva, sAkShAtkaraNasya samuccayapakShe, cittavikShepahetutvAt | sAkShAtkaraNasAdhyaM ca vidyAphalaM darshayanti shrutayaH -- yasya syAdaddhA na vicikitsAsti [chA.u. 3.14.4] iti, devo bhUtvA devAn apyeti [bR^i.A.u. 4.1.2] iti ca evamAdyAH | smR^itayashca -- sadA tadbhAvabhAvitaH ityevamAdyAH | tasmAt avishiShTaphalAnAM vidyAnAm anyatamAm AdAya tatparaH syAt, yAvadupAsyaviShayasAkShAtkaraNena tat phalaM prAptam iti ||

kAmyAdhikaraNam

|| 3.3.60 ||

kAmyAstu yathAkAmaM samuccIyeran na vA pUrvahetvabhAvAt || 

avishiShTaphalatvAd ityasya pratyudAharaNam | yAsu punaH kAmyAsu vidyAsu, sa ya etam evaM vAyuM dishAM vatsaM veda na putrarodaM roditi [chA.u. 3.15.2], sa yo nAma brahmetyupAste yAvan nAmno gataM tatrAsya yathAkAmacAro bhavati [chA.u. 7.1.5] iti caivamAdyAsu kriyAvat adR^iShTenAtmanA AtmIyaM phalaM sAdhayantIShu, sAkShAtkaraNApekShA nAsti | tA yathAkAmaM samuccIyeran, na vA samuccIyeran -- pUrvahetvabhAvAt, pUrvasya avishiShTaphalatvAd ityasya vikalpahetor abhAvAt ||60||

  -- o)0(o -- 
yathAshrayabhAvAdhikaraNam

|| 3.3.61 ||

aN^geShu yathAshrayabhAvaH || 

karmAN^geShu udgIthAdiShu ye AshritAH pratyayA vedatrayavihitAH, kiM te samuccIyeran, kiM vA yathAkAmaM syuH iti saMshaye -- yathAshrayabhAva ityAha | yathaiva eShAm AshrayAH stotrAdayaH sambhUya bhavanti, evaM pratyayA api, AshrayatantratvAt pratyayAnAm ||61||


|| 3.3.62 ||

shiShTeshca || 

yathA vA AshrayAH stotrAdayaH triShu vedeShu shiShyante, evam AshritA api pratyayAH -- nopadeshakR^ito.api kashcid visheSho.aN^gAnAM tadAshrayANAM ca pratyayAnAm ityarthaH ||62||

|| 3.3.63 ||

samAhArAt || 

hotR^iShadanAd dhaivApi durudgItam anusamAharati [chA.u. 1.5.5] iti ca -- praNavodgIthaikatvavij~nAnamAhAtmyAt udgAtA svakarmaNyutpannaM kShataM hautrAt karmaNaH pratisamAdadhAti -- iti bruvan vedAntaroditasya pratyayasya vedAntaroditapadArthasambandhasAmAnyAt sarvavedoditapratyayopasaMhAraM sUcayati -- iti liN^gadarshanam ||63||

|| 3.3.64 || 

guNasAdhAraNyashruteshca ||
