vidyAguNaM ca vidyAshrayaM santam oMkAraM vedatrayasAdhAraNaM shrAvayati -- teneyaM trayI vidyA vartata om ityAshrAvayaty om iti shaMsaty om ityudgAyati [chA.u. 1.1.9] iti ca | tatashca AshrayasAdhAraNyAt AshritasAdhAraNyam iti -- liN^gadarshanam eva | athavA guNasAdhAraNyashruteshceti | yadIme karmaguNA udgIthAdayaH sarve sarvaprayogasAdhAraNA na syuH, na syAt tataH tadAshrayANAM pratyayAnAM sahabhAvaH | te tu udgIthAdayaH sarvAN^gagrAhiNA prayogavacanena sarve sarvaprayogasAdhAraNAH shrAvyante | tatashca AshrayasahabhAvAt pratyayasahabhAva iti ||64||

|| 3.3.65 || 

na vA tatsahabhAvAshruteH || 

na veti pakShavyAvartanam | na yathAshrayabhAva AshritAnAm upAsanAnAM bhavitum arhati | kutaH ? tatsahabhAvAshruteH | yathA hi trivedavihitAnAm aN^gAnAM stotrAdInAM sahabhAvaH shrUyate -- grahaM vA gR^ihItvA camasaM vonnIya stotram upAkaroti, stutam anushaMsati, prastotaH sAma gAya, hotar etad yaja ityAdinA | naivam upAsanAnAM sahabhAvashrutir asti | 

nanu prayogavacana eShAM sahabhAvaM prApayet -- neti brUmaH, puruShArthatvAd upAsanAnAm | prayogavacano hi kratvarthAnAm udgIthAdInAM sahabhAvaM prApayet | udgIthAdyupAsanAni tu kratvarthAshrayANyapi godohanAdivat puruShArthAnItyavocAma pR^ithagghyapratibandhaH phalam [bra.saba. 3.3.42] ityatra | ayam eva ca upadeshAshrayo visheSho.aN^gAnAM tadAlambanAnAM ca upAsanAnAm -- yadekeShAM kratvarthatvam, ekeShAM puruShArthatvam iti | paraM ca liN^gadvayam akAraNam upAsanasahabhAvasya, shrutinyAyAbhAvAt | na ca pratiprayogam AshrayakArtsnyopasaMhArAd AshritAnAm api tathAtvaM vij~nAtuM shakyam, atatprayuktatvAd upAsanAnAm -- AshrayatantrANyapi hi upAsanAni kAmam AshrayAbhAve mA bhUvan | na tvashrayasahabhAvena sahabhAvaniyamam arhanti, tatsahabhAvAshruter eva | tasmAt yathAkAmam eva upAsanAnyanuShThIyeran ||65||

|| 3.3.66 ||

darshanAcca || 

darshayati ca shrutir asahabhAvaM pratyayAnAm -- evaMvid dha vai brahmA yaj~naM yajamAnaM sarvAMshca rtvajo.abhirakShati [chA.u. 4.17.10] iti | sarvapratyayopasaMhAre hi, sarve sarvavida iti na vij~nAnavatA brahmaNA paripAlyatvam itareShAM saN^kIrtyeta | tasmAt yathAkAmam upAsanAnAM samuccayo vikalpo veti || 

iti shrImatparamahaMsaparivrAjakAcAryasya shrIgovindabhagavatpUjyapAdashiShyasya shrImacchaN^karabhagavataH kR^itau shArIrakamImAMsAsUtrabhAShye 
tR^itIyAdhyAyasya tR^itIyaH pAdaH ||

|| 3.3 ||

(3.4)

|| tR^itIyo.adhyAye caturthaH pAdaH || 

atra nirguNavidyAyA antaraN^gabahiraN^gasAdhanavicAraH ||

1. puruShArthAdhikaraNam

|| 3.4.1 ||

athedAnIm aupaniShadam Atmaj~nAnaM kim adhikAridvAreNa karmaNyevAnupravishatyAho svit svatantram eva puruShArthasAdhanaM bhavatIti mImAMsamAnaH siddhAntenaiva tad upakramate -- 

puruShArtho.ataH shabdAd iti bAdarAyaNaH ||

asmAd vedAntavihitAd Atmaj~nAnAt svatantrAt puruShArthaH sidhyatIti bAdarAyaNa AcAryo manyate | kuta etad avagamyate? shabdAd ityAha | tathA hi -- tarati shokam Atmavit [chA.u. 7.1.3], sa yo ha vai tat paramaM brahma veda brahmaiva bhavati [mu.u. 3.2.9], brahmavid Apnoti param [tai.u. 2.1], AcAryavAn puruSho veda [chA.u. 6.14.2], tasya tAvad eva ciraM yAvan na vimokShye.atha sampatsye [chA.u. 6.14.2], ya AtmApahatapApmA ityupakramya, sa sarvAMshca lokAn Apnoti sarvAMshca kAmAn yaH tam AtmAnam anuvidya vijAnAti [chA.u. 8.7.1] iti | AtmA vA are draShTavyaH ityupakramya, etAvad are khalvamR^itatvam iti evaMjAtIyakA shrutiH kevalAyA vidyAyAH puruShArthahetutvaM shrAvayati ||1|| 

|| 3.4.2 || 

athAtra pratyavatiShThate -- 

sheShatvAt puruShArthavAdo yathA.anyeShviti jaiminiH ||

kartR^itvena AtmanaH karmasheShatvAt, tadvij~nAnam api vrIhiprokShaNAdivat viShayadvAreNa karmasambandhyeva -- ityataH, tasmin avagataprayojane Atmaj~nAne yA phalashrutiH, sA arthavAdaH -- iti jaiminir AcAryo manyate | yathA anyeShu dravyasaMskArakarmasu yasya parNamayI juhUr bhavati na sa pApaM shlokaM sR^iNoti [kR^i.ya.ve. 3.3.5.7], yadAN^kte cakShur eva bhrAtR^ivyasya vR^iN^kte [kR^i.ya.ve. 6.6.1.1], yat prayAjAnUyAjA ijyante, varma vA etadyaj~nasya kriyate varma yajamAnAya bhrAtR^ivyAbhibhUtyai [kR^i.ya.ve. 2.2.6.1] ityevaMjAtIyakA phalashrutiH arthavAdaH, tadvat | kathaM punar asya anArabhyAdhItasya Atmaj~nAnasya prakaraNAdInAm anyatamenApi hetunA vinA kratupravesha AshaN^kyate? kartR^idvAreNa vAkyAt tadvij~nAnasya kratusambandha iti cet, na, vAkyAd viniyogAnupapatteH -- avyabhicAriNA hi kenacid dvAreNa anArabhyAdhItAnAm api vAkyanimittaH kratusambandho.avakalpate | kartA tu vyabhicAri dvAram, laukikavaidikakarmasAdhAraNyAt | tasmAn na taddvAreNa Atmaj~nAnasya kratusambandhasiddhiH iti -- na, vyatirekavij~nAnasya vaidikebhyaH karmabhyo.anyatra anupayogAt | na hi dehavyatiriktAtmaj~nAnaM laukikeShu karmasu upayujyate, sarvathA dR^iShTArthapravR^ittyupapatteH | vaidikeShu tu dehapAtottarakAlaphaleShu dehavyatiriktAtmaj~nAnam antareNa pravR^ittiH nopapadyata iti, upayujyate vyatirekavij~nAnam | 

nanu apahatapApmatvAdivisheShaNAt asaMsAryAtmaviShayam aupaniShadaM darshanaM na pravR^ittyaN^gaM syAt -- na,priyAdisaMsUcitasya saMsAriNa eva Atmano draShTavyatvopadeshAt | apahatapApmatvAdi visheShaNaM tu stutyarthaM bhaviShyati | 

nanu tatra tatra prasAdhitam etat -- adhikam asaMsAri brahma jagatkAraNam | tad eva ca saMsAriNa AtmanaH pAramArthikaM svarUpam upaniShatsu upadishyata iti -- satyaM prasAdhitam | tasyaiva tu sthUNAnikhananavat phaladvAreNa AkShepasamAdhAne kriyete dArDhyam ||

|| 3.4.3 || 

AcAradarshanAt ||

janako ha vaideho bahudakShiNena yaj~neneje [bR^i.A.u. 3.1.1], yakShyamANo vai bhagavanto.aham asmi ity [chA.u. 5.11.5] evamAdIni brahmavidAm api anyapareShu vAkyeShu karmasambandhadarshanAni bhavanti | tathA uddAlakAdInAm api putrAnushAsanAdidarshanAt gArhasthyasambandho.avagamyate | kevalAccet j~nAnAt puruShArthasiddhiH syAt, kim artham anekAyAsasamanvitAni karmANi te kuryuH? atke cen madhu vindeta kim arthaM parvataM vrajet iti nyAyAt ||3||

|| 3.4.4 || 

tacchruteH || 

yad eva vidyayA karoti shraddhayopaniShadA tad eva vIryavattaraM bhavati [chA.u. 1.1.10] iti ca karmasheShatvashravaNAt vidyAyA na kevalAyAH puruShArthahetutvam ||4||

|| 3.4.5 || 

samanvArambhaNAt ||

taM vidyAkarmaNI samanvArabhete [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.2] iti ca vidyAkarmaNoH phalArambhe sAhityadarshanAt na svAtantryaM vidyAyAH ||

|| 3.4.6 || 

tadvato vidhAnAt ||

AcAryakulAd vedam adhItya yathAvidhAnaM guroH karmAtisheSheNAbhisamAvR^itya kuTumbe shucau deshe svAdhyAyam adhIyAnaH [chA.u. 8.15.1] iti ca evaMjAtIyakA shrutiH samastavedArthavij~nAnavataH karmAdhikAraM darshayati | tasmAd api na vij~nAnasya svAtantryeNa phalahetutvam ||6|| 

|| 3.4.7 ||

nanu atra adhItya ityadhyayanamAtraM vedasya shrUyate, na arthavij~nAnam -- naiSha doShaH | dR^iShTArthatvAt vedAdhyayanam arthAvabodhaparyantam iti sthitam ||

niyamAcca ||

kurvann eveha karmANi jijIviShecchataM samAH | 
evaM tvayi nAnyatheto.asti na karma lipyate nare || [Isho. 2] iti |

tathA etad vai jarAmaryaM satraM yad agnihotraM jarayA vA hyevAsmAn mucyate mR^ityunA vA -- ityevaMjAtIyakAt niyamAd api karmasheShatvam eva vidyAyA iti ||7|| 

|| 3.4.8 || 

evaM prApte, pratividhatte -- 

adhikopadeshAt tu bAdarAyaNasyaivaM taddarshanAt ||

tushabdAt pakSho viparivartate | yad uktam sheShatvAt puruShArthavAdaH iti, tan nopapadyate | kasmAt? adhikopadeshAt | yadi saMsAryeva AtmA shArIraH kartA bhoktA ca sharIramAtravyatirekeNa vedAnteShu upadiShTaH syAt, tato varNitena prakAreNa phalashruter arthavAdatvaM syAt | adhikaH tAvat shArIrAd Atmano.asaMsArI IshvaraH kartR^itvAd isaMsAridharmarahito.apahatapApmatvAdivisheShaNaH paramAtmA vedyatvenopadishyate vedAnteShu | na ca tadvij~nAnaM karmaNAM pravartakaM bhavati, pratyuta karmANyucchinatti -- iti vakShyati upamardaM ca ityatra | tasmAt puruShArtho.ataH shabdAt iti yan mataM bhagavato bAdarAyaNasya, tat tathaiva tiShThati | na sheShatvaprabhR^itibhir hetvAbhAsaishcAlayituM shakyate | tathA hi tam adhikaM shArIrAt Ishvaram AtmAnaM darshayanti shrutayaH -- yaH sarvaj~naH sarvavit [mu.u. 1.1.9], bhIShAsmAd vAtaH pavate [tai.u. 2.8], mahad bhayaM vajram udyatam etasya vA akSharasya prashAsane gArgi [chA.u. 3.8.9], tad aikShata bahu syAM prajAyeyeti tat tejo.asR^ijata [chA.u. 6.2.3] ityevam AdyAH | yat tu priyAdisaMsUcitasya saMsAriNa eva Atmano vedyatayA anukarShaNam -- AtmanaH tu kAmAya sarvaM priyaM bhavati | AtmA vA are draShTavyaH yaH prANena prANiti sa ta AtmA sarvAntaraH ya eSho.akShiNi puruSho dR^ishyate ityupakramya etaM tv eva te bhUyo.anuvyAkhyAsyAmi iti caivam Adi -- tad api, asya mahato bhUtasya niHshvasitam etad yad R^igvedaH yo.ashanAyApipAse shokaM mohaM jarAM mR^ityum atyeti paraM jyotir upasampadya svena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyate sa uttamaH puruShaH ityevamAdibhir vAkyasheShaiH satyAm eva adhikopadidikShAyAm, atyantAbhedAbhiprAyam ityavirodhaH | pArameshvaram eva hi shArIrasya pAramArthikaM svarUpam | upAdhikR^itaM tu shArIratvam, tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7], nAnyad ato.asti draShTR^i ityAdi shrutibhyaH | sarvaM ca etat vistareNAsmAbhiH purastAt tatra tatra varNitam ||8||


|| 3.4.9 ||

tulyaM tu darshanam ||

yat tUktam -- AcAradarshanAt karmasheSho vidyeti | atra brUmaH -- tulyam AcAradarshanam akarmasheShatve.api vidyAyAH | tathA hi shrutir bhavati -- etad dha sma vai tadvidvAMsaH Ahur R^iShayaH kAvaSheyAH kimarthA vayam adhyeShyAmahe, kimarthA vayaM yakShyAmahe, etad dha sma vai tat pUrve vidvAMso.agnihotraM na juhavAJNcakrire [?], etaM vai tam AtmAnaM viditvA brAhmaNAH putraiShaNAyAshca vittaiShaNAyAshca lokaiShaNAyAshca vyutthAyAtha bhikShAcaryaM caranti [bR^i.A.u. 3.5.1] ityevaMjAtIyakA | yAj~navalkyAdInAm api brahmavidAm akarmaniShThatvaM dR^ishyate --  maitreyi ! etAvad are khalvamR^itatvam iti hoktvA yAj~navalkyo vijahAra [bR^i.A.u. 4.5.15] ityAdi shrutibhyaH | api ca yakShyamANo vai bhagavanto.aham asmi ityetat liN^gadarshanaM vaishvAnaravidyAviShayam | sambhavati ca sopAdhikAyAM brahmavidyAyAM karmasAhityadarshanam | na tu atrApi karmAN^gatvam asti, prakaraNAdyabhAvAt ||9|| 

|| 3.4.10 ||

yat punar uktam tacchruteH iti, atra brUmaH -- 

asArvatrikI ||

yad eva vidyayA karoti ityeShA shrutir na sarvavidyAviShayA, prakR^itavidyAbhisambandhAt | prakR^itA ca udgIthavidyA -- om ityetad akSharam udgItham upAsIta [chA.u. 1.4.1] ityatra ||10||

|| 3.4.11 ||

vibhAgaH shatavat ||

yad apyuktam -- taM vidyAkarmaNI samanvArabhete [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.2] ityetat samanvArambhavacanam asvAtantrye vidyAyA liN^gam iti, tat pratyucyate -- vibhAgo.atra draShTavyaH -- vidyA anyaM puruSham anvArabhate, karma anyam iti | shatavat -- yathA shatam AbhyAM dIyatAm ityukte vibhajya dIyate -- paJNcAshad ekasmai paJNcAshad aparasmai, tadvat | na ca idaM samanvArambhavacanaM mumukShuviShayam -- iti nu kAmayamAnaH [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.6] iti saMsAriviShayatvopasaMhArAt, athAkAmayamAnaH [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.6] iti ca mumukShoH pR^ithagupakramAt | tatra saMsAriviShaye vidyA vihitA pratiShiddhA ca parigR^ihyate, visheShAbhAvAt | karmApi vihitaM pratiShiddhaM ca, yathAprAptAnuvAditvAt | evaM sati avibhAgenApi idaM samanvArambhavacanam avakalpate ||11|| 

|| 3.4.12 ||

yaccaitat, tadvato vidhAnAt iti, ata uttaraM paThati --  

adhyayanamAtravataH ||

AcAryakulAd vedam adhItya [chA.u. 8.15.1] ityatra adhyayanamAtrasya shravaNAt adhyayanamAtrakShavata eva karmavidhiH ityadhyavasyAmaH | 

nanu evaM sati avidyatvAt anadhikAraH karmasu prasajyeta -- naiSha doShaH | na vayam adhyayanaprabhavaM karmAvabodhanam adhikArakAraNaM vArayAmaH | kiM tarhi aupaniShadam Atmaj~nAnam, svAtantryeNaiva prayojanavat pratIyamAnam, na karmAdhikArakAraNatAM pratipadyate -- ityetat pratipAdayAmaH | yathA ca na kratvantaraj~nAnaM kratvantarAdhikAreNa apekShyate, evam etad api draShTavyam iti ||12|| 

|| 3.4.13 || 

yad apyuktam -- niyamAcca iti, atrAbhidhIyate -- 

nAvisheShAt ||

kurvann eveha karmANi jijIviShet [Isho. 2] ityevamAdiShu niyamashravaNeShu na viduSha iti visheSho.asti, avisheSheNa niyamavidhAnAt ||13||

|| 3.4.14 ||

stutaye.anumatir vA ||

kurvann eveha karmANi [Isho. 2] ityatra aparo visheSha AkhyAyate | yadyapi atra prakaraNasAmarthyAt vidvAn eva kurvann iti sambadhyeta, tathApi vidyAstutaye karmAnuj~nAnam etad draShTavyam | na karma lipyate nare iti hi vakShyati | etad uktaM bhavati -- yAvajjIvaM karma kurvatyapi tvayi viduShi puruShe na karma lepAya bhavati, vidyAsAmarthyAd iti tad evaM vidyA stUyate ||14||

|| 3.4.15 || 

kAmakAreNa caike ||

api ca eke vidvAMsaH pratyakShIkR^itavidyAphalAH santaH, tadavaShTambhAt phalAntarasAdhaneShu prajAdiShu prayojanAbhAvaM parAmR^ishanti kAmakAreNa, iti shrutir bhavati vAjasaneyinAm -- etad dha sma vai tatpUrve vidvAMsaH prajAM na kAmayante kiM prajayA kariShyAmo yeShAM no.ayam AtmAyaM loka [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.22] iti | anubhavArUDham eva ca vidyAphalaM na kriyAphalavat kAlAntarabhAvi -- ityasakR^id avocAma | ato.api na vidyAyAH karmasheShatvaM, nApi tadviShayAyAH phalashruter ayathArthatvaM shakyam Ashrayitum ||15||

|| 3.4.16 || 

upamardaM ca ||

api ca karmAdhikArahetoH kriyAkArakaphalalakShaNasya samastasya prapaJNcasya avidyAkR^itasya vidyAsAmarthyAt svarUpopamardam Amananti -- yatra tu asya sarvam AtmaivAbhUt tat kena kaM pashyet tat kena kaM jighret [bR^i.A.u. 4.5.15] ityAdinA | vedAntoditAtmaj~nAnapUrvikAM tu karmAdhikArasiddhiM pratyAshAsAnasya karmAdhikArocchittir eva prasajyeta | tasmAd api svAtantryaM vidyAyAH ||16||

|| 3.4.17 || 

UrdhvaretaHsu ca shabde hi ||

UrdhvaretaHsu ca AshrameShu vidyA shrUyate | na ca tatra karmAN^gatvaM vidyAyA upapadyate, karmAbhAvAt | na hi agnihotrAdIni vaidikAni karmANi teShAM santi | syAd etat, Urdhvaretasa AshramA na shrUyante veda iti -- tad api nAsti | te.api hi vaidikeShu shabdeShvavagamyante -- trayo dharmaskandhAH [chA.u. 2.23.1], ye ceme.araNye shraddhA tapa ityupAsate [chA.u. 5.10.1], tapaHshraddhe ye hyupavasantyaraNye [mu.u. 1.2.11], etam eva pravrAjino lokam icchantaH pravrajanti [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.22], brahmacaryAd eva pravrajet [jA.u. 4] ityevamAdiShu | pratipannApratipannagArhasthyAnAm apAkR^itAn apAkR^itarNatrayANAM ca UrdhvaretastvaM shrutismR^itiprasiddham | tasmAd api svAtantryaM vidyAyAH ||17||

  -- o)0(o -- 
2. parAmarshAdhikaraNam

|| 3.4.18 ||

parAmarshaM jaiminir acodanA cApavadati hi ||

trayo dharmaskandhAH [chA.u. 2.23.1] ityAdayo ye shabdA UrdhvaretasAm AshramANAM sadbhAvAya udAhR^itAH, na te tatpratipAdanAya prabhavanti | yataH parAmarsham eShu shabdeShvashramAntarANAM jaiminir AcAryo manyate, na vidhim | kutaH? na hi atra liN^AdInAm anyatamashcodanAshabdo.asti | arthAntaraparatvaM ca eShu pratyekam upalabhyate | trayo dharmaskandhAH ityatra tAvat yaj~no.adhyayanaM dAnam iti prathamaH tapa eva dvitIyo brahmacAryAcAryakulavAsI tR^itIyo.atyantam AtmAnam AcAryakule.avasAdayan sarva ete puNyalokA bhavanti iti parAmarshapUrvakamAshramANAm anAtyantikaphalatvaM saN^kIrtya, AtyantikaphalatayA brahmasaMsthatA stUyate -- brahmasaMstho.amR^itatvam eti [chA.u. 2.23.1] iti | 

nanu parAmarshe.api AshramA gamyanta eva -- satyaM gamyante | smR^ityAcArAbhyAM tu teShAM prasiddhiH, na pratyakShashruteH | atashca pratyakShashrutivirodhe sati anAdaraNIyAH te bhaviShyanti, anadhikR^itaviShayA vA | 

nanu gArhasthyam api sahaivordhvaretobhiH parAmR^iShTAm -- yaj~no.adhyayanaM dAnam iti prathamaH iti -- satyam evam | tathApi tu gR^ihasthaM pratyeva agnihotrAdInAM karmaNAM vidhAnAt shrutiprasiddham eva hi tad astitvam | tasmAt stutyartha evAyaM parAmarshaH, na codanArthaH | 

api ca, apavadati hi pratyakShA shrutir AshramAntaram -- vIrahA vA eSha devAnAM yo.agnim udvAsayate AcAryAya priyaM dhanam AhR^itya prajAtantuM mA vyavacchetsIH [tai. 1.11.1], nAputrasya loko.astIti tat sarve pashavo viduH ityevamAdyA | tathA ye ceme.araNye shraddhA tapa ityupAsate [chA.u. 5.10.1], tapaHshraddhe ye hyupavasantyaraNye [mu.u. 1.2.11] iti ca devayAnopadeshaH, na AshramAntaropadeshaH | sandigdhaM ca AshramAntarAbhidhAnam -- tapa eva dvitIyaH [chA.u. 2.23.1] ityevamAdiShu | tathA etam eva pravrAjino lokam icchantaH pravrajanti [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.22] iti lokasaMstavo.ayam, na pArivrAjyavidhiH | 

nanu brahmacaryAd eva pravrajet iti vispaShTam idaM pratyakShaM pArivrAjyavidhAnaM jAbAlAnAm -- satyam evam etat | anapekShya tu etAM shrutim ayaM vicAra iti draShTavyam ||18||

|| 3.4.19 ||

anuShTheyaM bAdarAyaNaH sAmyashruteH ||

anuShTheyam AshramAntaraM bAdarAyaNa AcAryo manyate -- vede.ashravaNAd agnihotrAdInAM ca avashyAnuShTheyatvAt tadvirodhAd anadhikR^itAnuShTheyam AshramAntaram -- iti hi imAM matiM nirAkaroti, gArhasthyavad eva AshramAntaram api anicchatA pratipattavyam iti manyamAnaH | kutaH? sAmyashruteH | samA hi gArhasthyenAshramAntarasya parAmarshashrutir dR^ishyate -- trayo dharmaskandhAH [chA.u. 2.23.1] ityAdyA | yathA iha shrutyantaravihitam eva gArhasthyaM parAmR^iShTAm, evam AshramAntaram apIti pratipattavyam -- yathA ca shAstrAntaraprAptayor eva nivItaprAcInAvItayoH parAmarsha upavItavidhipare vAkye | tasmAt tulyam anuShTheyatvaM gArhasthyena AshramAntarasya | tathA etam eva pravrAjino lokam icchantaH pravrajanti [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.22] ityasya vedAnuvacanAdibhiH samabhivyAhAraH | ye ceme.araNye shraddhA tapa ityupAsate [chA.u. 5.10.1] ityasya ca paJNcAgnividyayA | yat tUktam -- tapa eva dvitIyaH [chA.u. 2.23.1] ityAdiShvashramAntarAbhidhAnaM sandigdham iti | naiSha doShaH, nishcayakAraNasadbhAvAt | trayo dharmaskandhAH [chA.u. 2.23.1] iti hi dharmaskandhatritvaM pratij~nAtam | na ca yaj~nAdayo bhUyAMso dharmA utpattibhinnAH santo.anyatrAshramasambandhAt tritve.antarbhAvayituM shakyante | tatra yaj~nAdiliN^go gR^ihAshrama eko dharmaskandho nirdiShTaH, brahmacArIti ca spaShTa AshramanirdeshaH, tapa ityapi ko.anyaH tapaHpradhAnAd AshramAt dharmaskandho.abhyupagamyeta | ye ceme.araNye [chA.u. 5.10.1] iti ca araNyaliN^gAt shraddhAtapobhyAm AshramagR^ihItiH | tasmAt parAmarshe.apyanuShTheyam AshramAntaram ||19||

|| 3.4.20 || 

vidhir vA dhAraNavat ||

vidhir vA ayam AshramAntarasya, na parAmarshamAtram | 

nanu vidhitvAbhyupagame ekavAkyatApratItir uparudhyeta | pratIyate cAtraikavAkyatA -- puNyalokaphalAH trayo dharmaskandhAH, brahmasaMsthatA tu amR^itatvaphaleti -- satyam etat | satIm api tu ekavAkyatApratItiM parityajya vidhir evAbhyupagantavyaH, apUrvatvAt, vidhyantarasyAdarshanAt, vispaShTAccAshramAntarapratyayAt guNavAdakalpanayA ekavAkyatvayojanAnupapatteH | dhAraNavat -- yathA adhastAt samidhaM dhArayann anudraved upari hi devebhyo dhArayati ityatra satyAm apyadhodhAraNena ekavAkyatApratItau, vidhIyata eva uparidhAraNam, apUrvatvAt | tathA ca uktaM sheShalakShaNe vidhiH tu dhAraNe.apUrvatvAt iti | tadvat ihApi AshramaparAmarshashrutiH vidhir eveti kalpyate | 

yadApi parAmarsha evAyam AshramAntarANAm, tadApi brahmasaMsthatA tAvat, saMstavasAmarthyAd avashyaM vidheyA abhyupagantavyA | sA ca kiM caturShvashrameShu yasya kasyacit, Aho svit parivrAjakasyaiveti vivektavyam | yadi ca brahmacaryAnteShvashrameShu parAmR^ishyamAneShu parivrAjako.api parAmR^iShTaH, tatashcaturNAm apyAshramANAM parAmR^iShTatvAvisheShAt anAshramitvAnupapatteshca yaH kashciccaturShvashrameShu brahmasaMstho bhaviShyati | 

atha na parAmR^iShTaH, tataH parishiShyamANaH parivrAD eva brahmasaMstha iti setsyati | tatra tapaHshabdena vaikhAnasagrAhiNA parAmR^iShTAH parivrAD api iti kecit | tad ayuktam | na hi satyAM gatau vAnaprasthavisheShaNena parivrAjako grahaNam arhati | yathAtra brahmacArigR^ihamedhinau asAdhAraNenaiva svena svena visheShaNena visheShitau, evaM bhikShuvaikhAnasAvapIti yuktam | tapashca asAdhAraNo dharmo vAnaprasthAnAM kAyakleshapradhAnatvAt, tapaHshabdasya tatra rUDheH | bhikShoH tu dharma indriyasaMyamAdir lakShaNayaiva tapaHshabdenAbhilapyeta | catuShTvena ca prasiddhA AshramAH tritvena parAmR^ishyanta ityanyAyyam | 

api ca bhedavyapadesho.atra bhavati -- traya ete puNyalokabhAjaH, eko.amR^itatvabhAg iti | pR^ithaktve ca bhedavyapadesho.avakalpate | na hyevaM bhavati -- devadattayaj~nadattau mandapraj~nau, anyataraH tu anayor mahApraj~na iti | bhavati tv evam -- devadattayaj~nadattau mandapraj~nau, viShNumitraH tu mahApraj~na iti | tasmAt pUrve traya AshramiNaH puNyalokabhAjaH, parishiShyamANaH parivrAD amR^itatvabhAk | kathaM punaH brahmasaMsthashabdo yogAt pravartamAnaH sarvatra sambhavan parivrAjaka evAvatiShTheta ? rUDhyabhyupagame ca AshramamAtrAd amR^itatvaprApter j~nAnAnarthakyaprasaN^ga iti | 

atrocyate -- brahmasaMstha iti hi brahmaNi parisamAptiH ananyavyApAratArUpaM tanniShThatvam abhidhIyate | tacca trayANAm AshramANAM na sambhavati, svAshramavihitakarmAnanuShThAne pratyavAyashravaNAt | parivrAjakasya tu sarvakarmasaMnyAsAt pratyavAyo na sambhavati ananuShThAnanimittaH | shamadamAdiH tu tadIyo dharmo brahmasaMsthAyA upodbalakaH, na virodhI | brahmaniShThatvam eva hi tasya shamadamAdyupabR^iMhitaM svAshramavihitaM karma | yaj~nAdIni ca itareShAm | tadvyatikrame ca tasya pratyavAyaH | 

tathA ca nyAsa iti brahmA brahmA hi paraH paro hi brahmA | 
tAni vA etAnyavarANi tapAMsi nyAsa evAtyarecayat || [nA.u. 78], 

vedAntavij~nAnasunishcitArthAH saMnyAsayogAd yatayaH shuddhasattvAH [mu.u. 3.2.6. nA.u. 1.2.3. kaivalya. 3] ityAdyAH shrutayaHn|  smR^itayashca -- tadbuddhayaH tadAtmAnaH tanniShThAH tatparAyaNAH [gItA 5.17] ityAdyAH | brahmasaMsthasya karmAbhAvaM darshayanti | tasmAt parivrAjakasya AshramamAtrAd amR^itatvaprApter j~nAnAnarthakyaprasaN^ga ityeSho.api doSho nAvatarati | tad evaM parAmarshe.api itareShAm AshramANAm, pArivrAjyaM tAvad brahmasaMsthatAlakShaNaM labhyetaiva | anapekShyaiva jAbAlashrutim AshramAntaravidhAyinIm ayam AcAryeNa vicAraH pravartitaH | vidyata eva tu AshramAntaravidhishrutiH pratyakShA -- 

brahmacaryaM samApya gR^ihI bhaved gR^ihI bhUtvA vanI bhaved vanI bhUtvA pravrajet | yadi vetarathA brahmacaryAd eva pravrajed gR^ihAd vA vanAd vA || [jA.u. 4] iti | 

na ceyaM shrutiH anadhikR^itaviShayA shakyA vaktum, avisheShashravaNAt, pR^ithagvidhAnAcca anadhikR^itAnAm -- atha punar eva vratI vAvratI vA snAtako vAsnAtako votsannAgnir anagniko vA [jA.u. 4] ityAdinA | brahmaj~nAnaparipAkAN^gatvAcca pArivrAjyasya na anadhikR^itaviShayatvam, tacca darshayati -- atha parivrAD vivarNavAsA muNDo.aparigrahaH shucir adrohI bhaikShANo brahmabhUyAya bhavati [jA.u. 5] iti | tasmAt siddhA UrdhvaretasAm AshramAH | siddhaM ca UrdhvaretaHsu vidhAnAd vidyAyAH svAtantryam iti ||20||

  -- o)0(o -- 
3. stutimAtrAdhikaraNam

|| 3.4.21 ||

stutimAtram upAdAnAd iti cen nApUrvatvAt ||

sa eSha rasAnAM rasatamaH paramaH parAdrhyo.aShTAmo yad udgIthaH [chA.u. 1.1.3], iyam eva rgagniH sAma [chA.u. 1.6.1], ayaM vAva lokaH, eSho.agnishcitaH, tad idam evoktham, iyam eva pR^ithivI [?] ityevaMjAtIyakAH shrutayaH kim udgIthAdeH stutyarthAH, Aho svit upAsanAvidh arthA ityasmin saMshaye -- stutyarthA iti yuktam, udgIthAdIni karmAN^gAnyupAdAya shravaNAt | yathA iyam eva juhUr AdityaH kUrmaH svargo loka AhavanIyaH ityAdyA juhvAdistutyarthAH, tadvat -- iti cet, netyAha | na hi stutimAtram AsAM shrutInAM prayojanaM yuktam, apUrvatvAt | vidhyarthatAyAM hi apUrvo.artho vihito bhavati | stutyarthatAyAM tvanarthakyam eva syAt | vidhAyakasya hi shabdasya vAkyasheShabhAvaM pratipadyamAnA stutir upayujyata ityuktam vidhinA tv ekavAkyatvAt stutyarthena vidhInAM syuH ityatra | pradeshAntaravihitAnAM tu udgIthAdInAm iyaM pradeshAntarapaThitA stutiH vAkyasheShabhAvam apratipadyamAnA anarthikaiva syAt | iyam eva juhUH ityAdi tu vidhisaMnidhAv evAmnAtam iti vaiShamyam | tasmAt vidh arthA eva evaMjAtIyakAH shrutayaH ||21||

|| 3.4.22 ||

bhAvashabdAcca || 

udgItham upAsIta [chA.u. 1.1.1], sAmopAsIta [chA.u. 2.2.1], aham uktham asmIti vidyAt ityAdayashca vispaShTA vidhishabdAH shrUyante | te ca stutimAtraprayojanatAyAM vyAhanyeran | tathA ca nyAyavidAM smaraNam -- 

kuryAt kriyeta kartavyaM bhavet syAd iti paJNcamam | 
etat syAt sarvavedeShu niyataM vidhilakShaNam || iti | 

liN^Adyartho vidhiH iti manyamAnAsta evaM smaranti | pratiprakaraNaM ca phalAni shrAvyante -- ApayitA ha vai kAmAnAM bhavati [chA.u. 1.1.7], eSha hyeva kAmAgAnasyeShTe [chA.u. 1.1.7], kalpante hAsmai lokA UrdhvAshcAvR^ittAshca [chA.u. 2.2.3] ityAdIni | tasmAd apyupAsanavidhAnArthA udgIthAdishrutayaH ||22||

4. pAriplavAdhikaraNam

|| 3.4.23 ||

pAriplavArthA iti cen, na, visheShitatvAt || 

atha ha yAj~navalkyasya dve bhArye babhUvatur maitreyI ca kAtyAyanI ca [bR^i.A.u. 4.5.1], pratardano ha vai daivodAsiH indrasya priyaM dhAmopajagAma [kau.u. 3.1], jAnashrutir ha  pautrAyaNaH shraddhAdeyo bahudAyI bahupAkya Asa [chA.u. 4.1.1] ityevamAdiShu vedAntapaThiteShvakhyAneShu saMshayaH -- kim imAni pAriplavaprayogArthAni, Aho svit saMnihitavidyApratipattyarthAnIti | pAriplavArthA imA AkhyAnashrutayaH, AkhyAnasAmAnyAt, AkhyAnaprayogasya ca pAriplave coditatvAt | tatashca vidyApradhAnatvaM vedAntAnAM na syAt, mantravat prayogasheShatvAd iti cet -- tan na | kasmAt? visheShitatvAt, pAriplavam AcakShIta iti hi prakR^itya, manur vaivasvato rAjA ityevamAdIni kAnicid eva AkhyAnAni tatra visheShyante | AkhyAnasAmAnyAccet sarvagR^ihItiH syAt, anarthakam evedaM visheShaNaM bhavet | tasmAt na pAriplavArthA etA AkhyAnashrutayaH ||23||

|| 3.4.24 ||

tathA caikavAkyatopabandhAt ||

asati ca pAriplavArthatve AkhyAnAnAM saMnihitavidyApratipAdanopayogitaiva nyAyyA, ekavAkyatopabandhAt | tathA hi tatra tatra saMnihitAbhir vidyAbhir ekavAkyatA dR^ishyate prarocanopayogAt pratipattiH aukaryopayogAcca -- maitreyIbrAhmaNe tAvat -- AtmA vA are draShTavyaH [bR^i.A.u. 4.5.6] ityAdyayA vidyayA ekavAkyatA dR^ishyate | prAtardane.api prANo.asmi praj~nAtmA ityAdyayA | jAnashrutiH ityatrApi vAyur vAva saMvargaH [chA.u. 4.3.1] ityAdyayA, yathA sa Atmano vapAm udakhidat ityevamAdInAM karmashrutigatAnAm AkhyAnAnAM saMnihitavidhistutyarthatA, tadvat | tasmAn na pAriplavArthatvam ||24||

  -- o)0(o -- 
5. agnIndhanAdyadhikaraNam

|| 3.4.25 ||

ata eva cAgnIndhanAdyanapekShA ||

puruShArtho.ataH shabdAt ityetat vyavahitam api sambhavAt ataH iti parAmR^ishyate | ata eva ca vidyAyAH puruShArthahetutvAt agnIndhanAdInyAshramakarmANi vidyayA svArthasiddhau nApekShitavyAnIti AdyasyaivAdhikaraNasya phalam upasaMharatyadhikavivakShayA ||25||

  -- o)0(o -- 

6. sarvApekShAdhikaraNam

|| 3.4.26 ||

sarvApekShA ca yaj~nAdishruter ashvavat ||

idam idAnIM cintyate -- kiM vidyAyA atyantam evAnapekShA AshramakarmaNAm, uta asti kAcid apekSheti | tatra ata evAgnIndhanAdInyAshramakarmANi vidyayA svArthasiddhau nApekShyante | evam atyantam evAnapekShAyAM prAptAyAm, idam ucyate -- sarvApekShA ceti | apekShate ca vidyA sarvANyAshramakarmANi, nAtyantam anapekShaiva | 

nanu viruddham idaM vacanam -- apekShate ca AshramakarmANi vidyA, nApekShate ceti | neti brUmaH | utpannA hi vidyA phalasiddhiM prati na kiMcid anyad apekShate, utpattiM prati tu apekShate | kutaH? yaj~nAdishruteH | tathA hi shrutiH -- tam etaM vedAnuvacanena brAhmaNA vividiShanti yaj~nena dAnena tapasAnAshakena [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.22] iti, yaj~nAdInAM vidyAsAdhanabhAvaM darshayati | vividiShAsaMyogAccaiShAm utpattiH AdhanabhAvo.avasIyate | atha yad yaj~na ityAcakShate brahmacaryam eva tat ityatra ca vidyAsAdhanabhUtasya brahmacaryasya yaj~nAdibhiH saMstavAt yaj~nAdInAm api hi sAdhanabhAvaH sUcyate | 

sarve vedA yat padam Amananti 
tapAMsi sarvANi ca yad vadanti | 
yad icchanto brahmacaryaM caranti 
tat te padaM saMgraheNa bravImi || [ka.u. 1.2.15]

ityevamAdyA ca shrutiH AshramakarmaNAM vidyAsAdhanabhAvaM sUcayati | smR^itir api -- 

kaShAyapaktiH karmANi j~nAnaM tu paramA gatiH | 
kaShAye karmabhiH pakve tato j~nAnaM pravartate || ityevamAdyA | 

ashvavad iti yogyatAnidarshanam -- yathA ca yogyatAvashena ashvo na lAN^galAkarShaNe yujyate, rathacaryAyAM tu yujyate, evam AshramakarmANi vidyayA phalasiddhau nApekShyante, utpattau ca apekShyanta iti ||26||

|| 3.4.27 ||

shamadamAdyupetaH syAt tathApi tu tadvidheH tadaN^gatayA teShAm avashyAnuShTheyatvAt || 

yadi kashcin manyeta -- yaj~nAdInAM vidyAsAdhanabhAvo na nyAyyaH, vidhyabhAvAt | yaj~nena vividiShanti ityevaMjAtIyakA hi shrutiH anuvAdasvarUpA vidyAbhiShTAvaparA, na yaj~nAdividhiparA -- itthaM mahAbhAgA vidyA, yat yaj~nAdibhir etAm avAptum icchantIti -- tathApi tu shamadamAdyupetaH syAt vidyArthI, tasmAd evaMvicchAnto dAnta uparataH titikShuH samAhito bhUtvAtmanyevAtmAnaM pashyati [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.23] iti vidyAsAdhanatvena shamadamAdInAM vidhAnAt vihitAnAM ca avashyAnuShTheyatvAt | 

nanu atrApi shamAdyupeto bhUtvA pashyatIti vartamAnApadesha upalabhyate, na vidhiH -- neti brUmaH, tasmAt iti prakR^itaprashaMsAparigrahAd vidhitvapratIteH | pashyet iti ca mAdhyaMdinA vispaShTam eva vidhim adhIyate | tasmAt yaj~nAdyanapekShAyAm api shamAdInyapekShitavyAni | yaj~nAdInyapi tu apekShitavyAni, yaj~nAdishruter eva | 

nanu uktam -- yaj~nAdibhir vividiShantItyatra na vidhir upalabhyata iti -- satyam uktam | tathApi tu apUrvatvAt saMyogasya vidhiH parikalpyate | na hi ayaM yaj~nAdInAM vividiShAsaMyogaH pUrvaM prAptaH, yenAnUdyeta | tasmAt pUShA prapiShTAbhAgo.adantako hi ityevamAdiShu ca ashrutavidhikeShvapi vAkyeShu apUrvatvAd vidhiM parikalpya, pauShNaM peShaNaM vikR^itau pratIyeta -- ityAdivicAraH prathame tantre pravartitaH | tathA ca uktam vidhir vA dhAraNavat [ve.sU. 3.4.20] iti | smR^itiShvapi bhagavadgItAdyAsu anabhisandhAya phalam anuShThitAni yaj~nAdIni mumukShor j~nAnasAdhanAni bhavantIti prapaJNcitam | tasmAd yaj~nAdIni shamadamAdIni ca yathAshramaM sarvANyeva AshramakarmANi vidyotpattAvapekShitavyAni | tatrApi evaMvit iti vidyAsaMyogAt pratyAsannAni vidyAsAdhanAni shamAdIni, vividiShAsaMyogAt tu bAhyatarANi yaj~nAdInIti vivektavyam ||27||

  -- o)0(o -- 
7. sarvAnnAnumatyadhikaraNam

|| 3.4.28 ||

prANasaMvAde shrUyate chandogAnAm -- na ha vA evaMvidi kiMcanAnannaM bhavati [chA.u. 5.2.1] iti | tathA vAjasaneyinAm -- na ha vA asyAnannaM jagdhaM bhavati nAnannaM pratigR^ihItam [bR^i.A.u. 6.1.14] iti | sarvam asyAdanIyam eva bhavatItyarthaH | kimidaM sarvAnnAnuj~nAnaM shamAdivat vidyAN^gaM vidhIyate, uta stutyarthaM saN^kIrtyata iti saMshaye -- vidhiH iti tAvat prAptam | tathA hi pravR^ittivisheShakara upadesho bhavati | ataH prANavidyAsaMnidhAnAt tadaN^gatvena iyaM niyamanivR^ittir upadishyate | 

nanu evaM sati bhakShyAbhakShyavibhAgashAstravyAghAtaH syAt -- naiSha doShaH, sAmAnyavisheShabhAvAt bAdhopapatteH | yathA prANihiMsApratiShedhasya pashusaMj~napanavidhinA bAdhaH, yathA ca na kAMcana pariharet tad vratam [chA.u. 2.13.2] ityanena vAmadevyavidyAviShayeNa sarvastryaparihAravacanena sAmAnyaviShayaM gamyAgamyavibhAgashAstraM bAdhyate -- evam anenApi prANavidyAviShayeNa sarvAnnabhakShaNavacanena bhakShyAbhakShyavibhAgashAstraM bAdhyeta, ityevaM prApte, brUmaH -- 

sarvAnnAnumatishca prANAtyaye taddarshanAt ||

nedaM sarvAnnAnuj~nAnaM vidhIyata iti | na hi atra vidhAyakaH shabda upalabhyate, na ha vA evaMvidi kiMcanAnannaM bhavati [chA.u. 5.2.1] iti vartamAnApadeshAt | na ca asatyAm api vidhipratItau pravR^ittivisheShakaratvalobhenaiva vidhir abhyupagantuM shakyate | api ca shvAdimaryAdaM prANasyAnnam ityuktvA, idam ucyate -- naivaMvidaH kiMcid anannaM bhavatIti | na ca shvAdimaryAdam annaM mAnuSheNa dehenopabhoktuM shakyate | shakyate tu prANasyAnnam idaM sarvam iti vicintayitum | tasmAt prANAnnavij~nAnaprashaMsArtho.ayam arthavAdaH, na sarvAnnAnuj~nAnavidhiH | 

tad darshayati -- sarvAnnAnumatishca prANAtyaye iti | etad uktaM bhavati -- prANAtyaya eva hi parasyAm Apadi sarvam annam adanIyatvenAbhyanuj~nAyate, taddarshanAt | tathA hi shrutiH  cAkrAyaNasya R^iSheH kaShTAyAm avasthAyAm abhakShyabhakShaNe pravR^ittiM darshayati -- maTAcIhateShu kuruShu [chA.u. 1.10.1] ityasmin brAhmaNe -- cAkrAyaNaH kila R^iShiH Apadgata ibhyena sAmikhAditAn kulmAShAMshcakhAda | anupAnaM tu tadIyam ucchiShTAdoShAt pratyAcacakShe | kAraNaM cAtrovAca na vA ajIviShyam imAn akhAdan [chA.u. 1.10.4] iti, kAmo ma udapAnam [chA.u. 1.10.4] iti ca | punashca uttaredyuH tAn eva svaparocchiShTAn paryuShitAn kulmAShAn bhakShayAm babhUva -- iti | tad etad ucchiShTocchiShTaparyuShitabhakShaNaM darshayantyAH shruteH AshayAtishayo lakShyate -- prANAtyayaprasaN^ge prANasandhAraNAya abhakShyam api bhakShayitavyam iti | svasthAvasthAyAM tu tan na kartavyaM vidyAvatApi -- ityanupAnapratyAkhyAnAd gamyate | tasmAt arthavAdaH na ha vA evaMvidi [chA.u. 5.2.1] ityevamAdiH ||28||

|| 3.4.29 || 

abAdhAcca ||

evaM ca sati AhArashuddhau sattvashuddhiH [chA.u. 7.26.2] ityevamAdi bhakShyAbhakShyavibhAgashAstram abAdhitaM bhaviShyati ||29||

|| 3.4.30 || 

api ca smaryate ||

api ca Apadi sarvAnnabhakShaNam api smaryate viduSho.aviduShashca avisheSheNa -- 

jIvitAtyayam Apanno yo.annam atti yataH tataH | 
lipyate na sa pApena padmapatram ivAmbhasA || [manu 10.204] iti | 

tathA madyaM nityaM brAhmaNaH surApasya brAhmaNasyoShNAm AsiJNceyuH, surApAH kR^imayo bhavantyabhakShyabhakShaNAt iti ca -- smaryate varjanam anannasya ||30||

|| 3.4.31 || 

shabdashcAto.akAmakAre ||  

shabdashca anannasya pratiShedhakaH kAmakAranivR^ittiprayojanaH kaTahAnAM saMhitAyAM shrUyate -- tasmAd brAhmaNaH surAM na pibet iti | so.api na ha vA evaMvidi [chA.u. 5.2.1] ityasyArthavAdatvAt upapannataro bhavati | tasmAd evaMjAtIyakA arthavAdA na vidhaya iti ||31||

8. AshramakarmAdhikaraNam

|| 3.4.32 || 

atha yad uktam -- naivaM sati vidyAsAdhanatvam eShAM syAd iti, ata uttaraM paThati -- 

vihitatvAccAshramakarmApi ||

sarvApekShA ca [ve.sU. 3.4.23] ityatra AshramakarmaNAM vidyAsAdhanatvam avadhAritam | idAnIM tu kim amumukShor apyAshramamAtraniShThasya vidyAm akAmayamAnasya tAnyanuShTheyAni, utAho neti cintyate | tatra tam etaM vedAnuvacanena brAhmaNA vividiShanti [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.22] ityAdinA AshramakarmaNAM vidyAsAdhanatvena vihitatvAt vidyAm anicchataH phalAntaraM kAmayamAnasya nityAnyananuShTheyAni | atha tasyApyanuShTheyAni, na tarhi eShAM vidyAsAdhanatvam, nityAnityasaMyogavirodhAt -- ityasyAM prAptau, paThati -- AshramamAtraniShThasyApyamumukShoH kartavyAnyeva nityAni karmANi, yAvajjIvam agnihotraM juhoti ityAdinA vihitatvAt | na hi vacanasyAtibhAro nAma kashcid asti ||32||

 -- o)0(o -- 

|| 3.4.33 || 

sahakAritvena ca ||

vidyAsahakArINi ca etAni syuH, vihitatvAd eva tam etaM vedAnuvacanena brAhmaNA vividiShanti [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.22] ityAdinA | tad uktam -- sarvApekShA ca yaj~nAdishruterashvavat iti | na cedaM vidyAsahakAritvavacanam AshramakarmaNAM prayAjAdivat vidyAphalaviShayaM mantavyam, avidhilakShaNatvAd vidyAyAH, asAdhyatvAcca vidyAphalasya | vidhilakShaNaM hi sAdhanaM darshapUrNamAsAdisvargaphalasiShAdhayiShayA sahakArisAdhanAntaram apekShate, naivaM vidyA | tathA coktam -- ata eva cAgnIndhanAdyanapekShA iti | tasmAd utpattiH Adhanatva eva eShAM sahakAritvavAcoyuktiH | na ca atra nityAnityasaMyogavirodha AshaN^kyaH, karmAbhede.api saMyogabhedAt | nityo hi ekaH saMyogo yAvajjIvAdivAkyakalpitaH, na tasya vidyAphalatvam | anityaH tu aparaH saMyogaH tam etaM vedAnuvacanena [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.22] ityAdivAkyakalpitaH, tasya vidyAphalatvam -- yathA ekasyApi khAdiratvasya nityena saMyogena kratvarthatvam, anityena saMyogena puruShArthatvam, tadvat ||33||

|| 3.4.34 ||

sarvathA.api tu ta evobhayaliN^gAt ||

sarvathApi AshramakarmatvapakShe vidyAsahakAritvapakShe ca, ta eva agnihotrAdayo dharmA anuShTheyAH | ta eva ityavadhArayannAcAryaH kiM nivartayati? karmabhedashaN^kAm iti brUmaH | yathA kuNDApAyinAm ayane mAsam agnihotraM juhvati ityatra nityAd agnihotrAt karmAntaram upadishyate, naivam iha karmabhedo.astItyarthaH | kutaH? ubhayaliN^gAt, shrutiliN^gAt smR^itiliN^gAcca | shrutiliN^gaM tAvat -- tam etaM vedAnuvacanena brAhmaNA vividiShanti [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.22] iti siddhavad utpannarUpANyeva yaj~nAdIni vividiShAyAM viniyuN^kte, na tu juhvati ityAdivat apUrvameShAM rUpam utpAdayatIti | smR^itiliN^gam api -- anAshritaH karmaphalaM kAryaM karma karoti yaH [gItA 6.1] iti vij~nAtakartavyatAkam eva karma vidyotpattyarthaM darshayati | yasyaite.aShTAcatvAriMshat saMskArAH ityAdyA ca saMskAratvaprasiddhiH vaidikeShu karmasu tatsaMskR^itasya vidyotpattim abhipretya smR^itau bhaAhvati | tasmAt sAdhvidam abhedAvadhAraNam ||34||

|| 3.4.35 || 

anabhibhavaM ca darshayati ||

sahakAritvasyaiva etad upodbalakaM liN^gadarshanam | anabhibhavaM ca darshayati shrutiH brahmacaryAdisAdhanasampannasya rAgAdibhiH kleshaiH -- eSha hyAtmA na nashyati yaM brahmacaryeNAnuvindate ityAdinA | tasmAt yaj~nAdInyAshramakarmANi ca bhavanti vidyAsahakArINi ceti sthitam ||35||

  -- o)0(o -- 

9. vidhurAdhikaraNam

|| 3.4.36 ||

vidhurAdInAM dravyAdisampadrahitAnAM ca anyatamAshramapratipattihInAnAm antarAlavartinAM kiM vidyAyAm adhikAro.asti, kiM vA nAsti -- iti saMshaye, nAstIti tAvat prAptam, AshramakarmaNAM vidyAhetutvAvadhAraNAt, AshramakarmAsambhavAccaiteShAm -- ityevaM prApte, idam Aha -- 

antarA cApi tu taddR^iShTeH || 

antarA cApi tu -- anAshramitvena vartamAno.api vidyAyAm adhikriyate | kutaH? taddR^iShTeH -- raikvavAcaknavIprabhR^itInAm evambhUtAnAm api brahmavittvashrutyupalabdheH ||36||

|| 3.4.37 ||

api ca smaryate || 

saMvartaprabhR^itInAM ca nagnacaryAdiyogAt anapekShitAshramakarmaNAm api mahAyogitvaM smaryata itihAse ||37|| 

|| 3.4.38 ||

nanu liN^gam idaM shrutismR^itidarshanam upanyastam | kA nu khalu prAptiH iti, sA abhidhIyate -- 

visheShAnugrahashca || 

teShAm api ca vidhurAdInAm aviruddhaiH puruShamAtrasambandhibhir japopavAsadevatArAdhanAdibhir dharmavisheShair anugraho vidyAyAH sambhavati | tathA ca smR^itiH -- 

japyenaiva tu saMsidhyed brAhmaNo nAtra saMshayaH | 
kuryAd anyan na vA kuryAn maitro brAhmaNa ucyate || iti | 

asambhavadAshramakarmaNo.api japye.adhikAraM darshayati | janmAntarAnuShThitair api ca AshramakarmabhiH sambhavatyeva vidyAyA anugrahaH | tathA ca smR^itiH -- anekajanmasaMsiddhaH tato yAti parAM gatim [gItA 6.45] iti janmAntarasaJNcitAn api saMskAravisheShAn anugrahItn vidyAyAM darshayati | dR^iShTArthA ca vidyA pratiShedhAbhAvamAtreNApi arthinam adhikaroti shravaNAdiShu | tasmAt vidhurAdInAm apyadhikAro na virudhyate ||38||

|| 3.4.39 ||

ataH tvitarajjyAyo liN^gAcca ||

ataH tu antarAlavartitvAt itarat AshramavartitvaM jyAyo vidyAsAdhanam, shrutismR^itisandR^ibdhatvAt | shrutiliN^gAcca -- tenaiti brahmavit puNyakR^it taijasashca [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.1] iti | 

anAshramI na tiShTheta dinam ekam api dvijaH | 
saMvatsaram anAshramI sthitvA kR^iccharmekaM caret || iti ca smR^itiliN^gAt ||39||

  -- o)0(o -- 
10. tadbhUtAdhikaraNam 

|| 3.4.40 ||

tadbhUtasya tu nAtadbhAvo jaiminer api niyamAtadrUpAbhAvebhyaH ||

santi Urdhvaretasa AshramA iti sthApitam | tAMstu prAptasya kathaMcit tataH pracyutir asti, nAsti veti saMshayaH | pUrvadharmasvanuShThAnacikIrShayA vA rAgAdivashena vA pracyuto.api syAt visheShAbhAvAd ityevaM prApte, ucyate -- tadbhUtasya tu pratipannordhvaretobhAvasya na kathaMcid api atadbhAvaH, na tataH pracyutiH syAt | kutaH? niyamAtadrUpAbhAvebhyaH |

tathA hi -- atyantam AtmAnam AcAryakule.avasAdayan chA.u. 2.23.1] iti, araNyam iyAd iti padaM tato na punar eyAd ityupaniShat iti, AcAryeNAbhyanuj~nAtashcaturNAm ekam Ashramam | A vimokShAccharIrasya so.anutiShThed yathAvidhi iti ca evaMjAtIyako niyamaH pracyutyabhAvaM darshayati | yathA ca brahmacaryaM samApya gR^ihI bhavet... brahmacaryAd eva pravrajet [jA.u. 4], iti ca evamAdIni AroharUpANi vacAMsyupalabhyante, naivaM pratyavaroharUpANi | na caivam AcArAH shiShTA vidyante | yat tu pUrvadharmasvanuShThAnacikIrShayA pratyavarohaNam iti, tad asat -- shreyAn svadharmo viguNaH paradharmAt svanuShThitAt [gItA 3.35] iti smaraNAt, nyAyAcca -- yo hi yaM prati vidhIyate sa tasya dharmaH, na tu yo yena svanuShThAtuM shakyate, codanAlakShaNatvAd dharmasya | na ca rAgAdivashAt pracyutiH, niyamashAstrasya balIyastvAt | jaiminer apIti apishabdena jaiminibAdarAyaNayor atra sampratipattiM shAsti pratipattidADhyAya ||40||

  -- o)0(o -- 

11. AdhikArikAdhikaraNam 

|| 3.4.41 ||

na cAdhikArikam api patanAnumAnAttadayogAt ||

yadi naiShThiko brahmacArI pramAdAdavakIryeta, kiM tasya brahmacAryavakIrNI nar R^iShtaM gardabham Alabheta ityetatprAyashcittaM syAt, uta neti | netyucyate | yad api adhikAralakShaNe nirNItaM prAyashcittam avakIrNipashushca tadvad AdhAnasyAprAptakAlatvAt [jai.sU. 6.8.21] iti, tad api na naiShThikasya bhavitum arhati | kiM kAraNam? 

ArUDho naiShThikaM dharmaM yaH tu pracyavate punaH | 
prAyashcittaM na pashyAmi yena shudhyet sa AtmahA || 

iti apratisamAdheyapatanasmaraNAt chinnashirasa iva pratikriyAnupapatteH | upakurvANasya tu tAdR^ikpatanasmaraNAbhAvAd upapadyate tatprAyashcittam ||41||

|| 3.4.42 || 

upapUrvam api tv eke bhAvam ashanavat tad uktam ||

api tu eke AcAryA upapAtakam evaitad iti manyante | yat naiShThikasya gurudArAdibhyo.anyatra brahmacaryaM vishIryeta, na tat mahApAtakaM bhavati, gurutalpAdiShu mahApAtakeShvaparigaNanAt | tasmAt upakurvANavat naiShThikasyApi prAyashcittasya bhAvam icchanti, brahmacAritvAvisheShAt avakIrNitvAvisheShAcca | ashanavat -- yathA brahmacAriNo madhumAMsAshAne vratalopaH punaH saMskArashca, evam iti | ye hi prAyashcittasyAbhAvam icchanti, teShAM na mUlam upalabhyate | ye tu bhAvam icchanti, teShAM brahmacAryavakIrNI ityetad avisheShashravaNaM mUlam | tasmAt bhAvo yuktataraH | tad uktaM pramANalakShaNe -- samA vipratipattiH syAt [jai.sU. 1.3.8], shAstrasthA vA tannimittatvAt [jai.sU. 1.3.9] iti | prAyashcittAbhAvasmaraNaM tu evaM sati yatnagauravotpAdanArtham iti vyAkhyAtavyam | evaM bhikShuvaikhAnasayor api -- vAnaprastho dIkShAbhede kR^icchaddhaM dvAdasharAtraM caritvA mahAkakShaM vardhayet bhikShur vAnaprasthavat somavR^iddhivarjaM svashAstrasaMskArashca ityevamAdi prAyashcittasmaraNam anusartavyam ||42||

  -- o)0(o -- 

12. bahiradhikaraNam

|| 3.4.43 ||

bahiH tUbhayathA.api smR^iter AcArAcca ||

yadi UrdhvaretasAM svAshramebhyaH pracyavanaM mahApAtakam, yadi vA upapAtakam, ubhayathApi shiShTaiH te bahiShkartavyAH -- 

ArUDho naiShThikaM dharmaM yaH tu pracyavate punaH | 
prAyashcittaM na pashyAmi yena shudhyet sa AtmahA || iti,
ArUDhapatitaM vipraM maNDalAcca viniHsR^itam | 
udbaddhaM kR^imidaShTaM ca spR^iShTvA cAndrAyaNaM caret || 

iti ca evamAdinindAtishayasmR^itibhyaH, shiShTAcArAcca -- na hi yaj~nAdhyayanavivAhAdIni taiH saha Acaranti shiShTAH ||43||

 -- o)0(o -- 
13. svAmyadhikaraNam 

|| 3.4.44 ||

svAminaH phalashruteH ityAtreyaH ||  

aN^geShUpAsaneShu saMshayaH -- kiM tAni yajamAnakarmANi Aho svit R^itvikkarmANIti | kiM tAvat prAptam? yajamAnakarmANIti | kutaH? phalashruteH | phalaM hi shrUyate -- varShati hAsmai varShayati ha ya etad evaM vidvAn vR^iShTau paJNcavidhaM sAmopAste [chA.u. 2.3.2] ityAdi | tacca svAmigAmi nyAyyam, tasya sAN^ge prayoge.adhikR^itatvAt, adhikR^itAdhikAratvAcca evaMjAtIyakasya | phalaM ca kartari upAsanAnAM shrUyate -- varShatyasmai ya upAste ityAdi | 

nanu R^itvijo.api phalaM dR^iShTAm Atmane vA yajamAnAya vA yaM kAmaM kAmayate tam AgAyati [chA.u. 1.7.89] iti -- na, tasya vAcanikatvAt | tasmAt svAmina eva phalavatsu upAsaneShu kartR^itvam -- ityAtreya AcAryo manyate ||44||

|| 3.4.45 ||

Artvijyam ityauDulomiH tasmai hi parikriyate ||

naitad asti -- svAmikarmANyupAsanAnIti | R^itvikkarmANyetAni syuH -- ityauDulomir AcAryo manyate | kiM kAraNam? tasmai hi sAN^gAya karmaNe yajamAnena R^itvik parikriyate | tatprayogAntaHpAtIni ca udgIthAdyupAsanAni adhikR^itAdhikAratvAt | tasmAt godohanAdiniyamavad eva R^itvigbhir nirvartyeran | tathA ca -- taM ha bako dAlbhyo vidAMcakAra sa ha naimishIyAnAm udgAtA babhUva [chA.u. 1.2.13] ityudgAtR^ikartR^ikatAM vij~nAnasya darshayati | yat tUktaM kartrAshrayaM phalaM shrUyata iti -- naiSha doShaH, parArthatvAd R^itvijo.anyatra vacanAt phalasambandhAnupapatteH ||45||

|| 3.4.46 || 

shruteshca ||

yAM vai kAMcana yaj~na R^itvija AshiSham AshAsata iti yajamAnAyaiva tAm AshAsata iti hovAca iti, tasmAd u haivaMvid udgAtA brUyAt kaM te kAmam AgAyAni [chA.u. 1.7.89] iti ca R^itvikkartR^ikasya vij~nAnasya yajamAnagAmi phalaM darshayati | tasmAt aN^gopAsanAnAm R^itvikkarmatvasiddhiH ||46||

  -- o)0(o -- 
14. sahakAryantaravidhyadhikaraNam 

|| 3.4.47 || 

tasmAd brAhmaNaH pANDityaM nirvidya bAlyena tiShThAset | bAlyaM ca pANDityaM ca nirvidyAtha munir amaunaM ca maunaM ca nirvidyAtha brAhmaNaH [bR^i.A.u. 3.5.1] iti bR^ihadAraNyake shrUyate | 

tatra saMshayaH -- maunaM vidhIyate, na veti | na vidhIyata iti tAvat prAptam, bAlyena tiShThAset ityatraiva vidher avasitatvAt | na hi atha muniH ityatra vidhAyikA vibhaktir upalabhyate | tasmAd ayam anuvAdo yuktaH | kutaH prAptiH iti cet -- munipaNDitashabdayor j~nAnArthatvAt pANDityaM nirvidya ityevaM prAptaM maunam | api ca amaunaM ca maunaM ca nirvidyAtha brAhmaNaH ityatra tAvat na brAhmaNatvaM vidhIyate, prAg eva prAptatvAt | tasmAt atha brAhmaNaH iti prashaMsAvAdaH, tathaiva atha muniH ityapi bhavitum arhati, samAnanirdeshatvAt | ityevaM prApte, brUmaH -- 

sahakAryantaravidhiH pakSheNa tR^itIyaM tadvato vidhyAdivat ||

vidyAsahakAriNo maunasya bAlyapANDityavad vidhir eva AshrayitavyaH, apUrvatvAt | 

nanu pANDityashabdenaiva maunasyAvagatatvam uktam -- naiSha doShaH, munishabdasya j~nAnAtishayArthatvAt, mananAn muniH iti ca vyutpattiH ambhavAt, munInAm apyahaM vyAsaH iti ca prayogadarshanAt | 

nanu munishabda uttamAshramavacano.api shrUyate gArhasthyam AcAryakulaM maunaM vAnaprastham ityatra -- na, vAlmIkir munipuN^gavaH ityAdiShu vyabhicAradarshanAt | itarAshramasaMnidhAnAt tu pArisheShyAt tatra uttamAshramopAdAnam, j~nAnapradhAnatvAd uttamAshramasya | tasmAt bAlyapANDityApekShayA tR^itIyam idaM maunaM j~nAnAtishayarUpaM vidhIyate | yat tu bAlya eva vidhiparyavasAnam iti, tathApi apUrvatvAn munitvasya vidheyatvam AshrIyate -- muniH syAd iti | nirvedanIyatvanirdeshAd api maunasya bAlyapANDityavad vidheyatvAshrayaNam | tadvataH vidyAvataH saMnyAsinaH | kathaM ca vidyAvataH saMnyAsina ityavagamyate? tadadhikArAt -- AtmAnaM viditvA putrAdyeShaNAbhyo vyutthAya atha bhikShAcaryaM caranti iti | 

nanu sati vidyAvattve prApnotyeva tatrAtishayaH, kiM maunavidhinA ? ityata Aha -- pakSheNeti | etad uktaM bhavati -- yasmin pakShe bhedadarshanaprAbalyAt na prApnoti, tasmin eSha vidhiH iti | vidhyAdivat -- yathA darshapUrNamAsAbhyAM svargakAmo yajeta ityevaMjAtIyake vidhyAdau sahakAritvena agnyanvAdhAnAdikam aN^gajAtaM vidhIyate, evam avidhipradhAne.api asmin vidyAvAkye maunavidhiH ityarthaH ||47|| 

|| 3.4.48 || 

evaM bAlyAdivishiShTo kaivalyAshrame shrutimati vidyamAne, kasmAt chAndogye gR^ihiNA upasaMhAro.abhisamAvR^itya kuTumbe ityatra? tena hi upasaMharan tadviShayam AdaraM darshayati, ityata uttaraM paThati -- 

kR^itsnabhAvAt tu gR^ihiNopasaMhAraH ||

tushabdo visheShaNArthaH | kR^itsnabhAvo.asya visheShyate | bahulAyAsAni hi bahUnyAshramakarmANi yaj~nAdIni taM prati kartavyatayopadiShTAni, AshramAntarakarmANi ca yathAsambhavam ahiMsendriyasaMyamAdIni tasya vidyante | tasmAt gR^ihamedhinA upasaMhAro na virudhyate ||48||

|| 3.4.49 || 

maunavad itareShAm apyupadeshAt ||

yathA maunaM gArhasthyaM ca etAvashramau shrutimantau, evam itarAvapi vAnaprasthagurukulAvAsau | darshitA hi purastAcchrutiH -- tapa eva dvitIyo brahmacAryAcAryakulavAsI tR^itIyaH ityAdyA | tasmAt caturNAm apyAshramANAm upadeshAvisheShAt tulyavat vikalpasamuccayAbhyAM pratipattiH | itareShAm iti dvayor Ashramayor bahuvacanaM vR^ittibhedApekShayA anuShThAtR^ibhedApekShayA vA, iti draShTavyam ||49||

 -- o)0(o -- 
15. anAviShkArAdhikaraNam

|| 3.4.50 || 

tasmAd brAhmaNaH pANDityaM nirvidya bAlyena tiShThAset iti bAlyam anuShTheyatayA shrUyate | tatra bAlasya bhAvaH karma vA bAlyam iti tad dhite sati, bAlabhAvasya vayovisheShasya icchayA sampAdayitum ashakyatvAt, yathopapAdamUtrapurIShatvAdi bAlacaritam, antargatA vA bhAvavishuddhiH aprarUDhendriyatvaM dambhAdirahitatvaM vA bAlyaM syAd iti saMshayaH | kiM tAvat prAptam? kAmacAravAdabhakShatA yathopapAdamUtrapurIShatvaM ca prasiddhataraM loke bAlyam iti tadgrahaNaM yuktam |

nanu patitatvAdidoShaprApter na yuktaM kAmacAratAdyAshrayaNam -- na | vidyAvataH saMnyAsino vacanasAmarthyAt doShanivR^ittiH, pashuhiMsAdiShvivetyevaM prApte -- 

anAviShkurvann anvayAt ||

abhidhIyate -- na, vacanasya gatyantarasambhavAt | aviruddhe hi anyasmin bAlyashabdAbhilapye labhyamAne, na vidhyantaravyAghAtakalpanA yuktA | pradhAnopakArAya ca aN^gaM vidhIyate | j~nAnAbhyAsashca pradhAnam iha yatInAm anuShTheyam | na ca sakalAyAM bAlacaryAyAm aN^gIkriyamANAyAM j~nAnAbhyAsaH sambhAvyate | tasmAd Antaro bhAvavisheSho bAlasya aprarUDhendriyatvAd iH iha bAlyam AshrIyate | tad Aha -- anAviShkurvann iti| j~nAnAdhyayanadhArmikatvAdibhiH AtmAnam avikhyApayan dambhadarpAdirahito bhavet -- yathA bAlo.aprarUDhendriyatayA na pareShAm AtmAnam AviShkartum Ihate, tadvat | evaM hi asya vAkyasya pradhAnopakAryarthAnugama upapadyate | tathA ca uktaM smR^itikAraiH -- 

yaM na santaM na cAsantaM nAshrutaM na bahushrutam | 
na suvR^ittaM na durvR^ittaM veda kashcit sa brAhmaNaH || 
gUDhadharmAshrito vidvAn aj~nAtacaritaM caret |
andhavajjaDavaccApi mUkavacca mahIM caret |
avyaktaliN^go.avyaktAcAraH iti caivamAdi ||50||

  -- o)0(o -- 
16. aihikAdhikaraNam 

|| 3.4.51 ||

sarvApekShA ca yaj~nAdishruter ashvavat ityata Arabhya uccAvacaM vidyAsAdhanam avadhAritam | tatphalaM vidyA sidhyantI kim ihaiva janmani sidhyati, uta kadAcid amutrApIti cintyate | kiM tAvat prAptam? ihaiveti | kiM kAraNam? shravaNAdipUrvikA hi vidyA | na ca kashcid amutra me vidyA jAyatAm ityanusandhAya shravaNAdiShu pravartate | samAna eva tu janmani vidyAjanma abhisandhAya eteShu pravartamAno dR^ishyate | yaj~nAdInyapi shravaNAdidvAreNaiva vidyAM janayanti, pramANajanyatvAd vidyAyAH | tasmAd aihikam eva vidyAjanmetyevaM prApte -- 

aihikam apyaprastutapratibandhe taddarshanAt ||

vadAmaH -- aihikaM vidyAjanma bhavati, asati prastutapratibandha iti | etad uktaM bhavati -- yadA prakrAntasya vidyAsAdhanasya kashcit pratibandho na kriyate upasthitavipAkena karmAntareNa, tadA ihaiva vidyA utpadyate | yadA tu khalu tatpratibandhaH kriyate tadA amutreti | upasthitavipAkatvaM ca karmaNo deshakAlanimittopanipAtAd bhavati | yAni ca ekasya karmaNo vipAcakAni deshakAlanimittAni, tAnyeva anyasyApIti na niyantuM shakyate | yato viruddhaphalAnyapi karmANi bhavanti | shAstram api asya karmaNa idaM phalam ityetAvati paryavasitaM na deshakAlanimittavisheSham api saN^kIrtayati | sAdhanavIryavisheShAt tu atIndriyA kasyacicchaktir Avirbhavati, tatpratibaddhA parasya tiShThati | na cAvisheSheNa vidyAyAm, abhisandhir notpadyate -- iha amutra vA me vidyA jAyatAm iti, abhisandher niraN^kushatvAt | shravaNAdidvAreNApi vidyA utpadyamAnA pratibandhakShayApekShayaiva utpadyate | 

tathA ca shrutiH durbodhatvam Atmano darshayati -- 

shravaNAyApi bahubhir yo na labhyaH 
sR^iNvanto.api bahavo yaM na vidyuH | 
Ashcaryo.asya vaktA kushalo.asya labdhA
shcaryo j~nAtA kushalAnushiShTAH || [ka.u. 1.2.7] iti | 

garbhastha eva ca vAmadevaH pratipede brahmabhAvam iti vadantI janmAntarasaJNcitAt sAdhanAt janmAntare vidyotpattiM darshayati | na hi garbhasthasyaiva aihikaM kiMcit sAdhanaM sambhAvyate | 

smR^itAvapi -- aprApya yogasaMsiddhiM kAM gatiM kR^iShNa gacchati [gItA 6.37] ityarjunena pR^iShTo bhagavAn vAsudevaH na hi kalyANakR^it kashcid durgatiM tAta gacchati [gItA 6.40] ityuktvA, punaH tasya puNyalokaprAptiM sAdhukule sambhUtiM ca abhidhAya, anantaram tatra taM buddhisaMyogaM labhate paurvadehikam ityAdinA anekajanmasaMsiddhaH tato yAti parAM gatim [gItA 6.45] ityantena etad eva darshayati | tasmAt aihikam AmuShmikaM vA vidyAjanmapratibandhakShayApekShayeti sthitam ||51||

  -- o)0(o -- 
17. muktiphalAdhikaraNam

|| 3.4.52 || 

yathA mumukShor vidyAsAdhanAvalambinaH sAdhanavIryavisheShAd vidyAlakShaNe phale aihikAmuShmikaphalatvakR^ito visheShapratiniyamo dR^iShTaH, evaM muktilakShaNe.api utkarShApakarShakR^itaH kashcid visheShapratiniyamaH syAt, ityAshaN^kyAha -- 

evaM muktiphalAniyamaH 
tadavasthAvadhR^iteH tadavasthAvadhR^iteH || 

na khalu muktiphale kashcit evambhUto visheShapratiniyama AshaN^kitavyaH | kutaH? tadavasthAvadhR^iteH -- muktyavasthA hi sarvavedAnteShv ekarUpaiva avadhAryate | brahmaiva hi muktyavasthA | na ca brahmaNo.anekAkArayogo.asti, ekaliN^gatvAvadhAraNAt -- asthUlam anaNu  [bR^i.A.u. 3.8.8], sa eSha neti netyAtmA [bR^i.A.u. 3.9.23], yatra nAnyat pashyati [chA.u. 7.24.1], brahmaivedam amR^itaM purastAt [mu.u. 2.2.11], idaM sarvaM yad ayam AtmA [bR^i.A.u. 2.4.6], sa vA eSha mahAn aja AtmAjaro.amaro.amR^ito.abhayo brahma [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.25], yatra tu asya sarvam AtmaivAbhUt tat kena kaM pashyet [bR^i.A.u. 4.5.15] ityAdi shrutibhyaH | api ca vidyAsAdhanaM svavIryavisheShAt svaphala eva vidyAyAM kaMcid atishayam AsaJNjayet, na vidyAphale muktau | tad dhi asAdhyaM nityasiddhasvabhAvam eva vidyayA adhigamyata ityasakR^id avAdiShma | na ca tasyAm apyutkarShanikarShAtmako.atishaya upapadyate, nikR^iShTAyA vidyAtvAbhAvAt | utkR^iShtaiva hi vidyA bhavati | tasmAt tasyAM cirAcirotpattirUpo.atishayo bhavan bhavet | na tu muktau kashcit atishayasambhavo.asti | vidyAbhedAbhAvAd api tatphalabhedaniyamAbhAvaH, karmaphalavat | na hi muktisAdhanabhUtAyA vidyAyAH karmaNAm iva bhedo.asti | saguNAsu tu vidyAsu manomayaH prANasharIraH [chA.u.  3.14.2] ityAdyAsu guNAvApodvApavashAd bhedopapattau satyAm, upapadyate yathAsvaM phalabhedaniyamaH, karmaphalavat -- tathA ca liN^gadarshanam -- taM yathA yathopAsate tad eva bhavati iti | naivaM nirguNAyAM vidyAyAm, guNAbhAvAt | tathA ca smR^itiH -- na hi gatir adhikAsti kasyacit sati hi guNe pravadantyatulyatAm iti | 

tadavasthAvadhR^iteH tadavasthAvadhR^iteH iti padAbhyAso.adhyAyaparisamAptiM dyotayati ||52|| 

iti shrImatparamahaMsaparivrAjakAcAryasya shrIgovindabhagavatpUjyapAdashiShyasya shrImacchaN^karabhagavataH kR^itau shArIrakamImAMsAsUtrabhAShye
tR^itIyAdhyAye caturthaH pAdaH
|| 3.4 || 

 -- o)0(o -- 
 

(4.1)
|| caturtho.adhyAye prathamaH pAdaH || 

atra asmin phalAdhyAye prathamapAde jIvanmuktinirUpaNam ||

1. AvR^ittyadhikaraNam

|| 4.1.1 || 

tR^itIye adhyAye parA aparAsu vidyAsu sAdhana Ashrayo vicAraH prAyeNAtyagAt | atha iha caturthe phalAshraya AgamiShyati | prasaN^gAgataM ca anyad api kiJNcit cintayiShyate | prathamaM tAvat katibhiH cidadhikaraNaiH sAdhana AshrayavicArasheSham eva anusarAmaH ?

AtmA vA are draShTavyaH shrotavyo mantavyo nididhyAsitavyaH [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.5], tam eva dhIro vij~nAya praj~nAM kurvIta [bR^i.A.u. 4.5.6], so.anveShTavyaH sa vijij~nAsitavyaH [chA.u. 8.7.1] iti ca evamAdishravaNeShu saMshayaH -- kiM sakR^itpratyayaH kartavyaH, Aho svit AvR^ittyA ? iti | kiM tAvat prAptam? sakR^itpratyayaH syAt, prayAjAdivat, tAvatA shAstrasya kR^itArthatvAt | ashrUyamANAyAM hi AvR^ittau kriyamANAyAm ashAstrArthaH kR^ito bhavet |

nanu asakR^idupadeshA udAhR^itAH -- shrotavyo mantavyo nididhyAsitavyaH ityevamAdayaH -- evam api yAvacchabdam Avartayet | sakR^icchravaNaM sakR^in mananaM sakR^in nididhyAsanaM ceti, nAtiriktam | sakR^idupadesheShu tu veda upAsIta ityevam AdiShu anAvR^ittiH ityevaM prApte, brUmaH -- 

AvR^ittir asakR^idupadeshAt ||

pratyayAvR^ittiH kartavyA | kutaH? asakR^idupadeshAt -- shrotavyo mantavyo nididhyAsitavyaH ityevaMjAtIyako hi asakR^idupadeshaH pratyayAvR^ittiM sUcayati | 

nanUktam -- yAvacchabdam eva Avartayet, nAdhikam iti -- na, darshanaparyavasAnatvAd eShAm | darshanaparyavasAnAni hi shravaNAdInyAvartyamAnAni dR^iShTArthAni bhavanti -- yathA avaghAtAdIni taNDulAdiniShpattiparyavasAnAni hi, tadvat | api ca upAsanaM nididhyAsanaM cetyantarNItAvR^ittiguNaiva kriyA abhidhIyate | tathA hi loke gurum upAste rAjAnam upAste iti ca yaH tAtparyeNa gurvAdIn anuvartate, sa eva mucyate | tathA dhyAyati proShitanAthA patim iti -- yA nirantarasmaraNA patiM prati sotkaNThA, sA evam abhidhIyate | vidyupAstyoshca vedAnteShu avyatirekeNa prayogo dR^ishyate | kvacit vidinopakramya upAsinopasaMharati, yathA -- yaH tad veda yat sa veda sa mayaitad uktaH ityatra anu ma etAM bhagavo devatAM shAdhi yAM devatAm upAsse iti | kvacicca upAsinopakramya vidinopasaMharati, yathA -- mano brahmetyupAsIta ityatra bhAti ca tapati ca kIrtyA yashasA brahmavarcasena ya evaM veda iti | tasmAt sakR^idupadesheShvapi AvR^ittisiddhiH | asakR^idupadeshaH tu AvR^itteH sUcakaH ||1||

|| 4.1.2 || 

liN^gAcca || 

liN^gam api pratyayAvR^ittiM pratyAyayati | tathA hi -- udgIthavij~nAnaM prastutya, Aditya udgIthaH ityetat ekaputratAdoSheNApodya, rashmIMH tvaM paryAvartayAt iti rashmibahutvavij~nAnaM bahuputratAyai vidadhat siddhavat pratyayAvR^ittiM darshayati | tatsAmAnyAt sarvapratyayeShvavR^ittisiddhiH || 

atrAha -- bhavatu nAma sAdhyaphaleShu pratyayeShvavR^ittiH, teShvavR^ittisAdhyasyAtishayasya sambhavAt | yaH tu parabrahmaviShayaH pratyayo nityashuddhabuddhamuktasvabhAvam eva AtmabhUtaM paraM brahma samarpayati, tatra kimarthA AvR^ittiH iti | sakR^icchrutau ca brahmAtmatvapratItyanupapatter AvR^ittyabhyupagama iti cet, na, AvR^ittAvapi tadanupapatteH | yadi hi tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7] ityevaMjAtIyakaM vAkyaM sakR^icchrUyamANaM brahmAtmatvapratItiM notpAdayet, tataH tad eva AvartyamAnam utpAdayiShyatIti kA pratyAshA syAt ? 

athocyeta -- na kevalaM vAkyaM kaJNcid arthaM sAkShAtkartuM shaknoti | ato yuktyapekShaM vAkyam anubhAvayiShyati brahmAtmatvam iti -- tathApyAvR^ittyAnarthakyam eva | sApi hi yuktiH sakR^itpravR^ittaiva svam artham anubhAvayiShyati | athApi syAt -- yuktyA vAkyena ca sAmAnyaviShayam eva vij~nAnaM kriyate, na visheShaviShayam | yathA asti me hR^idaye shUlam ityato vAkyAt gAtrakampAdiliN^gAcca shUlasadbhAvasAmAnyam eva paraH pratipadyate, na visheSham anubhavati -- yathA sa eva shUlI | visheShAnubhavashca avidyAyA nivartakaH | tadarthA AvR^ittiH iti cet -- na, asakR^id api tAvanmAtre kriyamANe visheShavij~nAnotpattyasambhavAt | na hi sakR^itprayuktAbhyAM shAstrayuktibhyAm anavagato visheShaH shatakR^itvo.api prayujyamAnAbhyAm avagantuM shakyate | tasmAt yadi shAstrayuktibhyAM visheShaH pratipAdyeta, yadi vA sAmAnyam eva, ubhayathApi sakR^itpravR^itte eva te svakAryaM kuruta iti AvR^ittyanupayogaH | na ca sakR^itprayukte shAstrayuktI kasyacid apyanubhavaM notpAdayata iti shakyate niyantum, vicitrapraj~natvAt pratipattNAm | api ca anekAMshopete laukike padArthe sAmAnyavisheShavati ekenAvadhAnena ekam aMsham avadhArayati, apareNa aparam -- iti syAd apyabhyAsopayogaH, yathA dIrghaprapAThakagrahaNAdiShu | na tu nirvisheShe brahmaNi sAmAnyavisheSharahite caitanyamAtrAtmake pramotpattAvabhyAsApekShA yukteti || 

atrocyate -- bhaved AvR^ittyAnarthakyaM taM prati, yaH tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7] iti sakR^id uktam eva brahmAtmatvam anubhavituM shaknuyAt | yaH tu na shaknoti, taM prati upayujyata eva AvR^ittiH | tathA hi cchAndogye -- tat tvam asi shvetaketo [chA.u. 6.8.7] ityupadishya, bhUya eva mA bhagavAn vij~nApayatu iti punaH punaH paricodyamAnaH tattadAshaN^kAkAraNaM nirAkR^itya, tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7] ityevAsakR^idupadishati | tathA ca shrotavyo mantavyo nididhyAsitavyaH ityAdi darshitam | 

nanu uktam -- sakR^icchrutaM cet tat tvam asivAkyaM svam artham anubhAvayituM na shaknoti, tata AvartyamAnam api naiva shakShyatIti -- naiSha doShaH | na hi dR^iShTo.anupapannaM nAma | dR^ishyante hi sakR^icchrutAd vAkyAt mandapratItaM vAkyArtham AvartayantaH tattadAbhAsavyudAsena samyakpratipadyamAnAH | 

api ca tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7] ityetad vAkyaM tvaMpadArthasya tatpadArthabhAvam AcaShTe | tatpadena ca prakR^itaM sat brahma IkShitR^i jagato janmAdikAraNam abhidhIyate -- satyaM j~nAnam anantaM brahma [tai.u. 2.3], vij~nAnam AnandaM brahma [bR^i.A.u. 3.9.7], adR^iShTaM draShTR^i avij~nAtaM vij~nAtR^i ajam ajaram amaram asthUlam anaNvahrasvam adIrgham  [bR^i.A.u. 3.8.11] ityAdi shAstrasiddham | tatra ajAdishabdair janmAdayo bhAvavikArA nivartitAH | asthUlAdishabdaishca sthaulyAdayo dravyadharmAH | vij~nAnAdishabdaishca caitanyaprakAshAtmakatvam uktam | eSha vyAvR^ittasarvasaMsAradharmako.anubhavAtmako brahmasaMj~nakaH tatpadArtho vedAntAbhiyuktAnAM prasiddhaH | tathA tvaMpadArtho.api pratyagAtmA shrotA dehAd Arabhya pratyagAtmatayA sambhAvyamAnaH caitanyaparyantatvenAvadhAritaH | tatra yeShAm etau padArthau aj~nAnasaMshayaviparyayapratibaddhau, teShAM tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7] ityetad vAkyaM svArthe pramAM notpAdayituM shaknoti, padArthaj~nAnapUrvakatvAd vAkyArthaj~nAnasyeti | 

ataH, tAn pratyeShTavyaH padArthavivekaprayojanaH shAstrayuktyabhyAsaH | yadyapi ca pratipattavya AtmA niraMshaH, tathApi adhyAropitaM tasmin bahvaMshatvaM dehendriyamanobuddhiviShayavedanAdilakShaNam | tatra ekena avadhAnena ekam aMsham apohati, apareNa aparam iti yujyate | tatra kramavatI pratipattiH | tat tu pUrvarUpam eva AtmapratipatteH | yeShAM punaH nipuNamatInAM na aj~nAnasaMshayaviparyayalakShaNaH padArthaviShayaH pratibandho.asti, te shaknuvanti sakR^id uktam eva tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7] vAkyArtham anubhavitum iti, tAn prati AvR^ittyAnarthakyam iShTam eva | sakR^idutpannaiva hi AtmapratipattiH avidyAM nivartayatIti, nAtra kashcid api kramo.abhyupagamyate | satyam evaM yujyeta, yadi kasyacit evaM pratipattir bhavet | balavatI hi Atmano duHkhitvAdipratipattiH | 

ato na duHkhitvAdyabhAvaM kashcit pratipadyata iti cet -- na, dehAdyabhimAnavat duHkhitvAdyabhimAnasya mithyAbhimAnatvopapatteH | pratyakShaM hi dehe chidyamAne dahyamAne vA ahaM chidye dahye iti ca mithyAbhimAno dR^iShTaH | tathA bAhyatareShvapi putramitrAdiShu santapyamAneShu aham eva santapye ityadhyAropo dR^iShTaH | tathA duHkhitvAdyabhimAno.api syAt, dehAdivad eva caitanyAd bahirupalabhyamAnatvAd duHkhitvAdInAm, suShuptAdiShu ca ananuvR^itteH | caitanyasya tu suShupte.api anuvR^ittim Amananti -- yad vai tan na pashyati pashyan vai tan na pashyati [bR^i.A.u. 4.3.23] ityAdinA | tasmAt sarvaduHkhavinirmuktaikacaitanyAtmako.aham ityeSha AtmAnubhavaH | na caivam AtmAnam anubhavataH kiMcid anyat kR^ityam avashiShyate | tathA ca shrutiH -- kiM prajayA kariShyAmo yeShAM no.ayam AtmAyaM lokaH [bR^i.A.u. 4.3.22] ityAtmavidaH kartavyAbhAvaM darshayati | smR^itir api -- 

yaH tvatmaratir eva syAd AtmatR^iptashca mAnavaH | 
Atmanyeva ca santuShTaH tasya kAryaM na vidyate || [gItA 3.17] iti | 

yasya tu na eSho.anubhavo drAgiva jAyate, taM prati anubhavArtha eva AvR^ittyabhyupagamaH | tatrApi na tat tvam asivAkyArthAt pracyAvya AvR^ittau pravartayet | na hi varaghAtAya kanyAm udvAhayanti | niyuktasya ca asminn adhikR^ito.ahaM kartA mayedaM kartavyam ityavashyaM brahmapratyayAd viparItapratyaya utpadyate | yaH tu svayam eva mandamatiH apratibhAnAt taM vAkyArthaM jihAset, tasya etasminn eva vAkyArthe sthirIkAra AvR^ittyAdivAcoyuktyA abhyupeyate | tasmAt parabrahmaviShaye.api pratyaye tadupAyopadesheShvavR^ittisiddhiH ||2||

2. AtmatvopAsanAdhikaraNam

|| 4.1.3 ||

yaH shAstroktavisheShaNaH paramAtmA, sa kim aham iti grahItavyaH, kiM vA madanya iti -- etad vicArayati | kathaM punar Atmashabde pratyagAtmaviShaye shrUyamANe saMshaya iti, ucyate -- ayam Atmashabdo mukhyaH shakyate.abhyupagantum, sati jIveshvarayor abhedasambhave | itarathA tu gauNo.ayam abhyupagantavya iti manyate | kiM tAvat prAptam? na aham iti grAhyaH | na hi apahatapApmatvAdiguNo viparItaguNatvena shakyate grahItum, viparItaguNo vA apahatapApmatvAdiguNatvena | apahatapApmatvAdiguNashca parameshvaraH, tadviparItaguNaH tu shArIraH | Ishvarasya ca saMsAryAtmatve IshvarAbhAvaprasaN^gaH | tataH shAstrAnarthakyam | saMsAriNo.api IshvarAtmatve adhikAryabhAvAcchAstrAnarthakyam eva, pratyakShAdivirodhashca | anyatve.api tAdAtmyadarshanaM shAstrAt kartavyam -- pratimAdiShviva viShNvAdidarshanam iti cet -- kAmam evaM bhavatu | na tu saMsAriNo mukhya AtmA Ishvara ityetat naH prApayitavyam | evaM prApte,

Atmeti tUpagacchanti grAhayanti ca ||

brUmaH -- Atmetyeva parameshvaraH pratipattavyaH | tathA hi parameshvaraprakriyAyAM jAbAlA Atmatvenaiva etam upagacchanti -- tvaM vA aham asmi bhagavo devate.ahaM vai tvam asi devate [jAbAlashruti] iti | tathA anye.api ahaM brahmAsmi [bR^i.A.u. 1.4.10] ityevam Adaya AtmatvopagamA draShTavyAH | grAhayanti ca Atmatvenaiva IshvaraM vedAntavAkyAni -- eSha ta AtmA sarvAntaraH [bR^i.A.u. 3.4.1], eSha ta AtmAntaryAmyamR^itaH [bR^i.A.u. 3.7.4], tat satyaM sa AtmA tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7] ityevam AdIni | yad uktam -- pratIkadarshanam idaM viShNupratimAnyAyena bhaviShyatIti, tad ayuktam, gauNatvaprasaN^gAt, vAkyavairUpyAcca -- yatra hi pratIkadR^iShTir abhipreyate, sakR^id eva tatra vacanaM bhavati -- yathA mano brahma Adityo brahma ityAdi | iha punaH -- tvam aham asmi, ahaM ca tvam asItyAha -- ataH pratIkashrutivairUpyAt abhedapratipattiH | bhedadR^iShTApavAdAcca | tathA hi -- atha yo.anyAM devatAm upAste.anyo.asAvanyo.aham asmIti na sa veda mR^ityoH sa mR^ityum Apnoti ya iha nAneva pashyati sarvaM taM parAd Adyo.anyatrAtmanaH sarvaM veda [bR^i.A.u. 1.4.10] ityevam AdyA bhUyasI shrutiH bhedadarshanam apavadati | yat tUktam -- na viruddhaguNayor anyonyAtmatvasambhava iti, nAyaM doShaH, viruddhaguNatAyA mithyAtvopapatteH | yat punar uktam -- IshvarAbhAvaprasaN^ga iti, tad asat, shAstraprAmANyAt anabhyupagamAcca | na hi Ishvarasya saMsAryAtmatvaM pratipAdyata ityabhyupagacchAmaH | 

kiM tarhi, saMsAriNaH saMsAritvApohena IshvarAtmatvaM pratipipAdayiShitam iti | evaM ca sati advaiteshvarasya apahatapApmatvAdiguNatA viparItaguNatA tu itarasya -- mithyeti vyavatiShThate | yad apyuktam -- adhikAryabhAvaH pratyakShAdivirodhashceti, tad apyasat, prAkprabodhAt saMsAritvAbhyupagamAt, tadviShayatvAcca pratyakShAdivyavahArasya | yatra tu asya sarvam AtmaivAbhUt tat kena kaM pashyet [bR^i.A.u. 4.5.15] ityAdinA hi prabodhe pratyakShAdyabhAvaM darshayati | pratyakShAdyabhAve shruter apyabhAvaprasaN^ga iti cet, na, iShTatvAt | atra pitApitA bhavati ityupakramya, vedA avedAH iti vacanAt iShyata eva asmAbhiH shruter apyabhAvaH prabodhe | kasya punar ayam aprabodha iti cet, yaH tvaM pR^icchasi tasya te -- iti vadAmaH | nanu aham Ishvara evoktaH shrutyA -- yadyevaM pratibuddho.asi, nAsti kasyacid aprabodhaH | yo.api doShashcodyate -- kaishcid avidyayA kila AtmanaH sadvitIyatvAt advaitAnupapattiH iti, so.api etena pratyuktaH | tasmAd Atmetyeva Ishvare mano dadhIta ||3||

 -- o)0(o -- 
3. pratIkAdhikaraNam

|| 4.1.4 || 

mano brahmetyupAsIta ityadhyAtmam athAdhidaivatam AkAsho brahmeti tathA Adityo brahmetyAdeshaH sa yo nAma brahmetyupAste ityevamAdiShu pratIkopAsaneShu saMshayaH -- kiM teShvapi AtmagrahaH kartavyaH, na veti | kiM tAvat prAptam? teShvapi Atmagraha eva yuktaH kartum | kasmAt? brahmaNaH shrutiShu Atmatvena prasiddhatvAt, pratIkAnAm api brahmavikAratvAd brahmatve sati AtmatvopapatteH ityevaM prApte, brUmaH -- 

na pratIke na hi saH || 

na pratIkeShvatmamatiM badhnIyAt | na hi sa upAsakaH pratIkAni vyastAni Atmatvena Akalayet | yat punaH brahmavikAratvAt pratIkAnAM brahmatvaM tatashca Atmatvam iti, tad asat, pratIkAbhAvaprasaN^gAt | vikArasvarUpopamardena hi nAmAdijAtasya brahmatvam eva AshritaM bhavati | svarUpopamarde ca nAmAdInAM kutaH pratIkatvam Atmagraho vA? na ca brahmaNa AtmatvAt, brahmadR^iShTyopadesheShvatmadR^iShTiH kalpyA, kartR^itvAdyanirAkaraNAt | kartR^itvAd isarvasaMsAradharmanirAkaraNena hi brahmaNa AtmatvopadeshaH | tadanirAkaraNena ca upAsanavidhAnam | atashca upAsakasya pratIkaiH samatvAt Atmagraho nopapadyate | na hi rucakasvastikayoH itaretarAtmatvam asti | suvarNAtmaneva tu brahmAtmanA ekatve pratIkAbhAvaprasaN^gam avocAma | ato na pratIkeShvatmadR^iShTiH kriyate ||4||

 -- o)0(o -- 
4. brahmadR^iShTyadhikaraNam

|| 4.1.5 || 

teShv eva udAharaNeShvanyaH saMshayaH -- kim AdityAdidR^iShTayo brahmaNyadhyasitavyAH, kiM vA brahmadR^iShTir AdityAdiShviti | kutaH saMshayaH? sAmAnAdhikaraNye kAraNAnavadhAraNAt | atra hi brahmashabdasya AdityAdishabdaiH sAmAnAdhikaraNyam upalabhyate, Adityo brahma prANo brahma vidyud brahma ityAdisamAnavibhaktinirdeshAt | na cAtra AJNjasaM sAmAnAdhikaraNyam avakalpate, arthAntaravacanatvAd brahmAdityAdishabdAnAm | na hi bhavati -- gaur ashva iti sAmAnAdhikaraNyam | 

nanu prakR^itivikArabhAvAd brahmAdityAdInAM mR^iccharAvAdivat sAmAnAdhikaraNyaM syAt -- netyucyate | vikArapravilayo hyevaM prakR^itisAmAnAdhikaraNyAt syAt, tatashca pratIkAbhAvaprasaN^gam avocAma | paramAtmavAkyaM cedaM tadAnIM syAt, tatashcopAsanAdhikAro bAdhyeta, parimitavikAropAdAnaM ca vyartham | tasmAt brAhmaNo.agnir veshvAnaraH ityAdivat anyataratrAnyataradR^iShTyAdhyAse sati, kva kiM dR^iShTir adhyasyatAm iti saMshayaH | tatra aniyamaH, niyamakAriNaH shAstrasyAbhAvAd ityevaM prAptam | athavA AdityAdidR^iShTaya eva brahmaNi kartavyA ityevaM prAptam | evaM hi AdityAdidR^iShTibhiH brahma upAsitaM bhavati | brahmopAsanaM ca phalavad iti shAstramaryAdA | tasmAt na brahmadR^iShTir AdityAdiShvityevaM prApte -- 

brahmadR^iShTir utkarShAt ||

brUmaH -- brahmadR^iShTir eva AdityAdiShu syAd iti | kasmAt? utkarShAt | evam utkarSheNa AdityAdayo dR^iShTA bhavanti, utkR^iShTadR^iShTeH teShvadhyAsAt | tathA ca laukiko nyAyo.anugato bhavati | utkR^iShTadR^iShTir hi nikR^iShTo.adhyasitavyeti laukiko nyAyaH -- yathA rAjadR^iShTiH kShattari | sa ca anusartavyaH viparyaye pratyavAyaprasaN^gAt | na hi kShattR^idR^iShTiparigR^ihIto rAjA nikarShaM nIyamAnaH shreyase syAt | 

nanu shAstraprAmANyAd anAshaN^kanIyo.atra pratyavAyaprasaN^gaH, na ca laukikena nyAyena shAstrIyA dR^iShTir niyantuM yuktA, ityatrocyate -- nirdhArite shAstrArthe etad evaM syAt | sandigdhe tu tasmin, tannirNayaM prati laukiko.api nyAya AshrIyamANo na virudhyate | tena ca utkR^iShTadR^iShTyAdhyAse shAstrArthe.avadhAryamANe, nikR^iShTadR^iShTim adhyasyan pratyaveyAd iti shliShyate | prAthamyAcca AdityAdishabdAnAM mukhyArthatvam avirodhAt grahItavyam | taiH svArthavR^ittibhir avaruddhAyAM buddhau, pashcAd avatarato brahmashabdasya mukhyayA vR^ittyA sAmAnAdhikaraNyAsambhavAt, brahmadR^iShTividhAnArthataiva avatiShThate | itiparatvAd api brahmashabdasya eSha evArtho nyAyyaH | tathA hi -- brahmetyAdeshaH brahmetyupAsIta brahmetyupAste iti ca sarvatretiparaM brahmashabdam uccArayati, shuddhAMH tu AdityAdishabdAn | tatashca yathA shuktikAM rajatam iti pratyetItyatra, shuktivacana eva shuktikAshabdaH, rajatashabdaH tu rajatapratItilakShaNArthaH -- pratyetyeva hi kevalaM rajatam iti, na tu tatra rajatam asti -- evam atrApi AdityAdIn brahmeti pratIyAd iti gamyate | vAkyasheSho.api ca dvitIyAnirdeshena AdityAdIn eva upAstikriyayA vyApyamAnAn darshayati -- sa ya etad evaM vidvAn AdityaM brahmetyupAste yo vAcaM brahmetyupAste yaH saN^kalpaM brahmetyupAste iti ca | yat tUktam -- brahmopAsanam evAtra AdaraNIyaM phalavattvAyeti, tad ayuktam, uktena nyAyena AdityAdInAm eva upAsyatvAvagamAt | phalaM tu atithyAdyupAsana iva AdityAdyupAsane.api brahmaiva dAsyati, sarvAdhyakShatvAt | varNitaM caitat phalam ata upapatteH [ve.sU. 3.2.38] ityatra | IdR^ishaM ca atra brahmaNa upAsyatvam, yat pratIkeShu taddR^iShTyAdhyAropaNam -- pratimAdiShviva viShNvAdInAm ||5||

  -- o)0(o -- 
AdityAdimatyadhikaraNam

 || 4.1.6 ||

ya evAsau tapati tam udgItham upAsIta [chA.u. 1.3.1], lokeShu paJNcavidhaM sAmopAsIta [chA.u. 2.2.1], vAci saptavidhaM sAmopAsIta [chA.u. 2.8.1], iyam eva rg agniH sAma [chA.u. 1.6.1] ityevamAdiShu aN^gAvabaddheShu upAsaneShu saMshayaH -- kim AdityAdiShu udgIthAdidR^iShTayo vidhIyante, kiM vA udgIthAdiShv eva AdityAdidR^iShTaya iti | tatra aniyamaH, niyamakAraNAbhAvAt -- iti prAptam | na hi atra brahmaNa iva kasyacid utkarShavisheSho.avadhAryate | brahma hi samastajagatkAraNatvAt apahatapApmatvAdiguNayogAcca AdityAdibhya utkR^iShTam iti shakyam avadhArayitum | na tu AdityodgIthAdInAM vikAratvAvisheShAt kiMcid utkarShavisheShAvadhAraNe kAraNam asti |

athavA niyamenaiva udgIthAdimataya AdityAdiShu adhyasyeran | kasmAt? karmAtmakatvAd udgIthAdInAm, karmaNashca phalaprAptiprasiddhiH | udgIthAdimatibhir upAsyamAnA AdityAdayaH karmAtmakAH santaH phalahetavo bhaviShyanti | tathA ca iyam eva rg agniH sAma [chA.u. 1.6.1] ityatra tad etad etasyAm R^icyadhyUDhaM sAma iti R^ikshabdena pR^ithivIM nirdishati, sAmashabdenAgnim | tacca pR^ithivyagnyoH R^iksAmadR^iShTicikIrShAyAm avakalpate, na R^iksAmayoH pR^ithivyagnidR^iShTicikIrShAyAm | kShattari hi rAjadR^iShTikaraNAt rAjashabda upacaryate, na rAjani kShattR^ishabdaH | api ca lokeShu paJNcavidhaM sAmopAsIta iti adhikaraNanirdeshAt lokeShu sAma adhyasitavyam iti pratIyate | etad gAyatraM prANeShu protam iti ca etad eva darshayati | prathamanirdiShTeShu ca AdityAdiShu caramanirdiShTaM brahmAdhyastam -- Adityo brahmetyAdeshaH ityAdiShu | prathamanirdiShTashca pR^ithivyAdayaH, caramanirdiShTA hiMkArAdayaH -- pR^ithivI hiMkAraH ityAdishrutiShu | ato.anaN^geShvadityAdiShu aN^gam atikShepa ityevaM prApten, brUmaH -- 

AdityAdimatayashcAN^ga upapatteH || 

AdityAdimataya eva aN^geShu udgIthAdiShu kShipyeran | kutaH? upapatteH | upapadyate hyevam apUrvasaMnikarShAt AdityAdimatibhiH saMskriyamANeShu udgIthAdiShu karmasamR^iddhiH | yad eva vidyayA karoti shraddhayopaniShadA tad eva vIryavattaraM bhavati iti ca vidyAyAH karmasamR^iddhihetutvaM darshayati | bhavatu karmasamR^iddhiphaleShv evam | svatantraphaleShu tu katham ya etad evaM vidvAMl lokeShu paJNcavidhaM sAmopAste ityAdiShu? teShvapi adhikR^itAdhikArAt prakR^itApUrvasaMnikarSheNaiva phalakalpanA yuktA, godohanAdiniyamavat | phalAtmakatvAcca AdityAdInAm udgIthAdibhyaH karmAtmakebhyaH utkarShopapattiH | AdityAdiprAptilakShaNaM hi karmaphalaM shiShyate shrutiShu | api ca om ityetad akSharam udgItham upAsIta [chA.u. 1.4.1] khalv etasyaivAkSharasyopavyAkhyAnaM bhavati iti ca udgItham eva upAsyatvenopakramya, AdityAdimatIr vidadhAti | yat tUktam -- udgIthAdimatibhir upAsyamAnA AdityAdayaH karmabhUyaM bhUtvA phalaM kariShyantIti, tad ayuktam, svayam evopAsanasya karmatvAt phalavattvopapatteH AdityAdibhAvenApi ca dR^ishyamAnAnAm udgIthAdInAM karmAtmakatvAnapAyAt | tad etad etasyAm R^icyadhyUDhaM sAma iti tu lAkShaNika eva pR^ithivyagnyoH R^iksAmashabdaprayogaH | lakShaNA ca yathAsambhavaM saMnikR^iShTena viprakR^iShTena vA svArthasambandhena pravartate | tatra yadyapi R^iksAmayoH pR^ithivyagnidR^iShTicikIrShA, tathApi prasiddhayoH R^iksAmayor bhedenAnukIrtanAt, pR^ithivyagnyoshca saMnidhAnAt, tayor eva eSha R^iksAmashabdaprayogaH R^iksAmasambandhAd iti nishcIyate | kShattR^ishabdo.api hi kutashcit kAraNAd rAjAnam upasarpan na nivArayituM pAryate | iyam evarka iti ca yathAkSharanyAsam R^ica eva pR^ithivItvam avadhArayati | pR^ithivyA hi R^iktve.avadhAryamANe -- iyam R^ig evetyakSharanyAsaH syAt | ya evaM vidvAn sAma gAyati iti ca aN^gAshrayam avavij~nAnam upasaMharati, na pR^ithivyAdyAshrayam | tathA lokeShu paJNcavidhaM sAmopAsIta iti yadyapi saptamInirdiShTA lokAH, tathApi sAmnyeva te adhyasyeran, dvitIyAnirdeshena sAmna upAsyatvAvagamAt | sAmani hi lokeShvadhyasyamAneShu sAma lokAtmanopAsitaM bhavati, anyathA punaH lokAH sAmAtmanopAsitAH syuH | etena etad gAyatraM prANeShu protam ityAdi vyAkhyAtam | yatrApi tulyo dvitIyAnirdesho.atha khalvamum AdityaM saptavidhaM sAmopAsIta iti, tatrApi -- samastasya khalu sAmna upAsanaM sAdhu itiM tu paJNcavidhasya atha saptavidhasya iti ca sAmna eva upAsyatvopakramAt -- tasminn eva AdityAdyadhyAsaH | etasmAd eva ca sAmna upAsyatvAvagamAt pR^ithivI hiMkAraH ityAdi nirdeshaviparyaye.api hiMkArAdiShv eva pR^ithivyAdidR^iShTiH | tasmAt anaN^gAshrayA AdityAdimatayo.aN^geShUdgIthAdiShu kShipyerann iti siddham ||6||

  -- o)0(o -- 
AsInAdhikaraNam

|| 4.1.7 ||

AsInaH sambhavAt ||

karmAN^gasambarAShu tAvat upAsaneShu karmatantratvAt na AsanAdicintA | nApi samyagdarshane, vastutantratvAd vij~nAnasya | itareShu tu upAsaneShu kim aniyamena tiShThan AsInaH shayAno vA pravarteta uta niyamena AsIna eveti cintayati | tatra mAnasatvAvad upAsanasya aniyamaH sharIrasthiteH ityevaM prApte, bravIti -- AsIna evopAsIteti | kutaH? sambhavAt | upAsanaM nAma samAnapratyayapravAhakaraNam | na ca tat gacchato dhAvato vA 
sambhavati, gatyAdInAM cittavikShepakaratvAt | tiShThato.api dehadhAraNe vyApR^itaM mano na sUkShmavastunirIkShaNakShamaM bhavati | shayAnasyApi akasmAd eva nidrayA abhibhUyate | AsInasya tu evaMjAtIyako bhUyAn doShaH suparihara iti sambhavati tasyopAsanam ||7||

|| 4.1.8 || 

dhyAnAcca ||

api ca dhyAyatyartha eShaH, yat samAnapratyayapravAhakaraNam | dhyAyatishca prashithilAN^gaceShTeShu pratiShThitadR^iShTiShu ekaviShayAkShiptacitteShu upacaryamANo dR^ishyate -- dhyAyati bakaH, dhyAyati proShitabandhuH iti | AsInashca anAyAso bhavati | tasmAd api AsInakarmopAsanam ||8||

|| 4.1.9 || 

acalatvaM cApekShya ||

api ca dhyAyatIva pR^ithivI ityatra pR^ithivyAdiShu acalatvam evApekShya dhyAyativAdo bhavati | tacca liN^gam upAsanasya AsInakarmatve ||9||

|| 4.1.10 ||

smaranti ca ||

smarantyapi ca shiShTA upAsanAN^gatvena Asanam -- shucau deshe pratiShThApya sthiram Asanam AtmanaH ityAdinA | ata eva paskAdInAm AsanavisheShANAm upadesho yogashAstre ||10||

  -- o)0(o -- 

ekAgratAdhikaraNam 

|| 4.1.11 ||

yatraikAgratA tatrAvisheShAt ||

digdeshakAleShu saMshayaH -- kim asti kashcin niyamaH, nAsti veti | prAyeNa vaidikeShvarambheShu digAdiniyamadarshanAt, syAd ihApi kashcin niyama iti yasya matiH, taM pratyAha -- digdeshakAleShu arthalakShaNa eva niyamaH | yatraiva asya dishi deshe kAle vA manasaH saukaryeNaikAgratA bhavati, tatraivopAsIta, prAcIdikpUrvAhNaprAcInapravaNAdivat visheShAshravaNAt, ekAgratAyA iShTAyAH sarvatrAvisheShAt | 

nanu visheSham api kecid Amananti -- same shucau sharkarAvahnivAlukAvivarjite shabdajalAshrayAdibhiH | mano.anukUle na tu cakShuHpIDAne guhAnivAtAshrayaNe prayojayet iti yatheti -- ucyate | satyam asti evaMjAtIyako niyamaH | sati tv etasmin, tadgateShu visheSheShvaniyama iti suhR^id bhUtvA AcArya AcaShTe | mano.anukUle iti caiShA shrutiH yatraikAgratA tatraiva ityetad eva darshayati ||11||

  -- o)0(o -- 
AprAyaNAdhikaraNam

|| 4.1.12 || 

AprAyaNAt tatrApi hi dR^iShTAm ||

AvR^ittiH sarvopAsaneShvadartavyeti sthitam Adye.adhikaraNe | tatra yAni tAvat samyagdarshanArthAnyupAsanAni, tAni avaghAtAdivat kAryaparyavasAnAnIti j~nAtam eva eShAm AvR^ittiM parimANam | na hi samyagdarshane kArye niShpanne yatnAntaraM kiMcicchAsituM shakyam, aniyojyabrahmAtmatvapratipatteH shAstrasyAviShayatvAt | yAni punar abhyudayaphalAni, teShv eShA cintA -- kiM kiyantaMcit kAlaM pratyayam Avartya uparamet, uta yAvajjIvam Avartayed iti | kiM tAvat prAptam? kiyantaMcit kAlaM pratyayam abhyasya utsR^ijet, AvR^ittivishiShTasyopAsanashabdArthasya kR^itatvAd ityevaM prApte, brUmaH -- A prAyaNAd eva Avartayet pratyayam, antyapratyayavashAd adR^iShTaphalaprApteH | karmANyapi hi janmAntaropabhogyaM phalam ArabhamANAni tadanurUpaM bhAvanAvij~nAnaM prAyaNakAle AkShipanti -- savij~nAno bhavati savij~nAnam evAnvavakrAmati yaccittaH tenaiSha prANamAyAti prANaH tejasA yuktaH sahAtmanA yathAsaN^kalpitaM lokaM nayati iti caivamAdishrutibhyaH | tR^iNajalUkAnidarshanAcca | pratyayAH tv ete svarUpAnuvR^ittiM muktvA kim anyat prAyaNakAlabhAvi bhAvanAvij~nAnam apekSheran | tasmAt ye pratipattavyaphalabhAvanAtmakAH pratyayAH, teShu A prAyaNAt AvR^ittiH | tathA ca shrutiH -- sa yAvat kratur ayam asmAl lokAt praiti iti prAyaNakAle.api pratyayAnuvR^ittiM darshayati | smR^itir api -- 

yaM yaM vApi smaran bhAvaM tyajatyante kalevaram | 
taM tam evaiti kaunteya sadA tadbhAvabhAvitaH || iti |
prayANakAle manasAcalena iti ca | 

so.antavelAyAm etat trayaM pratipadyeta iti ca maraNavelAyAm api kartavyasheShaM shrAvayati ||12||

 -- o)0(o -- 
tadadhigamAdhikaraNam

|| 4.1.13 || 

gataH tR^itIyasheShaH | athedAnIM brahmavidyAphalaM prati cintA pratAyate | brahmAdhigame sati tadviparItaphalaM duritaM kShIyate, na kShIyate veti saMshayaH | kiM tAvat prAptam? phalArthatvAt karmaNaH phalam adattvA na sambhAvyate kShayaH | phaladAyinI hi asya shaktiH shrutyA samadhigatA | yadi tat antareNaiva phalopabhogam apavR^ijyeta, shrutiH kadarthitA syAt | smaranti ca -- na hi karma kShIyate iti | 

nanv evaM sati prAyashcittopadesho.anarthakaH prApnoti -- naiSha doShaH, prAyashcittAnAM naimittikatvopapatteH gR^ihadAheShTyAdivat | api ca prAyashcittAnAM doShasaMyogena vidhAnAd bhaved api doShakShapaNArthatA | na tv evaM brahmavidyAyAM vidhAnam asti | 

nanvanabhyupagamyamAne brahmavidaH karmakShaye tatphalasyAvashyabhoktavyatvAd anirmokShaH syAt -- netyucyate | deshakAlanimittApekSho mokShaH karmaphalavat bhaviShyati | tasmAn na brahmAdhigame duritanivR^ittiH ityevaM prApte -- 

tadadhigama uttarapUrvAghayor ashleShavinAshau tadvyapadeshAt || 

brUmaH -- tadadhigame brahmAdhigame sati uttarapUrvayor aghayor ashleShavinAshau bhavataH -- uttarasya ashleShaH, pUrvasya vinAshaH | kasmAt? tadvyapadeshAt | tathA hi brahmavidyAprakriyAyAM sambhAvyamAnasambandhasya AgAmino duritasyAnabhisambandhaM viduSho vyapadishati -- yathA puShkarapalAsha Apo na shliShyanta evam evaMvidi pApaM karma na shliShyate iti | tathA vinAsham api pUrvopacitasya duritasya vyapadishati -- tad yatheShIkAtUlam agnau protaM pradUyetaivaM hAsya sarve pApmAnaH pradUyante iti | ayam aparaH karmakShayavyapadesho bhavati -- 

bhidyate hR^idayagrandhishchidyante sarvasaMshayAH | 
kShIyante cAsya karmANi tasmin dR^iShTe parAvare || [mu.u. 2.2.8] iti |
