yad uktam -- anupabhuktaphalasya karmaNaH kShayakalpanAyAM shAstraM kadarthitaM syAd iti, naiSha doShaH | na hi vayaM karmaNaH phaladAyinIM shaktim avajAnImahe | vidyata eva sA | sA tu vidyAdinA kAraNAntareNa pratibadhyata iti vadAmaH | shaktisadbhAvamAtre ca shAstraM vyApriyate, na pratibandhApratibandhayor api | na hi karma kShIyate ityetad api smaraNam autsargikam -- na hi bhogAd R^ite karma kShIyate tadarthatvAd iti | iShyata eva tu prAyashcittAdinA tasya kShayaH -- sarvaM pApmAnaM tarati, tarati brahmahatyAm, yo.ashvamedhena yajate, ya u cainam evaM veda ityAdi shrutismR^itibhyaH | yat tUktam -- naimittikAni prAyashcittAni bhaviShyantIti, tad asat, doShasaMyogena codyamAnAnAm eShAM doShanirghAtaphalasambhave phalAntarakalpanAnupapatteH | 

yat punar etad uktam -- na prAyashcittavat doShakShayoddeshena vidyAvidhAnam astIti | atra brUmaH -- saguNAsu tAvad vidyAsu vidyata eva vidhAnam, tAsu ca vAkyasheShe aishvaryaprAptiH pApanivR^ittishca vidyAvata ucyate, tayoshcAvivakShAkAraNaM nAsti -- ityataH pApmaprahANapUrvakaishvaryaprAptiH tAsAM phalam iti nishcIyate | nirguNAyAM tu vidyAyAM yadyapi vidhAnaM nAsti, tathApi akartrAtmatvabodhAt karmapradAhasiddhiH | ashleSha iti ca AgAmiShu karmasu kartR^itvam eva na pratipadyate brahmavid iti darshayati | atikrAnteShu tu yadyapi mithyAj~nAnAt kartR^itvaM pratipeda iva, tathApi vidyAsAmarthyAn mithyAj~nAnanivR^itteH tAnyapi pravilIyanta ityAha -- vinAsha iti | pUrvasiddhakartR^itvabhoktR^itvaviparItaM hi triShvapi kAleShvakartR^itvAbhoktR^itvasvarUpaM brahmAham asmi, netaH pUrvam api kartA bhoktA vA aham Asam, nedAnIm, nApi bhaviShyatkAle -- iti brahmavid avagacchati | evam eva ca mokSha upapadyate | anyathA hi anAdikAlapravR^ittAnAM karmaNAM kShayAbhAve mokShAbhAvaH syAt | na ca deshakAlanimittApekSho mokShaH karmaphalavat bhavitum arhati | anityatvaprasaN^gAt, parokShatvAnupapatteshca j~nAnaphalasya | tasmAt brahmAdhigame duritakShaya iti sthitam ||13||

  -- o)0(o -- 

itarAsaMshleShAdhikaraNam

|| 4.1.14 || 

itarasyApyevam asaMshleShaH pAte tu ||

pUrvasminn adhikaraNe bandhahetor aghasya svAbhAvikasya ashleShavinAshau j~nAnanimittau shAstravyapadeshAn nirUpitau | dharmasya punaH shAstrIyatvAt shAstrIyeNa j~nAnena avirodha ityAshaN^kya tannirAkaraNAya pUrvAdhikaraNanyAyAtideshaH kriyate -- itarasyApi puNyasya karmaNaH evam aghavat asaMshleSho vinAshashca j~nAnavato bhavataH | kutaH? tasyApi 
svaphalahetutvena j~nAnaphalapratibandhitvaprasaN^gAt, ubhe u haivaiSha ete tarati ityAdi shrutiShu ca duShkR^itavat sukR^itasyApi praNAshavyapadeshAt, akartrAtmatvabodhanimittasya ca karmakShayasya sukR^itaduShkR^itayoH tulyatvAt, kShIyante cAsya karmANi iti ca avisheShashruteH | yatrApi kevala eva pApmashabdaH paThyate, tatrApi tenaiva puNyam apyAkalitam iti draShTavyam, j~nAnApekShayA nikR^iShTaphalatvAt | asti ca shrutau puNye.api pApmashabdaH -- nainaM setum ahorAtre tarataH ityatra saha duShkR^itena sukR^itam apyanukramya, sarve pApmAno.ato nivartante ityavisheSheNaiva prakR^ite puNye pApmashabdaprayogAt | pAte tu iti tushabdo.avadhAraNArthaH | evaM dharmAdharmayor bandhahetvoH vidyAsAmarthyAd ashleShavinAshasiddhiH avashyambhAvinI viduShaH sharIrapAte muktiH ityavadhArayati ||14||

 -- o)0(o -- 
anArabdhAdhikaraNam

|| 4.1.15 || 

anArabdhakArye eva tu pUrve tadavadheH ||

pUrvayor adhikaraNayor j~nAnanimittaH sukR^itaduShkR^itayor vinAsho.avadhAritaH | sa kim avisheSheNa ArabdhakAryayor anArabdhakAryayoshca bhavati, uta visheSheNAnArabdhakAryayor eveti vicAryate | tatra ubhe u haivaiSha ete tarati ityevamAdishrutiShvavisheShashravaNAd avisheSheNaiva kShaya ityevaM prApte, pratyAha -- anArabdhakArye eva tviti | apravR^ittaphale eva pUrve janmAntarasaJNcite, asminn api ca janmani prAgj~nAnotpatteH saJNcite, sukR^itaduShkR^ite j~nAnAdhigamAt kShIyete | na tu ArabdhakArye sAmibhuktaphale, yAbhyAm etat brahmaj~nAnAyatanaM janma nirmitam | kuta etat? tasya tAvad eva ciraM yAvan na vimokShye.atha sampatsye [chA.u. 6.14.2] iti sharIrapAtAvadhikaraNAt kShemaprApteH | itarathA hi j~nAnAd asheShakarmakShaye sati sthitihetvabhAvAt j~nAnaprAptyanantaram eva kShemam ashnuvIta | tatra sharIrapAtapratIkShAM nAcakShIta | 

nanu vastubalenaiva ayam akartrAtmAvabodhaH karmANi kShapayan kathaM kAnicit kShapayet kAniciccopekSheta? na hi samAne.agnibIjasamparke, keShAMcid bIjashaktiH kShIyate, keShAMcin na kShIyate -- iti shakyam aN^gIkartum iti | ucyate -- na tAvad anAshritya ArabdhakAryaM karmAshayaM j~nAnotpattir upapadyate | Ashrite ca tasmin kulAlacakravat pravR^ittavegasya antarAle pratibandhAsambhavAt bhavati vegakShayapratipAlanam | akartrAtmabodho.api hi mithyAj~nAnabAdhanena karmANyucchinatti | bAdhitam api tu mithyAj~nAnaM dvicandraj~nAnavat saMskAravashAt kaMcit kAlam anuvartata eva | api ca naivAtra vivaditavyam -- brahmavidA kaMcit kAlaM sharIraM dhrIyate na vA dhrIyata iti | kathaM hi ekasya svahR^idayapratyayaM brahmavedanaM dehadhAraNaM cApareNa pratikSheptuM shakyeta? shrutismR^itiShu ca sthitapraj~nalakShaNanirdeshena etad eva nir ucyate | tasmAd anArabdhakAryayor eva sukR^itaduShkR^itayor vidyAsAmarthyAtkShaya iti nirNayaH ||15||

  -- o)0(o -- 
 agnihotrAdyadhikaraNam

|| 4.1.16 || 

agnihotrAdi tu tatkAryAyaiva taddarshanAt ||
 
puNyasyApyashleShavinAshayor aghanyAyo.atidiShTAH | so.atideshaH sarvapuNyaviShaya ityAshaN^kya prativakti -- agnihotrAdi tviti | tushabda AshaN^kAm apanudati | yan nityaM karma vaidikam agnihotrAdi, tattatkAryAyaiva bhavati | j~nAnasya yat kAryaM tad eva asyApi kAryam ityarthaH | kutaH? tam etaM vedAnuvacanena brAhmaNA vividiShanti yaj~nena dAnena [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.22] ityAdi darshanAt | 

nanu j~nAnakarmaNor vilakShaNakAryatvAt kAryaikatvAnupapattiH -- naiSha doShaH, jvaramaraNakAryayor api dadhiviShayoH guDamantrasaMyuktayoH tR^iptipuShTikAryadarshanAt, tadvat karmaNo.api j~nAnasaMyuktasya mokShakAryopapatteH | 

nanu anArabhyo mokShaH, katham asya karmakAryatvam ucyate? naiSha doShaH, ArAd upakArakatvAt karmaNaH | j~nAnasyaiva hi prApakaM sat karma praNADyA mokShakAraNam ityupacaryate | ata eva ca atikrAntaviShayam etatkAryaikatvAbhidhAnam | na hi brahmavida AgAmyagnihotrAdi sambhavati, aniyojyabrahmAtmatvapratipatteH shAstrasyAviShayatvAt | saguNAsu tu vidyAsu kartR^itvAnativR^itteH sambhavati AgAmyapi agnihotrAdi | tasyApi nirabhisandhinaH kAryAntarAbhAvAd vidyAsaN^gatyupapattiH ||16|| 

|| 4.1.17 || 

kiMviShayaM punaH idam ashleShavinAshavacanam, kiMviShayaM vA ado viniyogavacanam ekeShAM shAkhinAm -- tasya putrA dAyam upayanti suhR^idaH sAdhukR^ityAM dviShantaH pApakR^ityAm iti -- ata uttaraM paThati -- 

ato.anyA.api hyekeShAm ubhayoH || 

ato.agnihotrAder nityAt karmaNo.anyApi hyasti sAdhukR^ityA, yA phalam abhisandhAya kriyate, tasyA eSha viniyoga uktaH ekeShAM shAkhinAm -- suhR^idaH sAdhukR^ityAm upayanti iti | tasyA eva ca idam aghavad ashleShavinAshanirUpaNam -- itarasyApyevam asaMshleSha iti | tathAjAtIyakasya kAmyasya karmaNo vidyAM pratyanupakArakatve sampratipattiH ubhayor api jaiminibAdarAyaNayor AcAryayoH ||17||

 -- o)0(o -- 
vidyAj~nAnasAdhanatvAdhikaraNam 

|| 4.1.18 ||

samadhigatam etadanantarAdhikaraNe -- nityam agnihotrAdikaM karma mumukShuNA mokShaprayojanoddeshena kR^itam upAttaduritakShayahetudvAreNa sattvashuddhikAraNatAM pratipadyamAnaM mokShaprayojanabrahmAdhigamanimittatvena brahmavidyayA saha ekakAryaM bhavatIti | tatra agnihotrAdi karmAN^gavyapAshrayavidyAsaMyuktaM kevalaM cAsti -- ya evaM vidvAn yajati ya evaM vidvAJNjuhoti ya evaM vidvAJNshaMsati ya evaM vidvAn gAyati tasmAd evaMvidam eva brahmANaM kurvIta tenobhau kuruto yashcaitad evaM veda yashca na veda ityAdivacanebhyo vidyAsaMyuktam asti, kevalam apyasti | 

tatredaM vicAryate -- kiM vidyAsaMyuktam eva agnihotrAdikaM karma mumukShor vidyAhetutvena tayA saha ekakAryatvaM pratipadyate, na kevalam | uta vidyAsaMyuktaM kevalaM ca avisheSheNeti | kutaH saMshayaH? tam etam AtmAnaM yaj~nena vividiShanti iti yaj~nAdInAm avisheSheNa AtmavedanAN^gatvena shravaNAt, vidyAsaMyuktasya ca agnihotrAder vishiShTatvAvagamAt | kiM tAvat prAptam? vidyAsaMyuktam eva karma agnihotrAdi AtmavidyAsheShatvaM pratipadyate, na vidyAhInam, vidyopetasya vishiShTatvAvagamAd vidyAvihInAt -- yad ahar eva juhoti tad ahaH punar mR^ityum apajayatyevaM vidvAn ityAdishrutibhyaH, buddhyA yukto yayA pArtha karmabandhaM prahAsyasi dUreNa hyavaraM karma buddhiyogAd dhanaMjaya ityAdismR^itibhyashca ityevaM prApte, pratipAdyate -- 

yad eva vidyayeti hi ||

satyam etat -- vidyAsaMyuktaM karma agnihotrAdikaM vidyAvihInAt karmaNo.agnihotrAd vishiShTam, vidvAn iva brAhmaNo vidyAvihInAd brAhmaNAt | tathApi nAtyantam anapekShaM vidyAvihInaM karma agnihotrAdikam | kasmAt? tam etam AtmAnaM yaj~nena vividiShanti ityavisheSheNa agnihotrAder vidyAhetutvena shrutatvAt | 

nanu vidyAsaMyuktasya agnihotrAder vidyAvihInAd vishiShTatvAvagamAt vidyAvihInam agnihotrAdi AtmavidyAhetutvenAnapekSham eveti yuktam -- naitad evam | vidyAsahAyasyAgnihotrAder vidyAnimittena sAmarthyAtishayena yogAt Atmaj~nAnaM prati kashcit kAraNatvAt ishayo bhaviShyati, na tathA vidyAvihInasya -- iti yuktaM kalpayitum | na tu yaj~nena vividiShanti ityatrAvisheSheNAtmaj~nAnAN^gatvena shrutasyAgnihotrAder anaN^gatvaM shakyam abhyupagantum | tathA hi shrutiH -- yad eva vidyayA karoti shraddhayopaniShadA tad eva vIryavattaraM bhavati iti vidyAsaMyuktasya karmaNo.agnihotrAder vIryavattaratvAbhidhAnena svakAryaM prati kaMcid atishayaM bruvANA vidyAvihInasya tasyaiva tatprayojanaM prati vIryavattvaM darshayati | karmaNashca vIryavattvaM tat, yat svaprayojanasAdhanasahatvam | tasmAd vidyAsaMyuktaM nityam agnihotrAdi vidyAvihInaM ca ubhayam api mumukShuNA mokShaprayojanoddeshena iha janmani janmAntare ca prAgj~nAnotpatteH kR^itaM yataH, tad yathAsAmarthyaM brahmAdhigamapratibandhakAraNopAttaduritakShayahetutvadvAreNa brahmAdhigamakAraNatvaM pratipadyamAnaM shravaNamananashraddhAtAtparyAdyantaraN^gakAraNApekShaM brahmavidyayA saha ekakAryaM bhavatIti sthitam ||18||

  -- o)0(o -- 
itarakShapaNAdhikaraNam

|| 4.1.19 ||

bhogena tvitare kShapayitvA sampadyate ||

anArabdhakAryayoH puNyapApayor vidyAsAmarthyAtkShaya uktaH | itare tu ArabdhakArye puNyapApe upabhogena kShapayitvA brahma sampadyate, tasya tAvad eva ciraM yAvan na vimokShye.atha sampatsye [chA.u. 6.14.2] iti, brahmaiva san brahmApyeti [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.7] iti ca evamAdishrutibhyaH | 

nanu satyapi samyagdarshane yathA prAgdehapAtAd bhedadarshanaM dvicandradarshananyAyenAnuvR^ittam, evaM pashcAd apyanuvarteta -- na, nimittAbhavAt | upabhogasheShakShapaNaM hi tatrAnuvR^ittinimittam, na ca tAdR^isham atra kiMcid asti | 

nanu aparaH karmAshayo.abhinavam upabhogam Arapsyate -- na, tasya dagdhabIjatvAt | mithyAj~nAnAvaShTAmbhaM hi karmAntaraM dehapAta upabhogAntaram Arabheta | tacca mithyAj~nAnaM samyagj~nAnena dagdham -- ityataH sAdhv etat ArabdhakAryakShaye viduShaH kaivalyam avashyaM bhavatIti ||19|| 

iti shrImatparamahaMsaparivrAjakAcAryasya shrIgovindabhagavatpUjyapAdashiShyasya
shrImacchaN^karabhagavataH kR^itau shArIrakamImAMsAsUtrabhAShye
caturthAdhyAyasya prathamaH pAdaH || 

|| 4.1 ||

  -- o)0(o -- 


 
(4.2)
|| caturtho.adhyAye dvitIyaH pAdaH || 

atra pAde utkrAntigatinirUpaNam ||

1. vAgadhikaraNam

|| 4.2.1 || 

atha aparAsu vidyAsu phalaprAptaye devayAnaM panthAnam avatArayiShyan prathamaM tAvat yathAshAstram utkrAntikramam anvAcaShTe | samAnA hi vidvat aviduShoH utkrAntiH iti vakShyati | asti prAyaNaviShayA shrutiH -- asya somya puruShasya prayato vAN^ manasi sampadyate manaH prANe prANaH tejasi tejaH parasyAM devatAyAm [chA.u. 6.8.6] iti | 

kim iha vAca eva vR^ittimatyA manasi sampattir ucyate, uta vAgvR^itteH ? iti viShayaH | tatra vAg eva tAvat manasi sampadyata iti prAptam | tathA hi shrutir anugR^ihItA bhavati | itarathA lakShaNA syAt | shrutilakShaNAviShaye ca shrutir nyAyyA, na lakShaNA | tasmAt vAca eva ayaM manasi pralaya iti | evaM prApte, brUmaH -- 

vAN^ manasi darshanAcchabdAcca ||

vAgvR^ittir manasi sampadyata iti | kathaM vAgvR^ittiH iti vyAkhyAyate, yAvatA vAN^ manasi ityeva AcAryaH paThati? satyam etat | paThiShyati tu parastAt -- avibhAgo vacanAt iti | tasmAd atra vR^ittyupashamamAtraM vivakShatIti gamyate | tattvapralayavivakShAyAM tu sarvatraiva avibhAgasAmyAt kiM paratraiva vishiMShyAt -- avibhAgaH iti | tasmAd atra vR^ittyupasaMhAravivakShA | vAgvR^ittiH pUrvam upasaMhriyate hAravivatAvavasthitAyAm ityarthaH | kasmAt? darshanAt -- dR^ishyate hi vAgvR^itteH pUrvopasaMhAro manovR^ittau vidyamAnAyAm | na tu vAca eva vR^ittimattyA manasyupasaMhAraH kenacid api draShTuM shakyate |

nanu shrutisAmarthyAt vAca evAyaM manasyapyayo yukta ityuktam -- netyAha, atatprakR^ititvAt | yasya hi yata utpattiH, tasya tatra pralayo nyAyyaH, mR^idIva sharAvasya | na ca manaso vAg utpadyata iti kiMcana pramANam asti | vR^ittyudbhavAbhibhavau tu aprakR^itisamAshrayAvapi dR^ishyete | pArthivebhyo hi indhanebhyaH taijasasyAgner vR^ittir udbhavati, apsu ca upashAmyati | kathaM tarhi asmin pakShe shabdaH -- vAN^ manasi sampadyate iti? ata Aha -- shabdAcceti | shabdo.apyasmin pakShe.avakalpate, vR^ittivR^ittimator abhedopacArAd ityarthaH ||1|||

|| 4.2.2 ||

ata eva ca sarvANyanu || 

tasmAd upashAntatejAH punar bhavam indriyair manasi sampadyamAnaiH ityatra avisheSheNa sarveShAm evendriyANAM manasi sampattiH shrUyate | tatrApi ata eva vAca iva cakShurAdInAm api savR^ittike manasyavasthite vR^ittilopadarshanAt tattvapralayAsambhavAt shabdopapatteshca vR^ittidvAreNaiva sarvANIndriyANi mano.anuvartante | sarveShAM karaNAnAM manasyupasaMhArAvisheShe sati vAcaH pR^ithaggrahaNam vAN^ manasi sampadyate ityudAharaNAnurodhena ||2||

2. mano.adhikaraNam

|| 4.2.3 ||

samadhigatam etat -- vAN^ manasi sampadyate ityatra vR^ittisampattivivakSheti | atha yad uttaraM vAkyam manaH prANe iti, kim atrApi vR^ittisampattir eva vivakShyate, uta vR^ittimat sampattiH -- iti vicikitsAyAm, vR^ittimatsampattir eva atra iti prAptam, shrutyanugrahAt | tatprakR^ititvopapatteshca | tathA hi -- annamayaM hi somya mana ApomayaH prANaH ityannayoni mana Amananti, abyoniM ca prANam | ApashcAnnam asR^ijanta iti shrutiH | atashca yan manaH prANe pralIyate, annam eva tad apsu pralIyate | annaM hi manaH, Apashca prANaH, prakR^itivikArAbhedAd iti | evaM prApte, brUmaH -- 

tanmanaH prANa uttarAt ||

tad api AgR^ihItabAhyendriyavR^itti mano vR^ittidvAreNaiva prANe pralIyata iti uttarAd vAkyAd avagantavyam | tathA hi suShupsor mumUrShoshca prANavR^ittau parispandAtmikAyAm avasthitAyAm, manovR^ittInAm upashamo dR^ishyate | na ca manasaH svarUpApyayaH prANe sambhavati | atatprakR^ititvAt | 

nanu darshitaM manasaH prANaprakR^ititvam -- naitat sAram | na hi IdR^ishena prANADikena tatprakR^ititvena manaH prANe sampattum arhati | evam api hi anne manaH sampadyeta, apsu cAnnam, apsv eva ca prANaH | na hyetasminn api pakShe prANabhAvapariNatAbhyo.adbhyo mano jAyata iti kiMcana pramANam asti | tasmAt na manasaH prANe svarUpApyayaH | vR^ittyapyaye.api tu shabdo.avakalpate, vR^ittivR^ittimator abhedopacArAt iti darshitam ||3||

 --o)0(o--
3. adhyakShAdhikaraNam

|| 4.2.4 || 

so.adhyakShe tadupagamAdibhyaH ||

sthitam etat -- yasya yato notpattiH, tasya tasmin vR^ittipralayaH, na svarUpapralaya iti | idam idAnIm prANaH tejasi ityatra cintyate -- kiM yathAshruti prANasya tejasyeva vR^ittyupasaMhAraH, kiM vA dehendriyapaJNjarAdhyakShe jIva iti | tatra shruter anatishaN^kyatvAt prANasya tejasyeva sampattiH syAt, ashrutakalpanAyA anyAyyatvAt | ityevaM prApte pratipadyate -- so.adhyakSha iti | sa prakR^itaH prANaH, adhyakShe avidyAkarmapUrvapraj~nopAdhike vij~nAnAtmani avatiShThate | tatpradhAnA prANavR^ittir bhavatItyarthaH | kutaH? tadupagamAdibhyaH -- evam evemam AtmAnam antakAle sarve prANA abhisamAyanti yatraitad UrdhvocchvAsI bhavati [bR^i.A.u. 4.3.38] iti hi shrutyantaram adhyakShopagAminaH sarvAn prANAn avisheSheNa darshayati | visheSheNa ca tam utkrAmantaM prANo.anUtkrAmati iti paJNcavR^itteH prANasya adhyakShAnugAmitAM darshayati, tadanuvR^ittitAM ca itareShAm prANam anUtkrAmantaM sarve prANA anUtkrAmanti [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.2] iti | savij~nAno bhavati iti ca adhyakShasya antarvij~nAnavattvapradarshanena tasmin apItakaraNagrAmasya prANasya avasthAnaM gamayati | 

nanu prANaH tejasi iti shrUyate | kathaM prANo.adhyakShe ityadhikAvApaH kriyate? naiSha doShaH, adhyakShapradhAnatvAd utkramaNAdivyavahArasya, shrutyantaragatasyApi ca visheShasyApekShaNIyatvAt ||4|| 

|| 4.2.5 || 

kathaM tarhi prANaH tejasi iti shrutiH ityata Aha -- 

bhUteShu tacchruteH || 

sa prANasampR^ikto.adhyakShaH tejaHsahacariteShu bhUteShu dehabIjabhUteShu sUkShmeShu avatiShThata ityavagantavyam, prANaH tejasi iti shruteH | 

nanu ca iyaM shrutiH prANasya tejasi sthitiM darshayati, na prANasampR^iktasyAdhyakShasya -- naiSha doShaH, so.adhyakShe -- iti adhyakShasyApyantarAla upasaMkhyAtatvAt | yo.api hi srughnAn mathurAM gatvA mathurAyAH pATAliputraM vrajati, so.api srughnAt pATAliputraM yAtIti shakyate vaditum | tasmAt prANaH tejasi iti prANasampR^iktasyAdhyakShasyaiva etat tejaHsahacariteShu bhUteShvavasthAnam ||5|| 

|| 4.2.6 ||

kathaM tejaHsahacariteShu bhUteShvityucyate, yAvatA ekam eva tejaH shrUyate -- prANaH tejasi iti? ata Aha -- 

naikasmin darshayato hi ||

na ekasminn eva tejasi sharIrAntaraprepsAvelAyAM jIvo.avatiShThate, kAryasya sharIrasyAnekAtmakatvadarshanAt | darshayatashca etam arthaM prashnaprativacane ApaH puruShavacasaH iti | tad vyAkhyAtam tryAtmakatvAt tu bhUyastvAt ityatra | shrutismR^itI ca etam arthaM darshayataH | shrutiH -- pR^ithvImaya Apomayo vAyumaya AkAshamayaH tejomayaH ityAdyA | smR^itir api -- 

aNvyo mAtrAvinAshinyo dashArdhAnAM tu yAH smR^itAH | 
tAbhiH sArdham idaM sarvaM sambhavatyanupUrvashaH || ityAdyA | 

nanu ca upasaMhR^iteShu vAgAdiShu karaNeShu sharIrAntaraprepsAvelAyAm kvAyaM tadA puruSho bhavati ityupakramya shrutyantaraM karmAshrayatAM nirUpayati -- tau ha yad UcatuH karma haiva tad Ucatur atha ha yat prashashaMsatuH karma haiva tat prashashaMsatuH iti | atrocyate -- tatra karmaprayuktasya grahAtigrahasaMj~nakasya indriyaviShayAtmakasya bandhanasya pravR^ittiH iti karmAshrayatoktA | iha punaH bhUtopAdAnAd dehAntarotpattiH iti bhUtAshrayatvam uktam | prashaMsAshabdAd api tatra prAdhAnyamAtraM karmaNaH pradarshitam, na tvashrayAntaraM nivAritam | tasmAd avirodhaH ||6||

AsR^ityupakramAdhikaraNam

|| 4.2.7 || 

seyam utkrAntiH kiM vidvadaviduShoH samAnA, kiM vA visheShavatI -- iti vishayAnAnAM visheShavatIti tAvat prAptam | bhUtAshrayavishiShTA hyeShA | punar bhavAya ca bhUtAnyAshrIyante | na ca viduShaH punarbhavaH sambhavati | amR^itatvaM hi vidvAn ashnute iti sthitiH | tasmAd aviduSha eva eShA utkrAntiH | 

nanu vidyAprakaraNe samAmnAnAt viduSha eva eShA bhavet -- na, svApAdivat yathAprAptAnukIrtanAt | yathA hi yatraitat puruShaH svapiti nAma [chA.u. 6.8.1] ashishiShati nAma pipAsati nAma iti ca sarvaprANisAdhAraNA eva svApAdayo.anukIrtyante vidyAprakaraNe.api pratipipAdayiShitavastupratipAdanAnuguNyena, na tu viduSho visheShavanto vidhitsyante | evam iyam api utkrAntiH mahAjanagataivAnukIrtyate, yasyAM parasyAM devatAyAM puruShasya prayataH tejaH sampadyate sa AtmA tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7] ityetat pratipAdayitum | pratiShiddhA ca eShA viduShaH -- na tasya prANA utkrAmanti [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.6] iti | tasmAt aviduSha evaiSheti || evaM prApte, brUmaH -- 

samAnA cAsR^ityupakramAd amR^itatvaM cAnupoShya ||

samAnA caiShA utkrAntiH vAN^ manasi ityAdyA vidvadaviduShoH AsR^ityupakramAt bhavitum arhati, avisheShashravaNAt | avidvAn dehabIjabhUtAni bhUtasUkShmANyAshritya karmaprayukto dehagrahaNam anubhavan saMsarati, vidvAMH tu j~nAnaprakAshitaM mokShanADIdvAram Ashrayate, tad etat AsR^ityupakramAt ityuktam | 

nanu amR^itatvaM viduShA prAptavyam, na ca taddeshAntarAyattam, tatra kuto bhUtAshrayatvaM sR^ityupakramo veti ? atrocyate -- anupoShya ca | idam adagdhvA atyantam avidyAdIn kleshAn, aparavidyAsAmarthyAt ApekShikam amR^itatvaM prepsate sambhavati tatra sR^ityupakramaH | bhUtAshrayatvaM ca -- na hi nirAshrayANAM prANAnAM gatir upapadyate | tasmAd adoShaH ||7||

 --o)0(o--
saMsAravyapadeshAdhikaraNam

|| 4.2.8 ||

tejaH parasyAM devatAyAm ityatra prakaraNasAmarthyAt tat yathA prakR^itaM tejaH sAdhyakShaM saprANaM sakaraNagrAmaM bhUtAntarasahitaM prayataH puMsaH parasyAM devatAyAM sampadyata ityetad uktaM bhavati | kIdR^ishI punaH iyaM sampattiH syAd ? iti cintyate | tatra Atyantika eva tAvat svarUpapravilaya iti prAptam, tatprakR^ititvopapatteH | sarvasya hi janimato vastujAtasya prakR^itiH parA devateti pratiShThApitam | tasmAt AtyantikI iyam avibhAgApattiH iti | evaM prApte, brUmaH -- 

tad A pIteH saMsAravyapadeshAt ||

tat tejAdi bhUtasUkShmaM shrotrAdikaraNAshrayabhUtam A pIteH A saMsAramokShAt samyagj~nAnanimittAt avatiShThate -- yonim anye prapadyante sharIratvAya dehinaH | sthANum anye.anusaMyanti yathAkarma yathAshrutam ityAdisaMsAravyapadeshAt | anyathA hi sarvaH prAyaNasamaya eva upAdhipratyastamayAd atyantaM brahma sampadyeta, tatra vidhishAstram anarthakaM syAt, vidyAshAstraM ca | mithyAj~nAnanimittashca bandho na samyagj~nAnAd R^ite visraMsitum arhati | tasmAt tatprakR^ititve.api suShuptipralayavat bIjabhAvAvasheShaiva eShA satsampattiH iti ||8||

|| 4.2.9 ||

sUkShmaM pramANatashca tathopalabdheH ||

tacca itarabhUtasahitaM tejo jIvasya asmAccharIrAt pravasata AshrayabhUtaM svarUpataH parimANatashca sUkShmaM bhavitum arhati | tathA hi nADIniShkramaNashravaNAdibhyo.asya saukShmyam upalabhyate | tatra tanutvAt saMcAropapattiH | svacchatvAcca apratighAtopapattiH | ata eva ca dehAn nirgacchat pArshvasthair nopalabhyate ||9||

|| 4.2.10 ||

nopamardenAtaH || 

ata eva ca sUkShmatvAt nAsya sthUlasya sharIrasyopamardena dAhAdinimittena itarat sUkShmaM sharIram upamR^idyate ||10||

|| 4.2.11 ||

asyaiva copapatter eSha UShmA  ||

asyaiva ca sUkShmasya sharIrasya eSha UShmA, yam etasmiJNjIvaccharIre saMsparshenoShmANaM vijAnanti | tathA hi mR^itAvasthAyAm avasthite.api dehe vidyamAneShvapi ca rUpAdiShu dehaguNeShu, na UShmA upalabhyate, jIvadavasthAyAm eva tu upalabhyate -- ityata upapadyate prasiddhasharIravyatiriktavyapAshraya eva eSha UShmeti | tathA ca shrutiH -- uShNa eva jIviShyaJNshIto mariShyan iti ||11||

6. pratiShedhAdhikaraNam 

|| 4.2.12 ||

pratiShedhAd iti cenna shArIrAt ||

 amR^itatvaM cAnupoShya ityato visheShaNAt Atyantike.amR^itatve gatyutkrAntyor abhAvo.abhyupagataH | tatrApi kenacitkAraNena utkrAntimAshaN^kya pratiShedhati -- athAkAmayamAno yo.akAmo niShkAma AptakAma AtmakAmo bhavati na tasya prANA utkrAmanti [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.6], brahmaiva san brahmApyeti [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.7] iti | ataH paravidyAviShayAt pratiShedhAt na parabrahmavido dehAt prANAnAm utkrAntirastIti cet, netyucyate, yataH shArIrAdAtmana eSha utkrAntipratiShedhaH prANAnAm, na sharIrAt | katham avagamyate? na tasmAt prANA utkrAmanti iti shAkhAntare paJNcamIprayogAt | sambandhasAmAnyaviShayA hi ShaShThI shAkhAntaragatayA paJNcamyA sambandhavisheShe vyavasthApyate | tasmAt iti ca prAdhAnyAt abhyudayaniHshreyasAdhikR^ito dehI sambadhyate, na dehaH | na tasmAd uccikramiShor jIvAt prANA apakrAmanti, sahaiva tena bhavanti -- ityarthaH | saprANasya ca pravasato bhavatyutkrAntir dehAd iti ||12|| 

|| 4.2.13 ||

evaM prApte, pratyucyate -- 
spaShTo hyekeShAm ||

naitad asti -- yad uktam, parabrahmavido.api dehAt astyutkrAntiH utkrAntipratiShedhasya dehyapAdAnatvAd iti | yato dehApAdAna eva utkrAntipratiShedha ekeShAM samAmnAtNAM spaShTa upalabhyate | tathA hi ArtabhAgaprashne -- yatrAyaM puruSho mriyata udasmAt prANAH krAmantyAho neti [bR^i.A.u. 3.2.11] ityatra, neti hovAca yAj~navalkyaH ityanutkrAntipakShaM parigR^ihya, na tarhyayam anutkrAnteShu prANeShu mR^itaH ityasyAm AshaN^kAyAm atraiva samavanIyante iti pravilayaM prANAnAM pratij~nAya, tatsiddhaye sa ucchvayatyAdhmAyatyAdhmAto mR^itaH shete iti sashabdaparAmR^iShTasya prakR^itasya utkrAntyavadheH ucchvayanAdIni samAmananti | dehasya ca etAni syuH na dehinaH | tatsAmAnyAt, na tasmAt prANA utkrAmantyatraiva samavanIyante ityatrApi -- abhedopacAreNa dehApAdAnasyaiva utkramaNasya pratiShedhaH -- yadyapi prAdhAnyaM dehinaH iti vyAkhyeyam, yeShAM paJNcamIpAThaH | 

yeShAM tu ShaShThIpAThaH, teShAM vidvatsambandhinI utkrAntiH pratiShidhyata iti, prAptotkrAntipratiShedhArthatvAt asya vAkyasya, dehApAdAnaiva sA pratiShiddhA bhavati dehAd utkrAntiH prAptA, na dehinaH | api ca cakShuShTo vA mUrdhno vAnyebhyo vA sharIradeshebhyaH tam utkrAmantaM prANo.anUtkrAmati prANam anUtkrAmantaM sarve prANA anUtkrAmanti [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.2] ityevam avidvadviShaye saprapaJNcam utkramaNaM saMsAragamanaM ca darshayitvA, iti nu kAmayamAnaH iti upasaMhR^itya avidvatkathAm, athAkAmayamAnaH iti vyapadishya vidvAMsam -- yadi tadviShaye.apyutkrAntim eva prApayet, asamaJNjasa eva vyapadeshaH syAt | tasmAt avidvadviShaye prAptayor gatyutkrAntyoH vidvadviShaye pratiShedhaH -- ityevam eva vyAkhyeyam, vyapadeshArthavattvAya | na ca brahmavidaH sarvagatabrahmAtmabhUtasya prakShINakAmakarmaNaH utkrAntiH gatir vA upapadyate, nimittAbhAvAt | atra brahma samashnute iti ca evaMjAtIyakAH shrutayo gatyutkrAntyor abhAvaM sUcayanti ||13||

|| 4.2.14 || 

smaryate ca || 

smaryate.api ca mahAbhArate gatyutkrAntyor abhAvaH -- 

sarvabhUtAtmabhUtasya samyag bhUtAni pashyataH | 
devA api mArgo muhyantyapadasya padaiShiNaH || iti | 

nanu gatir api brahmavidaH sarvagatabrahmAtmabhUtasya smaryate -- shukaH kila vaiyAsakir mumukShur AdityamaNDalam abhipratasthe pitrA cAnugamyAhUto bho iti pratishushrAva iti -- na | sasharIrasyaiva ayaM yogabalena vishiShTAdeshaprAptipUrvakaH sharIrotsarga iti draShTavyam, sarvabhUtadR^ishyatvAd yupanyAsAt | na hi asharIraM gacchantaM sarvabhUtAni draShTuM shaknuyuH | tathA ca tatraivopasaMhR^itam -- shukaH tu mArutAcchIghrAM gatiM kR^itvAntarikShaga  | darshayitvA prabhAvaM svaM sarvabhUtagato.abhavat iti | tasmAd abhAvaH parabrahmavido gatyutkrAntyoH | gatishrutInAM tu viShayam upariShTAd vyAkhyAsyAmaH ||14||

 --o)0(o--
6. vAgAdilayAdhikaraNam 

|| 4.2.15 ||

tAni pare tathA hyAha ||

tAni punaH prANashabdoditAni indriyANi bhUtAni ca parabrahmavidaH tasminn eva parasminn Atmani pralIyante | kasmAt? tathA hi Aha shrutiH -- evam evAsya paridraShTurimAH ShoDasha kalAH puruShAyaNAH puruShaM prApyAstaM gacchanti iti | 

nanu gatAH kalAH paJNcadasha pratiShThAH iti vidvadviShayaivAparA shrutiH parasmAd Atmano.anyatrApi kalAnAM pralayam Aha sma -- na | sA khalu vyavahArApekShA -- pArthivAdyAH kalAH pR^ithivyAdIr eva svaprakR^itIrapiyantIti | itarA tu vidvatpratipattyapekShA -- kR^itsnaM kalAjAtaM parabrahmavido brahmaiva sampadyata iti | tasmAd adoShaH ||

 --o)0(o--
avibhAgAdhikaraNam 

|| 4.2.16 ||

avibhAgo vacanAt ||

sa punar viduShaH kalApralayaH kim itareShAm iva sAvasheSho bhavati, AhosvinniravasheSha iti | tatra pralayasAmAnyAt shaktyavasheShatAprasaktau bravIti -- avibhAgApattir eveti | kutaH? vacanAt | tathA hi kalApralayamuktvA vakti -- bhidyete tAsAM nAmarUpe puruSha ityevaM procyate sa eSho.akalo.amR^ito bhavati iti | avidyAnimittAnAM ca kalAnAM na vidyAnimitte pralaye sAvasheShatvopapattiH | tasmAd avibhAga eveti||

 --o)0(o--
tadoko.adhikaraNam 

|| 4.2.17 ||

tadoko.agrajvalanaM tatprakAshitadvAro vidyAsAmarthyAt 
taccheShagatyanusmR^itiyogAcca hArdAnugR^ihItaH shatAdhikayA ||

samAptA prAsaN^gikI paravidyAgatA cintA | samprati tu aparavidyAviShayAm eva cintAmanuvartayati | samAnA ca AsR^ityupakramAt vidvadaviduShorutkrAntiH -- ityuktam | tam idAnIM sR^ityupakramaM darshayati | tasya upasaMhR^itavAgAdikalApasyoccikramiShato vij~nAnAtmanaH, okaH AyatanaM hR^idayam -- sa etAstejomAtrAH samabhyAdadAno hR^idayam evAnvavakrAmati iti shruteH, tadagraprajvalanapUrvikA cakShurAdisthAnApAdAnA ca utkrAntiH shrUyate -- tasya haitasya hR^idayasyAgraM pradyotate tena pradyotenaiSha AtmA niShkrAmati cakShuShTo vA mUrdhno vAnyebhyo vA sharIradeshebhyaH iti | sA kim aniyamenaiva vidvadaviduShor bhavati, athAsti kashcidviduSho visheShaniyamaH iti vicikitsAyAm, shrutyavisheShAdaniyamaprAptau, AcaShTo -- samAne.api hi vidvadaviduShor hR^idayAgrapradyotane tatprakAshitadvAratve ca, mUrdhasthAnAd eva vidvAnniShkrAmati, sthAnAntarebhyaH tu itare | kutaH? vidyAsAmarthyAt | yadi vidvAnapi itaravat yataH kutashciddehadeshAt utkrAmet, naiva utkR^iShTAM lokaM labheta, tatra anarthikaiva vidyA syAt | taccheShagatyanusmR^itiyogAcca -- vidyAsheShabhUtA ca mUrdhanyanADIsambaddhA gatiH anushIlayitavyA vidyAvisheSheShu vihitA | tAmabhyasyan tayaiva pratiShThata iti yuktam | tasmAt hR^idayAlayena brahmaNA sUpAsitena anugR^ihItaH tadbhAvaM samApanno vidvAn mUrdhanyayaiva shatAdhikayA shatAdatiriktayA ekashatatamyA nADyA niShkrAmati, itarAbhiH itare | tathA hi hArdavidyAM prakR^itya samAmananti -- shataM caikA ca hR^idayasya nADyAH tAsAM mUrdhAnam abhiniHsR^itaikA | tayordhvam Ayann amR^itatvam eti viShvag anyA utkramaNe bhavanti [chA.u. 8.6.6] iti ||17||

 --o)0(o--
rashmyadhikaraNam

|| 4.2.18 ||

rashmyanusArI || 

asti hArdavidyA -- atha yad idam asmin brahmapure daharaM puNDarIkaM veshma [chA.u. 8.1.1] ityupakramya vihitA | tatprakriyAyAm atha yA etA hR^idayasya nADyAH ityupakramya saprapaJNcaM nADIrashmisambandhamuktvA uktam -- atha yatraitadasmAccharIrAd utkrAmatyathaitair eva rashmibhirUrdhvamAkramate iti | punashcoktam -- tayordhvamAyannamR^itatvameti iti | tasmAt shatAdhikayA nADyA niShkrAman rashmyanusArI niShkrAmatIti gamyate | tat kim avisheSheNaiva ahani rAtrau vA mriyamANasya rashmyanusAritvam, Aho svid ahanyeva iti saMshaye sati, avisheShashravaNAt avisheSheNaiva tAvat rashmyanusArIti pratij~nAyate||

|| 4.2.19 || 

nishi neti cen na sambandhasya yAvad dehabhAvitvAd darshayati ca ||

asti ahani nADIrashmisambandha iti ahani mR^itasya syAt rashmyanusAritvam | rAtrau tu pretasya na syAt, nADIrashmisambandhavicchedAt -- iti cet, na, nADIrashmisambandhasya yAvaddehabhAvitvAt | yAvaddehabhAvI hi shirAkiraNasamparkaH | darshayati caitam arthaM shrutiH -- amuShmAd AdityAt pratAyante tA Asu nADIShu sR^iptA Abhyo nADIbhyaH pratAyante te.amuShminn Aditye sR^iptAH iti | nidAghasamaye ca nishAsvapi kiraNAnuvR^ittir upalabhyate, pratApAdikAryadarshanAt | stokAnuvR^itteH tu durlakShyatvam R^itvantararajanIShu, shaishireShviva durdineShu | ahar evaitad rAtrau dadhAti iti ca etad eva darshayati | yadi ca rAtrau pretaH vinaiva rashmyanusAreNa Urdhvam Akrameta, rashmyanusArAnarthakyaM bhavet | na hyetat vishiShya abhidhIyate -- yo divA praiti, sa rashmIn apekShyordhvam Akramate, yaH tu rAtrau so.anapekShyaiveti | atha tu vidvAn api rAtriprAyaNAparAdhamAtreNa nordhvam Akrameta, pAkShikaphalA vidyeti apravR^ittir eva tasyAM syAt, mR^ityukAlAniyamAt | athApi rAtrAv uparato.aharAgamam udIkSheta, aharAgame.apyasya kadAcit arashmisambandhArhaM sharIraM syAt pAvakAdisamparkAt | sa yAvat kShipyen manaH tAvad AdityaM gacchati iti ca shrutiH anudIkShAM darshayati | tasmAt avisheSheNaiva idaM rAtriMdivaM rashmyanusAritvam ||19||

  -- o)0(o -- 
dakShiNAyanAdhikaraNam

|| 4.2.20 || 

atashcAyane.api dakShiNe ||

ata eva ca udIkShAnupapatteH, apAkShikaphalatvAcca vidyAyAH, aniyatakAlatvAcca mR^ityoH, dakShiNAyane.api mriyamANo vidvAn prApnotyeva vidyAphalam | uttarAyaNam araNaprAshastyaprasiddhiH, bhIShmasya ca pratIkShAdarshanAt, ApUryamANapakShAdyAn ShaNmAsAn udaNN [bR^i.A.u. 6.1.15] iti ca shruteH, apekShitavyam uttarAyaNam -- itImAm AshaN^kAm anena sUtreNApanudati | prAshastyaprasiddhiH avidvadviShayA | bhIShmasya pratipAlanam AcAraparipAlanArthaM pitR^iprasAdalabdhasvacchandamR^ityutAkhyApanArthaM ca | shruteH tu arthaM vakShyati AtivAhikAH talliN^gAt iti ||20|| 


|| 4.2.21 || 

nanu ca yatra kAle tu anAvR^ittim AvR^ittiM caiva yoginaH | prayAtA yAnti taM kAlaM vakShyAmi bharatarShabha iti kAlaprAdhAnyena upakramya aharAdikAlavisheShaH smR^itAvanAvR^ittaye niyataH | kathaM rAtrau dakShiNAyane vA prayAto.anAvR^ittiM yAyAt -- ityatrocyate -- 

yoginaH prati ca smaryate smArte caite ||

yoginaH prati ca ayam aharAdikAlaviniyogo.anAvR^ittaye smaryate | smArte caite yogasAN^khye, na shraute | ato viShayabhedAt pramANavisheShAcca nAsya smArtasya kAlaviniyogasya shrauteShu vij~nAneShu avatAraH | 

nanu,
agnirjyotirahaHshuklaHShaNmAsA uttarAyaNam | 
dhUmo rAtriH tathA kR^iShNaH ShaNmAsA dakShiNAyanam || iti ca |

shrautAv etau devayAnapitR^iyANau pratyabhij~nAyete smR^itAvapIti, ucyate -- taM kAlaM vakShyAmi iti smR^itau kAlapratij~nAnAt virodham AshaN^kya ayaM parihAraH uktaH | yadA punaH smR^itAvapi agnyAdyA devatA eva AtivAhikyo gR^ihyante, tadA na kashcid virodha iti ||

iti shrImatparamahaMsaparivrAjakAcAryasya shrIgovindabhagavatpUjyapAdashiShyasya shrImacchaN^karabhagavataH kR^itau shArIrakamImAMsAsUtrabhAShye
caturthAdhyAyasya dvitIyaH pAdaH ||

(4.3)

|| caturtho.adhyAye tR^itIyaH pAdaH || 

atra pAde saguNavidyAvato mR^itasya uttaramArga abhidhAnam ||
1. arcirAdyadhikaraNam

|| 4.3.1 ||

AsR^iti upakramAt samAna utkrAntiH iti uktam | sR^itiH tu shrutyantareShu anekadhA shrUyate | nADIrashmisambandhena ekadhA -- athaitair eva rashmibhir Urdhva Akramate [chA.u. 8.6.5] iti | arcirAdika ekA -- te.arciSham abhisambhavantyarciSho.ahaH [bR^i.A.u. 6.2.15] iti | sa etaM devayAnaM panthAnam AsAdyAgnilokam Agacchati [kau.u. 1.3] iti anyA | yadA vai puruSho.asmAl lokAt praiti sa vAyum Agacchati [bR^i.A.u. 5.10.1] iti aparA | sUryadvAreNa te virajAH prayAnti [mu.u.  1.2.11] iti cAparA |

tatra saMshayaH -- kiM parasparaM bhinnA etAH sR^itayaH, kiM va ekA eva anekavisheShaNAH ? iti | tatra prAptaM tAvat bhinnAH etAH sR^itaya iti, bhinnaprakaraNatvAt, bhinnopAsanAsheShatvAcca | 

api ca athaitair eva rashmibhiH [chA.u. 8.6.5] iti avadhAraNam arcirAdyapekShAyAm uparudhyeta | tvarAvacanaM ca pIDyeta, sa yAvat kShipyen manaH tAvad AdityaM gacchati [chA.u. 8.6.5] iti | tasmAt anyonyabhinnA eva ete panthAna iti | evaM prApte abhidadhmahe -- 

arcirAdinA tatprathiteH ||

sarvo brahma prepsuH arcirAdinaivAdhvanA raMhatIti pratijAnImahe | kutaH? tatprathiteH | prathito hyeSha mArgaH sarveShAM viduShAm | tathA hi paJNcAgnividyAprakaraNe -- ye cAmI araNye shraddhAM satyam upAsate iti vidyAntarashIlinAm api arcirAdikA sR^itiH shrAvyate | syAd etat -- yAsu vidyAsu na kAcid gatir ucyate, tAsu iyam arcirAdikA upatiShThatAm | yAsu tu anyA shrAvyate, tAsu kim ityarcirAdyAshrayaNam iti, atrocyate -- bhaved etad evam, yadyatyantabhinnA eva etAH sR^itayaH syuH | ekaiva tv eShA sR^itiH anekavisheShaNA brahmalokaprapadanI kvacit kenacit visheShaNenopalakShiteti vadAmaH, sarvatraikadeshapratyabhij~nAnAt itaretaravisheShaNavisheShyabhAvopapatteH | prakaraNabhede.api hi vidyaikatve bhavati itaretaravisheShaNopasaMhAravat gativisheShaNAnAm apyupasaMhAraH | vidyAbhede.api tu gatyekadeshapratyabhij~nAnAt gantavyAbhedAcca gatyabheda eva | tathA hi -- te teShu brahmalokeShu parAH parAvato vasanti tasmin vasanti shAshvatIH samAH sA yA brahmaNo jitiryA vyuShTistAM jitiM jayati tAM vyuShTiM vyashnute tad ya evaitaM brahmalokaM brahmacaryeNAnuvindati iti ca tatra tatra tad eva ekaM phalaM brahmalokaprAptilakShaNaM pradarshyate | yat tu etair eva ityavadhAraNam arcirAdyAshrayaNe na syAd iti, naiSha doShaH, rashmiprAptiparatvAd asya | na hi eka eva shabdo rashmIMshca prApayitum arhati, arcirAdIMshca vyAvartayitum | tasmAt rashmisambandha evAyam avadhAryata iti draShTavyam | tvarAvacanaM tu arcirAdyapekShAyAm api gantavyAntarApekShayA kShaipryArthatvAt noparudhyate -- yathA nimeShamAtreNAtrAgamyata iti | api ca athaitayoH pathor na katareNacana iti mArgadvayabhraShTAnAM kaShTaM tR^itIyaM sthAnam AcakShANA pitR^iyANavyatiriktam ekam eva devayAnam arcirAdiparvANaM panthAnaM prathayati | bhUyAMsyarcirAdisR^itau mArgaparvANi, alpIyAMsi tu anyatra | bhUyasAM ca AnuguNyena alpIyasAM nayanaM nyAyyam ityato.api arcirAdinA tatprathiteH ityuktam ||1||

  -- o)0(o -- 
vAyvadhikaraNam

|| 4.3.2 ||

vAyum abdAd avisheShavisheShAbhyAm ||

kena punaH saMniveshavisheSheNa gativisheShaNAnAm itaretaravisheShaNavisheShyabhAvaH -- iti tad etat suhR^id bhUtvA AcAryo grathayati | sa etaM devayAnaM panthAnam AsAdyAgnilokam Agacchati sa vAyulokaM sa varuNalokaM sa indralokaM sa prajApatilokaM sa brahmalokam iti kauShItakinAM devayAnaH panthAH paThyate | tatra arciragnilokashabdau tAvat ekArthau jvalanavacanatvAd iti nAtra saMniveshakramaH kashcid anveShyaH | vAyuH tu arcirAdau vartmani katamasmin sthAne niveshayitavya iti, ucyate -- te.arciSham evAbhisambhavantyarciSho.ahar ahna ApUryamANapakSham ApUryamANapakShAdyAn ShaD udaN^N^Ati mAsAMH tAn mAsebhyaH saMvatsaraM saMvatsarAd Adityam ityatra saMvatsarAt parAJNcam AdityAd arvAJNcaM vAyum abhisambhavanti | kasmAt? avisheShavisheShAbhyAm | tathA hi sa vAyulokam ityatra avisheShopadiShTasya vAyoH shrutyantareNa visheShopadesho dR^ishyate -- yadA vai puruSho.asmAl lokAt praiti sa vAyum Agacchati tasmai sa tatra vijihIte yathA rathacakrasya khaM tena sa Urdhvam Akramate sa Adityam Agacchati iti | etasmAt AdityAt vAyoH pUrvatvadarshanAt visheShAt abdAdityayor antarAle vAyur niveshayitavyaH | kasmAt punar agneH paratvadarshanAd visheShAd arciSho.anantaraM vAyur na niveshyate? naiSho.asti visheSha iti vadAmaH | 

nanUdAhR^itA shrutiH -- sa etaM devayAnaM panthAnam AsAdyAgnilokam Agacchati sa vAyulokaM sa varuNalokam iti | ucyate -- kevalo.atra pAThaH paurvAparyeNAvasthitaH, nAtra kramavacanaH kashcicchabdo.asti | padArthopadarshanamAtraM hyatra kriyate -- etam etaM ca AgacchatIti | itaratra punaH, vAyuprattena rathacakramAtreNa cchipANa UrdhvamAkramya Adityam AgacchatIti -- avagamyate kramaH | tasmAt sUktam avisheShavisheShAbhyAm iti | vAjasaneyinaH tu mAsebhyo devalokaM devalokAd Adityam iti samAmananti | tatra AdityAnantaryAya devalokAd vAyum abhisambhaveyuH | vAyum abdAt iti tu cchandogashrutyapekShayoktam | chAndogyavAjasaneyakayoH tu ekatra devaloko na vidyate, paratra saMvatsaraH | tatra shrutidvayapratyayAt ubhAvapi ubhayatra grathayitavyau | tatrApi mAsasambandhAt saMvatsaraH pUrvaH pashcimo devaloka iti vivektavyam ||2||

  -- o)0(o -- 
3. taDidadhikaraNam

|| 4.3.3 ||

taDito.adhi varuNaH sambandhAt ||

AdityAccandramasaM candramaso vidyutam [chA.u. 4.15.5] ityasyA vidyuta upariShTAt sa varuNalokam ityayaM varuNaH sambadhyeta | asti hi sambandho vidyudvaruNayoH | yadA hi vishAlA vidyutaH tIvrastanitanirghoShA jImUtodareShu pranR^ityanti, atha ApaH prapatanti | vidyotate stanayati varShiShyati vA [chA.u. 7.11.1] iti ca brAhmaNam | apAM ca adhipatir varuNa iti shrutismR^itiprasiddhiH | varuNAd adhi indraprajApatI sthAnAntarAbhAvAt pAThasAmarthyAcca | AgantukatvAd api varuNAdInAm ante eva niveshaH, vaisheShikasthAnAbhAvAt | vidyucca antyA arcirAdau vartmani ||3||

  -- o)0(o -- 
4. AtivAhikAdhikaraNam

|| 4.3.4 ||

teShv eva arcirAdiShu saMshayaH -- kim etAni mArgacihnAni, uta bhogabhUmayaH, athavA netAro gantNAm iti | tatra mArgalakShaNabhUtA arcirAdaya iti tAvat prAptam, tatsvarUpatvAd upadeshasya | yathA hi loke kashcid grAmaM nagaraM vA pratiShThAsamAno.anushiShyate -- gaccha itastvamamuM giriM tato nyagrodhaM tato nadIM tato grAmaM tato nagaraM vA prApsyasIti -- evam ihApi arciSho.aharahna ApUryamANapakSham ityAdyAha | athavA bhogabhUmaya iti prAptam | tathA hi lokashabdena agnyAdIn anubadhnAti, agnilokam Agacchati [kau.u. 1.3] ityAdi | lokashabdashca prANinAM bhogAyataneShu bhAShyate -- manuShyalokaH pitR^iloko devalokaH [bR^i.A.u. 1.5.16] iti ca | tathA ca brAhmaNam -- ahorAtreShu te lokeShu sajjante ityAdi | tasmAn nAtivAhikA arcirAdayaH | acetanatvAd apyeShAm AtivAhikatvAnupapattiH | cetanA hi loke rAjaniyuktAH puruShA durgeShu mArgeShvativAhyAn ativAhayantIti | evaM prApte, brUmaH -- 

AtivAhikAH talliN^gAt ||

AtivAhikA evaite bhavitum arhanti | kutaH? talliN^gAt | tathA hi -- candramaso vidyutaM tatpuruSho.amAnavaH sa etAn brahma gamayati [chA.u. 4.15.5] iti siddhavad gamayitR^itvaM darshayati | tad vacanaM tadviShayam evopakShINam iti cet, na, prAptamAnavatvanivR^ittiparatvAd visheShaNasya | yadyarcirAdiShu puruShA gamayitAraH prAptAH te ca mAnavAH, tato yuktaM tannivR^ittyarthaM puruShavisheShaNam -- amAnava iti ||4|| 

|| 4.3.5 ||

nanu talliN^gamAtram agamakam, nyAyAbhAvAt | naiSha doShaH -- 

ubhayavyAmohAt tatsiddhiH || 

ye tAvadarcirAdimArgagAH te dehaviyogAt sampiNDitakaraNagrAmA iti asvatantrAH, arcirAdInAm apyacetanatvAd asvAtantryam -- ityato.arcirAdyabhimAninashcetanA devatAvisheShA atiyAtrAyAM niyuktA iti gamyate | loke.api hi mattamUrchitAdayaH sampiNDitakaraNAH paraprayuktavartmAno bhavanti | anavasthitatvAd apyarcirAdInAM na mArgalakShaNatvopapattiH | na hi rAtrau pretasya ahaHsvarUpAbhisambhava upapadyate | na ca pratipAlanam astItyuktaM purastAt | dhruvatvAt tu devatAtmanAM nAyaM doSho bhavati | arcirAdishabdatA ca eShAm arcirAdyabhimAnAd upapadyate | arciSho.ahaH [chA.u. 4.15.5, 5.10.1] ityAdinirdeshaH tu AtivAhikatve.api na virudhyate -- arciShA hetunA ahar abhisambhavati, ahnA hetunA 
ApUryamANapakSham iti | tathA ca loke prasiddheShvapyAtivAhikeShu evaMjAtIyaka upadesho dR^ishyate -- gaccha tvam ito balavarmANaM tato jayasiMhaM tataH kR^iShNaguptam iti | api ca upakrame te.arcir abhisambhavanti [bR^i.A.u. 6.2.15] iti sambandhamAtram uktam, na sambandhavisheShaH kashcit | upasaMhAre tu sa etAn brahma gamayati [chA.u. 4.15.6] iti sambandhavisheSho.ativAhyAtivAhakatvalakShaNa uktaH | tena sa evopakrame.apIti nirdhAryate | sampiNDitakaraNatvAd eva ca gantNAM na tatra bhogasambhavaH | lokashabdaH tu anupabhuJNjAneShvapi gantR^iShu gamayituM shakyate, anyeShAM tallokavAsinAM bhogabhUmitvAt | ato.agnisvAmikaM lokaM prApto.agninA ativAhyate, vAyusvAmikaM prApto vAyunA -- iti yojayitavyam ||5|| 


|| 4.3.6 ||

kathaM punar AtivAhikatvapakShe varuNAdiShu tatsambhavaH? vidyuto hyadhi varuNAdaya upakShiptAH, vidyutaH tu anantaram A brahmaprApteH amAnavasyaiva puruShasya gamayitR^itvaM shrutam -- ityata uttaraM paThati --  

vaidyutenaiva tataH tacchruteH ||

tato vidyud abhisambhavanAd UrdhvaM vidyudanantaravartinaivAmAnavena puruSheNa varuNalokAdiShvativAhyamAnA brahmalokaM gacchantItyavagantavyam, tAn vaidyutAt puruSho.amAnavaH sa etya brahmalokaM gamayati iti tasyaiva gamayitR^itvashruteH | varuNAdayaH tu tasyaiva apratibandhakaraNena sAhAyyAnuShThAnena vA kenacit anugrAhakA ityavagantavyam | tasmAt sAdhUktam -- AtivAhikA devatAtmAno.arcirAdaya iti ||6||

 --o)0(o--
5. kAryAdhikaraNam 

|| 4.3.7 || 

kAryaM bAdarirasya gatyupapatteH ||

sa enAn brahma gamayati [chA.u. 4.15.5] ityatra vicikitsyate -- kiM kAryam aparaM brahma gamayati, Aho svit param evAvikR^itaM mukhyaM brahmeti | kutaH saMshayaH? brahmashabdaprayogAt, gatishruteshca | tatra kAryam eva saguNam aparaM brahma enAn gamayatyamAnavaH puruSha iti bAdarir AcAryo manyate | kutaH? asya gatyupapatteH -- asya hi kAryabrahmaNo gantavyatvam upapadyate, pradeshavattvAt | na tu parasmin brahmaNi gantR^itvaM gantavyatvaM gatir vA avakalpate, sarvagatatvAt pratyagAtmatvAcca gantNAm ||7||

|| 4.3.8 ||

visheShitatvAcca ||

brahmalokAn gamayati te teShu brahmalokeShu parAH parAvato vasanti [bR^i.A.u. 6.2.15] iti ca shrutyantare visheShitatvAt kAryabrahmaviShayaiva gatiH iti gamyate | na hi bahuvacanena visheShaNaM parasmin brahmaNyavakalpate | kArye tu avasthAbhedopapatteH sambhavati bahuvacanam | lokashrutir api vikAragocarAyAm eva saMniveshavishiShTAyAM bhogabhUmAvaJNjasI | gauNI tu anyatra brahmaiva loka eSha samrAT ityAdiShu | adhikaraNAdhikartavyanirdesho.api parasmin brahmaNi anAJNjasaH syAt | tasmAt kAryaviShayam evedaM nayanam ||8|| 

|| 4.3.9 ||

nanu kAryaviShaye.api brahmashabdo nopapadyate, samanvaye hi samastasya jagato janmAdikAraNaM brahmeti sthApitam -- ityatrocyate -- 

sAmIpyAtu tadvyapadeshaH ||

tushabda AshaN^kAvyAvR^ittyarthaH | parabrahmasAmIpyAt aparasya brahmaNaH, tasminn api brahmashabdaprayogo na virudhyate | param eva hi brahma vishuddhopAdhisambandhaM kvacit kaishcid vikAradharmair manomayatvAdibhiH upAsanAya upadishyamAnam aparam iti sthitiH ||9||

|| 4.3.10 || 

nanu kAryaprAptau anAvR^ittishravaNaM na ghaTate | na hi parasmAd brahmaNo.anyatra kvacin nityatAM sambhAvayanti | darshayati ca devayAnena pathA prasthitAnAm anAvR^ittim -- etena pratipadyamAnA imaM mAnavam AvartaM nAvartante [chA.u. 4.15.6] iti, teShAm iha na punar AvR^ittir asti -- tayor dhvamAyann amR^itatvam eti [chA.u. 8.6.6, ka.u. 6.16] iti ca | atra brUmaH -- 

kAryAtyaye tadadhyakSheNa sahAtaH param abhidhAnAt ||

kAryabrahmalokapralayapratyupasthAne sati tatraiva utpannasamyagdarshanAH santaH, tadadhyakSheNa hiraNyagarbheNa saha, ataH para parishuddhaM viShNoH paramaM padaM pratipadyante -- itItthaM kramamuktiH anAvR^ittyAdishrutyabhidhAnebhyo.abhyupagantavyA | na hyaJNjasaiva gatipUrvikA paraprAptiH sambhavatItyupapAditam ||10||

|| 4.3.11 ||

smR^iteshca ||

smR^itir apyetam artham anujAnAti -- brahmaNA saha te sarve samprApte pratisaMcare | parasyAnte kR^itAtmAnaH pravishanti paraM padam iti | tasmAt kAryabrahmaviShayA eva gatishrutayaH iti siddhAntaH ||11|| 

|| 4.3.12 || 

kaM punaH pUrvapakSham AshaN^kya ayaM siddhAntaH pratiShThApitaH kAryaM bAdariH ityAdineti, sa idAnIM sUtrair evopadarshyate -- 

paraM jaiminir mukhyatvAt ||

jaiminiH tvacAryaH sa enAn brahma gamayati ityatra param eva brahma prApayatIti manyate | kutaH? mukhyatvAt | paraM hi brahma brahmashabdasya mukhyam Alambanam, gauNam aparam | mukhyagauNayoshca mukhye sampratyayo bhavati ||12||

|| 4.3.13 ||

darshanAcca ||

tayordhvam Ayann amR^itatvam eti [chA.u. 8.6.6, ka.u. 6.16] iti ca gatipUrvakam amR^itatvaM darshayati | amR^itatvaM ca parasmin brahmaNyupapadyate, na kArye, vinAshitvAt kAryasya -- atha yatrAnyat pashyati tad alpaM tan matryam [chA.u. 7.24.1] iti pravacanAt paraviShayaiva ca eShA gatiH kaThavallIShu paThyate | na hi tatra vidyAntaraprakramo.asti -- anyatra dharmAd anyatrAdharmAt [ka.u. 1.2.14] iti parasyaiva brahmaNaH prakrAntatvAt ||13||

|| 4.3.14 || 

na ca kArye pratipattyabhisandhiH ||

api ca prajApateH sabhAM veshma prapadye [chA.u. 8.14.1] iti nAyaM kAryaviShayaH pratipattyabhisandhiH, nAmarUpayor nirvahitA te yad antarA tad brahma [chA.u. 8.14.1] iti kAryavilakShaNasya parasyaiva brahmaNaH prakR^itatvAt | yasho.ahaM bhavAmi brAhmaNAnAm [chA.u. 8.14.1] iti ca sarvAtmatvenopakramaNAt | na tasya pratimA asti yasya nAma mahad yashaH [shve.u. 4.19] iti ca parasyaiva brahmaNo yashonAmatvaprasiddhiH | sA ceyaM veshmapratipattir gatipUrvikA hArdavidyAyAm uditA -- tad aparAjitA pUr brahmaNaH prabhuvimitaM hiraNmayam [chA.u. 8.5.3] ityatra | 

pader api ca gatyarthatvAt mArgApekShatAvasIyate | tasmAt parabrahmaviShayA gatishrutaya iti pakShAntaram | tAv etau dvau pakShAvacAryeNa sUtritau -- gatyupapattyAdibhir ekaH, mukhyatvAdibhir aparaH | tatra gatyupapattyAdayaH prabhavanti mukhyatvAdIn AbhAsayitum, na tu mukhyatvAdayo gatyupapattyAdIn -- iti Adya eva siddhAnto vyAkhyAtaH, dvitIyaH tu pUrvapakShaH | na hyasatyapi sambhave mukhyasyaivArthasya grahaNam iti kashcid Aj~nApayitA vidyate | paravidyAprakaraNe.api ca tatstutyarthaM vidyAntarAshrayagatyanukIrtanam upapadyate -- viShvaN^N^ anyA utkramaNe bhavanti [chA.u. 8.6.6] itivat | prajApateH sabhAM veshma prapadye [chA.u. 8.14.1] iti tu pUrvavAkyavicchedena kArye.api pratipattyabhisandhir na virudhyate | saguNe.api ca brahmaNi sarvAtmatvasaN^kIrtanam sarvakarmA sarvakAmaH ityAdivat avakalpate | tasmAd aparaviShayA eva gatishrutayaH || 

kecit punaH pUrvANi pUrvapakShasUtrANi bhavanti uttarANi siddhAntasUtrANi -- ityetAM vyavasthAm anurudhyamAnAH paraviShayA eva gatishrutIH pratiShThApayanti | tat anupapannam, gantavyatvAnupapatter brahmaNaH | yat sarvagataM sarvAntaraM sarvAtmakaM ca paraM brahma AkAshavat sarvagatashca nityaH yat sAkShAd aparokShAd brahma ya AtmA sarvAntaraH AtmaivedaM sarvam [chA.u. 7.25.2], brahmaivedaM vishvam idaM variShTham ityAdi shrutinirdhAritavisheSham -- tasya gantavyatA na kadAcid apyupapadyate | na hi gatam eva gamyate | anyo hyanyad gacchatIti prasiddhaM loke | 

nanu loke gatasyApi gantavyatA deshAntaravishiShTasya dR^iShTA -- yathA pR^ithivIstha eva pR^ithivIM deshAntaradvAreNa gacchati, tathA ananyatve.api bAlasya kAlAntaravishiShTaM vArdhakaM svAtmabhUtam eva gantavyaM dR^iShTam, tadvat brahmaNo.api sarvashaktyupetatvAt kathaMcit gantavyatA syAd iti -- na, pratiShiddhasarvavisheShatvAd brahmaNaH | niShkalaM niShkriyaM shAntaM niravadyaM niraJNjanam [shve.u. 6.19], asthUlam anaNvahrasvam adIrgham sa bAhyAbhyantaro hyajaH [bR^i.A.u. 3.8.8], sa vA eSha mahAn aja AtmAjaro.amaro.amR^ito.abhayo brahma [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.25], sa eSha neti netyAtmA [bR^i.A.u. 3.9.26, 4.2.4, 4.4.22] ityAdi shrutismR^itinyAyebhyo na deshakAlAdivisheShayogaH paramAtmani kalpayituM shakyate, yena bhUpradeshavayo.avasthAnyAyenAsya gantavyatA syAt | bhUvayasoH tu pradeshAvasthAdivisheShayogAd upapadyate deshakAlavishiShTA gantavyatA | jagadutpattisthitipralayahetutvashruter anekashaktitvaM brahmaNa iti cet, na, visheShanirAkaraNashrutInAm ananyArthatvAt | utpattyAdishrutInAm api samAnam ananyArthatvam iti cet, na, tAsAm ekatvapratipAdanaparatvAt | mR^idAdidR^iShTAntair hi sato brahmaNa ekasya satyatvaM vikArasya ca anR^itatvaM pratipAdayat shAstraM notpattyAdiparaM bhavitum arhati || 

kasmAt punar utpattyAdishrutInAM visheShanirAkaraNashrutisheShatvam, na punaH itarasheShatvam itarAsAm iti, ucyate -- visheShanirAkaraNashrutInAM nirAkAN^kShArthatvAt | na hi Atmana ekatvanityatvashuddhatvAdyavagatau satyAM bhUyaH kAcid AkAN^kShA upajAyate, puruShArthasamAptibuddhyutpatteH, tatra ko mohaH kaH shoka ekatvam anupashyataH [Isho. 7], abhayaM vai janaka prApto.asi [bR^i.A.u. 4.2.4], vidvAn na bibheti kutashcana | etaM ha vAva na tapati | kim ahaM sAdhu nAkaravam | kim ahaM pApam akaravam [tai.u. 2.9.1] ityAdi shrutibhyaH, tathaiva ca viduShAM tuShTyanubhavAdidarshanAt, vikArAnR^itAbhisandhyapavAdAcca -- mR^ityoH sa mR^ityum Apnoti ya iha nAneva pashyati iti | ato na visheShanirAkaraNashrutInAmanyasheShatvamavagantuM shakyam | naivam utpattyAdishrutInAM nirAkAN^kShArthapratipAdanasAmarthyam asti | pratyakShaM tu tAsAm anyArthatvaM samanugamyate | tathA hi -- tatraitacchuN^gam utpatitaM somya vijAnIhi nedam amUlaM bhaviShyati ityupanyasya, udarke sata evaikasya jaganmUlasya vij~neyatvaM darshayati | yato vA imAni bhUtAni jAyante | yena jAtAni jIvanti | yat prayantyabhisaMvishanti | tad vijij~nAsasva | tad brahma [tai.u. 3.1] iti ca | evam utpattyAdishrutInAm aikAtmyAvagamaparatvAt nAnekashaktiyogo brahmaNaH | atashca gantavyatvAnupapattiH | na tasya prANA utkrAmanti [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.6] brahmaiva san brahmApyeti [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.7] iti ca parasmin brahmaNi gatiM nivArayati | tad vyakhyAtam spaShTo hyekeShAm ityatra || 

gatikalpanAyAM ca gantA jIvo gantavyasya brahmaNo.avayavaH vikAro.anyo vA tataH syAt, atyantatAdAtmye gamanAnupapatteH | yadyevam, tataH kiM syAt? ata ucyate -- yadyekadeshaH, tena ekadeshino nityaprAptatvAt na punar brahmagamanam upapadyate | ekadeshaikadeshitvakalpanA ca brahmaNyanupapannA, niravayavatvaprasiddhiH | vikArapakShe.apyetat tulyam, vikAreNApi vikAriNo nityaprAptatvAt | na hi ghaTe mR^idAtmatAM parityajya avatiShThate, parityAge vA abhAvaprApteH | vikArAvayavapakShayoshca tadvataH sthiratvAt brahmaNaH saMsAragamanam api anavakptam | atha anya eva jIvo brahmaNaH, so.aNuH vyApI madhyamaparimANo vA bhavitum arhati | vyApitve gamanAnupapattiH | madhyamaparimANatve ca anityatvaprasaN^gaH | aNutve kR^itsnasharIravedanAnupapattiH | pratiShiddhe ca aNutvamadhyamaparimANatve vistareNa purastAt | parasmAcca anyatve jIvasya tat tvam asi ityAdishAstrabAdhaprasaN^gaH | vikArAvayavapakShayor api samAno.ayaM doShaH | vikArAvayavayoH tadvato.ananyatvAt adoSha iti cet, na, mukhyaikatvAnupapatteH | sarveShu ca eteShu pakSheShu anirmokShaprasaN^gaH, saMsAryAtmatvAnivR^itteH | nivR^ittau vA svarUpanAshaprasaN^gaH, brahmAtmatvAnabhyupagamAcca || 

yat tu kaishcijjalpyate -- nityAni naimittikAni ca karmANyanuShThIyante pratyavAyAnutpattaye, kAmyAni pratiShiddhAni ca parihriyante svarganarakAnavAptaye, sAmpratadehopabhogyAni ca karmANyupabhogenaiva kShipyante -- ityato vartamAnadehapAtAd UrdhvaM dehAntarapratisandhAnakAraNAbhAvAt svarUpAvasthAnalakShaNaM kaivalyaM vinApi brahmAtmatayA evaMvR^ittasya setsyatIti -- tad asat, pramANAbhAvAt | 

na hyetat shAstreNa kenacit pratipAditam -- mokShArthI itthaM samAcared iti | svamanIShayA tu etat tarkitam -- yasmAt karmanimittaH saMsAraH tasmAn nimittAbhAvAn na bhaviShyatIti | na caitat tarkayituM shakyate, nimittAbhAvasya durj~nAnatvAt | bahUni hi karmANi jAtyantarasaJNcitAni iShTAniShTavipAkAni ekaikasya jantoH sambhAvyante | teShAM viruddhaphalAnAM yugapadupabhogAsambhavAt kAnicil labdhAvasarANi idaM janma nirmimate, kAnicit tu deshakAlanimittapratIkShANyAsate -- ityataH teShAm avashiShTAnAM sAmpratenopabhogena kShapaNAsambhavAt na yathAvarNitacaritasyApi vartamAnadehapAte dehAntaranimittAbhAvaH shakyate nishcetum | karmasheShasadbhAvasiddhishca tad ya iha ramaNIyacaraNAH tataH sheSheNa ityAdi shrutismR^itibhyaH | syAd etat -- nityanaimittikAni teShAM kShepakANi bhaviShyantIti -- tat na, virodhAbhAvAt | sati hi virodhe kShepyakShepakabhAvo bhavati | na ca janmAntarasaJNcitAnAM sukR^itAnAM nityanaimittikair asti virodhaH, shuddhirUpatvAvisheShAt | duritAnAM tu ashuddhirUpatvAt sati virodhe bhavatu kShapaNam | na tu tAvatA dehAntaranimittAbhAvasiddhiH, sukR^itanimittatvopapatteH, duritasyApyasheShakShapaNAnavagamAt | na ca nityanaimittikAnuShThAnAt pratyavAyAnutpattimAtram, na punaH phalAntarotpattiH iti pramANam asti, phalAntarasyApyanuniShpAdinaH sambhavAt | smarati hi ApastambaH -- tad yathA Amre phalArthe nimitte chAyAgandhAvanUtpadyete evaM dharmaM caryamANam arthA anUtpadyante iti | na ca asati samyagdarshane sarvAtmanA kAmyapratiShiddhavarjanaM janmaprAyaNAntarAle kenacitpratij~nAtuM shakyam, sunipuNAnAm api sUkShmAparAdhadarshanAt | saMshayitavyaM tu bhavati | tathApi nimittAbhAvasya dur j~nAnatvam eva | na ca anabhyupagamyamAne j~nAnagamye brahmAtmatve kartR^itvabhoktR^itvasvabhAvasya AtmanaH kaivalyamAkAN^kShituM shakyam, agnyauShNyavat svabhAvasyAparihAryatvAt | syAd etat -- kartR^itvabhoktR^itvakAryam anarthaH, na tacchaktiH, tena shaktyavasthAne.api kAryaparihArAdupapanno mokSha iti -- tacca na | shaktisadbhAve kAryaprasavasya durnivAratvAt | athApi syAt -- na kevalA shaktiH kAryam Arabhate anapekShya anyAni nimittAni | ata ekAkinI sA sthitApi nAparAdhyatIti -- tacca na, nimittAnAm api shaktilakShaNena sambandhena nityasambaddhatvAt | tasmAt kartR^itvabhoktR^itvasvabhAve sati Atmani, asatyAM vidyAgamyAyAM brahmAtmatAyAm, na kathaMcana mokShaM prati AshA asti | shrutishca -- nAnyaH panthA vidyate.ayanAya iti j~nAnAdanyaM mokShamArgaM vArayati || 

parasmAd ananyatve.api jIvasya sarvavyavahAralopaprasaN^gaH, pratyakShAdipramANApravR^itteH iti cet -- na, prAkprabodhAt svapnavyavahAravat tadupapatteH | shAstraM ca yatra hi dvaitam iva bhavati taditara itaraM pashyati ityAdinA aprabuddhaviShaye pratyakShAdivyavahAram uktvA, punaH prabuddhaviShaye -- yatra tu asya sarvam AtmaivAbhUt tat kena kaM pashyet [bR^i.A.u. 4.5.15] ityAdinA tad abhAvaM darshayati | 

tad evaM parabrahmavido gantavyAdivij~nAnasya bAdhitatvAt na kathaMcana gatir upapAdayituM shakyA | kiMviShayAH punar gatishrutaya iti, ucyate -- saguNavidyAviShayA bhaviShyanti | tathA hi -- kvacit paJNcAgnividyAM prakR^itya gatir ucyate, kvacit paryaN^kavidyAm, kvacid vaishvAnaravidyAm | yatrApi brahma prakR^itya gatir ucyate -- yathA prANo brahma kaM brahma khaM brahma iti atha yad idam asmin brahmapure daharaM puNDarIkaM veshma [chA.u. 8.1.1] iti ca, tatrApi vAmanItvAdibhiH satyakAmAdibhishca guNaiH saguNasyaiva upAsyatvAt sambhavati gatiH | na kvacit parabrahmaviShayA gatiH shrAvyate, yathA gatipratiShedhaH shrAvitaH -- na tasya prANA utkrAmanti [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.6] iti | brahmavid Apnoti param [tai.u. 2.1] ityAdiShu tu, satyapi Apnotergatyarthatve, varNitena nyAyena deshAntaraprAptyasambhavAt svarUpapratipattir eveyam avidyAdhyAropitanAmarUpapravilayApekShayA abhidhIyate -- brahmaiva san brahmApyeti [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.7] ityAdivat iti draShTavyam | api ca paraviShayA gatir vyAkhyAyamAnA prarocanAya vA syAt, anucintanAya vA | tatra prarocanaM tAvat brahmavido na gatyuktyA kriyate, svasaMvedyenaiva avyavahitena vidyAsamarpitena svAsthyena tatsiddhiH | na ca nityasiddhaniHshreyasanivedanasya asAdhyaphalasya vij~nAnasya gatyanucintane kAcid apekShA upapadyate | tasmAd aparaviShayA gatiH | tatra parAparabrahmavivekAnavadhAraNena aparasmin brahmaNi vartamAnA gatishrutayaH parasminn adhyAropyante | 

kiM dve brahmaNI -- param aparaM ceti? bADham -- etad vai satyakAma paraM cAparaM ca brahma yad oMkAraH ityAdi darshanAt | kiM punaH paraM brahma kim aparam iti, ucyate -- yatra avidyAkR^itanAmarUpAdivisheShapratiShedhAt asthUlAdishabdair brahmopadishyate, tat param | tad eva yatra nAmarUpAdivisheSheNa kenacid vishiShTam upAsanAyopadishyate -- manomayaH prANasharIro bhArUpaH [chA.u. 3.14.2] ityAdi shabdaiH, tad aparam | 

nanu evam advitIyashrutir uparudhyeta -- na, avidyAkR^itanAmarUpopAdhikatayA parihR^itatvAt | tasya ca aparabrahmopAsanasya tatsaMnidhau shrUyamANam sa yadi pitR^ilokakAmo bhavati ityAdi jagadaishvaryalakShaNaM saMsAragocaram eva phalaM bhavati, anivartitatvAd avidyAyAH | tasya ca deshavisheShAvabaddhatvAt tatprAptyarthaM gamanam aviruddham | sarvagatatve.api ca AtmanaH, AkAshasyeva ghaTAdigamane, buddhyAdyupAdhigamane gamanaprasiddhiH ityavAdiShma tadguNasAratvAt ityatra | tasmAt kAryaM bAdariH ityeSha eva sthitaH pakShaH | paraM jaiminiH iti tu pakShAntarapratibhAnamAtrapradarshanaM praj~nAvikAsanAyeti draShTavyam ||14||

  -- o)0(o -- 
6. apratIkAlambanAdhikaraNam

|| 4.3.15 || 

sthitam etat -- kAryaviShayA gatiH, na paraviShayeti | idam idAnIM sandihyate -- kiM sarvAn vikArAlambanAn avisheSheNaiva amAnavaH puruShaH prApayati brahmalokam, uta kAMshcid eveti | kiM tAvat prAptam? sarveShAm eva eShAM viduShAm anyatra parasmAd brahmaNaH gatiH syAt | tathA hi aniyamaH sarvAsAm ityatra avisheSheNaiva eShA vidyAntareShvavatAriteti | evaM prApte, pratyAha -- 

apratIkAlambanAn nayatIti bAdarAyaNa 
ubhayathAdoShAt tatkratushca ||

pratIkAlambanAn varjayitvA sarvAn anyAn vikArAlambanAn nayati brahmalokam -- iti bAdarAyaNa AcAryo manyate | na hyevam ubhayathAbhAvAbhyupagame kashcid doSho.asti, aniyamanyAyasya pratIkavyatirikteShvapyupAsaneShUpapatteH | tat kratushca asya ubhayathAbhAvasya samarthako hetur draShTavyaH | yo hi brahmakratuH, sa brAhmam aishvaryam AsIded iti shliShyate, taM yathA yathopAsate tad eva bhavati iti shruteH, na tu pratIkeShu brahmakratutvam asti, pratIkapradhAnatvAd upAsanasya | 

nanu, abrahmakratur api brahma gacchatIti shrUyate | yathA paJNcAgnividyAyAm -- sa enAn brahma gamayati iti | bhavatu, yatra evam AhatyavAda upalabhyate | tadabhAve tu autsargikeNa tatkratunyAyena brahmakratUnAm eva tatprAptiH, netareShAm iti gamyate ||15||

|| 4.3.16 || 

visheShaM ca darshayati ||

nAmAdiShu pratIkopAsaneShu pUrvasmAt pUrvasmAt phalavisheSham uttarasminn uttarasmin upAsane darshayati -- yAvan nAmno gataM tatrAsya yathAkAmacAro bhavati vAg vAva nAmno bhUyasI yAvad vAco gataM tatrAsya yathAkAmacAro bhavati mano vAva vAco bhUyaH ityAdinA | sa cAyaM phalavisheShaH pratIkatantratvAd upAsanAnAm upapadyate | brahmatantratve tu brahmaNo.avishiShTatvAt kathaM phalavisheShaH syAt ? tasmAt na pratIkAlambanAnAm itaraiH tulyaphalatvam iti ||16||

iti shrImatparamahaMsaparivrAjakAcAryasya shrIgovindabhagavatpUjyapAdashiShyasya 
shrImacchaN^karabhagavataH kR^itau shArIrakamImAMsAsUtrabhAShye
caturthAdhyAyasya tR^itIyaH pAdaH || 
|| 4.3 ||

  -- o)0(o -- 

 
(4.4)
|| caturtho.adhyAye caturthaH pAdaH || 

atra pAde brahmaprAptibrahmalokasthitinirUpaNam ||

1. sampadyAvirbhAvAdhikaraNam 

|| 4.4.1 ||

evam eva eSha samprasAdaH asmAt sharIrAt samutthAya paraM jyotiH upasampadya svena rUpeNa abhiniShpadyata iti shrUyate | tatra saMshayaH -- kiM devalokAdyupabhogasthAneShviva Agantukena kenacit visheSheNa abhiniShpadyata Aho svit AtmamAtreNa ? iti | kiM tAvat prAptam ? sthAnAntareShu ivAgantukena kenacit rUpeNa abhiniShpattiH syAt | mokShasyApi  phalatvaprasiddheH | abhiniShpadyata iti ca utpattiparyAyatvAt | svarUpamAtreNa cet abhiniShpattiH pUrvAsu api avasthAsu svarUpAnApAyAd vibhAvyeta | tasmAt visheSheNa kenacit abhiniShpadyata iti | evaM prApte brUmaH -- 

sampadyAvirbhAvaH svena shabdAt ||

kevalenaiva AtmanA Avirbhavati, na dharmAntareNeti | kutaH? svena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyate iti svashabdAt | anyathA hi svashabdena visheShaNam anavakptaM syAt | 

nanu, AtmIyAbhiprAyaH svashabdo bhaviShyati -- na, tasyAvacanIyatvAt | yenaiva hi kenacid rUpeNAbhiniShpadyate, tasyaiva AtmIyatvopapatteH, sveneti visheShaNam anarthakaM syAt | AtmavacanatAyAM tu arthavat -- kevalenaiva AtmarUpeNAbhiniShpadyate, na AgantukenApararUpeNApIti ||1|| 

|| 4.4.2 || 

kaH punar visheShaH pUrvAvasthAsu, iha ca svarUpAnapAyasAmye satItyata Aha -- 

muktaH pratij~nAnAt ||

yo.atra abhiniShpadyata ityuktaH, sa sarvabandhavinirmuktaH shurAnaiva AtmanA avatiShThate | pUrvatra tu andho bhavatyapi roditIva vinAsham evApIto bhavati iti ca avasthAtrayakaluShitena AtmanA -- ityayaM visheShaH | kathaM punar avagamyate mukto.ayam idAnIM bhavatIti? pratij~nAnAd ityAha | tathA hi -- etaM tv eva te bhUyo.anuvyAkhyAsyAmi iti avasthAtrayadoShavihInam AtmAnam vyAkhyeyatvena pratij~nAya, asharIraM vAva santaM na priyApriye spR^ishataH iti ca upanyasya, svena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyate sa uttamaH puruShaH iti ca upasaMharati | tathA AkhyAyikopakrame.api ya AtmApahatapApmA [chA.u. 8.7.1] ityAdi muktAtmaviShayam eva pratij~nAnam | phalatvaprasiddhir api mokShasya bandhanivR^ittimAtrApekShA, na apUrvopajanApekShA | yad api abhiniShpadyata ityutpattiparyAyatvam, tad api na apUrvAvasthApekSham -- yathA roganivR^ittau arogo.abhiniShpadyata iti, tadvat | tasmAd adoShaH ||2||

|| 4.4.3 || 

AtmA prakaraNAt ||

kathaM punar mukta ityucyate, yAvatA paraM jyotir upasampadya iti kAryagocaram eva enaM shrAvayati, jyotiHshabdasya bhautike jyotiShi rUDhatvAt ? na ca anativR^itto vikAraviShayAt kashcin mukto bhavitum arhati, vikArasya ArtatvaprasiddheH iti -- naiSha doShaH, yataH AtmaivAtra jyotiHshabdena Avedyate, prakaraNAt | ya AtmApahatapApmA vijaro vimR^ityuH [chA.u. 8.7.1] iti prakR^ite parasminn Atmani na akasmAd bhautikaM jyotiH shakyaM grahItum, prakR^itahAnAprakR^itaprakriyAprasaN^gAt | jyotiHshabdaH tu Atmanyapi dR^ishyate -- tad devA jyotiShAM jyotiH iti | prapaJNcitaM ca etat jyotirdarshanAt ityatra ||3||

 -- o)0(o -- 
2. avibhAgenadR^iShTatvAdhikaraNam

|| 4.4.4 ||

avibhAgena dR^iShTatvAt || 

paraM jyotir upasampadya svena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyate yaH, sa kiM parasmAd AtmanaH pR^ithag eva bhavati, uta avibhAgenaivAvatiShThate ? iti vIkShAyAm, sa tatra paryeti [chA.u. 8.12.3] ityadhikaraNAdhikartavyanirdeshAt, jyotir upasampadya [chA.u. 8.12.3] iti ca kartR^ikarmanirdeshAt bhedenaivAvasthAnam iti yasya matiH, taM vyutpAdayati -- avibhakta eva pareNa AtmanA mukto.avatiShThate | kutaH? dR^iShTatvAt | tathA hi -- tat tvam asi [chA.u. 6.8.7], ahaM brahmAsmi [bR^i.A.u. 1.4.10], yatra nAnyat pashyati [chA.u. 7.24.1], na tu tad dvitIyam asti tato.anyad vibhaktaM yat pashyet [bR^i.A.u. 4.3.23] ityevam AdIni vAkyAnyavibhAgenaiva paramAtmAnaM darshayanti | yathAdarshanam eva ca phalaM yuktam, tatkratunyAyAt | yathodakaM shurA shuddham AsiktaM tAdR^ig eva bhavati | evaM muner vijAnata AtmA bhavati gautama iti ca evamAdIni muktasvarUpanirUpaNaparANi vAkyAnyavibhAgam eva darshayanti | nadIsamudrAdinidarshanAni ca | bhedanirdeshaH tu abhede.apyupacaryate -- sa bhagavaH kasmin pratiShThita iti sve mahimni [chA.u. 7.24.1] iti, Atmaratir AtmakrIDAH [chA.u. 7.25.2] iti ca evamAdidarshanAt ||4||

  -- o)0(o -- 
3. brAhmAdhikaraNam

|| 4.4.5 ||

brAhmeNa jaiminir upanyAsAdibhyaH ||

sthitam etat svena rUpeNa [chA.u. 8.3.4] ityatra -- AtmamAtrarUpeNAbhiniShpadyate, na AgantukenApararUpeNeti | adhunA tu tadvisheShabubhutsAyAm abhidhIyate -- svam asya rUpaM brAhmam apahatapApmatvAdisatyasaN^kalpatvAvasAnaM tathA sarvaj~natvaM sarveshvaratvaM ca, tena svarUpeNAbhiniShpadyata iti jaiminir AcAryo manyate | kutaH? upanyAsAdibhyaH tathAtvAvagamAt | tathA hi ya AtmApahatapApmA [chA.u. 8.7.1] ityAdinA satyakAmaH satyasaN^kalpaH [chA.u. 8.7.1] ityevam antena upanyAsena evam AtmakatAm Atmano bodhayati | tathA sa tatra paryeti jakShat krIDan ramamANaH iti aishvaryarUpam Avedayati, tasya sarveShu lokeShu kAmacAro bhavati iti ca | sarvaj~naH sarveshvaraH ityAdivyapadeshAshca evam upapannA bhaviShyantIti ||5||

|| 4.4.6 || 

cititanmAtreNa tadAtmakatvAd ityauDulomiH || 

yadyapi apahatapApmatvAdayo bhedenaiva dharmA nirdishyante, tathApi shabdavikalpajA eva ete | pApmAdinivR^ittimAtraM hi tatra gamyate | caitanyam eva tu asya AtmanaH svarUpam iti tanmAtreNa svarUpeNa abhiniShpattir yuktA | tathA ca shrutiH -- evaM vA are.ayam AtmAnantaro.abAhyaH kR^itsnaH praj~nAnaghana eva [bR^i.A.u. 4.5.13] ityevaMjAtIyakA anugR^ihItA bhaviShyati | satyakAmatvAdayaH tu yadyapi vastusvarUpeNaiva dharmA ucyante -- satyAH kAmA asya iti, tathApi upAdhisambandhAdhInatvAt teShAM na caitanyavat svarUpatvasambhavaH, anekAkAratvapratiShedhAt | pratiShiddhaM hi brahmaNo.anekAkAratvam, na sthAnato.api parasyobhayaliN^gam [ve.sU. 3.2.11] ityatra | 

ata eva ca jakShaNAdisaN^kIrtanam api duHkhAbhAvamAtrAbhiprAyaM stutyartham AtmaratiH [chA.u. 7.25.2] ityAdivat | na hi mukhyAnyeva ratikrIDAmithunAni AtmanimittAni shakyante varNayitum, dvitIyaviShayatvAt teShAm | tasmAn nirastAsheShaprapaJNcena prasannena avyapadeshyena bodhAtmanA abhiniShpadyata ityauDulomir AcAryo manyate ||6||

|| 4.4.7 || 

evam apyupanyAsAt pUrvabhAvAd avirodhaM bAdarAyaNaH ||

evam api pAramArthikacaitanyamAtrasvarUpAbhyupagame.api vyavahArApekShayA pUrvasyApi upanyAsAdibhyo.avagatasya brAhmasya aishvaryarUpasya apratyAkhyAnAd avirodhaM bAdarAyaNa AcAryo manyate ||7||

  -- o)0(o -- 
4. saN^kalpAdhikaraNam 

|| 4.4.8 ||

hArdavidyAyAM shrUyate -- sa yadi pitR^ilokakAmo bhavati saN^kalpAd evAsya pitaraH samuttiShThanti [chA.u. 8.2.1] ityAdi | 

tatra saMshayaH -- kiM saN^kalpa eva kevalaH pitrAdisamutthAne hetuH, uta nimittAntarasahitaH ? iti | tatra satyapi saN^kalpAd eva iti shravaNe lokavat nimittAntarApekShatA yuktA | yathA loke asmadAdInAM saN^kalpAt gamanAdibhyashca hetubhyaH pitrAdisampattir bhavati, evaM muktasyApi syAt | evaM dR^iShTaviparItaM na kalpitaM bhaviShyati | saN^kalpAd eva iti tu rAj~na iva saN^kalpitArthasiddhikarIM sAdhanAntarasAmagrIM sulabhAm apekShya yokShyate | na ca saN^kalpamAtrasamutthAnAH pitrAdayaH manorathavijR^imbhitavat caJNcalatvAt puShkalaM bhogaM samarpayituM paryAptAH syuH iti | evaM prApte, brUmaH -- 

saN^kalpAd eva tu tacchruteH || 

saN^kalpAd eva tu kevalAt pitrAdisamutthAnam iti | kutaH? tacchruteH | saN^kalpAd evAsya pitaraH samuttiShThanti [chA.u. 8.2.1] ityAdikA hi shrutir nimittAntarApekShAyAM pIDyeta | nimittAntaram api tu yadi saN^kalpAnuvidhAyyeva syAt, bhavatu | na tu prayatnAntarasampAdyaM nimittAntaram iShyate, prAksampatteH vandhyasaN^kalpatvaprasaN^gAt | 

na ca shrutyavagamye.arthe lokavad iti sAmAnyato dR^iShTaM kramate | saN^kalpabalAd eva ca eShAM yAvatprayojanaM sthairyopapattiH, prAkR^itasaN^kalpavilakShaNatvAn muktasaN^kalpasya ||8||

|| 4.4.9 || 

ata eva cAnanyAdhipatiH ||

ata eva ca avandhyasaN^kalpatvAt ananyAdhipatir vidvAn bhavati -- nAsyAnyo.adhipatir bhavatItyarthaH | na hi prAkR^ito.api saN^kalpayan anyasvAmikatvam AtmanaH satyAM gatau saN^kalpayati | shrutishcaitad darshayati -- atha ya ihAtmAnam anuvidya vrajantyetAMshca satyAn kAmAMH teShAM sarveShu lokeShu kAmacAro bhavati [chA.u. 8.1.6] iti ||9||

  -- o)0(o -- 
5. abhAvAdhikaraNam 

|| 4.4.10 ||

abhAvaM bAdarir Aha hyevam || 

saN^kalpAd evAsya pitaraH samuttiShThanti [chA.u. 8.2.1] ityataH shruteH manaH tAvat saN^kalpasAdhanaM siddham | sharIrendriyANi punaH prAptaishvaryasya viduShaH santi, na vA santi -- iti samIkShyate | tatra bAdariH tAvad AcAryaH sharIrasyendriyANAM ca abhAvaM mahIyamAnasya viduSho manyate | kasmAt? evaM hi Aha AmnAyaH -- manasaitAn kAmAn pashyan ramate [chA.u. 8.12.5], ya ete brahmaloke [chA.u. 8.13.1] iti | yadi manasA sharIrendriyaishca vihareta, manaseti visheShaNaM na syAt | tasmAd abhAvaH sharIrendriyANAM mokShe ||10||

|| 4.4.11 ||

bhAvaM jaiminir vikalpAmananAt ||

jaiminiH tvacAryaH manovat sharIrasyApi sendriyasya bhAvaM muktaM prati manyate | yataH sa ekadhA bhavati tridhA bhavati [chA.u. 7.23.2] ityAdinA anekadhA bhAvavikalpam Amananti | na hi anekavidhatA vinA sharIrabhedena AJNjasI syAt | yadyapi nirguNAyAM bhUmavidyAyAm ayam anekadhAbhAvavikalpaH paThyate, tathApi vidyamAnam evedaM saguNAvasthAyAm aishvaryaM bhUmavidyAstutaye saN^kIrtyata ityataH saguNavidyAphalabhAvena upatiShThata iti ||11||

|| 4.4.12 ||

ucyate -- 
dvAdashAhavad ubhayavidhaM bAdarAyaNo.ataH || 

bAdarAyaNaH punar AcAryo.ata eva ubhayaliN^gashrutidarshanAt ubhayavidhatvaM sAdhu manyate -- yadA sasharIratAM saN^kalpayati tadA sasharIro bhavati, yadA tu asharIratAM tadA asharIra iti, satyasaN^kalpatvAt, saN^kalpavaicitryAcca | dvAdashAhavat -- yathA dvAdashAhaH satram ahInashca bhavati, ubhayaliN^gashrutidarshanAtevam idam apIti ||12||

|| 4.4.13 || 

tanvabhAve sandhyavadupapatteH ||

yadA tanoH sendriyasya sharIrasya abhAvaH, tadA, yathA sandhye sthAne sharIrendriyaviShayeShvavidyamAneShvapi upalabdhimAtrA eva pitrAdikAmA bhavanti, evaM mokShe.api syuH | evaM hyetad upapadyate ||13||

|| 4.4.14 || 

bhAve jAgradvat ||

bhAve punaH tanoH, yathA jAgarite vidyamAnA eva pitrAdikAmA bhavanti, evaM muktasyApyupapadyate ||14||

  -- o)0(o -- 
6. pradIpAdhikaraNam

|| 4.4.15 ||

bhAvaM jaiminir vikalpAmananAt ityatra sasharIratvaM muktasyoktam | tatra tridhAbhAvAdiShu anekasharIrasargo kiM nirAtmakAni sharIrANi dAruyantravat sR^ijyante, kiM vA sAtmakAnyasmadAdisharIravat -- iti bhavati vIkShA | tatra ca AtmamanasoH bhedAnupapatteH ekena sharIreNa yogAt itarANi sharIrANi nirAtmakAnItyevaM prApte, pratipadyate -- 

pradIpavad AveshaH tathA hi darshayati ||

yathA pradIpa eko.anekapradIpabhAvam Apadyate, vikArashaktiyogAt, evam eko.api san vidvAn aishvaryayogAd anekabhAvam Apadya sarvANi sharIrANyAvishati | kutaH? tathA hi darshayati shAstram ekasyAnekabhAvam -- sa ekadhA bhavati tridhA bhavati paJNcadhA saptadhA navadhA [chA.u. 7.26.2] ityAdi | naitad dAruyantropamAbhyupagame.avakalpate, nApi jIvAntarAveshe | na ca nirAtmakAnAM sharIrANAM pravR^ittiH sambhavati | yat tu Atmamanasor bhedAnupapatteH anekasharIrayogAsambhava iti -- naiSha doShaH | ekamano.anuvartIni samanaskAnyevAparANi sharIrANi satyasaN^kalpatvAt srakShyati | sR^iShTeShu ca teShu upAdhibhedAt Atmano.api bhedenAdhiShThAtR^itvaM yokShyate | eShaiva ca yogashAstreShu yoginAm anekasharIrayogaprakriyA ||15|| 

|| 4.4.16 ||

kathaM punaH muktasya anekasharIrAveshAdilakShaNam aishvaryam abhyupagamyate, yAvatA tat kena kaM vijAnIyAt [bR^i.A.u. 4.5.15], na tu tad dvitIyam asti tato.anyad vibhaktaM yad vijAnIyAt [bR^i.A.u. 4.3.30], salila eko draShTAdvaito bhavati [bR^i.A.u. 4.3.32] iti caivaMjAtIyakA shrutiH visheShavij~nAnaM vArayati | ityata uttaraM paThati -- 

svApyayasampattyor anyatarApekSham AviShkR^itaM hi ||

svApyayaH suShuptam, svam apIto bhavati tasmAd enaM svapitItyAcakShate [chA.u. 6.8.1] iti shruteH | sampattiH kaivalyam, brahmaiva san brahmApyeti [bR^i.A.u. 4.4.7] iti shruteH | tayor anyatarAm avasthAm apekShya etat visheShasaMj~nAbhAvavacanam -- kvacit suShuptAvasthAm apekShyocyate, kvacit kaivalyAvasthAm | katham avagamyate? yataH tatraiva etad adhikAravashAt AviShkR^itam -- etebhyo bhUtebhyaH samutthAya tAnyevAnu vinashyati na pretya saMj~nAsti [bR^i.A.u. 2.4.14], yatra tu asya sarvam AtmaivAbhUt [bR^i.A.u. 4.5.15], yatra supto na kaJNcana kAmaM kAmayate, na kaJNcana svapnaM pashyati [bR^i.A.u. 4.3.19, mA.u. 5] ityAdishrutibhyaH | saguNavidyAvipAkasthAnaM tu etat svargAdivat avasthAntaram, yatraitad aishvaryam upavarNyate | tasmAd adoShaH ||16||

  -- o)0(o -- 
7. jagadvyApArAdhikaraNam

|| 4.4.17 ||

ye saguNabrahmopAsanAt sahaiva manasA IshvarasAyujyaM vrajanti, kiM teShAM niravagraham aishvaryaM bhavati, Aho svit sAvagraham iti saMshayaH | kiM tAvat prAptam? niraN^kusham eva eShAm aishvaryaM bhavitum arhati, Apnoti svArAjyam [tai.u. 1.6.2], sarve.asmai devA balim Avahanti [tai.u. 1.5.3], teShAM sarveShu lokeShu kAmacAro bhavati [chA.u. 7.25.2, 8.1.6] ityAdishrutibhya iti | evaM prApte, paThati -- 

jagadvyApAravarjaM prakaraNAd asaMnihitatvAcca || 

jagadutpattyAdivyApAraM varjayitvA anyat aNimAdyAtmakam aishvaryaM muktAnAM bhavitum arhati, jagadvyApAraH tu nityasiddhasyaiva Ishvarasya | kutaH? tasya tatra prakR^itatvAt | asaMnihitatvAccetareShAm | para eva hi Ishvaro jagadvyapAre.adhikR^itaH, tam eva prakR^itya utpattyAdyupadeshAt, nityashabdanibandhanatvAcca | tadanveShaNavijij~nAsanapUrvakaM tu itareShAm aNimAdyaishvaryaM shrUyate | tenAsaMnihitAH te jagadvyApAre | samanaskatvAd eva ca eteShAm anaikamatye, kasyacit sthityabhiprAyaH kasyacit saMhArAbhiprAya ityevaM virodho.api kadAcit syAt | atha kasyacit saN^kalpam anu anyasya saN^kalpa ityavirodhaH samarthyeta, tataH parameshvarAkUtatantratvam evetareShAm iti vyavatiShThate ||17||


|| 4.4.18 || 

pratyakShopadeshAd iti cen nAdhikArikamaNDalasthokteH ||

atha yad uktam -- Apnoti svArAjyam [tai.u. 1.6.2] ityAdi pratyakShopadeshAt niravagraham aishvaryaM viduShAM nyAyyam iti, tat parihartavyam | atrocyate -- nAyaM doShaH, AdhikArikamaNDalasthokteH | AdhikAriko yaH savitR^imaNDalAdiShu visheShAyataneShvavasthitaH para IshvaraH, tadAyattaiva iyaM svArAjyaprAptir ucyate | yatkAraNam anantaram Apnoti manasaspatim [tai.u. 1.6.2] ityAha | yo hi sarvam anasAM patiH pUrvasiddha IshvaraH taM prApnotItyetad uktaM bhavati | tadanusAreNaiva ca anantaram vAkpatishcakShuShpatiH shrotrapatir vij~nAnapatiH ca bhavati [tai.u. 1.6.2] ityAha | evam anyatrApi yathAsambhavaM nityasiddhaishvarAyattam eva itareShAm aishvaryaM yojayitavyam ||18||

|| 4.4.19 || 

vikArAvarti ca tathA hi sthitim Aha ||

vikArAvartyapi ca nityamuktaM pArameshvaraM rUpam, na kevalaM vikAramAtragocaraM savitR^imaNDalAdyadhiShThAnam | tathA hi asya dvirUpAM sthitim Aha AmnAyaH -- 

tAvAn asya mahimA tato jyAyAMshca puruShaH | 
pAdo.asya sarvA bhUtAni tripAdasyAmR^itaM divi || [chA.u. 3.12.6] ityevam AdiH | 

na ca tat nirvikArarUpam itarAlambanAH prApnuvantIti shakyaM vaktum atatkratutvAt teShAm | atashca yathaiva dvirUpe parameshvare nirguNaM rUpam anavApya saguNa evAvatiShThante, evaM saguNe.api niravagraham aishvaryam anavApya sAvagraha evAvatiShThanta iti draShTavyam ||19||

|| 4.4.20 || 

darshayatashcaivaM pratyakShAnumAne ||

darshayatashca vikArAvartitvaM parasya jyotiShaH shrutismR^itI -- na tatra sUryo bhAti na candratArakaM nemA vidyuto bhAnti kuto.ayam agniH [ka.u. 5.15, shve.u. 6.14., mu.u. 2.2.10] iti, na tad bhAsayate sUryo na shashAN^ko na pAvakaH [gItA 15.6] iti ca | tad evaM vikArAvartitvaM parasya jyotiShaH prasiddham ityabhiprAyaH ||20||

|| 4.4.21 || 

bhogamAtrasAmyaliN^gAcca || 

itashca na niraN^kushaM vikArAlambanAnAm aishvaryam, yasmAt bhogamAtram eva eShAm anAdisiddhineshvareNa samAnam iti shrUyate -- tam AhApo vai khalu mIyante loko.asau iti sa yathaitAM devatAM sarvANi bhUtAnyavantyevaM haivaM vidaM sarvANi bhUtAnyavanti tena etasyai devatAyai sAyujyaM salokatAM jayati [bR^i.A.u. 1.5.23] ityAdi bhedavyapadeshaliN^gebhyaH ||21|| 

|| 4.4.22 ||

nanu evaM sati sAtishayatvAd antavattvam aishvaryasya syAt | tatashca eShAm AvR^ittiH prasajyeta -- ityataH uttaraM bhagavAn bAdarAyaNa AcAryaH paThati -- 

anAvR^ittiH shabdAd anAvR^ittiH shabdAt || 

nADIr ashmisamanvitena arcirAdiparvaNA devayAnena pathA ye brahmalokaM shAstroktavisheShaNaM gacchanti -- yasmin narashca ha vai NyashcArNavau brahmaloke tR^itIyasyAm ito divi, yasminn airaM madIyaM saraH, yasminn ashvatthaH somasavanaH, yasminn aparAjitA pUrbrahmaNaH, yasmiMshca prabhuvimitaM hiraNmayaM veshma, yashcAnekadhA mantrArthavAdAdipradesheShu prapaJNcyate -- te taM prApya na candralokAd iva bhuktabhogA Avartante | kutaH? tayordhvam Ayann amR^itatvam eti teShAM na punar AvR^ittiH etena pratipadyamAnA imaM mAnavam AvartaM nAvartante [chA.u. 4.15.5], brahmalokam abhisampadyante [chA.u. 8.15.1], na ca punar Avartate [chA.u. 8.15.1] ityAdi shabdebhyaH | antavattve.api tu aishvaryasya yathA anAvR^ittiH tathA varNitam -- kAryAtyaye tadadhyakSheNa sahAtaH param [ve.sU. 4.3.10] ityatra | samyagdarshanavidhvastatamasAM tu nityasiddhanirvANaparAyaNAnAM siddhaiva anAvR^ittiH | tadAshrayaNenaiva hi saguNasharaNAnAm apyanAvR^ittisiddhiH iti | anAvR^ittiH shabdAd anAvR^ittiH shabdAt -- iti sUtrAbhyAsaH shAstraparisamAptiM dyotayati ||22||

|| iti shrImatparamahaMsaparivrAjakAcAryAsya shrIgovindabhagavatpUjyapAdashiShyasya
shrImacchaN^karabhagavataH kR^itau shArIrakamImAMsAsUtrabhAShye 
caturthAdhyAyasya caturthaH pAdaH ||

|| iti shrImacchArIrakamImAMsAsUtrabhAShyaM sampUrNam ||
